biʃːunɡo tsebe allaɡʔas zobɡi rakʔɡi biʒana
tʃʼoboɡo bukʼana ʒeɡi rakʔ wa ɡʔjeɬul kuts bukʼintʃʼo betsʼab nakʼkʼ tʼad tʼuparab tʼinu ɬalareb ʁwariɬiɡi ʁwaridal ɬinazda tʼad ɡʔuri ɡʼadin borʒanqχuleb ɡʼitsʼɡo allaɡʔasul ruχʼɡi bukʼana
allaɡʔas abuna
biʒa kanɬi jan
wa kanɬi biʒana
allaɡʔasda biχʔana kanɬijaɬul ɬikʼɬi wa ɡʔjes kanɬi betsʼɬijaldasa batʼa ɡʔabuna
kanɬijalda tsʼar qʼojilan ɬuna betsʼɬijalda tsʼar sordojilan aχʼana
bukʼana qʼasimeχ naqχeɡi roɡʔjel ɡʔjedin ana tʼotsebeseb qʼo
tsinɡi allaɡʔas abuna
ɬinal kʼijide rikʔize ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔob qʼwakʼarab pardaw biʒa jan wa ɡʔjedin kːana
allaɡʔas qʼwakʼarab pardaw biʒana wa ɡʔjelda ʁorkʔɡi tʼadɡi ɬinal kʼijide rikʔana
ɡʔjeb pardawalda tsʼar allaɡʔas zobilan ɬuna
bukʼana qʼasimeχ naqχeɡi roɡʔjel ɡʔjedin ana kʼiabileb qʼo
wa allaɡʔas abuna
zobalazda ʁorkʔ ruɡel kinalɡo ɬinal tsojide rakʼare wa raqʼdalɬi qʼwatʼibe bakːa jan
wa ɡʔjedin kːana
raqʼdalɬijalda tsʼar allaɡʔas rakʔilan ɬuna tsotsazde dandeɬaral ɬinazda tsʼar raɬadal abun aχʼana allaɡʔasda biχʔana ɡʔjeb ɬikʼ kːej
allaɡʔas abuna
rakʔaɬ batʼi batʼijab ɡʼurtʃːinɬi biʒizabe χʔon buɡeb tʼjeɡʔ χerɡi buɡʼa roɬɡi wa χʔon buɡeb piqχ kʔolel ʁutʼbiɡi
wa ɡʔjedin kːana
rakʔaɬ biʒizabuna batʼi batʼijab ɡʼurtʃːinɬi tʼjeɡʔ χerɡi buɡʼa roɬɡi piqχ kʔolel ʁutʼbiɡi ɡʔjezul ʃːibaɬul ʒindi ʒindir tajpajaɬul χʔonɡi bukʼana rakʔuɬ bekʔani tsʼidasan ʒib biʒuleb allaɡʔasda biχʔana ɡʔjeb ɬikʼ kːej
bukʼana qʼasimeχ naqχeɡi roɡʔjel ɡʔjedin ana ɬababileb qʼo
allaɡʔas abuna
zodil pardawalda riʒa sordoɡi qʼoɡi batʼa ɡʔabulel zamanaɬul batʼi batʼijab riɡʔɡi ɡʼuʒɡi biχʔizabulel wa qʼojalɡi sonalɡi rikʼkʼine baʒarulel ɡwanʁaral tʃiraqχal
zodil pardawalda kentʃʼjeze ritʃːante ɡʔjel rakʔaɬe kanɬi kʔjeze
wa ɡʔjedin kːana
allaɡʔas kʼiɡo kʼudijab tʃiraqχ biʒana ɡʔjezul kʼudijab qʼojaze χanɬi ɡʔabize ɡʔitʼinabab sardaze χanɬi ɡʔabize ɡʔjedinɡo tsʼwabiɡi riʒana
allaɡʔas ɡʔjel zodil pardawalda ɬuna ɡʔjez dunjal ɡwanʁizabize
qʼojazeɡi sardazeɡi χanɬi ɡʔabize wa kanɬiɡi betsʼɬiɡi tsotsazdasa batʼa ɡʔabize allaɡʔasda biχʔana ɡʔjeb ɬikʼ kːej
bukʼana qʼasimeχ naqχeɡi roɡʔjel ɡʔjedin ana unqʼabileb qʼo
allaɡʔas abuna
ɬinaz biʒizabe ɡʼjemerab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi zodiqχ ɡʔawajalda χʼantʃʼiɡi rorʒanqχe
ɡʔjedin allaɡʔas riʒana raɬdal azdaɡʔabiɡi ɬadaɬ rukʼunel ɡʼjemeral batʼi batʼijal ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬabiɡi zodiqχ rorʒanqχulel batʼi batʼijab tajpajaɬul χʼantʃʼiɡi
allaɡʔasda biχʔana ɡʔjeb ɬikʼ kːej
wa ɡʔjeb kinaldaɡo barakatɡi ɬun allaɡʔas amru ɡʔabuna
nuʒerɡo tʼintʃʼ qʼed tsʼikʼkʼinabe nuʒɡo ɡʼjemerɬizare wa raɬadazul ɬinal nuʒedaɬun tsʼjezare ritʃːante rakʔalda tʼad χʼantʃʼiɡi ɡʼjemerɬize
bukʼana qʼasimeχ naqχeɡi roɡʔjel ɡʔjedin ana ʃːuabileb qʼo
allaɡʔas abuna
rakʔaɬ riʒizare batʼi batʼijab tajpajaɬul ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬabi χʼajwanalɡi rakʔaldasan ʃurulel ʒalɡi wa ɡʼalχul ʒanawaralɡi
wa ɡʔjedin kːana
allaɡʔas riʒana batʼi batʼijab tajpajaɬul ɡʼalχul ʒanawaral χʼajwanal wa rakʔaldasan ʃuruleb batʼi batʼijab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi allaɡʔasda biχʔana ɡʔjeb ɬikʼ kːej
allaɡʔas abuna
ratʃʼa niɬer suratalda wa niɬer sipatalda reqʼon insan
ɡʔjedin allaɡʔas insan wiʒana ʒindirɡo sipat suratalda reqʼon
allaɡʔasul sipat suratalda wiʒana ɡʔjes insan
biχʔintʃiɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanɡi kʼijalɡo riʒana
allaɡʔas ɡʔjezda barakat ɬuna wa ɡʔadin abuna
nuʒetsa ɬimal tsʼikʼkʼun ɡʔare nuʒɡo ɡʼjemerɬize rukʼine rakʔ tsʼjezabe wa ɡʔjelda tʼad kwerʃːel ɡʔabe raɬadazuɬ ruɡel tʃːuɡʼbuzdaɡi zobalazda rorʒanqχulel χʼantʃʼazdaɡi wa rakʔaldasan χʔwadulelʃːinal ʒalazdaɡi tʼad kwerʃːel ɡʔabe
ʒeɡi allaɡʔas abuna
ɡʔale ditsa nuʒee niɡʼmatɬun kʔuna rakʔalda biʒarabʃːinab χʔon buɡeb tʼjeɡʔ χer wa χʔon buɡeb piqχ kʔolel ʁutʼbi
ɡʼalχul ʒanawarazeɡi χʼantʃʼazeɡi rakʔaldasan ʃurulelʃːinal ʒalazeɡi aj ruχʼ buɡebʃːinaɬe ditsa kinabniɡi ɡʼurtʃːinab χer kʔoleb buɡo kwanaze
wa ɡʔjedin kːana
allaɡʔ walaɡʔana ʒintsaɡo biʒanʃːinaɬuqχ tsʼaqʼ ɬikʼ bukʼana ɡʔjeb
bukʼana qʼasimeχ naqχeɡi roɡʔjel ɡʔjedin ana anɬabileb qʼo

ɡʔjedin riʒana zobɡi rakʔɡi wa zob rakʔalda buɡebʃːinabɡi
ankʔabileb qʼojalde allaɡʔas ʒindirɡo χʼaltʼi raɡʼalde baqχinabuna wa kinalɡo χʼaltʼabiɡi qʼotʼizarun ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjes χʼalχʔi ɡʔabuna
ankʔabileb qʼojalda barakatɡi ɬun allaɡʔas ɡʔjeb χirijab qʼoɬun ɡʔabuna ʃːajɡureɬul kinalɡo iʃalɡi tʼuran ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjes χʼuχʔbaqχidal
ɡʔale ɡʔadinab buɡo zobɡi rakʔɡi kin biʒarabali bitsuneb qʼisa
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas rakʔɡi zobɡi biʒarab qʼojaɬ
rakʔalda ʒeɡi bukʼintʃʼo tsoniɡi qχaraqχ jaɡi tsoniɡi χaril sum ʃːajɡureɬul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas rakʔalde ʒeɡi tsʼad bazabuleb bukʼintʃʼjeɬul wa rakʔ χʼaltʼizabize insanɡi wukʼintʃʼjeɬul
rakʔaɬe reɡʔjel kʔoleb bukʼana ɡʼitsʼɡo rakʔul tʃoχʔonisan batʃʼuneb χʼuχʔjelaɬ
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas insan ɡʔawuna rakʔul χʼurudasan wa ɡʔjesul maɡʼarzuqχe ɡʼumrujaɬul χʼuχʔjelɡi pun ɡʔjew tʃʼaɡojab ruχʼɬun ɬuɡʔinawuna
χadub edemalda baqʼbakːuda betʼjerhan allaɡʔas aχ biʒizabuna wa ʒintsaɡo wiʒaraw insan ɡʔjeniw tana
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔjenir riʒizaruna batʼi batʼijal piqχil ʁutʼbi riχʔize bertsinal wa piqχ ɡʔuinal aχ bakʔuɬ biʒizabuna ɡʼumrujaɬul ʁwetʼɡi ɬikʼɬi kweʃɬi ɬazabuleb ʁwetʼɡi
edemaldasan ɡʔjeb aχɡi ɬaɬalaɡo tʃwaχuleb bukʼana kʼudijab ɡʼor tsinɡi eχebeɡʼan unqʼide bikʔuleb bukʼana ɡʔitʼinal ɡʼoral ɬuɡʔun
ɡʔjezul tsojalda tsʼar kːola piʃon ɡʔjeb tʃwaχula mesed ɡʼjemerab χʼawila aburab ulka qʼotʼun
ɡʔjenib mesedɡi buɡo maχʼɡʔuinal pitsʼalɡi ruɡo oniks abuleb baɡʔa χirijab ʒawɡʔarɡi buɡo
kʼiabileb ɡʼoralda tsʼar buɡo ɡiχon ɡʔjeb tʃwaχula tʼolabɡo kuʃ ulkajaldasan
ɬababileb ɡʼoralda tsʼar buɡo tiɡr
edemaɬul aχikʔ tana betʼjerhan allaɡʔas insan ɡʔjeb aχ χʼaltʼizabize wa ɡʔjeɬul tʼalab ɡʔabize
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas insanasda ɬazabuna
bokʔarab ʁotʼodasa piqχ kwanaze beɡʔula dutsa
amma ɬikʼɬiɡi kweʃɬiɡi ɬazabuleb ʁotʼodasa piqχ kwanaɡe naɡaɡʔ ɡʔjeb dutsa kwanani mun ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬɡo χweze wuɡo
χadub betʼjerhan allaɡʔas abuna
ʒiwɡo tsoχʼo wukʼin insanase ɬikʼ ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjesije dande kːolew kumektʃi wiʒila ditsa
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas rakʔudasan riʒana kinalɡo χʼajwanalɡi zobalazul χʼantʃʼiɡi ɡʔjel kinalɡo ɡʔjes insanasda askʼore ratʃana ɡʔjezda insanas kinal tsʼaral ɬolelali χal ɡʔabize insanas kinab tsʼar ɬuniɡi ɡʔjeb tsʼar χutʼana ʃːibab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijalda
insanas tsʼaral ɬuna kinalniɡi ruqʼaɬul χʼajwanazda kinalniɡi zobalazul χʼantʃʼazda wa kinalniɡi ɡʼalχul ʒanawarazda amma ʒindije dande kːolew kumektʃi ɡʔjesda watitʃʼo
ɡʔjebmeχalda betʼjerhan allaɡʔas insanasde ʁwaridab makʔu batʃʼinabuna wa ɡʔjew kʔiʒun kːarawɡo ɡʔjesul tso χʔabalaqχaɡʼutʃʼɡi baqχun ɡʔjeb bukʼarab bakʼ ɡʔanatsa batsana
ɡʔjeb χʔabalaqχaɡʼutʃʼaldasan betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬe kuts muqχ ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjej insanasda askʼoje jatʃana
insanas abuna
ɡʔale dir rakʔajaldasan rakʔa
dir tʃerχaldasan tʃerχ
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan bukʼina ɡʔjelda tsʼar
biχʔintʃijasdasan josaraj jiɡeɬul
ɡʔjedinɬidal ebel emenɡi reχun tun ʒindirɡo tʃʼuʒuɡun wukʼina biχʔintʃi wa ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo tsoɬun tsoχʼo tʃerχ ɡʼadin ɬuɡʔina
ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo biχʔintʃiɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanɡi ɡʼitsʼɡo rukʼana amma ɡʔjel ɡʔjeldasa netʃolaroan

betʼjerhan allaɡʔas riʒaral kinalɡo ɡʼalχul ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬabazda ɡʔorkʔob biʃːunɡo siχʼirab bukʼana boroχʔ ɡʔjeɬ tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanalda ɡʔiqʼana
ɡʔab aχikʔa tsoniɡi ʁotʼodasa piqχ kwanaze bitʃːaleb ɡʔjetʃʼin nuʒee allaɡʔasilan aburab ʒo bitʼarab buɡiʃː abun
aχikʔ ruɡel ʁutʼbuzdasa piqχ kwanaze niʒee iznu buɡo jan ʒawab kʔuna tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ
amma aχ bakʔuɬ buɡeb ʁotʼol raqχaɬ allaɡʔas abuna ɡʔjelda tʼasa piqχ kwanaɡejilan ɡʔjelda kwertsin qχwaɡejilan ɡuroni niʒ χolilan
χolarelχa jan abuna borχʔitsa
allaɡʔasda ɬala ɡʔjeb ʁotʼol piqχ kwarab meχalda nuʒer beral raɡʔulebɬi wa allaɡʔasda ɡʼadin ɬikʼɬiɡi kweʃɬiɡi ɬalel ɡʼadamalɬun nuʒ ɬuɡʔunebɬi
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanalda biχʔana ɡʔjeb ʁotʼol piqχ kwanaze ɬikʼabɡi biχʔize bertsinabɡi ɡʼaqʼilɬi tsʼodorɬi kʔoleb bukʼinaɬ ʒinde ʁira kːezabulebɡi bukʼin ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjeb ʁotʼodasa piqχ tʼuna kwanana wa askʼow wukʼaraw rosaseɡi kʔuna ɡʔjesɡi kwanana
ɡʔjebsaɡʼataldaɡo ɡʔjezul beral raɡʔun ratʃʼana wa ʒalɡo ɡʼitsʼɡo rukʼin biχʔana ɡʔjebmeχaɬ inʒiraɬul ʁotʼol tʼanχazul χʔuχʔun ʒiderɡo ɡʼawrat baχtʃize ʒo ɡʔabuna ɡʔjez
baqʼaniɡʼuʒaɬul ɡʔoɡʔomarab ɡʔuri baqχindal ɡʔjezda raɡʼana betʼjerhan allaɡʔ aχikʔan watʃʼunew wa ʁutʼbuzda naqχa raχtʃana ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo
mun kiw wuɡew in aχʼana betʼjerhan allaɡʔas insanasde
dida raɡʼana mun aχikʔan watʃʼunew abun ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjes dudasa χʼinqʼun waχtʃun wuɡo dun ʃːajɡureɬul dun ɡʼitsʼɡo wuɡeɬul
ɬitsa duda aburab mun ɡʼitsʼɡo wuɡilan ditsa duda kwanaɡejan abun bukʼarab ʁotʼodasa piqχiʃː kwanarab in tsʼjeχana ɡʔjes
insanas ɡʔjesije ʒawab ɡʔabuna
dutsa dije kʔuraj tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan jiɡo dunɡun ɡʔjeɬ kʔuna dije dob ʁotʼodasa piqχ ditsaɡi kwanana jan
dutsa ɡʔaburab ʃːib an ɡʔiqʼana betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanalda
ɡʔjeɬ ʒawab kʔuna
borχʔitsa ɡukːana dun ɡʔjedin kwana ditsa ɡʔjeb
tsinɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔas borχʔida abuna
dutsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔaburaɬuqχ naɡʼana buɡo duje kinalɡo ʒanawarazdaɡi χʼajwanazdaɡi ʁorɬ naɡʼanabatadɬun bukʼina mun tʼolabɡo ɡʼumrujaɬ mun tʃeχʔalda qχurʃːila dur kwenɬunɡi χʼur bukʼina
munɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanɡi tsotsaze tuʃbabiɬun ɡʔarila ditsa tuʃmanɬi bukʼina dur tʼantʃʼazdaɡi ɡʔjeɬul naslujaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔjeɬul wasas dur betʼjer tʃʼintʼila dutsa ɡʔjesul χʼatʼiaʁada χʼantʃʼila
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanalda ɡʔjes abuna
ɬimadul χʼara tʃʼwarab meχaɬ ɡʼazab tsʼikʼkʼinabila ditsa duje ɡʼazab ɡʼaqʼubajalda ɡʔarila dutsa ɬimal buɡoniɡi ros wokʔila duje amma rosas duda tʼad kwerʃːel ɡʔabila
adamida betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔadin abuna
durɡo ɬaduqχɡi ɡʼjenekːun kwanaɡejan ditsa duda ɬazabun bukʼarab ɡʔjeb piqχ kwanana dutsa ɡʔanʒe mun sababɬun ɡʔab rakʔaɬeɡi naɡʼana buɡo ɡʼazab ɡʼaqʼuba biχʔun χʼaltʼila mun tʼolabɡo ɡʼumrujaɬ rakʔaldasa niɡʼmat ʃːwejaɬe ɡʼolo
zazɡi tʃʼaχʼɡi biʒila rakʔaɬ duje wa χurisa batʃʼarab ʒo bukʼina duje kwanije
ɡʼjetʼ betsʼtsʼun ɡuroni ʃːwelaro duje kwine ʒo rakʔaldasan wiʒaraw mun rakʔuɬe tʼad wusːineɡʼan mun rakʔ wuɡeɬul naqχeɡi rakʔude swerize wuɡo
adamitsa
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas qʼoχʔol partal ɡʔabuna adamijeɡi ɡʔjesul ɬadujeɡi wa ɡʔjeb ɡʔjezda retʼana
tsinɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔas abuna
ɡʔale ɡʔanʒe insan ɬuɡʔun wuɡo niɬer tsojaw ɡʼadinaw ɬikʼɬiɡi kweʃɬiɡi ɬana ɡʔjesda ɡʔanʒe dob ɡʼumrujaɬul ʁotʼodeɡi kwer beɡʔize ɡurin ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬul piqχɡi kwanan χwel ɡʔjetʃʼjewɬun ɬuɡʔine
tsinɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔas insan edemaɬul aχikʔa qʼwatʼiwe ʁuna wa ʒindasan ɡʔjew wiʒarab rakʔ χʼaltʼizabize witʼana
allaɡʔas insanɡi qʼwatʼiwe ʁun edemaɬul aχil baqʼbakːul raqχalda kinabɡo raqχalde χʔwaɡʼuleb tsʼadul χwaltʃenɡun χeruwimal

adam ʒindirɡo ɬadi χʼawada askʼow weɡana ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana wa qʼabil
ɡʔjeɬ abuna
betʼjerhanasul kumekaldaɬun dije insan ʃːwana jan
χaduw ɡʔjeɬije ɡʔawuna qʼabilil wats ɡʔabil
ɡʔabil ɡʼijaweχʔɬun ɬuɡʔana qʼabilin abuni wekʔaruqχanɬun waqχana
tso zamanaldasan qʼabilitsa betʼjerhanase χurul batʃʼinalda tʼasa χirijab sadaqʼa kʔuna
ɡʔabilitsaɡi ʒindirɡo reqχaɬa tʼotsere ɡʔarural χuχalɡi qχun tʼasa riʃːaral kʔari kʔarijal ɡʔanal keskal betʼjerhanase qʼurban ɡʔaruna ɡʔabilidaɡi ɡʔjesul qʼurban sadaqʼajaldaɡi raziɬana betʼjerhan
qʼabiliqχɡi ɡʔjesul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬuqχɡijan abuni ɡʔjew walaɡʔizetsin walaɡʔitʃʼo ɡʔjebmeχaɬ tsːidatsa kʔjerχinabuna qʼabilil ɡʔumer
betʼjerhanas qʼabilida abuna
ʃːaj dur tsːin baqχarab ʃːaj dur ɡʔumer kʔjerχarab
dutsa bitʼarab ɡʔabuleb buɡoni ɡʔumer bitʼun walaɡʔilariʃː mun amma dutsa bitʼarab ɡʔabuleb ɡʔjetʃʼoni munaɡʔ buɡo dur nutsʼiqχ baχtʃun tʃʼun duda tʼad kwerʃːel ɡʔabize bokʔun buɡo munaɡʔaɬe amma munaɡʔalda tʼad χanɬi ɡʔabize kːola dutsa
qʼabilitsa ʒindirɡo wats ɡʔabilida abuna
riɬːa tso maʁiɬe tira swerize
ɡʔjenire ʃːwaralɡo qʼabilitsa toχɬukʔje tʼadɡi retʃʼtʃʼun ʒindirɡo wats ɡʔabil tʃʼwana
dur wats ɡʔabil kiw wuɡew in ɡʔiqʼana betʼjerhanas qʼabilida
dida ɬalaro jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjes dun ɡʔjesda tʼad taraw qχarawuliʃː
dutsa ɡʔaburab ʒo ʃːib in abuna betʼjerhanas dur watsasul ɡʼodobe tʼurab bi buɡo rakʔuɬan dide aχʼi baleb
ɡʔanʒe abadijaɬul naɡʼana buɡo duje dur watsasul dutsa ɡʼodobe tʼurab bi ɡʔjeqʼarab rakʔaɬ munɡi naqχ tʃʼwana ɡʔanʒe
kiɡʼan tsʼikʼkʼun mun χʼaltʼaniɡi tʼokʼaɬ χʔiχʔilaro ɡʔjeɬ mun ɡʔanʒejaldasa χaduw mun aparaɡɬuda rakʔalda tirulew χutʼila
dida batʃːize kʼolareb tamiχʼ ʒaza buɡo ɡʔjeb in abuna qʼabilitsa betʼjerhanasda
ɡʔale dutsa rakʔaldasa naqχe qʼotʼulew wuɡo dun dur berda tsewesa naqχe ɡʔawulew wuɡo aparaɡɬuda bakʼ bakʼalde ɡotʃun rakʔalda tirulew χutʼaraw dun tsewe kːaraw tʃijas tʃʼwan reχilariʃː
ɬitsaniɡi qʼabil tʃʼwani ɡʔjesdasa ankʔtsʼulɡo qʼisas bosize buɡo jan abuna betʼjerhanas
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas qʼabilida χasab ɡʼuʒ ɬuna ɡʔjew kiw wataniɡi ɬitsaɡo tʃʼwatʃʼoɡo wukʼine
tsinɡi qʼabil betʼjerhanasda askʼosa naqχe ana wa edemaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda buɡeb nod ulkajalda tʃʼana
qʼabil ʒindirɡo tʃʼuʒujalda askʼow weɡana ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer ɬuɡʔana wa ɡʔjesije was ɡʔawuna jenoχ abun tsʼarɡi ɬuna qʼabilitsa ɡʔjeb zamanalda ʃaɡʔar baleb bukʼana ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔaraldaɡi ɬuna ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo wasasul tsʼar jenoχ
jenoχije ɡʔawuna was ɡʼirad ɡʼiradije ɡʔawuna meχʼujael meχʼujaelije ɡʔawuna metuʃael metuʃaelije ɡʔawuna lameχ
lameχitsa jatʃana kʼiɡo ɬadi tsojalda tsʼar bukʼana ɡʼada tsoɡidalda tsilla
ɡʼadatsa ɡʔawuna was jawal ɡʔjesdasan ɬuɡʔana tʃadrazuqχ jaʃaw ɡʔabulel wa ɡʼi botsʼi χʔiχʔulel ɡʼadamal
ɡʔjesul wats juwalidasan ɬuɡʔana lirajalda wa ʃːwantʼiχalda baqʼnal ratʃine ɬalel tʃaɡʼi
tsillatsa ɡʔawuna was tuwal qʼabil mazɡarul wa maχːul tʼaɡʼjelal ɡʔarulew ustar tuwal qʼabilil jikʼana naɡʼamajin abulej jats
lameχitsa ʒindirɡo ɬudbuzda abuna
diqχ ɡʼjenekːeja nuʒ ɡʼada wa tsilla
ditsa bitsuneɬuqχ ɡʼintʼame lameχil ɬudbi
ditsa biχʔintʃi tʃʼwana ɡʔjes dun ɬuqʼaraɬuqχ
ɡʔitʼinaw ɡʼoloqχantʃiɡi tʃʼwana ɡʔjes dida kʔaburaɬuqχ
qʼabil tʃʼwarasdasa qʼisas ankʔɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼun bosula
amma lameχ tʃʼwarasdasa qʼisas ɬabqʼojalda antsʼila ankʔɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼun bosila
adam naqχeɡi tʃʼuʒujalda askʼow weɡana ɡʔjeɬ was ɡʔawuna wa ɡʔjesda tsʼar ʃet ɬuna ɡʔjeɬ abuna qʼabilitsa tʃʼwaraw ɡʔabilil bakʼalda allaɡʔas dije tsoɡi ɬimer kʔuna
ʃetijeɡi was ɡʔawuna wa ɡʔjesda tsʼar enoʃilan
ɡʔjeldasa naqχe ɡʼadamaz bajbiχʔana betʼjerhanase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize

ɡʔale adamil naslabazul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ qʼisa
allaɡʔas insan wiʒarab meχaɬ ʒindirɡo sipat suratalda wiʒana ɡʔjes ɡʔjew
allaɡʔas riʒana biχʔintʃiɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanɡi wa ɡʔjezda barakat ɬuna ɡʔjel riʒarab qʼojaɬ ɡʔjes ɡʔjezda tsʼarɡi insan abun ɬuna
adamitsa nusijalda ɬeberɡo son barab meχaɬ ʒindirɡo ɡʼadab sipat surataɬul was ɡʔawuna ɡʔjesije
ʃet abun tsʼar ɬuna adamitsa ɡʔjesda ʃet ɡʔawun χadubɡi adamitsa dunjalalda bana mikʔnusɡo son ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
kinabniɡi itʃʼnusijalda ɬeberɡo sonɡi ban adam χwana
ʃetitsa nusijalda ʃːuɡo son barab meχaɬ ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was enoʃ
enoʃ ɡʔawun χadubɡi ʃetitsa dunjalalda bana mikʔnusijalda ankʔɡo son ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
kinabniɡi itʃʼnusijalda antsʼila kʼiɡo sonɡi ban ʃet χwana
enoʃitsa unqʼojalda antsʼɡo son barab meχaɬ ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was kenan
kenan ɡʔawun χadubɡi enoʃitsa dunjalalda bana mikʔnusijalda antsʼila ʃːuɡo son ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
kinabniɡi itʃʼnusijalda ʃːuɡo sonɡi ban enoʃ χwana
kenanitsa ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo son barab meχaɬ ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was maɡʔalalel
maɡʔalalel ɡʔawun χadubɡi kenanitsa dunjalalda bana mikʔnusijalda kʼiqʼoɡo son ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
kinabniɡi itʃʼnusijalda antsʼɡo sonɡi ban kenan χwana
maɡʔalalelitsa ɬabqʼojalda ʃːuɡo son barab meχaɬ ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was jered
jered ɡʔawun χadubɡi maɡʔalalelitsa dunjalalda bana mikʔnusijalda ɬeberɡo son ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
kinabniɡi mikʔnusijalda unqʼojalda antsʼila ʃːuɡo sonɡi ban maɡʔalalel χwana
jereditsa nusijalda ɬabqʼojalda kʼiɡo son barab meχaɬ ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was idris
idris ɡʔawun χadubɡi jereditsa dunjalalda bana mikʔnusɡo son ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
kinabniɡi itʃʼnusijalda ɬabqʼojalda kʼiɡo sonɡi ban jered χwana
idrisitsa ɬabqʼojalda ʃːuɡo son barab meχaɬ ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was metuʃelaχʼ
metuʃelaχʼ ɡʔawun χadubɡi idrisitsa dunjalalda bana ɬabnusɡo son rakʼ rakʼaɬɡo allaɡʔase χʼjelun χʔwadana ɡʔjew ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
kinabniɡi ɬabnusijalda ɬabqʼojalda ʃːuɡo son bana idrisitsa
rakʼ rakʼaɬɡo allaɡʔase χʼjelun χʔwadana idris tsinɡi ɡʔjew tʼaɡʼana ʃːajɡureɬul allaɡʔas ɡʔjew ʒindiqχeɡo zobalazde watʃun ana
metuʃelaχʼitsa nusijalda unqʼojalda ankʔɡo son barab meχaɬ ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was lameχ
lameχ ɡʔawun χadubɡi metuʃelaχʼitsa dunjalalda bana ankʔnusijalda unqʼojalda kʼiɡo son ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
kinabniɡi itʃʼnusijalda ɬabqʼojalda itʃʼɡo sonɡi ban metuʃelaχʼ χwana
lameχitsa nusijalda unqʼojalda kʼiɡo son barab meχaɬ ɡʔjesije was ɡʔawuna
wasasda nuχʼilan tsʼarɡi ɬun ɡʔjes abuna niɬer iʃazuɬ wa betʼjerɡʔanas naɡʼana kʔurab ɡʔab rakʔalda ɡʔarulel χʼaltʼabazuɬ niɬer rekʼjee χʼalχʔi ɬuɡʔinabila ɡʔas abun
nuχʼ ɡʔawun χadubɡi lameχitsa dunjalalda bana ʃːunusijalda unqʼojalda antsʼila ʃːuɡo son ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
kinabniɡi ankʔnusijalda ɬabqʼojalda antsʼila ankʔɡo sonɡi ban lameχ χwana
nuχʼitsa ʃːunusɡo son bana wa ɡʔjesije ɡʔaruna wasal ʃem χam wa jafet

dunjalalda ɡʼadamal ɡʼjemerɬize ɬuɡʔana wa ɡʔjezije jasalɡi ɡʔarulel rukʼana
ɡʼadamil jasazul bertsinɬi biχʔun allaɡʔasul wasaz
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas abuna
insanasuɬ dir χʼuχʔjel ruχʼ abadijaɬɡo bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjew ɡʼitsʼab ɡʔanal tʃerχ ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjesul ɡʼumruɡi nusijalda qʼoɡo sonaldasa tʼade ine ɡʔjetʃʼo
ɡʔjeb zamanaldaɡi ɡʔjeldasa χadubɡi rakʔalda tʼad rukʼana nefilimalin abulel borχatab laɡa tʃerχaɬul zalimal ɡʼadamal allaɡʔasul wasal χʔwadulel rukʼindalχa ɡʼadamazul jasazuqχe wa ɡʔjezdasan ɬimalɡi ɡʔarulel rukʼindal tsebe zamanaldaɡo tsʼar raɡʼaral ɡutʃal baχʼarzal rukʼana ɡʔjel
tsinɡi betʼjerhanasda biχʔana rakʔalda ɡʼadamazul kweʃɬi χʼataldasa un ɡʼjemerɬun bukʼin ɡʔjezul kinabɡo pikru qʼasdɡi tʃʼjetʃʼoɡo kweʃɬijaɬe χʼaltʼuleb bukʼin
rakʔalda insan wiʒijaldasa rakʼ buχʼana betʼjerhanasul wa kutakalda rekʼjeqʼɬun
betʼjerhanas abuna
ditsaɡo riʒaral kinalɡo ɡʼadamalɡi ɡʔjezdaɡo tsadaqχ χʼajwanalɡi ʒanawaralɡi χʼantʃʼiɡi rakʔaldasa ɬuɡʼizarila ditsa dir rakʼ buχʼana ɡʔjel riʒijaldasa
ɡʼitsʼɡo nuχʼidasa raziɡo wukʼana betʼjerhan
ɡʔale nuχʼil wa ɡʔjesul naslujaɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ qʼisa
dob zamanaɬul ɡʼadamazda ɡʔorkʔow ɡʼitsʼɡo nuχʼ wukʼana allaɡʔase mutʼiɡʼaw rakʼbatsʼtsʼadaw wa witʼaraw tʃi
nuχʼil wukʼana ɬabɡo was ʃem χam wa jafet
allaɡʔasda tsebe dunjal tʼuban pasaɬarab zaman batʃʼana kweʃɬijaɬɡi zulmujaɬɡi tsʼun bukʼana rakʔ
allaɡʔasda biχʔana dunjal pasaɬun bukʼin wa dunjalalda biʒarabʃːinabɡi qʼosun kːun bukʼin
tsinɡi allaɡʔas nuχʼida abuna
rakʔalda biʒanʃːinab tʼaɡʼinabize χʼukmu ɡʔabuna ditsa ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjezul kweʃɬijaɬɡi zulmujaɬɡi tsʼjezabun buɡo dunjal ditsa ɡʔjelɡi ɡʔjezdaɡo tsadaqχ rakʔɡi tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡo
amma dutsa dujeɡo ɡʔabe ɡofer aburab tsʼulal ɡama wa ʒanisanɡi qʼwatʼisanɡi ɡʔjelda qχil baχe
ɡʔjeɬul χalaɬijalda bukʼine kːola ɬabnusɡo natʼ ɡʼjebɬijalda kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo wa borχaɬijalda ɬeberɡo natʼ
ɡamil tʼoχɡi ɡʔabe ɡʔjeɬul tsotsada dande batʃarab bakʼaɬul beɡʼjerɬi tso natʼitsa borχaɬuleduqχ χʔibilalda nutsʼaɡi ɡʔabe ɡamida ʒanib bukʼine bitʃːante tʼotsebesebɡi kʼiabilebɡi wa ɬababilebɡi tʼala
ditsajin abuni rakʔ ɬadaɬ tʼjerχʔinabila wa zobalazda ʁorkʔ ruχʼ buɡebʃːinab ʒoɡi tʼaɡʼinabila rakʔalda buɡebʃːinab ʒo χwela
amma durɡun ditsa qʼotʼi ɡʔabila durɡo wasalɡun ɬadiɡun wa wasazul ɬudbiɡun tsadaqχ mun ɡamida ʒaniwe ɬuɡʔina
dutsa tsadaqχ batʃe kinalɡo ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬabazul ʃːibab tajpajaɬul tso biχʔinabɡi tso tsʼujabɡi duda tsadaqχ ɡʔjelɡi tʃʼaɡo χutʼize
ʃːibab χʼintʃʼ ʁedujaɬul ʃːibab χʼajwanaɬul wa rakʔaldasan ʃurulelʃːinal ʒalazul kʼi kʼijab ɬuɡʔinabe dudaɡo tsadaqχ ɡamida ʒanibe ɡʔjel tʃʼaɡo χutʼize
batʼi batʼijab kwanil niɡʼmatalɡi rose tsadaqχ dujeɡi ɡʔjezijeɡi ɡʼoleb qʼadaralda
ɡʔjedin allaɡʔas amru ɡʔabunʃːinab tʼubazabuna nuχʼitsa

betʼjerhanas nuχʼida abuna
durɡo qχizan ɬimalɡi ratʃun ɡamida ʒaniwe ɬuɡʔa dida biχʔuleb buɡo ɡʔab ɡʼjelalda ɡʔorkʔow dida tsewe rakʼbatsʼtsʼadaw tʃi tsoχʼo mun wuɡebɬi
dutsa tsadaqχ ratʃe χʼalalal χʼajwanazul kinalɡo tajpabazdasan ankʔɡo biχʔinabɡi ankʔɡo tsʼujabɡi kwanije χʼaramal χʼajwanazul kinalɡo tajpabazdasan tso biχʔinabɡi tso tsʼujabɡi
wa zobalazul χʼantʃʼazdasanɡi ankʔɡo biχʔinabɡi ankʔɡo tsʼujabɡi ɡʔjezul tajpabi rakʔalda tʃʼaɡo χutʼize rukʼine
ankʔɡo qʼojaldasan ditsa rakʔalde tsʼad bazabila kʼiqʼoɡo sordo qʼojaɬ ɡʔorkʔob qʼotʼitʃʼoɡo baze buɡo ɡʔjeb tsʼad wa ditsaɡo rakʔalda biʒarab χʼuχʔjel tsʼalebʃːinab ʒo ditsa dunjalaldasa tʼaɡʼinabize buɡo
ɡʔjedin betʼjerhanas amru ɡʔabunʃːinab tʼubazabuna nuχʼitsa
rakʔalde tʼupan tʼjeze bajbiχʔarab meχaɬ nuχʼitsa anɬnusɡo son ban bukʼana
ʒindirɡo wasalɡun ɬadiɡun wa wasazul ɬudbiɡun tsadaqχ ɡamide waχana ɡʔjew tʼupanaldasa χwasarɬize
ratsʼtsʼadalɡi qχubalɡi χʼajwanazul ɡʔjedinɡo χʼantʃʼazul wa rakʔalda bukʼarabʃːinab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijaɬul
biχʔinabɡi tsʼujabɡi kʼi kʼi reqʼon batʃʼana nuχʼiqχe wa ɡʔjel kinalɡo ɡamida ʒanire ɬuɡʔana allaɡʔas amru ɡʔabun bukʼarab kutsaɬ
ankʔɡo qʼo ana wa rakʔalde tʼupan tʼjeze ɬuɡʔana
nuχʼil ɡʼumrujaɬul anɬnusabileb sonaɬ ɬaɡʼalil kʼiabileb motsʼaɬ ɡʔjeb motsʼrol antsʼila ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ kʼudijab ʁwariɬijaɬul itsːal qʼwatʼire kʼantsʼana zobalazul ɡordal raɡʔana
wa kʼiqʼoɡo sordo qʼojaɬ rakʔalde tʼupan tʼuna
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ nuχʼɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi ʃemɡi χamɡi jafetɡi nuχʼil ɬadiɡi ɬabawɡo wasasul ɬudbiɡi ɡamide raχana
ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ ɡʔjenire raχana ʒanawarazul wa ɡʼi botsʼul ʃːibab tajpa rakʔaldasan ʃurulel ʒalazul ʃːibab tajpa kinalɡo χʼantʃʼazul wa rorʒunelʃːinal ʒalazul ʃːibab tajpa
nuχʼide allaɡʔas amru ɡʔabun bukʼarab kutsaɬ ɡʔjel kinalɡo ɡʔjesda askʼore ɡamida ʒanire ratʃʼana kʼi kʼikːun χʼuχʔjel tsʼalebʃːinaɬul biχʔinabɡi tsʼujabɡi
tsinɡi allaɡʔas nuχʼida χadub ɡamil nutsʼa qʼana
kʼiqʼoɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔorkʔosa qʼotʼitʃʼoɡo rakʔalde ɬim tʃwaχana ɬim tʼade baχindal ɬadatsa ɡama kodobe bosana
ɬim eχede baχunebɡo baχuneb wa rakʔ ɬadaɬe tʼjerχʔuneb bukʼana ɡamaɡi ɬedon uneb bukʼana
ɡʔjedin ɬim eχede baχana zobalazda ʁorkʔ ruɡel biʃːunɡo rorχatal muɡʼrul ʁorɬe tʼjerχʔineɡʼan
ɡʔjezdasaɡi antsʼila ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ eχede baχana ɬim muɡʼrulɡi ɬadaɬe tʼjerχʔana
ɡʔjebmeχalda rakʔalda bukʼarabʃːinab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi χwana χʼantʃʼiɡi χʼajwanalɡi rakʔaldasan ʃurulel ʒalɡi wa kinalɡo ɡʼadamalɡi χwana
maɡʼarzuqχan χʼuχʔjel tsʼalebʃːinab raqʼdalɬijaɬul aɡʔlu χwana
rakʔalda rukʼaralʃːinal kinalɡo ɡʼadamalɡi χʼajwanalɡi tsoɡidal ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬabiɡi kina ʃːinalɡo rakʔaldasa tʼaɡʼinaruna tʃʼaɡo χutʼana ɡʼitsʼɡo nuχʼɡi ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ ɡamida rukʼaralɡi
nusijalda kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo qʼojaɬ rakʔ ɬadaɬ ʁanqʼun bukʼana

amma allaɡʔasda kʼotʃon tetʃʼo nuχʼɡi wa nuχʼida tsadaqχ ɡamida rukʼaral ruqʼaɬul χʼajwanalɡi ɡʼalχul ʒanawaralɡi allaɡʔas rakʔalde ɡʔuri bitʼana wa ɬim naqχe qʼaze bajbiχʔana
kʼudijab ʁwariɬijaɬul itsːalɡi qʼotʼana zobalazul ɡordalɡi qʼana tsʼadal tʃwaχiɡi ɬuɡʼana
ɬim daɡʔ daɡʔkːun rakʔaldasa naqχe ine bajbiχʔana nusijalda kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo qʼojaldasan rakʔaldasa ɬim ʒeɡi naqχe uneb bukʼana
wa ankʔabileb motsʼaɬul antsʼila ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ ɡama ararat maɡʼarda tʼad tʃʼana
ɬaɡʼalil antsʼabileb motsʼ ʃːwezeɡʼan ɬim daɡʔ daɡʔkːun naqχe uneb bukʼana wa antsʼabileb motsʼrol tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ muɡʼruzul tʼoɡʔal qʼwatʼire rakːana
ɡʔjeldasa χadubɡi kʼiqʼoɡo qʼo ana ɡamil ɡordoɡi raɡʔun
nuχʼitsa ʁedu qʼwatʼibe bitʃːana tsin un tsinɡi tʼad busːun borʒanqχuleb bukʼana ɡʔjeb rakʔ baqʼwazeɡʼan
tsinɡi mikːiɡi bitʃːana nuχʼitsa rakʔaldasa ɬim ɬuɡʼun buɡiʃːali ɬaze
amma mikːijalda reʃːtʼine baqʼwarab bakʼ batitʃʼo wa tʼolabɡo rakʔ ʒeɡi ɬadaɬ tʼjerχʔun bukʼun ɡʔjeb tʼadbusːun batʃʼana qʼwatʼibe kwerɡi beɡʔun tʼadbusːun ɡamida ʒanibe batʃana nuχʼitsa mikːi
ankʔɡo qʼojaldasan ɡʔjes mikːi naqχeɡi qʼwatʼibe bitʃːana
qʼasijaldeχun tʼadbusːun batʃʼana ɡʔjeb kʼaldib kːun zajtunaɬul ʁotʼol tʼamaχɡun wa nuχʼida bitʃʼtʃʼana rakʔaldasa ɬim ɬuɡʼun bukʼin
ʒeɡi ankʔɡo qʼojaɬɡi tʃʼun naqχeɡi borʒine bitʃːana ɡʔjes mikːi ɡʔjeb tʼokʼaɬ tʼadbusːun batʃʼintʃʼo
nuχʼil ɡʼumrujaɬul anɬnusijalda tsoabileb sonaɬul tʼotsebeseb motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ rakʔaldasa ɬim tʼuban naqχe ana wa nuχʼitsa ɡama raɡʔarab meχaɬ ɡʔjesda biχʔana rakʔ baqʼwaleb bukʼin
kʼiabileb motsʼaɬul ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ rakʔ tʼubanɡo baqʼwarab meχaɬ
allaɡʔas nuχʼida abuna
qχizanɡun wasalɡun wasazul ɬudbiɡun tsadaqχ ɡamidasa qʼwatʼiwe ɬuɡʔa
kinabɡo ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬiɡi qʼwatʼibe batʃe χʼantʃʼiɡi χʼajwanalɡi rakʔaldasan ʃurulel ʒalɡi bitʃːante ɡʔjez rakʔ tsʼjezabize bitʃːante ɡʔjezul tʼintʃʼ qʼed tsʼikʼkʼine wa ʒalɡoɡi ɡʼjemerɬize
tsinɡi wasalɡun ɬadiɡun wa wasazul ɬudbiɡun tsadaqχ nuχʼ ɡamidasa qʼwatʼiwe ɬuɡʔana
ɡʔjezdaɡo χadur ʒanawaral rakʔaldasan ʃurulel ʒal χʼantʃʼi ɡʔjezul kinalɡo tajpabi tsojalda χadur tsojal qʼwatʼire raqχana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nuχʼitsa betʼjerhanase qʼurban bakʼ bana wa kinalɡo χʼalalal χʼajwanazdasanɡi χʼantʃʼazdasanɡi tso tso ʒo tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχuna
qʼurbanaɬe ruχʼaral χʼajwanazul wa χʼantʃʼazul ɡʔuinab maχʼ tʃʼwana betʼjerhanasda wa betʼjerhanas ʒindaɡo abuna
ɡʼadamal sababɬun rakʔaɬe naɡʼana kʔjelaro ditsa tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔitʼinab meχaldasaɡo ɡʔjezul pikrabi kweʃɬijalde rusːaral ruɡoniɡi ɡʔab χʼalaɬ kinabɡo tʃʼaɡojabʃːinab tʼokʼaɬ χwezabilaro ditsa
dunjal buɡebɡʼan zamanalda ɡʔorkʔosa qʼotʼilaro rekʔiɡi ɬiɬiɡi tsʼorojɡi χinɬiɡi riiɡi χaselɡi qʼoɡi sordoɡi

nuχʼidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazdaɡi barakat ɬun allaɡʔas abuna
ɡʼjemeral ɬimal ɡʔare nuʒerɡo qʼadar tsʼikʼkʼinabe wa ɡʔab rakʔ tsʼjezabe
kinalɡo rakʔalda ruɡel ʒanawaralɡi zobalazdasan rorʒanqχulel χʼantʃʼiɡi rakʔaldasan ʃurulel ʒalɡi raɬadazuɬ ruɡel tʃːuɡʼbiɡi nuʒedasa χʼinqʼize ritʃːante ɡʔjel nuʒer iχtijaralde kʔun ruɡo
kinabniɡi ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi nuʒee kwanije kʔoleb buɡo ditsa tsebe nuʒee kwanije rakʔul niɡʼmat kʔun bukʼarab ɡʼadin ɡʔjeb kinabɡoɡi kʔoleb buɡo nuʒee kwanaze
amma ʒeɡi ʒindiɬ ruχʼ buɡeb aj ʒindiɬ bi buɡeb
nuʒer ɡʼodobe tʼurab biduqχ aj nuʒer ruχʼal raqχaraɬuqχ insan tʃʼwarab ʒanawar bukʼaniɡi jaɡi tsoɡidaw tʃi tʃʼwaraw insan wukʼaniɡi ɡʼajibijal ditsa ʒawabalde tsʼala
ɬitsaniɡi pulanaw tʃijasul bi ɡʼodobe tʼuni tsoɡidas ɡʔjew bidulasul biɡi ɡʼodobe tʼjela insan wiʒun wuɡeɬulχa allaɡʔasul suratalda
nuʒetsa ɡʼjemeral ɬimal ɡʔare nuʒerɡo qʼadar tsʼikʼkʼinabe wa ɡʔab rakʔ tsʼjezabe
χadub allaɡʔas nuχʼidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazdaɡi abuna
ditsa nuʒerɡun wa nuʒer naslujaɬulɡun qʼotʼi ɡʔabuleb buɡo
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡamidasa qʼwatʼibe ɬuɡʔanʃːinab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijaɬulɡun χʼantʃʼazulɡun χʼajwanazulɡun wa ʒanawarazulɡun aj dunjalaɬul kinabɡo ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijaɬulɡun
nuʒerɡun ditsa ɡʔadinab qʼotʼi ɡʔabuleb buɡo
ɡʔanʒejaldasa χadub tʼupanaɬul ɬadaɬ ʁanqʼun tʼolabɡo tʃʼaɡojabʃːinab χweze ɡʔjetʃʼo tʼokʼaɬ kidaniɡi tʼupanaɬ dunjal χwezabize ɡʔjetʃʼo
allaɡʔas abuna
ditsa nuʒerɡun wa kinabɡo tʃʼaɡojabʃːinaɬulɡun ɡʔabuleb buɡeb naslabazuqχa naslabazuqχe kʔoleb abadijab qʼotʼijaɬul ɡʼalamat ɡʔale
ditsa nakʼkʼazda ɡʔorkʔob nur
ditsa zodir nakʼkʼal dande rakʼararab meχaɬ ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔob nur tʃʼjeze buɡo
ɡʔjeldaɬun dida rakʼalda bukʼina nuʒerɡunɡi tʃʼaɡojabʃːinaɬulɡunɡi ɡʔaburab dirɡo qʼotʼi tʼolabɡo tʃʼaɡojabʃːinab χwezabuleb tʼupanɡi tʼokʼaɬ bukʼinaro
nakʼkʼazda ɡʔorkʔob nur ɬuɡʔina wa ɡʔjeb biχʔarabɡo dida rakʼalde ʃːwela dunjalalda kinabɡo tʃʼaɡojabʃːinaɬulɡun ɡʔaburab dirɡo abadijab qʼotʼi
allaɡʔas nuχʼida abuna
ɡʔjeb buɡo dunjalalda buɡeb tʼolabɡo tʃʼaɡojabʃːinaɬulɡun ditsa ɡʔaburab qʼotʼijaɬul ɡʼalamat
ɡʔale ɡamidasa qʼwatʼire ɬuɡʔaral nuχʼil wasal ʃem χam wa jafet χam wuɡo χanaanil emen
ɡʔjel ɬabalɡo rukʼana nuχʼil wasal wa ɡʔjezdasan ɬuɡʔana dunjalaɬul kinalɡo χalqʼal
nuχʼitsa rakʔ χʼaltʼizabize bajbiχʔana wa tsʼolbol aχ tʃʼana
tso qʼojaɬ tsʼolbol tʃaʁirɡi ɡʔjeqʼon meχtana nuχʼ wa tʼad retʼjelɡi ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo tʃadiraɬuw weɡun wukʼana
ɡʔjedin ɡʼitsʼɡo wuɡew emen wiχʔana χamida χanaanil insuda wa tʃadiraɬusa qʼwatʼiweɡi watʃʼun ɡʔjeb watsazda bitsana
ɡʔjebmeχalda ʃemitsaɡi jafetitsaɡi partal muʁalde reχana wa naqχasa naqχe un insul tʃadiralda ʒanire ɬuɡʔana tʼade partalɡi reχun baχtʃana ɡʔjez insul ɡʼitsʼab tʃerχ ɡʔjel insul raqχalde ralaɡʔitʃʼo ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjezda insul ɡʼitsʼɬiɡi biχʔitʃʼo
nuχʼ meχtalidasaɡi makʔidasaɡi wiɡʔarawɡo ʒindirɡo ɡʔitʼinaw wasas ɡʔaburab ʒoɡi ɬan
ɡʔjes abuna
χanaanije naɡʼana bataɡi
ʒindirɡo watsazul biʃːun ɡʼodoweɡʼanaw laʁɬun wukʼina ɡʔjew
tsoɡi ɡʔjes abuna
ʃemitsa ɡʼibadat ɡʔabulew betʼjerhan allaɡʔase retsː
χanaanin abuni ɡʔjesul laʁɬun wukʼina
bitʃːante allaɡʔas tsʼikʼkʼinabize jafetil mal mulk
jafet wukʼine witʃːante ʃemil tʃadrazuqχ
χanaanin abuni ɡʔjesul laʁɬun wukʼina
tʼupanaldasa χadubɡi nuχʼitsa bana ʒeɡi ɬabnusijalda kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo son
kinabniɡi itʃʼnusijalda kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo sonɡi ban nuχʼ χwana

ɡʔale nuχʼil wasal ʃemil χamil jafetil wa ɡʔjezdasan ɬuɡʔaral naslabazul qʼisa
tʼupanaldasa χadub ʃemijeɡi χamijeɡi jafetijeɡi ɬimal ɡʔaruna
jafetil wasal ɡomer maɡoɡ madaj jawan tuwal meʃeχ wa tiras
ɡomeril wasal aʃkenaz rifat wa toɡarma
jawanil wasal eliʃa tarʃiʃ kittim wa dodanim
ɡʔjel tʃʼana raɬdal raɡʼalda ruɡel rakʔazda
ɡʔjedinal rukʼana ɡʔjezul rakʔalɡi qʼawmalɡi tuχumalɡi wa ɡʔjezul kinazulɡo ʒide ʒider matsʼɡi bukʼana
χamil wasal kuʃ misri put wa χanaan
kuʃil wasal sewa χʼawila sawta raɡʼma wa sawteχa
raɡʼmal wasal ʃewa wa dedan
kuʃil wukʼana nimrod aburaw was dunjalaɬul tʼotsewesew ɡutʃ berɡʔaraw baɡʔadur
wa betʼjerhanasdasan ɡʔunar ʃːwaraw biʃːun tsʼaqʼaw tʃanaqχan ɡʔjeldasan batʃʼarab buɡo ɡʔadinab abiɡi betʼjerhanasdasan ɡʔunar ʃːwaraw nimrod ɡʼadaw tsʼaqʼaw tʃanaqχan
tsin ɡʔjesul χanɬijalda ɡʔorkʔobe unaan wawilon ereχ wa akːad ɡʔjel kinalɡo rukʼana ʃinar ulkajalda
ɡʔjeb ulkajaldasa ɡʔjew ana asːirijalde ɡʔjenir ɡʔjes rana ninewija reχowot ir wa kalaχ abural ʃaɡʔaral
ɡʔjedinɡo ninewijaldaɡi kalaχaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob resen ʃaɡʔarɡi ɡʔjeb bukʼana kʼudijab ʃaɡʔar
misridasan ɬuɡʔana ludijal anamijal leɡʔawijal naftuχʼijal patrusijal
kasluχijal ɡʔjezdasan ɬuɡʔana pilistimal wa kaftorijal
χanaanidasan ɬuɡʔana sidon ɡʔjesul tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw was wa χet
ɡʔjedinɡo jewusijal amorijal ɡirɡaʃijal
χiwijal ɡʼarkijal sinijal
arwadijal tsemarijal wa χʼamatijal
zamanaldasan χanaanijazul qʼawmal kisa kireɡo tʼiritʼana
sidonaldasa baqχarab ɡeraraɬul raqχaldeχun ɡazajalde ʃːwezeɡʼan wa sodomaɬul ɡomorrajaɬul admajaɬul wa tsewoimaɬul raqχaldeχun laʃaɡʼalde ʃːwezeɡʼan rakʔal ɡʔjezuqχ rukʼana
ɡʔjel ruɡo χamil naslabi wa ɡʔjesdasan ɬuɡʔaral χalqʼal ʒide ʒider matsʼalɡun wa rakʔalɡun
ʃemilɡi rukʼana ɬimal ɡʔjew kːola jafetil kʼudijaw wats wa jeweril naslujaɬul emen
ʃemil wasal jelam aʃur arpaχʃad lud wa aram
aramil wasal ɡʼuts χʼul ɡeter wa maʃ
arpaχʃadil was wukʼana ʃelaχ ʃelaχil was kːola jewer
jewerije ɡʔawuna kʼiɡo was ɡʔjeb zamanalda rakʔal rikʔun rukʼindal tsojasda tsʼar ɬuna peleɡ
jaktanil wasal rukʼana almodad ʃelef χatsarmawet jaraχʼ
ɡʔadoram uzal dikla
ɡʼowal awimael ʃewa
ofir χʼawila wa jowaw ɡʔjel kinalɡo ruɡo jaktanil wasal
ɡʔjezul rakʔalɡi ruɡo meʃajaldasa baqχarab baqʼbakːudeχun sefarajaɬul muɡʼruzde ʃːwezeɡʼan
ɡʔjel ruɡo ʃemidasan ɬuɡʔaral naslabi wa ɡʔjesdasan ɬuɡʔaral χalqʼal ʒide ʒider matsʼalɡun wa rakʔalɡun
ɡʔjedinal ruɡo nuχʼil wasazul naslabiɡi ɡʔjezdasan ɬuɡʔaral qʼawmalɡi χalqʼalɡi tʼupanaldasa χadub ɡʔjezdasan ɬuɡʔana dunjalaɬul tʼolalɡo χalqʼal

dob zamanajalda tʼolabɡo dunjalalda bukʼana tsoɡo matsʼ tsoɡo luʁat
baqʼbakːul raqχaldasan ɡʼadamal riɬːana ʃinar ulkajaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalde ʃːwezeɡʼan wa ɡʔjenir tʃʼana
ratʃʼa niɬetsa χʼarʃːul kirpitʃal ɡʔarize tsʼaduɬɡi reʒun in abuna ɡʔjez tsotsazda
tsinɡi ɡʔjez bajbiχʔana ɡantʃʼil bakʼalda χʼarʃːul kirpitʃ χʼaltʼizabize χʼarʃːul bakʼaldaɡi qʼadaje qχil χʼaltʼizabize
ratʃʼa niɬetsa zodib tsuleb siɡi buɡeb ʃaɡʔarɡi ban niɬerɡo tsʼar kʼodo ɡʔabize niɬɡo dunjalalda kidaniɡi rikʔa riχːun intʃʼoɡo rukʼine jan abuna ɡʼadamaz
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan ɡʼodowe reʃːtʼana ɡʼadamaz tʼadeɬun baleb buɡeb ʃaɡʔarɡi siɡi biχʔize
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas abuna
ɡʔale tsoɬarab χalqʼɡi kinazulɡo tsoɡo matsʼɡi awalaldaɡo ɡʔadinab iʃ ɡʔabize bajbiχʔun batani ɡʔjezuqχa ɡʔabun baʒarulareb ʒoɡi ʃːibɡo bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo
ratʃʼa ɡʔjezuqχe reʃːtʼun niɬetsa ɡʔjezul matsʼal rikʔizarize ɡʔjel tsotsazda ritʃʼtʃʼulareb χʼalaɬ
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas ɡʔjel tʼolabɡo dunjalalda rikʔa riχːizaruna wa ʃaɡʔar ban ɬuɡʼizabize kʼwetʃʼo ɡʔjezda
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔaralda tsʼarɡi buɡo wawilon
ɡʔale ʃemil wa ɡʔjesdasan ɬuɡʔaral naslabazul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ qʼisa
tʼupanaldasa χadub kʼiɡo ɬaɡʼjel indal ʃemitsa nusɡo son barab meχalda ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was arpaχʃad
arpaχʃad ɡʔawun χadubɡi ʃemitsa bana ʃːunusɡo son wa ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
arpaχʃaditsa ɬeberalda ʃːuɡo son barab meχalda ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was ʃelaχ
ʃelaχ ɡʔawun χadubɡi arpaχʃaditsa bana unqʼnusijalda ɬabɡo son wa ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
ʃelaχitsa ɬeberɡo son barab meχalda ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was jewer
jewer ɡʔawun χadub ʃelaχitsa bana unqʼnusijalda ɬabɡo son wa ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
jeweritsa ɬeberalda unqʼɡo son barab meχalda ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was peleɡ
peleɡ ɡʔawun χadub jeweritsa bana unqʼnusijalda ɬeberɡo son wa ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
peleɡitsa ɬeberɡo son barab meχalda ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was reɡʼu
reɡʼu ɡʔawun χadub peleɡitsa bana kʼinusijalda itʃʼɡo son wa ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
reɡʼutsa ɬeberalda kʼiɡo son barab meχalda ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was seruɡ
seruɡ ɡʔawun χadub reɡʼutsa bana kʼinusijalda ankʔɡo son wa ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
seruɡitsa ɬeberɡo son barab meχalda ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was naχor
naχor ɡʔawun χadub seruɡitsa bana kʼinusɡo son wa ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
naχoritsa qʼolo itʃʼɡo son barab meχalda ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna was teraχʼ
teraχʼ ɡʔawun χadub naχoritsa bana nusijalda antsʼila itʃʼɡo son wa ɡʔjesije ʒeɡi wasal jasalɡi ɡʔaruna
teraχʼitsa ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo son barab meχalda ɡʔjesije ɡʔaruna wasal ibram naχor wa ɡʔaran
ɡʔale teraχʼil wa ɡʔjesdasan ɬuɡʔaral naslabazul qʼisa
teraχʼije ɡʔaruna wasal ibram naχor wa ɡʔaran ɡʔaranil was wukʼana lutʼ
ɡʔaran χwana emen teraχʼ tʃʼaɡo wuɡeb meχaldaɡo ʒindirɡo watʼanalda χaldejazul ur abuleb bakʼalda
ibramitsaɡi naχoritsaɡi ɬudbi ratʃana ibramitsa jatʃana saraj naχoritsa jatʃana milka ɡʔaranil jas ɡʔaran kːola milkalɡi iskalɡi emen
saraj jikʼana ɬimer ɡʔabularej ɡʼadan
χaldejazul urɡi tun χanaanaɬul rakʔaldeχun nuχda waqχana teraχʼ tsadaqχ ʒindirɡo was ibramɡun wasasul was ɡʔarunil was lutʼɡun wa ibramil ɬadi ʒindirɡo nus sarajɡun χarran abuleb bakʼalde ʃːwedal ɡʔjenir tʃʼana ɡʔjel
ɡʔjeniw kʼinusijalda ʃːuɡo sonaɬul ɡʼumrujalde waχarab meχalda teraχʼ χwana

betʼjerhanas ibramida abuna
durɡo ulkaɡi ɡʼaɡarɬiɡi insul ruqʼɡi reχun tun ditsa biχʔizaburab rakʔalde a
ditsa dudasan kʼudijab χalqʼ ɬuɡʔinabila wa dude barakat reʃːtʼinabila ditsa dur tsʼar kʼodo ɡʔabila wa mun barakatawɬun ɡʔawila
duje barakat ɡʔarulezda ditsaɡi barakat ɬela
duje naɡʼana kʔuraze ditsaɡi naɡʼana kʔjela
dudasan barakat ʃːweze buɡo dunjalaɬul kinalɡo χalqʼaze
betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ibram saparaɬ waqχana lutʼɡi ana ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ χarranaldasa qʼwatʼiwe waqχarab meχalda ibramitsa ban bukʼana ɬabqʼojalda antsʼila ʃːuɡo son
ɡʔjes tsadaqχ ratʃana ʒindirɡo ɬadi sarajɡi watsasul was lutʼɡi ʒindirɡo botsʼi panzɡi χarranalda ritʃun rosaral laʁzalɡi wa ɡʔjelɡun tsadaqχ ibramitsa χanaanalde sapar buχʔana
aχirɡi ɡʔjel ʃːwana χanaanalde
ʃeχem ʃaɡʔaralda askʼob buɡeb more abuleb mikːil ʁotʼoqχe dob zamanalda ɡʔjeb rakʔalda ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bukʼana χanaanijaz
ɡʔjeniw betʼjerhan zaɡʔirɬana ibramije wa ɡʔjes abuna
ɡʔab rakʔ ditsa dur naslabaze kʔjeze buɡo jan
ʒindije zaɡʔirɬaraw betʼjerhanase ibramitsa ɡʔjenib qʼurban bakʼ bana
ɡʔjeldasa χaduw ɡʔjew ana bet el ʃaɡʔaraɬul baqʼbakːuda ruɡel muɡʼruzde wa ɡʔjenib tʃʼjel ɡʔabuna ɡʔjesdasa baqʼtʼjerχʔudeχun bukʼana bet el baqʼbakːudeχun ɡaj ibramitsa ɡʔjenib tsoɡi qʼurban bakʼ bana wa betʼjerhanase ɡʼibadat ɡʔabuna
ɡʔjenisaɡi ana ibram bakʼ bakʼalda tʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabulaɡo neɡewaldeχun walaɡʔun
kweʃab raqʼi tʼibitʼana ɡʔjeb rakʔalda tsʼaqʼ kutakab raqʼi bukʼana ɡʔjeb ɡʔjedinɬidal ibramitsa misrijalde sapar buχʔana
misrijalde ɡʼaɡarɬarab meχalda ɡʔjes sarajida abuna
dida ɬala mun tsʼaqʼ bertsinaj ɡʼadan jiɡebɬi
misrijazda mun jiχʔila wa dir ɬadi jikʼin bitʃʼtʃʼila tsinɡi ɡʔjez mun tʃʼaɡo tela dun tʃʼwala
dutsa ɡʔjezda abe mun dir jats jiɡilan ɡʔjebmeχalda mun sababɬun ɡʔjel dideχun ɬikʼ rukʼina wa dun tʃʼaɡo tela
ibram misrijalde ʃːwana wa misrijazda biχʔana sarajil bertsinɬi
pirɡʼawnasul raɡʔtʼatelazdaɡi jiχʔana ɡʔjej wa ɡʔjez pirɡʼawnase betsːana ɡʔjeɬul bertsinɬiɡi ɡʔajbatɬiɡi wa saraj pirɡʼawnasuqχe kʼalɡʼajalde jatʃun ana
ɡʔjedin sarajije ɡʼolo ibramil iʃ ɬikʼ bukʼana ɡʔjesije ʃːwana ɡʼi botsʼiɡi χʼamulɡi laʁzalɡi ʁarawaʃalɡi waranabiɡi
amma betʼjerhanas pirɡʼawnasdeɡi ɡʔjesul tʃaɡʼazdeɡi kweʃal untabi reʃːtʼinaruna ibramil ɬadi ɡʔjes ʒindiqχeɡo jatʃaraɬuqχ
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ pirɡʼawnas ibram tʼade aχʼana wa ɡʔjesda abuna
dutsa dije ɡʔaburab ʃːib
ɡʔaj dur ɬadi jikʼin ʃːaj baɬɡo ɡʔaburab ɡʔaj jats jiɡilan ʃːaj aburab ɡʔjedin abidal ɡuriʃː ditsa ɡʔaj dijeɡo ɬadiɬun jikʼine jatʃaraj
ɡʔale dur ɬadi jatʃe ɡʔjejɡi naqχe a jan abuna pirɡʼawnas
tsinɡi pirɡʼawnas ʒindirɡo tʃaɡʼazde amru ɡʔabuna tsadaqχ ɬadiɡun ɡʼi botsʼiɡun wa kinabɡo betʃeɬiɡun ibram ɡʔjenisa naqχe witʼjejilan

misrijaldasa tʼadɡi wusːun naqχeɡi neɡewalde ɡotʃana ibram ʒindirɡo ɬadiɡun wa kinabɡo botsʼi betʃeɬiɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ wukʼana lutʼɡi
ibram tsʼaqʼ betʃeɬana ɡʼjemerab botsʼiɡi ɡʼarats mesedɡi bukʼana ɡʔjesul
neɡewaldasaɡi un ɡʔjew ɡotʃana bet elalde bet elaldaɡi ɡajaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ʒintsaɡo tsebe tʃʼjel ɡʔabun bukʼarab wa
tʼotsewe ɡʔjeniwe ʃːwarab meχaɬɡo qʼurban bakʼ ban bukʼarab bakʼalde ɡʔjenib betʼjerhanase ɡʼibadat ɡʔabuna ibramitsa
ibramida tsadaqχ ɡotʃarulew wuɡew lutʼilɡi bukʼana ɡʼi botsʼiɡi ʒindirɡo tʃadralɡi
ɡʔanʒe kʼijazeɡo ɡʔjeb rakʔ ɡʼoleb bukʼintʃʼo botsʼi betʃeɬi ɡʼjemerɬun tsadaqχ tʃʼjeze bakʼ qʼwariɬana ɡʔjezije
wa ibramilɡi lutʼilɡi ɡʼuχʔbuzul daɡʼba raɡʼi kːoleb bukʼana dob zamanalda ɡʔjeb rakʔalda ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bukʼana χanaanijazɡi perizijazɡi
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ibramitsa lutʼida abuna
niɬ ɡʼaɡaral tʃaɡʼi ruɡeɬul ja niɬeda ɡʔorkʔob jaɡi durɡi dirɡi ɡʼuχʔbuzda ɡʔorkʔob kʔal bukʼine beɡʔularo
ɡʔale kinabɡo rakʔ duda tsebe buɡo ratʃʼa niɬ ratʼaɬize mun kweɡʼisa ani dun kwaranisa ina mun kwaranisa ani dun kweɡʼisa ina
lutʼ sweruqχe walaɡʔana wa ɡʔjesda biχʔana iordanaɬul rasaɬi betʼjerɡʔanasul aχ ɡʼadab bakʼ bukʼana ɡʔjeb tsoɡʼar ʃaɡʔaralde ɡʼuntʼun ɬaɬaze ɬimɡi ɡʔarzajab misrijaɬul ɡʼadab beenab rakʔɡi buɡeb betʼjerɡʔanas sodomɡi ɡomorraɡi tʼaɡʼinabilalde tsebe zaman bukʼana ɡʔjeb
tsinɡi lutʼitsa iordanaɬul rasaɬi tʼasa biʃːana wa baqʼbakːudeχun walaɡʔun ana ɡʔjedin rikʔana ɡʔjezul nuχal
ibram χanaanalda tʃʼana lutʼ rasaɬijaɬul ʃaɡʔarazda tʃʼana lutʼitsa ʒindirɡo tʃadral tʃʼwana sodomalde ʃːwezeɡʼan
sodomaɬul alqʼin abuni tsʼaqʼ kweʃɬun bukʼana betʼjerhanase riχarabʃːinab ɡʔabuleb bukʼana ɡʔjez
lutʼ naqχe arab meχaɬ betʼjerhanas ibramida abuna
dutsa kisa kibeɡo sweruqχɬijalde ber ʃːwezabe mun walaɡʔje ʃimalaɬulɡi qʼilbajaɬulɡi raqχalde walaɡʔje baqʼbakːulɡi baqʼtʼjerχʔulɡi raqχalde
ɡʔjeb tʼolabɡo duda biχʔulebʃːinab rakʔ ditsa abadijaɬeɡo dujeɡi dur naslabazeɡi kʔoleb buɡo
rakʔul χʼurɡʼanɡi ɡʼjemerɬizarila ditsa dur naslabi χʼurul qʼatʼrabi rikʼkʼine baʒaruleb batani dur naslujaɬul ɡʼadamalɡi rikʼkʼine baʒarila
ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬuqχ walaɡʔize a ɡʔjeɬul ɡʼjebɬuqχeɡi χalaɬuqχeɡi ʃːwa duje kʔoleb buɡeɬul ditsa ɡʔjeb
ibram ɡʔjenisan ana χewronalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχe mamrel mikːil ʁutʼbi ruɡeb bakʼalde ʃːwezeɡʼan wa ɡʔjeniw tʃʼana ibramitsa ɡʔjenibɡi betʼjerhanase qʼurban bakʼ bana

dob zamanalda ʃinaraɬul χan amrafelɡi ellasaraɬul χan arioχɡi jelamaɬul χan kedorlaomerɡi ɡojimaɬul χan tidɡʼalɡi
raʁulel rukʼana sodomaɬul χan beraɡʼidaɡi ɡomorrajaɬul χan birʃaɡʼidaɡi admajaɬul χan ʃinawidaɡi tsewoimaɬul χan ʃemeweridaɡi belaɡʼaɬul aj tsoɡʼaraɬul χanasdaɡi dande
ɡʔjezul kinalɡo bojal dande rakʼarun rukʼana siddimaɬul rasaɬijalda ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjenib tsʼamɡʼalab raɬad buɡo
antsʼila kʼiɡo sonaɬ kedorlaomeril laʁɬijalda ʁorkʔ rukʼana ɡʔjel amma antsʼila ɬababileb sonaɬ ɡʔjez dandetʃʼjej ɡʔabize bajbiχʔana
antsʼila unqʼabileb sonaɬin abuni ʒindir raqχ kːural χanzabiɡun tsadaqχ kedorlaomeritsa ʁurana aʃterot karnajimalda refaimal
wa muɡʼruzul ulka seiralda tʃʼaral χorijalɡi ʁurana ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχaɬul raɡʼalda buɡeb elʔ paranalde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjezda χadurɡi ɬuɡʔun
ɡʔjenisa ɡʔjel swerana en miʃpatalde ɡʔjebɡo kadeʃ wa χatsetson tamaralda tʃʼaral amalekijazulɡi amorijazulɡi kinalɡo rakʔal raqχana
ɡʔjezda dande raqχana sodomaɬul ɡomorrajaɬul admajaɬul tsewoimaɬul wa belaɡʼaɬul aj tsoɡʼaraɬul χanzabi siddimaɬul rasaɬijalda ɡʔjez raʁ ɡʔabuna
jelamaɬul χan kedorlaomeridaɡi ɡojimaɬul χan tidɡʼalidaɡi ʃinaraɬul χan amrafelidaɡi ellasaraɬul χan arioχidaɡi dande unqʼɡo χan waʁulew wukʼana ʃːuɡojasda dande
siddimaɬul rasaɬijalda rukʼana tʼabiɡʼijab pitsʼil tsʼural ɡʼjemeral ɡwendal sodomaɬul wa ɡomorrajaɬul χanzabi ɬutize ɬuɡʔana ɬutun unel rukʼaral ɡʔjezul ɡʼjemerisel raʁuqχabi pitsʼil ɡwendazuqχe rortana wa ɡʔjenir qʼan χutʼana χutʼaral muɡʼruzde ɬutun ana
tuʃbabi abuni sodomaɬul wa ɡomorrajaɬul tʼolabɡo betʃeɬiɡun χazina naqχratelɡi qχamal ɡʔabun ɡʔjenisa naqχe ana
ɡʔjez tsadaqχ watʃun ana sodomalda jaʃaw ɡʔabun wukʼaraw ibramil watsasul was lutʼɡi wa ɡʔjesul kinabɡo botsʼi betʃeɬiɡi qχamal ɡʔabuna
ɬutun χwasarɬarazdasan tso tʃi watʃʼana ʒuɡʔutʼaw ibramiqχe wa ɡʔjesda kinabɡo bitsana mamre abulew amorijasul mikːil ʁutʼbuzda askʼob tʃʼjel ɡʔabun bukʼana ɡʔjeb zamanalda ibramitsa mamrelɡun wa ɡʔjesul watsal eʃkolilɡun wa ɡʼanerilɡun ibramil bukʼana qʼotʼi qʼajaɬulab buχʔjen
watsasul was asirɬun watʃun un wukʼin ɬajdal ibramitsa dande rakʼarana ʒindirɡo ɡʼadamal ɡʔawurab qʼojaldasaɡo ɡʔjesul mulkɬijalda wukʼaraw ɬabnusijalda antsʼila mikʔɡo raʁde waqχine jaraɡʔunew tʃi wa tuʃbabazda χaduw ɬuɡʔana danalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ
sardiɬ ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo tʃaɡʼi qʼoqʼabi ɡʔarun rikʔana tsinɡi ɡʔjel tuʃbabazde tʼade kʼantsʼana wa tuʃbabi ɬutizaruna damaskaldasa ʃimalaldeχun buɡeb χowajalde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɬutizaruna ɡʔjel
ɡʔjes tuʃbabazuqχa kinabɡo naqχe baqχana ɡʔjedinɡo lutʼɡi ɡʔjesul botsʼi betʃeɬiɡi rutʃːabiɡi wa tsoɡidal kinalɡo asiralɡi naqχe ratʃana
kedorlaomerida wa ɡʔjesul raqχ kːural χanzabazda tʼad berɡʔjenɬiɡi bosun ibram naqχwusːun watʃʼuneb zamanalda ʃawe rasaɬijalde aj χanasul rasaɬijalde ɡʔjesda dandtʃʼwaze watʃʼana sodomaɬul χan
salimaɬul χan melkitsedek watʃʼana ibramida dande tʃedɡi tʃaʁirɡi bosun tʼadeɡʼanaw allaɡʔase
wa ɡʔjes ibramije duɡʼa ɡʔabun abuna
zobɡi rakʔɡi biʒaraw tʼadeɡʼanaw allaɡʔasul barakat reʃːtʼaɡi ibramide
dur tuʃbabi dur kwerde kʔuraw tʼadeɡʼanaw allaɡʔase retsː
ibramitsa melkitsedekije kʔuna tʼolabɡo dawlajaɬul antsʼil butʼa
sodomaɬul χanas ibramida abuna
dir ɡʼadamal naqχe kʔje dawla dujeɡo te jan
ibramitsa ʒawab kʔuna
zobɡi rakʔɡi biʒaraw betʼjerhanasda tʼadeɡʼanaw allaɡʔasda tsere kweral kːun ɡʔjedulew wuɡo dun
dur betʃeɬijaldasan tso kun kwarɡitsin jaɡi χʔital ruχʔuneb tʃʼoloɡitsin ditsa dijeɡo bosilarilan ditsa betʃeɬizawunin ibramilan tso qʼojaɬ dutsa abitʃʼoɡo bukʼine
dije ʃːibniɡi χʼaʒat ɡʔjetʃʼo dir ɡʼadamaz kwanarab ʒo χutʼizeɡʼan dida tsadaqχ raʁaral ɡʼaneritsaɡi eʃkolitsaɡi mamretsaɡi bosejan abe ʒiderɡo butʼa

ɡʔjeldasa χadub ilɡʔam
mun χʼinqʼuɡe ibram
dun duje qχalqχanɬun wukʼina
duje ʃːweze buɡeb ʃapaqʼat tsʼaqʼ kʼudijab buɡo
ibramitsa abuna
ja dir χʼalkʼolew betʼjerhan ʃːib dutsa dije kʔjeleb ɬimerɡo ɡʔjetʃʼjew tʃijase dir irsilawɬunɡi ɡʔaw damaskaldasa elijezer wukʼina
ibramitsa ʒeɡi abuna
dutsa dije naslu kʔjetʃʼjeɬulχa dir qʼawuɬ ɡʔawuraw laʁ wukʼina dir irsilawɬun abun
amma betʼjerhanasdasan ɡʔadinab kalima reʃːtʼana ibramije
ɡʔjew wukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo dur irsilawɬun
durɡo χʔonaldasan ɬuɡʔina duje irsilaw
qʼwatʼiweɡi watʃun ɡʔjes ibramida abuna
zodiqχe walaɡʔje wa dol tsʼwabi rikʼkʼje ɡʔjel rikʼkʼine duqχa baʒaruleb batani
tsinɡi betʼjerɡʔanas abuna
ɡʔjediɡʼanɡi ɡʼjemer rukʼina dur naslabi jan
ibram betʼjerhanasda boʒana wa ɡʔjeldaɬun betʼjerɡʔanasda biχʔana ɡʔjew ʒindije ritʼuqχaw tʃi wukʼin
ibramida betʼjerhanas abuna
dun wuɡo ɡʔab rakʔ dur mulkɬun duje kʔjeze χaldejazul uraldasa mun ɡʔaniwe watʃaraw betʼjerhan
ja dir χʼalkʼolew allaɡʔ in abuna ibramitsa ɡʔab rakʔ χʼaqʼɬunɡo dir bukʼinalda sundaɬun dun boʒilew
betʼjerɡʔanas abuna
ɡʔanire dida tsere ratʃe ɬabɡo son barab ɡʼakaɡi ɬabɡo son barab tsʼtsʼjeɡi ɬabɡo son barab ɬabɡo kujɡi ɡʔjedinɡo roχʔil mikːiɡi mikːidul tʼintʃʼɡi
ibramitsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna ɡʔjes χʼajwanal kʼiχʼi qʼotʼana wa tsojab rakʔqχen tsoɡidalda dandbitʼun ɬuna
kwatʼitʃʼoɡo tʃudkal rorʒun ratʃʼana amma ibramitsa askʼore qʼaze ritʃːalel rukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjel
baqʼ tʼjerχʔuneb ɡʼuʒalda ibramide tsʼaqʼ bakʼab makʔu reʃːtʼana wa ɡʔale tsindaɡo kutakalda χʼinqʼarab betsʼɬukʔje kːana ibram
wa betʼjerɡʔanas ɡʔjesda abuna
duda ɬan bukʼa unqʼnusɡo sonaɬ dur naslabaz tʃijar rakʔalda laʁɬijaldaɡi zulmujaldaɡi ʁorkʔ jaʃaw ɡʔabize buɡo
amma ɡʔjel laʁɬijalde kːezaburab χalqʼaɬe ditsa diwan qʼotʼila ɡʔjebmeχaɬ dur naslabiɡi ɡʔjenisa naqχe ina ɡʼjemerab betʃeɬiɡun
munin abuni paraχatɡo ina durɡo umumuzda askʼowe
ɡʼjemeral sonalɡi ran χerɬijalde waχindal ina χabaɬe
dudasan ɬuɡʔaral naslabazul unqʼabileb kʔjer
baqʼɡi tʼjerχʔun dunjal betsʼɬarabɡo tsindaɡo bakːun batʃʼana kʼkʼujdutsa batsarab borkʔarab qʼonoɡi ɡʔjeleɡʔarab tsʼaduɬ bosarab sunturɡi wa kʼiχʼi qʼotʼaral χʼajwanazul rakʔqχenazda ɡʔorkʔosan ana
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanas ibramilɡun qʼotʼi ɡʔabuna
dur naslabaze kʔoleb buɡo ditsa ɡʔab rakʔ misrijaɬul ɬaraqχa
kenijazul kenizijazul kadmonijazul
χitijazul perizijazul refaimazul
amorijazul χanaanijazul ɡirɡaʃijazul wa jewusijazul tʼolalɡo rakʔal

ibramil ɬadi sarajije ɬimer ɡʔabuleb bukʼintʃʼo ɡʔaʒarilan tsʼar buɡej misrijaldasa ʁarawaʃ jikʼana ɡʔjeɬul
sarajitsa ibramida abuna
betʼjerhanas dije ɬimer kʔoleb ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔaj dir ʁarawaʃ jatʃe ɡʔjeldasaɡʼaɡi dije was ʃːweze beɡʔula
ibram sarajiqχ ɡʼjenekːana
ɡʔjeɬ ʒindirɡo ʁarawaʃ kʔuna ibramije misrijaldasa ɡʔaʒar ibram χanaanalda tʃʼun antsʼɡo son arab zaman bukʼana ɡʔjeb
ibram ɡʔaʒarida askʼow weɡana wa ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana ʒijɡo ɬimade jikʼin ɬajdal χwaʒain χʼaqʼir ɡʔajize ɬuɡʔana ɡʔaʒar
dun χʼaqʼir ɡʔajijaɬe ɡʼajibijaw mun wuɡo jan abuna sarajitsa ibramida ditsa dirɡo ʁarawaʃ duda askʼoj jeɡize kʔuna ɡʔanʒe ɬimer urɡʔibe kːedal ɡʔjeɬ dun rikʼkʼunej ɡʔjetʃʼo bitʃːante betʼjerhanas χʼukmu qʼotʼize dudaɡi didaɡi ɡʔorkʔob
wa ibramitsa abuna
ɡʔjej dur ʁarawaʃ jiɡo dujeɡo bokʔarab ɡʔabe ɡʔjelda
tsinɡi sarajitsa ɡʔaʒarije ɡʼumru qʼwarid ɡʔabuna aχirɡi ɡʔjelda askʼosa ɬutun ine kːana ɡʔaʒar
ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχalda ʃuralde uneb nuχda tso itsːuqχ betʼjerhanasul malaikasda jatana ɡʔaʒar
ɡʔjes ɡʔiqʼana
ja sarajil ʁarawaʃ ɡʔaʒar mun kisa jatʃʼunej jiɡej wa kije unej jiɡej abun
ɡʔjeɬ ʒawab kʔuna
dirɡo χwaʒain sarajida askʼosa ɬutun unej jiɡo dun in
betʼjerhanasul malaikas abuna
durɡo χwaʒainalda askʼoje tʼadjusːa wa ɡʔjeɬije mutʼiɡʼɬe
betʼjerhanasul malaikas ʒeɡi abuna
ditsa dur naslujaɬul ɡʼadamal rikʼkʼun χʼal kʼolareb χʼalaɬ ɡʼjemerɬizarila
dur urɡʔib ɬimer buɡo jan abuna betʼjerhanasul malaikas duje was ɡʔawila ismaɡʼil ɬe dutsa ɡʔjesda tsʼar dur qʼwariɬi betʼjerhanasda raɡʼun buɡeɬul
ɡʼalχul χʼama ɡʼadaw was wukʼina dur
kinalɡoɡun kʔalda wukʼina ɡʔjew kinalɡo ɡʔjewɡunɡi kʔalda rukʼina
watsazulɡun kʔalda ina ɡʔjesul ɡʼumru
ʒindeχun kʼaɬaraw betʼjerhanasda ɡʔaʒaritsa ɬuna elʔ roi
ɡʔjedinɬidal dob ʁujalda tsʼar buɡo beer laχaj roi
ɡʔaʒaritsa ibramije was ɡʔawuna wa ɡʔjew wasasda tsʼar ismaɡʼil ɬuna ibramitsa
ɡʔjeb zamanalda ibramitsa ban bukʼana unqʼojalda anɬɡo son

ibramitsa unqʼojalda antsʼila itʃʼɡo son barab meχalda ilɡʔam ɡʔabun betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesda abuna
dun wuɡo χʼalkʼolew allaɡʔ
ditsa qʼotʼi ɡʔabila didaɡi dudaɡi ɡʔorkʔob wa rikʼkʼun χʼalkʼolarelɡʼan ɡʼjemeral naslabi kʔjela duje
ibram allaɡʔasda tsewe kʼalaʁorkʔje kːana wa allaɡʔas ʒeɡi abuna
ɡʔale ditsa durɡun qʼotʼi ɡʔabuleb buɡo mun wukʼina ɡʼjemeral χalqʼazul emenɬun
duda tsʼarɡi ibram bukʼinaro ibraɡʔim
kutakalda ɡʼjemerɬizabila ditsa dur naslu dudasan χalqʼal ɬuɡʔina dur naslujaldasan χanzabi raqχina
ditsa didaɡi dudaɡi wa dur rukʼinesel naslabazdaɡi ɡʔorkʔob qʼotʼi ɡʔabila naslabaz naslabazuqχe kʔoleb abadijab qʼotʼi bukʼina ɡʔjeb dun wuɡo allaɡʔ durɡi dur naslabazulɡi allaɡʔ
ditsa duje wa dur naslabaze kʔjeze buɡo duje ɡʔabsaɡʼat tʃijarabɬun kːoleb ɡʔab rakʔ χanaanaɬul tʼolabɡo rakʔ abadijab mulkɬun kʔjeze buɡo ditsa dur naslabaze wa ɡʔjel dir χalqʼɬun rukʼine ruɡo
allaɡʔas ibraɡʔimida abuna
amma dutsaɡi dir qʼotʼi tʼubazabe dutsaɡi dur naslabazul ʃːibab kʔjeraɬɡi tʼubazabize kːola ɡʔjeb
ɡʔab didaɡi dudaɡi wa dur naslabazdaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔaburab qʼotʼi tʼubazabizeɬun nuʒer kinalɡo biχʔinaze sunnat ɡʔabize kːola
sunnat ɡʔabun ɡʼawrataɬul raɡʼal qʼotʼje ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo didaɡi nuʒedaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔaburab qʼotʼijaɬul ɡʼalamatɬun
nuʒer ʃːiwaw wasase ɡʔawun mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ sunnat ɡʔabize tʼadab buɡo ɡʔjedin ɡʔabe kinalɡo ratʃʼunel ɡʼjelazɡi durɡo roqʼow ɡʔawurase ɡurebɡi dur χʔonaldasan ɬuɡʔintʃʼjew batʼijab χalqʼaɬuqχa witʃun wosaraw laʁaseɡi
roqʼow ɡʔawuraseɡi witʃun wosaraseɡi tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo sunnat ɡʔabize kːola ɡʔjedin χisulareb muɡʔru ɡʼalamatɬun bukʼina dir abadijab qʼotʼi nuʒer tʃerχalda
sunnat ɡʔabitʃʼjew aj ɡʼawrataɬul raɡʼal qʼotʼitʃʼjew biχʔintʃi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼaɡʼinawize wuɡo dir qʼotʼi ɡʔjes χwezaburaɬuqχ
tsoɡi ɡʔadin abuna allaɡʔas ibraɡʔimida
ɡʔanʒejaldasa naqχe dur ɬaduda tsʼar saraj ɡureb sara bukʼine buɡo
ditsa ɡʔjelda barakat ɬela wa ɡʔjeldasan duje was ɡʔawila ditsa ɡʔjelda barakat ɬela wa ɡʔjeldasan χalqʼal ɬuɡʔina ɡʔjeɬul naslujaldasan χalqʼazul patʃazabi raqχina
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ allaɡʔasda tsewe kʼalaʁorkʔje kːaraw ibraɡʔim ʒanisanɡo weɬanqχana wa ɡʔjes pikru ɡʔabuna nusɡo son baraw χeraw tʃijasdasan ɬimer ɬuɡʔunebiʃː unqʼojalda antsʼɡo son baraj saratsaɡi ɬimer kin ɡʔabuleb in
tsinɡi ɡʔjes allaɡʔasda ɡʔarana
ismaɡʼilidaɡʼaɡi dutsa barakat ɬolebaniχa jan
allaɡʔas abuna
dur ɬadi saratsa ɡʔawize wuɡo duje was wa dutsa ɡʔjesije isχʼaqʼ abun tsʼarɡi kʔjeze buɡo ɡʔjesulɡun wa ɡʔjesul naslabazulɡun bukʼine buɡo dir qʼotʼi abadijab qʼotʼi
ismaɡʼilil raqχaɬ dur ɡʔariɡi ditsa qʼabul ɡʔabuna ɡʔjesdaɡi barakat ɬela ditsa wa ɡʼjemeral ɬimalɡi kʔun ɡʔjesul naslabazul qʼadarɡi tsʼikʼkʼinabila ismaɡʼilidasan waqχina χalqʼaɬul antsʼila kʼiɡo tseweqχan wa kʼudijab χalqʼaɬul emenɬun ɬuɡʔina ɡʔjew
amma dirɡo qʼotʼi ditsa ɡʔabila isχʼaqʼilɡun tso ɬaɡʼalidasan ɡʔabɡo zamanalda saratsa duje ɡʔawize wuɡew wasɡun
ibraɡʔimida ɡʔjedinɡi abun allaɡʔ naqχe ana
ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ ʒindirɡo was ismaɡʼilijeɡi ʒindasan ɬuɡʔaral kinalɡo biχʔinazeɡi ritʃun rosaral ʒindirɡo laʁzaderijeɡi qʼawuɬ ruɡelʃːinal kinalɡo biχʔinaze sunnat ɡʔabuna ibraɡʔimitsa allaɡʔas ʒinde amru ɡʔabunʃːinab tʼubazabuna ɡʔjes
ibraɡʔimitsa unqʼojalda antsʼila itʃʼɡo son ban bukʼana ʒindijeɡo sunnat ɡʔaburab zamanalda
ɡʔjesul was ismaɡʼilil bukʼana antsʼila ɬabɡo son
tsoχʼo qʼojaɬ sunnat ɡʔabuna ibraɡʔimijeɡi ɡʔjesul was ismaɡʼilijeɡi
ibraɡʔimil qʼawuɬ ɡʔarural biχʔinazeɡi ɡʔjedinɡo tsoɡidal χalqʼazuqχa ritʃun rosaral laʁzaderijeɡi

baqʼ buχʼarab qʼaɬul ɡʼuʒalda mamrel mikːil ʁutʼbi ruɡeb bakʼalda ʒindirɡo tʃadiraɬul raɡʔduqχ ɡʼodow tʃʼun wukʼaraw ibraɡʔimije zaɡʔirɬana betʼjerhan
betʼjer borχun walaɡʔidal ibraɡʔimida wiχʔana ɬabɡo tʃi ɡʔjezda dandeɡi wortun rakʔalda nodo tʃʼwan ɡʼodoweɡi qʼulun
ɡʔjes abuna
ja betʼjerɡʔan beɡʔuleb batani dur laʁasda reʃːtʼintʃʼoɡo unɡe
nuʒer χʼatʼal tʃurize ɡʔabsaɡʼat ɬimɡi batʃʼina wa ɡʔab ʁotʼoda ʁorkʔ nuʒetsa χʼalχʔiɡi ɡʔabila
ditsajin abuni nuʒee kwen tʼjeχ χʼadurila saparalda nuʒer χʼal daɡʔɬitʃʼoɡo bukʼine dida nuʒer laʁasda askʼosan unelɬidalχa nuʒ ruɡel
ɬikʼ buɡo jan abuna ɡʔjez ɡʔjesda dutsaɡo abuqχe ɡʔabe
wekerun tʃadiralda ʒaniweɡi un ibraɡʔimitsa sarada abuna
biʃːunɡo ɬikʼab χanʒdal tso qʼaliɡi butsun χeχɡo tʃed beʒe
tsinɡi ɡʔjew wekerana ʒindirɡo reχʔjed buɡeb bakʼalde wa kʔarijab tʼasa biʃːun betʃeɡi batʃun laʁasda ɬazabuna χeχɡo ɡʔjebɡi qχun ɡʔan χʼadurejan
χadub ibraɡʔimitsa ʒintsaɡo bosun ɡʔalbaderida tsebe ɬuna χʼanɡi raχʔɡi batʃil ɡʔanɡi wa ɡʔjel kwanan raqχineɡʼan ʁotʼoda ʁorkʔ waqχun tʃʼana
dur ɬadi sara kij jiɡej jan ɡʔiqʼana ɡʔjez ibraɡʔimida
ɡʔanij tʃadiraɬuj jiɡo jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjes
dun itʃʼɡo motsʼidasan tʼadwusːina ɡʔaniwe jan abuna ɡʔjezul tsojas ɡʔjebmeχalda dur ɬadi saral was wukʼine wuɡo
tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa ɡʔjesda naqχa tʃʼun ɡʼjenekːun jikʼana sara
ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo ibraɡʔimɡi saraɡi rukʼana tsereɡo ɡʼoloqχanɬijaldasa aral χeral tʃaɡʼi rutʃːabazul χʼajiz batʃʼinɡi qʼotʼun bukʼana saral
ɡʔjedinɬidal reɬi batʃʼun ɡʔjeɬ pikru ɡʔabuna ɡʔanʒe dun tʼujan χerɬarab meχaɬ ɡʔjedinab roχel ʃːwelariʃːχa dije dir betʼjerɡʔantʃiɡi χerɬun wuɡeɬul abun
amma betʼjerhanas ibraɡʔimida abuna
ʃːaj dur ɬadi sara jeɬanqχulej jiɡej ʒintsa χeraj ɡʼadamaɬ ɬimer kin ɡʔabulebilanɡi abun
betʼjerhanasda χʼalkʼolareb ʃːibniɡi ʒo buɡebiʃː ditsa aburab zamanalda itʃʼɡo motsʼidasan tʼadwusːine wuɡo dun duqχe ɡʔjebmeχalda saral kodow was wukʼine wuɡo
dun jeɬanqχitʃʼo jan ɡʔjeresi bitsana χʼinqʼaraj saratsa
ɡuro jan abuna ɡʔjes ɡʔjelda mun jeɬanqχana
ʒiderɡo nuχda ine tʼade raqχana ɡʔjel tʃaɡʼi tsinɡi ʁore rasaɬude sodomaɬul raqχaldeχun ralaɡʔana ibraɡʔim ɡʔjel tʼoritʼize ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ wiɬːana
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas abuna
dida rakʼalda buɡeb ʒo ibraɡʔimidasa baɬɡo ɡʔabiliʃː ditsa
ibraɡʔimidasan ɬuɡʔine buɡeɬulχa kʼudijab wa ɡutʃab χalqʼ dunjalaɬul kinalɡo qʼawmaze barakatɡi ʃːweze buɡeɬul ibraɡʔimidasan
ditsa tʼasa wiʃːana ibraɡʔim betʼjerhanasul nuχdasan χʔwadejilan ritʼuqχɡo wa χʼalalɡo ɡʼumru ɡʔabejilan ʒindirɡo ɬimalazeɡi ʒindasan ɬuɡʔaral naslabazeɡi ɡʔjes amru ɡʔabize wa betʼjerhanasɡi tʼubazabila ibraɡʔimije raɡʼi kʔun bukʼarabʃːinab
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas abuna
sodomaɬul wa ɡomorrajaɬul χalqʼaɬul kweʃɬijaɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ kutakal ɡʔarkʔal raɡʼulel ruɡo dida ɡʼasijal munaɡʔal ɡʔarulel ruɡo ɡʔjez
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo diqχe batʃʼarab kweʃab aχʼi bitʼarab buɡiʃːali χal ɡʔabize ɡʔjezuqχe reʃːtʼina dun ɡʔjedin buɡiʃː jaɡi ɡʔjetʃʼiʃːali ɡʔjeɬul χal ɡʔabila
sodomaɬul raqχaldeχun swerun ana ɡʔjel tʃaɡʼi amma betʼjerhan ibraɡʔimida askʼow tʃʼowuqχe wukʼana
tsinɡi ɡʔjesda askʼoweɡʼan qʼan ibraɡʔimitsa abuna
kweʃal tʃaɡʼazda tsadaqχɡo boʒi imanaɬul tʃaɡʼiɡi χwezariliʃːχa dutsa
naɡaɡʔ ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔaralda watani kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo muʔminaw tʃi ɡʔjew kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡojase ɡʼoloɡʼaɡi ɡurχʼjel tsʼob ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔar tʼaɡʼine ɡʔabiliʃːχa dutsa
ɡʔjedinab ʒo dutsa ɡʔabulareɬulχa kweʃazda tsadaqχ ɬikʼal tʃaɡʼiɡi χwezarilaro ritʼarazdeɡi tʼjeqʼazdeɡi tsoɡo ʒaza reʃːtʼinabilaro ɡʔjedinab ʒo bukʼine res ɡʔjetʃʼo tʼolabɡo dunjalaɬul diwantʃijas ritʼuqχab diwan qʼotʼilariʃːχa
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas ʒawab kʔuna
sodomalda dida kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo muʔmintʃi watani ɡʔjezije ɡʼolo dun ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔaralda ɡurχʼila
ɡʔjebmeχalda naqχeɡi ibraɡʔimitsa abuna
dun duda tsewe zarra wuɡo χʼur wuɡo buɡoniɡi dir betʼjerɡʔanasda kʼaɬaze ditsa tawakːal tʼamila
kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ɡʼjeze ʃːuɡo kamuraw muʔmintʃi ɡʔjeniw watani ɡʔjew ʃːuɡojaw kamunilan dutsa tʼubarab ʃaɡʔar pasaɬizabiliʃːχa
tsinɡi betʼjerɡʔanas abuna
kʼiqʼojalda ʃːuɡo muʔmintʃi ɡʔjeniw watani ditsa ɡʔjeb pasaɬizabilaro
ibraɡʔimitsa naqχeɡi ɡʔiqʼana
naɡaɡʔ kʼiqʼoɡo ɡuroni muʔmintʃi ɡʔjeniw watitʃʼoni
tsinɡi betʼjerɡʔanas ʒawab kʔuna
kʼiqʼoɡo wataniɡi pasaɬizabilaro ditsa ɡʔjeb
ibraɡʔimitsa abuna
ditsa aburalda tsːin baqχunɡeχa dir betʼjerɡʔanasul naɡaɡʔ ɡʔjeniw ɬeberɡo ɡuroni muʔmintʃi watitʃʼoni
tsinɡi betʼjerɡʔanas ʒawab kʔuna
ɡʔjeniw ɬeberɡo muʔmintʃi watani ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔaralda dun ɡurχʼila
ibraɡʔimitsa abuna
ɡʔale ditsa dir betʼjerɡʔanasda ɡʔiqʼuleb buɡo qʼoɡo ɡuroni watitʃʼoni
tsinɡi betʼjerɡʔanas ʒawab kʔuna
qʼoɡojase ɡʼoloɡi dun ɡurχʼila ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔaralda
ibraɡʔimitsa abuna
dir betʼjerɡʔanasul tsːin baqχunɡeχa aχiriseb nuχaɬɡi kʼaɬalin ɡʔjeniw antsʼɡo ɡuroni muʔmintʃi watitʃʼoni
tsinɡi betʼjerɡʔanas ʒawab kʔuna
antsʼɡojase ɡʼoloɡi ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔar tʼaɡʼinabilaro
ɡʔjedinɡi abun betʼjerhan ɡʔjesda tsewesa naqχe ana ibraɡʔimɡi roqʼowe tʼad wusːana

kʼiɡo malaik watʃʼana sodomalde markʼatʃʼuber rukʼkʼuneb ɡʼuʒalda ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabaqχ ɡodekʼaniw ɡʼodow tʃʼun wukʼana lutʼ ɡʔjel riχʔidal tʼadeɡi waqχun ɡʔjezda dande ana ɡʔjew wa ɡʼodob ɡʔumer tsuzeɡʼan ɡʔjezije betʼjer qʼulana
tsinɡi ɡʔjes abuna
betʼjertʃʼaqχajal riɬːa dir nuʒer laʁasul bakʼalde nuʒerɡo χʼatʼalɡi tʃurize χʼalχʔiɡi ɡʔabize radal ine beɡʔila nuʒerɡo nuχda
riɬːinaro jan abuna ɡʔjez ɡʔanir qʼotʼnorɡo tʃʼjela niʒ qʼasi
amma lutʼitsa tʼasa witʃʼitʃʼoɡo ɡʔaridal ɡʔjel raziɬana wa ɡʔjewɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjesul roqʼore riɬːana lutʼitsa retʃːeb tʼjetʃʼjel panqʼalɡi reʒun ɬikʼab ɡʔobolɬi ɡʔabuna ɡʔjezije wa ɡʔjel kwanana
qʼasi ɡʔjel reɡilalde ʃaɡʔaraɬul ɡʼadamaz ɡʼoloqχabazdasa baqχarab χarabazde ɡʼuntʼun sodomaɬul kinalɡo biχʔinaz unqʼabɡo raqχaldasan swerun kːuna lutʼil mina
duqχe sordo baze ratʃʼaral ɡʼadamal kir ruɡel abun aχʼdana ɡʔjel ɡʔanire niʒeqχe kʔje ɡʔjel ɡʔjezdasan niʒetsa lazat bosize
ʒindaɡo χadub nutsʼaɡi qʼan lutʼ qʼwatʼiwe watʃʼana
ɡʔjes abuna
te watsal ɡʔjeb iʃ ɡʔabuɡe ɡʔjeb qχubɬi
dir kʼiɡo jas jiɡo kʼijajɡoɡi jasɡʼadan ɡʔjel kʔjela ditsa nuʒeqχe nuʒeeɡo bokʔarab ɡʔabe ɡʔjezije amma ɡʔal tʃaɡʼazda qχwaɡe ɡʔal dir qʼawuɬe ratʃʼaral dir ɡʔalbal ruɡeɬul
tʼaɡʼa tsewesa jan abuna ɡʔjez ɡʔjesda mun wuɡo tʃijar rakʔaldasa watʃʼaraw aparaɡ ɡʔanʒe niʒeda maɬːarizejiʃː qʼasd kːarab ɡʔjezijejaldasaɡi kweʃab ɡʔabila niʒetsa duje
ɡʔjedin aχʼi χʼuralda ɡʔjel lutʼida tʼadeɬana wa nutsʼa bekize ɬuɡʔana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ lutʼil kʼijawɡo ɡʔobolas qʼwatʼire kweralɡi reɡʔun roqʼowe ʒaniwe tsʼan ana lutʼ wa ʒanisaχun nutsʼa raχana
wa raɡʔduqχe rakʼarun rukʼaralʃːinal ɡʼisinal tʃʼaχʼijal kinalɡo biχʔinal betsːɬizaruna ɡʔjez kiɡʼan balaɡʔaniɡi ruqʼaɬul kawu batuleb bukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjezda
tsinɡi kʼijawɡo tʃijas lutʼida abuna
ɡʔab ʃaɡʔaralda tsoɡi ʃːiw wuɡew dur durtsal wasal jasal jaɡi tsoɡi ʃːal rataniɡi kinalɡo ɡʔanisa naqχe ratʃe
niʒetsa ɡʔab ʃaɡʔar tʼaɡʼinabizeqχin buɡo ɡʔab ʃaɡʔaraɬul ɡʼadamazul ɡʼorqχoɬa arab kweʃɬijaɬul kutakab qχuj raɡʼuleb buɡo betʼjerhanasda wa betʼjerhanas niʒ ritʼun ruɡo ɡʔab ʃaɡʔar pasat ɡʔabize
ʒindirɡo jasal abural ɡʼoloqχabazuqχe wiɬːana lutʼ wa ɡʔjes abuna
χeχɡo ɡʔab ʃaɡʔaraldasa naqχe a betʼjerhanas ɡʔalda tʼade balaɡʔ bitʃːazeqχin buɡo
amma ɡʔjezda kːana lutʼil maχsara batililan
qχaχʼɬi baleb ɡʼuʒalda malaikzabi ɬuɡʔana lutʼ ɡʼjedeɡʼizawize
durɡo ɬadiɡi jasalɡi ratʃun χeχɡo ɡʔanisa naqχe a ɡʔab ʃaɡʔaraɬe ʒaza ɡʔabuleb meχaɬ munɡoɡi χweze ɡurin
kinɡoɡi lutʼ ɡʼjedeɡʼulew wukʼintʃʼo amma betʼjerhan ɡurχʼana lutʼida ɡʔjedinɬidal kːun kweralɡun lutʼɡi ɡʔjesul ɬadiɡi kʼijajɡo jasɡi malaikzabaz ʒidetsaɡo ʃaɡʔaraldasa qʼwatʼire ʃːwezaruna
ʃaɡʔar tun qʼwatʼire ʃːwedal ɡʔjezul tsojas lutʼida abuna
ɡʔanʒe ɬuta χwasarɬize ɡʼamal ɡʔabe ja naqχe walaɡʔuɡe ja ɡʔab rasaɬijalda kiwniɡi ɬalqχuɡe muɡʼruzde ɬuta ɡuroni munɡi χweze wuɡo
baʒarularo dir betʼjerɡʔan in ʒawab ɡʔabuna lutʼitsa
dije durɡo laʁase ɬikʼɬi ɡʔabuleb buɡo dutsa dideχun dur ɡurχʼjel tsʼobɡi kʼudijab buɡo dutsa dir ɡʼumru χwasar ɡʔabuna amma muɡʼruzde ɬutize diqχa baʒarularo ɡʔjeb balaɡʔ dida χadub ɡʼuntʼila dunɡi χwela
dole tso ɡʼaɡardaɡo buɡeb ʃaɡʔar dowe ʃːwezeɡʼan wekerize kʼwela dida dowe wekerizin dun dob ɡʔitʼinabɡo ʃaɡʔar buɡeɬul dowa dunɡi χwasarɬila
ɬikʼ buɡo jan abuna malaikas duje ɡʼolo ɡʔjebɡi ɡʔabila ditsa dutsa bitsuneb buɡeb ɡʔjeb ɡʔitʼinab ʃaɡʔar χwezabilaro
ɡʔa ɡʔanʒe χeχɡo wekere mun dowe ʃːwezeɡʼan ditsa ʃːibɡo bajbiχʔize beɡʔularin ɡʔjedinɬidalin ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔaralda tsʼar tsoɡʼar
baqʼ bakːuleb ɡʼuʒalda lutʼ tsoɡʼaralde ʃːwana
tsinɡi betʼjerhanasul amrujaldaɬun sodomaldeɡi ɡomorrajaldeɡi zobalazdasan tsʼad ɡʼadin tsʼa rekʼarab tʃʼabatʼ tʃwaχana betʼjerhanasdasan batʃʼana ɡʔjeb
wa pasat ɡʔabuna kʼijabɡo ʃaɡʔarɡi tʼolabɡo rasaɬiɡi kinalɡo ɡʔjenir rukʼaral ɡʼadamalɡi rakʔalda biʒarabʃːinabɡi
lutʼida tsadaqχ ɬutun unej jikʼaraj ɡʔjesul ɬadijin abuni naqχjusːun jalaɡʔana wa ɡʔjebsaɡʼatɡo tsʼamul χʼubijalde swerana
radal χeχɡo waqχun ibraɡʔim wiɬːana noɬ betʼjerhanasda tsewe ʒiwɡo waqχun tʃʼun wukʼarab bakʼalde
sodomaldeχunɡi ɡomorrajaldeχunɡi wa rasaɬijaldeχunɡi walaɡʔidal koroqχ ɡʼadin kʼkʼujdutsa batsun biχʔana rakʔ
palχʼasil rasaɬijaɬul ʃaɡʔaral pasat ɡʔaruleb meχaɬ allaɡʔasda ibraɡʔim rakʼalde ʃːwana lutʼ wukʼaral ʃaɡʔaral tʼaɡʼinaruleb meχaɬ allaɡʔas lutʼ balaɡʔaɬukʔa wortʃʼizawuna
tsoɡʼaralda tʃʼjeze χʼinqʼun kʼijajɡo jasɡi jatʃun lutʼ muɡʼruzde ana ɡʔjeniw tso noqχoda tʃʼana lutʼ ʒindirɡo jasalɡun
tso qʼojaɬ kʼudijaj jasaɬ ɡʔitʼinalda abuna
emen χerɬulew wuɡo ɡʔab dunjalaɬul ɡʼadatalda reqʼon niɬɡun rukʼine tʼokʼaɬ biχʔinalɡi ɡʔjetʃʼo rakʔalda
ratʃʼa niɬetsa tʃaʁirɡi ɡʔjeqʼeze kʔun emen meχtizawize wa ɡʔjesda askʼor reɡize ɡʔjedin niɬerɡo insul naslu tʼaɡʼine bitʃːalaro niɬetsa
ɡʔjeb sordojaɬ ɡʔjez emen ɡʔjeqʼezawuna kʼudijaj jas ɡʔjesda askʼoj jeɡana amma ɡʔjesda ʃːibɡo bitʃʼtʃʼitʃʼo kin ɡʔjej ʒinda askʼoj jeɡarajaliɡi kin naqχe arajaliɡi
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeɬ jatsalda abuna
noɬ dun insuda askʼoj jeɡana ratʃʼa tʃaʁirɡi kʔun qʼasiɡi ɡʔjew meχtizawize wa munɡi jeɡize ɡʔjesda askʼoj ɡʔjedin niɬerɡo insul naslu tʼaɡʼine bitʃːalaro niɬetsa
ɡʔjeb sordojaɬɡi ɡʔjez emen ɡʔjeqʼezawuna tsinɡi ɡʔitʼinaj jasɡi jeɡana ɡʔjesda askʼoj amma ɡʔjesda ʃːibɡo bitʃʼtʃʼitʃʼo kin ɡʔjej ʒinda askʼoj jeɡarajaliɡi kin naqχe arajaliɡi
ɡʔjedin ʒiderɡo insudasan lutʼil kʼijajɡo jasaɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana
kʼudijaɬe was ɡʔawuna ɡʔjesda tsʼar moɡʼaw ɬuna ɡʔjesdasan ɬuɡʔaral ruɡo dol moɡʼawijal
ɡʔitʼinaɬeɡi was ɡʔawuna ɡʔjesda tsʼar ben ammi ɬuna ɡʔjesdasan ɬuɡʔaral ruɡo dol ammonijal

ibraɡʔim ɡʔjenisa neɡewalde ana wa kadeʃaldaɡi ʃuraldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob buɡeb ɡeraralda jaʃaw ɡʔabun tʃʼana
sara ʒindir jats jiɡilan abuna ɡʔjes ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡeraraɬul χan awimeleχitsa sarada χadur tʃaɡʼi ritʼana wa ɡʔjej ʒindiqχeɡo jatʃana
amma tso sordojaɬ makʔiɬ allaɡʔas awimeleχida abuna
ɡʔjej ɡʼadan duqχeɡo jatʃaraɬuqχ mun χweze wuɡo ɡʔjeɬul ros wuɡo
awimeleχ ʒeɡi ɡʔjelda qχwan wukʼintʃʼo
ja dir betʼjerɡʔan abun ɡʔardana ɡʔjew ɡʼajibɡo ɡʔjetʃʼjeb χalqʼɡi χwezabilebiʃːχa dutsa
ɡʔjew tʃijas dida abuna ɡʔjej ʒindir jats jiɡilan ɡʔjeɬ ʒintsaɡoɡi abuna ɡʔjew ʒindir wats wuɡin ɡʔjeb iʃaɬuɬ dir namus batsʼtsʼadab buɡo ditsa munaɡʔɡi ɡʔabitʃʼo
bitʼarab buɡo jan abuna allaɡʔas makʔiɬ dida ɬala dur namus batsʼtsʼadab bukʼin ɡʔjedinɬidal ditsa mun munaɡʔaldasa tsʼunana ditsa witʃːatʃʼo mun ɡʔjelda qχwaze
amma ɡʔanʒe dutsa ɡʔjej ɡʼadan rosasuqχe naqχ jusːinaje ɡʔjew awaraɡ wuɡeɬul ɡʔjes duɡʼa ɡʔabila mun tʃʼaɡo χutʼaɡijilan duda ɬajχa ɡʔjej rosasuqχe naqχe kʔjetʃʼoni munɡi dur tʼolabɡo ɡʼaɡarɬiɡi χwalikʔa rortʃʼize ɡʔjetʃʼo
radal awimeleχitsa ʒindirɡo tʃuqʼa raχʔan dande aχʼana wa kːarabʃːinab ɡʔjezda bitsana ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjel kinalɡo kutakalda χʼinqʼana
tsinɡi ibraɡʔim ʒindiqχeɡo aχʼana awimeleχitsa wa ɡʔjesda abuna
dutsa niʒee ɡʔaburab ʒo ʃːib ditsa duje ʃːib kweʃɬi ɡʔabun bukʼarab ɡʔjediɡʼan kʼudijab munaɡʔalde dunɡi dir tʼolabɡo χanɬiɡi tsʼaze kːani ɡʔjedinab ʒo ɡʔabize beɡʔularoɡuri
ʃːaj dutsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔaburab in ɡʔiqʼana awimeleχitsa ibraɡʔimida
ibraɡʔimitsa ʒawab kʔuna
dida rakʼalde kːana ɡʔab rakʔalda ɡʼadamal allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼulel ɡʔjetʃʼin wa ɬadi sababɬun dunɡi tʃʼwalin
ɡʔjelda tʼadeɡi χʼaqʼiqʼataldaɡi ɡʔjej dir jats kːola dir insuje tsoɡidaj tʃʼuʒujaɬ ɡʔajuraj jas jiɡeɬul ɡʔjej dir ɬadiɬun ɬuɡʔana
wa insul ruqʼɡi reχun tun saparalde waqχajilan allaɡʔas dije amru ɡʔaburab meχaɬ ditsa ɡʔjelda abuna dije ɬikʼ bukʼine bokʔun batani niɬ kire ʃːwaniɡi dutsa abe dun dur wats wuɡilan
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ awimeleχitsa ibraɡʔimije ɡʼiɡi ɡʼatʃiɡi laʁzalɡi ʁarawaʃalɡi sajʁat ɡʔaruna wa saraɡi naqχe kʔuna
ɡʔjes ibraɡʔimida abuna
ɡʔab kinabɡo dir rakʔ duda tsebe buɡo dujeɡo bokʔarab bakʼalda jaʃaw ɡʔabe
sarada ɡʔjes abuna
ditsa dur watsase kʔoleb buɡo azarɡo ɡʼartsul ʃekel dur rakʼ χwezabijaɬuqχ retsʼalije wa dur tʼolabɡo ɡʼaɡarɬijalda tsee mun namus batsʼtsʼadaj jikʼin ɬaze kʔoleb buɡo ɡʔjeb
tsinɡi ibraɡʔimitsa allaɡʔasde duɡʼa ɡʔabuna wa allaɡʔas awimeleχɡi ɡʔjesul ɬadiɡi ʁarawaʃalɡi saχɬizaruna naqχeɡi ɬimal ɡʔarize bajbiχʔana ɡʔjez
ibraɡʔimil ɬadi sara sababɬun awimeleχil qʼawuɬ ruɡel kinalɡo rutʃːabi ɬimal ɡʔarularelɬun ɬuɡʔinarun rukʼana betʼjerhanas

ʒintsaɡo raɡʼi kʔun bukʼarab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ betʼjerhanas sarade barakat reʃːtʼinabuna ʒindirɡo raɡʼi betʼjerhanas tʼubazabuna
saral urɡʔibe ɬimer ɬuɡʔana wa allaɡʔas aburab bolʒal ʃːwarabɡo χeraw ibraɡʔimije ɡʔjeɬ was ɡʔawuna
saratsa ɡʔawuraw ʒindirɡo wasasda tsʼar isχʼaqʼ ɬuna ibraɡʔimitsa
wa ɡʔawun mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ allaɡʔasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjesije sunnat ɡʔabuna
isχʼaqʼ ɡʔawurab meχaɬ ibraɡʔimitsa nusɡo son ban bukʼana
ɡʔjebmeχalda saratsa abuna
reɬanqχize batʃʼuneb iʃ ɡʔabuna dije allaɡʔas
ɡʔab χabar raɡʼarawʃːinaw tʃi weɬanqχila
ʒeɡi ɡʔjeɬ abuna
keren kʔun saratsa ɬimer χaχizabize buɡilan ibraɡʔimida abize ɬidaɡo rakʼaldetsin kːelaroan amma ɡʔale χerab qʼojaɬ ɡʔjesije ditsa was ɡʔawuna
ɬimer kʼudijab ɡʼoleb bukʼana ɡʔjew karandasa tʼurab qʼojaɬ ibraɡʔimitsa kʼudijab suχʼmat ɡʔabuna
ibraɡʔimidasan misrijaj ɡʔaʒaritsa ɡʔawuraw was ʒindir was isχʼaqʼɡun wasandulew wiχʔidal
saratsa ibraɡʔimida abuna
ɡʔaʁaj ʁarawaʃ ʁoɬul wasɡun tsadaqχ naqχe jatʃaqχe ɡʔanisa dir was isχʼaqʼida baʃːad ɡʔjew ʁarawaʃaɬul wasɡi dur irsilawɬun wukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo
ʒindirɡo wasasul raqχaɬ abural ɡʔjel raɡʼabi rekʼjeɬ χʼunsana ibraɡʔimida
amma allaɡʔas ɡʔjesda abuna
ja wasasul jaɡi ɡʔjej ʁarawaʃaɬul pikrabaz rakʼ qʼwariɬuɡe dur saratsa aburab ɡʔabe isχʼaqʼidasan ɬuɡʔine ruɡo dur naslabi
amma ʁarawaʃaɬul wasasdasanɡi ditsa tʼubarab χalqʼ ɬuɡʔinabila ɡʔjewɡi dur ɬimerɬidalχa
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ radal ibraɡʔimitsa ɡʔaʒariqχe kwenɡi ɬadal tsʼurab raqχɬenɡi kʔuna ɡʔjeɬul muʁzada ɡʔjebɡi ɬun ɡʔjes abuna wasɡi watʃun naqχe ajilan ɡʔaʒar ɡʔjenisa ana wa beer ʃewajaɬul ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχalda nuχɡi qʼosun χutʼana
kwatʼitʃʼoɡo raqχɬenaɬub bukʼarab ɬimɡi ɬuɡʼana ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ʒindirɡo wasɡi tso qχarqχida ʁorkʔ tun
dojeɡʼan ana ɡʔjej χolew wuɡew ɡʔjew wiχʔize bokʔitʃʼoɡo tʃʼorbutʼaɬ retʃʼtʃʼuleb tʃʼoril manzilaɬ rikʼkʼadeɡi un ɡʼodoj tʃʼana wa ɡʼjek ɡʼjekijalda ɡʼodana ɡʔjej
amma allaɡʔasda wasasul ɡʼodi raɡʼana wa allaɡʔasul malaikas zobalazdasan ɡʔaʒaride aχʼana
duje ʃːib ɡʔaʒar mun χʼinqʼuɡe dutsa dowa taraw was ɡʼoduleb ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼana allaɡʔasda
jaqχun ɡʔanʒe durɡo wasasda askʼoje a wa ɡʔjew kwerɡi kːun tʼade waqχinawe kʼudijab χalqʼ ɬuɡʔinabize buɡo ditsa ɡʔjesdasan
wa allaɡʔas ɡʔaʒarida biχʔizabuna ʁuj buɡeb bakʼ askʼoje un ɡʔjeɬ raqχɬen tsʼjezabuna wa wasase ɡʔjeqʼeze ɬim kʔuna
ɡʔjeldasa naqχe allaɡʔas ɡʔjew was reχun tetʃʼo ɡʔjew kʼudijaw ɡʼuna ɡʼalaχ awlaqχalda jaʃaw ɡʔabun tʃʼana tʃʼorbutʼaɬ tʃan ɡʔabize ruɡʔunɬana
paran abuleb salul awlaqχalda jaʃaw ɡʔabuleb bukʼana ɡʔjes misrijaldasa ɬadiɡi jatʃana ebelaɬ ɡʔjesije
ɡʔjeb zamanalda ʒindirɡo bodul tseweqχan piχolɡun tsadaqχ watʃʼun awimeleχitsa ibraɡʔimida abuna
dur kinabɡo kwerraʁarijaɬuɬ allaɡʔas duje kumek ɡʔabuleb buɡo
ɡʔanʒe mun ɡʔjede ja dije ja dir ɬimalaze ja dir kinabɡo naslujaɬe χijanat ɡʔabilarilan wa duje dir raɡʼi χwetʃʼjeb ɡʼadin dije wa mun qʼabul ɡʔawurab dir ulkajaɬe dur raɡʼiɡi χwelarilan
ibraɡʔimitsa abuna
dun duje ɡʔjedila jan
amma tsin ɡʔjes awimeleχije badibtʃʼwaj ɡʔabuna ɡʔjesul tʃaɡʼatsa ʒindir ʁuj naqχe baqχanilan
ɡʔjeb ɬitsa ɡʔaburabali dida ɬalaro jan abuna awimeleχitsa dutsa ɡʔjeɬul raqχaɬ dida ʃːibɡo bitsintʃʼoɡuri tʼotsebe raɡʼuleb buɡo dida ɡʔjeb
tsinɡi ibraɡʔimitsa awimeleχije sajʁat ɡʔaruna ɡʼiɡi ɡʼatʃiɡi wa ɡʔjesulɡun raqʼlil qʼotʼi qʼajɡi ɡʔabuna
ibraɡʔimitsa ankʔɡo χuχ batʼa tʃʼjezabun bukʼana
wa awimeleχitsa ɡʔiqʼana
ɡʔab ankʔabɡo χuχ dutsa batʼa ɡʔabijaɬe ɡʼilla ʃːib abun
ɡʔjelɡi ratʃe dujeɡo ɡʔab ʁuj ditsa buqχarab bukʼinalda dur raziɬi tasdiqʼ ɡʔabun in ʒawab kʔuna ibraɡʔimitsa
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjez tsotsaze ɡʔa barab qʼojaldasa naqχe ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tsʼar ɬuna beer ʃewa abun
ɡʔjedin ɡʔjeb beer ʃewajalda ɡʔjez raqʼlil qʼotʼi qʼaj ɡʔabuna tsinɡi awimeleχɡi ɡʔjesul bodul tseweqχan piχolɡi roqʼore pilistimazul rakʔalde tʼadrusːun ana
ibraɡʔimitsa beer ʃewajalda tamariskaɬul ʁwetʼ tʃʼana wa abadijaw betʼjerhan allaɡʔasde ɡʔardon duɡʼa ɡʔabuna
ɡʔjeldasa χadubɡi ɡʼjezeɡʼan zamanajaɬ jaʃaw ɡʔabuna ibraɡʔimitsa pilistimazul rakʔalda

tsinɡi allaɡʔas ibraɡʔimil χʼalbiχʔana
ibraɡʔim in abuna ɡʔjes
ɡʔale dun in dande ʒawab ɡʔabuna ibraɡʔimitsa
tsinɡi allaɡʔas abuna
ɡʔjew tsoχʼo wuɡew durɡo χirijaw was isχʼaqʼɡi tsadaqχ watʃun morija abuleb rakʔalde a ɡʔjenib ditsa biχʔizaburab maɡʼarda tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχwe dutsa ɡʔjew
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ radal tsudunɡo waqχun ibraɡʔimitsa χʼama kʔolona kʼiɡo raɡʔtʼatelɡi tsadaqχ watʃana ʒindirɡo was isχʼaqʼɡi watʃana wa qʼurban buχʼize tsʼulɡi bitʃʼun allaɡʔas ʒinda aburab bakʼaldeχun walaɡʔun nuχda waqχana ibraɡʔim
nuχda waqχun ɬababileb qʼojaɬ tsewe walaɡʔidal ibraɡʔimida rikʼkʼadasanɡo ɡʔjeb bakʼ biχʔana
ɡʔab χʼamil tʼalab ɡʔabun ɡʔanir tʃʼa nuʒ in abuna ɡʔjes raɡʔtʼatelazda dunɡi wasɡi allaɡʔase ɡʼibadataɬe ina wa ɡʔanire naqχ rusːina
qʼurban buχʼize χʼadurarab tsʼul ɡʔjes isχʼaqʼil muʁalda ɬuna tsinɡi tsʼaɡi nusɡi bosana wa isχʼaqʼɡi watʃun ɡʔjew tseweχun ana
dada jan aχʼana isχʼaqʼitsa ibraɡʔimide
ʃːib dir was in abuna ibraɡʔimitsa
wasas ɡʔiqʼana
niɬeqχ tsʼaɡi buɡo tsʼulɡi buɡo qʼurbanaɬe qχweze kʔjeɡʼjer kibχa buɡeb
allaɡʔas biχʔizabila dir was ʒindijeɡo qʼurbanaɬe qχweze kʔjeɡʼjer kib buɡebali jan abuna ibraɡʔimitsa
ʒeɡi tsereχun ana ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo
allaɡʔas ʒinda abun bukʼarab bakʼalde ʃːwedal ibraɡʔimitsa qʼurbanaɬe bakʼ qʼatʃʼana wa ɡʔjenib tsʼul reqʼezabuna tsinɡi ɡʔjes isχʼaqʼ wuχʔana wa qʼurbanaɬe qʼatʃʼarab bakʼalda tsʼulada tʼad ɡʔjewɡi ɬun
was qχweze nus kodobe bosana
amma tsintʼaɡo zobalazdasan betʼjerhanasul malaikas ɡʔjesde aχʼana
ibraɡʔim ibraɡʔim
ɡʔale dun ilan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjes
wasasde kwer borχuɡe jan abuna malaikas ʃːibɡo ɡʔabuɡe ɡʔjesije ɡʔanʒe dida ɬana mun allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼulew tʃi wukʼin tsoχʼo wuɡew durɡo was dije kʔjeze baraχʃːitʃʼo mun
tsinɡi tsewe walaɡʔidal ibraɡʔimida biχʔana ɡʔjenib qχarqχazuɬ ɬːurdulɡi qʼan χutʼarab kuj askʼowe un ɡʔjes kuj tsebe batʃana wa wasasul bakʼalda tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe ɡʔjeb qχuna
ɡʔjeb iʃ kːarab bakʼalda tsʼar betʼjerhanas kʔjela
ɡʔjeldasan batʃʼarab buɡo betʼjerhanasul maɡʼarda sabab batila jan abiɡi
zobalazdasan kʼiabizeɡi betʼjerhanasul malaikas ibraɡʔimide aχʼana
wa ɡʔjes abuna
dutsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔaburaɬuqχ tsoχʼo wuɡew was kʔjeze mun baraχʃːitʃʼjeɬul dirɡo tsʼaraldaɬun ɡʔjedulew wuɡo dun
ditsa dude barakat reʃːtʼinabila ditsa duje ɡʼjemeral naslabi kʔjela zodiqχ tsʼwabiɡʼanɡi raɬdal raɡʼalda saliɡʼanɡi tsʼikʼkʼinabila ɡʔjezul qʼadar wa dur naslabaz tuʃbabazul ʃaɡʔaral kwerde rosila
mun dije mutʼiɡʼɬaraɬuqχ dunjalaɬul kinalɡo χalqʼaze barakat ʃːwela ɡʔjezdasan
tsinɡi raɡʔtʼatelal tun rukʼarab bakʼalde tʼad wusːana ibraɡʔim wa ɡʔjelɡun tsadaqχ beer ʃewajalde ana beer ʃewajalda jaʃaw ɡʔabun tʃʼana ibraɡʔim
tso zamanaldasan ibraɡʔimida ɬana ʒindir wats naχorilɡi rukʼin ɡʔjesul ɬadi milkatsa ɡʔarural wasal
ɡʼutsɡi tʼotsewesew was ɡʔjesda χadusew buzɡi kemuelɡi ɡʔjew kːola aramil emen
kesedɡi χʼazoɡi pildaʃɡi idlafɡi betuelɡi
betuelije ɡʔajuna jas riwka
ɡʔjew mikʔawɡo was ɡʔawuna milkatsa ibraɡʔimil wats naχorije
ɡʔjezda tʼadeɡi reuma abun tsʼar buɡej naχoril ʁarawaʃaɬɡi ɡʔjesije ɡʔaruna tewaχ ɡaχam taχaʃ wa maɡʼaχa abural ɬimal

saratsa bana nusijalda qʼolo ankʔɡo son
ɡʔjej χwana kirjat arbaɡʼalda χewronalda χanaanijazul rakʔalda ɡʔjenib saraqχ maɡʼu tʼuna ibraɡʔimitsa ɡʔjeɬul ʒanazajalde qʼulun ɡʼjek ɡʼjekijalda ɡʼodana ɡʔjew
tsinɡi ɬadul ʒanazajalda askʼosa waqχun un ɡʔjew χitijazda kʼaɬana
dun wuɡo qʼwatʼib rakʔaldasa ɡotʃun watʃʼaraw aparaɡ nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabize res ʃːwaraw tʃi dir χwaraj ɬadi juqʼize bakʼ kʔje dije nuʒer rakʔalda
χitijaz ibraɡʔimije ʒawab kʔuna
ɡʼjenekːe betʼjertʃʼaqχad mun wuɡo qʼadrujaw allaɡʔase χirijaw tʃi jan abuna χitijaz niʒer χabalazul biʃːunɡo ɬikʼab bakʼ tʼasa biʃːe wa ɡʔjenij juqʼe durɡo ɬadi bokʔaraw tʃijas iznu kʔjela duje ʒindirɡo tuχumaɬul χabalaɬ ɡʔjeɬije bakʼ ɡʔabize
ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬul ɡʼadamaze aj χitijaze betʼjerɡi qʼulun
ibraɡʔimitsa abuna
dir χwaraj ɬadi ɡʔanij juqʼize nuʒer iznu buɡeb batani dir ɡʔari qʼabul ɡʔabun tsoχaril was efronida abe
ɡʔjesul χurul raɡʼalda buɡeb maχpelajaɬul noqχo dije kʔjejilan nuʒɡi nuɡʼzalɬun rukʼaɡo ditsa ɡʔjeb bitʃun bosila ɡʼurab baɡʔaɡi kʔun χabalaze bukʼine
ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawuduqχe ɡodekʼanire rakʼararal χitijazda ɡʔorkʔow ɡʼodow tʃʼun wukʼana ʒiwɡo efronɡi wa kinazdaɡo raɡʼun ɡʔjes ibraɡʔimida abuna
bitʃun kʔjelaro dir betʼjertʃʼaqχad ɡʼjenekːe diqχ ɡʔjeb χurɡi noqχoɡi tʃʼoboɡo kʔoleb buɡo ditsa duje ɡʔal dir rakʔtsojazda tsebesan ditsa duje kʔoleb buɡo ɡʔjeb ɡʔjenij durɡo χwaraj ɬadi juqʼize
ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬul ɡʼadamaze naqχeɡi betʼjerɡi qʼulun
ibraɡʔimitsa kinazdaɡo raɡʼun efronida abuna
ɡʔarula duda ɡʔjeb χuruqχ kːoleb ɡʼarats bose diqχa tsinɡi ditsa dir χwaraj ɬadi juqʼila ɡʔjenij
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ efronitsa abuna
ɡʼjenekːe betʼjertʃʼaqχad ɡʔjeb χurul baɡʔa buɡo unqʼnusɡo ʃekel ɡʼartsul kʼudijab baɡʔajiʃː ɡʔjeb buɡeb dujeɡi dijeɡi durɡo χwaraj ɬadi juqʼe ɡʔjenij
efronitsa aburab baɡʔajalda reqʼana ibraɡʔim wa χitijalɡi nuɡʼɬijaɬe tʃʼjezarun ɡʔjes biχʔizaburab qʼadaralda bazarɡabazda ɡʔorkʔob biɬːanqχarab bakʼɬijaɬul unqʼnusɡo ʃekel ɡʼartsul kʔuna ɡʔjesije
ɡʔjedin mamrejaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda maχpelajalda buɡeb χurulɡi ɡʔjeldaɡo tsadaqχ noqχodulɡi wa ɡʔjeb χurir ruɡelʃːinal ʁutʼbuzulɡi
betʼjerɡʔanɬun waqχana ibraɡʔim ɡʔjeɬije nuɡʼzalɬunɡi rukʼana ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawuduqχ ɡodekʼanire rakʼararal χitijal
tsinɡi ibraɡʔimitsa ʒindirɡo ɬadi sara juqʼana χanaanijazul rakʔalda mamrejalda ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjelda χewronilan abula ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ maχpelajaɬul χurib buɡeb noqχoda
ɡʔjeb χurɡi noqχoɡi χabalaze bakʼ χʼisabalda χitijazuqχan ibraɡʔimil betʼjerɡʔanɬijalde batʃʼana

ibraɡʔim tsʼaqʼɡo χerɬun wukʼana wa sunduɬɡo betʼjerhanasul barakatɡi nasibɬun bukʼana ɡʔjesije
tsinɡi ibraɡʔimitsa ʒindirɡo ruqʼaɬul iʃɡi maɡʼiʃatɡi tʼadqʼaraw kʼudijaw laʁasda abuna
ɡʔab dir matʃʼalda kwerɡi ɬun
zobalazulɡi rakʔaɬulɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul tsʼarɡi reχson ɡʔjede mun dutsa dir wasase ɡʔab rakʔaɬul χanaanijazda ɡʔorkʔosa jas jatʃinarilan
mun a dir ulkajalde dir ɡʼaɡaral tʃaɡʼazuqχe wa ɡʔjenisa jatʃe isχʼaqʼije ɬadi
laʁas ɡʔiqʼana
dida tsadaqχ ɡʔanije ɡʔab rakʔalde jatʃʼine dojasa jasaɬe bokʔitʃʼoni ʃːib ɡʔabileb ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsa dur was dob mun naqχe ɡotʃarab ulkajalde ʃːwezawize kːolewiʃː abun
woreɡiχa ʃːwezawuɡe jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjesije ibraɡʔimitsa dir was dowe watʃunɡe dutsa
dirɡo insul ruqʼɡi reχun tun dun tʃijar rakʔalde watʃaraw zobalazul betʼjerhan allaɡʔ kʼaɬana dunɡun wa ɡʔjew ɡʔjedana ɡʔab rakʔ dir naslujaɬe kʔjelilan ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo malaik witʼila duda tsewe tsewe dir wasase ɬadiɡi jatʃun watʃʼine duje kumekaɬe
duda tsadaqχ jatʃʼine jasaɬe bokʔitʃʼoni dur ɡʔjedijaldasa mun erkenɬila amma dir was dutsa dowe watʃunɡe
ʒindirɡo χwaʒainasul matʃʼalda kwerɡi ɬun laʁ ɡʔjedana ɡʔjedin ɡʔabililan
tsinɡi ʒindirɡo χwaʒainasul waranabazda ɡʔorkʔosa antsʼɡo waraniɡi batʃun χiri χirijal sajiʁatalɡi rosun ɡʔjew saparalde waqχana aram naɡʔaraimalde naχor wuɡeb ʃaɡʔaralde
baqʼtʼjerχʔul ɡʼuʒ bukʼana ʃaɡʔaralda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ ʁujalda askʼor ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo waranabi tʃʼjezarurab meχalda ɡʔjeb bukʼana ʃaɡʔaraldasa rutʃːabi ɬede ratʃʼuneb ɡʼuʒ
tsinɡi ibraɡʔimil laʁas duɡʼa ɡʔabuna
ja betʼjerhan dir χwaʒain ibraɡʔimil allaɡʔ ɡʔarula duda ʒaqʼa dije iqʼbal nasib ɡʔabe wa dir χwaʒainasul rekʼjel murad tʼubazabe
ɡʔale dun ɡʔaniw ʁujalda askʼow ʃaɡʔaraldasa jasal ɬadare ratʃʼuneb bakʼalda waqχun tʃʼjela
ditsa ɡʔanije jatʃʼaraj jasalda abuni dur ɡʼjertʼinisa ɬim kʔjejilan wa ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjeqʼejin dur waranabiɡi ɡʔjeqʼezarilin ʒintsajan ʒawab kʔuni ɡʔjeldaɬun bitʃʼtʃʼila dida dutsa durɡo laʁ isχʼaqʼije baχʼaraj tʼasa jiʃːarabɬi ɡʔjebmeχalda dida biχʔila dutsa raχʼmu tsʼob ɬun bukʼin dir χwaʒainasda
ɡʔjel raɡʼabi kʼaldisa qʼwatʼire ratʃʼinalde ɡʼjeretʼɡi ʁaʒilda ban ɬadal tsʼjeze jatʃʼana milkalɡi ibraɡʔimil wats naχorilɡi was betuelil jas riwka
ɡʔjej jikʼana tsʼaqʼ bertsinaj ʒeɡi rosase intʃʼjej jas ʁujaɬuqχe un ɡʼjeretʼ tsʼuna ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjej naqχjusːun unaɡo
χaduwɡi wekerun ibraɡʔimil laʁas abuna
beɡʔuleb batani dije ɡʔjeqʼeze ɬim kʔje dur ɡʼjertʼinisa jan
ɡʔjeqʼe χʼurmatijaw in ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjeɬ
wa ɡʔjebsaɡʼatɡo ʁaʒildasa ɡʼjeretʼɡi baqχun ibraɡʔimil laʁase ɡʔjeqʼeze ɬim kʔuna
tsinɡi ɡʔjeɬ abuna
ɡʔabsaɡʼat ditsa dur waranabazeɡi batʃːila ɬim ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan ɡʔjeqʼeze
botsʼi ɡʔjeqʼeze ɬurab rosonibe χeχɡo ɡʼjeretʼɡi tʃʼjeχʔon naqχeɡi ʁujaɬuqχe jekerana ɡʔjej ɡʔjedin ɬim batʃːana kinalɡo waranabi ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan
wutsʼtsʼun tʃʼun ɡʔjeɬuqχ walaɡʔun wukʼana laʁ allaɡʔas ɡʔjesul saparalda barakat ɬun bukʼinalda rakʼtʃʼjezeɡʼan
waranabi ɡʔjeqʼon raqχarab meχalda ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬije kʔuna baʃːdab ʃekelaɬul
ɡʔjes ɡʔjelda ɡʔiqʼana
mun ɬil jas kːolej dur insul qʼaji swerijalda niʒee sordo baze bakʼ ɡʔjetʃʼodaj abun
ɡʔjeɬ ʒawab kʔuna
milkalɡi naχorilɡi was betuelil jas jiɡo dun
ɡʔjeɬ tʼadeɡi ʒubana
niʒer ɡʼjemerab nakːuɡi buɡo waranabi tʼad reɡize ɡʔjezije kʔjeze kʼaltsʼi χerɡi buɡo nuʒee sordo baze bakʼɡi bukʼina
tsinɡi nakabazdeɡi kːun ɡʼodob nodoɡi tʃʼwan betʼjerhanase retsː ɡʔabuna ɡʔjew tʃijas
wa ɡʔjes abuna
tsʼob ɡʼatʼidaw wa raɡʼi χolarew wuɡo dir χwaʒain ibraɡʔimil betʼjerhan allaɡʔ ɡʔjes dir χwaʒain reχun tetʃʼo betʼjerhanas dun watʃana bitʼaqχe dir χwaʒainasul watsasul roqʼowe
jekerun roqʼojeɡi un riwkatsa ebelalda bitsana kinabɡo kːara taraɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ
lawan abun tsʼar buɡew wats wukʼana riwkal ɡʔjew ʁujaɬuqχe wekerana nuχlulasda askʼowe
jatsaɬul kʼilikʼɡi kurχʔabiɡi riχʔidal wa ɡʔjes riwkada aburabɡi raɡʼidal lawan ɡʔjew tʃijasuqχe ɡʼjedeɡʼana ibraɡʔimil laʁ ʒindirɡo waranabiɡun ʒeɡi ʁujalda askʼowɡo tʃʼun wukʼana
ɡʔjesda lawanitsa abuna
ɬikʼ ʃːwaraw betʼjerhanasul barakat reʃːtʼaraw ɡʔaniw waqχun tʃʼun ʃːibulew mun ditsa duje ruqʼɡi dur waranabaze bakʼɡi qʼatʃʼan buɡo
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ibraɡʔimil laʁ ɡʔjesul bakʼalde wiɬːana waranabazdasa qʼaji baqχana ɡʔjezije nakːuɡi kʼaltsʼi χerɡi batʃʼana ɡʔobolaseɡi ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ rukʼarazeɡi χʼatʼal tʃurize ɬimɡi batʃʼana
χadub ɡʔjezda tsebe kwen ɬuna amma laʁas abuna
ɡʔaniwe dun ʃːaj witʼarawali bitsun baqχineɡʼan kwanalaro dun
bitseχa jan abuna ɡʔjesda lawanitsa
ɡʔjes abuna
dun wuɡo ibraɡʔimil laʁ
betʼjerhanas kʼudijab barakat ɬun buɡo dir χwaʒainasda wa ɡʔjesije kʔun buɡo ɡʼjemerab betʃeɬi ɡʼiɡi ɡʼatʃiɡi ɡʼarats mesedɡi laʁzalɡi ʁarawaʃalɡi waranabiɡi χʼamulɡi
dir χwaʒainasul ɬadi saratsa ɡʔjesije was ɡʔawuna χerɬarab meχaɬ wa ʒindirɡo buɡebʃːinab χazina betʃeɬi dir χwaʒainas ɡʔjew wasase kʔjeze amru ɡʔabuna
dir χwaʒainas dun ɡʔjedizawuna ditsa ɡʔjesul wasase dob χanaanijazul rakʔaldasa ɡʼadan jatʃinarilan
wa ɡʔjesul watʼanalde ɡʔjesul ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬuqχe un ɡʔjenisa ɡʔjesul wasase baχʼarajɡi jatʃun watʃʼinilan
ditsa dirɡo χwaʒainasda tsʼjeχana ɡʔjenisa jasaɬe dida tsadaqχ jatʃʼine bokʔitʃʼoni ʃːib ɡʔabilebilan
ɡʔjes dije ʒawab kʔuna dun boʒaraw dir betʼjerhanas duda tsadaqχ ʒindirɡo malaik witʼila wa ɡʔjes dur saparalda barakat ɬezabila dir tuχumaldasa dir insul kʔolbodasa jasɡi dir wasase jatʃun mun watʃʼine
mun dir ɡʼaɡaral tʃaɡʼazuqχeɡi ʃːun ɡʔjez duda tsadaqχ jas jitʼize inkar ɡʔabuni mun durɡo ɡʔajaldasa erkenɬila jan
ʒaqʼa ʁujalda askʼowe ʃːwedal ditsa duɡʼa ɡʔabuna ja betʼjerhan dir χwaʒain ibraɡʔimil allaɡʔ ɡʔarula duda dir ɡʔab saparalda barakat ɬe
ɡʔale dun ɡʔab ʁujalda askʼow waqχun tʃʼjela ɬadal ɡʼjeretʼ tsʼjeze ɡʔanije jas jatʃʼarab meχalda ditsa ɡʔjelda abila dur ɡʼjertʼinisa ɬim ɡʔjeqʼeze kʔjejilan
ɡʔjeɬ dije ʒawab kʔuni ɡʔjeqʼe dur waranabazeɡi batʃːila ditsa ɬim abun ɡʔjeɬul maɡʼna bukʼina betʼjerhanas ɡʔjej jas tʼasa jiʃːun jikʼin dir χwaʒainasul wasase ɬadiɬun jatʃine
ɡʔjedin duɡʼa ɡʔabun baqχinaldeɡo ʁaʒilda ɡʼjeretʼɡi ɬun jatʃʼana riwka ʁujaɬuqχeɡi un ɡʔjeɬ ɡʼjeretʼ ɬadal tsʼjedal ɡʔjeqʼeze ɬim kʔjejilan ɡʔarana ditsa ɡʔjelda
ɡʔjeqʼe dur waranabazeɡi batʃːila ditsa ɬim in abuna ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjebsaɡʼat ʁaʒildasa bosun ɡʼjeretʼɡi diqχe kʔun ditsa ɬim ɡʔjeqʼon baqχindal waranabazeɡi batʃːana ɡʔjeɬ ɬim
mun ɬil jasilan ɡʔiqʼidal ɡʔjeɬ ʒawab kʔuna milkalɡi naχorilɡi was betuelil jas jiɡo jan ɡʔjebmeχalda ditsa ɡʔjeɬije maɡʼarzuqʼalazda baze kʼilikʼɡi kwerazda χːeze kurχʔabiɡi kʔuna
tsinɡi ditsa betʼjerhanase suʒda ɡʔabuna wa betʼjerhanase dir χwaʒain ibraɡʔimil allaɡʔase retsː baqʼ ɡʔabuna χwaʒainasul wasase ɡʔjesul kʔolbodasa jas jatʃine ɡʔjes dun bitʼaqχe ɡʔaniwe tʼowitʼaraɬuqχ
ɡʔanʒe nuʒetsa ʃːib abileb nuʒee qʼabulɬiliʃː dir χwaʒainasul ɡʔari tʼubazabize ditsa ʃːib ɡʔabilebali ɬaze ʒawab kʔjeχa ɡʔanʒe nuʒetsa
lawanitsaɡi betuelitsaɡi ʒawab kʔuna
ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasdasan ɬuɡʔarab iʃ buɡo ja kweʃab jaɡi ɬikʼab bitsun ɡʔjelda tʼad kʼaɬaze bakʼ ɡʔjetʃʼo niʒee
ɡʔale riwka jatʃe ɡʔjej dudaɡo tsadaqχ betʼjerhanase bokʔuqχe bukʼine bitʃːante ɡʔjeb iʃ wa dur χwaʒainasul wasas ɡʔjej ɬadiɬun jatʃine jitʃːante
ɡʔjeb raɡʼidal ibraɡʔimil laʁas betʼjerhanase nodo tʃʼwan suʒda ɡʔabuna
tsinɡi ɡʔjes qʼwatʼire raqχana riwkaje ritʼaral mesedilɡi ɡʼartsulɡi tʼaɡʼjelal retʼjel kun ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔjeɬul watsaseɡi ebelaɬeɡi ritʼaral χirijal sajʁatal
tsinɡi ɡʔjewɡi ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ rukʼaralɡi kwana ɡʔjeqʼana wa kʔiʒize reɡana radal tʼade raqχindal ibraɡʔimil laʁas abuna
dirɡo χwaʒainasuqχe tʼad wusːine iznu kʔje dije jan
riwkal watsasɡi ebelaɬɡi abuna
