jitʃːante antsʼɡo qʼojaɬɡi ɡʔjej niʒeda askʼoj tʃʼjeze tsinɡi nuʒ ɡʔjejɡun tsadaqχ nuχda ritʼila
ɡʔaniw tʃʼun zaman inabuɡe dir betʼjerhanas dir saparalda barakat ɬun bukʼaɡo witʃːante dun dirɡo χwaʒainasuqχe naqχ wusːine jan abuna ibraɡʔimil laʁas
doj aχʼizin doɬ ʃːib abuliʃːali tsʼjeχeze jan abuna ɡʔjez
ɡʔjez riwka aχʼana wa ɡʔjelda ɡʔiqʼana
ɡʔaw tʃijasda tsadaqχ ine razi jiɡiʃː mun in
ɡʔjeɬ ʒawab kʔuna
razi jiɡo jan
ɡʔjebmeχalda riwkaɡi ɡʔjeɬul raχʔdal ebelɡi ibraɡʔimil laʁɡi ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ rukʼaral tʃaɡʼiɡi nuχareɡʼize χʼadurɬana ɡʔjel
ɡʔjezulɡun qʼo ɬikʼ ɡʔabuleɬul riwkada barakat ɬeɡijan ɡʔadinab duɡʼa ɡʔabuna ɡʔjez
ja niʒer jats ɡʼjemeral naslabi ɬuɡʔaɡi dudasan wa
aza azar antsʼaza azar tʃi ɡʼjeɡi ɡʔjezul
dur ɬimalaz kwerde rosaɡi
tuʃbabazul ʃaɡʔaral
riwkaɡi ɡʔjeɬul ʁarawaʃalɡi waranabazda rekʼana wa ibraɡʔimil laʁasda tsadaqχ qʼwatʼire raqχana ɡʔjedin riwkaɡi jatʃun roqʼowe qʼoqʼana ɡʔjew
isχʼaqʼ beer laχaj roijaldasa dob zamanalda ɡʔjew neɡewalda jaʃaw ɡʔabun wukʼana roqʼowe tʼadwusːarab ɡʼuʒ bukʼana ɡʔjeb
baqʼtʼjerχʔul ɡʼuʒaɬ ɡʔjew maʁiɬe ana urʁize wa duɡʼa ɡʔabize betʼjer borχidal rikʼkʼadasanɡo waranabazul qʼapila batʃʼuneb biχʔana ɡʔjesda
riwkadaɡi wiχʔana isχʼaqʼ ɡʔjeb parajaɬɡo waranijaldasa ʁorkʔjeɡi reʃːtʼun
ɡʔjeɬ ibraɡʔimil laʁasda ɡʔiqʼana
niɬeda dande watʃʼunew wuɡew ɡʔadaw tʃi ʃːiw an
dow dir χwaʒain wuɡo jan abuna laʁas
ɡʔjebmeχalda riwkatsa tʃadrajaɬ ɡʔumer baχtʃana
laʁas isχʼaqʼida bitsana saparalda kːara taraɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ
tsinɡi isχʼaqʼitsa riwka jatʃana ʒindirɡo ebel saral bukʼarab tʃadiraɬuje wa riwka ɡʔjesul ɬadiɬun ɬuɡʔana isχʼaqʼije jokʔana riwka wa χwaraj ebelaɬuqχ ruχʼjel ɡʼodotsana

ibraɡʔimitsa tsoɡi tʃʼuʒu jatʃana ɡʔjelda tsʼar ketura bukʼana
ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjesije ɡʔaruna wasal zimran jokʃan medan midjan iʃbaqʼ wa ʃuaχʼ
jokʃanije ɡʔaruna ʃewa wa dedan dedanil naslujaɬul kːola aʃurijal letuʃijal wa leumijal
midjanil wasal kːola ɡʼjefa ɡʼjefer jenoχ awida wa eldaɡa ɡʔjel kinalɡo ruɡo ketural naslabi
ʒindirɡo tʼolabɡo betʃeɬi ibraɡʔimitsa isχʼaqʼije kʔuna
ibraɡʔimitsa ʒiwɡo tʃʼaɡo wuɡeb meχaldaɡo betʃedal sajʁatalɡi kʔun baqʼbakːudeχun ruɡel rakʔazde ritʼana ʁarawaʃaz ɡʔarural wasal isχʼaqʼidasa rikʼkʼad ɡʔarun
ibraɡʔimitsa kinabniɡi nusijalda ɬabqʼojalda antsʼila ʃːuɡo son bana
tsʼaqʼɡo χerɬarab meχalda ɡʼumrujaɬul sonazdasaɡi ɡʼortsʼun ʒindirɡo umumuzda χaduw ana ibraɡʔim
ɡʔjesul wasaz isχʼaqʼitsaɡi ismaɡʼilitsaɡi ɡʔjew wuqʼana mamrejalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ maχpelajaɬul χurib buɡeb noqχoda aj tsoχaril was χitijaw efronil rakʔalda
ibraɡʔimitsa χitijazuqχa bosun bukʼana ɡʔjeb χur ɡʔjenir ruqʼun ruɡo ibraɡʔimɡi saraɡi
ibraɡʔim χun χadub ɡʔjesul was isχʼaqʼide barakat reʃːtʼinabuna betʼjerhanas isχʼaqʼitsa jaʃaw ɡʔabuleb bukʼana beer laχaj roijalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ
ɡʔale saral ʁarawaʃ misrijaldasa ɡʔaʒaritsa ibraɡʔimije ɡʔawuraw was ismaɡʼililɡi ɡʔjesul naslujaɬulɡi qʼisa
tsʼikʼkʼarasdasan bajbiχʔun ismaɡʼilil wasazul tsʼaral newajot ismaɡʼilije tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw kedar adbeel miwsam
miʃma duma masːa
χʼadad tema jetur nafiʃ wa kedma
ɡʔjel ruɡo ismaɡʼilil wasal antsʼila kʼiɡo qʼawmaɬul antsʼila kʼiɡo betʼjer ismaɡʼilil wasazul tsʼaral ɬun ruɡo ɡʔjel tʃʼun rukʼaral bakʼazda wa rosabazda
kinabniɡi nusijalda ɬeberalda ankʔɡo sonɡi ban ismaɡʼil χwana wa ʒindirɡo umumuzda χaduw ana
ɡʔjesdasan ɬuɡʔaral naslabi tʃʼana χʼawilajaldasa baqχarab ʃuralde ʃːwezeɡʼan ruɡel rakʔazda ɡʔjeb ʃur buɡo misrijaldasa baqʼbakːul raqχaldeχun asːirijalde uneb nuχda ʒiderɡo kinalɡo watsazulɡun tuʃmanɬijalda rukʼana ɡʔjel
ɡʔale ibraɡʔimil was isχʼaqʼilɡi ɡʔjesul naslabazulɡi qʼisa
ibraɡʔimije ɡʔawuna was isχʼaqʼ
kʼiqʼoɡo son barab meχalda isχʼaqʼitsa ɬadiɬun jatʃana paddan aramaldasa aramejaw betuelil jas riwka ɡʔjej jikʼana aramejaw lawanil jats
isχʼaqʼil ɬaduje ɬimer ɡʔabuleb bukʼintʃʼo ʒindir ɬaduda ɡurχʼajan ɡʔardana isχʼaqʼ betʼjerhanasda wa betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesul ɡʔari qʼabul ɡʔabuna riwkal urɡʔibe ɬimer ɬuɡʔana
ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔir ɬimal tsotsada tenkeze ɬuɡʔana
waχʼ in abuna riwkatsa ɡʔadin bukʼine batani ʃːaj dije ɡʔab qʼwariɡʼarab
tsinɡi ɡʔjelda ban betʼjerhanasul amru ɬaze duɡʼa ɡʔabuna ɡʔjeɬ
betʼjerhanas ɡʔjelda abuna
kʼiɡo χalqʼ buɡo dur urɡʔib
kʼiɡo qʼawm batʃʼina dur tʃoχʔonisa qʼwatʼibe
tsojab qʼawm tsojaldasa qʼuwatab bukʼina
kʼudijawaw wukʼina ɡʔitʼinasul laʁɬun
ɬimer ɡʔabize zaman ʃːwedal ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔib kʼiɡo ɬimer bukʼin zaɡʔirɬana
tʼotsewe ɡʔawuna baɡʼarkːarab kʔjeraɬul kʼurɡʼarab rasutsa tʼubanɡo tʃerχ batsaraw was ɡʔjesda tsʼar ɬuna ɡʼisaw
ɡʼisawil χʼatʼil eʁeɡi qʼan kːun ɡʔjesdaɡo χaduw tsoɡidawɡi watʃʼana ɡʔjesda tsʼar ɬuna jaqʼub
wasal kʼudijal ɡʼuna ɡʼisaw ɬuɡʔana ɡʔunar buɡew tʃanaqχan meʁ rakʔaɬul tʃi jaqʼub wukʼana roqʼow wukʼine bokʔulew paraχataw tʃi
ɡʔjezul emen isχʼaqʼije tʃanil ɡʔan bokʔulaan ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjesije ɡʼisawɡi wokʔulaan amma riwkaje jaqʼub wokʔulaan
tso nuχalda jaqʼub tʃurpa ɡʔabulew wuɡeb meχalda tʃanasa wusːun watʃʼana swakan tatu χwaraw ɡʼisaw
dun waqʼutsa χolew wuɡin ɡʔjele ɡʔjeb dur baɡʼarab tʃurpa kʔje dije kwanaze jan abuna ɡʔjes jaqʼubida ɡʔjedinɬidalin ɡʔjesda edom
tʼotsewe ɡʔawurasul iχtijar dije bitʃani kʔjela jan abuna jaqʼubitsa
tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw wukʼinaɬul pajda ʃːib dije dun waqʼutsa χwezeqχin wuɡeb meχaɬ in abuna ɡʼisawitsa
ɡʔjedin batani ɡʔjedeχa jan abuna jaqʼubitsa
ɡʼisaw ɡʔjedana tʼotsewe ɡʔawurasul daraʒa jaqʼubije bitʃanilan
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ jaqʼubitsaɡi ɡʔjesije tʃedɡi χiɬalodul tʃurpaɡi kʔuna ɡʔjew kwanana ɡʔjeqʼana tsinɡi tʼade waqχun naqχe ana ɡʔjedin ʃːibɡo qʼimat ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo tana ɡʼisawitsa tʼotsewe ɡʔawijaɬul daraʒa

ulkajalda ɡʔanʒeɡi raqʼul zaman batʃʼana tsebe dob ibraɡʔimil zamanaldaɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjedinɬidal pilistimazul χan awimeleχiqχe ɡeraralde ana isχʼaqʼ
ɡʔjeniw betʼjerhan zaɡʔirɬana isχʼaqʼije wa ɡʔjes abuna
mun misrijalde unɡe ditsa duda biχʔizaburab rakʔalda tʃʼa
ɡʔjeniw mun ɬikʼ wukʼina ditsa duje kumek ɡʔabila wa dude barakatɡi reʃːtʼinabila ɡʔal kinalɡo rakʔal dujeɡi dur naslabazeɡi kʔjelilan dur emen ibraɡʔimije ɡʔjedarab ɡʔaɡi ditsa tʼubazabila
ditsa dur naslabazul ɡʼadamal zodiqχ tsʼwabiɡʼanɡi ɡʼjemerɬizarila wa ɡʔjezije kʔjela ɡʔal kinalɡo rakʔal dunjalaɬul tʼolalɡo χalqʼaze barakat ʃːweze buɡo dur naslujaldasan
dur emen ibraɡʔim diqχ ɡʼjenekːaraɬuqχ wa dir amrabiɡi tʼadqʼajalɡi qʼanunalɡi χʼukmabiɡi ɡʔjes tʼurazaruraɬuqχ
tsinɡi isχʼaqʼ ɡeraralda tʃʼana
ɡʔjeb bakʼaɬul ɡʼadamaz riwka ʃːijilan ɡʔiqʼidal ɡʔaj dir jats jiɡilan abuna ɡʔjes bertsinaj riwka sababɬun ʒiwɡo tʃʼwalilan ɡʔjej ʒindir ɬadi jiɡilan abize χʼinqʼana ɡʔjew
ɡʔjedin ana ɬikʼalanɡo zaman tso nuχalda pilistimazul χan awimeleχida ɡorduqχan biχʔana isχʼaqʼitsa riwka jeedulej
tsinɡi ɡʔjes isχʼaqʼ ʒindiqχeɡo aχʼana wa ɡʔjesda kʼaɬana
dur ɬadi jikʼun jiɡoɡuri ɡʔaj ʃːajχa tsinɡi dutsa ɡʔjej dur jats jiɡilan aburab
isχʼaqʼitsa ʒawab kʔuna
ɡʔjej sababɬun dunɡo tʃʼwalilan χʼinqʼana dun in
dutsa niʒee ɡʔabuleb buɡeb ʃːib an abuna awimeleχitsa niʒer tsoniɡijaw dur ɬaduda askʼow weɡarawani ʃːib ɡʔabileb bukʼarab kʼudijab munaɡʔalde kːelaroaniʃː niʒ
wa awimeleχitsa ʒindirɡo χalqʼalda ɬazabuna
ɡʔaw tʃijasda jaɡi ɡʔasul ɬaduda qχwaraw tʃi tʃʼwaze wuɡo jan
ɡʔjenir χurzal rekʔize bajbiχʔana isχʼaqʼitsa betʼjerhanas kʼudijab barakat ɬuna ɡʔjesda nusɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼarab batʃʼin ʃːwana ɡʔjesije ɡʔjeb sonaɬ
isχʼaqʼ betʃeɬulewɡo betʃeɬulew wukʼana aχirɡi kutakalda betʃedaw tʃi ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjesul
ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjesul rukʼana ɡʼijal reqχabiɡi ɡʼatʃijazul reχʔjedalɡi ɡʼjemeral laʁzalɡi ɡʔjedinɬidal pilistimazul ɡʔjesde ʒaχʼda kːeze bajbiχʔana
wa ibraɡʔimil zamanaldaɡo ɡʔjesul laʁzaderitsa ruqχun rukʼaral kinalɡo ʁujal ratsizaruna ɡʔjez
awimeleχitsaɡi isχʼaqʼida abuna
naqχe a niʒer rakʔaldasa niʒeda dandekːun ɡʼjemerɡo qʼuwatawɬun ɬuɡʔana mun ɡʔanʒe
ɡʔjenisa naqχe un isχʼaqʼitsa ɡerar abuleb rasaɬijalda tʃadral tʃʼwana wa ɡʔjeniw tʃʼana
ibraɡʔimil zamanaldaɡo ruqχun rukʼaral wa ibraɡʔim χun χadub pilistimaz ʒanibe rakʔ ban ratsaral ʁujal tsʼidasan ruqχana ɡʔjes kidajaliɡo ibraɡʔimitsa ɡʔjezda ɬun rukʼaral tsʼaralɡi tsʼidasan ɬuna ɡʔjes ɡʔjel ʁujazda
tso nuχalda ɡʔjesul laʁzal rukʼana rasaɬijalda ɬim balaɡʔize rakʔ buqχulel wa ɡʔjezda ɡʔjenib itsː batana
amma tʼade ratʃʼun ɡeraraɬul ɡʼuχʔbi isχʼaqʼil ɡʼuχʔbiɡun daɡʼbadize ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjeb ʒider ɬim buɡilan ɡʔjeb ʁuj sababɬun daɡʼba kːedal esek
tsoɡi ʁuj buqχana isχʼaqʼil laʁzaderitsa amma ɡʔjeb sababɬunɡi kːana pitna wa ɡʔjelda tsʼarɡi sitna
ɡʔjebmeχalda isχʼaqʼ ɡʔjeb bakʼaldasa daɡʔawɡi doweɡʼan ɡotʃana wa tsoɡi ʁuj buqχana ɡʔab nuχaɬ ʃːibɡo daɡʼba qʼets kːetʃʼo
ɡʔab rakʔalda niɬ ɡʼjemerɬize aχirɡi betʼjerhanas ɡʼatʼiɬi kʔuna niɬee janɡi abun isχʼaqʼitsa ɡʔjeb ʁujalda tsʼar ɬuna reχowot
tsinɡi isχʼaqʼ beer ʃewajalde tʼad wusːana
ɡʔjeniwe ʃːwarab sordojaɬɡo ilɡʔam ɬuɡʔun betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesda abuna
dun wuɡo dur emen ibraɡʔimil allaɡʔ mun χʼinqʼuɡe ditsa kidaɡo kumek ɡʔabize buɡo duje dir laʁ ibraɡʔimije ɡʼolo ditsa duda barakat ɬela wa dur nasluɡi tsʼikʼkʼinabila
ɡʔjenib qʼurbanaɬe bakʼɡi ban allaɡʔase duɡʼaɡi ɡʔabun isχʼaqʼitsa ʒindirɡo tʃadral tʃʼwana ɡʔjesul laʁzalɡi ʁuj buqχize ɬuɡʔana
ɡʔjeb zamanalda awimeleχ watʃʼana ɡeraraldasa isχʼaqʼiqχe ʒindirɡo wazir aχuzatɡun wa bodul tseweqχan pikolɡun tsadaqχ
isχʼaqʼitsa ɡʔjezda abuna
nuʒ ʃːib qʼwariɡʼun ratʃʼaral nuʒee wokʔitʃʼoɡo naqχe qʼotʼanaɡuri dun nuʒetsa jan
ɡʔjez abuna
niʒeda biχʔuleb buɡo betʼjerhanas duje kumek ɡʔabuleb bukʼin ɡʔjedinɬidal niʒee bokʔun buɡo niɬetsa tsotsaje raɡʼi kʔjeze wa dudaɡi niʒedaɡi ɡʔorkʔob raqʼlilab qʼotʼi qʼaj bukʼine ratʃʼa qʼotʼi ɡʔabize
dutsa niʒee kweʃɬi ɡʔabilarilan niʒetsaɡi duje ɬikʼɬi ɡuroni ʃːibɡo kweʃɬi ɡʔabitʃʼo wa paraχat naqχe ine resɡi kʔuna duje ɡʔanʒe betʼjerhanas dude barakat reʃːtʼinabun buɡo
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ isχʼaqʼitsa ɡʔjezije kʼudijab kwana ɡʔjeqʼej ɡʔabuna
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ radalɡo tʼadeɡi raqχun ɡʔjez tsotsaze ɡʔajal ɡʔjedana tsinɡi isχʼaqʼitsa ɡʔalbal nuχareɡʼana ɡʔjelɡi paraχatɡo naqχrusːun ana
ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ ʁuj buqχulel laʁzaz isχʼaqʼida ɬazabuna ɬim batanilan
isχʼaqʼitsa ɡʔjeb ʁujalda tsʼar ɬuna ʃiwa
kʼiqʼoɡo son barab meχalda ɡʼisawitsa ɬudbi ratʃana χitijaw beeril jas jeɡʔudit wa χitijaw elonil jas basemat
isχʼaqʼijeɡi riwkajeɡi ɡʼjemerab rakʼbaqʼwaj bukʼana ɡʔjel sababɬun

χerɬunɡi betsːɬunɡi wuɡew isχʼaqʼitsa tso qʼojaɬ kʼudijaw was ʒindaɡo askʼowe aχʼana
ja dir was in aχʼana ɡʔjes
dun ɡʔaniw wuɡo dada jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʼisawitsa
isχʼaqʼitsa abuna
dun ɡʔanʒe χerɬun wuɡo χweze tʃan qʼo χutʼun buɡebaliɡi ɬalaro
bose durɡo jaraʁɡi tʃʼorbutʼɡi tʃʼoralɡi wa tʃanawe a
tʃanil ɡʔanɡi bosun watʃʼun ɡʔjeɬul kwen ɡʔabe dije bokʔuleb qʼaɡʼidajaɬ ɡʔjebɡi kwanan dunɡo χwelalde tsebe ditsa duje duɡʼa ɡʔabila betʼjerhanasul barakat dude reʃːtʼine
riwkada raɡʼana isχʼaqʼitsa ʒindirɡo was ɡʼisawida abural ɡʔjel raɡʼabi ɡʼisaw tʃanawe arawɡo
ɡʔjeɬ jaqʼubida abuna
dida raɡʼana dur insutsa ɡʼisawida abuleb
tʃanil ɡʔanɡi bosun watʃʼun dije bokʔuleb qʼaɡʼidajaɬ ɡʔjeɬul kwen ɡʔabe ɡʔjeb ɡʔanɡi kwanan dunɡo χwelalde tsebe ditsa duje duɡʼa ɡʔabila betʼjerhanasul barakat dude reʃːtʼine jan
ɡʔanʒe dir was mun muχʼkanɡo diqχ ɡʼjenekːe wa ditsa maɬarab ɡʔabe
wekerun un reqχaɬa tʼasa biʃːun kʼiɡo ɬikʼab burutʼɡi batʃun watʃʼa ditsa ɡʔjezul ɡʔanal dur insuje bokʔuleb qʼaɡʼidajaɬ tʼaɡʼamab kwen ɡʔabila
ɡʔjebɡi bosun mun insuqχe ina ɡʔjes ɡʔjebɡi kwanan duje duɡʼa ɡʔabize wa ʒiwɡo χwelalde tsebe barakatɡi duje kʔjeze
amma isχʼaqʼitsa riwkada abuna
dir wats wuɡo rasul tsʼuraw tʃi dirin abuni tsʼwakarab tʼom buɡo
naɡaɡʔ insutsa dida kwer qχwani ʃːib ɡʔabileb ditsa ɡʔjew ɡukːulew wukʼin tʼatani ɡʔjes dije barakat kʔjelaro naɡʼana kʔjela
amma ebelaɬ abuna
ɡʔjeb naɡʼana ditsa didaɡo tʼade bosila dir was munin abuni diqχ ɡʼjenekːe burtʼal ratʃine a
jaqʼubitsa burtʼal ratʃun ratʃʼana riwkatsa isχʼaqʼije bokʔuleb qʼaɡʼidajaɬ tʼaɡʼamab kwen χʼadurana
tsinɡi ɡʔjeɬ qʼawuɬ batarab ʒindirɡo tsʼikʼkʼaraw was ɡʼisawil biʃːunɡo ɬikʼab retʼjel ɡʔitʼinaw was jaqʼubida retʼinabuna
ɡʔjesul kweralɡi ɡaburɡi burtʼazul tsʼakatsa ratsizaruna
tsinɡi buχʼilaɡo kwenɡi tʃedɡi jaqʼubiqχe kʔuna
dada jan abuna ɡʔjes insuda tʼadeɡi un
ja dir was in abuna isχʼaqʼitsa mun kinawaw
dun ɡʼisaw wuɡo duje tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw in ʒawab kʔuna jaqʼubitsa insuje dutsa aburabʃːinab ɡʔabuna ditsa tʼade worχun ɡʼodow tʃʼa tʃanil ɡʔan kwanaze wa dije barakatɡi kʔjeze
isχʼaqʼitsa ɡʔiqʼana
ja dir was ɡʔjediɡʼan χeχɡo tʃan kin duqχe ʃːwarab
ɡʔjes ʒawab kʔuna
betʼjerhanas dur allaɡʔas kwerbaqʼana dije jan
ɡʔaniwe askʼoweɡʼan watʃʼa dir was in abuna isχʼaqʼitsa χʼaqʼɬunɡo mun ɡʼisaw wuɡiʃːali tso kwer kwaʃilin duda
jaqʼub insuda askʼowe ana wa ɡʔjes ɡʔasda kwerɡi kwaʃːun abuna
ɡʔarakʔ jaqʼubil buɡo kweral ɡʼisawil ruɡo jan
ɡʼisawilɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjesul kweralɡi rasul tsʼun ratidal isχʼaqʼida ɬatʃʼo ɡʔjew jaqʼub wukʼin wa ɡʔjesije duɡʼa ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔana
mun dir was ɡʼisawiʃːχa jan ɡʔiqʼana ɡʔjes jaqʼubida
u dir dada jan abuna ɡʔas
isχʼaqʼitsa abuna
dutsa batʃʼarab tʃanil ɡʔan kʔje dir was kwanaze χadub ditsa duje barakat kʔoleb duɡʼa ɡʔabila
jaqʼubitsa insuda tsebe ɬuna kwenɡi tʃaʁirɡi kwana ɡʔjeqʼon waqχarab meχalda
isχʼaqʼitsa abuna
askʼowe watʃʼun ubatʃ ɡʔabe dir was dida
insuda askʼoweɡʼanɡi qʼan ubatʃ ɡʔabuna jaqʼubitsa ɡʔjesul ratʼlidasan maχʼ tʃʼwajdal ɡʔjesije barakat kʔun isχʼaqʼitsa ɡʔadin abuna
betʼjerhanas barakat ɬurab
meɡʼjer ɡʼalaχaɬul maχʼ buɡo dir wasasdasan
allaɡʔas duje ɡʔarzaɡo kʔjeɡi
zobalazdasan roɡʔalil ʃːubɡi rakʔaldasan niɡʼmatalɡi
dur χurul batʃʼin tsʼikʼkʼaɡi tʃaʁirɡi ɡʼjemerɬaɡi
bitʃːante χalqʼaz duj qχuluqχ ɡʔabize
qʼawmazɡi bitʃːante duje betʼjer qʼulize
watsazda tʼadɡi mun χan wukʼina
dur ebelaɬul naslabaz betʼjer qʼulila duje
duje naɡʼana kʔuraze naɡʼana ʃːwela
duda barakat ɬeɡijan aburazda barakatɡi ɬela
isχʼaqʼitsa barakatɡi kʔun jaqʼub isχʼaqʼida askʼosa qʼwatʼiwe ɬuɡʔarawɡo tʃanasa wusːun tʼade ʃːwana ɡʔjesul wats ɡʼisaw
insuje bokʔuleb kwen ɡʔabuna ɡʔjesɡi wa ɡʔjebɡi bosun watʃʼun insuda abuna
tʼade worχa dir dada ditsa batʃʼarab tʃanil ɡʔan kwanaze wa dida barakat ɬoleb duɡʼaɡi ɡʔabize
mun ʃːiw an ɡʔiqʼana isχʼaqʼitsa
dun wuɡo dur was duje tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw was ɡʼisaw abun ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔas
ʁarʁar ʃːun sorodana tsinɡi isχʼaqʼ wa ɡʔjes abuna
tʃanil ɡʔan dida kwanazaburaw dow tʃi ʃːiwχa kːolew ɡʔjedin batani mun watʃʼinalde tsebe ditsa ɡʔjesije barakatɡi kʔun ɡʔabunaɡuri duɡʼa ɡʔjesda tʼad bukʼina ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjeb barakat
ɡʔjel raɡʼabi raɡʼidal tʃara buχʼun aχʼdeze ɬuɡʔana ɡʼisaw tsinɡi ɡʔjes insuda ɡʔarana
dijeɡi barakat kʔjeχa dir dada dijeɡi barakat kʔjeχa abun
amma ɡʔjes ʒawab kʔuna
dur watsas watʃʼun maχsarode kːuna dun wa ɡʔjes baqχun ana duje kʔjeze kːoleb bukʼarab barakat
ɡʼisawitsa abuna
tʃʼalɡʼade ɡuro dosda jaqʼubilan abuleb kʼitsʼulɡo ɡukːana dos dun
tsinɡi ɡʼisawitsa insuda abuna dije kʔjeze barakatɡojiʃːχa dur χutʼitʃʼjeb in
isχʼaqʼitsa ʒawab kʔuna
duda tʼad χanɬun ɡʔawuna ditsa dow kinabɡo ɡʼaɡarɬiɡi dosul laʁzalɬun ɡʔaruna χurul batʃʼinɡi tʃaʁirɡi dosije nasibɬize ɡʔabuna ɡʔanʒe ditsa duje ʃːibχa kʔjeleb dir was
tsoχʼo barakatiʃːχa dir dada dur bukʼarab dijeɡi kʔjeχa dada barakat inɡi abun ɡʼisaw ɡʼjek ɡʼjekijalda ɡʼodana
wa isχʼaqʼitsa abuna
ɬikʼab tʼorʃːel biʒulel χurzabazdasaɡi
zodisan reʃːtʼuneb roɡʔalil ʃːubaldasaɡi
rikʼkʼad rukʼina dutsa jaʃaw ɡʔabulel bakʼal
dur betʼjerbaqχiɡi χwaltʃadaɬun bukʼina
durɡo watsase laʁɬun wukʼina mun
amma mun ɡʔjesda dande qʼerkʔjela
wa ɡʔjesul rukʔɡi tʼasa reχun erkenɬi ʃːwela
insul barakat ɡʔjesije ʃːwejaɬ jaqʼubida kutakalda tsːin baqχun wukʼana ɡʼisaw
insuqχ tʃʼjeɡʼjer baral qʼojal ratʃʼindal tʃʼwan reχila ditsa dirɡo wats jaqʼub abun pikrabazda wukʼana ɡʔjew
amma riwkada ɬana ɡʔjeɬul kʼudijaw wasasul rakʼalda buɡeb qʼasd ɡʔitʼinaw was jaqʼubɡi askʼowe aχʼun ɡʔjeɬ abuna
mun tʃʼwaze qʼasd buɡo dur wats ɡʼisawil
ditsa maɬarab ɡʔabe dir was dir wats lawaniqχe χarranalde ɬuta mun
dur watsasul tsːin ɡʼodobusːineɡʼan
dude buɡeb ɡʔjesul ɡʔalaɡab tsːin tʃutʃizeɡʼan wa dutsa ɡʔjesije ɡʔaburab χʼilla makru ɡʔjesda kʼotʃon tezeɡʼan dowa tʃʼa χadub ditsa duda χaduw tʃi witʼila mun dowasa naqχe watʃine ɡuroni tsoɡo qʼojaɬ kʼijawɡo wasasdasa jatʼaɬarab qʼo batʃʼineqχin buɡo dida tʼade
riwkatsa isχʼaqʼida abuna
ɡʔal χitijazul jasaz dunjal riχinabun buɡo dida ɡʔanʒe ɡʔazdaɡo reɬːaraj χitijaj jaqʼubitsaɡi jatʃani ɡʼumruɡo ʃːaj dije

isχʼaqʼitsa jaqʼub askʼowe aχʼana wa ɡʔjesije barakatɡi ɡʔarun ɡʔadinab nasiχʼat ɡʔabuna
χanaanijazul jas jatʃunɡe dutsa
paddan aramalde a durɡo ebelaɬul insul ulkajalde wa ebelaɬul wats lawanil jasazdasan tsojaj jatʃe ɬadiɬun
χʼalkʼolew
ibraɡʔimije ʃːwarab barakat dudeɡi dur naslabazdeɡi reʃːtʼinabeɡi allaɡʔas ʒaqʼa mun aparaɡ χʼisabalda χʔwadulew wuɡeb wa allaɡʔas ibraɡʔimije sajʁat ɡʔaburab ɡʔab rakʔ dur mulkɬun ɬuɡʔine
χadub isχʼaqʼitsa wasasulɡun qʼo ɬikʼ ɡʔabuna wa jaqʼub paddan aramalde lawaniqχe ana ɡʔjew lawan wukʼana jaqʼubilɡi ɡʼisawilɡi ebel riwkal wats aramejaw betuelil was
ɡʼisawida ɬana barakataɬul duɡʼaɡi ɡʔabun isχʼaqʼitsa jaqʼub ɬadi jatʃine paddan aramalde witʼarawɬi ɡʔjedinɡo raɡʼana barakat ɬejanɡi ɡʔarun ɡʔjes jaqʼubida ɬazaburabɬi χanaanijazul jas ɬadiɬun jatʃunɡejilan
wa jaqʼub insutsaɡi ebelaɬɡi maɬarab ɡʔabun paddan aramalde un wukʼinɡi
ɡʔjebmeχalda χanaanijazdasan ratʃaral nusal insuje rekʼjee ɡʼolel ɡʔjetʃʼoɬiɡi bitʃʼtʃʼun
ɡʼisaw ismaɡʼililazuqχe ana wa ɡʔjenisa ʒindijeɡo jatʃana maχʼalat abulej tsoɡi ɬadi ɡʔjej jikʼana ibraɡʔimil was ismaɡʼilil jas wa newajotil jats
beer ʃewajaldasa un jaqʼub χarranaldeχun walaɡʔun saparalde waqχana
tso pulanab bakʼalde ʃːwarab meχalda markʼatʃʼuber rukʼkʼuneb bukʼun sordo baze reʃːtʼana ɡʔjew wa qʼadanib ɡamatʃʼɡi ɬun weɡana
ɡʔjeb bakʼalda makʔu biχʔana jaqʼubida makʔiɬ tso mali biχʔana ɡʔjesda zodibɡi ɡʼodobɡi tsurab wa allaɡʔasul malaikzabi rukʼana ɡʔjenisan tsojal ʁorkʔje reʃːtʼunel tsoɡijal tʼade raχunel
ɡʔjeb malijaɬul tʼoɡʔiw tʃʼun wukʼana betʼjerhan wa ɡʔjes jaqʼubida abuna
dun wuɡo betʼjerhan dur kʼudijaw emen ibraɡʔimilɡi dur emen isχʼaqʼilɡi allaɡʔ mun tʼad weɡun wuɡeb ɡʔjeb kinabɡo rakʔ dujeɡi dur naslabazeɡi sajʁat ɡʔabuleb buɡo ditsa
saliɡʼan ɡʼjemer rukʼine ruɡo dur naslabi wa ɡʔjel tʃʼjeze ruɡo baqʼtʼjerχʔudeχunɡi baqʼbakːudeχunɡi ʃimalaldeχunɡi qʼilbajaldeχunɡi kinalɡo χalqʼaze barakat ʃːweze buɡo dudasan wa dur naslujaldasan
duda kʼotʃonɡe dun munɡun wukʼin kiwe kːaniɡi ditsa tsʼunila mun wa ɡʔab rakʔalde tʼad wusːinawila ditsa mun reχun telaro duje kʔurab raɡʼi tʼubazabila
makʔidasa wiɡʔindal jaqʼubitsa abuna
χʼaqʼɬunɡo betʼjerhan wuɡo ɡʔab bakʼalda didani ɬatʃʼo ɡʔjeb
kutakab χʼinqʼi rekʼjeɬe ɬuɡʔaraw jaqʼubitsa abuna
kiɡʼan χʼinqʼarab bakʼχa ɡʔab buɡeb allaɡʔasul ruqʼ buɡoɡuri ɡʔab zobalazul kawu buɡoɡuri ɡʔanib
radal tʼade waqχindal ɡʔjeb bakʼalda baqχun tʃʼjezabuna jaqʼubitsa qʼasi ʒindirɡo qʼadanib ɬun bukʼarab ɡamatʃʼ wa ɡʔjelda tʼade zajtunaɬul naχ tʼuna
bet el abun ɬuna ɡʔjes ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tsʼar
tsinɡi jaqʼubitsa allaɡʔasda tsebe nazru ɡʔabun ɡʔadin abuna
ɡʔab saparalda dije kwanaze kwenɡi kʔun retʼine partalɡi kʔun allaɡʔas dun tsʼunani
wa saχ salamatɡo dun dirɡo insul roqʼoweɡi tʼadwusːani ɡʼumrujaɬɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔase ɡʼibadat ɡʔabila ditsa
ɡʔab ɡamatʃʼ eχetarab bakʼɡi allaɡʔasul ruqʼɬun ɬuɡʔina wa allaɡʔas dije kʔunʃːinaɬul antsʼil butʼa ditsa allaɡʔaseɡi kʔjela

tsinɡi jaqʼub ʒindirɡo nuχda ana maʃriqʼaɬul χalqʼazul rakʔalde ʃːwedal
awlaqχalda tso ʁuj biχʔana ɡʔjesda ɡʔjelda askʼob ɡʼijal ɬabɡo reqχenɡi buɡoan ɡʔjeb buɡoan botsʼi ɡʔjeqʼoleb bakʼ ʁujaɬul kʼaltʼujalda tʼad kʼudijab ɡamatʃʼ ɬun bukʼana
kinalɡo reqχabi ɡʔjenire rakʼararab meχalda ɡʼuχʔbuz ɡamatʃʼ naqχe qχurʃːizabulaan wa ɡʼiɡi ɡʔjeqʼezabun naqχeɡi ʁujaɬul kʼaltʼu batsulaan
nuʒ kisa watsal abun ɡʔiqʼana jaqʼubitsa ɡʼuχʔbuzda
χarranaldasa ruɡilan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjez
naχoril wasasul was lawan ɬaliʃː nuʒeda jan ɡʔiqʼana ɡʔjes
ɬalilan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjez
ɡʔjew kinχa wuɡew in ɡʔiqʼana jaqʼubitsa
ɬikʼ wuɡo jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjez dole dosul jas raχel jatʃʼunej jiɡo ɡʼi ɡʔjeqʼezabize
baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan ʒeɡi ɡʼjezeɡʼan zaman buɡoɡuri jan abuna jaqʼubitsa ɡʼuχʔbuzda ɡʼi dande bakʼarize zaman ʃːun ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʼi ɡʔjeqʼezabe wa naqχeɡi ɡʼalaχalde ratʃe reqχabi
amma ɡʔjez abuna
kinalɡo reqχabi dandeɬitʃʼoɡo ɡʼi ɡʔjeqʼezabun baʒarularo ɡʔjebmeχalda naqχe qχurʃːizabila ʁujaɬul kʼaltʼa buɡeb ɡamatʃʼ tsinɡi niʒetsa ɡʼiɡi ɡʔjeqʼezabila
ɡʔjedin ɡarɡadulel ɡʔjel ruɡeb meχalda raχel tʼade ʃːwana insul ɡʼijal reqχenɡi batʃun ɡʼijaweχʔɬi ɡʔabuleb bukʼana ɡʔjeɬ
imɡʼal lawanil ɡʼijal reqχenɡi batʃun raχel jatʃʼunej jiχʔidal jaqʼub ʁujaɬuqχe ana wa ɡamatʃʼɡi naqχe qχurʃːizabun ɡʔjeɬul ɡʼi ɡʔjeqʼezabuna
tsinɡi ɡʔjelda ubatʃɡi ɡʔabun ɡʼjek ɡʼjekijalda ɡʼodana jaqʼub
ʒiw dur insul jats riwkal was wuɡilanɡi abun ɡʔjeb insuda bitsine jekerun ana raχel
jatsaɬul was watʃʼun wuɡilan raɡʼidal lawan wekerana ɡʔobolasda dandtʃʼwaze karande qʼan ɡʔjesda qʼotʃardana wa ɡʔjew roqʼowe watʃana tsinɡi jaqʼubitsa ɡʔjesda kinabɡo kːara tarab bitsana
lawanitsa abuna
χʼaqʼɬunɡo mun dir ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi wuɡo jan
ɡʔjedin jaqʼubitsa lawanil bakʼalda motsʼ bana
tsinɡi lawanitsa ɡʔjesda abuna
mun dir ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi wuɡinɡi abun tʃʼowoɡo χʼaltʼizawize beɡʔilaro bitse dida kinab muχʔ duje kʔjeleb
lawanil jikʼana kʼiɡo jas kʼudijalda tsʼar bukʼana leja ɡʔitʼinalda raχel
lejal beral tsodaɡʔal zaɡʼipal rukʼana raχelin abuni laɡa tʃorχoɬanɡi ɡʔajbataj ɡʔumerɡi bertsinaj jas jikʼana
jaqʼubil raχeliqχ rokʔi kːana ɡʔjes lawanida abuna
dur ɡʔitʼinaj jas raχel dije kʔuni dun ankʔɡo sonaɬ χʼaltʼila duda tsewe jan
ɬikʼ buɡo jan abuna lawanitsa tʃijae kʔjejaldasa ɡʔjej duje kʔjej ɬikʼ ɡʔaniw tʃʼa durɡo
raχelije ɡʼolo ankʔɡo sonaɬ χʼaltʼana ɡʔjesda tsewe jaqʼub amma ɡʔjeb ankʔabɡo son kin arabali ɬatʃʼoɡo ana ɡʔjej jokʔulej jikʼindalχa ɡʔjesije
ɡʔale aχirɡi ɡʔjes lawanida abuna
dir χʼaltʼul sonal aχiralde ʃːwana ɡʔanʒe kʔje dije dir baχʼaraj jan
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ lawanitsa kinalɡo rosutsojalɡi aχʼun bertin ɡʔabuna
amma sordo rukʼkʼarab meχaɬ ɡʔjes jatʃun ʒindirɡo jas leja ʃːwezajuna jaqʼubiqχe wa jaqʼub ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡana
lejae raɡʔtʼatel χʼisabalda lawanitsa kʔuna ʒindirɡo ʁarawaʃ zilpa
sordo roɡʔana ɡʔale jaqʼubida tsee jiɡo leja
dutsa dije ɡʔaburab ʃːib raχelije ɡʼolo ɡurewiʃː dun duda tsewe χʼaltʼaraw ʃːaj dutsa dun ɡukːaraw in abuna jaqʼubitsa lawanida
kʼudijajɡi roqʼoj tun ɡʔitʼinaj jas rosase kʔoleb ɡʼadat ɡʔjetʃʼo niʒer raqχalda jan abuna lawanitsa
ɡʔab bertadul ankʔ arabɡo ɡʔitʼinajɡi kʔjela niʒetsa duje mun ʒeɡi ankʔɡo sonaɬɡi dida tsewe χʼaltʼani
jaqʼubitsa ɡʔjes abuqχe ɡʔabuna bertadul ankʔ arabɡo lawanitsa ɡʔjesije ʒindirɡo jas raχelɡi kʔuna
ɡʔjeɬije raɡʔtʼatelɬun ɡʔjes kʔuna ʒindirɡo ʁarawaʃ bilɡʔa
jaqʼub raχelida askʼow weɡana wa lejadasa tsʼikʼkʼun jokʔana ɡʔjesije ɡʔjej ʒeɡi ankʔɡo sonaɬɡi lawanida tsewe χʼaltʼana jaqʼub
leja jokʔulej ɡʔjetʃʼoɬiɡi biχʔun betʼjerhanas ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer kːezabuna raχelin abuni ɬimer ɬuɡʔunarejɬun ɡʔajuna
lejal urɡʔibe ɬimer ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjeɬ was ɡʔawuna wa ɡʔjesda tsʼar ruwim
dir paʃmanɬi betʼjerhanasda biχʔana jan abuna ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔanʒeni dun rosase jokʔila
ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe naqχeɡi ɬimer kːana tsoɡi was ɡʔawuna
dun jokʔulej ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi raɡʼana betʼjerhanasda jan abuna ɡʔjeɬ tsoɡi was kʔuna dije
tsinɡi ɡʔjew wasasda tsʼar ʃimeon ɬuna
naqχeɡi ɬimer kːana ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɡʔab nuχaɬɡi was ɡʔawuna
ɡʔanʒeni dideχun χurχen ʃːulaɬila dir rosasul in abuna ɡʔjeɬ ditsa ɡʔjesije ɬabɡo was ɡʔawidalχa
tsinɡi ɡʔjew wasasda tsʼar lewij ɬuna
tsoɡi nuχaɬ kːana ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer ɡʔanʒeɡi was ɡʔawuna
ɡʔanʒe ditsa betʼjerhanase retsː ɡʔabila jan abuna ɡʔjeɬ wa wasasda tsʼar jaɡʔuda ɬuna

jaqʼubije ʒintsaɡo ɬimer ɡʔabize baʒaruleb ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi biχʔun jatsaldeχun buɡeb ʒaχʼdajaɬ kwerde josun jikʼana raχel
dije ɬimal kʔje jaɡi dun χwela jan abuna ɡʔjeɬ jaqʼubida
jaqʼubil ɡʔjelda tsːin baqχana wa ɡʔjes abuna
dun allaɡʔiʃː wuɡew ɡʔjesɬidal duje ɬimal kʔolel ɡʔjetʃʼjel in
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjeɬ abuna
ɡʔale dir ʁarawaʃ bilɡʔa bitʃːante ɡʔjeɬ dir nakabazda ɬeze ɬimer ɡʔabize tsinɡi ɡʔjeldasan kːaralɡʼaɡi ɬimal rukʼina dir
ɡʔjedin raχelitsa ɡʔjesije kʔuna ʒindirɡo ʁarawaʃ bilɡʔa jaqʼubitsa ɡʔjejɡun busen ɡʼaχʔal ɡʔabize bajbiχʔana
ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana wa ɡʔjeɬ was ɡʔawuna
allaɡʔas χʼukmu qʼotʼana jan abuna raχelitsa dir ɡʔari duɡʼa qʼabul ɡʔabun was kʔuna dije
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjeɬ wasasda tsʼar dan ɬuna
raχelil ʁarawaʃ bilɡʔal urɡʔibe naqχeɡi ɬimer kːana wa jaqʼubije ɡʔjeɬ tsoɡi was ɡʔawuna
dirɡo jatsalda dande kutakalda qʼerkʔana dun wa aχirɡi berɡʔana jan abuna raχelitsa
wa ɡʔjeɬ wasasda tsʼar naftali ɬuna
ɡʔjeb zamanalda ʒindir tʼokʼab ɬimer bukʼunarilanɡi kːun lejatsa jaqʼubije ʒindirɡo ʁarawaʃ zilpa kʔuna
zilpatsaɡi kwatʼitʃʼoɡo jaqʼubije was ɡʔawuna
iqʼbal kːana jan abuna lejatsa
wa ɡʔjeɬ wasasda tsʼar ɡad ɬuna
zilpatsa jaqʼubije kʼiabilewɡi was ɡʔawuna
taliχʼ kːana jan abuna lejatsa taliχʼajilan abila dida rutʃːabaz
wa ɡʔjeɬ wasasda tsʼar aʃer ɬuna
tso nuχalda roɬ ɬiɬuleb ɡʼuʒalda ruwimida χurir ratana mandraɡorabi
dur wasasda rataral mandraɡorabi kʔje dije jan
dir ros dutsa dida kodosa waqχaraw ɡʼun ɡʔjetʃʼiʃː duje dir wasasda rataral mandraɡorabiɡijiʃː duje ɡʔanʒe qʼwariɡʼun ruɡel in abuna lejatsa
ɡʔjel mandraɡorabi dije kʔuni ditsa qʼasi ros duda askʼowe witʃːala jan abuna raχelitsa
qʼasi jaqʼub roqʼowe watʃʼuneb meχalda ɡʔjesda dande ana leja wa ɡʔjeɬ abuna
diqχe wiɬːa dir wasasda rataral mandraɡorabazuqχ χisun bosana ditsa jatsaɬuqχa qʼasi sordo
ɡʔjeb sordo jaqʼubitsa lejada askʼob bana
allaɡʔas qʼabul ɡʔabuna ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔari ɡʔanʒeɡi ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana wa ɡʔjeɬ jaqʼubije ʃːuabilewɡi was ɡʔawuna
rosase ditsa dirɡo ʁarawaʃ kʔjedal allaɡʔas dije ʃapaqʼat kʔuna jan abuna lejatsa
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjeɬ wasasda tsʼar isːaχar ɬuna
naqχeɡi lejal urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana wa ɡʔjeɬ jaqʼubije anɬabilew was ɡʔawuna
allaɡʔas kʼudijab barakat kʔuna dije ɡʔanʒeni rosas kʼodo ɡʔajila dun ditsa ɡʔjesije anɬɡo was ɡʔawidalχa jan abuna ɡʔjeɬ
wa ɡʔjeɬ wasasda tsʼar zewulun ɬuna
χadub lejae jasɡi ɡʔajuna wa ɡʔjelda tsʼar dina ɬuna
raχelidaɡi ɡurχʼana allaɡʔ wa ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔari qʼabul ɡʔabuna urɡʔibe ɬimer kːolejɬun ɡʔajuna ɡʔjejɡi
ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer ɬuɡʔana wa ɡʔjeɬ was ɡʔawuna tsinɡi raχelitsa abuna
allaɡʔas roɡʔo nitʃ tʼasa bosana didasa jan
betʼjerɡʔanas dije tsoɡi was kʔjeɡi janɡi abun ɡʔjeɬ wasasda tsʼar jusup
jusup ɡʔawurab meχalda jaqʼubitsa lawanida abuna
dirɡo ɬimalɡi wa ʒidee ɡʼolo dun duda tsewe χʼaltʼaral ɬudbiɡi ratʃun roqʼowe dirɡo watʼanalde tʼad wusːine iznu kʔje dije dudaɡo ɬalaχa kiɡʼan ɡʼjemer dun duda tsewe χʼaltʼarawali
lawanitsa abuna beɡʔuleb batani diqχ ɡʼjenekːe duje ɡʼolo dijeɡi betʼjerhanasul barakat ʃːun bukʼin bitʃʼtʃʼana dida
dije χʼaltʼaraɬuqχ dujeɡo bokʔarab muχʔ abe wa ditsa kʔjela ɡʔjeb in
jaqʼubitsa abuna
dudaɡo ɬala kin dun duda tsewe χʼaltʼarawali ditsa χʔiχʔun dur reqχabi kiɡʼan kʼodoɬaralali
ɡʼjemerab ɡʼi bukʼintʃʼo dur dun ɡʔaniwe watʃʼarab meχalda ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjezul ɡʼjemerɬi biχʔuliʃː ɡʔjele ɡʔjedin barakat ɬuna betʼjerhanas duda dun watʃʼaraldasa naqχe dirɡo qχizan ɬimalaze dun kida χʼaltʼize wuɡew
lawanitsa ɡʔiqʼana kinab uʒra muχʔχa duje bokʔun buɡeb in
jaqʼubitsa ʒawab kʔuna
dudasan dije ʃːibniɡi χʼaʒat ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔadinab qʼotʼijalda mun raziɬani ditsa ɡʔanʒejaldasa naqχeɡi χʔiχʔila dur ɡʼi wa ɡʔjeɬul tʼalabɡi ɡʔabila
ratʃʼa ʒaqʼa niɬ riɬːinin reqχabi riχʔize dutsa ɡʔjenisa naqχe ratʃe kinalɡo tʼankʼal ruɡelɡi tʃaralɡi tʃʼjeɡʼjeralɡi ɡʼijal wa ɡʔjedinɡo tʼankʼal ruɡelɡi tʃaralɡi tsʼtsʼani χadubkːun ɡʔjedinab tajpajaɬul ɡʼi tsʼani dije muχʔaɬe rukʼine ritʃːante
dir rakʼbatsʼtsʼaɬi ɬaze biɡʔa bukʼina duje ɡʔanʒejaldasa χadub dije muχʔdaqχ kʔurazda ɡʔorkʔob tʼankʼal ruɡelɡi tʃaralɡi ɡuroni tsʼtsʼani jaɡi tʃʼjeɡʼjerab kʔjer ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ɡʼi batani ɡʔjel dur riqʼaralɬun rikʼkʼine beɡʔila dutsa
ɡʔjeb qʼotʼijalda dun razi wuɡo jan abuna lawanitsa dutsa abuqχe bukʼine bitʃːante
ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ lawanitsa reqχaɬa ratʼa ɡʔaruna kinalɡo tʼankʼal ruɡelɡi tʃaralɡi duɡʼbi kinalɡo tʼankʼal ruɡelɡi tʃaralɡi aj qχaχʼtʃaral tsʼtsʼani kinalɡo tʃʼjeɡʼjeral ɡʼijal ratʃun ʒindirɡo ɬimalazuqχe kʔuna ɡʔjes ɡʔjel
wa jaqʼubil qʼaji tʃʼwarab bakʼaldasa ɬabɡo qʼojil nuχaɬ rikʼkʼadeɡʼan ana ɡʔjel lawanil tsoɡidal ɡʼi tsʼani χʔiχʔun jaqʼubɡi χutʼana
biɡʔarodul mindalaɬul tʃinaridul ʁutʼbuzul tsʼi kʼantsʼaral tʃʼoral qʼotʼana jaqʼubitsa wa ɡʔjezda tʼasa qχal baqχana tʃʼalal ɡʔarun bakʼbakʼaldasa qχaχʼab tsʼul bakːizeɡʼan
ɡʔjel tʃʼoral ɡʔjes ɬuna botsʼi ɡʔjeqʼoleb bakʼalda reqχen ɡʔjeqʼeze batʃʼarab meχalda kujdukʔje jaɡi daɡʼnikʔje ine qʼatʃʼaral ɡʼi tsʼanazda ɡʔjel riχʔuleb kutsalda
kujdukʔje jaɡi daɡʼnikʔje ine qʼatʃʼaral ɡʼi tsʼani ɡʔjel tʃʼalal ɡʔarun qχal tʼasa baqχaral tʃʼorazuqχ ralaɡʔulaan wa ɡʔjezije ɡʔarulaan tʼankʼal ruɡel wa tʃaral kʔaɡʼi burtʼal
jaqʼubitsa ratʼa ɡʔarulaan tʃaralɡi tʃʼjeɡʼjeralɡi ɡʼi tsʼani wa lawanil ɡʼi tsʼanazdasa batʼaɡo χʔiχʔulaan ɡʔjedinab χʼalalda jaqʼubil ʒiwɡo betʼjerɡʔanal reqχabi ɡʼolel rukʼana
kʔarijal wa tʃʼaχʼijal ɡʼi tsʼani kujdukʔje jaɡi daɡʼnikʔje uneb zamanalda jaqʼubitsa ɡʔjel tʃʼoral ɬim ɡʔjeqʼoleb bakʼalda ɬolaan ɡʔjezda riχʔuleb bakʼalda ɡʔjel tʃʼorazda askʼor ɡʔjel tʼade kʼantsʼize
χʼalaqʼal qʼadarazde kʼantsʼuleb zamanalda ɡʔjes tʃʼoral naqχe rosulaan ɡʔjedin χʼalaqʼab qʼadarab ɡʼi lawanije unaan kʔarijab tʃʼaχʼijab ɡʼi jaqʼubije ʃːolaan
kutakalda betʃedaw tʃi ɬuɡʔana jaqʼub ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjesul rukʼana ɡʼijazulɡi tsʼtsʼanazulɡi reqχabi ʁarawaʃal wa laʁzal waranabi wa χʼamul

ʒindir χʼaqʼaɬuɬ lawanil wasaz ɡʔadin abuleb bukʼin raɡʼana jaqʼubida
niɬer insul bukʼarabʃːinab betʃeɬi kwerde bosanaɡuri jaqʼubitsa insul botsʼi riqʼzijaldaɬun betʃeɬaraw tʃi wuɡo dow
jaqʼubida ʒindaɡoɡi biχʔuleb bukʼana dob tsebe ɡʼadab ɡʔuinɬi ɡʔorkʔobɬi lawanil ʒindeχun ɡʔjetʃʼjebɬi
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas jaqʼubida abuna
durɡo umumuzul rakʔalde wa durɡo ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬuqχe tʼad wusːa ditsa duje kumek ɡʔabila
jaqʼubitsa raχelideɡi lejadeɡi ruɡʔjel bitʼana reqχabi kwanaleb ɡʼalaχalde ratʃʼajilan
tsinɡi ɡʔjes ɡʔjezda abuna
nuʒer emen ɡʔanʒe diqχ tsewe ɡʼadin walaɡʔulew ɡʔjetʃʼjewɬi biχʔuleb buɡo dida amma dir insutsa ɡʼibadat ɡʔabulew allaɡʔas dun reχun tetʃʼo
nuʒeda ɬala ruχʼɡi ʒanɡi kʔun χʼaltʼana dun nuʒer insuda tsewe
amma ɡʔjes dun ɡukːana wa dije biχʔizaburab muχʔɡi tʃamaliɡo nuχaɬ χisizabuna ɡʼitsʼɡo allaɡʔas bitʃːatʃʼo ɡʔjes dije kweʃɬi ɡʔabize
nuʒer insutsa dida abuni tʼankʼal ruɡel duje muχʔaɬe kʔjelilan kinabɡo tʼintʃʼ tʼankʼal ruɡeb ɬuɡʔunaan tʃaralʃːinal duje muχʔaɬe kʔjelilan ɡʔjes aburab meχalda kinabɡo tʼintʃʼ tʃarab ɬuɡʔunaan
ɡʔjele ɡʔjedin nuʒer insuqχaɡi raqχun allaɡʔas dije kʔuna reqχabi
tso nuχalda ɡʼi dande bitʃːarab zamanalda makʔu biχʔana dida ɡʔjeb makʔiɬ tsʼtsʼanaɬe ritʃːaral kinalɡo duɡʼbi tʼankʼal ruɡel jaɡi tʃaral rukʼana
jaqʼub in aχʼana makʔiɬ allaɡʔasul malaikas dide ja abun ʒawab kʔuna ditsa
tsinɡi ɡʔjes dida abuna
riχʔuliʃː tsʼtsʼanazde kʼantsʼulel ruɡel kinalɡo duɡʼbi ruɡo ja tʼankʼal ruɡel jaɡi tʃaral dida biχʔuleb buɡo lawanitsa duje ɡʔaburabʃːinab
dun wuɡo doba bet ejelalda eχetarab ɡantʃʼide zajtunaɬul naχɡi tʼun mun dije ɡʔjedaraw allaɡʔ ɡʔanʒe ɡʔab ulkajaldasa naqχe a mun durɡo ɡʼaɡarab rakʔalde tʼadwusːa jan
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ raχelitsaɡi lejatsaɡi jaqʼubida abuna
insul mulkaldasan niʒee kinabɡʼaɡi butʼa buɡebiʃː
tʃijar tʃaɡʼazdeχun ɡʼadab ɡurebiʃː ɡʔjesul niʒedeχun berbalaɡʔi buɡeb ɡʔjes ritʃana niʒ wa niʒee kʔjeze kːoleb bukʼarabɡi ʒintsaɡo kwanana
ɡʔajɡʔaj allaɡʔas niʒer insuqχa baqχarabʃːinab botsʼi betʃeɬijaɬul betʼjerɡʔabi ruɡo niɬɡi niɬer ɬimalɡi ɡʔjedinɬidal allaɡʔas duda abuqχe ɡʔabe
jaqʼubitsa ɬimalɡi ɬudbiɡi waranabazda rekʼinaruna wa
ʒindirɡo paddan aramalda ʃːwarab kinabɡo betʃeɬiɡi bakʼa baχarun ɡʼi botsʼul reqχabiɡi tsere qʼotʼun ʒindirɡo emen isχʼaqʼiqχe χanaanalde ine nuχda waqχana
ɡʔjeb zamanalda lawan roqʼow wukʼintʃʼo ɡʼi qʼuntsʼize un wukʼana raχelitsajin abuni insul rukʼaral ruqʼaɬul allaɡʔzabi riqʼana
ɡʔjedin aramejaw lawanɡi toχɬizawun ʃːibniɡi ɡʔjesdaɡi abitʃʼoɡo ana jaqʼub
ʒindijeɡo ʃːwarab kinabɡo botsʼi riqʼziɡi bosun jefrat ɡʼorɡi baχun ɡilɡʼadaɬul muɡʼruzdeχun walaɡʔun qʼoqʼana ɡʔjew
ɬababileb qʼojaɬ lawaniqχe χabar ʃːwana jaqʼub naqχe un wuɡilan
ʒindirɡo ɡʼaɡaral tʃaɡʼiɡi ratʃun lawan jaqʼubida χaduw ɬuɡʔana wa ankʔɡo qʼojaldasan ɡilɡʼadaɬul muɡʼruzda ɡʔjesda χaduw ɡʼuntʼana
ɡʔjeb sordojaɬ makʔiɬ allaɡʔas aramejaw lawanida abuna
wore dutsa jaqʼubida ja ɬikʼab ja kweʃab ʃːibniɡi abuɡe jan
lawan ɡʔanʒe jaqʼub wuɡeb bakʼalde ɡʼaɡarɬun wukʼana jaqʼub ɡilɡʼadaɬul muɡʼruzda reʃːtʼun wukʼana ɡʔjesda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ lawanɡi tʃʼana ʒindirɡo tʃaɡʼiɡun tsadaqχ
lawanitsa jaqʼubide aχʼana
dutsa ɡʔaburab ʃːib dutsa ɡukːanaɡuri dun raʁda asirɬude rosaral tʃaɡʼi ɡʼadin dir jasal qχamulel ruɡo dutsa
didasa baɬɡo ʃːaj mun araw ʃːibniɡi dida tsʼarɡi baqχitʃʼoɡo kʼudijab roχalida ʒerʁen kʼutʼun baqʼnal ratʃun awadanal kutʃʼdulɡi aχʼulaɡo tʼowitʼilaanɡuri ditsa mun
dir jasazulɡun wa ɡʔjezul ɬimalazulɡun qʼo ɬikʼ ɡʔabizetsin res kʔjetʃʼo dutsa dije ɡʼantab ʒojin dutsa ɡʔaburab
ditsa ɡʔjeɬuqχ ɬikʼɡo retsʼjel bosilaan dudasa amma noɬ dur insul allaɡʔas abuna dida wore dutsa jaqʼubije ʃːibniɡi ɡʔabuɡe jan
ɡʔa ɡʔanʒe un wuɡo mun in kʼaɬana naqχeɡi lawan mun dida askʼosa naqχe un watize beɡʔula durɡo insul roqʼobe rakʼʃːun bukʼun amma dir allaɡʔzabi ʃːaj riqʼaral dutsa
χʼinqʼun wukʼana dun dutsa χʼal ɡʔabun durɡo jasal diqχa naqχe ratʃinilan rakʼaldeɡi kːun in ʒawab kʔuna lawanije jaqʼubitsa
amma dur allaɡʔzabi kodor rataraw tʃijase ɡʼumru bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo nuɡʼɬijaɬe ɡʔjel niɬer ɡʼaɡaral tʃaɡʼiɡi tʃʼjezarun tʃʼuχʔ baj dir ɡʔanib buɡebʃːinaɬul mun betʼjerɡʔanab ʒo batani naqχe bose
jaqʼubida ɬaleb bukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjel allaɡʔzabi raχelitsa riqʼun rukʼin
lawanitsa tʃʼuχʔ bana jaqʼubil lejal wa kʼijajɡo ʁarawaʃaɬul tʃadrazuqχ amma ʃːibniɡi batitʃʼo ɡʔjenib lejal tʃadiraɬusa raχelil tʃadiraɬuwe wiɬːana ɡʔjew
raχelitsa ɡʔjel ruqʼaɬul allaɡʔzabi waranidul kʔoloda ʒanir raχtʃana ʒijɡoɡi ɡʔjelda tʼad ɡʼodoj tʃʼana insutsa ɡʔjeɬul tʃadiraɬubɡi tʃʼuχʔ bana amma ʃːibɡo batitʃʼo
raχelitsa ɡʔjesda abuna
dur dida tsːin baqχuɡe dir emen duda tsee jaqχun tʃʼjeze beɡʔuleb χʼal ɡʔjetʃʼo dir rutʃːabazul bukʼuneb ɡʼuzru χʼajiz ɬuɡʔun buɡo
lawanitsa kinabɡo beɡa bitʼana amma allaɡʔzabi ratitʃʼo
ɡʔanʒe jaqʼubil kutakalda tsːin baqχana lawanida wa ɡʔjesda kʼalɡʔiqʼize ɬuɡʔana
ʃːaj mun dida χaduw ɬuɡʔaraw ʃːib ɡʼajib bukʼun ʃːib taqʼsir bukʼun
dutsa dir kinabɡo qʼaji beɡa bitʼana mun betʼjerɡʔanab ʒo ʃːibχa duda ɡʔjenib batarab biχʔizabe durɡo dur ɡʼaɡaral tʃaɡʼaz niɬee diwan qʼotʼize
qʼoɡo sonaɬ χʼaltʼana dun duda tsewe tsoniɡi tʃaqχdatsa jaɡi tsʼtsʼjetsa tʼintʃʼ reχize bitʃːatʃʼoɡo weχʔɬi ɡʔabuna dur reqχaɬa kujdul qχun ɡʔanɡi ditsa kwanatʃʼo
naɡaɡʔ reqχaɬ qχumur retʃʼtʃʼun tʃaqχu tsʼtsʼje tʃʼwani ɡʔjebɡi bosun duda askʼowe watʃʼintʃʼo ditsaɡo betsʼana qʼad tʼaɡʼaraɬuqχɡi qʼasi biqʼaraɬuqχɡi retsʼjel tʼalab ɡʔabuna dutsa didasa
qʼad baqʼutsa workʔulaan qʼasi kwatʃaɬ ɡʼazab kʔun ber dande batʃunaroan
qʼoɡo son ana ɡʔjedin duda askʼob antsʼila unqʼɡo sonaɬ χʼaltʼana dur jasaze qχalimaɬe anɬɡo sonaɬ dijeɡo ɡʼi ɡʼjezabizeɡi χʼaltʼana antsʼɡo nuχaɬ χis χisizabuna dutsa dije biχʔizaburab muχʔɡi
dir insulɡi ibraɡʔimilɡi allaɡʔas isχʼaqʼ ʒindikʔa χʼinqʼulew allaɡʔas dije kumek ɡʔabitʃʼjebani dutsa dun tʃʼowoɡo naqχe witʼilaan amma allaɡʔasda biχʔana ditsa χʼjeχʔarab qʼwariɬiɡi batʃːarab zaχʼmatɡi ʒiwɡo allaɡʔ waqχana noɬ dije χʼalaje
lawanitsa jaqʼubida abuna
ɡʔal rutʃːabiɡi dir jasal ruɡo ɬimalɡi dir ɬimalazul ɬimal ɡʔal reqχabiɡi dir ɡʔab kinabɡo dur berda tsebe buɡeb betʃeɬiɡi dir dirɡo jasalɡi ɡʔjezul ɬimalɡi ditsa qʼwarid ɡʔariliʃː
ɡʔjedinɬidal ratʃʼa niɬetsa qʼotʼi qʼaj ɡʔabize ɡʔjeɬije nuɡʼɡi bukʼine bitʃːante
ɡʔjebmeχalda jaqʼubitsa tso kʼudijab ɡamatʃʼ baqχun tʃʼjezabuna
wa ɡantʃʼal rakʼarejan abuna ʒindirɡo ɡʼaɡaral tʃaɡʼazda
ɡʔjez rakʼarun ɡantʃʼazul ɡoχʼ ɬuɡʔinabuna wa ɡʔjelda askʼob kwanaze ɡʼodor tʃʼjeze bakʼɡi qʼatʃʼana
lawanitsa ɡʔjeb ɡoχʼalda tsʼar ɬuna jeɡar saχaduta jaqʼubitsa ɬuna ɡal ed
lawanitsa abuna
niɬer qʼotʼijaɬul nuɡʼ buɡo ɡʔab ɡoχʼ in
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjeb ɡoχʼalda tsʼar buɡo ɡal ed
tsoɡidab tsʼar buɡo mitspa
tsotsazdasa niɬ ratʼaɬarab wa rikʼkʼaɬarab meχaɬ bitʃːante betʼjerhanas niɬeda χadub χal kːweze
dutsa dir jasal qʼwarid ɡʔaruni jaɡi ɡʔazda tʼade ɬudbi ratʃani duda ɬan bukʼa insan ɡurew allaɡʔ wukʼina niɬee nuɡʼɬun
tsinɡi lawanitsa jaqʼubida abuna
ɡʔab ɡantʃʼazul ɡoχʼaɬuqχɡi niɬeda ɡʔorkʔob ditsa baqχun tʃʼjezaburab ɡantʃʼiqχɡi walaɡʔje
ɡʔjel ruɡo niɬer qʼotʼijaɬul nuɡʼzal kweʃab qʼasdɡun dun watʃʼinaro ɡʔab ɡoχʼɡi baχun dur raqχaldeχun munɡi kweʃab qʼasdɡun watʃʼunɡe ɡʔab ɡoχʼɡi muqʼadasab ɡamatʃʼɡi baχun dir raqχaldeχun
bitʃːante ibraɡʔimilɡi naχorilɡi ɡʔjezul insulɡi allaɡʔas diwan qʼotʼize niɬeda ɡʔorkʔob
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ jaqʼub ɡʔjedana ʒindirɡo emen isχʼaqʼ χʼinqʼulew allaɡʔasul tsʼarɡi baqχun
χadub jaqʼubitsa ɡʔjenib maɡʼarda qʼurban qχuna wa kinabɡo ɡʼaɡarɬi kwanaze aχʼana kwananɡi raqχun sordo baze ɡʔjenir tʃʼana ɡʔjel
radal lawanitsa ʒindirɡo jasazulɡun wa ɡʔjezul ɬimalazulɡun qʼo ɬikʼ ɡʔabuna ɡʔjezije barakatɡi ɡʔarun ɡʔjezda ubatʃal ɡʔaruna wa roqʼowe naqχwusːun ana

ɡʔjedin nuχda unaɡo allaɡʔasul malaikzabi dande kːana jaqʼubida
ɡʔjel riχʔidal jaqʼubitsa abuna
allaɡʔasul bojaɬ urdu tʃʼwarab bakʼ biχʔula ɡʔab in wa ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tsʼar ɬuna maχanaim
ʒindirɡo wats ɡʼisawiqχe edomaɬul ulkajalde seiraɬul rakʔalde tʃaparzabi tsere ritʼana jaqʼubitsa
ʒindir betʼjerɡʔan ɡʼisawida ɡʔadin abejilan tʼadqʼajɡun
dur laʁ jaqʼubitsa ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo ɡʔanʒeɬizeɡʼan lawanida askʼob ɡʼumru ɡʔabuna ditsa
ɡʔanʒe dir ruɡo otsalɡi χʼamulɡi ɡʼi tsʼaniɡi laʁzalɡi ʁarawaʃalɡi ditsa bitʼuleb buɡo duqχe dirɡo betʼjerɡʔanasuqχe ɡʔab χabar dideχun dur rakʼ ɬikʼɬililan χʔulɡun
tʼadrusːun ratʃʼun tʃaparzabaz jaqʼubida abuna
niʒ dur wats ɡʼisawiqχe ʃːwana ɡʔanʒe unqʼnusɡo tʃiɡun tsadaqχ duda dande watʃʼunew wuɡo dow
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ kʼudijab χʼinqʼi reʃːtʼana jaqʼubil rekʼjeɬe urʁalabaz tʃʼwalew ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo ɡʼadamalɡi ɡʼi botsʼiɡi waranabiɡi kʼijide rikʔana wa kʼiɡo batʼijab bakʼalda tʃʼjezaruna
tso qʼawude ɡʼisaw tʼade kʼantsʼani jan pikru ɡʔabuna jaqʼubitsa tsoɡidab qʼawuda ruɡelalɡʼaɡi ɬutun rortʃʼila
tsinɡi jaqʼubitsa duɡʼa ɡʔabuna
ja χirijaw allaɡʔ dir kʼudijaw emen ibraɡʔimilɡi dir emen isχʼaqʼilɡi allaɡʔ roqʼowe ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬuqχe tʼadwusːajilan dije amru ɡʔaburaw wa dije χʼalaje waqχine raɡʼi kʔuraw betʼjerhan
naqχasa qʼotʼitʃʼoɡo dutsa dide durɡo laʁasde reʃːtʼinaburab barakataɬeɡi dur raχʼmujaɬeɡi mustaχʼiqʼaw ɡʔjetʃʼo dun ɡʔab iordan ɡʼor baχarab meχaɬ dir qχatikʔ ɡʼansa ɡuroni bukʼintʃʼo ɡʔanʒe dir kʼiɡo qʼawujaɬe ɡʼurab ɡʼi botsʼi buɡo
ɡʔarula duda dir wats ɡʼisawidasa χwasar ɡʔawe dun dun χʼinqʼun wuɡo watʃʼun ɡʔjes rutʃːabiɡun ɬimalɡun tsadaqχ niʒ kinalɡo ʁurililan
dutsa dije raɡʼi kʔun bukʼindal dida barakat ɬelilan wa raɬdal saliɡʼanɡi ɡʼjemer naslabi didasan ɬuɡʔinarililan
jaqʼubitsa sordo ɡʔjenib bana wa ɡʼisawije sajʁataɬe kʔjeze ʒindirɡo reqχabaɬa tʼasa riʃːun ratʼa ɡʔaruna
kʼinusɡo tsʼtsʼje qʼoɡo deɡʼjen kʼinusɡo tʃaqχu qʼoɡo kuj
ɬeberɡo betʃʼtʃʼuleb warani wa ɡʔjezul tʼantʃʼi kʼiqʼoɡo ɡʼaka antsʼɡo ots qʼoɡo tsʼuχʼama wa antsʼɡo biχʔinχʼama
ɡʔjes ɡʔjel laʁzaderida tsere ʁuna ʃːibab reqχaduj tso tso weχʔ kːoleb χʼalaɬ tsinɡi ɡʔjezda abuna
ɡʔanʒe nuʒ tsere tsere a tsotsazda ɡʔorkʔob manzilɡi tun
dir wats ɡʼisaw dandtʃʼwarab meχaɬ in abuna jaqʼubitsa biʃːunɡo tsewe witʼulew wuɡew weχʔasda dos duda ɡʔiqʼila mun ɬil laʁ kiwe unew tʃi ɡʔab duda tsebe buɡeb botsʼi ɬil abun
dutsa ʒawab kʔje dur laʁ jaqʼubil botsʼi buɡo ɡʔab ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo betʼjerɡʔan ɡʼisawije sajʁataɬe bitʼarab ʒiwɡo jaqʼubɡi χadu χaduw watʃʼunew wuɡo jan
ɡʔjelɡo raɡʼabi abejin ɡʼisawidajan amru ɡʔabuna jaqʼubitsa kʼiabilew weχʔasdeɡi ɬababilesdeɡi wa tsoɡidazdeɡi
tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo tʼade ʒubaj dur laʁ jaqʼubɡi χadu χaduw watʃʼunew wuɡo jan ɬazabuna ɡʔjes ɡʼuχʔbuzda
ɡʔjedin tsere ritʼaral sajʁataz ɡʼisaw ʒindaɡo ɡurχʼizawilarodajan χʔul bukʼana jaqʼubil tsinɡi dunɡoɡi ɡʔjesda askʼowe ʃːwarab meχaɬ dida ɬikʼab dandtʃʼwaj ɡʔabizeɡi beɡʔula ɡʔjes jan pikru ɡʔabuna jaqʼubitsa
ɡʔjedin sajʁatalɡi tsere ritʼun jaqʼub ʒindirɡo qʼaji tʃʼwarab bakʼalda sordo baze tʃʼana
ɡʔjeb sordojaɬ jaqʼubitsa kʼijajɡo ɬadiɡi kʼijajɡo ʁarawaʃɡi antsʼila tso wasɡi tʼade raqχinaruna wa ɡʔjezda jabbok ɡʼor baχinabuna
ɡʔjel kinalɡo ɡʔjes ɡʼurul dob tsojab raɡʼalde ʃːwezaruna ʒindirɡo kinabɡo betʃeɬiɡun tsadaqχ
ʒiwɡo ɡʔab raqχalda tʃʼana
wa tso ʃːiwaliɡo qʼerkʔjeze ɬuɡʔana ɡʔawɡun tʼubarab sordo ana ɡʔjedin
jaqʼub qʼurkʔizawize kʼolew ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi biχʔun ɡʔjew ɡʔjesul matʃʼalda qχwana wa rakʔajaldasa ʃːekʼ batʼaɬizabuna
tsinɡi ɡʔjes jaqʼubida abuna
dun witʃːante qχaχʼɬi baleb buɡin
dije barakat kʔjetʃʼoɡo witʃːalaro jan ʒawab kʔuna jaqʼubitsa
duda tsʼar ʃːib an ɡʔiqʼana ɡʔjes
jaqʼub buɡo
tsinɡi ɡʔjes abuna
ɡʔanʒejaldasa χadub mun jaqʼub ɡuro ɡʼizrail
dur tsʼarɡi bitseχa dida jan ɡʔarana jaqʼubitsa
dir tsʼar ɬan ʃːaj duje jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjes
tsinɡi ɡʔjes jaqʼubida barakat ɬuna
ɡʔjeb iʃ kːarab bakʼalda tsʼar peni el
baqʼ bakːuleb bukʼana jaqʼub peni elaldasa naqχe uneb meχaɬ wa ɡʔjew reqʼdulew wukʼana
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʼizrailil naslabazul ɡʼadamaz ɡʼi botsʼul matʃʼalzul ɡʔan kunaro dow qχwajdalχa jaqʼubil matʃʼalda

tsewe walaɡʔidal jaqʼubida rikʼkʼadasanɡo ɡʼisaw wiχʔana ʒinda dande watʃʼunew unqʼnusɡo tʃiɡun tsadaqχ jaqʼubitsa lejalɡi raχelilɡi wa kʼijajɡo ʁarawaʃaɬulɡi ɬimalazda ɬazabuna ʒiderɡo ulbuzda askʼor raqχun tʃʼajan
ɡʔadin tʃʼjezaruna ɡʔjes ɡʔjel biʃːunɡo tsere ʁarawaʃalɡi ɡʔjezul ɬimalɡi ɡʔjezda naqχa lejaɡi ɡʔjeɬul ɬimalɡi ɡʔjezdaɡi naqχa raχelɡi jusupɡi
ʒiwɡo jaqʼub tsewe watʃʼana wa watsasde ɡʼaɡarɬilalde ankʔɡo nuχaɬ qʼulana ɡʔjesije ɡʼodob nodoɡi tsun
amma ɡʼisaw ɡʔjesda askʼowe kʼantsʼun watʃʼana qʼwalɡi ban karande qʼana wa ubatʃ ɡʔabuna tsinɡi kʼijalɡo ɡʼodana
rutʃːabiɡi ɬimalɡi riχʔidal ɡʼisawitsa ɡʔiqʼana
ɡʔal kinalɡo ʃːal duje kːolel in
jaqʼubitsa ʒawab kʔuna
dur laʁase allaɡʔas tsʼob ɬun ɡʔarural ɬimal ruɡo ɡʔal
ʁarawaʃal ʒiderɡo ɬimalɡun tsadaqχ tsere ratʃʼana wa ɡʼisawije qʼulana
tsinɡi ʒindirɡo ɬimalɡi ratʃun leja askʼoje jatʃʼana wa ɡʔjesda tsee qʼulana biʃːun aχiralda raχelɡi qʼulana ɡʔjesije jusupɡun tsadaqχ
dida dande kːaral ɡʔadal reqχabi tsere ritʼijaɬul maɡʼna ʃːib abun ɡʔiqʼana ɡʼisawitsa
mun ɡurχʼilarodajilan ritʼun rukʼana dir betʼjerɡʔan abun ʒawab kʔuna jaqʼubitsa
ɡʼunɡi tʼokʼab betʃeɬi buɡo wats dir an abuna ɡʼisawitsa durɡo botsʼi dujeɡo te
ɡʔarula dideχun dur rakʼ batsʼtsʼadab batani ɡʔal dir sajʁatal naqχtʃʼwaɡe jan abuna jaqʼubitsa mun ɡʔjedin ɬikʼ dandtʃʼwajdal allaɡʔ wiχʔijalda baʃːaɬana dije ɡʔjeb
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔarula duda qʼabul ɡʔare dir sajʁatal allaɡʔas dije ɡʼjemerab botsʼi riqʼzi kʔuna kinabɡo ɡʼunɡi tʼokʼaɬ buɡo dir
jaqʼubitsa ɡʔara kʼatʃun ɡʼisaw raziɬana ɡʔjesul sajʁatal rosize
χadub ɡʼisawitsa abuna
ɡʔanʒe nuχda raqχun ɬikʼ dun duda tsadaqχ wiɬːina
amma jaqʼubitsa abuna
duda ɬalaχa dir betʼjerɡʔan ɬimal zaɡʼipal ʒal rukʼunebɬi ɡʔjedinɡo retʃʼtʃʼulel tʃaqχabiɡi ɡʼatʃiɡi ruɡo niʒeda tsadaqχ kʔabun ɡʔjel tsere ratʃani ʁob qʼojaɬɡo ɡʼodor kːun χwela
mun dir betʼjerɡʔan tsewe un ɬikʼ dun dur laʁ botsʼiɡi ɬimalɡi ratʃun baʒaruleb χʼalaɬ biɡʔa ɡʔawun χaduw watʃʼina duqχe dir betʼjerɡʔanasuqχe seiralde
tsinɡi ɡʼisawitsa abuna
ratʃʼa ditsa dir ɡʼadamazdasan tso qʼoqʼa duda tsadaqχ telin an
amma jaqʼubitsa ʒawab ɡʔabuna
ʃːaj dir betʼjerɡʔan dideχun ɬikʼ wukʼinɡi ɡʼun buɡo dije
tsinɡi ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬɡo ɡʼisaw naqχwusːun seiralde ana
jaqʼubɡi sukːotaldeχun walaɡʔun ana ɡʔjenir ɡʔjes rana ʒindijeɡo minaɡi botsʼuje tʼadqχelalɡi ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tsʼar buɡo sukːot
paddan aramaldasa waqχaraw jaqʼub saχ salamatɡo ʃːwana χanaanalda buɡeb ʃeχem ʃaɡʔaralde wa ɡʔjeniw ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ tʃʼana
χamoril wasazuqχa ɡʼartsul nusɡo ʃekelɡi kʔun jaqʼubitsa ʒindijeɡo rakʔ bosana χamor wukʼana ʃeχemil emen
ɡʔjenib ɡʔjes qʼurbanaɬe bakʼ bana wa ɡʔjelda tsʼarɡi el eloɡʔje ɡʼizrail

jaqʼubilɡi lejalɡi jas dina jiɬːana tso qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeb bakʼaɬul jasalɡun ɬaj qχwaj ɡʔabize
ɡʔjeb ulkajaɬul χan χiwijaw χamoril was ʃeχemida jiχʔana ɡʔjej wa kːun jatʃun basra ɡʔajuna
ɡʔjeldasa χadub dinaqχ kutakalda rokʔi kːana ɡʔjesul ɡʔjelda χʼjerenɡo ɡarɡadize ʒuwana
wa ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo emen χamorida abuna
ɡʔaj jas dije jatʃe jan
jaqʼubida ɬana ʒindir jas dina basra ɡʔajun jikʼin ɡʔjeb zamanalda ɡʔjesul wasal botsʼi χʔiχʔun ɡʼalaχalda rukʼana ɡʔjel ratʃʼineɡʼan siχʼ qʼotʼun tʃʼana jaqʼub
ɡʔjebɡo zamanalda ʃeχemil emen χamor watʃʼana jaqʼubiqχe ɡʔjesda kʼaɬaze
kːarab ʒo ɬarab saɡʼataldaɡo jaqʼubil wasalɡi roqʼore ratʃʼana kutakalda tsːidaχun rukʼana ɡʔjel ʃːajɡureɬul ʃeχemitsa jaqʼubil jasɡi basra ɡʔajun kʼudijab roɡʔo batʃana ɡʼizrailide kutakalda inʒitab qʼabiχʼab ʒo ɡʔabuna ɡʔjes
χamoritsa abuna
dir was ʃeχem nuʒer jasaɬ χʼajran ɡʔawun wuɡo ɡʔjej ɡʔjesije kʔjejilan ɡʔarize watʃʼun wuɡo dun
niɬeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼaɡarɬiɡi ɬuɡʔina nuʒer jasal niʒer wasazeɡi kʔjela niʒer jasal nuʒer wasazɡi ratʃina
niʒeda askʼor ɡʔanir tʃʼa ɡʔab niʒer ulka nuʒeda tsebe buɡo erkenɡo jaʃaw ɡʔabe daran bazaralde rusːa wa botsʼi betʃeɬi tsʼikʼkʼinabe
ʃeχemitsa dinal insudaɡi watsazdaɡi abuna
nuʒetsa dun qʼabul ɡʔawuni ditsa nuʒee ʃːib bokʔaniɡi kʔjela
biʃːun kʼudijab qχalimɡi tʃʼjezabe baχʼaraɬuqχ biʃːun betʃedal sajʁatalɡi tʼalab ɡʔare kinabɡo kʔjela ɡʼitsʼɡo ɡʔjej jas kʔje dije
ɡʔanʒe ʃeχemijeɡi ɡʔjesul emen χamorijeɡi jaqʼubil wasaz siχʼirab ʒawab kʔuna ʃeχemitsa ɡʔjezul jats dina basra ɡʔajun jiɡeɬul
ɡʔjeb ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize kʼolaro niʒeda jan abuna ɡʔjez niʒee roɡʔo nitʃ buɡo sunnat ɡʔabitʃʼjew tʃijase niʒer jats kʔjej
niʒ raziɬize kːani tso ʃartʼ buɡo ɡʔjelda ɡʔorkʔob nuʒer kinalɡo biχʔinazɡi sunnat ɡʔabize kːola niʒeda reɬːine
ɡʔjeldasa χadub niʒetsa niʒerɡo jasal nuʒer wasazeɡi kʔjela wa nuʒer jasal niʒeeɡoɡi ratʃina tsinɡi niʒɡi nuʒeda askʼor ɡʔanir tʃʼjela wa nuʒeda tsadaqχ tso χalqʼɬun ɬuɡʔina
amma nuʒ niʒeqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼoni wa sunnatɡi ɡʔabitʃʼoni niʒerɡo jatsɡi jatʃun niʒ naqχe ina ɡʔanisa
χamoridaɡi ʃeχemidaɡi ɬikʼ biχʔana ɡʔjeb
naqχbaqχitʃʼoɡo tʼubazabuna ʃeχemitsa ɡʔjez tʼalab ɡʔaburab ʒo kutakalda jaqʼubil jas jokʔun jikʼindal ɡʔjesije ɡʔjew ʃeχemin abuni insul tuχum kʔibilalda ʒaniw biʃːunɡo qʼadru qʼimat buɡew tʃi wukʼana
ɡʔale ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabazuqχɡi tʃʼun χamoritsaɡi ʃeχemitsaɡi ʃaɡʔaraɬul χalqʼalde χitʼab ɡʔabuna
ɡʔal ɡʼadamazdasan ʃːibɡo χʼinqʼi ɡʔjetʃʼo niɬee ritʃːante ɡʔal niɬer rakʔalda tʃʼjeze wa ɡʔjez erkenɡo maɡʼiʃat ɡʔabize ɡʔjezije rakʔ ɡʼjezeɡʼan buɡo ɡʔanib niɬetsa ɡʔjezul jasal ratʃina ɡʔjezije niɬerɡo jasalɡi kʔjela
amma niɬeda askʼor tʃʼjeze wa niɬeda tsadaqχ tsoɡo χalqʼɬun ɬuɡʔine ɡʔal raziɬulel ruɡo ɡʔadinab ʃartʼaldaɬun ɡʔjezul biχʔinalɡo ɡʼadin niɬer biχʔinalɡi sunnat ɡʔabural rukʼine kːola
ɡʔjezul reqχabiɡi ɡʔjezul betʃeɬiɡi ɡʔjezul botsʼiɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo niɬer bukʼinariʃːχa ɡʔjezul ʃartʼ niɬetsa qʼabul ɡʔabuni wa ɡʔjel niɬɡun ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼani
kawabazuqχe ɡodekʼanire ratʃʼun rukʼaralʃːinal χamoritsaɡi ʃeχemitsaɡi bitsaralda raziɬana wa ʃaɡʔaraɬul kinalɡo biχʔinaz sunnat ɡʔabuna
amma ɬababileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjel untun busada rukʼaɡo jaqʼubil wasal aj dinal watsal ʃimeonɡi lewijɡi raqχun χwaltʃabiɡun toχɬukʔje ʃaɡʔaralda ʒanire ɬuɡʔana wa tso χutʼitʃʼoɡo ɡʔjezul biχʔinal tʃʼwana
χwaltʃatsa qχuna ɡʔjez χamorɡi ʃeχemɡi wa ʃeχemil roqʼosa dinaɡi jatʃun naqχe ana
tsinɡi jaqʼubil wasaz talawur ɡʔabuna ʒider jats basra ɡʔajurab ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔar
ɡʔjez ɡʔjenisa qχamuna ɡʼi botsʼi χʼamul wa ʃaɡʔaraldaɡi maʁiɬɡi batarabʃːinab kinabɡo ʒideeɡo bosana
ʃaɡʔaraɬul ɡʼadamazul bukʼarab kinabɡo betʃeɬi qχamal ɡʔabuna ɡʔjezul ɬimalɡi rutʃːabiɡi asir ɡʔaruna wa ɡʔjezul roqʼob bukʼarabʃːinabɡi bosana
tsinɡi jaqʼubitsa ʃimeonidaɡi lewijidaɡi abuna
dir betʼjeralde balaɡʔ batʃana nuʒetsa ɡʔab rakʔaɬul ɡʼadamazda χanaanijazdaɡi perizijazdaɡi dun riχinawuna dir ɡʼjemeral tʃaɡʼi ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul ɡʔjelin abuni tsoɬila tsinɡi tʼade kʼantsʼun dunɡi tʃʼwala wa dida tsadaqχ kinabɡo dir aɡʔluɡi χwela
amma ʃimeonitsaɡi lewijitsaɡi abuna
niʒer jats qχaχʼba ɡʼadin basra ɡʔajizejiʃːχa beɡʔulej jikʼaraj

ɡʔjebmeχaɬ allaɡʔas jaqʼubida abuna
ɡʔanʒe mun bet elalde a dowa reʃːtʼa wa durɡo wats ɡʼisawidasa ɬutun mun uneb meχaɬ duje zaɡʔirɬaraw allaɡʔase qʼurban bakʼ baj ɡʔjenib
jaqʼubitsa ʒindir kinabɡo qχizamalda wa ʒindir kinalɡo ɡʼadamazda abuna
nuʒeqχ ruɡel kinalɡo tʃijar allaɡʔzabi naqχe reχe tʃerχɡi tʃure retʼjelɡi χise
ɡʔanʒe niɬ bet elalde riɬːine ruɡo ditsa doba baze kːola dide balaɡʔ batʃʼarab meχaɬ χʼalaje wataraw wa saparazda dije kumek ɡʔaburaw allaɡʔase qʼurban bakʼ
ɡʔjez jaqʼubiqχe kʔuna ʒideqχɡo rukʼaral tʃijar allaɡʔzabi ɡʼunduzdasa raqχun kʼilkʼalɡi kʔuna ɡʔjeb kinabɡo jaqʼubitsa ʃeχemaɬul mikːil ʁotʼokʔ buqʼana
ɡʔanʒe ɡʔal nuχda raqχana jaqʼubil allaɡʔasukʔa ɡʼjemer χʼinqʼijaɬ ɡʔjesul wasazda χadur ɬuɡʔinejan pikrutsin ɡʔabitʃʼo sweruqχ ruɡel ʃaɡʔarazul ɡʼadamaz
ʒindirɡo ɡʼadamalɡun tsadaqχ jaqʼub ʃːwana χanaanijazul rakʔalda buɡeb luz ɡʔjebɡo bet el ʃaɡʔaralde
wa ɡʔjenib qʼurban bakʼ bana ɡʔjes ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tsʼar ɬuna elʔ bet elʔ abun watsasdasa ɬutun uneb meχaɬ ɡʔjeniwɬidalχa ɡʔjesije allaɡʔ zaɡʔirɬaraw
ɡʔjenij χwana riwkal raχʔdal ebel dewora ɡʔjej juqʼana bet elalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ mikːil ʁotʼoda ʁorkʔ tsinɡi ɡʔjeb mikːil ʁotʼoda tsʼar ɬuna allon baχut
paddan aramaldasa jaqʼub tʼad wusːarab meχalda allaɡʔ naqχeɡi zaɡʔirɬana jaqʼubije wa ɡʔjesda barakat ɬuna
allaɡʔas ɡʔjesda abuna
duda tsʼar jaqʼub buɡo amma tʼokʼaɬ duda jaqʼubilan abize ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔanʒejaldasa naqχe duda tsʼar ɡʼizrail buɡo
ɡʔjedin allaɡʔas ɡʔjesije ɡʼizrail aburab tsʼar kʔuna
tsinɡi allaɡʔas ɡʔjesda abuna
dun wuɡo χʼalkʼolew allaɡʔ bitʃːante duje ɬimal ɡʼjemer ɡʔarize wa dur naslabiɡi tsʼikʼkʼine dudasan χalqʼ ɬuɡʔina χalqʼazul tʼubarab tʃitʼir ɬuɡʔina dudasan χanzabi ɬuɡʔina
ditsa ibraɡʔimije wa isχʼaqʼije kʔurab rakʔɡi dujeɡi dur naslabazeɡi kʔjela
allaɡʔ jaqʼubida tsewesa arab meχaɬ
jaqʼubitsa muqʼadasab ɡamatʃʼ ɬuna allaɡʔ ʒinda kʼaɬarab bakʼalda wa allaɡʔase χirijab sajʁat χʼisabalda ɡʔjelda tʼade tʼuna tʃaʁirɡi zajtunaɬul naχɡi
allaɡʔ ʒiwɡun kʼaɬarab bakʼ bukʼinaɬin jaqʼubitsa ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tsʼar bet el ɬurab
bet elaldasa raqχun un efratajalde ɡʼaɡarɬidal ɬimer ɡʔabize χʼara tʃʼwana raχelida ɬimer ɡʔabize tsʼaqʼ zaχʼmaɬuleb bukʼana
ɡʼazab ɡʼaqʼubajalda jikʼana ɡʔjej wa tʃʼaraqχanaɬ abuna
χʼinqʼuɡe ɡʔale duje tsoɡi was ɡʔawuna jan
χolej jiɡej raχelitsa aχiriseb χʼuχʔjel tsʼalaɡo wasasde tsʼar aχʼana ben oni abun amma insutsa ɡʔjesda tsʼar bunjamin ɬuna
ɡʔjedin χwana raχel efratajalde uneb nuχda ɡʔanʒe bet leχem abuleb bakʼalda juqʼana ɡʔjej
jaqʼubitsa ɡʔjeɬul χabada zani tʃʼwana ɡʔanʒeɡi buɡo ɡʔjenib ɡʔjeb raχelil χabada tʃʼwarab zani
ɡʔjenisaɡi un ɡʼizrail jeder abuleb sijalda naqχa ɬalqχana
ɡʔjenib qʼaji tʃʼwan tʃʼun ruɡeb zamanalda ruwim ʒindirɡo insul ʁarawaʃ bilɡʔada askʼowe ɬuɡʔana wa ɡʔjejɡun weɡana insudaɡi ɬana ɡʔjeb
jaqʼubil wukʼana kinawniɡi antsʼila kʼiɡo was
lejal wasal ruwim jaqʼubije tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw ʃimeon lewij jaɡʔuda isːaχar wa zewulun
raχelil wasal jusup wa bunjamin
raχelil ʁarawaʃ bilɡʔal wasal dan wa naftali
lejal ʁarawaʃ zilpal wasal ɡad wa aʃer ɡʔjel ruɡo paddan aramalda ɡʔarural jaqʼubil wasal
aχirɡi kirjat arbaɡʼalda χewronalda buɡeb mamrejalde ʒindirɡo emen isχʼaqʼiqχe ʃːwana jaqʼub kidajaliɡo ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bukʼana ibraɡʔimitsa χadub isχʼaqʼitsaɡi
kinabniɡi nusijalda unqʼoɡo son bana isχʼaqʼitsa
ɡʼumrujaɬɡi ɡʼortsʼun tʼuwan χerɬizeɡi χerɬun χwana isχʼaqʼ wa ʒindirɡo umumuzda χaduw ana ɡʔjesul wasaz ɡʼisawitsaɡi jaqʼubitsaɡi wuqʼana ɡʔjew

ɡʔale ɡʼisawil edomil wa ɡʔjesul naslabazul qʼisa
ɡʼisawitsa ɬudbi ratʃana χanaanijazda ɡʔorkʔosa ɡʼada wa oɡoliwama ɡʼada jikʼana χitijaw elonil jas oɡoliwama χiwijaw tsiweonil was ɡʼanal jas
ɡʔjezda tʼade ɡʔjes basematɡi jatʃana ɡʔjej jikʼana ismaɡʼilil jas wa newajotil jats
ɡʼisawije ɡʼadatsa ɡʔawuna elifaz basematitsa ɡʔawuna reɡuel
oɡoliwamatsa ɡʔaruna jeɡuʃ jaɡlam wa qʼoraχʼ ɡʔjel ruɡo χanaanalda ɡʼisawije ɡʔarural wasal
ʒindirɡo ɬudbiɡun wasalɡun jasalɡun wa kinalɡo ɡʼadamalɡun tsadaqχ χanaanalda dandeɬarab kinabɡo botsʼi betʃeɬiɡun ɡʼisaw jaqʼubida askʼosa tsoɡidab rakʔalde ɡotʃana
ɡʔjezda dandeɬun bukʼana ɡʼjemerab botsʼi wa tsadaqχ tʃʼjeze bakʼ qʼwariɬana ɡʔjezije ɡʔjel tʃʼarab rakʔ ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjel kʼijazulɡo reqχabaze ɡʼoleb bukʼintʃʼo
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʼisaw edom reʃːtʼana seir maɡʼarda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ
ɡʔale seiraɬul muɡʼruzda tʃʼaral edomilazul emen ɡʼisawilɡi ɡʔjesul naslabazulɡi qʼisa
ɡʼisawil wasal elifaz ɡʼisawije ɡʼadatsa ɡʔawuraw wa reɡuel ɡʼisawije basematitsa ɡʔawuraw
elifazil wasal teman omar tsefo ɡatam wa kenaz
elifazil ʁarawaʃ timnatsa ɡʔjesije ɡʔawuna amalek ɡʔjel ruɡo ɡʼadatsa ɡʔarural wasazdasan ɬuɡʔaral ɡʼisawil naslabi
reɡuelil wasal naχʼat zeraχʼ ʃamma wa miza ɡʔjel ruɡo ɡʼisawije basematitsa ɡʔarural wasal
tsiweonil ɡʼanal jas oɡoliwamatsa ɡʼisawije ɡʔaruna jeɡuʃ jaɡlam wa qʼoraχʼ
ɡʔjele ɡʼisawidasan ɬuɡʔaral tuχumazul butʼrul
ɡʼisawije tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw was elifazil naslabi temanil tuχum omaril tuχum tsefol tuχum kenazil tuχum
qʼoraχʼil tuχum ɡatamil tuχum wa amalekil tuχum ɡʔjel ruɡo elifazil tuχumal ɡʼadatsa ɡʔarural wasazdasan ɬuɡʔaral ɡʼisawil naslabi ɡʔjez jaʃaw ɡʔabula edomaɬul rakʔalda
ɡʼisawil was reɡuelil naslabi naχʼatil tuχum zeraχʼil tuχum ʃammal tuχum wa mizal tuχum ɡʔjel ruɡo reɡuelil tuχumal basematitsa ɡʔarural wasazdasan ɬuɡʔaral ɡʼisawil naslabi ɡʔjezɡi jaʃaw ɡʔabula edomaɬul rakʔalda
oɡoliwamatsa ɡʔarural wasazdasan ɬuɡʔaral ɡʼisawil naslabi jeɡuʃil tuχum jaɡlamil tuχum wa qʼoraχʼil tuχum ɡʔjel ruɡo ɡʼanal jas ɡʼisawil ɬadi oɡoliwamatsa ɡʔarural wasazdasan ɬuɡʔaral tuχumal ɡʔjedinal ruɡo
ɡʼisawil edomil naslabi wa ɡʔjezul tuχumal
ɡʔjeb ulkajalda rukʼaral χorijaw seiril wasal lutʼan ʃowal tsiweon ɡʼana
diʃon etser wa diʃan ɡʔjel ruɡo edomaɬul rakʔalda rukʼaral χorijaw seiridasan ɬuɡʔaral tuχumal
lutʼanil wasal χori wa ɡemam lutʼanil jatsalda tsʼar bukʼana timna
ʃowalil wasal alwan manaχat ɡewal ʃefo wa onam
tsiweonil wasal ajja wa ɡʼana ʒindirɡo emen tsiweonil χʼamul χʔiχʔun wuɡeb meχaɬ ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχalda itsː bataraw ɡʼana wuɡo ɡʔjew
ɡʼanal ɬimal kːola was diʃonɡi jas oɡoliwamaɡi
diʃonil wasal χemdan eʃban jitran wa keran
etseril wasal bilɡʔan zaawan wa akan
diʃanil wasal ɡʼuts wa aran
ɡʔadinal ruɡo χorijazul tuχumal lutʼanil tuχum ʃowalil tuχum tsiweonil tuχum ɡʼanal tuχum
diʃonil tuχum etseril tuχum wa diʃanil tuχum seiraɬul rakʔalda rukʼaral χorijazul tuχumazul sijaχʼ buɡo ɡʔjeb
ɡʔale ɡʼizrailazul patʃaɬi ɬuɡʔinaldeɡo edomalda rukʼaral χanzabi
edomalda tʼotsewe χanɬun wukʼana beoril was bela ɡʔjesul taχʃaɡʔaralda tsʼar bukʼana dinɡʔawa
bela χwarab meχalda ɡʔjew χisana botsrajaldasa zeraχʼil was jowawitsa
jowaw χun χadub χanɬi ɡʔabuna temanil naslabazul ulkajaldasa χʼuʃamitsa
χʼuʃam χun χadub χanɬi ɡʔabuna bedadil was ɡʔadaditsa ɡʔjesin moɡʼawaɬul awlaqχazda midjanijal ʁuraral ɡʔjesul taχʃaɡʔaralda tsʼar bukʼana awit
ɡʔadad χun χadub χanɬi ɡʔabuna masrekajaldasa samlatsa
samla χun χadub χanɬi ɡʔabuna jefrat ɡʼurul raɡʼalda buɡeb reχowotaldasa ʃaulitsa
ʃaul χun χadub χanɬi ɡʔabuna aχboril was baɡʼal χananitsa
aχboril was baɡʼal χanan χun χadub χanɬi ɡʔabuna ɡʔadaritsa ɡʔjesul taχʃaɡʔaralda tsʼar bukʼana paɡʼu wa ɡʔjesul ɬadi jikʼana meɡʔjetawel me zaɡʔawil jasaɬul matredil jas
ɡʔale ɡʼisawidasan ɬuɡʔaral tuχumal ɡʔjel tuχumazul butʼruzul tsʼaral kʔun rukʼana ɡʔjezul kʔibilazeɡi rosabazeɡi timnal tuχum alwal tuχum jetetil tuχum
oɡoliwamal tuχum elal tuχum pinonil tuχum
kenazil tuχum temanil tuχum miwtsaril tuχum
maɡdielil tuχum wa iramil tuχum
ɡʔanir reχson ruɡo edomijazul tuχumalɡi ɡʔjezul rosabiɡi edomijazul χalqʼaɬul emen kːola ɡʼisaw

jaqʼubin abuni tsewe ʒindirɡo emen wukʼarab bakʼalda χanaanalda ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼana
ɡʔale jaqʼubilɡi ɡʔjesul naslabazulɡi qʼisa
jusup wukʼana antsʼila ankʔɡo son baraw ɡʼoloqχantʃi watsazda tsadaqχ ɡʼi χʔiχʔun wukʼana ɡʔjew bilɡʔal wa zilpal wasaze kumek ɡʔabun ɡʔjez ʃːib ɡʔabuniɡi ɡʔjeb jusupitsa insuda bitsunaan
jusup wukʼana jaqʼubije χerab qʼojaɬ ɡʔawuraw was ɡʔjedinɬidal tsoɡidal wasazdasa tsʼikʼkʼun wokʔulaan jaqʼubije ɡʔjew wa naqʼiʃal uɡʔarab χirijab ɡurdetsin sajʁat ɡʔabuna ɡʔjes jusupije
insuje jusup ʒidedasaɡo tsʼikʼkʼun wokʔulew wukʼin biχʔun watsazul ɡʔjesdeχun rokʔuqʼɬi bukʼana bertsinab kʼaltsin kʼaɬalaroan ɡʔjez ɡʔasda
tso nuχaɬ jusupida makʔu biχʔana ʒindirɡo watsazda ɡʔjeb makʔu bitsaraldasa χadub ʒeɡi tsʼikʼkʼun riχana ɡʔjezije ɡʔaw
ɡʼjenekːe jan abuna ɡʔjes dida biχʔarab makʔu bitsinin
niɬ ruɡo χurir ɡul qʼalel tsinɡi dir ɡul baqχun tʃʼana amma nuʒer ɡulaz ɡʔjelda sweruqχ tʃʼun ɡʔjeɬije suʒda ɡʔabuna
watsaz abuna
ɡʔa ɡʔanʒe niʒer χanɬunɡi waqχun niʒee betʼjerɬi ɡʔabize qʼasdtsin ɡuriʃː dur buɡeb
tsinɡi ʒeɡi tsʼikʼkʼana ɡʔjezuɬ ɡʔasde rokʔuqʼɬi ɡʔjesul makʔabi sababɬunɡi χarbal sababɬunɡi
tsinɡi naqχeɡi makʔu biχʔana jusupida wa ɡʔjebɡi bitsana ʒindirɡo watsazda
tsoɡi makʔu biχʔana dida baqʼɡi motsʼɡi antsʼila tso tsʼwaɡi dida tsere suʒdajalda tʃʼana
ɡʔjeb makʔu ɡʔjes insudaɡi watsazdaɡi bitsindal emen ɡʔjesde semana
ɡʔalɡo kinal makʔabi duda riχʔulel ruɡel unɡo unɡoɬunɡi duda rakʼaldejiʃː kːoleb niʒ kinalɡo dunɡi dur ebelɡi watsalɡi ratʃʼun duda tsere suʒdajalda tʃʼjeze ruɡin abun
watsazul kʼudijab ʒaχʼda bukʼana jusupideχun amma insutsa rekʼjeɬ tsʼunana ɡʔjes bitsarab makʔu
tso nuχalda jusupil watsal insul ɡʼi kwanazabize ana ʃeχemalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχe
ɡʼizrailitsa jusupida abuna
dur watsal ʃeχemalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ ɡʼi kwanazabulel ruɡo ditsa munɡi witʼilin ɡʔjezda χaduw
ine χʼadur wuɡo dada jan abuna jusupitsa insuda
aχa dir was in abuna ɡʔjes dol saχ salamat ruɡiʃːali wa ɡʼi kin buɡebali χal ɡʔabe tsinɡi tʼadwusːun watʃʼun dida bitse
ɡʔjedinɡi abun insutsa jusup nuχareɡʼana χewronaɬul rasaɬiɡi naqχa tun ɡʔjew ʃeχemalde ana
ɡʔjeniw ɡʔjesda tso tʃi dandtʃʼwana
ʃːib dutsa ɡʔanib balaɡʔuleb buɡeb in ɡʔiqʼana ɡʔjes awlaqχalda tirulew wataraw jusupida
dirɡo watsal ralaɡʔulew wuɡo jan ʒawab kʔuna jusupitsa reqχabiɡun ɡʔjel ruɡeb bakʼ ɬalariʃː duda
ɡʔjel ɡʔanisa ana jan abuna dos dida raɡʼana ɡʔjez dotanaldeχun
jusup watsazda χaduw ana wa dotanalda ratana ɡʔjesda ɡʔjel
rikʼkʼadasanɡo wiχʔana ɡʔjezda jusup wa ɡʔjew askʼowe ɡʼaɡarɬilalde ɡʔjezul qʼotʼi kːana wats tʃʼwaze
dole niɬer makʔabi riχʔulew tʃi jan abuna ɡʔjez tsotsazda
tʃʼwazeɡi tʃʼwan ɡʔaniw tso ɡwandiniwe reχila niɬetsa dow wa ʒanawaraɬ tʃʼwanilan abila ɡʔjebmeχalda biχʔila dosul makʔabi kin tʼuralelali
amma ruwimida ɡʔjeb raɡʼidal ɡʔjes jusup tʃʼwaze witʃːatʃʼo
tʃʼwaze kːelaro dow in abuna ɡʔjes
bi ɡʼodobe tʼun ʃːaj niɬee ɡʔjedin dosde kwer borχijaldasa dole doba ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχaɬul bakʔuɬ buɡeb ɡwandiniwe reχun ɬikʼ niɬetsa dow
χʼaqʼiqʼatalda ɡʔjesije bokʔun bukʼana jusup χwasar ɡʔawize wa ɡʔjew insuqχe naqχ wusːinawize
jusup watsazda askʼowe ʃːwarawɡo ɡʔjez ɡʔasda tʼasa baqχana batʼi batʼijal naqʼiʃal tʼad uɡʔarab ɡurde
wa kːwezeɡi kːun ɡwandiniwe reχana ɡʔjeb ɬim bakʼaruleb ɡwend ɡʔjeb zamanalda tʃʼoboɡo bukʼana
tsinɡi watsal kwanaze ɡʼodor tʃʼana ɡʼodor tʃʼun meχ balelde ɡilɡʼadaɬul raqχaldasan batʃʼuneb biχʔana ismaɡʼililazul qʼapila waranabazda ɬun maχʼɡʔuinal pitsʼalɡi ladanɡi balʔzamɡi bosun misrijalde unel rukʼana ɡʔjel
jaɡʔudatsa ʒindirɡo watsazda abuna
ɡʔjew tʃʼwajaldasa wa ɡʼodobe tʼurab bi baɬɡo ɡʔabijaldasa ʃːib pajda niɬee buɡeb
ratʃʼa niɬetsa ɡʔjew ismaɡʼililaze witʃize tsinɡi niɬeda tʼad bidul χʼaqʼɡi bukʼinaro niɬer watsɬidalχa ɡʔjew
watsal ɡʔjelda raziɬana
midjanaɬul bazarɡabi askʼoreɡʼan ʃːwarab meχalda watsaz ɡwandinisaɡi waqχun jusup ismaɡʼililaze witʃana ɡʼartsul qʼoɡo ʃekelaɬuqχ wa ɡʔjezɡi ɡʔjew misrijalde watʃun ana
tsodaɡʔab zamanaldasa ruwim tʼadwusːun watʃʼana wa ɡwandiqχe ana amma jusup ɡʔjeniw watitʃʼo ɡʔjebmeχaɬ tʃara buχʼun ʒindaɡo tʼad bukʼarab retʼjel biqχana ruwimitsa
watsazda askʼoweɡi watʃʼun ɡʔjes abuna
was dowa ɡʔjetʃʼoɡuri ɡʔanʒe ditsa ʃːib ɡʔabileb dun kiwe kʼantsʼilew
watsazin abuni jusupil naqʼiʃal tʼad uɡʔarab ɡurde tso deɡʼjenɡi qχun ɡʔjeɬul bidul tsʼjezabuna
tsinɡi ɡʔjebɡi bosun insuqχe riɬːana wa ɡʔjesda abuna
balaɡʔje niʒeda batarab ʒo dur wasasul ɡurde buɡiʃː ɡʔabali χalɡʔabe
balaɡʔarab saɡʼataɬɡo ɡʔjebɡi ɬan jaqʼubitsa abuna
waj dir wasasul ɡurde ʒanawaraɬ tʃʼwan wuɡo dir was tʃʼwazeɡi tʃʼwan ɡʔjeɬ tʼutʼun wan wuɡo jusup
ʒindaɡo tʼad bukʼarab retʼjelɡi biqχ biqχun χʼjebtil χːamil tso kesekɡi ɡʼitsʼab tʃerχalda ʒemun ɡʼjemeral qʼojaz tʼatʼala jusupiqχ maɡʼu tʼuna jaqʼubitsa
kinalɡo ɬimal ratʃʼana ɡʔjesda askʼore ɡʔjesul rakʼbatizabize amma jaqʼubil rekʼjee ʃːibniɡi biɡʔaɬi bukʼintʃʼo
te dun ɡʼodilewɡo ɡʼodilew wukʼina wa tʼolaɡo maɡʼuɡun ina dirɡo wasasuqχe barzaχaldeɡi
ɡʔjedin jusupiqχ ɡʼodilew wukʼana jaqʼub
ɡʔjeb zamanalda midjanijaz jusup misrijalde watʃana wa potifarije witʃana ɡʔjew wukʼana pirɡʼawn tsʼunulel raʁuqχabazul betʼjer

ɡʔjeb zamanalda jaɡʔuda watsalɡi tun tsoɡidab bakʼalde ana ɡʼumru ɡʔabize wa χira abun tsʼar buɡew adulamaldasa tso tʃijasda askʼow tʃʼana
ɡʔjenij ɡʔjesda jiχʔana ʃuaɡʼ aburaw tso χanaanijasul jas wa ɡʔjej jatʃana jaɡʔudatsa ʒindijeɡo ɬadiɬun
ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana wa ɡʔjeɬije was ɡʔawuna jaɡʔudatsa ɡʔjesda tsʼar ɡʼjer abun ɬuna
ɡʔjesul ɬadude naqχeɡi ɬimer kːana kʼiabilewɡi was ɡʔawuna wa ɡʔjesda tsʼar onan ɬuna
χadub ɡʔjeɬ tsoɡi was ɡʔawuna wa ɡʔjesda tsʼar ʃela ɬuna ɡʔjeb kːana keziwalda
ʒindirɡo kʼudijaw was ɡʼjerije jaɡʔudatsa jatʃana tamar abun tsʼar buɡej jas
amma ɡʼjeril kweʃab ɡʼamal sababɬun betʼjerhanasda riχana ɡʔjew wa betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesije ɡʼaʒal batana
jaɡʔudatsa onanida abuna
watsasul jikʼaraj tʃʼuʒu jatʃe watsasul bakʼ kːwe ɡʔjesul naslu bukʼine jan
amma onanida ɬalaan tamaritsa ɡʔaburab ɬimer ʒindirɬun rikʼkʼunarebɬi ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡanʃːinaqχe ʒindirɡo batʃʼuneb mani ɡʔjes ɡʼodobe tʃwaχizabulaan watsasul tsʼar tʃʼwaze wa ɡʔjesul nasluɬun ɬuɡʔine ɬimer ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo bukʼine
amma ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanase bokʔulareb iʃ ɡʔaburaɬuqχ ɡʔjesijeɡi betʼjerhanas ɡʼaʒal batana
ɡʔanʒe kʼudijal wasalɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔitʼinawɡi χweze ɡurin χʼinqʼaraw jaɡʔudatsa ʒindirɡo nus tamarida abuna
dir was ʃela kʼudijaw ɡʼjezeɡʼan durɡo ebel insuda askʼoje un qʼorolɬuda tʃʼa jan
ɡʔjedin tamar ʒindirɡo ebel insul roqʼoje naqχ jusːana
ɡʔjeldasa naqχe ɡʼjemerab zaman ana jaɡʔudal ɬadi ʃuaɡʼil jas χwana ɡʔjelda χadur maɡʼil qʼojal aχiralde ʃːwedal jaɡʔuda adulamaldasa ʒindirɡo ɡʔudul χiraɡi tsadaqχ watʃun timnajalde wiɬːana ʒindirɡo ɡʼi qʼuntsʼize
wakʔad timnajalde ɡʼi qʼuntsʼize unew wukʼin ɬana tamarida
ɡʔjeɬ qʼorolaɬul retʼjel tʼasa baqχana wa tʃadrajaɬ ɡʔumerɡi batsun timnajalde uneb nuχda buɡeb jenaim ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawuduqχ ɡʼodoj tʃʼana ɡʔjelda biχʔuleb bukʼindalχa ʃela kʼudijaw ɡʼun wuɡoniɡi ɡʔjesije ʒij jatʃunej ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi
ɡʔjej jiχʔidal jaɡʔudada kːana ɡʔjej qχaχʼba jiɡilan tʃadrajaɬ baχtʃun bukʼindal ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔumer
ɡʔjew ɡʔjelda askʼowe watʃʼana nuχlul raɡʼalda ɡʼodoj tʃʼun jiɡej ɡʔjelda jaɡʔudatsa abuna
jiɬːa dunɡun jeɡize jan ɡʔjesda ɬaleb bukʼintʃʼjeɬulχa ɡʔjej ʒindirɡo nus jiɡebɬi ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔiqʼana
dunɡun weɡaraɬuqχ dutsa dije ʃːib kʔjeleb in
ditsa duje tso burutʼ bitʼila jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjes
ɡʔjeb bitʼun batʃʼineɡʼan ʁorkʔɬalije ʃːibniɡi kʔjelebiʃː an abuna ɡʔjeɬ
ʁorkʔɬalije ʃːib duje bokʔileb an ɡʔiqʼana jaɡʔudatsa
ɡʔjeɬ ʒawab kʔuna
tʃalujalda buχʔarab dur muɡʔruɡi duda kodob buɡeb ɡʼansaɡi kʔje jan
ɡʔjeɬ aburab kʔuna ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬije ɡʔjew ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡana wa tamaril urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana
χaduj ɡʔjej roqʼoje tʼadjusːana wa ɡʔurmadasa tʃadraɡi naqχe reχun naqχeɡi qʼorolaɬul retʼjel retʼana
adulamaldasa dow ʒindirɡo ɡʔudul witʼana jaɡʔudatsa ɡʔjeɬije burutʼɡi batʃun dol ʁorkʔɬalije ɬural ʒal naqχe rosize amma kiɡʼan jalaɡʔaniɡi ɡʔjesda ɡʔjej jatitʃʼo
ɡʔjeb bakʼaɬul ɡʼadamazda tsʼjeχoldize ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjew
jenaimalda nuχda ɡʼodoj tʃʼun jikʼaraj qχaχʼba kij jiɡej abun
doja ɡʔjedinaj ɡʼadan jikʼintʃʼo jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjez
tʼadwusːun watʃʼun ɡʔjes jaɡʔudada abuna
dida doj jatitʃʼo dob bakʼaɬul ɡʼadamazɡi abuna doja qχaχʼba jikʼintʃʼilan
jaɡʔudatsa abuna
ritʃːante ɡʔjel ʒal doɬuqχɡo χutʼize niɬedaɡo tʼad ɡʼadamal reɬanqχitʃʼoɡo rukʼine ditsa rakʼbatsʼtsʼadɡo mun ɡʔjeɬije burutʼɡi batʃun witʼana duqχajin abuni ɡʔjej jalaɡʔun baʒaritʃʼo
ɬabɡo motsʼɡʼan zaman indal jaɡʔudaqχe χabar batʃʼana
dur nus tamaritsa zina ɡʔabun raɡʼula ɬimerɡi kːun buɡo ɡʔjelde
ʃaɡʔar tun qʼwatʼijeχunɡi jatʃun tsʼadutsa juχʼje ɡʔjej jan abuna jaɡʔudatsa
tʃʼwaze roqʼosa qʼwatʼije ɡʔjej jatʃine ɬuɡʔarab meχalda tamaritsa χabar bitʼana wakʔadasuqχe
ɡʔale ɡʔazul χwaʒainasdasan kːana dide ɬimer walaɡʔun wiχʔje ɡʔazuqχ ɡʔab tʃalujalda buχʔarab muɡʔruɡi ɡʔab ɡʼansaɡi ɬil kːolebali ɬaliʃː duda
jaɡʔudada ɬana ɡʔjel ʒindir rukʼin ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjes abuna
ɡʔjej jitʼaraj jiɡo dun meqʼi wuɡo ɡʔjeb kinabɡo kːana ɡʔjej ditsa dirɡo was ʃelaje jatʃintʃʼoɬi sababɬun
tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡitʃʼo jaɡʔuda
tamaritsa ɬimer ɡʔabize meχ ʃːwana kʼiɡo ɬimer kːun batana ɡʔjelda
ɬimer ɡʔabuleb zamanalda tso kwer qʼwatʼibe bakːana tʃʼaraqχanaɬ ɡʔjelda baɡʼarab tʃʼolo buχʔana
ɡʔaw tsewe ɡʔawuna janɡi abun
amma ɡʔjeb ɬimatsa kwer naqχbusːun ʒanibe bosun ana wa ɡʔjesdasa tsewe qʼwatʼiwe watʃʼana ɡʔjesul wats
waχʼ kin dutsa qʼwatʼibe nuχ baqχarab abun ɡʼaʒaibɬana tʃʼaraqχan tsinɡi ɡʔjeb ɬimada tsʼar ɬuna parets
ɡʔjesda χaduw ɡʔawuna kwerda baɡʼarab tʃʼolo buχʔarawɡi ɡʔjesda tsʼar ɬuna zeraχʼ

jusup ismaɡʼililaz misrijalde watʃana wa ɡʔjeniw potifar abun tsʼar buɡew tso misrijase witʃana potifar wukʼana pirɡʼawnasul χʼakim wa ɡʔjew tsʼunaral raʁuqχabazul betʼjer
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas jusupije kumek ɡʔabuleb bukʼana wa ʒindirɡo χwaʒainasul roqʼob sunduɬɡoɡi bitʼ kːoleb bukʼana ɡʔjesije
ɡʔjew tʃijasda biχʔana jusupɡun betʼjerhan wukʼin wa jusupitsa ʃːib ɡʔabuleb buɡoniɡi betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesije kwerbaqʼuleb bukʼin
misrijas ɡʔjesdasa raziɬun ʒindirɡo kumektʃiɬun tʼamuna jusup kwatʼitʃʼoɡo ʒindirɡo buɡebʃːinabɡi jusupil tʼalabtʃiɬijalda ʁorkʔje kʔuna ɡʔjes
ɡʔjeldasa χadub jusupije ɡʼolo betʼjerhanas barakat reʃːtʼinabuna ɡʔjew misrijasul kinabɡo buɡoɬijalde ruqʼ qʼajaldeɡi aχ χuraldeɡi
ʒindirɡo buɡebʃːinab ʒo jusupil kwerʃːalikʔje kʔuna ɡʔjesul χwaʒainas kwana ɡʔjeqʼej ɡuroni tʼokʼab ʒojaɬul urʁel ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo raχʼatalda wukʼana ɡʔanʒe misrijaw
jusup wukʼana ɡʔumerɡi bertsinaw laɡa tʃerχɡi tʃʼurkanaw tʃi
χwaʒainasul ɬadutsa beral retʃʼtʃʼarizarulel rukʼana ɡʔjesde tso qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjesda abuna ʒinda askʼow weɡajilan
amma inkar ɡʔabun jusupitsa abuna
χwaʒainas dir iχtijaralde kʔuna ʒindirɡo buɡebʃːinab ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjes sundulɡo urʁel ɡʔabize kːolaro
ɡʔab qʼawuɬ ɡʔjesda baʃːadɡo amru bujuruqχ kʔjeze iznuɡi buɡo dije dije ɡʔuqʼarab ʒoɡi ʃːibɡo ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔanib tsoχʼo mun χutʼizeɡʼan mun ɡʔjesul ɬadi jiɡeɬul tsinɡi ɡʔjedinab χʼaliχʔaɬi kinχa ditsa ɡʔabileb allaɡʔasda tsebe ɡʔjedinab munaɡʔ kin bitʃːaleb
qʼojidasa qʼojide ɡʔjew mukʼur ɡʔawize tʼadeɬana ɡʔjej amma jusup ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡize raziɬitʃʼo
tso nuχalda ʒindirɡo qχuluqχ tʼubazabize jusup χwaʒainasul roqʼowe ɬuɡʔindal ruqʼaɬul aɡʔlujaɬul tsoniɡi tʃi wukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjeniw
ɡʔjebmeχalda ɡʔjej ɡʼadanaɬ qʼan kːuna ɡʔasul retʼjel ʒinda askʼow weɡajilanɡi abun amma ɡʔjeɬul qχatikʔ ʒindirɡo retʼjelɡi tun jusupitsa χeχɡo nutsʼiqχe nuχ bosana wa minajaldasa qʼwatʼiwe ɬutana
jusup ɬutun arawɬi biχʔidal wa ɡʔjesul retʼjelɡi ʒinda kodob χutʼidal
raɡʔtʼatelazde aχʼi ban ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjezda abuna
biχʔuliʃː ɡʔaʁaw ʒuɡʔutʼaw watʃun watʃʼana ɡʔaniwe niɬ inʒit χʼaqʼir ɡʔarize watʃʼun tʼadeɡun dun basra ɡʔajize bokʔun ɬuɡʔana ʁow amma ditsa aχʼi baqχinabuna
dun aχʼdeze ɬuɡʔindal ʒindirɡo retʼjeltsin ɡʔanibɡo tun qʼwatʼiwe kʼantsʼana wa ɬutun ana
ros watʃʼineɡʼan ʒindiqχɡo tana ɡʔjeɬ jusupil retʼjel
tsinɡi rosasdaɡi ɡʔjebɡo χabar bitsana
diqχe watʃʼun dun basra ɡʔajize ɬuɡʔun wukʼana ɡʔaʁaw dutsa watʃun watʃʼaraw ʒuɡʔutʼaw laʁ
dun aχʼdeze tʃʼtʃʼitʃʼtʃʼidize ɬuɡʔarab meχalda retʼjelɡi ɡʔanibɡo tun tʼurun ana qʼwatʼiwe
dur laʁas ʒij inʒit ɡʔajizeqχin jikʼanilan ɬadutsa χabar bitsindal jusupil χwaʒainasul tsːin ɡʔalaɡɬana
kːun watʃun jusup patʃajasul tusnaqχalde reχejilan bujurana ɡʔjes
ɡʔjedin tusnaqχaɬuwe kːana jusup
amma betʼjerhanas reχun tetʃʼo ɡʔjew wa ɡʔjesda raχʼmu tsʼob ɬuna tusnaqχaɬul betʼjerase rekʼjee ɡʼuna jusup
ʒanir tʼamun ruɡel kinalɡo tusnaqχal ɡʔjes jusupil iχtijaralde kʔuna ɡʔanʒe tusnaqχaɬul betʼjerasul bakʼalda jusupitsa ɡʔabuleb bukʼana kinabɡo
ɡʔjewin abuni sundulɡo urʁel ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo paraχat wukʼana jusupɡun betʼjerhan wukʼindalχa ɡʔabulebʃːinaɬuɬ ɡʔjes jusupije kwerbaqʼulebɡi bukʼindal

tso zamanaldasan misrijaɬul patʃajasul kʼudijaw tʃaʁirtʃijasulɡi tʃed beʒulew tʃijasulɡi ʒiderɡo patʃajasda tsebe taqʼsir kːana
pirɡʼawnasul kutakalda tsːin baqχana ɡʔjel ʒindirɡo qχuluqχtʃaɡʼazda tʃaʁirtʃijasdaɡi tʃed beʒulew tʃijasdaɡi
wa ɡʔjes ɡʔjel ʒindirɡo qχarawulzabazul betʼjerasul roqʼob buɡeb tusnaqχalda tʼamuna ɡʔjeniwɡo wukʼana jusupɡi
qχarawulzabazul betʼjeras jusup tʼamuna ɡʔjezije qχuluqχ ɡʔabulew tʃiɬun wa ɡʔjedin uneb bukʼana zaman
tso sordojaɬ ɡʔjew kʼijawɡo tusnaqχasda patʃajasul tʃaʁirtʃijasda wa patʃajasul tʃed beʒulew tʃijasda makʔabi riχʔana ʃːiwasul makʔujaɬul ʒindirɡo maɡʼnaɡi bukʼana
radal ɡʔjezda askʼowe watʃʼarab meχaɬ ɡʔjel raχʼat χun paʃmanɡo ratana jusupida
ʃːaj nuʒ paʃmanɡo ruɡel in ɡʔiqʼana jusupitsa jusupida tsadaqχ ɡʔjesul χwaʒainasul roqʼor tusnaqχalda tʼamun ruɡel ɡʔjel pirɡʼawnasul qχuluqχtʃaɡʼaz
ʒawab kʔuna
niʒeda makʔabi riχʔana amma ɡʔjel qʼotʼize tʃi ɡʔaniw ɡʔjetʃʼo jan
jusupitsa abuna
makʔu qʼotʼi allaɡʔasdasan ɡuriʃː bukʼuneb dida ritse nuʒer makʔabi jan
tsinɡi betʼjeraw tʃaʁirtʃijas bitsana
dida makʔiɬ biχʔana tso tsʼolbol ʁabu
ɡʔjelda bukʼana ɬabɡo tʃʼor ɡʔjel χalaɬun ratʃʼana tʼjeɡʔana tsʼolbol χʔopal riʒana wa tsʼibil barʃːana
dir qχatikʔ bukʼana pirɡʼawnase tʃaʁir tʼoleb ʃːurun ditsa tsʼolbol χʔopal tʼuna ɡʔjel ʃːurminire tsʼtsʼuna wa pirɡʼawnasuqχe kʔuna
ɡʔale ɡʔjeb makʔujaɬul maɡʼna jan abuna ɡʔjesda jusupitsa ɬabɡo tʃʼor kːola ɬabɡo qʼo
ɬabɡo qʼojaldasan pirɡʼawnas mun naqχeɡi tʼadeɡʼan ɡʔawila durɡo bukʼarab iʃalde tʼad wusːinawila wa tsebeɡo ɡʼadin naqχeɡi ɡʔjesul ʃːurminibe tʃaʁir tʼjela wa ɡʔjeb ɡʔjesuqχe kʔjela
tso ɬikʼɬi ɡʔabe dije taliχʼaɬ duda qʼwal barab qʼojaɬ dunɡi rakʼalde ʃːwa pirɡʼawnasulɡun χabar kːarab bakʼalda dir raqχaɬ kʼaɬaj ɡʔabe wa ɡʔanisa qʼwatʼiwe wortʃʼizawe dun
dun wuɡo ʒuɡʔutʼazul rakʔaldasa qχamuraw tʃi tusnaqχalda tʼamizeɡʼanaseb kweʃɬi ɡʔanibɡi ɡʔabitʃʼo ditsa
betʼjeraw tʃed beʒulew tʃijasda biχʔana ɡʔjes makʔu ɬikʼaɬe qʼotʼuleb bukʼin wa ɡʔjes jusupida abuna
didaɡi biχʔana makʔu dir betʼjeralda tʼad ɬabɡo tʃʼjep bukʼana
biʃːun tʼasa buɡeb tʃʼjepaɬub bukʼana pirɡʼawnase beʒarab batʼi batʼijab niɡʼmat wa χʼantʃʼi rukʼana dir botʼroda ɬurab ɡʔjeb tʃʼjepaɬusan kwanalel
ɡʔale ɡʔjeb makʔujaɬul maɡʼna jan abuna jusupitsa ɡʔjesda ɬabɡo tʃʼjep kːola ɬabɡo qʼo
ɬabɡo qʼojaldasan pirɡʼawnas munɡi tʼade worχizawila χʼoboda wala ɡʔjes mun wa dur tʃerχɡi χʼantʃʼaz tʼutʼun bala
ɬabɡo qʼojaldasan bukʼana pirɡʼawn ɡʔawurab qʼo ʒindirɡo qχuluqχtʃaɡʼaze bertin toj ɡʔabuna ɡʔjes wa kinazdaɡo tseresan betʼjeraw tʃaʁirtʃiɡi betʼjeraw tʃed beʒulew tʃiɡi tusnaqχaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃana
betʼjeraw tʃaʁirtʃi naqχeɡi ʒindirɡo iʃalde tʼamuna wa ɡʔjes tsʼidasan tʃoʁrolɡi tsʼun ʃːurun pirɡʼawnasuqχe kʔuna
betʼjeraw tʃed beʒulew tʃijase χʼukmu qʼotʼana wa ɡʔjew χʼoboda wana kinabɡo kːana jusupitsa makʔu qʼotʼarab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ
amma betʼjeraw tʃaʁir tʼolew tʃijasda jusupɡi ɡʔjesul ɡʔariɡi rakʼaldetsin ʃːwetʃʼo ɡʔjesda kʼotʃon tana ɡʔjeb

ɡʔjeldasa χadub ana kʼiɡo son wa tso sordojaɬ pirɡʼawnasda makʔu biχʔana makʔiɬ ɡʔjew nil ɡʼoraɬul raɡʼalda waqχun tʃʼun wukʼana wa
ɡʼuruɬa qʼwatʼibe ankʔɡo bertsinab kʔarijab ɡʼaka batʃʼana ɡʔjel ɡʼatʃi ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjenib raɡʼalda bukʼarab mutsʼi kwanaze
ɡʔjezdaɡo χadub nil ɡʼuruɬa qʼwatʼibe batʃʼana tsʼaqʼɡo χʼalaqʼab suruqʼab ʒeɡi ankʔɡo ɡʼaka wa dozda askʼor nil ɡʼurul raɡʼalda tʃʼana ɡʔjel
ɡʔale χʼalaqʼal suruqʼal ɡʼatʃijaz kʼkʼun reχulel ruɡo dol bertsinal kʔarijal ɡʼatʃi tsinɡi pirɡʼawn makʔidasa wiɡʔana
naqχeɡi kʔiʒun kːedal batʼijab makʔu biχʔana ɡʔjesda tso χʼoboda biʒun buɡo muɡʔ tsʼubarab ɬikʼab ankʔɡo tʼor
ɡʔjezdaɡo χadub rakʔaldasan bakːana buχʼarab ɡʔorotsa baqʼwazaburab ɡʔodorab ankʔɡo tʼorɡi
ɡʔale ɡʔjel raqʼwaral tʼoraz qʼultʃʼun reχana dol muɡʔ tsʼubaral tʼoral wa pirɡʼawn makʔidasa wortʃʼana ɡʔjedinab bukʼana ɡʔjesda biχʔarab makʔu
ɡʔjeb makʔujaɬ raχʼat χwezaburaw ɡʔjes radal tʼadeɡi waqχun misrijaɬul kinalɡo siχʼrutʃaɡʼiɡi makʔu qʼotʼulel tʃaɡʼiɡi ɡʼaqʼilal ɡʼadamalɡi rakʼarun ɡʔjezda bitsana ʒindirɡo makʔu amma ɬidaniɡi kʼwetʃʼo ɡʔjeb makʔu qʼotʼize
ɡʔjebmeχalda betʼjeraw tʃaʁir tʼolew tʃijas pirɡʼawnasda abuna
ɡʔanʒe dida rakʼalde ʃːwana dirɡo χatʼa
tso qʼojaɬ pirɡʼawnasul tsːin baqχana ʒindirɡo laʁzaderida wa dun dowa qχarawulzabazul betʼjerasul bakʼalda ʒaniw tʼamejan bujurana dida tsadaqχ ʒaniw tʼamuna betʼjeraw tʃed beʒulew tʃiɡi
tso sordojaɬ niʒ kʼijazdaɡo makʔabi riχʔana ʃːiwasul makʔujaɬul ʒindirɡo χasab maɡʼnaɡi bukʼana
niʒee qχuluqχaɬe tun wukʼana tso ʒuɡʔutʼaw qχarawulzabazul betʼjerasul laʁ niʒetsa ɡʔjesda ritsana niʒerɡo makʔabi wa ɡʔjes bitsana ʃːiwasul makʔil maɡʼna
ɡʔjes niʒeda bitsuqχe kːezeɡi kːana dun dirɡo tsebe bukʼarab iʃalde tʼad wusːinawuna dow tsojaw kwaridaɡi wan ʁanqʼana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ pirɡʼawnas jusup watʃine tʃi witʼana χeχɡo tusnaqχaldasa qʼwatʼiweɡi watʃun meɡeʒ betʼjerɡi kʼkʼwan tsʼijab retʼjelɡi retʼun pirɡʼawnasda tsewe tʃʼjezawuna ɡʔjew pirɡʼawnas jusupida abuna
dida tso makʔu biχʔana amma ɬidaniɡi kʼoleb ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjeb qʼotʼize dida raɡʼana bitsarab saɡʼataɬɡo makʔu qʼotʼize ɬalin dudajilan
ditsa ɡuro allaɡʔas qʼotʼila ɡʔjeb makʔu pirɡʼawnase ɬikʼaɬe jan abuna jusupitsa
tsinɡi pirɡʼawnas jusupida makʔu bitsana
dida makʔiɬ biχʔana dun nil ɡʼoraɬul raɡʼalda waqχun tʃʼun
tsinɡi nil ɡʼuruɬa qʼwatʼibe batʃʼana kʔarijab bertsinab ankʔɡo ɡʼaka ɡʔjel ɡʼatʃi ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjenib raɡʼalda bukʼarab mutsʼi kwanaze
ɡʔjezdaɡo χadub nil ɡʼuruɬa qʼwatʼibe batʃʼana rokʔoda ɡʔan baqʼwarab χʼalaqʼab qʼadarab ankʔɡo ɡʼaka misrijalda kirniɡi riχʔitʃʼo dida ɡʔjediɡʼanɡo χʼalaqʼal ɡʼatʃi
ɡʔjel χʼalaqʼal qʼadaral ɡʼatʃijaz kwanana dob ankʔabɡo kʔarijab ɡʼaka
ɡʔjel urɡʔire aniɡi ɡʔjezul tʃaχʔal rukʼaqχe χutʼana rukʼaral ɡʼadal χʼalaqʼal qʼadaral ʒal χutʼana ɡʔjel ɡʼatʃi tsinɡi dun makʔidasa wortʃʼana
ɡʔjeldasa χadub dida tsoɡi makʔu biχʔana tso χʼoboda biʒana muɡʔ tsʼubarab ɬikʼab ankʔɡo tʼor
ɡʔjezdaɡo χadub tʼade bakːun batʃʼana tʼjerenab ɡʔodorab buχʼarab ɡʔorotsa baqʼwazaburab ankʔɡo tʼorɡi
ɡʔjel tʼjerenal tʼoraz tʼubanɡo qʼultʃʼana dob ankʔabɡo ɬikʼab tʼor makʔu qʼotʼulel tʃaɡʼazda ritsana ditsa ɡʔjel dida riχʔaral makʔabi amma ɡʔjel makʔabi qʼotʼize baʒaritʃʼo ɡʔjezuqχa
tsinɡi jusupitsa pirɡʼawnasda abuna
pirɡʼawnasda kʼiɡo ɡureb tso makʔu biχʔun buɡo allaɡʔas pirɡʼawnase raɡʔuleb buɡo ʒindirɡo χʼukmu
ankʔɡo kʔarijab ɬikʼab ɡʼaka kːola ankʔɡo son ankʔɡo ɬikʼab tʼorɡi kːola ankʔɡo son ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjeb buɡo tsoɡo makʔu
dozdaɡo χadub tsun ankʔɡo χʼalaqʼab qʼadarab ɡʼaka batʃʼinaɬul maɡʼna kːola χaduseb ankʔɡo son buχʼarab ɡʔorotsa baqʼwazaburab ɡʔodorab ankʔɡo tʼoraɬul maɡʼnaɡi ɡʔjedinabɡo buɡo ɡʔjeb kːola ankʔɡo raqʼul son
ɡʔjeɬin ditsa abuleb bukʼarab allaɡʔas pirɡʼawnase ʒindirɡo χʼukmu raɡʔuleb buɡilan
misrijaɬul tʼolabɡo rakʔalda kutakalda ɡʔarzajab ankʔɡo son batʃʼuneb buɡo
amma ɡʔjezdasa χadub ankʔɡo raqʼul sonɡi batʃʼine buɡo tsebe bukʼarab ɡʔarzaɬijaɬul ɬalkʼtsin naqχe χutʼilaro ɡʔjel sonaz raqʼul ɡʼazabaɬ ulka rakʔɡo tʃʼuntizabila
ɡʼasijab raqʼi bukʼine buɡo ɡʔjeb tsebeseb ɡʔarzaɬijaɬul ɬalkʼtsin naqχe χutʼulareb
kʼiɡo nuχaɬ makʔu biχʔijaɬul maɡʼna kːola rakʼtʃʼun allaɡʔas χʼukmu qʼotʼun bukʼin wa ɡʔjeb ɡʔjes kwatʼitʃʼoɡo tʼubazabize bukʼin
bitʃːante ɡʔanʒe pirɡʼawnas tʼasa wiʃːize iʃ ɬalew wa ɡʼaqʼilaw tʃi wa ɡʔjesda tʼad qʼaze misrijaɬe betʼjerɬi ɡʔabize
bitʃːante pirɡʼawnas tʼolabɡo ulkajalda qχuluqχtʃaɡʼi tʼamize tʼade ʃːoleb buɡeb ankʔabɡo sonaɬ χurisa batʃʼarab tʼorʃːalil ʃːujil butʼa χalqʼaɬuqχa bakʼarize
bitʃːante ɡʔjez bakʼarize ɡʔjel ɬikʼal sonaz ʃːwarab tʼolabɡo batʃʼin wa pirɡʼawnasul amrujaldaɬun ʃaɡʔarazda χʼaluqχen bakʼarulel bakʼal naqχratelaɬul tsʼjezarize
ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuni misrijalda bukʼina dob batʃʼuneb ankʔabɡo raqʼul sonaɬe ɡʼurab naqχratel wa baqʼutsa χwelaro misrijaɬul χalqʼ
pirɡʼawnaseɡi ɡʔjesul qχuluqχtʃaɡʼazeɡi rekʼjee ɡʼuna jusupil ɡʔjel raɡʼabi
ɡʔadinaw tʃi niɬee tʼokʼaw ʃːwelaro jan abuna pirɡʼawnas ʒindirɡo tʃuqʼa raχʔanalda allaɡʔasul ruχʼ buɡo ɡʔasda tʼad
tsinɡi ɡʔjes jusupida abuna
allaɡʔas duje ɡʔjeb kinabɡo raɡʔun buɡeɬul dudasa ɡʼaqʼilawɡi bitʃʼtʃʼi buɡewɡi tʃi tʼokʼaw watularo
ɡʔanʒejaldasa χadub dutsa kwerʃːel ɡʔabize buɡo dir rakʔalda tʼad wa dir χalqʼɡi duqχ ɡʼjenekːize buɡo ɡʼitsʼɡo patʃajasulab daraʒajaɬ dudasa tʼadeɡʼanawɬun wukʼina dun
ɡʼjenekːe jan abuna pirɡʼawnas jusupida tʼolabɡo misrijaɬul kwerʃːeltʃiɬun ɡʔawulew wuɡo ditsa mun
baqχun ɡʔjes jusupil kilʃːida χːuna ʒindirɡo muɡʔru tʼad bikʼarab barʁitʃ ɡʔjes jusupida tʼad retʼana ɬoɬol kunaɬ besːarab χirijab χːamil retʼjel wa mesedil raχasɡi bana ɡʔjesul ɡarbida
patʃaliqχalda kʼiabileb daraʒajaɬul tʃijasul tʃolɡʔokoɡi tʃujalɡi kʔuna pirɡʼawnas jusupije ɡʔjelda rekʼun jusup uneb meχaɬ pirɡʼawnasul tʃaɡʼaz aχʼulaan nakabazda tʃʼa jan ɡʔjedin pirɡʼawnas jusup tʼolabɡo misrijaɬul kwerʃːeltʃiɬun ɡʔawuna
pirɡʼawnas jusupida abuna
ɡʔale dir amru pirɡʼawnasul amru ɡʔanʒejaldasa χadub dur iznu ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo misrijaɬul tʼolabɡo rakʔalda ɬitsaniɡi ja χʼjetʼje ja kwer baʁarize ɡʔjetʃʼo
pirɡʼawnas jusupida tsʼijab tsʼar ɬuna tsafnat paneaχ abun on aburab ʃaɡʔaraɬul kaʃiʃ poti feril jas asenatɡi jatʃana ɡʔjesije ɡʔjedin misrijaɬul tʼolabɡo rakʔalda tʼibitʼana jusupil iχtijartʃiɬi
misrijaɬul patʃajase aj pirɡʼawnase qχuluqχ ɡʔabize bajbiχʔarab zamanalda jusupitsa ban bukʼana ɬeberɡo son wa misrijaɬul tʼolabɡo rakʔaɬuqχ balaɡʔize sapar buχʔana ɡʔjes
ɡʔarzajab ankʔɡo sonaɬ kutakalda ɡʼjemerab tʼorʃːel bakʼarana misrijaɬul rakʔazdasa
ɡʔjel sonazda misrijalda bakʼararab tʼorʃːel jusupitsa ʃaɡʔarazda ɡʔorkʔob bikʔana ʃːibab ʃaɡʔaralda pirɡʼawnase naqχratel ɡʔabuna ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔaralda sweruqχ ruɡel rakʔazdasa bakʼararab tʼorʃːalil
raɬdal saliɡʼan ɡʼjemerab χʼaluqχen bakʼarana jusupitsa ɡʔjeɬul χʼisab ɡʔabitsin tana ɡʼjemerɬijaɬ ɡʔjeb ɡʔabize kʼoleb χʼal bukʼintʃʼo
ɡʔjeb zamanalda ʒeɡi raqʼi bakːilalde on ʃaɡʔaraɬul kaʃiʃ poti feril jas asenatitsa jusupije kʼiɡo was ɡʔawuna
allaɡʔas dida kʼotʃenabuna dir qʼwariɬiɡi ebel insul ruqʼaɬuqχ urqχijaɬul ruχʼiɡi janɡi abun tʼotsewe ɡʔawurasda jusupitsa manasː
dije ɡʼazab ɡʼaqʼuba bukʼarab rakʔalda χur tsʼun batʃʼinabuna dije allaɡʔas inɡi abun kʼiabilesda tsʼar jusupitsa jefraim
misrijaɬul rakʔalda ɡʔarzajab batʃʼinaɬul ankʔɡo son aχiralde ʃːwana
wa jusupitsa tsebekːunɡo bitsun bukʼaralda reqʼon ankʔɡo raqʼul son tʼade ɡʼuntʼana ɡʔjeb raqʼi tʼibitʼana kinalɡo ulkabazda amma misrijalda kisa kibɡo tʼorʃːalil naqχratel ɡʔabun bukʼana
misrijaɬul χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔob raqʼi baʁaridal tʼorʃːel ɡʔarun pirɡʼawnasuqχe ratʃʼine ɬuɡʔana ɡʼadamal tsinɡi ɡʔjes abuna
nuʒ jusupiqχe a wa ɡʔjes aburab ɡʔabe jan
tʼolabɡo ulkajalda tʼibitʼana raqʼi jusupitsa naqχratelaɬul ruqʼzal raɡʔana wa misrijaze tʼorʃːel bitʃize bajbiχʔana ɡʼasijab raqʼi bukʼana misrijalda
kinalɡo rakʔazdasa ɡʼadamal misrijalde jusupiqχe ratʃʼunel rukʼana tʼorʃːel bosize ʃːajɡureɬul tʼolabɡo dunjalalda tʼibitʼana kutakab raqʼi

misrijalda tʼorʃːel buɡebɬi ɬana jaqʼubida wa ɡʔjes wasazda abuna
kidalɬizeɡʼan nuʒ tsotsaqχ ralaɡʔun tʃʼjeze ruɡel
misrijalda tʼorʃːel buɡilan abuleb buɡo niɬɡo raqʼutsa χwelalde ɡʔjenireɡi un tʼorʃːelɡi bosun ratʃʼa
jusupil antsʼawɡo watsas misrijalde sapar buχʔana ɡʔjenisa tʼorʃːel bosize
jusupil tʼul bikʔaraw wats bunjaminin abuni jaqʼubitsa ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ witʃːatʃʼo ɡʔjesije ʃːibɡʼaɡi kːeze ɡurilan χʼinqʼun
tʼorʃːel ɡʔarun misrijalde ratʃʼaral ɡʼadamazul rukːaliɬe kːana ɡʼizrailil wasalɡi tʼolabɡo χanaanaldaɡo raqʼul ɡʼazab reʃːtʼun bukʼindalχa
ɡʔjel ratʃʼarab ulkajaɬul kwerʃːeltʃiɬun jusup wukʼana wa ɡʔjenire ratʃʼaralʃːinal ɡʼadamaze tʼorʃːelɡi ɡʔjes bitʃuleb bukʼana watsal ratʃʼana jusupiqχe wa ɡʼodob ɡʔumerɡi tsun ɡʔjesda tsere nakabazda tʃʼana
ber kʼutʼarabɡo ɬana ɡʔjesda ɡʔjel amma ɡʔjew tʃijar tʃi ɡʼadin tʃʼana wa qχatʃʼɡo ɡʔiqʼana
kisa ratʃʼaral tʃaɡʼi nuʒ in
χanaanaldasa ratʃʼun ruɡo tʼorʃːel bosize jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjez
jusupida watsal ɬaniɡi ɡʔjezda ɡʔjew ɬatʃʼo
ɡʔjezul raqχaɬ ʒindaɡo tsere riχʔun rukʼaral makʔabiɡi rakʼalde ʃːun jusupitsa abuna
nuʒ ruɡo baɬɡojal ʒasusal niʒer ulkajaɬul zaɡʼipal bakʼal ralaɡʔize ratʃʼaral tʃaɡʼi ratula nuʒ
ɡuro niʒer betʼjerɡʔan abun ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjez niʒ ruɡo tʼorʃːel bitʃun bosize ratʃʼaral dur laʁzal
niʒ kinalɡo watsal ruɡo tso insul wasal rakʼ batsʼtsʼadal ɡʼadamal ruɡo niʒ niʒ ruɡo dur laʁzal wa ʒasusalɬunɡi kidaniɡi rukʼintʃʼo
ɡʔjeresi buɡo jan abuna jusupitsa niʒer ulkajaɬul zaɡʼipal bakʼal ralaɡʔize ratʃʼun ruɡo nuʒ
amma ɡʔjez abuna
niʒer dur laʁzaderil antsʼila kʼiɡo wats wukʼana χanaanaldasa tso insul ɬimal ruɡo niʒ ɡʔitʼinaw wats insuda askʼow tana niʒer tso watsɡi tseweɡo tʼaɡʼana
ɡʔjeleχa jan abuna jusupitsa ditsa abitʃʼiʃː nuʒ ʒasusal ruɡilan
ditsa χʼalbiχʔila nuʒer pirɡʼawnasul ɡʼumrujalχʼa ɡʔitʼinaw wats ɡʔaniwe watʃʼintʃʼoɡo nuʒ ɡʔanisa naqχe ine ɡʔjetʃʼo
nuʒer tsojaw witʼje ɡʔjesda χaduw χutʼaral ɡʔanir tusnaqχalda rukʼina tsinɡi balaɡʔila nuʒer ɡʔjel χarbal ritʼaral ruɡiʃːali bitʼarab bitsuneb batitʃʼoni pirɡʼawnasul ɡʼumrujalχʼa nuʒ ʒasusal kːola
tsinɡi jusupitsa ɡʔjel ɬabɡo qʼojaɬ tusnaqχaɬur tʼamuna
ɬababileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjes ɡʔjezda abuna
