ditsa aburab ɡʔabuni nuʒ tʃʼaɡo χutʼila dun allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼuleɬulχa
nuʒ rakʼbatsʼtsʼadal ɡʼadamal ratani nuʒer tsojaw ɡʔaniw tusnaqχaɬuw tʃʼa χutʼaral naqχe a nuʒer raqʼun ruɡel qχizamaze tʼorʃːelɡi bosun
tsinɡi ɡʔitʼinaw watsɡi watʃun tʼad rusːa nuʒer ɡʔjel raɡʼabi ritʼuqχɬani nuʒ tʃʼaɡo χutʼila
ɡʔjel ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize mukʼurɬana
watsasul χʼaqʼ betsʼuleb buɡo niɬeda niɬeda biχʔana dosda tʃʼun bukʼarab qʼo amma kiɡʼan dow ɡʔardaniɡi niɬ ɡurχʼitʃʼo ɡʔjedinɬidalin niɬeda tʼade ɡʔab balaɡʔ batʃʼarab in abun kʼaɬana ɡʔjel tsotsazda
ruwimitsa tʼade ʒubana
ditsa abitʃʼiʃː nuʒeda ɡʔjew wasase kweʃɬi ɡʔabuɡejan nuʒ diqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼo ɡʔanʒe niɬeda betsʼuleb buɡo ɡʔjesul bidul χʼaqʼ
watsazda ɬaleb bukʼintʃʼo ʒider χabar jusupida bitʃʼtʃʼuleb bukʼin jusup ɡʔjelɡun kʼaɬalew wukʼindalχa tarʒamatʃijasul kumekaldaɬun
doweɡʼanɡi un ɡʼodana jusup χaduw askʼowe watʃʼun ɡʔjelɡun kʼaɬana wa watsazda ɡʔorkʔosa ʃimeonɡi tʼasa wiʃːun ɡʔjezul berda tsebe amru ɡʔabuna ɡʔjew wuχʔjejilan
χadub jusupil bujuruqχaldaɬun ɡʔjezul qʼandaɬabi tʼorʃːalil tsʼjezaruna ʃːiwasul qʼandaɬojaɬub ɡʔjesuqχa tʼorʃːaliqχ bosarab ɡʼaratsɡi baχtʃana nuχda χʼaʒaɬuleb kwen tʼjeχɡi kʔuna
ɡʔiralɡi χʼamuzda qʼan watsaz roqʼore tʼadrusːine sapar buχʔana
sordo baze tʃʼarab bakʼalda ɡʔjezul tsojas χʼamije kʼaltsʼi baze ʒindirɡo qʼandaɬojaɬul kʼal bitʃana wa qʼandaɬojaɬul kʼalaldaɡo batana ʒindirɡo ɡʼarats
dir ɡʼarats ɬun buɡo ɡʔanib ɡʔale ɡʔanib dir qʼandaɬojaɬub in aχʼana ɡʔjes
ɡʔab ʃːib allaɡʔas niɬee ɡʔabuleb buɡeb ʒo janɡi abun rakʼ tʼun arab ɡʼadin ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjel ɡʔjebmeχaɬ wa ɡʼjemer χʼinqʼijaɬ sorodana
ɡʔjeb χʼalalda χanaanalde insuqχe tʼad rusːana watsal wa kinabɡo ʒideeɡo ɬuɡʔarab taraɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ ɡʔjesda bitsana
dob rakʔaɬul kwerʃːeltʃi niʒedeχun qχatʃʼɡo kʼaɬana niʒ ʒasusal ruɡilan kːana dosda
niʒetsa abuna niʒ ʒasusal ɡurin rakʼbatsʼtsʼadal ɡʼadamal ruɡin
niʒer antsʼila kʼiɡo wats wuɡin tso insuje ɡʔarural tso wats tʼaɡʼanin tsoɡidaw biʃːunɡo ɡʔitʼinaw χanaanalda insuda askʼow tanin
amma dob rakʔaɬul kwerʃːeltʃijas abuna ɡʔale ɡʔadin χal ɡʔabila ditsa nuʒetsa bitʼarab bitsuneb buɡiʃːali nuʒer tso wats ɡʔaniw te χutʼaralin abuni raqʼun ruɡel qχizamaze tʼorʃːelɡi bosun nuʒerɡo nuχda a
tsinɡi biʃːunɡo ɡʔitʼinaw watsɡi watʃun ratʃʼa ɡʔjebmeχalda ɬala dida nuʒ ʒasusal ɡurel rakʼbatsʼtsʼadal ɡʼadamal rukʼin nuʒer watsɡi naqχe witʃːala dir tʼolabɡo rakʔalda daran bazar ɡʔabize nuʒee iznuɡi kʔjela jan
ʒiderɡo qʼandaɬabi tʃʼjeχʔjeze ɡʔjel ɬuɡʔindal ʃːiwasul qʼandaɬojaɬub batana ɡʼarats ɬurab kisa ɡʔjeb biχʔidal emenɡi wasalɡi kutakalda χʼinqʼana
tsotsada χadur diqχa ɬimal raqχulel ruɡo nuʒetsa jan abuna ɡʔjezul emen jaqʼubitsa jusup tʼokʼaw ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔanʒe ʃimeonɡi ɡʔjetʃʼo bunjaminɡi watʃineqχin wuɡo kinabɡo dida dande baʁana ɡʔanʒe
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ruwimitsa insuda abuna
bunjaminɡi watʃun dun tʼadwusːun watʃʼintʃʼoni dir kʼiɡo was tʃʼwaze kʔjela ditsa dida boʒiɬi ɡʔabun witʼje ditsa ɡʔjew duqχe tʼadwusːun watʃina
amma jaqʼubitsa abuna
dir was nuʒeda tsadaqχ witʃːalaro ditsa ɡʔjesul tʼul bikʔaraw wats χwana bunjamin tsoχʼo χutʼun wuɡo dije nuχda ɡʔjesije qʼwariɬi kːani ʃːib ɡʔabileb nuʒer ɡʼajibaldaɬun dun betʼjer qχaχʼɬaraw χeraw ɡʔjesda χadub buχʼarab rakʼaɬ barzaχalde kːelariʃː

amma raqʼul kutak ʒeɡi tsʼikʼkʼana rakʔalda
misrijaldasa batʃʼarab tʼorʃːel ɬuɡʼarab meχaɬ insutsa wasazda abuna
naqχeɡi dore un tsodaɡʔabɡi tʼorʃːel bosun ratʃʼa jan
amma jaɡʔudatsa abuna
dow tʃijas niʒeda tsʼaqʼ kʔwarun ɬazabuna ɡʔitʼinaw wats tsadaqχ watʃintʃʼoɡo ʒinda riχʔuleb bakʼalde rakːuɡejilan
dutsa ɡʔjew niʒeda tsadaqχ witʃːani duje tʼorʃːel bosize ina niʒ
dutsa ɡʔjew witʃːatʃʼoni ɡʔjenire inaɬul pajda ɡʔjetʃʼo wats watʃintʃʼoɡo ʒinda riχʔuleb bakʼalde rakːuɡejilan ɬazabun buɡeɬulχa dow tʃijas
ʃːajχa nuʒetsa ɡʔab balaɡʔ dide batʃʼinaburab in abuna ɡʼizrailitsa nuʒer tsoɡi wats wuɡilan ʃːaj bitsarab
ɡʔjez ʒawab kʔuna
kinabɡo tsʼjeχedalχa dos niʒerɡo χʼaqʼaɬuɬɡi niʒer ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬɡi emen tʃʼaɡo wuɡiʃːilan ɡʔiqʼana niʒer tsoɡiɡi watsal ruɡiʃːilan tsʼjeχana ɡʔjes tsʼjeχedalin niʒetsa ɡʔjeb bitsarab ɬidaχa ɬaleb bukʼarab ɡʔitʼinaw watsɡi watʃun ʒindiqχe ratʃʼajilan ɡʔjes amru ɡʔabulebɬi
tsinɡi jaɡʔudatsa ʒindirɡo emen ɡʼizrailida abuna
witʃːaj ɡʔjew niʒeda tsadaqχ niʒ χeχɡo nuχda ine wa niʒɡi munɡi niʒer ɬimalɡi raqʼutsa χwetʃʼoɡo rukʼine
betʼjer qʼotʼize kʔjela ditsa ɡʔjew tʼad wusːintʃʼoni ditsa didaɡo tʼade bosila ɡʔjeɬul ɡʼajib duda askʼowe ɡʔjew tʼadwusːun watʃine baʒaritʃʼoni χwezeɡʼan duda tsewe ɡʼajibijawɬunɡi χutʼila dun
ɡʔadin niɬetsaɡo kwalkwalal ɡʔaritʃʼjelani nekʼoɡo kʼitsʼulniɡi doreɡi ʃːun tʼadrusːinaan
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʼizrailitsa abuna
ɡʔjedin qχwan batani ʃːibχa ɡʔabileb nuʒetsa ɡʔadin ɡʔabe ɡʔab niɬer rakʔaɬul niɡʼmatazdasan sajʁatal rose dosije balʔzamɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi ladanɡi maχʼɡʔuinal pitsʼalɡi fistaʃkabiɡi mindalʔɡi
kʼiɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼun ɡʼaratsɡi bose tsadaqχ dob nuʒer qʼandaɬabazuqχ ɬun batarabɡi naqχ busːinabize doba dozul ʁalatʼ kːun buɡo dir χʼisabalda
bunjaminɡi tsadaqχ watʃe wa naqχeɡi a dow tʃijasuqχe
χʼalkʼolew allaɡʔas dow nuʒeda ɡurχʼizaweɡi dowa taraw watsɡi bunjaminɡi dos naqχe ritʃːaze dunin abuni ɬimalazdasa maχʼrumɬize qχwan batani maχʼrumɬun wukʼinaχa
watsaz sajʁatal qʼatʃʼana tsebe bukʼaraldasaɡi kʼiɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼun ɡʼaratsɡi bosana tsadaqχ tsinɡi misrijalde ratʃʼun jusupida tsere tʃʼana ɡʔab nuχalda bunjaminɡi wukʼana tsadaqχ
ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ bunjamin wiχʔarab meχalda jusupitsa ʒindirɡo ruqʼ qʼajaɬul betʼjeraw qχuluqχtʃijasda abuna
ɡʔal tʃaɡʼi diqχe roqʼore ratʃe tso ʒoɡi qχun kwen ɡʔabe ʒaqʼa qʼaɬuda ɡʔjez dirɡun kwen ɡʼaχʔal ɡʔabize buɡo
jusupil bujuruqχ tʼubazabun qχuluqχtʃijas watsal ɡʔjesul bakʼalde ratʃana
amma ɡʔjenire unaɡo nuχda χʼinqʼi rekʼjeɬe kːun watsal tsotsada ɡarɡadize ɬuɡʔana
dob meχalda niɬer qʼandaɬabazuqχ ɬun batarab ɡʼarats sababɬun ratʃunel ratila niɬ dore tʼade kʼantsʼun doz niɬ kːwela wa laʁzalɬun ɡʔanir tʃʼjezarila niɬer χʼamulɡi raqχila
jusupil minajaɬul raɡʔduqχe ʃːwarab meχalda qχuluqχtʃijasda askʼoreɡʼanɡi riɬːun ɡʔjez abuna
betʼjertʃʼaqχad tso kʼaɬaze iznu kʔje tsereɡi tso nuχaɬ ɡʔanire tʼorʃːel bosize ratʃʼun rukʼana niʒ
naqχrusːun unaɡo sordo baze reʃːtʼarab bakʼalda niʒerɡo qʼandaɬabazul kʼal bitʃana niʒetsa niʒer ʃːiwasda qʼandaɬabazul kʼalaldaɡo tʼasa kamitʃʼoɡo batana ʒindi ʒindir ɡʼarats niʒetsa ɡʔjeb naqχbusːun ɡʔanibe bosun buɡo
tsʼijab tʼorʃːaliqχ kʔjeze tʼadeɡi ɡʼaratsɡi bosun buɡo dob meχalda niʒer qʼandaɬabazuqχ ɡʔjeb ɡʼarats ɬitsa ɬurabaliɡi ɬalaro niʒeda
nuʒeda urʁel kːoɡe nuʒ χʼinqʼize bakʼ ɡʔjetʃʼo jan abuna ɡʔjezda qχuluqχtʃijas nuʒer allaɡʔas nuʒer insul allaɡʔas baɬɡo ɬun batila ɡʔjeb ɡʔjenib dob meχalda nuʒetsa kʔurab ɡʼarats diqχe tʼasa kamitʃʼoɡo ʃːwana
tsinɡi ɡʔjes ɡʔazda askʼowe ʃimeon watʃun watʃʼana
ɡʔjel kinalɡo tsadaqχ ɡʔjes jusupil roqʼore ratʃana ɡʔjezul χʼatʼal tʃurize ɬimɡi kʔuna χʼamuze kʼaltsʼiɡi bana
watsaz ʒiderɡo sajʁatal tsere raqχana wa qʼaɬul ɡʼuʒalda jusupida dandtʃʼwaze χʼadurɬana ɡʔjel ɡʔazda abun bukʼana dora qʼade kwanaze ruɡin nuʒilan
jusup roqʼowe watʃʼarab meχalda ɡʔaz ɡʔjesije sajʁatal kʔuna wa ɡʼodob ɡʔumerɡi tsuzabun ɡʔjesda tsebe suʒda ɡʔabuna
tsinɡi ɡʔjezulɡun salam kalamɡi ɡʔabun jusupitsa ɡʔiqʼana
nuʒetsa dida bitsun bukʼaraw nuʒer χeraw emen kin wuɡew ɡʔjew ʒeɡi saχ salamat wuɡiʃː an
ɡʔjesije betʼjerɡi qʼulun watsaz abuna
dur laʁ niʒer emen saχ salamat wuɡo jan
ɡʔjebmeχalda ʒindirɡo tʼul bikʔaraw wats bunjamin wiχʔana jusupida wa ɡʔjes abuna
ɡʔawiʃː dow nuʒer ɡʔitʼinaw wats allaɡʔasul tsʼob ɬeɡi duda dir was in
watsasdeχun rekʼjeɬ ɡʔultʃarab χʼjerenɬi nedeɡʔɬijaɬul karatʃelaɬ jusupil ɡʼodize batʃʼana χeχɡo tsojab roqʼoweɡi ɬuɡʔun ɡʼodana ɡʔjew
tsinɡi berkʼalɡi tʃurun naqχeɡi ɡʔalbaderida askʼowe wiɬːana jusup wa jaχʼ ɡʔabun kwen bosejilan bujurana
jusupije batʼaɡo ɡʔalbaderije batʼaɡo misrijaze batʼaɡo ɬuna kwen misrijazul dinalda reqʼon ʒuɡʔutʼazda tsadaqχ kwanaze ɡʔjezije ɡʔuqʼarab bukʼana
kʼudijasdasa ɡʔitʼinasde ʃːwezeɡʼan irɡadal jusupida tsere ɡʼodor tʃʼjezaruna watsal χʼikmaɬun tsotsaqχ ralaɡʔana ɡʔjel
ʒindirɡo tepsijaldasa kwen bitʼun batʃʼuneb bukʼana ɡʔazije jusupitsa wa bunjaminije kʔoleb butʼa tsoɡidazulaldasa ʃːuɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼarab bukʼana ɡʔjedin jusupida tsadaqχ ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwana ɡʔjeqʼana ɡʔjel

jusupitsa ʒindirɡo qχuluqχtʃijase bujuruqχ kʔuna
ɡʔal tʃaɡʼazul qʼandaɬabi ruɡʼun tsʼjezare batʃːize kʼolebɡʼan tʼorʃːelɡi ban ʃːiwasul qʼandaɬojaɬub ɬe ɡʔjes kʔurab ɡʼaratsɡi
biʃːun ɡʔitʼinasul qʼandaɬojaɬub ɡʼartsuda tsadaqχ dir ɡʼartsul ʃːurunɡi ɬe
jusupitsa abuqχe ɡʔabuna qχuluqχtʃijas
qχaχʼɬi barabɡo χʼamulɡi ratʃun ɡʔalbal nuχda ɬuna
amma watsal ʃaɡʔaraldasa rikʼkʼaɬileldeɡo jusupitsa qχuluqχtʃijasda abuna
χeχɡo dozda χaduw a wa dozda abe ɬikʼɬijaɬuqχ kweʃɬi ʃːaj nuʒetsa ɡʔaburab
dir betʼjerɡʔanas tʃaʁir ɡʔjeqʼoleb ɡʔjedinɡo baɬɡoɬi tʼatinabuleb wa bukʼineseb ɬazabuleb ʃːurun ɡuriʃː ɡʔjeb kʼudijab kweʃɬi ɡʔabun buɡo nuʒetsa jan
ɡʔjezda χaduw ɡʼuntʼidal qχuluqχtʃijas ʒinda tʼadqʼarab ɡʔabun ɡʔjezda ɡʔjel raɡʼabi abuna
watsaz ʒawab kʔuna
ʃːaj niʒer betʼjerɡʔan dutsa ɡʔjedin abuleb allaɡʔas tsʼunaɡi dur laʁzal ɡʔjedinab ʒo ɡʔabijaldasa
tsebeseb nuχaɬ niʒer qʼandaɬabazuqχ batarab ɡʼaratsɡitsin niʒetsa χanaanaldasa tʼad busːinaburab meχaɬ dur betʼjerɡʔanasul roqʼosa ɡʼarats jaɡi mesed kin niʒetsa biqʼuleb
niʒer tsoniɡijasuqχ biqʼarab ʒo batani bitʃːante ɡʔjewɡi tʃʼwaze wa niʒ kinalɡoɡi niʒer betʼjerɡʔanasul laʁzalɬun χutʼize
nuʒetsa abuqχe bukʼine bitʃːante jan abuna qχuluqχtʃijas amma laʁɬun χutʼila biqʼarab ʒindiqχ bataraw tʃi tsoɡidal ritʃːan tela
watsaz χeχɬi ɡʔabun χʼamuzdasa ɡʔiral raqχana wa qʼandaɬabazul kʼalal ritʃana
qχuluqχtʃijas kinazdaɡo irɡadal tʃʼuχʔ bana kʼudijasdasa baqχarab ɡʔitʼinasde ʃːwezeɡʼan ʃːurun bunjaminiqχ batana
tsinɡi tʃara buχʼaral watsaz ʒideda tʼad bukʼarab retʼjel biqχ biqχun bana wa tsʼidasan χʼamuzda ɡʔiralɡi qʼan ɡʔjel ʃaɡʔaralde tʼad rusːana
jaɡʔudaɡi watsalɡi tʼade ʃːwarab meχaɬ jusup ʒeɡi roqʼow wukʼana wa ɡʔal ɡʔjesda tsere nakabazda tʃʼana
jusupitsa ɡʔjezda abuna
kinɡʼaɡi kʼwarab nuʒeda ɡʔjeb iʃ ɡʔabize unɡo nuʒeda ɬalarebiʃː dun ɡʼadinal tʃaɡʼazul baɬɡoɬi tʼatinabize ɡʔunar bukʼunebɬi
duda niʒer betʼjerɡʔanasda abize ʒo ʃːibχa niʒer bukʼineb abun kʼaɬana jaɡʔuda ʃːib bitsun niʒɡo ritʼuqχ ɡʔarilel allaɡʔas tʼatinabuna niʒer ɡʼajib χatʼa ɡʔanʒejaldasa naqχe niʒ rukʼine ruɡo niʒer betʼjerɡʔanasul laʁzalɬun ʃːurun kodob batarawɡi wa tsoɡidal kinalɡoɡi
jusupitsa abuna allaɡʔas tsʼunaɡi dun ɡʔjedinab iʃ ɡʔabijaldasa ʃːurun biqʼaraw tʃi wukʼina dir laʁɬun tsoɡidal saχ salamatɡo insuda askʼore ine beɡʔula
jusupida askʼoweɡʼanɡi qʼan jaɡʔudatsa abuna
ja dir betʼjerɡʔan dije durɡo laʁase iznu kʔje dudeχun kʼaɬaze durɡo laʁasda tsːin baqχunɡe dir betʼjerɡʔan mun pirɡʼawnasda waʃːadaw tʃi wuɡeɬul
dir betʼjerɡʔan dutsa ɡʔiqʼana niʒeda durɡo laʁzaderida niʒer emen wuɡiʃːilan wa niʒer tsoɡi watsal ruɡiʃːilan
niʒetsa duje niʒer betʼjerɡʔanase ʒawab kʔuna niʒer χeraw emen wuɡin wa tsoɡi biʃːunɡo ɡʔitʼinaw watsɡi wuɡin insuje χaradunib ɡʔaburab ɬimer kːola ɡʔjew ɡʔjezul ebelaɬ ɡʔarurazul tsoχʼo ɡʔjew χutʼana tʃʼaɡo ɡʔjesul wats χwana insuje ɡʔjew tsʼaqʼ χirijaw wuɡo
tsinɡi dutsa niʒee dur laʁzaderije amru ɡʔabuna ɡʔjew ɡʔaniwe wiχʔize watʃejilan
niʒetsa duda niʒer betʼjerɡʔanasda abuna ɡʔjes emen reχun teze beɡʔularilan ɡʔjesdasa watʼaɬi insuda χʼjeχʔjeze kʼolarilan
amma dutsa niʒeda dur laʁzaderida abuna ɡʔitʼinaw watsɡi tsadaqχ watʃun ɡuroni niʒ tʼokʼaɬ mun wiχʔuleb bakʼalde rakːuɡejan
niʒ niʒerɡo insuqχe dur laʁasuqχe tʼadrusːarab meχalda niʒetsa ɡʔjesda bitsana dutsa niʒer betʼjerɡʔanas aburabʃːinab
tsinɡi tsodaɡʔabɡi tʼorʃːel bosize ajilan insutsa amru ɡʔaburab meχalda
niʒetsa abuna ɡʔitʼinaw wats tsadaqχ ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo inarilan ɡʔjew tsadaqχ ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo mun wiχʔuleb bakʼalde rakːize niʒee iznu ɡʔjetʃʼilan
ɡʔjebmeχalda niʒer insutsa dur laʁas niʒeda ɡʔadin abuna nuʒeda ɬala dir ɬadutsa dije kʼiɡo was ɡʔawurawɬi
tsojaw tʼaɡʼana ʒanawaraɬ tʃʼwan tʼu tʼun wan watilaχa tʼokʼaw dida wiχʔitʃʼo ɡʔjew
ɡʔanʒe nuʒetsa kʼiabilewɡi watʃun unew wuɡo ɡʔjesijeɡi qʼwariɬi kːani ʃːib ɡʔabileb ɡʔab dir qχaχʼab betʼjeralde balaɡʔɡi reʃːtʼinabun barzaχalde tʼowitʼila nuʒetsa dun in
ɡʔjedinɬidal dida kʼweliʃː insuqχe dur laʁasuqχe ɡʔjediɡʼan dosije χirijaw wasɡi watʃintʃʼoɡo tʼadwusːine
was niʒeda tsadaqχ ɡʔjetʃʼjewɬi biχʔarab laχʼzataɬɡo emen χwela wa dur laʁzal niʒ sababɬun kʼudijab ruχʼaliɬ barzaχalde ina ɡʔjew
ditsa dur laʁas insuje ʃːulijab raɡʼi kʔuna wats tʼadwusːun watʃinilan naɡaɡʔ watʃintʃʼoni χwezeɡʼan insuda tsebe ɡʼajibɡi dida tʼad bukʼinilan
ɡʔanʒe dur laʁ dun tʃʼjezawe ɡʔaniw ɡʔjesul bakʼalda ɡʔjewin abuni watsazda tsadaqχ tʼadwusːine witʃːante
kinχa dun ɡʔjewɡi watʃintʃʼoɡo insuqχe tʼadwusːinew wa ɡʔjedinab balaɡʔaɬ emen tʃʼwani ɡʔjeb kin χʼjeχʔjeleb

jusupida tʼokʼaɬ jaχʼ ɡʔabun baʒaruleb bukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjedinɬidal
kinalɡo qʼwatʼire a jan bujurana jusupitsa ʒindirɡo tʃaɡʼaze
watsalɡun ʒiwɡo tsoχʼo χutʼarab meχaɬ ɡʔjes ɡʔjezda bitsana ʒiwɡo ʃːiw kːolewali
wa bitʃːan ɡʔarakʔɡun ɡʼodana jusup ɡʔjesul ɡʼodi raɡʼana misrijazdaɡi wa pirɡʼawnasul kʼalɡʼajaɬul aɡʔlujaldaɡi
dun jusup wuɡo jan abuna ɡʔjes watsazda unɡo dir emen tʃʼaɡo wuɡewiʃː
amma ɡʔjeb raɡʼidal ɡʼunun tsʼoron χutʼun raɡʼi abize kʼoleb χʼalalda rukʼintʃʼo watsal
askʼoreɡʼan ratʃʼa jan abuna jusupitsa tsinɡi watsal ɡʔjesda askʼoreɡʼan riɬːana
ɡʔale dun jusup nuʒetsa misrijalde witʃaraw nuʒer wats in abuna ɡʔjezda jusupitsa
amma ɡʔjeb sababɬun ɡʔanʒe nuʒeeɡo ɡʼazab kʔoɡe nuʒedaɡo ɡʼajibɡi tʃʼwaɡe allaɡʔasɬidal dun ɡʔaniwe witʼaraw nuʒer ɡʼumru χwasar ɡʔabize
ɡʔale kʼijabɡo ɬaɡʼjel ana raqʼi batʃʼaraldasa ʒeɡi ʃːuɡoɡi sonaɬ ja rekʔi ja ɬiɬi bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo
allaɡʔas nuʒedasa tsewe dun ɡʔaniwe witʼana rakʔaldasa nuʒer naslu tʼaɡʼintʃʼoɡo bukʼine wa kʼudijab tarqχanɬijaldaɬun nuʒer ɡʼumru χwasarɬize
nuʒetsa ɡurew allaɡʔasin dun ɡʔaniwe witʼaraw wa pirɡʼawnasul emenɬunɡi ɡʔjesul buɡebʃːinalda tʼad betʼjerɡʔanɬunɡi misrijaɬul tʼolabɡo rakʔalda kwerʃːeltʃiɬunɡi ɡʔawuraw
ɡʔanʒe χeχɡo insuqχe tʼadrusːa wa ɡʔjesda bitse ɡʔadin abunin jusupitsa allaɡʔas dun tʼolabɡo misrijaɬul kwerʃːeltʃiɬun ɡʔawuna kʼwanaɡʼan χeχɡo diqχe watʃʼa
ɬimalɡun wa ɬimalazul ɬimalɡun kinabɡo ɡʼi botsʼiɡun wa buɡoɬiɡun tsadaqχ mun tʃʼjela dida ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ ɡoʃenaɬul rakʔalda
ɡʔjenib dur tʼalab ɡʔabila ditsa munɡi dur tʼolabɡo qχizan qʼajɡi dur ɡʼi botsʼiɡi jaziqχɬitʃʼoɡo bukʼine ʒeɡi ʃːuɡo sonaɬ raqʼi bukʼine buɡeɬulχa
ɡʔale nuʒeda wa dir wats bunjaminida biχʔuleb buɡo nuʒeda kʼaɬalew tʃi dun jusup wukʼin
insuda bitse misrijalda dir buɡeb kʼudijab adab χʼurmataɬulɡi nuʒeda biχʔarabʃːinaɬulɡi emen χeχɡo ɡʔaniwe watʃe
wa ʒindirɡo wats bunjaminida qʼwalɡi ban ɡʼodana jusup ɡʔjesda qʼwalɡi ban bunjaminɡi ɡʼodana
ɡʔjedinɡo tsoɡidal watsazdaɡi qʼwalalɡi ran ɡʼodana jusup ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjelɡi riɡʔa ritʃun jusupɡun χabaralde ʒurana
jusupiqχe watsal ratʃʼun ruɡilan χabar ʃːwana pirɡʼawnasul kʼalɡʼajaldeɡi pirɡʼawnɡi ɡʔjesul tseresel ɡʼadamalɡi ɡʔjeb χabaraldasa roχana
wa pirɡʼawnas jusupida abuna
watsazda abe χʼamuzda ɡʔiralɡi qʼan χanaanalde tʼadrusːajilan
ɡʔjenisa emenɡi qχizamalɡi ɡʔanire ratʃine misrijaɬul biʃːunɡo ɬikʼabʃːinab kʔjela ditsa ɡʔjezije bitʃːante ɡʔjez ɡʔab niɬer ulkajaɬul ɡʔarzaɬijaldasa lazat bosize
ɡʔjezda abe ɬimalɡi rutʃːabiɡi rekʼine misrijaldasa tʃujalɡun tʃolɡʔakal ratʃejilan wa emenɡi tsadaqχ watʃun ɡʔanire naqχ rusːajilan
ɡʔjenib χutʼarab ʒiderɡo mal mulkaɬul urʁel ɡʔabize kːelaro ɡʔjez misrijalda buɡeldasa ɬikʼab tʼasa biʃːun kʔjela ɡʔjezije
ɡʔjedin ɡʔabizeɡi ɡʔabuna ɡʼizrailil wasaz pirɡʼawnas amru ɡʔaburab qʼaɡʼidajalda tʃujalɡun tʃolɡʔakalɡi kʔuna ɡʔjezije jusupitsa nuχda kwenɡi ɬuna
ɡʔjezul ʃːiwase tsʼijab retʼjelɡi kʔuna bunjaminijejin abuni ɡʔjes ɡʼartsul ɬabnusɡo ʃekelɡi kʔuna ʃːuɡo tsʼijab retʼjelɡi kʔuna
ɡʔjedinɡo insuje ɡʔjes ritʼana antsʼɡo biχʔinχʼamida qʼaral misrijaɬul rakʔaɬul betʃeɬijaldasan χiri χirijal sajʁatal wa antsʼɡo tsʼuχʼamida qʼarab tʼorʃːel tʃed wa tsoɡidabɡi nuχda kwanaze ʒo
nuχda kweʃal pikrabi botʼroɬe ritʃːaɡe
ɡʔjedin ɡʔjel misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire raqχana wa χanaanalde insuqχe tʼadrusːana
jusup tʃʼaɡo wuɡo wa ɡʔjesda kodob buɡo kinabɡo misrijaɬul rakʔ in ɡʔjez aburab meχaɬ jaqʼubil rakʼ tʃʼun χutʼanilan kːana ɡʔjelda boʒize kʼolaroɡo wukʼana emen
amma wasaz ɡʔjesda ʃːwalde ʃːun bitsana jusupitsa aburabʃːinab wa ɡʔjesda ʒindirɡo berazda biχʔana ʒiw watʃine jusupitsa ritʼun ratʃʼaral tʃolɡʔakalɡi tʃujalɡi ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjezul emen jaqʼub ruχʼ χʼal batʃʼun ɬuɡʔana
tʼokʼaɬɡi ʃːibχa dije qʼwariɡʼarab in abuna ɡʼizrailitsa jaqʼubitsa dir was jusup tʃʼaɡo wuɡo ɡʔanʒe dunɡo χwelalde tsewe ɡʔjew wiχʔize ina

ɡʼizrail kinabɡo ʒindirɡo buɡoɬiɡi dande bakʼarun nuχda waqχana beer ʃewajalde ʃːwarab meχalda ʒindirɡo emen isχʼaqʼitsa iman ɬuraw allaɡʔase qʼurbanal ɡʔaruna ɡʼizrailitsa
wa ɡʔjenib qʼasi makʔiɬ ilɡʔam ɬuɡʔun allaɡʔas ɡʔjesde aχʼana
jaqʼub jaqʼub in
ɡʔale dun ilan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʼizrailitsa
allaɡʔas abuna
dun wuɡo allaɡʔ dur insutsa iman ɬuraw allaɡʔ ʃːibɡo χʼinqʼitʃʼoɡo misrijalde a doba ditsa dudasan ɬuɡʔinabila kʼudijab χalqʼ
ditsa kumek ɡʔabila duje misrijalde buχʔarab dur saparalda wa χadub ditsa batʃina dur naslu dobasa qʼwatʼibeɡi jusupitsa ʒindirɡo kweraɬ qʼanʃːizarila dur beral
tsinɡi beer ʃewaɡi tun jaqʼub saparaɬ waqχana
pirɡʼawnas kʔural tʃolɡʔakazda tʼad rekʼinarun rukʼana ɡʼizrailil wasaz emenɡi ɬimalɡi rutʃːabiɡi
tsere qʼotʼun unel ɡʼi botsʼul reqχabiɡi rukʼana wa χanaanalda dande ɡʔaburab ʒiderɡo buɡoɬiɡi bukʼana ɡʔjez tsadaqχ bosun uneb ɡʔjedin ʒindirɡo tʼolabɡo nasluɡun tsadaqχ jaqʼubitsa misrijalde ɡʔiʒra ɡʔabuna
ɬimalɡun ɬimalazul ɬimalɡun ʒindirɡo tʼolabɡo aɡʔlu batʃana ɡʔjes misrijalde
ɡʔale misrijalde ɡʔiʒra ɡʔabural ɡʼizrailil wasazul tsʼaral
jaqʼubije tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw ruwim
ruwimil wasal jenoχ palu χʼjetsron wa karmi
ʃimeonil wasal
jemuel jamin oɡʔad jaχin tsoχar wa χanaanijazulaɬ ɡʔawuraw was ʃaul
lewijil wasal
ɡerʃon keχat wa merari
jaɡʔudal wasal
er onan ʃela parets wa zeraχʼ erɡi onanɡi χwana χanaanalda paretsije ɡʔaruna χʼjetsronɡi χamulɡi
isːaχaril wasal
tola puwa jow wa ʃimron
zewulunil wasal
sered elon wa jaχliel
ruwimɡi ʃimeonɡi lewijɡi jaɡʔudaɡi isːaχarɡi zewulunɡi ɡʔjezul jats dinaɡi kːola jaqʼubije lejatsa paddan aramalda ɡʔarural ɬimal kinawniɡi wasalɡi jasalɡi rikʼkʼun ɡʔjezul ɬeberalda ɬabɡo tʃi wukʼana
ɡadil wasal
tsefon χaɡɡi ʃuni etsbon eri arodi arieli
aʃeril wasal
imnaɡʔ jiʃwaɡʔ jiʃwi wa beriaɡʔ ɡʔjezul jats seraχʼ beriaɡʔil wasal χewer wa malkiel
ɡʔjeb buɡo lawanitsa ʒindirɡo jas lejae ʁarawaʃɬun kʔun jikʼaraj zilpadasan jaqʼubije ɬuɡʔarab naslu antsʼila anɬɡo tʃi
jaqʼubije raχelitsa ɡʔarural wasal
jusupɡi bunjaminɡi
on aburab ʃaɡʔaraɬul kaʃiʃ poti feril jas asenatitsa misrijalda jusupije ɡʔaruna manasːɡi jefraimɡi
bunjaminil wasal
bela beχer aʃbel ɡera naaman eχi roʃ mupim χupim wa ard
ɡʔjeb buɡo raχelidasan jaqʼubije ɬuɡʔarab naslu antsʼila unqʼɡo tʃi
danil was χuʃim
naftalil wasal jaχtseel ɡuni jetser wa ʃilem
ɡʔjeb buɡo lawanitsa ʒindirɡo jas raχelije ʁarawaʃɬun kʔun jikʼaraj bilɡʔadasan jaqʼubije ɬuɡʔarab naslu ankʔɡo tʃi
jaqʼubida tsadaqχ misrijalde ratʃʼana nusal rikʼkʼintʃʼoɡo ɡʔjesul naslujaɬul ɬabqʼojalda anɬɡo tʃi
misrijalda jusupijeɡi ɡʔarun rukʼana kʼiɡojal ɡʔjelɡi rikʼkʼun misrijalde ɡotʃarab jaqʼubil naslujaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo tʃi
jaqʼubitsa jaɡʔuda jusupiqχe tsewe witʼana ɡoʃenalde nuχ ɬazabize ɡʔjel ɡoʃenalde ʃːwaralɡo
tʃolɡʔakazda tʃujalɡi ran jusupɡi ɡʼjedeɡʼana ɡoʃenalde ʒindirɡo emen ɡʼizrailida dandtʃʼwaze emen wiχʔidal ɡʔjesda qʼwalɡi ban ɡʼjemerab meχaɬ ɡʼodana ɡʔjew
tsinɡi ɡʼizrailitsa jusupida abuna
ɡʔanʒe mun tʃʼaɡo dir berazda wiχʔarab meχaɬ χwaniɡi urʁel ɡʔjetʃʼo dije jan
jusupitsa ʒindirɡo kinalɡo watsazdaɡi wa tʼolabɡo insul qχizan aɡʔlujaldaɡi abuna
dun pirɡʼawnasuqχe ineqχin wuɡo diqχe χanaanaldasa watsalɡi kinabɡo dir insul qχizan aɡʔluɡi batʃʼun buɡin abize
ɡʔjel ɡʼuχʔbi ruɡin ɡʼi χʔiχʔulin ɡʔjez ɡʼi botsʼiɡi kinabɡo ʒiderɡo buɡoɬiɡi tsadaqχ batʃʼun buɡin ɡʔjezin abize
pirɡʼawnas ʒindiqχeɡo aχʼarab meχalda nuʒeda ɡʔiqʼani sunduje maχʃːel buɡebilan
nuʒetsa ɡʔadin abe niʒ dur laʁzal niʒerɡo umumul ɡʼadin ɡʔitʼinab qʼojaldasa naqχeɡo ɡʼuχʔbi ruɡo ɡʔjebmeχalda ɡʔjesɡi nuʒ ɡoʃenaɬul rakʔalda tela riχarab ʒoɬun rikʼkʼuneɬulχa misrijaz ɡʼijaweχʔɬi

pirɡʼawnasuqχe wiɬːun jusupitsa ɡʔjesda abuna
dir emenɡi watsalɡi χanaanaldasa ratʃʼun ruɡo ɡʼi botsʼiɡun wa ʒiderɡo buɡoɬiɡun ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjel ɡoʃenaɬul rakʔalde ʃːun ruɡo
jusupitsa watsazul ʃːuɡojawɡi watʃana pirɡʼawnasuqχe
pirɡʼawnas ɡʔiqʼana nuʒer maχʃːel piʃa ʃːibilan ɡʔjezɡi ʒawab kʔuna
niʒetsa dur laʁzaderitsa niʒer umumuzɡo ɡʼadin ɡʼi χʔiχʔula jan
tsoɡi ɡʔjez abuna
niʒ ɡʔab rakʔalde ratʃʼun ruɡo aparaɡzabi χʼisabalda niʒee dur laʁzaderije ɡʼi χʔiχʔize bakʼ ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo buɡo ʃːajɡureɬul χanaanalda kʼudijab raqʼi buɡeɬul ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔarula duda iznu kʔje niʒee dur laʁzaderije ɡoʃenaɬul rakʔalda tʃʼjeze
pirɡʼawnas jusupida abuna
dur emenɡi watsalɡi ratʃʼun ruɡeɬul duqχe
ɡʔab ulka rakʔaɬul biʃːunɡo ɬikʼal bakʼal kʔje ɡʔjezije tʼolabɡo misrijaɬul ulka dur iχtijaralda buɡo ritʃːante ɡʔjel ɡoʃenaɬul rakʔalda tʃʼjeze ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔor maχʃːel buɡel tʃaɡʼi ratani dir reqχabazul tʼalab ɡʔabizeɡi tʼadqʼaj ɡʔjezda
jusupitsa pirɡʼawnasda tsewe watʃana ʒindirɡo emen jaqʼub ɡʔjes pirɡʼawnase barakataɬul duɡʼa ɡʔabuna
tsinɡi ɡʔjes jaqʼubida ɡʔiqʼana
dutsa tʃan son barab in
nusijalda ɬeberɡo sonaɬul sapar ɡʔabuna ditsa ɡʔab dunjalaɬul roqʼob in ʒawab kʔuna jaqʼubitsa dir ɡʼumrujaɬul sonal daɡʔal wa zaχʼmatal rukʼana dir umumuzul ɡʼumrujaɬul sonazde raχunaro ɡʔjel
aχiraldaɡi pirɡʼawnase barakatɡi ɡʔarun jaqʼub ɡʔjesda askʼosa naqχe wiɬːana
pirɡʼawnasul amrujalda reqʼon jusupitsa emenɡi watsalɡi ratʃana misrijaɬul biʃːunɡo ɬikʼab rakʔalde raamses wilajatalde wa ɡʔjenir ɡʔjezije rakʔalɡi kʔuna
jusupitsa insujeɡi watsazeɡi insul tʼolabɡo zurijataɬeɡi kwen tʼjeχɡi tʃʼjezabuna ʒib ʒib qχizamaɬe ɡʔjezul tʃan tʃi wuɡewali χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
aχirɡi batʃʼana kibniɡi buɡʼa roɬ χutʼitʃʼjeb zaman ɡʔjediɡʼanɡi kutakab raqʼi bukʼana dunjalalda misriɡi χanaanɡi tʼuran jaziqχɬana ɡʔjel raqʼul sonaz
ɡʼadamaze tʼorʃːel bitʃun jusupitsa pirɡʼawnasul χazinajalde bakʼarana misrijaɬul rakʔaldaɡi χanaanaɬul rakʔaldaɡi bukʼanʃːinab ɡʼarats
ja misrijalda ja χanaanalda tʼokʼab ɡʼarats χutʼitʃʼjeb meχalda jusupiqχeɡi ratʃʼun kinalɡo misrijaz abuna
ɡʔarula niʒee tʼorʃːel kʔjejan ɡuroni dur berda tsere raqʼutsa χwezeqχin ruɡo niʒ tʼokʼaɬ ɡʼaratsɡi χutʼitʃʼo niʒeqχ
ɡʼarats ɬuɡʼarab batani jan abuna jusupitsa nuʒerɡo botsʼiɡi batʃun ratʃʼa botsʼuqχ χisun kʔjela buɡʼa roɬ
tsinɡi ɡʔjez ʒiderɡo ɡʼi botsʼi batʃun batʃʼana wa jusupitsa bajbiχʔana ɡʼi botsʼuqχ χisun ɡʼadamaze buɡʼa roɬ kʔjeze tʃujazuqχ ɡʼijaqχ tsʼtsʼanazuqχ ɡʼatʃijazuqχ wa χʼamuzuqχ palχʼasil ɡʔjeb sonaɬ ɡʔjes ɡʔjezije tʼorʃːel kʔuna ɡʼi botsʼuqχ χisun
ɡʔjelda χaduseb sonaɬ naqχeɡi ratʃʼana ɡʔjel jusupiqχe wa ɡʔjez abuna
ja niʒer betʼjerɡʔan bitʼaqχe bitsani niʒer ɡʼaratsɡi ɬuɡʼana niʒer botsʼiɡi duqχ buɡo ɡʔanʒe niʒɡoɡi tʃʼoroɡojal χurzalɡi ɡuroni duje niʒer betʼjerɡʔanase kʔjeze tʼokʼab ʃːibniɡi χutʼitʃʼo
dur berda tsere χweze teze beɡʔiliʃːχa niʒɡi niʒer rakʔalɡi dutsa kwaniqχ ritʃun rose niʒɡi niʒer χurzalɡi niʒerɡo χurzalɡun tsadaqχ pirɡʼawnasul laʁzalɬun rukʼinɡo ɬikʼ niʒee niʒee χurib bekʔize χʔon kʔje niʒɡi tʃʼaɡo χutʼize χurzalɡi ɡʼalaχalde sweritʃʼoɡo rukʼine
ɡʔjedin jusupitsa pirɡʼawnase rosana misrijaɬul tʼolalɡo χurzal misrijaz tso χutʼitʃʼoɡo ʒiderɡo χurzal ritʃana ɡʔjesije ɡʔjediɡʼanɡi kutakab bukʼana raqʼi kinalɡo χurzal pirɡʼawnasul mulkɬun ɬuɡʔana
ɡʔjedin ulkajaɬul tso raɡʼaldasa tsoɡidab raɡʼalde ʃːwezeɡʼan kinalɡo misrijal pirɡʼawnasul laʁzalɬun ɬuɡʔinaruna jusupitsa
ɡʼitsʼɡo kaʃiʃzabazul χurzal ritʃun rositʃʼo jusupitsa ʃːajɡureɬul kaʃiʃzabaze pirɡʼawnasdasan napaqʼa tʃʼjezabun bukʼana ɡʔjeɬ χʔiχʔulaan ɡʔjel ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjez ʒiderɡo χurzal ritʃize kːetʃʼo
jusupitsa misrijazda abuna
ɡʔanʒe ditsa nuʒɡi nuʒer χurzalɡi pirɡʼawnase ritʃun rosarab meχalda bose nuʒeeɡo χʔoduje buɡʼa roɬ wa χurzal rekʔje
ɡʔanʒejaldasa χadub χurisa batʃʼaraɬul ʃːuɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa pirɡʼawnase kʔjeze kːola nuʒetsa χutʼarab unqʼɡo butʼa te χʔoduje wa nuʒeeɡi roqʼosezeɡi ɬimalazeɡi kwanije
dutsa χwasar ɡʔabuna niʒer ɡʼumru jan abuna misrijaz mun niʒeda ɡurχʼana niʒer betʼjerɡʔan ɡʔanʒejaldasa naqχe niʒ pirɡʼawnasul laʁzal ruɡo
jusupitsa dob meχalda misrijalda tʃʼjezaburab qʼanun ɡʔabsaɡʼatɡi qʼuwatalda buɡo χurisa batʃʼaraɬul ʃːujil butʼa pirɡʼawnase kʔola ɡʼitsʼɡo kaʃiʃazul χurzabazul betʼjerɡʔanɬun waqχintʃʼo pirɡʼawn
ɡʼizrailal misrijalda tʃʼana wa ɡoʃenaɬul rakʔal ɡʔjezije kʔuna ɡʔjenir ɡʔjezije ɡʼjemeral ɬimal ɡʔaruna wa χalqʼɡi tsʼikʼkʼana
antsʼila ankʔɡo son bana jaqʼubitsa misrijalda kinabniɡi ɡʔjes bana nusijalda kʼiqʼojalda ankʔɡo son
χweze zaman ɡʼaɡarɬidal jusupɡi askʼowe aχʼun ɡʔjes abuna
ja dir was dutsa dir χʼurmat ɡʔabuleb batani dida tʼad kwerɡi ɬun ɡʔjede dutsa dir murad tʼubazabilin wa dun misrijalda wuqʼilarin
dir ruχʼ niɬerɡo umumuzuqχe arab meχalda misrijalda toɡe dun umumuzul χabalaɬ wuqʼize dowe wose
dutsa abuqχe ɡʔabila ditsa jan ʒawab kʔuna jusupitsa
ɡʔjede dida tsewe jan abuna jaqʼubitsa
jusup ɡʔjedana wa busada weɡun wukʼaraw jaqʼubitsaɡi qʼandaɬojalda tʼade betʼjerɡi qʼulizabun suʒda ɡʔabuna

tso zamanaldasan emen untun wuɡin χabar batʃʼana jusupiqχe ɡʔjebmeχaɬ tsadaqχ ʒindirɡo wasal manasːɡi jefraimɡi ratʃun insuqχe wiɬːana jusup
dur was jusup watʃʼun wuɡo duqχe jan abuleb raɡʼarab meχaɬ tʃorχol ruχʼ ʒanɡi bakʼarun jaqʼub busada ɡʼodow tʃʼana
tsinɡi ɡʔjes jusupida abuna
tsebeɡo luzalda χanaanaɬul rakʔalda χʼalkʼolew allaɡʔ
ɡʔjes abuna ditsa dur naslu tsʼikʼkʼinabila ɬimal ɡʼjemeral kʔjela wa dudasan χalqʼazul tʼubarab tʃitʼir ɬuɡʔinabila ɡʔab rakʔɡi abadijaɬeɡo dur naslabaze kʔjela jan
ɡʔale ʒaqʼa ditsa dirɡo wasalɬun ɡʔarulel ruɡo dun ɡʔaniwe watʃʼinaldeɡo misrijalda duje ɡʔarural dur wasal ruwimɡi ʃimeonɡi ɡʼadin jefraimɡi manasːɡi dir wasalɬun rukʼina
χadur ɡʔarural wasal dur rukʼina amma ʒindirɡo kʼudijal watsazul naslabazda ɡʔorkʔore ratʃina wa ɡʔjezul butʼajaldasa irsɡi bukʼina ɡʔjezije
paddanaldasa tʼadwusːun watʃʼunaɡo χanaanalda efratajalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ nuχda χwana dir raχel doja efratajalde bet leχemalde uneb nuχda juqʼana ditsa ɡʔjej
tsinɡi jusupil ɬimalazda ber tʃʼwana ɡʼizrailil wa ɡʔjes ɡʔiqʼana
ɡʔal ʃːal abun
ɡʔal ruɡo ɡʔanir misrijalda allaɡʔas dije kʔural dir wasal abun ʒawab kʔuna jusupitsa
ɡʔanire dida askʼoreɡʼan ratʃe ɡʔjel ditsa ɡʔjezije duɡʼa ɡʔabize jan abuna jaqʼubitsa
χerɬijaɬ berzul kanɬi sun bukʼana ɡʼizrailil tsʼaqʼɡo muqʼsanɡo ɡuroni ʃːibɡo biχʔularoan jusupitsa ɬimal ɡʔjesda askʼoreɡʼan ratʃana ɡʼizrailitsa ɡʔjezda ubatʃal ɡʔaruna karande qʼana
tsinɡi jusupida abuna
mun wiχʔililantsin χʔul bukʼintʃʼo dir ɡʔale allaɡʔas dur ɬimalɡitsin riχʔizaruna
jusupitsa ɬimal insul nakabazdasa naqχe ratʃana wa ɡʼodob betʼjer tsuzeɡʼan insuje suʒda ɡʔabuna
ʒindirɡo kwaranab raqχalda ɡʼizrailil kweɡʼab raqχalda jefraim tʃʼjezawuna ɡʔjes kweɡʼab raqχalda ɡʼizrailil kwaranab raqχalda manasː tʃʼjezawuna wa ɡʔjel ɡʼizrailida askʼoreɡʼan ratʃana
amma ɡʼizrailitsa kwaranab kwer tsebe bitʼun ɡʔjeb jefraimil ɡʔitʼinasul betʼjeralda ɬuna kweɡʼab kwer ɡʔjes manasːil kʼudijasul betʼjeralda ɬuna ɡʔjedin qχantʃil suratalda ɬuna ɡʔjes kweral ɬimalazul butʼruzda
tsinɡi jusupijeɡi ɡʔjesul ɬimalazeɡi barakataɬul duɡʼa ɡʔabuna jaqʼubitsa
dir umumul ibraɡʔimitsaɡi isχʼaqʼitsaɡi ʒindir nuχ kːuraw allaɡʔ
ɡʔawurab qʼojaldasa naqχe ɡʔanʒeɬizeɡʼan dun χʔiχʔaraw dir weχʔ
ʃːibab kweʃɬijaldasa dun χwasarɬizawuraw dir malaik ɡʔarula barakat ɬe ɡʔal ɬimalazda dirɡi dir umumul ibraɡʔimilɡi isχʼaqʼilɡi tsʼar χutʼaɡi ɡʔazuɬ ɡʔazul naslu qʼedɡi ɡʼjemerɬaɡi ɡʔab rakʔalda
jefraimil betʼjeralda insutsa kwaranab kwer ɬun biχʔidal ɡʔjeb insutsa ɬatʃʼoɡo ɡʔaburab ʒo buɡin kːun jusupitsa ɡʔjesul kwer jefraimil betʼjeraldasaɡi bosun manasːil betʼjeralda ɬezeqχin bukʼana
wa ɡʔjes abuna
ɡʔjedin ɡuro dada ɡʔale dije tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw ɡʔasul betʼjeralda ɬe kwaranab kwer
amma insutsa abuna
dida ɬala dir was dida ɬala ɡʔjesdasanɡi kʼudijab χalqʼ ɬuɡʔine bukʼin amma ɡʔitʼinaw wats ɡʔjesdasaɡi tʼadeɡʼanɬila wa ɡʔjesul χʔonaldasan ɡʼjemeral χalqʼal ɬuɡʔina
ɡʔale dob qʼojaɬ ɡʔjezije barakat ɡʔarun ɡʼizrailitsa abural raɡʼabi
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬe barakatalɬun ɬuɡʔina nuʒ
ɡʔjez tsotsaje ɡʔara raχʔi ɡʔabuleɬul abila
jefraimidaɡi dosul wats manasːidaɡi
reɬːinaweɡi allaɡʔas mun in
ɡʔjedin jefraim manasːidasa tʼadeɡʼanɬizawuna ɡʔjes
tsinɡi ɡʼizrailitsa jusupida abuna
kwatʼitʃʼoɡo dun χwela amma allaɡʔas nuʒ reχun telaro wa nuʒerɡo umumuzul rakʔalde tʼadrusːun ratʃina
watsazdasa tʼokʼ ɡʔawun duje kʔoleb buɡo ditsa dunɡo waʁun amorijazuqχa baqχarab rorχatal ʃːobazul meɡʼjeraɬul ʁwelɡi

jaqʼubitsa ʒindirɡo wasal askʼore aχʼana wa ɡʔadin abuna
dida askʼoreɡʼan ratʃʼa ditsa nuʒee χadub bukʼine buɡeb bitsinin ɡʔanʒe
dandeɬe wa ɡʼjenekːe jaqʼubil wasal
ɡʼjenekːe ɡʼizrailiqχ nuʒerɡo insuqχ
ruwim dir tʼotsewesew was dir ɡutʃ
biχʔinab baluʁɬijaɬul tʼotsebeseb piqχ
qʼadru qʼudrataɬul tʼotsebeseb iχtijarɡi dur
amma ɬadal tʃwaχijaldaɡʼanɡi napsalda tʃanɡit baze kʼolarew
tʼotsewesewɬun ɡʔanʒe tʼokʼaɬ wukʼinaro mun
insul tʃʼuʒujaɬul busade waχindal
dir ɡʔjeb busen dutsa qχubɬizabidal
ʃimeonɡi lewijɡi kʼijawɡoɡi wats
ɡʔjezul qχatikʔ χwaltʃen zulmudul jaraʁ
dun ɡʔjezul iʃazul ɡʼaχʔaltʃi ɡuro
ɡʔjezul qʼoqʼajalda ʁorɬɡi dun ɡʔjetʃʼo
ʃːajɡureɬul tsːidakʔje ɡʼadamal tʃʼwana ɡʔjez
wa otsazul ʃːukʼdul qʼotʼana ɡʔjezije buɡeb ɡʼazabaldasa kepɡi bosulaɡo
naɡʼana bataɡi ɡʔjezul tsːidaje
ɡʼasijab waχʼʃijab buɡeɬul ɡʔjezul tsːin
jaqʼubil naslabazuɬ ʃːuʃːazarila ditsa ɡʔjel
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼazuɬ rikʔ rikʔize ɡʔarila
jaɡʔuda
duje naku tʃʼwala dur insul wasaz
tuʃbabazul ʁwanʃːida tʼad bukʼina dur qχat
jaɡʔuda dir was mun ɡʼoloqχanab ʁalbatsʼalda reɬːuna
dawlaɡun tʃanasa busːuneb
ʁalbatsʼaɬ ɡʼadin rakʔalda weɡun ʁorkʔtʃʼjel ɡʔabula ɡʔas
ebelab ʁalbatsʼaɬ ɡʼadin ɡʔjelda qχatʼize kʼolew tʃi ʃːiw wukʼunew
jaɡʔudal kodosa patʃaɬijaɬul ɡʼansa kidaɡo bortilaro
patʃaɬijaɬul ɡʼansa daim ɡʔjesuqχ bukʼina
ɡʔjeɬul unɡo unɡojaw betʼjerɡʔanɬun ʒiw kːolew
wa kinalɡoɡi χalqʼal ʒindije mutʼiɡʼɬulew watʃʼine meχ ʃːwezeɡʼan
ɡʔjes χʼama tsʼolbol ʁabujalda buχʔina
ʁabujaɬul biʃːun ɬikʼab tʃʼoralda kʼjert buχʔina
ʒindirɡo retʼjel ɡʔjes tʃoʁroɬ tʃurila
ɡʼabaɡi tsʼolbol biduɬ tʃurila
tʃaʁiraldasaɡi tʃʼjeɡʼjeral ruɡo ɡʔjesul beral
raχʔdadasaɡi qχaχʼal ruɡo kʼaldir tsabiɡi
zewulun wukʼina raɬdal raɡʼalda
paraχatɡo ɡumi tʃʼoleb raɡʼalɬijalda
sidonalde ɡʼuntʼila ɡʔjesul ɡʼorqχi
isːaχar qʼuwatab χʼama
rutʃnazda ɡʔorkʔow weɡun wuɡew
raχʼat χʼalχʔijaɬe ɬikʼab
ɡʔajbatab rakʔ ʒindir bukʼin biχʔidal
ɡʔjes bitʃːala ʒindirɡo muʁzada tʃijar ɡʔir batʃːize
wa zulmujalda ʁorkʔ laʁɬun χʼaltʼize raziɬila
dan wukʼina ʒindirɡo qʼawmaɬul betʼjerɬuda
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬul tsojab qʼawmalda tʼad
witʃːante dan wukʼine nuχda boroχʔɬun
suqχmaqχazda zaɡʔrujab boroχʔɬun
tʃol boχalda χʼantʃʼuleb
wa rekʼaraw ʁorkʔje reχuleb
oɡʔ betʼjerɡʔan tsoχʼo dutsa χwasar ɡʔarilin buɡo dir χʔul
ɡadida tʼade kʼantsʼize qʼerkʔolel rukʼina qχatʃaʁal
amma ɡʔjezda χaduwɡi ɬuɡʔun ɡʔjes ɡʔjel ʒalɡo talawur ɡʔarila
aʃeril kwen tʼjeχ ɡʔarzajab
χanzabazda reqʼaral niɡʼmatal tʃʼjezarila ɡʔjes
naftali erkenab ʒajran
ɡʔajbatab naslujaɬul emen
jusup reɬːuna barakatab tsʼolbol ʁabujalda ɡʼjemerab piqχ kʔoleb
itsːuqχ ʒib biʒarab wa ʁabujaɬul tʃʼoratsa qʼedɡo batsarab
kiɡʼan kutakalda ɡʔjesije zaral ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔaniɡi
rokʔuqʼɡo ɡʔjesda tʃʼoral retʃʼtʃʼaniɡi
ɡʔjesul tʃʼorbutʼaɬul butʼ kidaɡo tʃutʃilaro
ɡʔjesul kwerzul qʼuwatɡi tʼaɡʼinaro ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeɬije kʔutʃʼ
jaqʼubil qʼudrataw betʼjerɡʔanasul qʼwakʼarab kwer wa
ɡʼizrailije kʔuruɬunɡi weχʔɬunɡi tʃʼarasul tsʼar
ɡʔjew dur insul allaɡʔ ɡʔjes χadubɡi kwerbaqʼaɡi duje
χʼalkʼoɬi tsʼikʼkʼaras duje barakat kʔjeɡi
zodil borχaɬudasanɡi
raɬdal ʁwariɬudasanɡi
ɡʔjes duje ɡʼjemeral ɬimal kʔjeɡi ɡʼi botsʼul tʼintʃʼ qʼed tsʼikʼkʼinabeɡi
dur insudasan batʃʼuneb barakat
nekʼsijal muɡʼruzul barakataldasaɡi
abadijal ɡoχʼazul barakataɬul ɡʔarzajal iχːazdasaɡi tʼadeɡʼanab buɡo
bitʃːante ɡʔjeb tʃwaχize jusupil betʼjeralde
watsazda ɡʔorkʔow tʼasa wiʃːarasde
bunjamin qχantʼarab batsʼalda reɬːuna
radalɡo tʃanil ɡʔan qχarsuneb
qʼasi dawla tʼutʼun baleb
ɡʔjele ɡʼizrailil antsʼila kʼijabɡo qʼawmaɬul butʼrulɡi ɡʔjezda insutsa abural aχirisel barakataɬul raɡʼabiɡi ʃːibab qʼawmaɬe χasab barakat kʔuna
jaqʼubitsa wasazde ɡʔadinab wasijat ɡʔabuna
kwatʼitʃʼoɡo dun dirɡo umumuzda χaduw ina nuʒetsa dun wuqʼe umumuzda askʼow χitijaw efronil χurib buɡeb noqχoda
ɡʔjeb noqχo buɡo χanaanaɬul rakʔalda mamrejalda askʼob maχpelajaɬul χurib noqχoɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjeb χur ibraɡʔimitsa χitijaw efroniqχa bosun bukʼana χabalaze teze
ɡʔjenir tsotsada askʼor ruqʼun ruɡo ibraɡʔimɡi ɡʔjesul ɬadi saraɡi isχʼaqʼɡi ɡʔjesul ɬadi riwkaɡi ɡʔjenijɡo ditsa lejaɡi juqʼana
dob χurɡi χurib buɡeb noqχoɡi χitijazuqχa rosaral ruɡo
wasaze ɡʔjedinab wasijatɡi ɡʔabun jaqʼub busada weɡana wa ɡʔjesul ruχʼ bosana ɡʔjew ʒindirɡo umumuzda χaduw ana

insul ʒanazajalda qʼwalɡi ban ɡʼjek ɡʼjekijalda ɡʼodana jusup ɡʔjesul ɡʔurmada ubatʃal ɡʔaruna
wa ʒindirɡo toχturzabaze ɡʔjes bujuruqχ kʔuna maχʼ baqχine bitʃːalarel darabiɡi ɡʔarun ɡʼizrailil ʒanaza qʼatʃʼajilan toχturzabi ɡʔjebsaɡʼataɬɡo ɡʔjesul bujuruqχ tʼubazabize ɬuɡʔana wa
ɡʔjeɬije tʃʼjezaburab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ kʼiqʼoɡo qʼojalda ʒanib darabiɡi ritʃːan qʼatʃʼana ʒanaza misrijaz ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo qʼojaɬ maɡʼu baqχana ɡʔjesda χadub
tʃʼjeɡʼjer bajaɬul bolʒal indal jusupitsa pirɡʼawnasul tseresel tʃaɡʼazda abuna
dije ɬikʼɬi ɡʔabun nuʒetsa pirɡʼawnasda dir raqχaɬ abe
dir insutsa dun ɡʔjedizawun wuɡo χwarab meχalda ʒiw ʒindije tsebekːunɡo qʼatʃʼarab χabaɬ χanaanalda wuqʼejilan beɡʔuleb batani witʃːante dun emen wuqʼize ine ɡʔjewɡi wuqʼun dun tʼadwusːun watʃʼina
pirɡʼawnas abuna
duje nuχ bitʼaɡi dutsaɡo ɡʔjedarab ɡʔa tʼubazabun emen wuqʼize a jan
jusup emen wuqʼize ine nuχda waqχana ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ ana pirɡʼawnasul kinalɡo tseresel tʃaɡʼiɡi ɡʔjesul tʃʼuχʼbi χʼakimzabiɡi tʃʼaχʼijal qχuluqχtʃaɡʼiɡi misrijaɬul kʼudijal tʃaɡʼiɡi
jusupil qχizanɡi ɡʔjesul kinalɡo watsalɡi insul aɡʔlu qʼedɡi ɡʼitsʼɡo ɡʔjezul ɬimalɡi botsʼiɡi ɡuroni χutʼitʃʼo ɡoʃenaɬul rakʔalda
ran tʃujalɡun tʃolɡʔakalɡi tʃotʼaqχabazul qʼoqʼaɡi tsʼaqʼ ɡʼjemerab χalqʼɡi bukʼana ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ
iordan baχun tsebeχun buɡeb atadil ɡʔotsʼire ʃːwedal ɡʔjenib ɡʔjez kutakalda maɡʼu baqχana ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʼodana ɡʔjel jusupil insuda χadur
atadil ɡʔotsʼib ɡʼoduleb ɡʼalam biχʔidal ɡʔjeb rakʔalda ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel χanaanijaz tsotsazda abuleb bukʼana misrijal ɡʼodulel ruɡeb kuts biχʔulariʃː ɡʔjedinɬidalin iordan baχun tsebeχun buɡeb ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tsʼarɡi awel mitsraimilan ɬurab
palχʼasil ɡʼizrailil wasaz insul wasijat tʼubazabuna
ɡʔjesul ʒanaza χanaanalde bosana wa tsebeɡo ibraɡʔimitsa χabalaze bukʼine χitijaw efroniqχa bosarab mamrejalda askʼob maχpelajaɬul χurib buɡeb noqχoda buqʼana
χwelɡi buqʼun jusupɡi ɡʔjesul watsalɡi ɡʔjesul emen wuqʼize ratʃʼun rukʼaralʃːinalɡi misrijalde tʼad rusːana
ɡʔanʒe emen χun χadub jusupil watsaz pikru ɡʔabuna niɬetsa ʃːib ɡʔabileb jusupil niɬeda ʒeɡi tsːin baqχun batani wa niɬetsa ɡʔjesije ɡʔaburabʃːinab kweʃɬi betsʼize ɡʔjesda rakʼalda batani
wa ɡʔjez jusupiqχe χabar bitʼana
χwalda tsebe insutsa wasijat ɡʔabuna
niʒetsa duda abejila ʒintsa duda ɡʔaruleb buɡin watsazul munaɡʔaldasa ɡʔjezul ɡʼajib χatʼajaldasa ɡʔjez duje ɡʔaburab kweʃɬijaldasa tʼasaɬuɡʔajilan ɡʔjedinɬidal niʒɡi dur insul allaɡʔasul laʁzal ruɡeɬul niʒeda tʼasaɬuɡʔa
ɡʔjeb ruɡʔjel batʃʼindal ɡʼodana jusup
ratʃʼun watsazɡi ɡʔjesda tsere nakabazdaɡi tʃʼun abuna
ritʃːante niʒ dur laʁzalɬun rukʼine jan
nuʒ χʼinqʼuɡe jan ʒawab kʔuna jusupitsa dun allaɡʔiʃː wuɡew
nuʒetsa dije kweʃɬi urʁana amma allaɡʔasul qʼadaraldaɬun ɡʔjeb ɬikʼɬijalde swerana ɡʔjeb sababɬun kiɡʼan ɡʼjemeral tʃaɡʼiχa χwasarɬaral
ɡʔanʒe nuʒ sunkʔaniɡi χʼinqʼize kːelaro ditsa χʔiχʔila nuʒɡi nuʒer ɬimalɡi
ɡʔjel raɡʼabaz watsal ɡʼodore ritʃːazaruna wa ɡʔjesul χʼjerenab kʼaɬajaɬ ɡʔjezul rakʼaze asar ɡʔabuna
ɡʔjedin misrijalda ɡʼumru ɡʔabuna jusupitsa ʒindirɡo insul kinabɡo aɡʔlu qʼedɡun tsadaqχ nusijalda antsʼɡo son bana ɡʔjes
ʒindirɡo was jefraimil ɬimalɡi wa ɡʔjezul ɬimalɡi riχʔana jusupida ɡʔjedinɡo manasːil was maχirije ɡʔarural ɬimal riχʔizeɡi ʃːwana ɡʔjesije
dun kwatʼitʃʼoɡo χwela jan abuna tso qʼojaɬ jusupitsa watsazda amma allaɡʔasul raχʼmu tsʼob nuʒede reʃːtʼarab ɡʔjew nuʒee kumekaɬe ɬuɡʔarab wa niɬee kʔjelilan ibraɡʔimijeɡi isχʼaqʼijeɡi jaqʼubijeɡi ɡʔjew ɡʔjedun wukʼarab rakʔalde nuʒ ɡʔanisa naqχe ratʃuneb qʼo χʼaqʼɬunɡo tʼade ʃːweze buɡo
tsinɡi jusupitsa ɡʼizrailil wasal ɡʔjedizaruna allaɡʔasul raχʼmu tsʼob reʃːtʼarab wa ɡʔjezije kumekaɬe ɡʔjew ɬuɡʔarab meχ batʃʼindal ʒindir ʒanaza ɡʔjez misrijaldasa naqχe bosililan
nusijalda antsʼɡo son barab meχaɬ jusup χwana ɡʔjesul ʒanaza maχʼ baqχine wa turize bitʃːalarel darabazɡi qʼatʃʼan misrijalda tabutaɬub ɬun tana

ʒindi ʒindir qχizan aɡʔluɡun misrijalde ɡʼizrailɡun jaqʼubɡun ratʃʼaral ɡʔjesul wasazul tsʼaral ɡʔadinal rukʼana
ruwim ʃimeon lewij jaɡʔuda
isːaχar zewulun bunjamin
dan naftali ɡad wa aʃer
kinawniɡi ɡʔjezul aj jaqʼubil naslujaɬul tʃaɡʼazul dob meχalda misrijalda tʃʼjej ɡʔabun wukʼaraw jusupɡi maɬun wukʼana ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo tʃi
zaman ana jusupɡi ɡʔjesul watsalɡi ɡʔjezul ɡʼjelaɬul tʼolalɡo ɡʼadamalɡi χwana
ɡʼizrailaze ɡʼjemeral ɬimal ɡʔaruna ɡʔjezul qʼadar wa ɡʔjezul ɡutʃ tʼadejaldasa tʼade tsʼikʼkʼana wa tʼolabɡo ulkajalda tʼibitʼana ɡʔjezul χalqʼ
ɡʔorkʔob zaman ana wa misrijalda waqχana jusupil χʼaqʼaɬuɬ ʒinda ʃːibɡo ɬalarew tsʼijaw patʃa
ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo χalqʼalda abuna
ralaɡʔje ɡʼizrailal χʼalkʼun ɡʼjemerɬulel wa niɬedasaɡi tsʼaqʼɡo qʼuwatalɬun ɬuɡʔunel ruɡo
niɬ tsʼodorɡo χʼaltʼizin ɡʼizrailal ʒeɡi ɡʼjemerɬani wa ɡʔjeb meχalda raʁɡi kːani ɡʔjel niɬer tuʃbabiɡunɡi tsoɬun niɬeda dande raʁize beɡʔula wa niɬer ulkajaldasa naqχe ine beɡʔula
zaχʼmatab χʼaltʼudaɬun ɡʼizrailazul tatu χwezabizeɬun ɡʔjezije tʼadtʃaɡʼi tana misrijaz wa ɡʔjezda razaruna pirɡʼawnase naqχratel ʒanib tsʼunize pitom wa raamses abural ʃaɡʔaral
amma zulmu tsʼikʼkʼinabunaɡʼan ɡʼizrailazul qʼadarɡi tsʼikʼkʼuneb bukʼana wa misrijazda kʼudijab χʼinqʼi retʃʼtʃʼana
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjez ʒeɡi tsʼaqʼ ɡurχʼjel tun χʼaltʼize tʼamulel rukʼana ɡʼizrailal
ɡʔjezul ɡʼumru kʔoɡʼɬizabuna χʼatʼ buqχize samanaɬul kirpitʃal qʼotʼize wa χurzabaqχ χʼaltʼize tʼamun wa ɡurχʼjel raχʼmu tun kinabniɡi bakʼab χʼaltʼi ɡʔabize tʼamun
misrijaɬul patʃajas ʃifra wa pua abulel ʒuɡʔutʼazul tʃʼaraqχabaze
bujuruqχ kʔuna
ʒuɡʔutʼ rutʃːabaz ɬimer ɡʔabuleɬul nuʒeda biχʔani was ɡʔawulew wukʼin χwezawe ɡʔjew jas ɡʔajulej jiɡoni tʃʼaɡo te
amma tʃʼaraqχabi allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼaral rukʼun ɡʔjez misrijaɬul patʃajasul bujuruqχ tʼubazabitʃʼo wasal tʃʼaɡo tolel rukʼana
tsinɡi misrijaɬul patʃajas tʃʼaraqχabi tʼade aχʼana wa ɡʔjezda abuna
ʃːaj nuʒetsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuleb ʃːaj nuʒetsa wasal tʃʼaɡo tolel ruɡel
tʃʼaraqχabaz pirɡʼawnasda abuna
ʒuɡʔutʼazul rutʃːabi misrijaɬul ɡʼadal ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjel qʼwakʼaral ruɡo tʃʼaraqχabi tʼade ʃːwelaldeɡo ɬimer ɡʔabun batula ɡʔjez
ɡʔjedin ɡʔaburaɬuqχ allaɡʔas sunduɬɡo kwerbaqʼuleb bukʼana tʃʼaraqχabaze ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼɡi ʒeɡi ɡʼjemerɬana wa tʼadejaldasa tʼade ʃːulaɬuleb bukʼana
tʃʼaraqχabi allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼaral rukʼindal ɡʔjes ɡʔjezul qχizan ruqʼaldeɡo barakat reʃːtʼinabuna
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ pirɡʼawnas tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬe bujuruqχ kʔuna
ʒuɡʔutʼaze ɡʔawuraw ʃːiwaw was ɡʼuruɬe reχe jasal tʃʼaɡo te jan

lewijil kʔibilaɬul tso kinawaliɡo tʃijas ɡʔjebɡo kʔibilaɬul ɡʼadan ɬadiɬun jatʃana
ɡʔjej ɡʼadanaɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana wa ɡʔjeɬ was ɡʔawuna was kutakalda bertsinaw wukʼinɡi biχʔun ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjew ɬabɡo motsʼaɬ waχtʃana
amma tʼokʼaɬɡi ɡʔjew waχtʃize res qʼotʼidal ɡʔjeɬ mutsʼidul ɡʔaburab ɡʔjeɡʔ bosana wa ɡʔjelda qχilɡi pitsʼɡi baχana tsinɡi ɡʔjenib ʒanib ɬuna ʒindirɡo ɬimer wa ɡʔjeɡʔ ɡʼurul raɡʼalda mutsʼiduɬ ɬuna
ɡʔjesul jatsin abuni daɡʔaj dojeɡʼanɡi tʃʼun ɡʔjeb kinaɬulɡo ʃːibdaj kːelajan balaɡʔun jikʼana
ɡʔjeb meχalda pirɡʼawnasul jas jatʃʼana ɡʼurul raɡʼalde tʃwerdeze ʒindirɡo ʁarawaʃalɡun tsadaqχ mutsʼijalda ɡʔorkʔob buɡeb ɡʔjeɡʔ biχʔana ɡʔjelda wa ɡʔjeɬ ʒindirɡo ʁarawaʃ jitʼana ɡʔjeb bosize
ʒanije jakːidal ɡʔjenib ɡʔitʼinab ɬimer bukʼin biχʔana ɬimer ɡʼoduleb bukʼindal ɡʔjelda rakʼɡi ɡurχʼun ɡʔjeɬ abuna
ɡʔab ʒuɡʔutʼazul ɬimer batila jan
tsinɡi ɬimadul jatsaɬ pirɡʼawnasul jasalda abuna duje ɡʔjeb ɬimer χaχizabize tso ʒuɡʔutʼaj jalaɡʔize un ɬikʼ ɡurodaj dun in
pirɡʼawnasul jasaɬ abuna ɬikʼ buɡo a jan
ineɡi un jasaɬ ɬimadul ebel aχʼun jatʃʼana
pirɡʼawnasul jasaɬ ɡʔjelda abuna
ɡʔab ɬimer batʃe wa kerenɡi kʔun χʔiχʔje dije bukʼine ditsa ɡʔjeɬuqχ duje muχʔ kʔjela jan
ɡʔjej ɡʼadanaɬ ɬimer ʒindiqχeɡo batʃana wa kerenɡi kʔun χʔiχʔana
was kʼudijaw ɡʼjedal ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjew pirɡʼawnasul jasaɬuqχe ʃːwezawuna ɡʔjeɬɡi ɡʔjew ʒindirɡo wasɬun χʔiχʔana
ditsa ɬadaɬa qʼwatʼiwe waqχana ɡʔaw inɡi abun pirɡʼawnasul jasaɬ ɡʔjesije musa
qʼojal ana sonal swerana musa kʼudijaw ɡʼuna tso qʼojaɬ ʒindirɡo watsazuqχe ʒuɡʔutʼazuqχe wiɬːana musa wa ɡʔjesda biχʔana ɡʔjez ɡʔabuleb buɡeb zaχʼmatab χʼaltʼi misrijazul tsojas ɡʔjesul χalqʼtsojaw ʒuɡʔutʼaw wuχulew wukʼin biχʔana musada
raqχ raqχalde walaɡʔana ɡʔjew wa ʃːiwɡo tʃi sweruqχ ɡʔjetʃʼjebɬiɡi biχʔun ɡʔjes misrijaw tʃʼwana wa ɡʔjesul ʒanaza saluɬ baχtʃana
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ qʼwatʼiwe waqχindal ɡʔjesda biχʔana kʼiɡo ʒuɡʔutʼaw tsotsaɬ waʁulew dandijaw ʒinditsa qʼwarid ɡʔawulesdeχun ɡʔjes abuna ʃːaj dutsa durɡo ɡʔalmaʁ wuχulew in
dosɡi abuna niʒer tʼadtʃiɬun wa diwantʃiɬun ɬitsa mun taraw misrijawɡo ɡʼadin dunɡi tʃʼwazetsin ɡuriʃː mun urʁulew wuɡew in
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musa χʼinqʼana wa ɡʔjes pikru ɡʔabuna χʼaqʼiqʼataldaɡi ɡʔab iʃ qʼwatʼibe ɬan buɡo jan
ɡʔjeb iʃaɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ raɡʼana pirɡʼawnasdaɡi wa ɡʔjes musa tʃʼwaze χʼukmu qʼotʼana amma musa pirɡʼawnasdasa ɬutun midjanaɬul rakʔalde ana wa ɡʔjenib tso ʁujalda askʼob reʃːtʼjen ɡʔabuna
midjanaɬul kaʃiʃasul ankʔɡo jas jikʼana ɡʔjel ratʃʼana ʁujaɬuqχe wa ʒiderɡo insul ɡʼi ɡʔjeqʼeze rusbi ɬadal tsʼjezarize ɬuɡʔana
amma tsoɡidal ɡʼuχʔbi ratʃʼun ɡʔjez ɡʔjel naqχe qʼotʼana ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musa jasaze χʼalaje waqχana wa ɡʔjezul ɡʼiɡi ɡʔjeqʼezabuna
ʒiderɡo emen reɡueliqχe tʼadrusːindal ɡʔjes jasazda tsʼjeχana
kin nuʒ ʒaqʼa ɡʔadin χeχɡo ratʃʼaral in
ɡʔjez abuna niʒ naqχe qʼotʼize ɡʼuχʔbi ɬuɡʔindal tso kinawaliɡo misrijaw niʒee χʼalaje waqχana ɬim batʃːize wa ɡʼi ɡʔjeqʼezabize niʒee kumektsin ɡʔabuna ɡʔjes in
kiwχa ɡʔjew wuɡew in tsʼjeχana ɡʔjes jasazda ʃːaj nuʒetsa ɡʔjew dowa taraw kwanaze aχʼje dow
musa raziɬana ɡʔjew tʃijasul bakʼalda tʃʼjeze wa ɡʔjes musaje ʒindirɡo jas tsiporaɡi ɬadiɬun kʔuna
ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjesije was ɡʔawuna wa musatsa ɡʔjesda ɡerʃom
ɡʼjemerab zamanaldasan misrijaɬul dow patʃa χwana χʼaltʼul bakʼɬijaɬ ɡʼazab ɡʼaqʼubajalda kumek ɡʔarun uɡʔdileb bukʼana ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ wa ɡʔjezul uɡʔdi allaɡʔasuqχe ʃːwana
allaɡʔasda raɡʼana ɡʔjezul uɡʔdi ziɡardi wa allaɡʔasda rakʼalde ʃːwana ibraɡʔimilɡun isχʼaqʼilɡun wa jaqʼubilɡun ɡʔaburab ʒindirɡo qʼotʼi
ɡʔjezda buɡeb χʼalɡi biχʔun allaɡʔas ɡʔjezije kumekaɬe waqχine χʼukmu ɡʔabuna

musa wukʼana ʒindirɡo wakʔad midjanaɬul kaʃiʃ itrol
ɡʔjenib zazil qχarqχida rekʼarab tsʼadul sipatalda betʼjerhanasul malaik reʃːtʼana ɡʔjesuqχe musa balaɡʔula qχaraqχ tsʼadutsa buχʼuleb bukʼuna amma buχʼun ɬuɡʼularo
musatsa pikru ɡʔabuna
χalɡʔabizin tso ɡʔab kʼudijab χʼikmataɬuqχ tsʼa rekʼarab qχaraqχ ʃːaj buχʼun ɬuɡʼularebali biχʔize
betʼjerhanasda biχʔana ɡʔjew ɡʔjeɬuqχ walaɡʔize watʃʼunew wukʼin wa qχarqχida ʒanisan allaɡʔas ɡʔjesde aχʼana
musa musa jan
ɡʔjes ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔale dun in
allaɡʔas abuna ɡʔaniweɡʼan watʃʼunɡe χʔital tʼasa raqχe ʃːajɡureɬul dutsa χʼjetʼje tʃʼarab bakʼ χirijab bakʼ kːola
dun wuɡo dur umumuzul allaɡʔ ibraɡʔimilɡi isχʼaqʼilɡi jaqʼubilɡi allaɡʔ
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musatsa ʒindirɡo ɡʔumer baχtʃana allaɡʔasda bertʃʼwaze χʼinqʼun
betʼjerhanas abuna
dida tsebeɡo biχʔuleb buɡo misrijalda buɡeb dir χalqʼaɬul qʼwariɬi wa dida raɡʼuleb buɡo zulmutʃaɡʼazul kwerʃːalikʔ ruɡel ɡʔjezul uɡʔdi ziɡardi dida ɬala ɡʔjezije buɡeb ɡʼazab
ɡʔanʒe dun watʃʼun wuɡo misrijazul kwerʃːalikʔa ɡʔjel tarqχan ɡʔarize wa ɡʔjezul rakʔaldasa ɡʔjel naqχe ratʃine ditsa dirɡo χalqʼ batʃina ɬikʼab wa ɡʼatʼidab raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb rakʔalde χanaanijazul χitijazul amorijazul perizijazul χiwijazul wa jewusijazul rakʔalde
dida raɡʼun buɡeɬul ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬul uɡʔdi dida biχʔana misrijaz ɡʔjezije ɡʔabuleb buɡeb waχʼʃijab zulmu
ɡʔjedinɬidal ditsa mun witʼulew wuɡo pirɡʼawnasuqχe ɡʔanʒe mun a wa misrijaldasa qʼwatʼibe batʃe dir χalqʼ ɡʼizrailil naslu
musatsa allaɡʔasda abuna
ʃːiw tʃi kːolew dun pirɡʼawnasuqχeɡi un ditsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼibe batʃine kːani
allaɡʔas abuna
dun wukʼine wuɡeɬul duda tsadaqχ ɡʔale mun ditsa witʼun wukʼinaɬe duje ɡʼalamat misrijaldasa dutsa χalqʼ qʼwatʼibe batʃun χadub nuʒetsa allaɡʔase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabe ɡʔale ɡʔab meɡʼjeralda
tsinɡi musatsa allaɡʔasda abuna ɡʔale watʃʼina dun ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬuqχe wa ditsa ɡʔjezda abila nuʒer umumuzul allaɡʔas witʼana dun nuʒeqχe jan ɡʔjezin abuni tsʼjeχela dida tsʼar ʃːib ɡʔjesda jan ʃːibilan ditsa ɡʔjezda abileb
allaɡʔas musada abuna
dun kːola dun wuɡew ɡʔjedin abe dutsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda dun wuɡew abun tsʼar buɡes witʼana dun nuʒeqχe jan
tʼadeɡi abuna allaɡʔas musada
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɡʔadin abe nuʒer umumuzul betʼjerhan
ineɡi un ɡʼizrailaɬul kʼudijal tʃaɡʼi dande rakʼare wa ɡʔjezda abe nuʒer umumuzul betʼjerhan allaɡʔ ibraɡʔimil isχʼaqʼil wa jaqʼubil allaɡʔ zaɡʔirɬana dije wa ɡʔjes abuna dida ditsa muχʼkanɡo χal ɡʔabuna wa dida biχʔana misrijalda nuʒee ɡʔabuleb buɡebʃːinab
ɡʔale dir amru ditsa nuʒ tarqχan ɡʔarila misrijaɬul zulmujaldasa wa ratʃina raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb χanaanijazul χitijazul amorijazul perizijazul χiwijazul wa jewusijazul rakʔalde
ɡʔjel dur raɡʼuqχ ɡʼjenekːize ruɡo tsinɡi mun ratʃun tsadaqχ ɡʼizrailazul tsereqχabiɡun ina misrijaɬul patʃajasuqχe wa ɡʔjesda nuʒetsa ɡʔadin abila ʒuɡʔutʼazul betʼjerhan allaɡʔ watʃʼana niʒeqχe ɬabɡo qʼojil nuχ tun awlaqχalde ine ritʃːaj niʒ niʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔase qʼurbanal ɡʔarize
amma dida ɬala misrijaɬul patʃajas dir qʼuwat ɡutʃ biχʔun χadubtsin nuʒee ɡʔjenisa naqχe ine iznu kʔjeze ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi
ɡʔjedinɬidal ditsa dirɡo kwer borχila misrijalda dande wa kidaɡo riχʔa raɡʼitʃʼjel muɡʼʒizatazdaɬun ʁura tʃunkila ɡʔjeb ɡʔjeldasa χadub ɡʔjes nuʒ ritʃːan teze ruɡo
ditsaɡi misrijazul rakʼal ritʼizarila nuʒedeχun ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjenisa naqχe uneɬul nuʒ χʔwaɡʼun kweralɡun ine ɡʔjetʃʼo
ʃːijaj tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ ʒindirɡo maduɡʔalalda wa ɡʔjeɬul roqʼor tʃʼaral tsoɡi rutʃːabazda ɡʔarun kʔjezare mesedaɬulɡi ɡʼartsulɡi tʼaɡʼjelal wa retʼjel kun ɡʔjel nuʒerɡo jasazdaɡi wasazdaɡi tʼad retʼje ɡʔjeb qʼaɡʼidajaɬ kʼudijab dawlaɡun ina nuʒ misrijaldasa naqχe

tsinɡi musatsa ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjel dida boʒitʃʼoni dir raɡʼuqχɡi ɡʼjenekːitʃʼoni wa zaɡʔirɬitʃʼo duje betʼjerhanin abuni ʃːib ɡʔabileb
betʼjerhanas abuna ɡʔjeb duda kodob buɡeb ʒo ʃːib in
ɡʼansa buɡo jan abuna musatsa
ɡʼodobe reχe ɡʔjeb in abuna ɡʔjes
ɡʼodobe reχidal ɡʼansa borχʔide swerana wa musa ɡʔjeɬuqχa ɬutana
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas musada abuna
beɡʔun kwerɡun ɡʔjeɬul ratʃʼ kːwe jan musatsa ratʃʼ kːwedal ɡʔjesul kwerzukʔ boroχʔ naqχeɡi ɡʼanside swerana
ɡʼizrailazul umumuzul betʼjerhan allaɡʔ ibraɡʔimilɡi isχʼaqʼilɡi jaqʼubilɡi allaɡʔ duje zaɡʔirɬun wukʼinalda ɡʼizrailal boʒijaɬe buɡeb ɡʼalamat buɡo ɡʔjeb
χadubɡi betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesda abuna
durɡo kwer ɬoronib ɬe jan musatsa kwer ʒindirɡo ɬoronib ɬuna waamma ɡʔjeb ɡʔjenisa qʼwatʼibe baqχindal ɡʼazu kiniɡin qχaχʼɬun bukʼana kwer baras
naqχeɡi ɬe kwer durɡo ɬoronib in abuna ɡʔjes musatsa naqχeɡi ʒindirɡo kwer ɬoronib ɬuna wa qʼwatʼibe baqχindal ɡʔjeb batsʼtsʼaɬun bukʼarabɡo ɡʼadin ɬuɡʔana
betʼjerɡʔanas abuna ɡʔjel dur raɡʼuda boʒitʃʼoni wa tʼotsebeseb ɡʼalamataɬ mukʼur ɡʔaritʃʼoni ɡʔjel boʒila kʼiabileb ɡʼalamatalda
ɡʔjeb kʼijabɡo ɡʼalamataldaɡi boʒitʃʼoni dur raɡʼuqχɡi ɡʔjel ɡʼjenekːitʃʼoni nil ɡʼuruɬa ɬim bose wa baqʼwarab bakʼalde ɡʼodobe tʼje ɡʼodobe tʼjedal ɡʔjeb ɬim bijalde swerize buɡo
tsinɡi musatsa betʼjerhanasda abuna oɡʔ betʼjerɡʔan kidaɡo wukʼintʃʼo dun kʼaɬaze baʒari buɡew tʃiɬun ɡʔabsaɡʼatɡi dur laʁɡun mun kʼaɬaleɬulɡi ɡʔjedinawɡo wuɡo dun zaχʼmatɡo ɡuroni diqχa kʼaɬan baʒarularo bakʼab kʼal matsʼaɬul tʃi wuɡo dun
betʼjerhanas abuna insanase kʼal matsʼ ɬitsa kʔurab ɬitsa ɡʔarulel matsʼ ɬalarelɬun jaɡi ɡʼinqʼalɬun jaɡi kanɬi biχʔulelɬun jaɡi betsːalɬun ditsa betʼjerhanas ɡurebdaj
ɡʔanʒe mun a ditsa kumek ɡʔabila duje kʼaɬaze wa ditsa maɬila duda dutsa abize kːoleb ʒo
musatsa abuna ja betʼjerɡʔan ɡʔarula duda ɡʔjeb iʃaɬe dun tun tsoɡidaw dujeɡo bokʔaraw tʃi witʼje jan
ɡʔjebmeχalda betʼjerhanasul tsːin baqχana musada wa ɡʔjes abuna
dur wats ɡurewiʃː wuɡew ɡʔarunin aburaw lewijilazul tʃi dida ɬala ɡʔjesul kʼaɬaze maχʃːel bukʼin duda dandtʃʼwaze qʼwatʼiwe waqχun wuɡo ɡʔjew wa mun wiχʔidal ɡʔjew woχize wuɡo
dutsa ɡʔjesda bitse wa maɬe pirɡʼawnasda abize kːolebʃːinab ditsajin abuni nuʒee kʼijazeɡo kumek ɡʔabila wa maɬila ɡʔabize kːoleb ʒo
ɡʔarunitsa dur raɡʼabi χalqʼalda ritsine ruɡo awaraɡas allaɡʔasul kalima bitsuneb ɡʼadin
ɡʔab tʼilɡi kodob kːwe ɡʔjeldaɬun dutsa ɡʼalamatal riχʔizarize ruɡo
musa ʒindirɡo wakʔad itroqχe wiɬːana wa ɡʔjes wakʔadasda abuna witʃːaj dun misrijalde ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬuqχe tʼadwusːine ɡʔjel ʒeɡi tʃʼaɡo ruɡiʃːali balaɡʔize jan
itrotsa abuna sapar saɡʼat bitʼaɡi dir was in
midjanalda wukʼaɡo kʼaɬana musada betʼjerhan misrijalde tʼadwusːa mun tʃʼwaze bokʔaral χwana jan
musatsa qχizan ɬimal χʼamide raχinaruna kodob allaɡʔasul ɡʼansaɡi kːuna wa misrijalde tʼadwusːine sapar buχʔana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna misrijalde tʼad wusːindal kʼotʃonɡe pirɡʼawnasda tsebe ditsa duje kʔurab qʼuwataldaɬun dol muɡʼʒizatal riχʔizarize ditsajin abuni ɡʔjesul rekʼjeɬe ɡʼasiɬi reχila wa ɡʔjes χalqʼ naqχe bitʃːalaro
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ pirɡʼawnasda abe ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo betʼjerhanas ɡʼizrail wuɡo dir was dir tʼotsewesew was
ditsa abuna duda dir was dije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize witʃːan tejan dutsa ɡʔjew witʃːatʃʼo ɡʔanʒe ditsa dur tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw was tʃʼwaze wuɡo jan
nuχda sordo baze reʃːtʼarab bakʼalda betʼjerhanasda dande kːana ɡʔjew
ɡʔjebmeχalda tsiporatsa beɡʼjerab ɡantʃʼil nusɡi bosun ʒindirɡo wasasul ɡʼawrataɬul raɡʼal qʼotʼana wa ɡʔjebɡi ɡʔjesul χʼatʼazda qχwazabun ɡʔjeɬ abuna mun dir bidul baχʼaraw in
ɡʔjebmeχalda betʼjerhanas ɡʔjew ʒiwɡo tana bidul baχʼaraw ɡʔjedin ɡʔjeɬ abuleb bukʼana sunnat ɡʔabijalda
betʼjerhanas ɡʔarunida abuna musaɡun dandtʃʼwaze a awlaqχalde jan ɡʔarun ɡʔjesda dande nuχda waqχana wa allaɡʔasul maɡʼarda
musatsa ɡʔarunida kinabɡo bitsana ʃːib amruɡun betʼjerhanas ʒiw witʼarawaliɡi wa musatsa riχʔizarize ɡʔjesda tʼadqʼaral ɡʼalamatazul χʼaqʼaɬuɬɡi
tsinɡi musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼaɬul kʼudijal dande aχʼana
wa ɡʔarunitsa ɡʔjezije bitsana betʼjerhanas musada abunʃːinab wa χalqʼalda tsere dol ɡʼalamatalɡi riχʔizaruna
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ χalqʼ musada boʒana betʼjerhanas ʒideda raχʼmu tsʼob ɬun bukʼin wa ɡʔjesda ʒider qʼwariɬi biχʔun bukʼin bitʃʼtʃʼidal ɡʔjez allaɡʔase retsː baqʼɡun suʒda ɡʔabuna

ɡʔjeldasa χadub musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi ratʃʼana pirɡʼawnasuqχe wa ɡʔjez abuna
ɡʼizrailaɬul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo awlaqχalda dije bajram tʼobitʼize bukʼine dir χalqʼ bitʃːante jan
pirɡʼawnas abuna
dun ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼjenekːize wa ɡʼizrailal ditsa ritʃːan teze kːani ʃːiw kːolew betʼjerhan dida betʼjerhanɡi ɬalaro ɡʼizrailalɡi ditsa ritʃːalaro jan
ɡʔjez abuna
ʒuɡʔutʼazul allaɡʔ reʃːtʼana niʒeqχe ɬabɡo qʼojaɬ niʒ awlaqχalde ine ritʃːaj ɡʔjenib niʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔase qʼurbanal qχweze kːola niʒetsa ɡuroni ɡʔjes kweʃab unti jaɬuni raʁ bitʃːan ʒaza ɡʔabila niʒee
misrijaɬul patʃajas ʒawab ɡʔabuna
musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi ʃːib qʼwariɡʼun nuʒetsa χalqʼ χʼaltʼudasa busːinabuleb buɡeb nuʒeda tʼad ɬurab χʼaltʼi tʼubazabize a jan
pirɡʼawnas tʼadeɡi ʒubana
ɡʼjemerɬun buɡeb kuts biχʔulariʃː ɡʔab χalqʼ niʒer rakʔalda nuʒetsajin abuni ɡʔjezda χʼaltʼi reχun tezabuleb buɡo
ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ pirɡʼawnas χalqʼaɬul tʼadtʃaɡʼaze wa tsereqχabaze bujuruqχ kʔuna
ɡʔjezije tʼokʼaɬ tsebe ɡʼadin sumalo kʔoɡe samanaɬul kirpitʃal ɡʔarize bitʃːante ɡʔjez ʒalɡo un balaɡʔize ɡʔjeb
amma ɡʔjezdasa tʼalab ɡʔabe bukʼarab qʼadaralda saman qʼotʼi ɡʔjeɬul rotsen ɡʼodobeɡʼan batʃunɡe ɡʼurab χʼaltʼi ɡʔjetʃʼoɬijaɬ tasamaχʼɬun ruɡo ɡʔjel wa ɡʔjedinɬidalin ɡarɡadulelɡi ruɡel ritʃːante niʒ niʒerɡo allaɡʔase qʼurban qχweze ine jan
ɡʔjezije χʼaltʼi bakʼɬizabe χʼaltʼulel rukʼine ɡʔodoral χarbazuqχ ɡʼjenekːun rukʼintʃʼoɡo
tʼadtʃaɡʼiɡi tsereqχabiɡi ɡʔjenisa naqχe riɬːana wa χalqʼalda kʼaɬana
pirɡʼawnas abuleb buɡo ditsa tʼokʼaɬ nuʒee sumalo kʔjeze ɡʔjetʃʼo
nuʒɡo un bokʔaraɬusa baqχun balaɡʔje ɡʔjeb amma qʼojil χʼaltʼul rotsen ɡʼodobe batʃine ɡʔjetʃʼo jan
wa tʼolabɡo misrijalda biχːun sumalojaɬul bakʼalda χʼaltʼizabize χurzabaqχa sum ɡʼutʃʼ bakʼarize ɬuɡʔana χalqʼ
tʼadtʃaɡʼazɡi ɡʔjezda tʼad zulmu χʼal ɡʔabun abuleb bukʼana
nuʒee sumalo kʔoleb zamanaɬ bukʼarab ɡʼadab qʼojil χʼaltʼul rotsen tʼubazabe ɡʔanʒeɡi jan
pirɡʼawnasul tʼadtʃaɡʼaz ʒidetsaɡo ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔosa riʃːun ɡʔjezda tʼad taral tsereqχabi ruχulel rukʼana wa ɡʔjezda kʼalɡʔiqʼuleb bukʼana
ʃːaj nuʒetsa sonɡi ʒaqʼaɡi tsebekːun qʼotʼuleb bukʼarab ɡʼadab rotsenalda saman qʼotʼitʃʼjeb inɡi abun
ɡʼizrailazul tsereqχabi pirɡʼawnasuqχe ɡʼarzɡun ratʃʼana
ʃːaj ɡʔadinab zulmu χʼal ɡʔabuleb buɡeb dutsa durɡo laʁzaderida tʼad
niʒee dur laʁzaderije sumalo kʔoleb ɡʔjetʃʼo amma saman qʼotʼi tʼalab ɡʔabuleb buɡo ɡʔjeb ɡurebɡi dur tʼadtʃaɡʼaz niʒ ruχulelɡi ruɡo χʼaqʼ tʃʼola dur χalqʼalda tʼad
pirɡʼawnas abuna
χʼaltʼize kʼwaχʼalɬunin nuʒ ruɡel nuʒ ruɡo tʃamɡʼalal tʃaɡʼi ɡʔjele ɡʔjedinɬidalin nuʒetsa abuleb buɡeb ritʃːante niʒ awlaqχalde ine betʼjerhanase qʼurbanal tʼoritʼize jan
χʼaltʼize a nuʒee sumalo kʔjeze ɡʔjetʃʼo amma biχʔizaburab qʼadaralda saman nuʒetsa qʼotʼize buɡo
biχʔizaburab qʼadaraldasa tso saman tʼasa kamize bitʃːaɡe ʃːibab qʼojaɬ in abuleb raɡʼidal ɡʼizrailazul tsereqχabazda bitʃʼtʃʼana ʒal balaɡʔaɬukʔje kːarabɬi
pirɡʼawnasuqχa qʼwatʼire ratʃʼuneɬul ɡʔjezuqχ ralaɡʔun tʃʼun rukʼaral musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi riχʔana ɡʔjezda
wa ɡʔjez abuna
betʼjerhanasda biχʔaɡi nuʒetsa ɡʔabun tarab wa ɡʔjesɡo ʒazaɡi ɡʔabeɡi nuʒee nuʒ sababɬun niʒ tʼuran riχana pirɡʼawnasdaɡi ɡʔjesul ɡʼaɡa boʒarazdaɡi wa niʒ tʃʼwaze nus ɬuna nuʒetsa ɡʔjezul qχatinib
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musa betʼjerhanasde ɡʔardana wa ɡʔjes abuna
ja betʼjerɡʔan ʃːaj dutsa ɡʔab χalqʼalde tʼade ɡʔab balaɡʔ batʃarab ʃːaj dutsa dun ɡʔaniwe witʼaraw
dur tsʼaraldasan kʼaɬaze dun pirɡʼawnasuqχe araldasa naqχe ɡʔjes χalqʼaɬe ɡʼazab ɡʼaqʼuba tʼadeɡi tsʼikʼkʼinabuna amma dutsa kiliʃːtsin ʃurizabitʃʼo durɡo χalqʼ χwasar ɡʔabijaɬe

ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanas musada abuna ɡʔanʒe duda biχʔila pirɡʼawnase ditsa ɡʔabuleb ʒo dir ɡutʃab kweraɬul bakʼɬi biχʔidal ɡʔjes ɡʼizrailal ritʃːan teze ruɡo dir ɡutʃab kweraɬul bakʼɬi biχʔidal ɡʔjes ɡʔjel ʒiderɡo ulkajaldasa qʼwatʼire qʼotʼize ruɡo
allaɡʔas musada abuna dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
dun zaɡʔirɬana ibraɡʔimije isχʼaqʼije wa jaqʼubije χʼalkʼolew allaɡʔ
ɡʔjezije tʃijarabɬun bukʼarab χanaanaɬul rakʔ ɡʔjezije kʔjeze amru ɡʔabuna ditsa wa ɡʔjezulɡun qʼotʼi ɡʔabuna
χadub dida raɡʼana misrijazul zulmujalda ʁorkʔ ɡʼizrailal uɡʔdulel kuts wa dirɡo qʼotʼiɡi rakʼalde ʃːwana
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʼizrailazda abe dun wuɡo betʼjerhan wa ditsa nuʒ misrijaɬul zulmujalda ʁorkʔa naqχe ratʃine ruɡo wa laʁɬijaldasa tarqχan ɡʔarize ruɡo ditsa χwasar ɡʔarila nuʒ misrijalde dir kwer borχun buɡo wa ʒazabi kutakal rukʼine ruɡo
ditsa nuʒ dirɡo χalqʼɬun χʔiχʔila wa dun nuʒer allaɡʔɬun wukʼina ɡʔjele ɡʔjeb meχalda ɬala nuʒeda misrijaɬul zulmujalda ʁorkʔa nuʒ qʼwatʼire ratʃaraw nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ dun wukʼin
ditsa nuʒ ratʃina ibraɡʔimije isχʼaqʼije wa jaqʼubije kʔjeze dun ɡʔjedarab rakʔalde wa ɡʔjeb nuʒee kʔjela dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
musatsa ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʼizrailazda bitsana amma ɡʔjez ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼintsin tʼamitʃʼo ʃːajɡureɬul waχʼʃijab zulmujaɬ ɡʔjezul rakʼ bekun χʔulɡi busːun bukʼana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ineɡi un pirɡʼawnasda misrijaɬul patʃajasda abe ʒindirɡo ulkajaldasa ɡʼizrailal naqχe ritʃːajan
amma musatsa betʼjerhanasda abuna ɡʼizrailaltsin diqχ ɡʼjenekːulel ɡʔjetʃʼoni pirɡʼawn kin diqχ ɡʼjenekːilew tsʼaqʼ kʼal matsʼ ɡʔjetʃʼjew tʃi wuɡeɬul dun
betʼjerhan kʼaɬana musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjes ritʼana ɡʔjel ɡʼizrailazuqχe wa pirɡʼawnasuqχe aj misrijaɬul patʃajasuqχe ɡʼizrailal misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃejan amruɡun
ɡʔale ɡʔjezul tuχumazul kʼudijal
ɡʼizrailil tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw wasasul aj ruwimil wasal jenoχ palu χʼjetsron wa karmi ɡʔjezdasan ratʃʼana ruwimil tuχumal
ʃimeonil wasal jemuel jamin oɡʔad jaχin tsoχar wa χanaanaldasa ɡʼadamaɬ ɡʔawuraw ʃaul ɡʔjezdasan ratʃʼana ʃimeonil tuχumal
ɡʔale lewijil wasazul tsʼaral kʼudijazdasa bajbiχʔun ɡerʃon keχat wa merari lewijitsa bana nusijalda ɬeberalda ankʔɡo son
ɡerʃonil wasal liwni wa ʃimɡʼi ɡʔjezul tuχumalɡun
keχatil wasal amram itsɡar χewron wa ɡʼuziel keχatitsa bana nusijalda ɬeberalda ɬabɡo son
meraril wasal maχli wa muʃi
ɡʔjel kːola lewijidasan ɬuɡʔaral tuχumal kʼudijazdasa bajbiχʔun
amramitsa jatʃun jikʼana ʒindirɡo insul jats joχewed ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjesije ɡʔaruna ɡʔarunɡi musaɡi amramitsa bana nusijalda ɬeberalda ankʔɡo son
itsɡaril wasal qʼoraχʼ nefeɡ wa ziχri
ɡʼuzielil wasal miʃael eltsafan wa sitri
ɡʔarunitsa jatʃana ɡʼaminadawil jas wa naχʼʃonil jats eliʃewa ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjesije ɡʔaruna nadaw awiɡʔu eleazar wa itamar
qʼoraχʼil wasal asir elkanaɡʔ wa awiasaf ɡʔjezdasan riʒana qʼoraχʼil tuχumal
ɡʔarunil was eleazaritsa jatʃana putielil jasazul tsojaj wa ɡʔjezije ɡʔawuna pinχas
ɡʔjele lewijilazul tuχumazul kʼudijal umumul
musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi kːola ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼibe batʃe jan ʒidede betʼjerhanas amru ɡʔabural tʃaɡʼi
ɡʔjedinɡo musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi kːola ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼibe batʃineɬun pirɡʼawnasda kʼaɬaral tʃaɡʼi
misrijalda musadeχun kʼaɬaleb meχalda
betʼjerhanas abuna dun wuɡo betʼjerhan pirɡʼawnasda misrijaɬul patʃajasda bitse ditsa duda abunʃːinab in
amma musatsa betʼjerhanasda abuna kʼal matsʼaɬul ɡʔunar ɡʔjetʃʼjew tʃi wuɡo dun pirɡʼawn kin diqχ ɡʼjenekːilew in

betʼjerhanas musada abuna diqχ ɡʼjenekːe ditsa mun pirɡʼawnasda tʼad allaɡʔɬun dur wats ɡʔarun dur awaraɡɬun tolew wuɡo
ditsa duje amru ɡʔabunʃːinab dutsa dur wats ɡʔarunida abe χadub ɡʔjes pirɡʼawnasda abize bitʃːaj ɡʔjes ɡʼizrailal ʒindirɡo ulkajaldasa qʼwatʼire ritʃːaze rukʼine
amma pirɡʼawnasul rekʼjeɬe ditsa soɡʼɬi bitʃːala wa kiɡʼan ɡʼjemer ɡʼalamatalɡi muɡʼʒizatalɡi misrijalda ditsa riχʔizaruniɡi
ɡʔjew nuʒeqχ ɡʼjenekːilaro ɡʔjeb meχalda ditsa dirɡo kwer misrijalda tʼade busːinabila wa ɡʔjezije tsʼob tun ʒaza ɡʔabila ditsa qʼwatʼibe batʃina dirɡo χalqʼ ɡʼizrailil naslu misrijaɬul rakʔaldasa
dir kweraɬul bakʼɬi ɬajdal wa ɡʔjenisa ɡʼizrailal qʼwatʼire ratʃindal ɬaze buɡo misrijazda dun betʼjerhan wukʼin
musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabuna kinabɡo
pirɡʼawnasda kʼaɬaze bajbiχʔarab meχalda musatsa ban bukʼana unqʼoɡo son ɡʔarunitsa unqʼojalda ɬabɡo son
musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi kʼaɬaleb meχaɬ betʼjerhanas musada abuna
pirɡʼawnas muɡʼʒizat biχʔizabejan aburab meχalda dutsa ɡʔarunida abe durɡo ɡʼansa pirɡʼawnasda tsebe reχe jan tsinɡi ɡʔjeb ɡʼansa borχʔide swerize buɡo
musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi ratʃʼana pirɡʼawnasuqχe wa ɡʔjez kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔarunitsa ʒindirɡo ɡʼansa reχana pirɡʼawnasdaɡi ɡʔjesul tseresel tʃaɡʼazdaɡi tsebe wa ɡʔjeb borχʔide swerana
ɡʔjebmeχalda pirɡʼawnas ʒindirɡo ɡʼaqʼilzabiɡi siχʼrutʃaɡʼiɡi aχʼana wa misrijaɬul siχʼrutʃaɡʼazɡi ɡʔjebɡo ʒo ɡʔabuna ʒiderɡo siχʼrujaldaɬun
ʃːiwas ɡʼodobe reχana ʒindirɡo ɡʼansa wa ɡʔjezul ʃːibab borχʔide swerana amma ɡʔarunil ɡʼansajaɬ ɡʔjezulal qʼultʃʼana
pirɡʼawnin abuni tʼirun tʃʼana betʼjerhanas abuqχe ɡʔjew ɡʔjezuqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼo
betʼjerhanas musada abuna pirɡʼawn tʼirun tʃʼun wuɡo χalqʼ naqχe bitʃːaze ɡʔjes inkar ɡʔabuleb buɡo
meter radal pirɡʼawn ɡʼurul raɡʼalde uneb meχalda mun dosda dande a borχʔide sweruleb ɡʼansaɡi kodob kːun dosda tsewe nilaɬul raɡʼalda waqχun tʃʼa
dutsa dosda abe
ʒuɡʔutʼazul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dun witʼana duda ɡʔadin abize dir χalqʼ dije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize awlaqχalde bitʃːaj dutsa jan amma ɡʔanʒeɬizeɡʼan dutsa ɡʔjeɬuqχ ɡʼin tʼamitʃʼo
ɡʔanʒe betʼjerhanas ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo duda biχʔila dun betʼjerhan wukʼin dir qχatikʔ buɡeb ɡʼansa ditsa kʔabize buɡo nilaɬul ɬadaɬ wa ɬim swerize buɡo bijalde
nilaɬul ɬadaɬ buɡeb tʃːuɡʼa χweze buɡo ɡʼoralda kweʃab maχʼ baqχine buɡo wa misrijazda ɡʔjeɬul ɬim ɡʔjeqʼeze kʼweze ɡʔjetʃʼo
betʼjerhanas musada abuna ɡʔarunida abe durɡo ɡʼansaɡi bosun ɡʔjeb χʔwaɡʼje misrijaɬul ɬinazda tʼade ɡʼorazde wa ɬadal raqχazde χʼorazde wa kinalɡʼaɡi ɬadal χʼawuzazde tʼade ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɬim bijalde swerize buɡo misrijalda bi bukʼine buɡo kisa kibeɡo tsʼulal wa ɡantʃʼil qχabazda ʒanibɡitsin
musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi kinabɡo betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabuna ɡʔarunitsa ɡʼansa eχede borχana wa pirɡʼawnasulɡi ɡʔjesul tseresel tʃaɡʼazulɡi berda tsebesan nilaɬul ɬadada kʔabuna wa ɡʔjeb bijalde swerana
nilaɬul ɬadaɬ bukʼarab tʃːuɡʼa χwana wa ɡʼoralda baqχarab kweʃab maχʼaɬ misrijazda tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔjeɬul ɬim ɡʔjeqʼeze kʼoleb bukʼintʃʼo misrijalda kisa kibeɡo bukʼana bi
amma misrijaɬul siχʼrutʃaɡʼazɡi ʒiderɡo siχʼrujaldaɬun ɡʔjebɡo ʒo ɡʔabuna pirɡʼawnin abuni tʼirun tʃʼana ɡʔjew ɡʼjenekːitʃʼo musaqχɡi ɡʔaruniqχɡi betʼjerhanas tsebekːunɡo abun bukʼarab qʼaɡʼidajalda
ɡʔjeɬul kʼwartsin ɡʔabitʃʼo misrijaɬul patʃajas kʔurun wusːun ʒindirɡo kʼalɡʼajaɬuwe ana ɡʔjew
tʼolabɡo misrijaɬul χalqʼ ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjeqʼeze beɡʔuleb ɬim balaɡʔize wa nilaɬul raɡʼalɬabazda ʁujal ruqχize ɡʼuruqχa ɬim ɡʔjeqʼeze beɡʔuleb bukʼintʃʼjeɬul
betʼjerhanas nilaɬul ɬadada kʔaburaldasa naqχe ankʔ ana

betʼjerhanas musada abuna pirɡʼawnasuqχe a wa ɡʔjesda abe betʼjerhanas ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo dir χalqʼ dije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize ine bitʃːaj
dutsa inkar ɡʔabuni ditsa dur ulkajalda tʼade qʼurqʼbi tʼamize ruɡo
tʼolabɡo nil qʼurqʼbuz tsʼjezabize buɡo ɡʼuruɬa qʼwatʼireɡi ratʃʼun ɡʔjel kʼantsʼize ruɡo dur kʼalɡʼajaɬure mun kʔiʒuleb roqʼore dur busade dur tseresel tʃaɡʼazul wa dur χalqʼaɬul minabazuqχe dur petʃaɬure wa ɡʼatʼ butsuleb χʼjertʃalda ʒanire
qʼurqʼbi ɬuɡʔine ruɡo duda tʼade wa dur χalqʼaldaɡi dur tseresel tʃaɡʼazdaɡi tʼade
betʼjerhanas musada abuna ɡʔarunida abe ɡʼansa borχe wa ɡʼorazdeɡi ɬadal raqχazdeɡi χʼorazdeɡi tʼade balaɡʔizabe wa misrijaɬul rakʔalde qʼurqʼbi reʃːtʼinare
ɡʔarunitsa ɡʼansaɡun kwer misrijaɬul ɬinazde tʼade balaɡʔun borχana wa ɡʔjenisa qʼwatʼire qʼurqʼbi ratʃʼana qʼurqʼbuz tsʼjezabuna tʼolabɡo misrijaɬul rakʔ
amma ʒiderɡo siχʼrujaldaɬun siχʼrutʃaɡʼazɡi ɡʔabuna ɡʔjebɡo ʒo ɡʔjezɡi qʼurqʼbi ritʃːana misrijalda tʼade
tsinɡi pirɡʼawnas musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi aχʼana wa ɡʔjezda abuna didaɡi dir χalqʼaldaɡi tʼasa qʼurqʼbi naqχe ratʃejan betʼjerhanasda ɡʔare ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsaɡi χalqʼ bitʃːala betʼjerhanase qʼurbanal tʼoritʼize
musatsa pirɡʼawnasda abuna ditsa ɡʔarila dutsa tʃʼjezaburab zamanalda durɡi dur tseresel tʃaɡʼazulɡi dur χalqʼaɬulɡi raqχaɬ ɡʔjebmeχaɬ qʼurqʼbi naqχe ine ruɡo duda tʼasaɡi nuʒer minabazuqχaɡi ɡʔjel ɡʼitsʼɡo nil ɡʼuruɬ χutʼize ruɡo
pirɡʼawnas abuna meterɡo ɡʔjel naqχe ine ɡʔare jan
musatsa ʒawab ɡʔabuna niʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda reɬːaraw ʃːiwɡo ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi duda ɬaze bukʼine dutsa abuqχe ɡʔabila
qʼurqʼbi naqχe ine ruɡo dudasa dur qχulbuzdasa dur tseresel tʃaɡʼazdasa wa dur χalqʼaldasa ɡʔjel χutʼize ruɡo ɡʼitsʼɡo nil ɡʼuruɬ in
musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi pirɡʼawnasda askʼosa naqχe ana wa musatsa betʼjerhanasda ɡʔarana pirɡʼawnasde tʼade ritʃːaral qʼurqʼbi naqχe ratʃejan
betʼjerhanas musal ɡʔari qʼabul ɡʔabuna ruqʼzabaqχ azbarazda wa awlaqχazda rukʼaral qʼurqʼbi χwana
ɡʔjel dande rakʼarulel rukʼana ɡoχʼa ɡoχʼal ɡʔarun wa bajbiχʔana ulkajaldaɡo ɡʔjezul kweʃab maχʼ tʼibitʼize
amma biɡʔaɬi ɬuɡʔuneb bukʼin biχʔidal pirɡʼawnasul rakʼ soɡʼɬana wa ɡʔjew ɡʔanʒesalaɡi ɡʼjenekːitʃʼo musaqχɡi ɡʔaruniqχɡi betʼjerhanas tsebekːunɡo abun bukʼarab qʼaɡʼidajalda
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔarunida abe eχedeɡi borχun durɡo ɡʼansa rakʔul χʼuruɬ kʔabe kisa kibeɡo misrijalda χʼur kʼkʼarajalde swerize buɡo jan
ɡʔjez ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna ɡʔarunitsa ɡʼansa eχedeɡi χʔwaɡʼun χʼuruɬ kʔabuna wa ɡʼadamazdaɡi botsʼudaɡi tʼade rorʒun ratʃʼana kʼkʼurbi kisa kibeɡo misrijaɬulɡo χʼur kʼkʼarajalde swerana
siχʼrutʃaɡʼiɡi qʼerkʔana ʒiderɡo siχʼrujaɬul kumekaldaɬun kʼkʼara batʃʼinabize amma ɡʔjezuqχa ɡʔjeb baʒaritʃʼo kʼkʼarajaɬ batsinabun bukʼana ɡʼadamazulɡi botsʼulɡi sipat
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ siχʼrutʃaɡʼaz pirɡʼawnasda abuna
ɡʔab buɡo allaɡʔasul χʼalkʼoɬijaɬ ɡʔaburab iʃ in
amma pirɡʼawn tʼirun tʃʼana ɡʔjew ɡʔjezuqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼo betʼjerhanas abuqχeɡo
betʼjerhanas musada abuna meter radakʔje pirɡʼawn ɡʼuruqχe uneb meχalda naqχeɡi ɡʔjesda dande a wa ɡʔjesda abe betʼjerhanas ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo dir χalqʼ dije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize ine bitʃːaj
bitʃːatʃʼoni ditsa dudeɡi dur tseresel tʃaɡʼazdeɡi dur χalqʼaldeɡi tʼade wa dur kʼalɡʼabazuqχeɡi tʼutʼazul nakʼkʼal ritʃːaze ruɡo misrijazul ruqʼzal tʼutʼazul tsʼjeze ruɡo tʼolabɡo rakʔɡi baχtʃizabize buɡo ɡʔjez
amma dir χalqʼaɬ tʃʼjej ɡʔaburab ɡoʃen rakʔalda tʼutʼal rukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo dun betʼjerhan wuɡebɬi wa ɡʔab rakʔalda ditsa kwerʃːel ɡʔabuleb bukʼin duda ɬan bukʼine
ditsa dir χalqʼaldaɡi dur χalqʼaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔabuleb batʼaɬi biχʔila duda meter bukʼina ɡʔjeb ɡʼalamat
betʼjerhanas ɡʔjedin ɡʔabizeɡi ɡʔabuna tʼutʼazul tʃʼjeɡʼjeral nakʼkʼal rorʒun ratʃʼana pirɡʼawnasul qχalajaɬure wa ɡʔjesul tseresel tʃaɡʼazul ruqʼzabazuqχe tʼutʼaz tʃʼwaleb bukʼana tʼolabɡo misrijaɬul rakʔ
pirɡʼawnas musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi tʼade aχʼana wa ɡʔjezda abuna nuʒerɡo allaɡʔase qʼurbanal tʼoritʼje ɡʔanir niʒer rakʔalda
amma musatsa abuna ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize beɡʔularo niʒetsa niʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔase qʼurban tʼobitʼi misrijaz surarab iʃɬun rikʼkʼuna ɡʔjezda tsebe niʒetsa ɡʔjezda surun biχʔuleb qʼurban ɡʔabuni ɡʔjez niʒ ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwaze ruɡo
niʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔase ɡʔjes tʼalab ɡʔabuleb qʼaɡʼidajalda qʼurban qχweze kːani niʒ ɬabɡo qʼojil nuχ tun awlaqχalde rikʼkʼaɬize kːola
pirɡʼawnas abuna
ditsa ritʃːala nuʒ awlaqχalde betʼjerhan allaɡʔase qʼurban qχweze amma nuʒ ɡʼjemer rikʼkʼadeɡʼan unɡe dijeɡi duɡʼa ɡʔabe
musatsa ʒawab ɡʔabuna
dun ɡʔanisa naqχe arawɡo betʼjerhanase duɡʼa ɡʔabize buɡo ditsa wa meterɡo munɡi dur tseresel tʃaɡʼiɡi tʼolabɡo misrijaɬul χalqʼɡi tʼutʼazdasa χwasarɬize ruɡo amma dutsaɡi niʒ tʼokʼaɬ ɡukːuɡe wa betʼjerhanase qʼurban qχweze ine niʒer χalqʼaɬe kwalkwal ɡʔabuɡe
musa ɡʔjenisa tʼadwusːana wa betʼjerhanase duɡʼa ɡʔabuna
betʼjerhanas tʼubazabuna musal ɡʔari pirɡʼawnɡi ɡʔjesul tseresel tʃaɡʼiɡi tʼolabɡo misrijaɬul χalqʼɡi tʼutʼazdasa erken ɡʔaruna tsoniɡi tʼutʼ naqχe χutʼitʃʼo
amma ɡʔabnuχaɬɡi pirɡʼawnasul rakʼ soɡʼɬana wa ɡʔjes χalqʼ qʼwatʼibe bitʃːatʃʼo

betʼjerhanas musada abuna pirɡʼawnasuqχe a wa ɡʔjesda abe ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo ʒuɡʔutʼazul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dir χalqʼ dije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize bitʃːaj
dutsa inkar ɡʔabuni wa χadubkːunɡi χalqʼ kːun tʃʼjezabuni
betʼjerhanas kutakab χwalil unti bitʃːaze buɡo meʁ rakʔalda buɡeb dur tʼolabɡo ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijalde tʃujazde χʼamuzde waranabazde tʃʼjeɡʼjerbotsʼude wa ɡʼi tsʼanazde
amma betʼjerhanas batʼaɬi ɡʔabize buɡo ɡʼizrailaɬul botsʼudaɡi misrijaɬul botsʼudaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼizrailazul tsoniɡi χʼajwan χweze ɡʔjetʃʼo
betʼjerhanas ɡʔjeɬije zaman tsʼana meter tʼolabɡo ulkajalda ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize buɡo betʼjerhanas
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanas ɡʔjedin ɡʔabizeɡi ɡʔabuna misrijazul kinabɡo botsʼi χwana amma ɡʼizrailazul tsoniɡi χʼajwan tʼasa kamitʃʼo
ɡʔjeɬul χal ɡʔabize tʃaɡʼi ritʼana pirɡʼawnas wa ɡʔjesda ɬana unɡo unɡoɬunɡi ɡʼizrailazul tsoniɡi χʼajwan χun ɡʔjetʃʼjebɬi amma ɡʔjew dodinɡo tʼirun tʃʼana wa ɡʔjes χalqʼɡi bitʃːatʃʼo
betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna danʁura tsʼun raqχu bose koronisa wa bitʃːante musatsa ɡʔjeb pirɡʼawnasda tsebesan ɡʔawajalde reχize
χʼur ɡʼadin tʼibitʼize buɡo ɡʔjeb tʼolabɡo misrijalda tʼad wa ulkajaldaɡo ruɡel ɡʼadamazdaɡi χʼajwanazdaɡi ɬuɡʔine ruɡo retsʼtsʼ tʃwaχulel tʼiχʔal
koroda ʒanisa raqχuɡi bosun ɡʔjel pirɡʼawnasda tsere tʃʼana musatsa raqχu ɡʔawajalde reχana wa ɡʔjebsaɡʼataldaɡo ɡʼadamazdaɡi botsʼudaɡi retsʼtsʼ tʃwaχulel tʼiχʔal raqχana
siχʼrutʃaɡʼazda tʼokʼaɬ musada dande raqχun baʒaritʃʼo ʃːajɡureɬul tsoɡidal misrijazulɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjezulɡi tʃerχ tʼiχʔazul tsʼuna
amma betʼjerhanas pirɡʼawnasul rekʼjeɬe soɡʼɬi bitʃːana wa betʼjerhanas musada abun bukʼaqχe ɡʔjew ɡʼjenekːitʃʼo ɡʔjezuqχ
betʼjerhanas musada abuna meter radakʔje waqχun pirɡʼawnasuqχe a wa ɡʔjesda abe ʒuɡʔutʼazul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo dir χalqʼ bitʃːaj dije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize ine
ɡʔab nuχalda ditsa dujeɡi dur tseresel tʃaɡʼazeɡi wa dur χalqʼaɬeɡi kutakab balaɡʔaldaɬun ʒaza ɡʔabize buɡo dun ɡʼadaw ɡʔab rakʔalda ɡʔjetʃʼjewɬi duda ɬan bukʼine
tso borχarab dir kiliʃːaɬ dudeɡi dur χalqʼaldeɡi χwalil unti bitʃːaze kʼolaan dida ɡʔjebmeχaɬ dunjalaldasaɡo tʼaɡʼinaan nuʒ
amma ditsa tʃʼaɡo tana mun duda dirɡo qʼuwat biχʔizabizeɬun wa dir tsʼar tʼolabɡo dunjalalda tʼibitʼizeɬun
mun ʒeɡi dir χalqʼalda dande tʃʼun wuɡo wa dutsa ɡʔjeb bitʃːan toleb ɡʔjetʃʼo
ɡʔanʒe ɡʼjenekːe meter ɡʔabɡo zamanalda ditsa misrijalda tʼade bitʃːaze buɡo kidaniɡi ɡʔjenib biχʔa raɡʼitʃʼjebɡʼan kutakab ɡoro tsʼjer
ɡʔjedinɬidal bujuruqχ kʔje botsʼiɡi tsoɡidab durɡo buɡoɬiɡi χʼinqʼi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb bakʼalde ʃːwezabize roqʼobe bakʼaritʃʼoɡo meʁ rakʔalda χutʼarabʃːinab botsʼi wa qʼwatʼir χutʼaral ɡʼadamal ɡoro tsʼjeraɬ tʃʼwaze ruɡo
betʼjerhanasul raɡʼukʔa χʼinqʼaral pirɡʼawnasul tseresel tʃaɡʼaz χeχɡo laʁzalɡi botsʼiɡi roqʼore rakʼarana
amma betʼjerhanasul raɡʼude kʼwar busːinabitʃʼjez ʒiderɡo laʁzalɡi botsʼiɡi qʼwatʼir tana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna kwer zodobe borχe tʼolabɡo misrijaɬul rakʔalde tʼade ɡoro tsʼjer baze buɡo ɡʼadamazde χʼajwanazde wa misrijaɬul rakʔalda biʒarabʃːinalde tʼade
musatsa ɡʼansa zodobe borχana ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanas zob ʁuʁadizabuna tsʼa pirχana wa tsʼadɬun ɡoro tsʼjer tʃwaχana zobalazdasa ɡʼodobe misrijaɬul rakʔalde
pirχuleb tsʼaɡun tsadaqχ baleb bukʼana kutakab ɡoro tsʼjer misri biʒaraldasa naqχe ɡʔjedinab ʒo kidaniɡi biχʔun ja raɡʼun bukʼintʃʼo misrijazda
ɡoro tsʼjeraɬ ʃːuʃːazabuna misrijaɬul rakʔalda tʼolabɡo qʼwatʼib χutʼarabʃːinab ʒo ɡʼadamal χʼajwanal χur χer wa ʁutʼbiɡitsin
ɡʼizrailaz ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb ɡoʃenaɬul rakʔaldajin abuni ɡoro tsʼjer batʃʼo
pirɡʼawnas musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi aχʼun ɡʔjezda abuna ɡʔab nuχalda ditsa munaɡʔ ɡʔabuna betʼjerhan witʼaraw wuɡo didaɡi dir χalqʼaldaɡijin abuni ɡʼajib kːana
betʼjerhanasda ɡʔare ɡʔab ɡʼasijab ʁuʁadiɡi ɡoro tsʼjerɡi ɡʼurab buɡo niʒee ditsa ritʃːala nuʒ tʼokʼaɬ nuʒ ɡʔanir tʃʼjezarilaro jan
musatsa ʒawab kʔuna ʃaɡʔaraldasa qʼwatʼiwe ɬuɡʔindal kweralɡi zodore rorχun betʼjerhanasda tsebe duɡʼa ɡʔabize buɡo ditsa wa ʁuʁadiɡi ɡoro tsʼjerɡi qʼotʼize buɡo ɡʔjebmeχaɬ duda biχʔila ɡʔab dunjalaɬul χwaʒainɬun betʼjerhan wukʼin
amma dida biχʔuleb buɡo munɡi dur tseresel ɡʼadamalɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔasukʔa ʒeɡi χʼinqʼulel ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi
ɬeɬɡi purtʃʼinaɡi χwana ɡʔjeb zamanajaɬ purtʃʼina tʼirʃːuleb bukʼun ɬeɬin abuni tʼjeɡʔan bukʼun
roɬɡi polbaɡi χwetʃʼo ɡʔjel kwatʼun ɡuroni ʃːolaroan
musa pirɡʼawnasul bakʼaldasa naqχe ana ʃaɡʔaraldasa qʼwatʼiwe wiɬːana wa kweralɡi rorχun ɡʔjes betʼjerhanasde duɡʼa ɡʔabuna ɡʔjebsaɡʼataldaɡo ʁuʁadiɡi ɡoro tsʼjerɡi qʼotʼana χadub tsʼadɡi tʃʼana
tsʼadɡi ʁuʁadiɡi ɡoro tsʼjerɡi qʼotʼarabɬi biχʔidal pirɡʼawn naqχeɡi ʒindirɡo ɡʼamalalde wusːana ɡʔjesulɡi ɡʔjesul tseresel tʃaɡʼazulɡi dodinɡo rakʼal soɡʼɬana
pirɡʼawn naqχeɡi tʼirun tʃʼana wa ɡʔjes ɡʼizrailal ritʃːatʃʼo betʼjerhanas musada tsebekːunɡo abun bukʼaqχe

betʼjerhanas musada abuna pirɡʼawnasuqχe a pirɡʼawnasulɡi ɡʔjesul tseresel ɡʼadamazulɡi rakʼazuɬe ditsa soɡʼɬi bitʃːaze buɡo ɡʔjezda ɡʼalamatal riχʔizarize rukʼine
wa dutsaɡi χadubkːun ɬimalazda wa ɡʔjezulɡi ɬimalazda bitsine bukʼine ditsa tsʼob tun misrijaze ɡʔaburab ʒazajaɬul wa ɡʔjezda riχʔizarural χʼikmatazul ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nuʒeda ɬan bukʼina dun betʼjerhan wukʼin
musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi pirɡʼawnasuqχe riɬːana wa ɡʔjez ɡʔjesda abuna
ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo ʒuɡʔutʼazul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kidalɬizeɡʼan dutsa inkar ɡʔabize buɡeb dije mutʼiɡʼɬize bitʃːaj dir χalqʼ dije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize ine
dutsa dir χalqʼ bitʃːatʃʼoni dur ulkajalde tʼade ditsa meterɡo ɡartsʼ tʼamize buɡo
ɡʔjeb kisa kibeɡo tʼibitʼize buɡo rakʔaɬul ɡʔumertsin biχʔulareb χʼalalda ɡʔjeɬ kwanaze buɡo ɡoro tsʼjer ban χadub χutʼarabʃːinabɡi meʁ rakʔalda biʒarabʃːinab ʁwetʼɡi
ɡartsʼaɬ tsʼjezarize ruɡo dur kʼalɡʼabi wa dur tseresel ɡʼadamazulɡi kinalɡo misrijazulɡi ruqʼzal ɡʔab rakʔalda riʒaraldasa naqχe ʒaqʼa qʼojalde ʃːwezeɡʼanɡi ja dur umumuzda ja dur umumuzulɡi umumuzda ɡʔjedinab ʒo ʒeɡi biχʔun bukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjedinɡi abun kʔurun wusːun musa pirɡʼawnasul bakʼaldasa naqχe ana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjesul tʃʼuχʼbi χʼakimzabaz pirɡʼawnasda abuna ʒeɡi kire ʃːwezeɡʼan dow tʃijas niɬ ɡʔab χʼalalda tʃʼjezarize ruɡel ʒiderɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize ine ritʃːaj dol tʃaɡʼi duda biχʔuleb ɡʔjetʃʼiʃː misrijaɬul iʃ aχiralde kːoleb bukʼin
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi pirɡʼawnasuqχe tʼad rusːinaruna
nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize a jan abuna ɡʔjes ʃːal ʃːal ɡʔjenire ine ruɡel
musatsa abuna niʒ ine ruɡo ɬimalɡun wa χarabiɡun wasal jasalɡun ɡʼi tsʼanazul reqχabiɡun wa botsʼul reχʔjedalɡun betʼjerhanase ɡʔabuleb bajramɬidal ɡʔjeb niʒer
pirɡʼawnas abuna ditsa ɬimalɡun tsadaqχ nuʒ ritʃːani bitʃːante betʼjerhanas kwerbaqʼi ɡʔabize nuʒee amma nuχda balaɡʔazukʔje kːeze ɡurinχa
ɡʔjeb bukʼunareb ʒo nuʒetsa ɡʔjediɡʼan tsʼaqʼ ɡʔaruleb buɡeɬul a betʼjerhanase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize amma tsoχʼo biχʔinal ɡuroni unɡe
tsinɡi ɡʔarunɡi musaɡi pirɡʼawnasda tseresa naqχe qʼotʼana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna misrijaɬul rakʔalde tʼade kwer borχe tsinɡi bakːila ɡartsʼ ɡʔjeɬ kwanaze buɡo rakʔalda biʒarabʃːinab ɡoro tsʼjer ban χadub naqχe χutʼanʃːinab
musatsa misrijalde tʼade ɡʼansa borχana wa betʼjerhanas rakʔalde tʼade bitʃːana baqʼbakːul ɡʔuri tʼubarab sordo qʼojaɬ ɡʔuri puna wa roɡʔalide ɡʔorotsa bosun batʃʼana ɡartsʼ
kutakalda ɡʼjemerab ɡartsʼ tʼadeɬana misrijalde wa ɡʔjeɬ tʼolabɡo ulka tsʼjezabuna ɡartsʼazul ɡʔjedinab tʃabqχen tsebekːun kidaniɡi bukʼintʃʼo wa χadubkːunɡi kidaniɡi bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo
ɡʔjeɬ tʃʼjeɡʼjerab nakʼkʼ ɬuɡʔun baχtʃizabuna tʼolabɡo rakʔ ɡoro tsʼjeraldasa χadub χutʼanʃːinab meʁ rakʔalda biʒuleb bukʼanʃːinabɡi ʁutʼbuzda χutʼarabʃːinab piqχɡi kwana ɡʔjeɬ tʼolabɡo misrijalda ja ʁutʼbuzda tʼamaχ ja rakʔalda ʃːibɡʼaɡi ɡʼurtʃːinɬi χutʼitʃʼo
pirɡʼawnas χeχɡo musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi tʼade aχʼana wa ɡʔjezda abuna dun munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːana nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsewe wa nuʒeda tsewe
aχiriseb nuχaɬɡi dida tʼasa ɬuɡʔa nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda ɡʔare ɡʔab χwalil kwarkʔi dida tʼasa naqχe batʃejan
musa pirɡʼawnasul bakʼaldasa naqχe ana wa ɡʔjes betʼjerhanasda ɡʔarun duɡʼa ɡʔabuna
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas kutakab ɡʔuri baqχinabuna baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχaldasan wa ɡʔjeb kutakab ɡʔorotsa baɡʼarab raɬdaqχe qχamun ana ɡartsʼ misrijalda tso ɡartsʼ χutʼitʃʼo
amma betʼjerhanas pirɡʼawnasul rekʼjeɬe soɡʼɬi bitʃːana wa ɡʔjes ɡʼizrailal ritʃːatʃʼo
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
zodobe kwer borχe wa misrijalde betsʼɬi reʃːtʼine buɡo laχʼtʃʼjeɡʼjerab betsʼɬi
musatsa zodobe kwer borχana wa laχʼtuɡʼan tʃʼjeɡʼjerab betsʼɬi reʃːtʼana tʼolabɡo misrijalde ɬabɡo qʼojaɬ
ɬabɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʼadamazda kʼoleb bukʼintʃʼo ja tsotsada riχʔize ja tʃʼarab bakʼaldasa dore ɡʔanire raʁarize ɡʼizrailazulin abuni aj ɡʔjezul tʃʼjej buɡeb bakʼalda kanɬi bukʼana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ pirɡʼawnas musa aχʼana wa ɡʔjesda abuna nuʒerɡo betʼjerhanase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize a ɡʼitsʼɡo nuʒer ɡʼi botsʼi ɡʔanibɡo te ɬimalin abuni nuʒɡun tsadaqχ ine beɡʔila
musatsa abuna dutsa niʒeda tsadaqχ botsʼiɡi bitʃːaze kːola niʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔase niʒetsa qʼurbanal wa tʼubanɡo ruχʼulel qʼurbanal tʼoritʼize rukʼine
niʒer kinabɡo botsʼi niʒeda tsadaqχ bukʼine kːola ɡʔjezul ʃːankʼlaltsin ɡʔanir χutʼize ɡʔjetʃʼo dore ʃːwarab meχalda niʒetsa tʼasa riʃːila niʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔase qʼurbanaɬe χʼajwanal dore ʃːwetʃʼoɡo niʒeda ɬalaro kinal χʼajwanal betʼjerhanase qʼurban ɡʔarize kːolelali
betʼjerɡʔanas pirɡʼawnasul rekʼjeɬe tʼiruntʃʼjej reχana wa ɡʔjew raziɬitʃʼo ɡʔjel ritʃːaze
ɡʔjes musada abuna
tʼaɡʼa dir berda tsewesa tʼokʼaɬ dida tsewe qʼaɡe mun dida tsewe watʃʼani duje χwel bukʼine buɡo
musatsa abuna ɡʔjeb bitʼarab buɡo tʼokʼaɬ duda dun wiχʔilaro

betʼjerhanas musada abuna ditsa pirɡʼawnasdeɡi misrijaldeɡi tʼade tsoɡi tso balaɡʔ bitʃːaleb buɡo ɡʔjeldasa χadub ɡʔjes nuʒ ritʃːan teze ruɡo wa ɡʔadinɡo ritʃːan teze ɡurel qʼwatʼire ratʃaqχize ruɡo
χalqʼalda abe biχʔinazɡi rutʃːabazɡi ʒiderɡo maduɡʔalzabazuqχa ɡʼartsul wa mesedil qʼaji ɡʔarejan
betʼjerhanas misrijazul rekʼjeɬ ʒindirɡo χalqʼaldeχun raχʼmu biʒizabuna ʒiwɡo musaɡi misrijaɬul tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ ɡʼadatijal tʃaɡʼazɡi pirɡʼawnasul tseresel tʃaɡʼazɡi qʼadrujaw tʃiɬun rikʼkʼunaan
musatsa pirɡʼawnasda abuna betʼjerhanas ɡʔadin ɬazabuleb buɡo sordo baʃːaɬuleb riɡʔalda dun misri qʼotʼun ine wuɡo
wa ʃːibab tʼotsebe ɡʔaburab ɬimer χweze buɡo misrijalda patʃajasul taχida wuɡew pirɡʼawnasul ɬimadasa bajbiχʔun ɡʔabida tsee kʼusaraj laʁaɬul ɬimade ʃːwezeɡʼan χʼajwanazul tʼotsebe ɡʔaburab tʼintʃʼɡi χweze buɡo
tʼolabɡo misrijalda bukʼine buɡo tsebe kidaniɡi bukʼintʃʼjebɡʼan wa χadubkːunɡi kidaniɡi bukʼinarebɡʼan kʼudijab maɡʼu
amma ɡʼizrailaze wa ɡʔjezul botsʼuje ɡʔoj χʼaparabɡʼanɡi zaral kːeze ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjele ɡʔjeb meχalda ɬala nuʒeda betʼjerhanas misrijaldaɡi ɡʼizrailaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob batʼaɬi ɡʔabuleb bukʼin
dur tseresel tʃaɡʼi ratʃʼina diqχe wa naku tʃʼwan ɡʔarila ɡʔjez munɡi duda χadub biɬːarab tʼolabɡo χalqʼɡi naqχe a ɡʔanisa jan ɡʔjeldasa χaduw dunɡi ina
tsinɡi musa tsːidatsa ʁanqʼulaɡo pirɡʼawnasda askʼosa naqχe ana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna pirɡʼawnas nuʒeqχ ɡʼin tʼamize ɡʔjetʃʼo amma ɡʔjedin bukʼine kːola ditsa misrijaɬul rakʔalda dirɡo χʼikmatal iʃal ʒeɡi tsʼikʼkʼinarize rukʼine
musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔal kinalɡo muɡʼʒizatal riχʔizaruna pirɡʼawnasda tsere amma betʼjerhanas pirɡʼawnasul rekʼjeɬe soɡʼɬi bitʃːana wa ɡʔjes ɡʼizrailal ʒindirɡo ulkajaldasa naqχe ine ritʃːatʃʼo

misrijalda rukʼaɡo musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi betʼjerhanas abuna
bitʃːante nuʒee ɡʔab motsʼ bukʼine tʼotsebeseb motsʼɬun ɬaɡʼalil awalɬun
tʼolabɡo ɡʼizrailaɬul ʒamaɡʼatalda abe ɡʔab motsʼaɬul antsʼabileb qʼojaɬ ʃːibab qχizan qʼajaɬ tso tso kʔjeɡʼjer bosejin
tʼubarab kʔjeɡʼjer kwanaze ɡʼurab qχizan ɡʔjetʃʼoni bitʃːante ɡʔjeb ʃːiwas kiɡʼan kwanaleb χʼisabaldeɡi bosun kinazeɡo ɡʼoleb qʼaɡʼidajalda biʃːun tseresel maduɡʔalzabazɡun ɡʼaχʔal ɡʔabize
ɡʔjel kʔaɡʼi rukʼine kːola ɬaɡʼjel baral biχʔinal wa ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjel ɡʔjel rukʼine beɡʔula kʔaɡʼi jaɡi burtʼal
ɡʔjel χʔiχʔje ɡʔab motsʼaɬul antsʼila unqʼabileb qʼojalde ʃːwezeɡʼan tsinɡi bitʃːante markʼatʃʼul ɡʼuʒalda ɡʼizrailazul tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬ ɡʔjel qχweze
qʼurbanaɬe qχural ʒalazul biɡi ɡʔjeb qʼurban nuʒetsa kwanaleb minajaɬul kawujaɬul kʼijabɡo raqχaldaɡi raχazdaɡi baχe
tsʼaduda tʼadɡi beʒun ɡʔjebɡo sordojaɬ kwanaj ɡʔjeb ɡʔan buɡʔurɡo tʃadalɡun
ɡʼatʼɡo jaɡi beɬun ɡʔan kwanaɡe amma tsʼaduda tʼad beʒizabun kwanaj betʼjerɡi χʼatʼalɡi urɡʔimesɡi tsadaqχ
radalalde ʃːibɡo ʒo naqχe toɡe roɡʔineɡʼan kwanatʃʼoɡo χutʼarab tsʼaduɬ buχʼje
ɡʔale nuʒetsa ɡʔjeb kwanaze kːoleb qʼaɡʼida saparalde qʼatʃʼaral tʃaɡʼi kiniɡin retʼun retʼjelɡun qʼan ratʃelɡun χʼatʼazda retʼun χʔitalɡun qχatikʔ kːun ɡʼansaɡun ɡʼjedeɡʼaliqχeɡo kwanaj ɡʔjeb ɡʔjeb kːola betʼjerhanasul pesaχ
ɡʔjeb sordojaɬ dun misri qʼotʼun ine wuɡo wa ditsa χwezarize ruɡo kinalɡo tʼotsere ɡʔarural ɬimalɡi botsʼul ʃːibab tʼotsebe ɡʔaburab tʼintʃʼɡi ditsa ʒaza ɡʔabize buɡo misrijaɬul tʼolalɡo allaɡʔzabaze dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
amma nuʒer minabazul kawabazda baχarab bi bukʼina nuʒ tsʼunuleb ɡʼalamatɬun ɡʔjeb bi biχʔidal dun askʼosan ine wuɡo misrijalda tʼade ditsa χwalil unti bitʃːajdal nuʒeda ɡʔjeb qχwaze ɡʔjetʃʼo
ɡʔjeb qʼo nuʒeda kidaɡo kʼotʃonɡe ɡʔjeb qʼo nuʒee bajramɬun bukʼa abe betʼjerhanase tʼobitʼuleb bajramɬun abadijaɬeɡo nuʒeda tʼad ɬurab bajram χʼisabalda ratʃʼunel ɡʼjelazɡi kʼodo ɡʔabize bitʃːaj ɡʔjeb qʼo
ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ retʃːeb ʒubatʃʼjel tʃadal ɡuroni kwanaɡe tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬɡo roqʼosa retʃːeb tʼaɡʼinabe ʃːaj abuni ɡʔjeb ankʔɡo qʼojalda ʒanib retʃːeb ɬun ɡʔaburab tʃed kwanaraw tʃi ɡʼizrailaɬul χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qʼotʼize kːola
ɡʔjel qʼojazul tʼotsebeseb qʼo χirijab qʼoɬun bukʼine kːola ankʔabileb qʼoɡi χirijabɬun bukʼine kːola ɡʔjel qʼojaz ʃːibɡo χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe nuʒeeɡo kwen χʼadur ɡʔabi tun batʼijab
buɡʔurɡo tʃadazul bajram tʼobitʼje ʃːajɡureɬul ditsa nuʒ askaral ɡʔarun misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃana ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeb qʼo kʼodo ɡʔabe χadusel ɡʼjelazɡi ɡʔjeb buɡo abadijaɬeɡo nuʒee buɡeb amru
tʼotsebeseb motsʼaɬul antsʼila unqʼabileb qʼojaɬul qʼasi ɡʼuʒaldasa bajbiχʔun qʼolo tsoabileb qʼojaɬul qʼasi ɡʼuʒalde ʃːwezeɡʼan kwanaj retʃːeb tʼjetʃʼjeb tʃed
ankʔɡo qʼojalda ʒanib nuʒer qʼawuɬ bukʼine beɡʔularo retʃːebaɬul qʼatʼra retʃːeb ʁorɬ buɡeb kwen kwanaraw tʃi ʃːiw ɡʔjew wataniɡi qʼwatʼisa ɡotʃun watʃʼaraw wukʼa nuʒer rakʔtsojaw wukʼa ɡʔjew tʃi ɡʼizrailaɬul ʒamaɡʼatalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qʼotʼize kːola
ɡʔjel qʼojaz nuʒ kir rukʼaniɡi retʃːeb ʁorɬ χʼaltʼizaburab kinabɡʼaɡi kwen kwanaɡe kwanaj buɡʔurɡo tʃadal
