musatsa ɡʼizrailaɬul tsereqχabi dande rakʼarana wa ɡʔjezda abuna ineɡi un nuʒerɡo qχizamaze tso tso kʔjeɡʼjer tʼasa biʃːe ʃːiwas wa pesaχaɬul qʼurbanal qχwe
tsinɡi isːopaɬul
misrijal tʃʼwaze betʼjerhan waqχarab meχalda ɡʔjesda biχʔila kawujaɬul kʼijabɡo raqχaldaɡi raχazdaɡi baχarab bi wa ɡʔjeb mina ɡʔjes ʒibɡo tela nuʒ tʃʼwaze tʃʼwazejan nuʒer minabazda ʒaniwe ɬuɡʔine ruχʼ baqχulew malaikase iznuɡi kʔjelaro
nuʒee wa nuʒer χadusel naslabaze abadijaɬeɡo tʃʼjezaburab tʼadqʼaj χʼisabalda tsʼune ɡʔjeb amru
betʼjerhanas nuʒee kʔjeze qʼotʼi ɡʔaburab rakʔalde ʃːwedal ɡʔjenibɡi biɬːanqχizabe ɡʔjeb ɡʼadat
ɡʔab ʃːib ɡʼadat in nuʒer ɬimalaz ɡʔiqʼidal
ɡʔjezda abe ɡʔab kːola betʼjerhanase tʼobitʼuleb pesaχaɬul qʼurban misrijal tʃʼwaleb meχalda ɡʔjew ɡʼizrailazul minabazda askʼosan ana wa niʒ tarqχan ɡʔaruna jan
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ tʼolabɡo χalqʼ nakabazde kːana wa betʼjerhanase retsː ɡʔabuna
betʼjerhanas musadeɡi ɡʔarunideɡi amru ɡʔabunʃːinab muχʼkanɡo tʼubazabuna ɡʼizrailaz
sordo baʃːaɬuda misrijaɬul rakʔalda ɡʔabunʃːinab tʼotsebeseb ɬimadul ruχʼ baqχana betʼjerhanas misrijaɬul patʃajasul aj pirɡʼawnasul tʼotsebeseb ɬimadasa bajbiχʔun tusnaqχalda tʼamun wuɡew taqʼsirtʃijasul tʼotsebeseb ɬimade ʃːwezeɡʼan wa tʼolabɡo botsʼul ʃːibab tʼotsebe ɡʔaburab tʼintʃʼɡi χwezabuna
pirɡʼawnɡi ɡʔjesul tseresel tʃaɡʼiɡi tʼolalɡo misrijalɡi tʼade raqχana ɡʔjeb sardiɬ wa kisa kibeɡo misrijalda kutakab maɡʼil ɡʔarakʔ baqχana tsoniɡi ruqʼ χutʼun bukʼintʃʼo ʒanib χwel kːetʃʼjeb
ɡʔjebɡo sordojaɬ pirɡʼawnas musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi tʼade aχʼana wa ɡʔjezda abuna raqχa nuʒetsa kʼijazɡo wa tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailaz dir χalqʼɡi dir rakʔɡi te nuʒetsa abuleb bukʼarab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ betʼjerhanase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize a
ɡʼiɡi batʃe botsʼiɡi batʃe wa nuʒerɡo nuχda a dijeɡi tso duɡʼa ɡʔabe jan
misrijaz χalqʼ ɡʼjedeɡʼizabuleb bukʼana ulka tun ine
ɡuroni niʒ kinalɡo χwezeqχin ruɡo jan abuleb bukʼana ɡʔjez
χalqʼaɬ tsadaqχ bosana retʃːebɡi ʁorɬe ʒubatʃʼoɡo butsarab roɬ ɡʔjeb ʒanib ɬural χʼjertʃal ratʼliɬ ʒemana wa ʁaʒibutʼruzda ɬuna
ɡʼizrailaz musatsa ɡʔjezda maɬarab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ misrijazda ɡʔarun kʔjezabuna ɡʼartsulɡi mesedilɡi tsʼaraɡʼ wa retʼjel
betʼjerhanas misrijazul rekʼjeɬe ɡʼizrailazdeχun raχʼmu biʒizabuna wa ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjez ʃːib ɡʔaraniɡi kʔoleb bukʼana ɡʔjezije ɡʔjeb χʼalalda ɡʔjezije misrijazuqχa kʼudijab betʃeɬi ʃːwana
ɡʼizrailal ana raamsesaldasa sukːotalde rutʃːabiɡi ɬimalɡi rikʼkʼintʃʼoɡo kinawniɡi ɡʔjezul wukʼana anɬnusazarɡo biχʔintʃi
ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ rukʼana ɡʼjemeral batʼi batʼijal χalqʼazul ɡʼadamalɡi wa tsʼikʼkʼarab qʼadaralda ɡʼi botsʼiɡi
misrijaldasa ʒidedaɡo tsadaqχ bosun batʃʼarab butsarab roɬul ɡʔjez tʃadal reʒana retʃːeb ʒuban bukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjenibe ɡʔjel ɡʼjedeɡʼun misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire raqχinarun rukʼindal ɡʔjezije zaman bukʼintʃʼo saparalde tsadaqχ bosize kwen χʼadurize
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬ misrijalda bana unqʼnusijalda ɬeberɡo son
durusɡo unqʼnusijalda ɬeberɡo son tʼubarab qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanasul χalqʼ kʼudijal askaral ɡʔarun misrijaldasa naqχe ana
ɡʔjeb sordo kːola betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo makʔu toleb sordo ɡʔjeb sordojaɬ ɡʔjes misrijaldasa ɡʼizrailal naqχe ratʃana ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasul sordo buɡo ɡʼizrailaɬul tʼolalɡo ɡʼjelaze ɡʔjeb sordo kːola makʔu toleb sordo
betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna ɡʔale pesaχaɬul qʼurban qχwejaɬul tadbir batʼijab rakʔaldasa tʃijas ɡʔjeb kwine beɡʔularo
dutsa witʃun wosaraw laʁas ɡʔjeb kwine beɡʔula dutsa ɡʔjesije sunnat ɡʔabun buɡoni
amma zamanajaɬe ɡʼumru ɡʔabun nuʒer rakʔalda tʃʼaraw tʃijas jaɡi muχʔdaqχ kːuraw χʼaltʼuqχanas ɡʔjeb kwine beɡʔularo
ɡʔjeb qʼurban kwine kːola ɡʔjeb χʼadurarab roqʼob ɡʔan roqʼosa qʼwatʼibe bosuɡe wa ɡʔjeɬul tsoniɡi rakʔa bekuɡe
ɡʼizrailaɬul tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬ tʼobitʼize kːola ɡʔjeb bajram
nuʒeda tsadaqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabun wuɡew qʼwatʼirakʔaldasa tʃijase betʼjerhanasul pesaχ kʼodo ɡʔabize bokʔun buɡoni ɡʔjesul roqʼor ɡʼumru ɡʔabun ruɡel kinalɡo biχʔinaze sunnat ɡʔabize kːola ɡʔjebmeχalda ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬuɬ ɡʼaχʔalɬi ɡʔabize beɡʔula nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔow ɡʔawuraw tʃijasɡo ɡʼadin sunnat ɡʔabitʃʼjew tʃijas ɡʼaχʔalɬi ɡʔabize beɡʔularo pesaχaɬul bajramaɬul tʼutʼalda
tsoɡo qʼanun χʼaltʼula nuʒer rakʔtsojazeɡi wa batʼijab rakʔaldasa ratʃʼun nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabun ruɡel ɡʼadamazeɡi
ɡʼizrailaz kinabɡo ɡʔabuna musadeɡi ɡʔarunideɡi betʼjerhanas ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon
ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanas misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃana ɡʼizrailal askarazdeɡi rikʔun

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailaze ɡʔaburab ʃːibab tʼotsebeseb biχʔinɬimer dije batʼa ɡʔabe insanasul ɬimer bukʼa botsʼul tʼintʃʼ bukʼa ebelaɬul tʼotsebeseb riʒi
musatsa χalqʼalda abuna nuʒeda kidaɡo rakʼalda bukʼa nuʒ misrijaldasa laʁɬijaɬul rakʔaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃarab qʼo ʒindirɡo ʃːulijab kweraldaɬun ratʃana nuʒ betʼjerhanas ɡʔjenisa qʼwatʼire ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ nuʒetsa kwanaɡe retʃːeb ʒubarab tʃed
ʒaqʼa awiw motsʼalda nuʒetsa ɡʔab rakʔ toleb buɡo
nuʒer umumuze betʼjerhanas ɡʔa ban bukʼana χanaanijazul χitijazul amorijazul jewusijazul wa χiwijazul rakʔ raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb rakʔ nuʒee kʔjelilan dos ratʃun nuʒ ɡʔjenire ʃːwarab meχalda ɡʔadinab ɡʼadat tsʼune awiw motsʼaɬ
ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ kwanaj retʃːeb ʁorɬ ɡʔjetʃʼjeb tʃed ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanase bajram ɡʔabe
palχʼasil ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ kwanaze kːola retʃːeb ʒubatʃʼjeb tʃed nuʒer qʼawuɬ ʃːibniɡi retʃːeb ɬurab ʒo bukʼine beɡʔularo nuʒ tʃʼarab bakʼaldaɡi bukʼine beɡʔularo retʃːebaɬul qʼatʼratsin
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ ʃːiwas ʒindirɡo ɬimalazda abize kːola ditsa ɡʔadin ɡʔabuleb buɡo misrijaldasa naqχe uneɬul betʼjerhanas dije ɡʔaburabʃːinaɬe ɡʼolo jan
ɡʔab ɡʼadat nuʒee bukʼina kweralda ɬurab ɡʼuʒɬun wa nodojalda qχwarab rakʼaldeʃːwejaɬul ɡʼalamatɬun betʼjerhanasul qʼanun kidaɡo nuʒer matsʼalda bukʼinaɬe ɡʼolo betʼjerhanasul qʼuwatab kweraldaɬunɬidal nuʒ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃaral
ɡʔab ɡʼadat tʼubazabe ʃːibab sonaɬ ɡʔjeɬije biχʔizaburab zamanalda
betʼjerhanas nuʒee wa nuʒer umumuze ɡʔa ban bukʼarab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ nuʒ χanaanijazul rakʔaldeɡi ratʃun ɡʔjeb nuʒee kʔun χadusa
betʼjerhanase batʼa ɡʔabe ʃːibab tʼotsebeseb biχʔinɬimer ɡʔjedinɡo nuʒer botsʼul ʃːibab tʼotsebeseb biχʔintʼintʃʼɡi betʼjerhanasul kːola
tʼotsebe ɡʔaburab kʼartiqχ χisun kʔjeɡʼjer kʔje χisize bokʔitʃʼoni kʼjert ɡabur kʔurun χwezabe ʃːiwaw nuʒer tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw wasasuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔjeze kːola
χadubkːun dur naslujaɬ ɡʔjeɬul maɡʼna ʃːib abun tsʼjeχani ɡʔjezda abe betʼjerhanas ʒindirɡo qʼuwataldaɬun niɬ misrijaldasa laʁɬijaɬul rakʔaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃana
pirɡʼawn tʼirun tʃʼana niɬ naqχe ritʃːaze bokʔitʃʼoɡo ɡʔjedinɬidal misrijalda ɡʔabunʃːinab insanasulɡi χʼajwanaɬulɡi tʼotsebeseb riʒi χwezabuna betʼjerhanas ɡʔjele ɡʔjedinɬidalin ʃːibab χʼajwanaɬul tʼotsebeseb tʼintʃʼ ditsa betʼjerhanase qʼurbanaɬe kʔoleb niɬer tʼotsere ɡʔarural wasazuqχin abuni χʼaqʼ kʔola
ɡʔjeb bukʼine kːola dur kwerda ɬurab ɡʼuʒ ɡʼadin wa dur nadalda buχʔarab tʃalma ɡʼadin ʒindirɡo qʼuwataldaɬun betʼjerhanas niɬ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃinaɬul ʒintsa bitsuneb nuɡʼɬun
pirɡʼawnas χalqʼ naqχe bitʃːarab meχalda allaɡʔas ɡʔjeb batʃintʃʼo pilistimazul rakʔaldasan kiɡʼanɡo ɡʔjenisan nuχ qʼoqʼab bukʼaniɡi allaɡʔas pikru ɡʔabuna
ɡʔjel nuχda raʁize kːani ɡʔjezul pikru χisize beɡʔula wa ɡʔjel misrijalde tʼadrusːine beɡʔula jan
allaɡʔas χalqʼ batʃana χalatab awlaqχaɬul nuχkːun baɡʼarab raɬdaqχe
musatsa jusupil ʒanazaɡi tsadaqχ bosana ʃːajɡureɬul jusupitsa ɡʼizrailal ɡʔjedizarun rukʼana
allaɡʔ tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo nuʒee kumekaɬe waqχine wuɡo ɡʔjeb meχalda dir ʒanazaɡi ɡʔanisa naqχe bose nuʒedaɡo tsadaqχ ilanɡi abun
sukːotaldasa raqχun salul awlaqχalda askʼob buɡeb etamalde ʃːwana ɡʼizrailal wa ɡʔjenir ɬalqχana
qʼad χʼubiɬun eχetarab nakʼkʼul partʃaduɬ ɡʔjezda tsewe ɡʔjezije nuχɡi biχʔizabulaɡo unaan betʼjerhan qʼasi ɡʔjezije kanɬi bukʼine ɡʔjew tsʼadul partʃadul χʼubijaɬuɬ wukʼunaan ɡʔjedinɬidal qʼasiɡi qʼadɡi ine res bukʼana ɡʔjezije
qʼad nakʼkʼul χʼubi qʼasi tsʼadul χʼubi kʼijabɡo tsoniɡi nuχaɬ χalqʼaldasa batʼaɬitʃʼo

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazda abe miɡdol aburab bakʼaldaɡi raɬdadaɡi ɡʔorkʔob buɡeb pi ɡʔaχirotaldeχun ralaɡʔun ajan wa ɡʔjenib ɬalqχi ɡʔabejan ritʃːante ɡʔjel raɬdal raɡʼalda bitʼun baɡʼal tsefonalda tsere tʃʼjeze
pirɡʼawnas pikru ɡʔabize buɡo awlaqχalda nuχɡi qʼosun swerdilel ratila ɡʼizrailal in
ditsa pirɡʼawnasul rekʼjeɬe soɡʼɬi bitʃːala wa ɡʔjew nuʒeda χaduw ɬuɡʔina amma pirɡʼawnasdaɬun wa ɡʔjesul askarazdaɬun dir tsʼaruje retsː bukʼina ɡʔjel ditsa qʼezarurab meχaɬ ɡʔjebmeχaɬ misrijazda ɬala dun betʼjerhan wukʼin ɡʼizrailaz ɡʔjedin ɡʔabizeɡi ɡʔabuna
misrijaɬul patʃajasda χalqʼ ɬutun anilan aburab meχalda pirɡʼawnasulɡi ɡʔjesul tseresel ɡʼadamazulɡi pikru χisana wa ɡʔjez abuna
niɬetsa ɡʔaburab ʒo ʃːib niɬetsa ɡʼizrailalɡi ritʃːan tun niɬɡo χʼaltʼuqχabazdasa maχʼrum ɡʔarunaɡuri
pirɡʼawnas ʒindirɡo tʃujalɡun tʃolɡʔoko χʼadurana wa ʒindirɡo askarɡi dande aχʼana
ɡʔjes tsadaqχ batʃana anɬnusɡo tʼasa biʃːarab tʃolɡʔokoɡi misrijaɬul tsoɡidal tʃolɡʔakazul askarɡi ʃːibab tʃolɡʔakida tʼad raʁuɬ ɬadararal raʁuqχabiɡi rukʼana
betʼjerhanas pirɡʼawnasul rekʼjeɬe soɡʼɬi bitʃːan bukʼun ɡʔjew ɡʼizrailazda χaduw wortana ɡʼizrailal nuχda unel rukʼana ʒidee ʃːibɡo χʼinqʼi ɡʔjetʃʼjel tʃaɡʼi ɡʼadin
pirɡʼawnasul tʃolɡʔakalɡun wa tʃotʼaqχabiɡun ɡʼizrailazda χadur rortaral misrijal ɡʔjezda χadur ɡʼuntʼana raɬdal raɡʼalda qʼajiɡi tʃʼwan pi ɡʔaχirotalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ baɡʼal tsefonalda ɡʼizrailal rukʼaɡo
ʒiderɡo askarɡun pirɡʼawn ɡʼaɡarɬulew wiχʔidal ɡʼizrailazda bitʃʼtʃʼana misrijal ʒideda χadur ɬuɡʔun rukʼin ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjel kutakalda χʼinqʼana wa ɡʔjez betʼjerhanasde aχʼi baze bajbiχʔana
misrijalda χabal rukʼintʃʼoɡojiʃː dutsa niʒ χweze awlaqχalde ratʃaral in musada kʼalɡʔiqʼize ʒurana ɡʔjel misrijaldasa qʼwatʼireɡi ratʃun dutsa niʒee ɡʔaburab ʃːib
misrijaldaɡo niʒetsa duda abuleb bukʼintʃʼiʃː niʒ ʒaχʼalɡo te misrijaze χʼaltʼize te niʒ in misrijazul laʁzalɬun χutʼizeɡo ɬikʼan niʒee ɡʔab awlaqχalda χwezeɡʼan
musa χalqʼalda kʼaɬana nuʒ χʼinqʼuɡe qʼwakʼun tʃʼa nuʒeda biχʔila betʼjerhanas nuʒ ʒaqʼa χwasar ɡʔaruleb kuts ɡʔabsaɡʼat nuʒer berazda tsere ruɡel dol misrijal nuʒeda tʼokʼaɬ kidaniɡi riχʔize ɡʔjetʃʼo
paraχat rukʼa betʼjerhan waʁize wuɡo ɡʔjelɡun nuʒee ɡʼolo
betʼjerhanas musada abuna ʃːaj dutsa dide aχʼi baleb ɡʼizrailal tsere ratʃe
durɡo ɡʼansa eχede borχe wa raɬdada tʼade balaɡʔizabe tsinɡi ɡʔjeb kʼijide bikʔize buɡo ɡʔjebmeχalda ɡʼizrailazda kʼweze buɡo raqʼdadasan kiniɡin raɬdal tʼinaldasan ine
ditsa misrijazul rekʼjeɬe soɡʼɬi bitʃːana ɡʔjelɡi nuʒeda χadur ɬuɡʔine ruɡo amma ʒindirɡo tʃolɡʔakalɡun tʃotʼaqχabiɡun wa tʼolabɡo askarɡun pirɡʼawnasda ditsa dirɡo qʼudrat biχʔizaburab meχaɬ dije kʼudijab retsː bukʼine buɡo
misrijazda ɬaze buɡo dun betʼjerhan wukʼin wa pirɡʼawnɡi ɡʔjesul tʃujalɡi tʃolɡʔakalɡi tʃotʼaqχabiɡi sababɬun dije retsː bukʼine buɡo
ɡʼizrailaɬul askaralda tsewe unew wukʼaraw allaɡʔasul malaik ɡʔjezda naqχeχun tʃʼana nakʼkʼul partʃaɡi ʒindirɡo bakʼaldasaɡi kʔurun busːun ɡʔjezda naqχa
misrijaɬul χalqʼaldaɡi ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob tʃʼana tʼolabɡo sordojaɬ nakʼkʼul partʃa tsojab raqχaɬe betsʼɬiɬun tsoɡidab raqχaɬe kanɬiɬun tʃʼana wa ɡʔjeb sordojaɬ betsʼɬiɡi kanɬiɡi tsotsaɬ ʒubatʃʼo
musatsa raɬdada tʼade kwer bitʼana wa betʼjerhanas tʼubarab sordojaɬ qʼuwatab baqʼbakːul ɡʔuriɡi baqχinabun raɬad bikʔana wa ɡʔjeɬul tʼinu raqʼdalɬijalde swerizabuna ɬim bikʔun ana
wa ɡʼizrailaz baqʼwarab tʼindasanɡi riɬːun raɬad baχana ɬim kʼiɡo qʼed ɡʔabun baqχun tʃʼun bukʼana tso ɡʔjezul kwaranab raqχalda tsoɡijab ɡʔjezul kweɡʼab raqχalda
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ misrijalɡi ɡʔjezda χadur rortana pirɡʼawnasul tʃujalɡi tʃolɡʔakalɡi tʃotʼaqχabiɡi kinalɡo raɬdal tʼinalde kʼantsʼana
roɡʔalil qχaχʼɬi reχuleb ɡʼuʒalda tsʼadul wa nakʼkʼul partʃaduɬan wakːun betʼjerhan walaɡʔana misrijazul askaraɬuqχ wa ɡʔjeb saɡʼataldaɡo ɡʔjezde kutakab χʼinqʼi reʃːtʼinabuna
ɡʔjezul tʃolɡʔakazul ɡʔakiburdul ʒaʁalɬana ɡʔjedinɬidal tʃujazeɡi riɬːine tsʼaqʼ zaχʼmaɬun kːana
tsinɡi misrijal aχʼdeze ɬuɡʔana
ɡʔanisa naqχe ɬutize kːola ɡʼizrailazul raqχaldasan misrijalda dande waʁulew wuɡo ʒiwɡo betʼjerhan in abun
ɡʔjeb meχaɬ betʼjerhanas musada abuna raɬdada tʼade kwer bitʼje ɬim tʼadbusːun misrijazde ɡʔjezul tʃujalɡun tʃolɡʔakazde wa tʃotʼaqχabazde tʼade tʃwaχize bukʼine
musatsa raɬdada tʼade kwer bitʼana wa roɡʔaliɬ ɬim ʒindirɡo bakʼalde tʼadbusːun tʃwaχana rekerun unel rukʼaral misrijal ɡʔultʃun batʃʼuneb ɬadakʔje kːana wa betʼjerhanas ɡʔjel raɬdal bakʔuɬ ɬadaɬ tʼjerχʔinaruna
tʼolabɡo ɬim tʼadbusːun batʃʼindal ɡʔjeɬ ʁanqʼizaruna tʃolɡʔakalɡi tʃotʼaqχabiɡi ɡʼizrailazda χadub raɬdaɬe bortarab pirɡʼawnasul tʼolabɡo askar ɡʔjezul tsoniɡijaw χwasarɬitʃʼo
ɡʼizrailazin abuni raɬad bakʔuɬan baqʼwarab tʼindasanɡi riɬːun baχana raɬad ɬim tso ɡʔjezul kwaranab raqχalda tsoɡidab kweɡʼab raqχalda kʼiɡo qʼed ɡʔabun baqχun tʃʼun bukʼana
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanas ɡʼizrail misrijazdasa χwasar ɡʔabuna wa ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔjezul ʒanazabi riχʔana raɬdal raɡʼalda
ʒindirɡo qʼudrataldaɬun betʼjerhanas misrijaze ɡʔaburab biχʔidal ɡʔjel betʼjerhanasutɬʼ:a kutakalda χʼinqʼana wa ɡʔjesde iman ɬuna ɡʔjesul laʁ musadaɡi boʒana

dur χalqʼ askʼosan un ɬuɡʼizeɡʼan dir betʼjerhan
dutsa dujeɡo tʼasa biʃːarab χalqʼ
dutsa dur χalqʼ χirijab maɡʼarde batʃina
ɡʔjenib dujeɡo ruqʼɬun tʼasa biʃːarab bakʼalda
ja dir betʼjerhan
dutsaɡo kʔutʃʼ ɬurab muqʼadasab bakʼalda
ɡʔjel tʃʼjeze rukʼine
dir betʼjerɡʔan
betʼjerhan wukʼina patʃaɬun abadul abadijaɬeɡo
pirɡʼawnasul tʃujalɡun tʃolɡʔakal wa tʃotʼaqχabi raɬdaɬe ɬuɡʔarab meχalda betʼjerhanas ɡʔjezda tʼade ritʃːana raɬdal karatʃelal ɡʼizrailil χalqʼin abuni raɬad qʼotʼun ana raqʼdadasan ɡʼadin
ɡʔarunil jats marjam awaraɡaɬ ʒerʁen kodobe bosana wa tʼolalɡo rutʃːabiɡi kodor ʒerʁabiɡi kːun ɡʔjelda χadur riɬːun kʔurdize ɬuɡʔana
marjamitsaɡi ketʃʼ aχʼana
betʼjerhanase ketʃʼ aχʼje
ɡʔjesul χʼalkʼoɬi ɡʔjesul tʼadeɡʼanɬi
tʃuɡi tʃotʼaqχanɡi
raɬdaɬe reχana ɡʔjes ilanɡi abun
musatsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ batʃana baɡʼarab raɬdal raɡʼalaldasa ʃur aburab salul awlaqχalde ɬabɡo qʼo bana ɡʔjez awlaqχalda χʔwadulel kibɡo ɬimɡi batularoɡo
mara abuleb bakʼalde ʃːwana ɡʔjel amma ɡʔjenibɡi ɬim ɡʔjeqʼeze kʼoleb bukʼintʃʼo ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb kʔoɡʼab bukʼun ɡʔjele ɡʔjedinɬidalin ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tsʼarɡi mara
naqχeɡi musadasa razi ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo ɬuɡʔana χalqʼ
niʒetsa ʃːib ɡʔjeqʼeze buɡeb abun qʼulqʼudana ɡʔjel
tsinɡi musatsa betʼjerhanasde aχʼi bana wa betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesda ʁwetʼ biχʔizabuna musatsa ɡʔjeɬul ɡʼarkʔjel ɬadaɬe reχana wa ɬim ɡʔuinabɬun ɬuɡʔana
ɡʔjeb bakʼalda betʼjerhanas ɡʔjezul boʒijaɬul χʼalbiχʔana wa ɡʔjezije qʼanunalɡi aχʼkamalɡi kʔuna
ɡʔjes abuna
nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul raɡʼuqχ nuʒ kʼwarkʔun ɡʼjenekːani wa ɡʔjesije bokʔarab ɡʔabuni nuʒetsa ɡʔjesul bujuruqχal tʼurazarulel ruɡoni wa ɡʔjesul amrabazda reqʼon ɡʼumru ɡʔabuni ditsa nuʒeda tʼade bitʃːaze ɡʔjetʃʼo misrijazde ritʃːaral untabazul tsoniɡijab dun nuʒ saχ ɡʔarulew betʼjerhan wuɡo
ɡʔjenisa ɡʔjel ana elimalde ɡʔjenib bukʼana antsʼila kʼiɡo itsːɡi ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo tʃamasdakil ʁwetʼɡi ɡʔjel itsːazda askʼor ɬalqχana ɡʼizrailal

ɡʼizrailaɬul χalqʼ elimaldasaɡi ana wa elimaldaɡi sinajaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob buɡeb sin abuleb salul awlaqχalde ʃːwana ɡʔjeb bukʼana misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ɡʼizrailal raqχun χaduseb kʼiabileb motsʼaɬul antsʼila ʃːuabileb qʼo
ɡʔjeb awlaqχalda rukʼaɡo ɡʼizrailal naqχeɡi musadeɡi ɡʔarunideɡi ɡʼajibal ɡʼuntʼizarun qʼulqʼudana
ɡʼizrailaz ɡʔjezda abuleb bukʼana
betʼjerhanasul kwerdasan misrijaldaɡo χweze ɬikʼab bukʼana niʒee doba niʒee χʔaɡal tsʼun beɬize ɡʔanɡi ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwanaze tʃedɡi bukʼana nuʒetsajin abuni tʼolabɡo χalqʼ baqʼutsa χwezabize niʒ baqʼwarab awlaqχalde ratʃana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanas musada abuna ditsa zodisa ʁorkʔje nuʒeda tʼade tsʼadɬun tʃwaχizabize buɡo tʃed bitʃːante χalqʼaɬ ʃːibab qʼojaɬ awlaqχaldeɡi un ʒideeɡo tso qʼojaɬe ɡʼurab tʃed bakʼarize ɡʔjedin ditsa χʼalbiχʔize buɡo ɡʔjezul ɡʔjel dir qʼanunazda naqχriɬːuniʃːali balaɡʔize
anɬabileb qʼojaɬ ruzman qʼojaɬ tsoɡi qʼojaz bakʼarulelda dande kːun bitʃːante ɡʔjez kʼiɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼun bakʼarize ɡʔjeb
musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazda abuna qʼasi nuʒeda ɬaze buɡo nuʒ betʼjerhanas ratʃun rukʼin misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire
meter radal nuʒeda biχʔila betʼjerhanasul χʼalkʼoɬi ʃːajɡureɬul betʼjerhanasda raɡʼana nuʒer ɡʔjesdeχun buɡeb razi ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi niʒɡun daɡʼbadize kːani niʒ ʃːal tʃaɡʼi
χadubɡi musatsa abuna
qʼasi betʼjerhanas ɡʔan kʔjeze buɡo nuʒee kwanaze radal ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan tʃed kʔjeze buɡo ɡʔjesda raɡʼun buɡeɬul nuʒer ɡʔjesdeχun buɡeb razi ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi niʒer bitsani ʃːal niʒ kːolel niʒeda ɡʼajibal tʃʼwalel tʃaɡʼi ɡuro nuʒ betʼjerhanasda ɡʼajibal tʃʼwalel tʃaɡʼi ruɡo
tsinɡi musatsa ɡʔarunida abuna
ɡʼizrailazul ʒamaɡʼatalda abe betʼjerhanasda tsere tʃʼjeze raqχa ɡʔjesda nuʒer razi ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi raɡʼun buɡeɬul
ɡʔarun ɡʼizrailil χalqʼɡun kʼaɬaleb meχaɬ ɡʔjel awlaqχaldeχun ralaɡʔana wa ɡʔjezije zaɡʔirɬana nakʼkʼul partʃaduɬ tʃʼarab betʼjerhanasul nur wa ɡʔjesul qʼudrat
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan kʼaɬana musada
dida raɡʼana ɡʼizrailazul ɡʼarzal ɡʔjezda abe markʼatʃʼul ɡʼuʒalda nuʒetsa ɡʔan kwanaze buɡo roɡʔalil ɡʼuʒaɬ nuʒer tʃaχʔal tʃaditsa ɡʼortsʼize ruɡo ɡʔjebmeχalda ɬaze buɡo nuʒeda nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ dun wukʼin
ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬul markʼatʃʼul ɡʼuʒaɬ rorʒun ratʃʼana tʃʼorolabi wa ɡʔjez tsʼjezabuna tʼolabɡo ɡʔjezul qʼaji tʃʼwarab bakʼ roɡʔalidejin abuni sweruqχɬiɡo ʃːubitsa baχtʃun batana
ʃːub tʼasa arab meχalda awlaqχaɬul ɡʔumeralda zaɡʔirɬana ɡʼisinab krupajalda reɬːarab ʒo
ɡʔjeb biχʔidal ɡʼizrailaz tsotsazda tsʼjeχoleb bukʼana
ɡʔab ʃːib in
ɡʔjezda ɬaleb bukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjeb kisa ʃːib ʒo kːolebali musatsa ɡʔjezda abuna ɡʔjeb buɡo nuʒee betʼjerhanas kʔurab tʃed
betʼjerhanas amru ɡʔabuna bitʃːante ʃːiwaw tʃijas ɡʔjeb bakʼarize ʒindijeɡo ɡʼurab qʼadaralda qχizanaɬul ʃːiwaw tʃi rikʼkʼun tso tso omer
ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna ɡʼizrailaz tsojaz tsʼikʼkʼun tsojaz daɡʔ bakʼarana
amma ɡʔjez omeraldaɬun ɡʔjeb bortsarab meχalda ɡʼjemer bakʼararazul tʼokʼɬiɡi daɡʔab bakʼararazul kamiɡi batitʃʼo ʃːiwas bakʼarun batana bitʼun ɡʔjesul qχizamaɬe ɡʼurab qʼadar
musatsa ɡʔjezda ɬazabuna
meteralde ɡʔjeɬul ɬitsaniɡi ʃːibniɡi ʒo naqχe toɡe jan
amma ɡʔjel musaqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼo wa ɡʔjez tso tso butʼa radalalde naqχe tana ɡʔjelda χʼapara bana kweʃab maχʼɡi baqχana ɡʔjeɬ musal tsʼaqʼ tsːin baqχana ɡʔjezda
radalɡo waqχun ʃːiwas bakʼarulaan ʒindije χʼaʒaɬuleb qʼadar ɡʼodob χutʼarab baqʼul χinɬi tʃʼwajdal biun tʼaɡʼunaan
anɬabileb qʼojaɬ ruzman qʼojaɬ ɡʔjez bakʼarana kʼiɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼun tso tʃi rikʼkʼun kʼiɡo omer χalqʼaɬul tsereqχabi ratʃʼana musaqχe wa ɡʔjeb ɡʔjesda bitsana
ɡʔjes ɡʔjezda abuna
ɡʔjedinin betʼjerhanas ɬazabun bukʼarab meter buɡo χʼalχʔijaɬul qʼo betʼjerhanasul χirijab ʃamatqʼo
musatsa aburab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ ɡʔjez χutʼarab naqχe tsʼunana χaduseb qʼo ʃːwezeɡʼan amma ɡʔab nuχalda ɡʔjelda χʼapara batʃʼo maχʼɡi baqχintʃʼo
ʒaqʼa ɡʔjeb kwanaj in abuna musatsa ʃːajɡureɬul ʒaqʼa buɡo betʼjerhanasul ʃamatqʼo ʒaqʼa nuʒeda awlaqχalda ʃːibɡo batize ɡʔjetʃʼo
nuʒetsa ɡʔjeb bakʼarize buɡo anɬɡo qʼojaɬ amma ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ ʃamatqʼojaɬ awlaqχalda nuʒeda ʃːibɡo batize ɡʔjetʃʼo
χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa tso tsojal ankʔabileb qʼojaɬɡi ɡʔjeb bakʼarize qʼwatʼire raqχana amma ɡʔjezda ʃːibɡo batitʃʼo
betʼjerhanas musada abuna kidalɬizeɡʼan nuʒ dir amrabazuqχɡi dir qʼanunazuqχɡi ɡʼjenekːilarel
nuʒeda ɬan bukʼa betʼjerhanas nuʒee kʔun buɡo ʃamatqʼo ɡʔjedinɬidal anɬabileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjes nuʒee kʔoleb buɡo kʼiɡo qʼojaɬe ɡʼurab tʃed ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ ʃːiwaw tʃi ʒindirɡo roqʼow tʃʼjeze kːola kiweniɡi qʼwatʼiwe waqχintʃʼoɡo
ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ χalqʼ χʼalχʔijalda tʃʼana
ɡʼizrailaɬul χalqʼaɬ ɡʔjeb kwanda tsʼar tana manna abun ɡʔjeb bukʼana ʁaranχeraɬul χʔonalda reɬːarab qχaχʼab kʔjeraɬul ɡʔatsʼul bakarabazul ɡʼadab tʼaɡʼam buɡeb niɡʼmat
musatsa abuna
ɡʔadinab buɡo betʼjerhanasul amru mannajaɬul tso omer bose wa ɡʔjeb naqχe tsʼunun te χadusel ɡʼjelaze misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃarab meχalda awlaqχalda ditsa nuʒee kwanaze kʔoleb bukʼarab tʃed ɡʔjezda biχʔun bukʼine
tsinɡi musatsa ɡʔarunida abuna
qχabaɡi bosun ɡʔjenibe ʒanibe mannajaɬul tso omer baj χadusel ɡʼjelaze tsʼunun bukʼineɬun ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɬe
musadasan zaɡʔirɬarab betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon mannajaɬul tsʼurab qχaba qʼotʼijaɬul ʁansida tsebe ɬuna ɡʔarunitsa
ɡʔjezije qχwarab χanaanaɬul rakʔaɬul ɡʼorqχabazde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʼizrailaz kʼiqʼoɡo sonaɬ manna kwanaleb bukʼana
omer kːola jefajaɬul

tsinɡi betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬ sin awlaqχ tana wa bakʼ bakʼalda ɬalqχiɡi ɡʔabulaɡo ɡotʃarileb bukʼana tso nuχalda ɡʔjel refidimalda ɬalqχana wa ɡʔjenib qʼaji tʃʼwana amma ɡʔjenib ɡʔjeqʼeze ɬim bukʼintʃʼo
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musada ɡʼajibal tʃʼwaze bajbiχʔana ɡʔjez
ɬim kʔje niʒee niʒ qʼetʃon ruɡo janɡi abun
ʃːaj nuʒetsa dideχun daɡʼba baleb in abuna musatsa ʃːaj nuʒetsa betʼjerhanasul χʼalbiχʔuleb
amma χalqʼ qʼetʃon tatu χun bukʼana wa musada kʼalɡʔiqʼize ɬuɡʔana
ʃːaj dutsa niʒ misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃaral niʒɡi niʒer ɬimalɡi ɡʼi botsʼiɡi qʼetʃon χwezarizejiʃː duje bokʔarab inɡi abun
wa musa betʼjerhanasde aχʼi baze ɬuɡʔana
ʃːib ɡʔabileb ditsa ɡʔab χalqʼalda dun ɡʔaz ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwazeqχin wuɡoɡuri jan
betʼjerhanas musaje ʒawab ɡʔabuna ɡʼizrailaɬul tsereqχabazul tso tʃanɡojawɡi tsadaqχ watʃun χalqʼalda tsewe waqχa nilalda kʔabun bukʼarab ɡʼansaɡi bose
dun χoriwaɬul kʔurda tʼad duda dandwitʼun tʃʼjela dutsa kʔurda kʔabe wa ɡʔjelda ʒanisa ɬim tʃwaχize buɡo tsinɡi χalqʼaɬul qʼetʃ busːina musatsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna ɡʼizrailazul tsereqχabazdaɡi biχʔun
musatsa ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tsʼar ɬuna masːa
amalekijal ratʃʼana wa refidimalda ruɡel ɡʼizrailazda tʼade kʼantsʼana
musatsa jeɡʔoʃuada abuna χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa lebalal biχʔinal tʼasa riʃːe amalekijalɡun raʁize dunin abuni meter kodob kːun allaɡʔasul ɡʼansaɡun ɡoχʼil tʼoɡʔiw tʃʼjela
jeɡʔoʃuatsa musatsa maɬarab ɡʔabuna wa naqχiseb qʼojaɬ amalekijazda dande raʁ bajbiχʔana musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi χʼurɡi ɡoχʼil tʼoɡʔire raχana
musatsa kweral rorχun ruɡebɡʼan meχaɬ ɡʼizrailal berɡʔunaan amma ɡʔjes kweral ɡʼodore ritʃːarab laχʼzataldaɡo amalekijal berɡʔunaan
amma musal kweral swakalel rukʼana ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔarunitsaɡi χʼuritsaɡi bosun ɡamatʃʼ ɬuna ɡʔjesda ʁorkʔ musa ɡʔjelda tʼad ɡʼodow tʃʼana ɡʔarunɡi χʼurɡi ɡʔjesul kʼijabɡo χʔolboqχ eχetana wa ɡʔjez kːun tʃʼjezaruna ɡʔjesul kweral tsojas tsojab raqχaldasan tsoɡidas tsoɡidab raqχaldasan baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan musal kweral rorχun tʃʼjezarun rukʼana wa
ɡʔjeb raʁuɬ jeɡʔoʃuatsa qʼezabuna amalekijazul askar
ɡʔjeldasa χadub betʼjerhanas musada abuna
dutsa ɡʔaɬul qχwaj qχwaɡʼaj ɡʔabe wa jeɡʔoʃuada bitse amalekil χalqʼ ditsa ɡʔab dunjalaldasa tʼubanɡo ɬuɡʼizabize buɡin
tsinɡi musatsa betʼjerɡʔanase qʼurbanaɬe bakʼ bana wa ɡʔjes ɡʔjelda jhwh nisːi
wa ɡʔjes abuna betʼjerhanasul taχide kwer borχun bukʼana ɡʔjedinɬidal betʼjerhanas raʁ ɡʔabila amalekɡun ɡʼasrabazuɬa ɡʼasrabazuɬe

midjanaɬul kaʃiʃasda aj musal wakʔad itroda raɡʼana allaɡʔas musajeɡi ʒindirɡo χalqʼ ɡʼizrailaɬeɡi ɡʔaburabʃːinaɬul wa betʼjerhanas ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼibe batʃinaɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musal wakʔad itro nuχda waqχana ʒindirɡo jas wa musal ɬadi tsiporaɡi jatʃana tsadaqχ ɡʔjej tsee ebel insul roqʼoje tʼadjusːinajun jikʼana musatsa
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔjeɬul kʼiɡo wasɡi watʃana ɡʔjezul tsojasda tsʼar ɬun bukʼana ɡerʃom
tsoɡidasda elijezer
wa musal wakʔad itro watʃʼana ratʃun ɡʔjesul wasalɡun wa ɬadiɡun salul awlaqχalde allaɡʔasul meɡʼjeralda askʼob musatsa qʼaji tʃʼwarab bakʼalde
itrotsa musaqχe χabar bitʼana
dun dur wakʔad itro watʃʼunew wuɡo duqχe dur ɬadiɡun wa dur kʼiɡo wasɡun tsadaqχ
musa wakʔadasda dandtʃʼwaze qʼwatʼiwe waqχana wakʔad wiχʔidal ɡʔjew ɡʔjesije qʼulana wa ɡʔjezul χinab dandtʃʼwaj kːana salam kalamɡi ɡʔabun ɡʔjel tʃadiraɬure ɬuɡʔana
musatsa wakʔadasda bitsana ɡʼizrailaɬe ɡʼolo betʼjerhanas pirɡʼawnaseɡi misrijazeɡi ɡʔaburabʃːinaɬul nuχda ʒidedaɡo riχʔaral zaχʼmaɬabazul wa betʼjerhanas ʒalɡo χwasar ɡʔarijaɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ
itro woχun wukʼana misrijaɬul kwerʃːalikʔa erkenɡi ɡʔarun betʼjerhanas ɡʼizrailaze kiɡʼan ɡʼjemer ɬikʼɬi ɡʔaburabali raɡʼidal
itrotsa abuna misrijaɬulɡi pirɡʼawnasulɡi kwerʃːalikʔa nuʒer χalqʼ erken ɡʔaburaw betʼjerhanase retsː
ɡʔanʒe dida ɬana betʼjerhan tsoɡidal allaɡʔzabazdasa kiɡʼanɡi tʼadeɡʼanaw wukʼin ɡʼamalkʼodoɡo zulmu χʼal ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔarazul kwerʃːalikʔa χalqʼ erken ɡʔaburaw
χadub musal wakʔad itrotsa allaɡʔase tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb qʼurbanɡi tsoɡidal qʼurbanalɡi ɡʔaruna tsadaqχ ɡʼizrailaɬul tsereqχabiɡun ɡʔarunɡi watʃʼana musal wakʔadasulɡun tʼutʼ ɡʼaχʔal ɡʔabize
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ musatsa bajbiχʔana χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔob kːara taraɬuqχ wa kinab bataniɡi daɡʼba qʼetsaɬuqχ ɡʼjenekːize wa ʃːibab sualaɬe reqʼarab χʼukmu qʼotʼize wa roɡʔalidasa baqχarab qʼasiɬizeɡʼan ɡʔjesda sweruqχ bakʼarun bukʼana χalqʼ
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo biχʔarab meχaɬ ɡʔjesul wakʔad itrotsa abuna
ɡʔab ʃːib dutsa χalqʼaɬe ɡʔabuleb buɡeb ʃːaj tsoχʼo dutsaɡo ɡʔabuleb ɡʔjeb χʼaltʼi tʼolabɡo χalqʼɡi roɡʔalidasa baqχarab qʼasiɬizeɡʼan duda sweruqχ baqχun tʃʼjezabun
musatsa ʒawab ɡʔabuna ɡʔjel diqχe ratʃʼuna kːara tarab ʒojaɬe allaɡʔasul χʼukmu balaɡʔize
ʒidedaɡo ɡʔorkʔob daɡʼba kːarab meχalda ɡʔjel ratʃʼuna diqχe ditsa χʼukmu qʼotʼula ɡʔjezije allaɡʔasul nizamalɡi qʼanunalɡi kʔotʃʼojeɡi rosun
musal wakʔadas abuna dutsa ɡʔjeb bitʼun ɡʔabuleb ɡʔjetʃʼo
durɡi duqχe ratʃʼunezulɡi swakan tatu χola ɡʔjedin ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb buɡo tsʼaqʼ zaχʼmatab χʼaltʼi tsoχʼo dutsaɡo tʼubazabize kʼoleb χʼaltʼi ɡuro ɡʔjeb
diqχ ɡʼjenekːe ditsa duje ɡʼaqʼlu kʔjela tsinɡi allaɡʔas kwerbaqʼaɡi duje mun wukʼa allaɡʔasdaɡi χalqʼaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔow ɡʔorkʔoqχanɬun wa dutsa ɡʔjesda tsere rose ɡʔjezul ɡʼarzal
ɡʔjedinɡo dutsa χalqʼalda maɬe nizamalɡi qʼanunalɡi bitʼarab nuχɡi χʔwada tʃʼwadiɡi
ɡʔjeldaɡo tsadaqχ χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼasa riʃːe baʒari buɡel allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼaral boʒi iman buɡel wa ɡʼartsuqχ jaχʼ bitʃularel ɡʼadamal wa ɡʔjelɡo tʼame azarɡojazda nusɡojazda kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡojazda wa antsʼɡojazda tʼad kʼudijalɬun
ɡʔjele ɡʔjez ɡʔabize bitʃːante ɡʼadamazda ɡʔorkʔob kːara taraɬul χʼisab sual zaχʼmatal iʃal kːani ritʃːante ɡʔjez ɡʔjel duqχe rosun ratʃʼine biɡʔajal iʃal ʒidetsaɡo tʼurazarize ritʃːaj dur ɡʔir ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔob bikʔani ɡʔjeb duje biɡʔaɬila
dutsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuni allaɡʔaseɡi ɡʔjeb qʼabulɬani dujeɡoɡi ɡʔir batʃːize biɡʔaɬila ɡʼadamalɡi raziɡo roqʼo roqʼore tʼadrusːina
musa wakʔadasuqχ ɡʼjenekːana wa kinabɡo ɡʔjes abuqχe ɡʔabuna
ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔosa ɡʔjes tʼasa riʃːana baʒari buɡel ɡʼadamal wa ɡʔjel tana χalqʼalda tʼad azarɡojazda nusɡojazda kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡojazda wa antsʼɡojazda tʼad
ɡʔjel ɬuɡʔana χalqʼaɬe χʼukmu qʼotʼulel diwantʃaɡʼiɬunɡi zaχʼmatal sualal ɡʔjez rosulaan musaqχe biɡʔajalin abuni ʒidetsaɡo tʼuralaan
tsodaɡʔab zamanaldasan musatsa wakʔad nuχareɡʼana wa itro ʒindirɡo ulkajalde tʼadwusːun ana

misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire raqχun ɬababileb motsʼaɬ ɡʼizrailal ʃːwana sinajaɬul salul awlaqχalde
refidimaldasa sinaj awlaqχalde ana ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ wa ɡʔjenib meɡʼjeralda askʼob qʼaji tʃʼwana
musa maɡʼarde waχana allaɡʔasda tsewe tʃʼjeze wa betʼjerhan kʼaɬana ɡʔjesda jaqʼubil zurijatalda ɡʔadin abe wa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɡʔadin bitse
nuʒeda biχʔana ditsa misrijaɬe ɡʔaburab wa ditsa nuʒ tsʼudul kwarkʔijalda kiniɡin rosun ɡʔanire diqχeɡo ratʃarabɬi
ɡʔanʒe diqχ ɡʼjenekːe nuʒ tʼubanɡo dije mutʼiɡʼɬulel ruɡoni wa nuʒetsa dirɡun qʼotʼi tʼubazabuleb buɡoni kinalɡʼaɡi χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔor ɡʼitsʼɡo nuʒ rukʼine ruɡo dir baɡʔa tʼadeɡʼanab χazinaɬun tʼolabɡo dunjal dir kːola
amma nuʒ rukʼine ruɡo dir χirijab χalqʼɬun dir kaʃiʃzabazul ummatɬun ɡʔjebin abe ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda
musa maɡʼardasa ʁorkʔje ɬuɡʔana wa χalqʼaɬul tsereqχabiɡi aχʼun ɡʔjezda bitsana betʼjerhanasul amru
tsinɡi χalqʼaɬ tsoχʼo kʼaldisan ɡʼadin abuna
niʒetsa tʼubazabize buɡo betʼjerhanas tʼadqʼarabʃːinab
musa ɡʔjezul ʒawab bosun betʼjerhanasda tsewe wiɬːana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
dun watʃʼine wuɡo duqχe butʃːarab nakʼkʼuɬ wa χalqʼalda tsewe duda kʼaɬaze wuɡo ɡʔjel abadijaɬeɡo duda boʒize rukʼine
tsinɡi musatsa betʼjerhanasda bitsana χalqʼaɬul ʒawab
betʼjerhanas musada abuna χalqʼaɬuqχeɡi un ʒaqʼaɡi meterɡi ɡʔjezije dinijab ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul nizam tʼobitʼje bitʃːante ɡʔjez ʒiderɡo retʼjel kun tʃurize
wa ɡʔjel ɬababileb qʼojalde χʼadurɡo rukʼine ʃːajɡureɬul ɬababileb qʼojaɬ betʼjerhan sinaj maɡʼarda reʃːtʼine wuɡo tʼolabɡo χalqʼalda tsewe
meɡʼjeralda sweruqχ χalqʼaɬe ɡʼorqχi tʃʼjezabe wa ɡʔjezda abe meɡʼjeralda tʼade raχinaldasa wa ɡʔjeɬul aχaɬijalda qχwajaldasa nuʒɡo tsʼune meɡʼjeralda qχwanʃːinase ɡʼaʒal bukʼine buɡo
ɡʔjew ɡantʃʼitsa jaɡi tʃʼoral retʃʼtʃʼun tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasda kwer qχwazeɡi beɡʔularo insan wukʼa ɡʔjew χʼajwan bukʼa ɡʔjeb tsoɡo ɡʼaʒal ɡʼitsʼɡo χalat baqχun sur pun χadusala raχine beɡʔula maɡʼarde tʼade
musa maɡʼardasa ʁorkʔje χalqʼaɬuqχe wiɬːana wa ɡʔjes χalqʼ batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabuleb tadbir tʼobitʼana ɡʔjez retʼjel kunɡi tʃurana
ɡʔjes χalqʼalda abuna
ɬababileb qʼojalde χʼadurɬi ɡʔabe ɬudbuzda qχwaɡe
ɬababileb qʼojaɬul roɡʔalil ɡʼuʒalda ʁuʁadana dunjal wa pirχana piri meɡʼjeralda tʼad butʃːarab nakʼkʼ ɬuna wa suraɬube puleb kutakalda kʼudijab ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼana tʼolabɡo χalqʼ ɡʼjemerab χʼinqʼijaɬ sorodize ɬuɡʔana
qʼaji tʃʼwarab bakʼaldasa musatsa χalqʼ batʃana allaɡʔasda dande wa meɡʼjeraɬul aχaɬuda eχetana
sinaj meɡʼjer kʼkʼujaɬ batsun bukʼana ʃːajɡureɬul betʼjerhan ɡʔjelda tʼad reʃːtʼana tsʼaduɬ ɡʔjeɬul tʼoɡʔisan koroda ʒanisa kiniɡin ɡʔawajalde baqχun uneb bukʼana kʼkʼuj wa tʼolabɡo meɡʼjer soroduleb bukʼana
sur puleb ɡʔarakʔɡi kʼwanaɡʼan kʼodoɬuleb bukʼana musa kʼaɬalew wukʼana wa allaɡʔas ɡʔjesije ʒawab kʔoleb bukʼana jaqʼinab ɡʔarkʔidaɬun
betʼjerhan reʃːtʼana sinaj meɡʼjeraɬul tʼoɡʔiwe wa ɡʔjes musa ɡʔjeniwe aχʼana musa tʼade waχarab meχalda
betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesda abuna ɡʼodoweɡi reʃːtʼun χalqʼalda ɬazabe betʼjerhanasuqχ ralaɡʔizejan abun tʃʼjezaburab ɡʼorqχi baχun ʒanibeχun ɡʔjez ɡali tʼamuɡejan ɡuroni ɡʔjezul ɡʼjemerisel χweze ruɡo
betʼjerhanasde ɡʼaɡarɬulel kaʃiʃzabazɡi ʒalɡo ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔarize kːola ɡuroni betʼjerhanas ɡʔjezije ʒaza ɡʔabize buɡo
musatsa betʼjerhanasda abuna
χalqʼ sinaj meɡʼjeralde tʼade baχine ɡʔjetʃʼo dutsaɡoɬidal niʒeda kʔwarun ɬazaburab meɡʼjer sweruqχ ɡʼorqχi tʃʼjezabe wa ɡʔjeb batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabe jan
betʼjerhanas ʒawab kʔuna
ɡʼodowe reʃːtʼa wa ɡʔarunɡun tsadaqχ tʼade watʃʼa kaʃiʃzabazɡi χalqʼaɬɡi betʼjerhanasda tsere ratʃʼinejan ɡʼorqχi baχine pikruɡitsin ɡʔabuɡejan abe ɡuroni ɡʔjes ɡʔjezije ʒaza ɡʔabize buɡo
musa χalqʼaɬuqχe ɡʼodowe reʃːtʼana wa ɡʔjeb kinabɡo χalqʼalda bitsana

betʼjerhanas ɡʔadin abuna
dun wuɡo nuʒer betʼjerhan laʁɬun nuʒ rukʼarab rakʔaldasa aj misrijaldasa nuʒ qʼwatʼire ratʃaraw nuʒer allaɡʔ
dun ɡurel batʼijal allaɡʔzabi nuʒer rukʼine beɡʔularo
nuʒeeɡo ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔ ɡʔawuɡe tʼad zobalazda buɡeɬul bukʼa ɡʼodob rakʔalda buɡeɬul bukʼa ɬadaɬ jaɡi rakʔuɬ buɡeɬul bukʼa kinabɡʼaɡi sipat surat ɡʔabuɡe
ɡʔjezije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabuɡe dun nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔɬidal χilipɬi χʼjeχʔolarew
amma dun wokʔulezul wa dir amrujal tʼurazarulezul naslabaze ɡʔjezul azarabileb ɡʼjelalde ɡʼuntʼunɡi raχʼmat bikʔulew
nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul tsʼar baqχuɡe kʼwar ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo
ʃamatqʼo kʼotʃonɡe ɡʔjeb χirijab qʼoɬun tsʼune
anɬɡo qʼojaɬ χʼaltʼje wa tʼolalɡo durɡo iʃal tʼurazare
amma ankʔabileb qʼo ɡʔjeb kːola dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔase batʼa ɡʔaburab ʃamatqʼo ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ nuʒetsa kinab buɡoniɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe ja dutsa ja nuʒer wasas jaɡi jasaɬ ja nuʒer laʁas jaɡi laʁaɬ ja nuʒer χʼajwanaɬ ja nuʒer ʃaɡʔaralda tʃʼjel ɡʔaburaw qʼwatʼirakʔaldasa tʃijas
anɬɡo qʼojalda ʒanib betʼjerhanas zobɡi rakʔɡi raɬadɡi wa ɡʔjezda tʼad ʁorkʔ buɡebʃːinabɡi biʒana ankʔabileb qʼojaɬin abuni χʼalχʔi ɡʔabuna ɡʔjedinɬidal betʼjerhanas ʃamatqʼojalda barakat ɬuna wa ɡʔjeb χirijab qʼoɬun ɡʔabuna
ebel insul adab qχatir ɡʔabe betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔurab rakʔalda nuʒerɡo ɡʼumru χalatab bukʼine
tʃi tʃʼwaɡe
zina ɡʔabuɡe
tsʼoɡʔ ɡʔabuɡe
ɡʔjeresinuɡʼɬi ɡʔabuɡe
tʃijar ruqʼalde χʔul ɬoɡe tʃijar ɬadude χʔul ɬoɡe ɡʔjesul laʁasde jaɡi laʁalde ɡʔjesul otsalde jaɬuni χʼamide ʃːibɡʼaɡi tʃijar ʒojalde χʔul ɬoɡe
tʼolabɡo χalqʼalda raɡʼuleb wa biχʔuleb bukʼana ʁuʁadiɡi pirχuleb piriɡi sur puleb ɡʔarakʔɡi kʼkʼujduɬ buɡeb meɡʼjerɡi χalqʼ kutakalda χʼinqʼun rikʼkʼadeɡʼan qʼan tʃʼana
munɡo kʼaɬaj niʒeda niʒ duqχ ɡʼjenekːila jan abuna ɡʔjez musada amma allaɡʔ niʒeda kʼaɬaɡejan ɡʔare niʒ χwetʃʼoɡo rukʼine
musatsa χalqʼalda abuna
nuʒ χʼinqʼuɡe allaɡʔ watʃʼun wuɡo nuʒer χʼalbiχʔize ɡʔjesukʔa χʼinqʼi nuʒer rakʼazuɬ biʒizabize nuʒetsa munaɡʔal teze rukʼine
χalqʼ rikʼkʼadeɡʼan eχetaraɬubɡo tʃʼana musajin abuni allaɡʔ ʒaniw wuɡeb betsʼab nakʼkʼul partʃajalda askʼowe ɡʼaɡarɬana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanas musada abuna ɡʼizrailazda abe nuʒedaɡo biχʔana dun zodisan nuʒɡun kʼaɬalew wukʼin
dir bakʼalda nuʒeeɡo ɡʼarats mesedaɬul allaɡʔzabi ɡʔaruɡe wa ɡʔjezije naku tʃʼwaɡe
dije qʼurban bakʼ baj χʼatʼul wa nuʒerɡo ɡʼi botsʼul reqχaɬa ratʃun qχwezeɡi qχun ɡʔjelda tʼad tʼoritʼje tʼuran ruχʼulel wa raqʼlil qʼurbanal ditsaɡo tʼasa biʃːarab ʃːibab bakʼalda dun nuʒeqχe watʃʼine wuɡo wa nuʒede barakat reʃːtʼinabize buɡo
dije qʼurban bakʼ ɡantʃʼil ɡʔabuleb buɡoni bekʼkʼarab ɡantʃʼil ɡʔabuɡe ɡʔjeb nuʒetsa kwartʼa kʼutʼidal ɡʔjeb qχubɬula
dir qʼurban bakʼalde boɬoduqχan tʼade raχunɡe ratʼlida ʁorkʔa nuʒer ɡʼitsʼɬi ɡʼadamazda biχʔitʃʼoɡo bukʼine

ɡʔale dutsa χalqʼaɬe zaɡʔir ɡʔarize kːolel qʼanunal
dutsa ʒuɡʔutʼaw laʁ witʃun wosun wuɡoni wa ɡʔjes duje anɬɡo sonaɬ qχuluqχɡi ɡʔabun batani ankʔabileb sonaɬ dutsa ɡʔjew erken ɡʔawize kːola ɡʔjesuqχ muχʔɡi bositʃʼoɡo
ɡʔjew ʒiwɡo tsoχʼo watʃʼun wukʼun watani erkenɡi ɡʔawila ʒiwɡo tsoχʼo wa ɬadiɡun wukʼun watani ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ erkenɬize te ɬadiɡi
naɡaɡʔ χwaʒainas laʁase ɬadi kʔun jikʼun jatani wa ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjesije ɬimalɡi ɡʔarun ruɡoni tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanɡi ɡʔjeɬul ɬimalɡi χutʼula χwaʒainase erkenɬi ʃːola ɡʼitsʼɡo ɡʔjesije
amma laʁas dije rokʔula dirɡo χwaʒainɡi ɬadiɡun ɬimalɡi ɡʔjedinɬidal dije erkenawɬun wukʼine bokʔun ɡʔjetʃʼo jan abuni
bitʃːante χwaʒainas ɡʔjew allaɡʔasda tsewe watʃine wa nutsʼida jaɡi nutsʼil χːenalda askʼowɡi tʃʼjezawun ɡʼjebujaɬ ɡʔjesul ɡʼin borɬize ɡʔjeldasa χadub ɡʔjew ɡʼumrujaɬɡo ɡʔjesul laʁɬun χutʼila
pulanaw tʃijas ʒindirɡo jas laʁɬijalde jitʃun jiɡoni ɡʔjej laʁɬijaldasa erken ɡʔajize beɡʔularo biχʔinal laʁzal erken ɡʔaruleb qʼaɡʼidajalda
χwaʒainas ɡʔjej ʒindijeɡo jatʃine josunɡi jikʼun amma ɡʔjesije ɡʔjej rekʼjee ɡʼun jatitʃʼoni ɡʔjes res kʔjeze kːola muχʔɡi kʔun ɡʔjej ʒinda askʼosa naqχe jatʃine amma ɡʔjesul iχtijar bukʼunaro ʒinditsaɡo naqχɡi tʃʼwan ɡʔjej tʃijae jitʃize
ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo wasase kʔjeze muradalda laʁ josun jatani ɡʔjeldeχun ʒindirɡo jasaldeχun ɡʼadab berbalaɡʔi bukʼine kːola ɡʔjesul
ɡʔjes tʼadeɡi ɬadi jatʃani maχʼrum ɡʔajuɡe tsee jatʃaraj ɬadi kwanidasaɡi ratʼlidasaɡi wa ros ɬadul bukʼuneb tsadaqχab ɡʼumrujaldasaɡi
ɡʔjeb ɬababɡo ʒo ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬije kʔoleb ɡʔjetʃʼoni ɡʔjeɬul iχtijar buɡo muχʔɡi kʔjetʃʼoɡo erkenɬize
tso kʔaburab ʒojaɬ tʃi χwezawuraw insan tʃʼwaze kːola
naɡaɡʔ ɡʔjeb toχɬukʔjeɡo kːarab iʃ buɡoni allaɡʔas ɡʔjedin kːeze qχwan bukʼun tʃʼwaze χijalɡi bukʼun batitʃʼoni witʃːante tʃʼwadaruqχan ɬutize ditsa biχʔizaburab bakʼalde
amma rekʼjeɬ tsːinɡi χʔiχʔun tsebekːunɡo urʁun tso tʃijas tsoɡidaw tʃi tʃʼwani dir qʼurban bakʼalde ɬutaniɡitsin ɡʔjenisaɡi naqχe watʃun ɡʔjew tʃi ɡʼumrujaldasa maχʼrum ɡʔawe
insuda jaɡi ebelalda kʔaburaw tʃi ʃːiw ɡʔjew wataniɡi tʃʼwaze kːola
laʁɬun witʃize jaɡi ʒindijeɡo χʼaltʼizawize pulanaw tʃi wiqʼaraw insan tʃʼwaze kːola
ebel emen qʼabiχʼ ɡʔarun kʼaɬalew tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola
naɡaɡʔ biχʔinal tsotsaɬ raʁulaɡo tsojas tsoɡidasda ɡamatʃʼ jaɡi zar kʔabani wa ɡʔjew χwetʃʼoni amma busade kːani
ɡʔjesda kʔaburaw tʃijase tamiχʼ ɡʔabize beɡʔularo wuχaraw tʼade waqχani wa ɡʼansideɡi kːun roqʼosa qʼwatʼiwe waqχine kʼoleb buɡoni amma kʔaburaw tʃijasuqχa ɡʼakʼa baqχize kːola wuχaraw busade kːejaldaɬun arab zamanaɬuqχɡi saχɬijaɬul muradalda ɡʔaburab daru sababaɬuqχɡi
χwaʒainas laʁasda jaɡi laʁalda tʼil kʔabuni wa ɡʔjebsaɡʼatɡo laʁ χwani χwaʒain tamiχʼalde tsʼaze kːola
amma laʁ tso kʼiɡo qʼojaɬ tʃʼaɡo χutʼani χwaʒainase tamiχʼ ɡʔabilaro ʃːajɡureɬul laʁ kːola ɡʔjesul mulk
biχʔinal tsotsaɬ raʁulaɡo ɬatʃʼoɡo qʼinaj ɡʼadanalda kʔabuni wa ɡʔjeldaɬun ɬimer biχːani amma ɡʔjeb ɡureb zaralɡi kːetʃʼoni tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanalda kʔaburasuqχa baqχize kːola ɡʔjeɬul rosas tʼalab ɡʔaburab wa diwantʃijas χʼukmu qʼotʼarab ɡʼakʼa
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬe zaral kːun buɡoni ɡʔjelda reqʼarab tamiχʼɡi ɡʔabe ɡʼumrujaɬuqχ ɡʼumru
beraɬuqχ ber ɡʼusaɬuqχ ɡʼus boχaɬuqχ boχ baqχe
buχʼarab bakʼaɬuqχ buχʼarab bakʼ ruʁunaɬuqχ ruʁun bi retʃinabijaɬuqχ bi retʃinabi
naɡaɡʔ χwaʒainas laʁasul jaɡi laʁaɬul badib zar kʔabuni wa ɡʔjezul ber baqχani ritʃːante beraldasa maχʼrumɬijaɬuqχ ɡʔjel laʁzal erken ɡʔarize
naɡaɡʔ χwaʒainas laʁasul jaɡi laʁaɬul ɡʼus bortizabuni ɡʔjelɡi ritʃːante erkenɬijalde ʒider raqχaral ɡʼusazuqχ
naɡaɡʔ biχʔintʃi jaɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan otsotsa merχʔun χwani ɡʔjeb ots ɡantʃʼalɡi retʃʼtʃʼun tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔanɡi kwine beɡʔularo otsol χwaʒainas ɡʔjeɬul ʒawab kʔjeze kːolaro
amma ots baʁuleb tajpajaɬul bukʼun batani wa χwaʒainasda ɡʔjeɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ abunɡi bukʼun buɡoni amma ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬul kʼwar ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo tani wa ɡʔjeɬ biχʔintʃi jaɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan tʃʼwani ɡantʃʼitsa buχun ɡʔjeb otsɡi tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjeɬul χwaʒainɡi tʃʼwaze kːola
amma ɡʔjew tʃʼwajaɬul bakʼalda ɡʔjesuqχa retsʼjel tʼalab ɡʔabize bokʔani bitsarab baɡʔa kinab bataniɡi kʔjeze kːola ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo ɡʼumrujaɬuqχ
ɡʔjebɡo qʼanun χʼaltʼizabula ots ɬimada baʁaniɡi jas jikʼa was wukʼa
otsotsa laʁ biχʔintʃi jaɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan tʃʼwani ɡʔjeɬul χwaʒainas dozul χwaʒainase kʔjeze kːola ɬeberɡo ʃekel
naɡaɡʔ tsoniɡi tʃijas ɡwendɡi buqχun ɡʔjelda tʼade rakʔ qχwatʃʼoɡo tun ɡʔjenibe ʒanibe ots jaɡi χʼama bortani
ɡwend buqχaras betsʼize kːola kːarab zaral ɡʔjes χwaʒainase ɡʼarats kʔjeze kːola amma χwarab χʼajwan ɡʔjesije χutʼula
ɬilniɡi ots tʃijar otsoɬ baʁani wa ɡʔjeb χwani tʃʼaɡo χutʼarab ots bitʃila wa ɡʔjeb bitʃun ʃːwarab ɡʼaratsɡi χwarab otsɡi ɡʔjezul beleɡʔabazda ɡʔorkʔob baʃːad bikʔila
amma ots baʁuleb tajpajaɬul bukʼun batani wa ɡʔjebɡi ɬalaɡo χwaʒainas ɡʔjeb bitʃːan tun bukʼun batani tʃʼwarab otsaɬuqχ ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo tʃʼaɡojab ots kʔjeze kːola wa tʃʼwarab ʒindijeɡo tela

naɡaɡʔ tsoniɡi tʃijas ots jaɡi ɡʼijaɬaʒo biqʼani wa ɡʔjeb qχuni jaɡi bitʃani ɡʔjes kʔjeze kːola tso biqʼarab otsaɬuqχ ʃːuɡo ots tso ɡʼijaɬaʒojaɬuqχ unqʼɡo ɡʼijaɬaʒo
tsʼoɡʔodize sardiɬ tso pulanab roqʼowe kʼantsʼulew wukʼaɡo kːuraw tsʼoɡʔor wuχun naɡaɡʔ χwani ɡʔjew wuχaraw tʃi ɡʼajibijawɬun rikʼkʼunaro
amma qʼad ɡʔjedinab ʒo kːani tsʼoɡʔor tʃʼwaraw tʃi ɡʼajibijawɬun rikʼkʼuna tsʼoɡʔor tʃʼaɡo χutʼani ɡʔjes biqʼarab betsʼize kːola ɡʔjesul ʃːibniɡi ɡʔjetʃʼoni ɡʔjew laʁɬijalde witʃe biqʼarab betsʼizeɬun
ɡʔjes biqʼarab botsʼi tʃʼaɡo batani ots χʼama jaɡi ɡʼijaɬaʒo batʼaɬi ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo ɡʔjesuqχa kʼitsʼulɡo tsʼikʼkʼun retsʼjel baqχize kːola
ɬitsaniɡi tʃijar χuribe jaɡi tsʼolbol aχikʔje ʒindirɡo botsʼi bitʃːani wa ɡʔjeb merχʔani kːarab zaralaɬuqχ retsʼjel χʼisabalda ɡʔjesuqχa baqχize kːola ʒindirɡo χurisa jaɡi tsʼolbol aχikʔa ʃːwarab batʃʼinaɬul biʃːun ɬikʼab butʼa
naɡaɡʔ tsʼaɡi rekʼun ʁutʼbi χaril ɡʼarqχal jaɡi χurisa ʒeɡi bakʼaritʃʼjeb tʼorʃːel buχʼani ɡʔjeb tsʼa rekʼine bitʃːan taraw tʃijas betsʼize kːola ɡʔjeldaɬun kːarab zaral
tso tʃijas tsoɡidasuqχe tsʼunize kʔurab ɡʼartsul tʼaɡʼjel jaɡi tsoɡidab qʼimatab qʼaji tsʼunize tʼade bosarasul roqʼosa tsʼoɡʔoras biqʼani wa ɡʔjew kːweze ʃːwani tsʼoɡʔorasuqχa baqχize kːola biqʼaraɬul kʼiɡo butʼa
amma tsʼoɡʔor kːweze ʃːwetʃʼoni tʃijar qʼaji tsʼunize tʼade bosaraw tʃi eχetize kːola diwantʃijasda tsewe wa ɡʔjedize kːola ʒintsa tʃijar χazinajalda kwer qχwatʃʼin abun
mulkaɬul iχtijaralda tʼasan kʼiɡojaw daɡʼbadulew wuɡoni ɡʔab dir kːolin abun ots χʼama tʃaqχu retʼjel jaɡi tsoɡidab bilarab qʼaji ɡʔjeb iʃ kʔjeze kːola diwantʃijasuqχe diwantʃijas meqʼawɬun rikʼkʼaraw tʃijas ritʼuqχ ɡʔawurase kʔjeze kːola kʼiɡo butʼa
tso tʃijas tsoɡidasuqχe χʔiχʔize kʔurab χʼama ots tʃaqχu jaɡi bokʔarab ruqʼaɬul χʼajwan ɬidaniɡi biχʔitʃʼoɡo χwani jaɡi ɬuqʼani jaɬuni biqʼani
botsʼi χʔiχʔize tʼade bosaraw tʃi ɡʔjedize kːola betʼjerhanasul tsʼaraldaɬun botsʼul χwaʒainasda tsewe ʒintsa tʃijar botsʼuda kwer qχwatʃʼin abun botsʼul χwaʒainas qʼabul ɡʔabize kːola ɡʔjesul ɡʔa ɡʔjebmeχaɬ retsʼjelɡi kʔjeze kːolaro
amma reqχada wukʼarasul ɡʼajibaldaɬun botsʼi biqʼun ani botsʼul χwaʒainase kːarab zaral betsʼize kːola ɡʔjes
naɡaɡʔ botsʼi ɡʼalχul χʼajwanaz tʃʼwan batani reqχada wukʼaras ɡʔjeɬul balkan biχʔizabize kːola ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʼalχul χʼajwanaz tʃʼwarab botsʼi betsʼize kːolaro
tsojas tsoɡidasuqχa zamanalda χʼaltʼizabizejan abun χʼajwan batʃani wa χwaʒain askʼow ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo ɡʔjeb χwani jaɡi ɬuqʼani ɡʔjeb betsʼize kːola
ɡʔjeb zamanalda χʼajwanaɬul χwaʒain askʼow wuɡoni batʃaraw tʃijas ɡʔjeb betsʼize kːolaro amma ɡʔjeb χʼajwan muχʔdaqχ batʃun bukʼun batani kːoleb muχʔ kʔjeze kːola
biχʔintʃijas ʒeɡi rosase intʃʼjej jas basra ɡʔajuni ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬuqχ baχʼaraɬul qχalim kʔjeze kːola wa ɡʔjej ɬadiɬun jatʃine kːola
naɡaɡʔ ɡʔjeɬul insutsa ɡʔjew tʃijase ɡʔjej ɬadiɬun kʔjeze inkar ɡʔabuni ɡʔjebmeχaldaɡi ɡʔjes kʔjeze kːola jasaɬuqχ kʔoleb baχʼaraɬul χʼaqʼ
siχʼrutʃʼuʒu paliqχan tʃʼaɡo toɡe
χʼajwanalɡun pasatal ɡʔorkʔorɬabi ɡʔarulew tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola
betʼjerhanase ɡureb batʼijal allaɡʔzabaze qʼurban ɡʔabulewʃːinaw tʃiɡi tʼaɡʼinawize kːola
tʃijar rakʔaldasa ratʃʼaral qʼwarid ɡʔaruɡe ɡʔjezije zulmu ɡʔabuɡe misrijalda nuʒɡoɡi rukʼindal tʃijar rakʔaldasa ratʃʼaralɬun
qʼorolalɡi besdalalɡi qʼwarid ɡʔaruɡe
nuʒetsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuni ɡʔjez kumek ɡʔarun aχʼi bala dide wa ditsa tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo qʼabul ɡʔabila ɡʔjezul ɡʔari
tsinɡi dir tsːin ɡʔalaɡɬila wa ditsa nuʒ χwaltʃatsa tʃʼwala ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nuʒer ɬudbiɡi qʼorolɬila nuʒer ɬimalɡi besdalɬila
dir χalqʼaɬul miskintʃijase dutsa qʼarzaɬe ɡʼarats kʔuni ɡʔjesuqχa tʼadeɡi ɡʼarats baqχuɡe
tsoɡidasuqχa ʁorkʔɬalije dutsa ɡʼaba bosani baqʼanil ɡʼuʒalde ɡʔjeb tʼadbusːinabitʃʼoɡo toɡe
ɡʔjeb ɡuroni tʼokʼab tʼad baze ʒo ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul ɡʔjesul kin ɡʔjew qʼasi kʔiʒilew tʼad baze ʒoɡi ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo dos dida ɡʔaridal dida raɡʼula ʃːajɡureɬul dun raχʼmujaw wuɡeɬul
allaɡʔasde χʔandoɡe wa nuʒerɡo χalqʼaɬul butʼrulɡi tsereqχabiɡi kakuɡe
bakʼararab tʼorʃːelaldasaɡi tsʼolbol tsʼtsʼujaldasaɡi χirijal sadaqʼabi kʔjeze kwatʼuɡe
tʼotsere ɡʔarural wasal dije kʔje
ɡʔjedinɡo nuʒetsa dije kʔjeze kːola nuʒer ɡʼi botsʼutsa ɡʔaburab tʼotsebeseb tʼintʃʼ ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeb ebelalda askʼob te wa mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ dije kʔje
nuʒ rukʼine kːola dir batsʼtsʼadab χalqʼɬun ɡʼalχul ʒanawaraɬ tʃʼwarab χʼajwanaɬul ɡʔan kwanaɡe ɡʔjeb ɡʔabzaze reχe

ɡʔjeresiχarbal tʼiritʼizaruɡe ɡʔjeresijab nuɡʼɬijaldaɬun ɡʼajibijase kumek ɡʔabuɡe
ɡʼjemerisez kweʃɬi ɡʔabuleb buɡoni ɡʔjezda naqχ riɬːunɡe ɡʼjemerisezda tʼadɡi reqʼon tʼjeqʼab diwanaɬe kwerbaqʼiɡi ɡʔabuɡe wa
miskinaw wuɡin abun tʃijasul taqʼsir baχtʃizeɡi kwerbaqʼuɡe
naɡaɡʔ dur tuʃmanasul ots jaɡi χʼama nuχ qʼosun kːun batani tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo ɡʔjesuqχe tʼadbusːinabe ɡʔjeb
naɡaɡʔ mun riχaraw tʃijasul χʼama tʼad buɡeb ɡʔirɡi bakʼɬun ɡʼodob kːani ɡʔjedin toɡe ɡʔjeb tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo kumek ɡʔabe ɡʔjeɬije
miskintʃijasul ɡʼarzaɬe ritʼuqχab diwan qʼotʼje
buɡʔtanazda tʼad reqʼoɡe wa ɡʼajib ɡʔjetʃʼjew rakʼbatsʼtsʼadaw tʃi χwalikʔje kːezawuɡe ɡʔjedinaw tʃijase ʒaza ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo tolaro ditsa
riʃwatal rosuɡe ɡʔjez kanɬi biχʔulelɡi betsɬizarula wa rakʼbatsʼtsʼadazul nuɡʼɬiɡi ɡʼaksalda swerizabula
qʼwatʼisa ɡotʃun ratʃʼaraze kweʃɬi ɡʔabuɡe nuʒeda ɬala ɡʔjezul χʼal ʃːajɡureɬul misrijalda nuʒɡi ɡʔjedinalɬun rukʼindal
anɬɡo sonaɬ χurzal rekʔje wa batʃʼin bakʼare
ankʔabileb sonaɬ χur χʼuχʔbaqχize te ɡʔjenib ʒibɡo biʒarabʃːinab miskinzabaz kwanaze bitʃːaj ɡʔjezuqχaɡi χutʼarab ɡʼalχul χʼajwanaz kwanaze te ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔabe tsʼolbol wa zajtunaɬul aχazeɡi
anɬɡo qʼojaɬ nuʒerɡo χʼaltʼabi ɡʔare ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ raχʼatalda rukʼa nuʒer otsaɬeɡi χʼamijeɡi χʼalχʔi ʃːweze bukʼine wa nuʒer roqʼow wiʒaraw laʁasdaɡi ɡotʃun watʃʼarasdaɡi ruχʼ ɬeze bukʼine
ditsa nuʒee amru ɡʔabunʃːinalde kʼwar kʔje tsoɡidal allaɡʔzabaze χʼjeluɡe ɡʔjezul tsʼaraltsin nuʒer kʼalaɬ takrar ɡʔaruɡe
ɬaɡʼalida ʒanib ɬabtsʼul dije bajram tʼobitʼje
buɡʔurɡo tʃadazul bajram tʼobitʼje ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ dir amrujalda reqʼon retʃːeb ɡʔjetʃʼjeb tʃed kwanaj awiw motsʼaɬul ɡʔjeɬije riχʔizarural qʼojazda
dije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize ratʃʼuneɬul tʃʼoroɡo ratʃʼunɡe
ɬiɬarijaɬul bajram tʼobitʼje ɬiɬari bajbiχʔuleb zamanalda
ɬaɡʼalil aχiralda χʼaluqχen bakʼarijaɬul bajramɡi tʼobitʼje
palχʼasil ɬaɡʼalida ʒanib ɬabɡo nuχalda tʼolalɡo biχʔinal rakʼarize kːola χʼalkʼolew betʼjerhanase ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize
dije qχoleb qʼurbanaɬul biɡun ʒubaze beɡʔularo ʃːibniɡi retʃːeb ʁorɬ buɡeb ʒo
bajramqʼojazul qʼurbanaɬul tʼatʼi roɡʔineɡʼan tsʼunize beɡʔularo
ɬiɬarijaɬul awalalda bakʼararab χʼaluqχenaɬul biʃːunɡo ɬikʼab butʼa ʃːwezabe betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul muqʼadasab roqʼobe
burutʼ ɡʔjeɬul ebelaɬul raχʔdaɬ beɬunɡe
ditsa malaik witʼulew wuɡo nuʒeda tsewe tsewe nuχda nuʒ tsʼunijaɬul wa ditsa nuʒee χʼadurarab rakʔalde nuʒ ratʃinaɬul muradalda
ɡʔjesda tsere bertsinɡo rukʼa wa ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼjenekːe ɡʔjesda dande tʃʼoɡe nuʒer munaɡʔazdasa tʼasaɬuɡʔine ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjew ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjesuɬ buɡo dir tsʼar
nuʒ ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼjenekːani ditsa maɬarabʃːinabɡi ɡʔabuni nuʒer tuʃbabaze tuʃmanɬun wukʼina dun wa nuʒeda dande tʃʼarazda dandeɡi tʃʼjela
nuʒeda tsewe tsewe ina dir malaik wa ɡʔjes ʃːwezarila nuʒ amorijazulɡi χitijazulɡi perizijazulɡi χanaanijazulɡi χiwijazulɡi wa jewusijazulɡi rakʔazde wa ditsa ɡʔjel χalqʼalɡi dunjalaldasa tʼaɡʼinarila
ɡʔjezul allaɡʔzabaze tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabuɡe wa ɡʔjel χalqʼazul ɡʼadatalɡi takrar ɡʔaruɡe ʃːuʃːaqχ riχːizare ɡʔjezul allaɡʔzabi wa ʁure ɡʔjezul muqʼadasal ɡantʃʼal
nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔase ɡʔabe tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat wa ɡʔjes ɡʔarzaɡo kʔjela nuʒee kwenɡi ɬimɡi unta ʃoqʼɬabazdasaɡi tsʼunila
wa nuʒer rakʔalda bukʼinaro ja ɬimer biχːi ja ɬimal ɡʔarunɡutʼi nuʒer ɡʼumrujaɬul qʼojazul qʼadarɡi tsʼikʼkʼinabila ditsa
ditsa kʼudijab χʼinqʼi reʃːtʼinabila nuχda nuʒeda dandtʃʼwaralʃːinal χalqʼazde wa tʼolalɡo nuʒer tuʃbabi tʼurizarila nuʒeda tseresa
nuʒeda tsere tsere ditsa kʼudijab tajpajaɬul kʔuʒnajal ritʼila χiwijalɡi χanaanijalɡi χitijalɡi nuʒeda tseresa naqχe ʁeze
amma ditsa tsojidasanɡo jaɬuni tso ɬaɡʼalida ʒanir naqχe ʁelaro ɡʔjel ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuni rakʔ tʃʼoboɡoɬuleɬul wa ɡʼalχul ʒanawaralɡi tsʼaqʼɡo ɡʼjemerɬuleɬul
daɡʔ daɡʔkːun naqχe aχʼila ditsa ɡʔjel nuʒeda tseresa ɡʔjeb rakʔalda nuʒer qʼadar tsʼikʼkʼineɡʼan wa tʼolabɡo rakʔalda tʼad kwerʃːel ɡʔabize nuʒee res reqʼezeɡʼan
ditsa nuʒee kʔjela baɡʼarab raɬdaqχa baqχarab jefrat ɡʼuruqχe ʃːwezeɡʼan tʼolabɡo rakʔ baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχalda nuʒer ɡʼorqχiɬun bukʼina pilistimijab raɬad wa baqʼbakːul raqχalda kʼudijab salul awlaqχ ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬul tʼolalɡo χalqʼal nuʒer iχtijaralde kʔjela ditsa wa nuʒetsa ɡʔjenisa naqχe ratʃaqχila ɡʔjel
ɡʔjezulɡun wa ɡʔjezul allaɡʔzabazulɡun kinabɡʼaɡi qʼotʼi qʼaj ɡʔabuɡe nuʒetsa
nuʒer rakʔalda ɡʔjel χalqʼal teze beɡʔularo ɡuroni ɡʔjez nuʒ dida dande munaɡʔal ɡʔarijalde kːezarize ruɡo ɡʔjezul allaɡʔzabaze suʒda ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔani nuʒ ɡʔjezul qʼorikʔje kːeze ruɡo

χadub betʼjerhanas musada abuna
betʼjerhanasda tsewe maɡʼarde watʃʼa tsadaqχ ɡʔarunɡun nadawɡun awiɡʔuɡun wa ɡʼizrailazul ɬabqʼojalda antsʼawɡo kʼudijawɡun nuʒetsa rikʼkʼadasan suʒda ɡʔabe dije
amma betʼjerhanasde ɡʼaɡarɬize wuɡo ɡʼitsʼɡo musa χutʼaral rikʼkʼadeɡʼan tʃʼa χalqʼin abuni maɡʼarde tʼade baχinejantsin ɬuɡʔunɡe
musa χalqʼaɬuqχe wiɬːana wa betʼjerhanasul raɡʼabiɡi ɡʔjesul qʼanunalɡi ɡʔjezije zaɡʔir ɡʔaruna ɡʔjelda dande χalqʼaɬ tsokʼalɡo ʒawab kʔuna
niʒetsa kinabɡo ɡʔabila betʼjerhanas maɬuqχe jan
betʼjerhanas maɬarab kinabɡo ʒojaɬul musatsa qχwaj qχwaɡʼaj ɡʔabuna χaduseb qʼojaɬ tsudunɡo tʼadeɡi waqχun meɡʼjeraɬul aχaɬijalda qʼurban bakʼ bana musatsa wa antsʼila kʼiɡo ɡantʃʼil χʼubi eχetizabuna ɡʔjenib ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬul ʃːibab qʼawm rikʼkʼun
ɡʔjes ɡʼizrailazul ɡʼoloqχabazul antsʼila kʼiɡo tʃijasda tʼad qʼana betʼjerhanase tʼuran ruχʼulel qʼurbanal tʼoritʼijaɬe wa raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe antsʼila kʼiɡo basi qχwejan
musatsa qʼurbanaɬe qχural otsazul baʃːdab bi ʃːurminibe tʼuna wa χutʼarab baʃːdab qʼurban bakʼalda tʼade ʃːwana
χadub ɡʔjes qʼotʼijaɬul tʼjeχʔ bosana wa ɡʔjeb χalqʼaɬe tsʼalana ɡʔjebmeχaɬ χalqʼaɬ abuna
niʒ betʼjerhanasul raɡʼuje mutʼiɡʼɬila wa kinabɡo ɡʔjes maɬuqχe ɡʔabila jan
musatsa qʼurbanaɬul χutʼarab bi χalqʼalde punqχana wa ɡʔjes abuna
ɡʔab buɡo betʼjerhanas nuʒerɡun ɡʔaburab wa ɡʔjesul qʼanunazdaɬun nuʒee zaɡʔir ɡʔaburab qʼotʼijaɬul bi jan
tsinɡi musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi nadawɡi awiɡʔuɡi ɡʼizrailaɬul χalqʼaɬul ɬabqʼojalda antsʼawɡo kʼudijawɡi riɬːana maɡʼarde
ɡʔjenib ɡʔjezda ɡʼizrailaɬul allaɡʔasul sipat biχʔana ɡʔjesul χʼatʼikʔ bukʼana sapfiraɬul ɡʔaburab ɡʼadab ratsʼtsʼadal qχaχʼilal zobalazda reɬːarab ʒo
amma allaɡʔasul sipat ɡʔjezda biχʔaniɡi ɡʼizrailazul kʼudijal tʃʼaɡo tana ɡʔjes wa ɡʔjel kinalɡo ɡʔjenir tsadaqχ kwana ɡʔjeqʼana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
dida askʼowe maɡʼarda tʼade watʃʼa ditsa kʔjela duqχe ditsaɡo ɡantʃʼil qʼanazda qχwaral dir amrabiɡi qʼanunalɡi jan
ʒindirɡo kumektʃi jeɡʔoʃuaɡun tsadaqχ musa allaɡʔasul maɡʼarde waχana
χalqʼaɬul kʼudijazda ɡʔjes abuna
nuʒ ɡʔanir tʃʼa niʒ nuʒeqχe tʼadrusːineɡʼan ɡʔarunɡi χʼurɡi tolel ruɡo nuʒeda tʼad kʼudijalɬun ʃːibɡʼaɡi qʼwariɡʼjel kːani ɡʔjezulɡun ɡʼaqʼlu dandbaj in
musa maɡʼarde wiɬːana meɡʼjer nakʼkʼutsa batsun bukʼana
wa betʼjerhanasul qʼudrat reʃːtʼana sinaj maɡʼarda anɬɡo qʼojaɬ nakʼkʼaz batsun bukʼana sinaj meɡʼjer ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjes nakʼkʼuɬan musade aχʼana
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda tʼadeɡʼanasul qʼudrat biχʔuleb bukʼana maɡʼarda bakarab wa tʼolɡo meɡʼjer tsʼurab kutakab tsʼadudaɬun
musa maɡʼarde waχana wa nakʼkʼuɬe ʒaniwe ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjes ɡʔjenib kʼiqʼoɡo sordo qʼo bana

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe dir muqʼadasab bakʼalde χirijal sadaqʼabi kʔjejan ʃːiwaw tʃijas ʒindijeɡo bokʔarab kʔjeze bitʃːante rekʼjel aχʼijalda reqʼon ɡʔjedin χirijal sadaqʼabi rakʼare
ɡʔjezuqχa bakʼare mesed ɡʼarats wa mazɡar
kantʃʼqχaχʼilab betsʼbaɡʼarab wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarab kwasul kun tʼjerenab χʼjebet wa tsʼtsʼjel kwas
baɡʼarkʔjeraɬ reɬaral ɡʼijal qʼuχʔdul tʼjerenal tsʼakal wa akatsijaɬul tsʼul
naχutʃiraqχaze tʼjeze zajtunaɬul naχ baχuneb χirijab naχ ɡʔabijaɬe wa χirijab bakʼalda ɡʔuinmaχʼal raqχinarijaɬe maχʼɡʔuinal pitsʼalɡun χurdul
efodalda wa kaʃiʃasul ratʼlil karanzul tsebebuχʔalda ɬeze oniks wa tsoɡidal ʒawɡʔaral
bitʃːante ɡʼizrailaz dije muqʼadasab ruqʼ baze dun ɡʔjeniw zaɡʔirɬize wukʼine
ɡʔjeb ruqʼɡi ɡʔjenib ʒanib ɬoleb kinabɡo qʼajiɡi ɡʔabe durusɡo ditsa duda biχʔizabuqχe
ɡʔjezda abe akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ʁamas ɡʔabejan kʼiɡoɡun baʃːdab natʼ χalaɬi buɡeb wa natʼɡun baʃːdab ɡʼjebɬiɡi borχaɬiɡi buɡeb
ʒanisanɡi tʼasanɡi ɡʔjelda mesed bekʔje wa ɡʔjelda swerun mesedil tʃʼoloɡi kːwe
biun mesedɡi tʼun unqʼɡo ɡor ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjel ʃːula ɡʔare ʁorkʔijal bokʼnazda kʼijabɡo raqχaɬan kʼi kʼi
tsinɡi akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ɡʼurdul ɡʔare wa ɡʔjezda tʼadɡi mesed bekʔje
ɡʔjel ɡʼurdul kːezare ʁamasaɬul kʼijabɡo raqχalda ruɡel ɡorazuɬe ʁamas batʃːize bukʼine ɡʔjel ɡʼurdulɡi kːun
ɡʼurdul kidaɡo ɡorazda ʒanir rukʼine kːola ɡʔjel ɡʔjenisa naqχe rosize beɡʔularo
ɡʔjeb ʁansinir ɬe ditsa duqχe kʔjeze ruɡel muqʼadasab qʼotʼijaɬul qʼanal
batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul tʼaɬelɡi ɡʔabe kʼiɡo natʼɡun baʃːdab χalaɬiɡi natʼɡun baʃːdab ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡeb
tʼaɬelaɬul kʼijabɡo raqχalda ratʃitʼaɡi buχun mesedaɬul kʼiɡo χeruwim ɡʔabe
tso χeruwim tso raɡʼalda tsoɡi χeruwim tsoɡidab raɡʼalda ɡʔabe ɡʔjel χeruwimal tʼaɬelɡun rekʼaral ɡʔare tso mesedil kesekaɬul
ritʃːante χeruwimazul kurkʔbi tʼaɬelalda tʼad tʼiritʼun rukʼine ɡʔjezul ɡʔurmalɡi tsotsazdeχunɡi rusːun tʼaɬelalde qʼulun rukʼine
ɡʔjeb tʼaɬel ʁamasalda tʼad ɬe ɡʔjenir ʒanir ɬe ditsa duqχe kʔolel ruɡel qʼotʼijaɬul qχwaj qχwaɡʼaj ɡʔabural qʼanal
ɡʔjeniw qʼotʼijaɬul ʁansil tʼaɬelalda tʼad ruɡel χeruwimazda ɡʔorkʔosan dun kʼaɬaze wuɡo munɡun wa munɡi ɡʔorkʔow kːun dir amrabiɡi kʔjeze ruɡo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬe
stol ɡʔabe akatsijaɬul tsʼulal kʼiɡo natʼaɬ χalatab tso natʼaɬ ɡʼjebab wa natʼɡun baʃːdaɬ borχatab
ɡʔjelda tʼadɡi kisanɡo mesed bekʔje wa sweruqχɡi ɡʔabe mesedil tʃalu
stolaɬul raɡʼalkːun kisanɡo ɡʔabe tso qχat borχaɬijalda buɡeb tʼjerenab qʼed wa ɡʔjelda tʼasan mesedil tʃalu batʃe
stolaɬe unqʼɡo mesedil ɡor ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjel rekʼinare stolaɬul bokʼnazda boχduzda tʼad
ɡoral rukʼine kːola raɡʼaldeɡʼan stol batʃːulel ɡʼurdul ʒanire kːezarize sanaɡʼatalda
ɡʼurdul ɡʔare akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ɡʔjezda tʼadɡi mesed bekʔje wa ɡʔjelɡi kːun batʃːe stol
ɡʔare batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul surkʼabiɡi ɡelalɡi ɡulɡunalɡi ʃːurmalɡi qʼurbanal tʼoritʼuleɬul χʼaltʼizarize rukʼine
ɡʔjeb stolalda tʼad kidaɡo muqʼadasab tʃed bukʼine kːola dida tsebe
batsʼtsʼadab mesedɡi ratʃitʼa buχun naχutʃiraqχ ɡʔabe ɡʔjeb batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul wa tsorekʼarab bukʼine kːola ɡʔjeɬul boχɡi ɡʼarkʔjelalɡi ɡʔjedinɡo surkʼabiɡun tʼantʃalɡi
naχutʃiraqχalda bukʼine kːola anɬɡo ɡʼarkʔjel ɬabɡo tsojab raqχalda ɬabɡo tsoɡidab raqχalda
bitʃːante ʃːibab ɡʼarkʔjelalda bukʼine ɬab ɬab surkʼa mindalaɬul tʼoɡʔol sipatalda tʼantʃalɡun ɡʔjedin bukʼine kːola naχutʃiraqχaɬul tso boχaldasa kʼijabɡo raqχalde bikʔarab anɬabɡo ɡʼarkʔjelalda
ʒibɡo naχutʃiraqχalda ɡʔjeɬul boχalda tʼadeχun bukʼine te tʼantʃalɡi ruɡeb mindalaɬul tʼoɡʔol sipatalda ɡʔaburab ʒeɡi unqʼɡo surkʼa
tso tʼoɡʔoqʼwatʃʼa bukʼine te naχutʃiraqχaɬul boχaldasan rakːaral ɡʼarkʔalabazul tʼotsebeseb ʒutalda ʁorkʔ kʼiabileb kʼiabileb ʒutalda ʁorkʔ ɬababileb ɬababileb ʒutalda ʁorkʔ wa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabe anɬabɡo ɡʼarkʔjelalda ʁorkʔ
bitʃːante batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul ɡʔarural tʼuɡʔdulɡi ɡʼarkʔalabiɡi tʃiraqχɡi tsorekʼaral rukʼine
ʒeɡi ɡʔabe naχɡi ʒanibe tʼun bakuleb ankʔɡo ɡʔitʼinab tʃiraqχ wa ɡʔjel reqʼezare naχutʃiraqχalda tʼad ʒinda tsebe buɡeb tʼolɡo sweruqχɬi ɡʔjez tsadaqχɡo ɡwanʁizabuleb kutsaɬ
ɡʔjedinɡo biltajaɬul ʁutsʼdulɡi ɡelalɡi rukʼine kːola batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul ɡʔarural
naχutʃiraqχɡi kinabɡo ɡʔjeɬul tsʼaraɡʼɡi ɡʔabijaɬe χʼaltʼizabe batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul tso talant
woreɡi maɡʼarda duda biχʔizaburab sipatalda reqʼon ɡʔabe kinabɡo

muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬe antsʼɡo pardaw ɡʔabe ɡʔjel pardawal resːe tʼjerenab χʼjebetɡi bosun kantʃʼqχaχʼilab betsʼbaɡʼarab wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarab kwasul kunɡi χʼaltʼizabun wa tʼad bertsinɡo χeruwimazul sipatalɡi uɡʔun
ritʃːante kinalɡo pardawal tsotsazda raʃːadal rukʼine qʼolo mikʔɡo natʼ χalaɬiɡi unqʼɡo natʼ ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡel
tsinɡi ʃːuɡo pardaw tsotsada buqʼun tso ɡʔabe wa χutʼarab ʃːuɡo pardawaɬeɡi ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔabe
ʃːuɡotsadaqχab pardawaɬul raɡʼalkːun eχede ɡʔare kantʃʼqχaχʼilab χːamil ʁantsʼakʼitʃʼal ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔabe kʼiabileb ʃːuɡotsadaqχab pardawaɬul raɡʼalkːun eχedeɡi
tʼotsebeseb pardawaɬul raɡʼalda ɡʔabe kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʁantsʼakʼitʃʼ wa kʼiabileb ʃːuɡotsadaqχab pardawaldaɡi ɡʔabe ɡʔjezda dande reqʼon kːoleduqχ kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʁantsʼakʼitʃʼ
χadub kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo mesedil ʁantsʼa ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjezdaɬun kʼijabɡo pardaw tsotsada rekʼinabe tʃadir tsokʼalab bukʼine
tʃadiralda tʼasan tʼamize tsʼtsʼjel kwasul antsʼila tso pardawɡi ɡʔabe
antsʼila tsojabɡo pardaw tsotsada baʃːadab bukʼine kːola ɬeberɡo natʼaɬul χalaɬiɡi unqʼɡo natʼaɬul ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡeb
ɡʔjezul ʃːuɡojab tsotsada buqʼe wa χutʼarab anɬɡojabɡi tsotsada buqʼe anɬabileb pardaw tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼujalda tsebesan kʼitʃʼwaj ɡʔjeb bukʼina kʼaltʼujalda tsebe biʁun
tsojab ʃːuɡotsadaqχab pardawaɬul raɡʼalkːun ɡʔabe kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʁantsʼakʼitʃʼ wa anɬɡotsadaqχab pardawaɬul raɡʼalkːunɡi ɡʔabe kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʁantsʼakʼitʃʼ
χadub ɡʔabe kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo mazɡarul ʁantsʼa wa ɡʔjezdaɬun ɡʔjeb kʼijabɡo pardawɡi tsoɬizabe tso pardaw kːezabize
pardawaɬul tʼokʼɬarab butʼa dalizabize kːola tʃadiralda naqχasan ɡʼodobe
pardawaɬul χalaɬijaɬul tʼokʼɬarab butʼaɡi kʼijabɡo χʔibilaldasa ɡʼodobe tso tso natʼ dalizabize kːola tʃadir batsuneb kutsaɬ
tʃadiralda tʼad baze baɡʼarkʔjeraɬ reɬaral ɡʼijal qʼuχʔduzul pardaw ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjezdaɡi tʼasan baze tʼjerenal tsʼakazul pardawɡi ɡʔabe
χadub tʃadiraɬe akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ramabi ɡʔare
ɡʔjel ramabi rukʼine kːola antsʼɡo natʼaɬul χalaɬiɡi natʼɡun baʃːdab ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡel
tsotsada dandbitʼarab bakʼalda kʼiɡo tsʼutʼjelɡi buɡel ɡʔjedinalɬun ɡʔare tʃadiraɬe kinalɡo ramabi
tʃadiraɬul qʼilbajaɬul raqχaɬe ɡʔabe qʼoɡo rama
wa ɡʔjezije ɡʼartsul kʼiqʼoɡo ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabe ʃːibab ramajaɬe kʼi kʼi ʁorkʔtʃʼjel ʃːibab tsʼutʼjelalda ʁorkʔ tso tso
tʃadiraɬul ʃimalijab raqχaldasanɡi ɡʔabe qʼoɡo rama
wa ɡʔjezije kʼiqʼoɡo ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi ʃːibab ramajalda ʁorkʔ kʼi kʼi
ʒeɡi anɬɡo rama ɡʔabe tʃadiraɬul naqχiseb raqχaɬe aj baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχaɬe
wa ʒeɡi kʼiɡo rama ɡʔjeɬul naqχeχunisel bokʼnazeɡi ɡʔabe
ɡʔjel bokʼnazul ramabi aχadasa kʼirikʔaral tʼoɡʔireχun tso ɡoraɬ dande ratʃaral rukʼine kːola ɡʔjedin ɡʔabe bokʼnazul kʼijabɡo rama
kinabniɡi ɡʔjenib bukʼina mikʔɡo rama wa antsʼila anɬɡo ɡʼartsul ʁorkʔtʃʼjel ʃːibab ramajalda ʁorkʔ kʼi kʼi ʁorkʔtʃʼjel
ʒeɡi ɡʔare akatsijaɬul tsʼulal raχal tʃadiraɬul tso raqχalda ruɡel ramabazda tʼad ʃːuɡo raχi
tsoɡidab raqχalda ruɡel ramabazdaɡi ʃːuɡo raχi wa naqχiseb raqχalda aj baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχalda ruɡel ramabazdaɡi ʃːuɡo raχi
tʃadiraɬul moqʼrukʔ bakʔuɬan tsojab raɡʼaldasa tsoɡidab raɡʼalde ʃːun ɬurab raχijaɬul kumekaldaɬun tsotsaɬ ruχʔina kinalɡo ramabi
ramabazda tʼad mesed bekʔje wa mesedaɬul ɡoral ɡʔare raχal kːweze raχazda tʼadɡi mesed bekʔje
muqʼadasab tʃadir ɡʔabe maɡʼarda duda biχʔizaburab sipatalda reqʼon
χasab pardaw besːe tʼjerenab χʼjebetɡi kantʃʼqχaχʼilab betsʼbaɡʼarab wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarab kwasul kunɡi bosun wa tʼad bertsinɡo χeruwimazul sipatalɡi uɡʔun
unqʼɡo χʼubi ɡʔabe akatsijaɬul tsʼulal wa ɡʔjezda tʼad mesed bekʔje ɡʔjel χʼubazda raj mesedaɬul ɡʔarural ʁuntsʼbi wa χʼubaze ɡʼartsul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal ɬe mesedil ʁuntsʼbuzda ɡʔjeb χasab pardawɡi baj
ɡʔjeb pardawalda naqχa ɬe qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas ɡʔjeb pardawaɬ batʼa tʼjezabize buɡo biʃːunɡo muqʼadasab bakʼ
biʃːunɡo muqʼadasab bakʼalda ɬurab qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamasalda tʼaɬel ɬe
pardawaldasa qʼwatʼibeχun raqχalda ɡʔjelda tsebe ɬe stol stolalda dandbitʼun ɬe naχutʃiraqχ stol ʃimalijab raqχaldeχun ɬeze kːola naχutʃiraqχin abuni qʼilbajaɬul raqχaldeχun
tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼujalda bazeɡi tʼjerenab χʼjebtil kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunazdaɬun besːarab tʃarab pardaw ɡʔabe
ɡʔjeb pardawaɬeɡi akatsijaɬul tsʼulal mesed tʼad bekʔarab wa mesedil ʁuntsʼbiɡi ruɡeb ʃːuɡo χʼubi ɡʔabe ɡʔjel χʼubaze mazɡarul biun tʼurab ʃːuɡo ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabe

qʼurban bakʼ ɡʔabe akatsijaɬul tsʼulal bitʃːante ɡʔjeb bukʼine unqʼbokʼonab ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ χalatab wa ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ ɡʼjebab
ɡʔjeɬul unqʼabɡo bokʼonalda ɬːurdul ɡʔare wa qʼurban bakʼ ɬːurdulɡun tsorekʼarab ɡʔabe ɡʔjeb kinaldaɡo tʼad mazɡar bitʃːaj
mazɡaraɬul ɡʔabe ɡʔjeɬije χʼaʒatab kinabɡo qʼajiɡi roqχo qʼwatʼibe batʃːulel qχubi kwarχabi bi tʼolel surkʼabi ɡʔan baze ɡʼutʃʼal wa buχʼarab tʼurtʃːi ɬolel tʼabkʼal
ʒeɡi qʼurban bakʼalda swerun kːweze mazɡarul χʔuri ɡʔabe wa χʔuridul unqʼabɡo bokʼonalda rekʼinabe mazɡarul tso tso ɡor
ɡʔjeb χʔuri kːwe qʼurban bakʼaɬul tʼasijab raqχalda ɡʔjeɬul borχaɬijaɬul baʃːaɬijalde ʃːoleduqχ
ɡʔjedinɡo qʼurban bakʼaɬe ɡʔare akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ɡʼurdul wa ɡʔjezda tʼadɡi mazɡar bitʃːaj
qʼurban bakʼ batʃːize sanaɡʼatalda ɡʔjeɬul kʼijabɡo raqχaldasan tso tso ɡʼjer ɡorazda ʒanibe kːezabe
qʼurban bakʼ ɡʔabe qχarʃːazul wa ʒanisa ɡʔodorabɬun ɡʔjeb ɡʔabize kːola maɡʼarda duda biχʔizaburab sipatalda reqʼon
tʃadiralda sweruqχ azbar ɡʔabe azbaraɬul qʼilbajaɬul raqχalda nusɡo natʼaɬ χalatab tʼjerenab χʼjebtil pardaw baze kːola
qʼoɡo χʼoboda χʼubaze qʼoɡo mazɡarul ʁorkʔtʃʼjel ɡʔabe ɡʔjezije ʁuntsʼbiɡi wa ɡʔjel tsotsada rekʼinarize ɡoralɡi ɡʼartsul ɡʔarize kːola
azbaraɬul ʃimalijab raqχaldaɡi ɡʔjedinɡo nusɡo natʼaɬ χalatab χʼjebtil pardaw baze kːola wa ɡʔjeɬijeɡi qʼoɡo χʼubi eχetize kːola ʃːibaɬe mazɡarul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabun wa ɡʼartsul ʁuntsʼbiɡi ɡʔjel tsotsada rekʼinarize ɡʼartsul ɡoralɡi tʼad ran
azbaraɬul baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχalda ɡʔjeɬul tʼolabɡo ɡʼjebɬijalda ʁorkʔtʃʼjelazda eχetarab antsʼɡo χʼoboda baze kːola kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo natʼaɬ χalatab pardaw
ɡʔjedinɡo azbaraɬul baqʼbakːul raqχɡi bukʼine kːola kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo natʼaɬ ɡʼjebab
ʒanire ɬuɡʔuneb kʼaltʼujaɬul tsojab raqχalda bitʃːante bukʼine antsʼila ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ χalatab ɬabɡo χʼoboda barab pardaw ʃːibab χʼubijaɬe ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabe
wa kʼaltʼujaɬul tsoɡidab raqχaldaɡi bukʼine bitʃːaj antsʼila ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ χalatab pardaw ɡʔjedinɡo ɬabɡo χʼoboda barab ʃːibaɬul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi buɡeb
azbaralde ɬuɡʔuneb kʼaltʼujaɬe ɡʔabize kːola qʼoɡo natʼaɬ χalatab tʃarab pardaw kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunɡi tʼjerenab χʼjebetɡi χʼaltʼizabun besːe ɡʔjeb ɡʔjeb pardawaɬe eχetize kːola unqʼɡo χʼubi wa ɡʔjezije unqʼɡo ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabize kːola
azbar swerun ruɡel kinalniɡi χʼubazda rukʼine kːola ɡʼartsul ɡoral χʼubaze ʁuntsʼbi ɡʼartsul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal mazɡarul ɡʔarize kːola
azbar bukʼine kːola nusɡo natʼaɬ χalatab kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo natʼaɬ ɡʼjebab azbar swerun barab pardaw ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ borχatab χʼubazul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal rukʼine kːola mazɡarul
muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul tʼolabɡo qʼaji tsʼaɡi wa ɡʔjeɬijeɡi azbaraɬul pardawazeɡi χʼaʒaɬulel ʁaziqχalɡi mazɡaraɬul ɡʔarize kːola
ɡʼizrailazda ɬazabe naχutʃiraqχalda ʒanibe tʼjeze biʃːun ɬikʼab zajtunaɬul naχ bosun ʃːwezabejan kidaɡo naχutʃiraqχalda kanɬi bakun bukʼine
ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi tsʼunize kːola qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas naqχa ɬurab pardawalda tsebe buɡeb naχutʃiraqχalda bakarab tsʼa dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub betʼjerhanasda tsebe markʼatʃʼudasa baqχarab roɡʔineɡʼan kanɬi swintʃʼoɡo bukʼine ɡʼizrailaz wa ɡʔjezul naslabaz daimɡo tsʼunize kːola ɡʔjeb nizam

ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa ratʼa ɡʔare durɡo wats ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi ɡʔjel dir kaʃiʃzabiɬun teze rukʼine aχʼje ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi nadawɡi awiɡʔuɡi eleazarɡi itamarɡi
ɡʔarunije durɡo watsase kaʃiʃzabazul partal ɡʔabe ɡʔjesul qʼimat tsʼikʼkʼarab dinijab qχuluqχalda reqʼarab
maχʃːel ɡʔunar tsʼikʼkʼaral wa ditsa baʒari kʔural ustarzabazda abe ɡʔarunije ɡʔjeb χasab partal buqʼejan ɡʔjew dije watʼa ɡʔawize wa dir kaʃiʃɬun wukʼine
ɡʔale ɡʔjez χʼadurize kːoleb partal karanda baleb tsebebuχʔ efod tʼasan retʼuneb riza naqʼiʃ besːarab ɡurde tʼaʁur wa ratʃel bitʃːante dur wats ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi ɡʔjeb χasab kaʃiʃzabazul partal buqʼize dije qχuluqχ ɡʔabuleb meχalda tʼad retʼine
ɡʔjeb partalaɬe χʼaltʼizabe mesedil kun wa kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kun wa tʼjerenab χʼjebet
efod ɡʔabize χʼaltʼizabe mesedil kun wa kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kun ɡʔjedinɡo tʼjerenab χʼjebet kʼudijab maχʃːalida uzdanɡo ɡʔabize kːola ɡʔjeb
efodaɬul kʼijabɡo raqχalda ruqʼe kʼiʁuʒduzda tʼad ɬolel ʒal
efodaɬul ratʃelɡi ɡʔjelda reɬːun besːize kːola kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunɡi tʼjerenab χʼjebetɡi χʼaltʼizabun efodɡun tsorekʼarab ɡʔabize kːola ɡʔjeb
tsinɡi kʼiɡo oniksaɬul ʒawɡʔar bose wa ɡʔjezda tʼad bikʼun qχwaj ɡʼizrailil wasazul tsʼaral
kʼudijasdasa bajbiχʔun anɬɡo tsʼar tso ʒawɡʔaralda wa anɬɡo tsoɡidab ʒawɡʔaralda
ɡʼizrailaɬul wasazul tsʼaral qχwaj kʼiɡo ʒawɡʔaralda muɡʔru bikʼulew ustaras ɡʼadinan ɡʔjel ʒawɡʔaral ɬe mesedil tʼjerenkunaz χʔuχʔun maχʃːalida ɡʔarural naɡʼli ɬolel ʒalazda
wa efodaɬul kʼiʁuʒduzda tʼad rekʼinare ɡʔjel ɡʼizrailil wasal rakʼaldeʃːwejaɬul ʒawɡʔaral χʼisabalda ɡʔarunitsa ɡʔjezul tsʼaral ʒindirɡo kʼiʁuʒduzda tʼad ɬun rukʼine te betʼjerhanasda ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ kidaɡo rakʼalda bukʼine
naɡʼli ɬolel ʒal ɡʔare mesedil tʼjerenkunazdaɬun naqʼiʃalɡi kːezarun
ɡʔjedinɡo batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul kʼiɡo kwar kʔurarab ɡʼadinab raχasɡi ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjel raχsal naɡʼli ɬolel ʒalazda rekʼinare
χadub ɡʔabe karanda baleb χʼukmu qʼotʼijaɬul abuleb qʼoqʼab tsebebuχʔ efodɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔabe ɡʔjebɡi tʼjerenab χʼjebtil wa mesedil kunaɬɡi kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunazɡi besːun
bitʃːante ɡʔjeb unqʼbokʼonab bukʼine tso rokʔobaɬul χalaɬiɡi ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡeb kʼiʁat ɡʔaburab χːamil
ɡʔjelda tʼad unqʼɡo kʔjer ɡʔabun ɬe mesedil ɡʔarural naɡʼli ɬolel ʒal ɡʔjezda ʒanir tʼotsebeseb kʔjerda ɬe rubin topaz wa zumrud
kʼiabileb kʔjerda piruza sapfir wa almas
ɬababileb kʔjerda ɡiatsint aɡat wa ametist
unqʼabileb kʔjerda zubarʒad oniks wa jaʃma ɡʔjel kinalɡo ɬe mesedil tʼjerenkunaɬ χʔuχʔaral naɡʼli ɬolel ʒalazda
kinabniɡi antsʼila kʼiɡo ʒawɡʔar bukʼine kːola ɡʼizrailil ʃːiwaw wasasul tsʼar rikʼkʼun ʃːibab ʒawɡʔaralda muɡʔrujalda ɡʼadin bikʼun bukʼine kːola antsʼila kʼiɡo qʼawmaɬul tso tso tsʼar
karanda baleb tsebebuχʔaɬe ɡʔare kʔuraral kwaral ɡʼadinal batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul raχsal
kʼiɡo mesedil barʁitʃɡi ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjel rekʼinare tsebebuχʔaɬul kʼijalɡo tʼadeχunal bokʼnazda
ɡʔjel barʁitʃazda rekʼinabe kʼijabɡo mesedil raχas
wa ɡʔjezul tsoɡidal raɡʼalal kʼiʁuʒduzda oniks ɬural ʒalazda rekʼinare
χadub ʒeɡi kʼiɡo mesedil barʁitʃ ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjel rekʼinare karanzul tsebebuχʔaɬul bokʼnazul ʒaniseb raqχalda
ɡʔabe ʒeɡi kʼiɡo mesedil barʁitʃ wa ɡʔjel rekʼinare efodaɬul kʼiʁuʒduzda ɬolel ʒalazda ʁorkʔjeχun tsebeχun raqχalda bitʼaqχe efodaɬul ratʃelaldasa tʼadeχun buɡeb muqχda askʼor kːoleduqχ
karanzul tsebebuχʔaɬul barʁitʃal ritʃːante efodaɬul barʁitʃazda kantʃʼqχaχʼilab tʃalujaɬ ruχʔun rukʼine tsebebuχʔɡi ratʃelɡi tsotsada rekʼinabun tsebebuχʔ qχuʃtʼulareb χʼalaɬ
muqʼadasab bakʼalde ɬuɡʔunaɡo ɡʔarunitsa rekʼjeda askʼor karanda bukʼuneb tsebebuχʔalda ran rukʼine ruɡo ɡʼizrailil wasazul tsʼaral betʼjerhanasda ɡʔjel kʼotʃene ritʃːalareb iɡʼlan kiniɡin
ʒeɡi qʼoqʼab tsebebuχʔalda ʒanib ɬe urimɡi tummimɡi
efodalda ʁorkʔan retʼuneb riza ɡʔabe qχaχʼilab kʔjeraɬul
ɡʔjelda bakʔuɬ betʼjer beɡʔize karatʼ ɡʔabe wa biqχulareb χʼalalda ɡʔjeb karatʼalda swerun ʃːulaɡo χːamil tʃʼolo buqʼe
sonoɡʼjetʃul suratal ɡʔare kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunalɡi rosun wa ɡʔjel ruqʼe rizajaɬul kwentʃʼjelazul raɡʼalkːun ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔo ɡʔorkʔor mesedaɬul ɡʔarural tsʼurmalɡi ruqʼe
mesedil tsʼurmalɡi sonoɡʼjetʃul suratalɡi rizajaɬul kinabɡo aχaɬijalda tsotsada χadur ruqʼize kːola
ɡʔarunitsa ɡʔjeb retʼine buɡo betʼjerhanase qχuluqχ ɡʔabuleɬul tsʼurmazul ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼize kːola ɡʔarun muqʼadasab bakʼalde betʼjerhanasda tsewe ɬuɡʔunaɡo wa ɡʔjenisa qʼwatʼiwe unaɡoɡi ɡʔjew χwetʃʼoɡo wukʼine
ʒeɡi ɡʔabe batsʼtsʼadab mesedɡi tʃʼintʼizabun mesedil tʼamatʃ wa muɡʔrujalda kiniɡin bikʼje ɡʔjelda
kantʃʼqχaχʼilab tʃalu baj ɡʔjelda wa ɡʔjeb buχʔje tʼaʁuralda tʼasan ɡʔjeɬul tsebeχun raqχalda
ɡʔjeb bukʼina ɡʔarunil nadalda wa ɡʔjes ʒindaɡo tʼade rosila qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi kʔolaɡo ɡʼizrailazuqχa kːarab ʃːibab munaɡʔ χatʼa ɡʔjeb bukʼina kidaɡo ɡʔarunil nadalda qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi betʼjerhanas qʼabul ɡʔarize rukʼine
batsʼtsʼadab χʼjebetaɬul ɡurdeɡi besːe ɡʔarunije ɡʔjeldaɡo reqʼarab batsʼtsʼadab χʼjebetaɬul tʼaʁurɡi ɡʔabe wa tʃarab ratʃelɡi besːe
ɡʔarunil wasazeɡi ɡʔabe ɡʔjezul qʼadru qʼimat tsʼikʼkʼinabulel ɡurdalɡi ratʃelalɡi botʼroda ɬeze tʼaʁralɡi
ɡʔjeb partal dutsa ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazdaɡi tʼad retʼje tsinɡi ɡʔjezda zajtunaɬul χirijab naχ baχe wa ɡʔjezda tʼadabɡi maɬun ratʼa ɡʔare ɡʔjel dir kaʃiʃzabiɬun rukʼine wa dije qχuluqχaɬe tʃʼjeze
ɡʔjezije χʼjebtil ʁorkʔan retʼjel ɡʔabe ratʃlikʔa boχduzde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʼitsʼɬi baχtʃize
ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi ɡʔjeb retʼjel kidaɡo retʼun bukʼine kːola tʃadiraɬure ɬuɡʔuneb meχalda jaɡi χirijab bakʼalda qχuluqχ ɡʔabijaɬe qʼurbanaɬul bakʼalde ɡʼaɡarɬuleb meχalda ɡʔjezda munaɡʔ kːetʃʼoɡo bukʼine wa ɡʔjel χwetʃʼoɡo rukʼine
ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi daimab nizamɬun

ɡʔjel dije kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamize rukʼine ɡʔadin ɡʔabe batʃe tso basiɡi kʼiɡo kujɡi ɡʔjel rukʼine kːola ʃːibɡo ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjel
reʒe biʃːun ɬikʼab roɬul χanʒdal retʃːeb tʼjetʃʼjel tʃadalɡi naχuda rutsaral retʃːeb tʼjetʃʼjel bakarabiɡi tʼad naχ baχaral retʃːeb tʼjetʃʼjel bakarabiɡi
wa ɡʔjel tso tʃʼjepalda ʒanir ɬe basijaldaɡi kujazdaɡi tsadaqχ bose ɡʔjeb tʃʼjep
ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje ratʃe wa ɡʔjezda ɬim baqχe
χadub bose kaʃiʃzabazul partal wa retʼje ɡʔarunida ɡurdeɡi efodalda ʁorkʔ bukʼuneb rizaɡi ʒibɡo efodɡi karanda bukʼuneb tsebebuχʔɡi wa efodalda tʼasan ratʃel qʼaj
ɡʔjesul botʼroda χasab tʼaʁur ɬe wa ɡʔjelda tʼasan buχʔje
tsinɡi zajtunaɬul χirijab naχ bose wa ɡʔjeb ɡʔjesda baχe botʼroda tʼadeɡi tʼun
tsinɡi ratʃe ɡʔjesul wasal wa ɡʔjezda ɡurdal retʼje
ɡʔarunidaɡo ɡʼadin ratʃelalɡi qʼaj wa botʼroda χasal tʼaʁralɡi ɬe ɡʔjeldasa naqχe kaʃiʃɬi daim ɡʔjezuqχ bukʼine buɡo ɡʔjedin ratʼa ɡʔarila dutsa ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi kaʃiʃalɬun rukʼine
χadub tʃadiralda tsebe batʃe basi wa ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi kweral ɬe ɡʔjeɬul betʼjeralda tʼad
tsinɡi tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa qχwe ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda tsebe
basijaɬul bi baχe qʼurban bakʼaɬul ɬːurduzda wa χutʼarab bi ɡʔjeɬul aχade tʼje
χadub bose ɡʔjeɬul tʃeχʔ bakʔaɬul kinabɡo tʼatʼiɡi tʼulal χalaseb butʼaɡi tʼatʼiɡun tsadaqχ urɡʔisalabiɡi wa ɡʔjeb kinabɡo qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼje
otsol ɡʔanɡi tʼomɡi tʃeχʔ bakʔɡi buχʼje χalqʼaɬ qʼaji tʃʼwarab bakʼ tun qʼwatʼibeχun ɡʔjeb buɡo munaɡʔal tʃurijaɬul
tsinɡi batʃe tso kuj wa ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi kweral ɬe ɡʔjeɬul betʼjeralda
χadub ɡʔjeb qχwe wa ɡʔjeɬul bi punqχizabe qʼurban bakʼalde ɡʔjeɬul unqʼabɡo raqχalde
kujdul qʼulaɡʼi keskazde qʼotʼje ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔimesɡi ritsʼimaχʼabiɡi tʃure wa betʼjeraldaɡi tsoɡidal keskazdaɡi tsadaqχ ɬe wa
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo qʼurban bakʼalda tʼadɡi ɬun buχʼje ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase rokʔulel maχʼal raqχinarijaɬe tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb tsʼadul qʼurban
batʃe tsoɡidab kuj wa ɡʔjeɬul betʼjeralda tʼad ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi kweral ɬe
χadub ɡʔjeb qχwe wa ɡʔjeɬul bi baχe ɡʔarunilɡi ɡʔjesul wasazulɡi kwaranab ɡʼinzul raɡʼalda wa kwaranab kweraɬulɡi χʼatʼilɡi kʼudijab kilʃːida tsinɡi bi qʼurban bakʼalde punqχe ɡʔjeɬul unqʼabɡo raqχalde
χadub qʼurban bakʼalda tʼasa tsodaɡʔab biɡi bosun ɡʔjeb χirijab naχɡun ʒubazabe wa ɡʔjeb punqχe ɡʔarunideɡi ɡʔjesul partalaldeɡi ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔjesul wasazdeɡi ɡʔjezul partalaldeɡi ɡʔjebmeχalda ɡʔjewɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi wa ɡʔjezul partalɡi dije qχuluqχaɬe ratʼa ɡʔaruralɬun kːola
χadub bose ɡʔjeb kujdul tʼatʼiɡi moχmoχɡi tʃeχʔ bakʔaɬul tʼatʼiɡi tʼulal χalaseb butʼaɡi tʼatʼiɡun tsadaqχ urɡʔisalabiɡi ɡʔjeb kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamijaɬe qχoleb qʼurban buɡeɬul ɡʔjeɬul kwaranab boχɡi bose
betʼjerhanasda tsebe bosun batʃʼarab tʃʼjepaɬusa bose tso tʃedɡi naχuda butsarab bakariɡi tso naχ baχarab bakariɡi
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo kʔje ɡʔaruniqχeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazuqχeɡi kodobe wa χʔwaɡʼjezabe betʼjerhanasda tsebe χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb sadaqʼa χʼisabalda
χadub ɡʔjezuqχaɡi bosun ɡʔjeb buχʼje qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjeb buɡo tsʼadudaɬun betʼjerhanase kʔoleb χirijab sadaqʼa betʼjerhanase χirijab buɡo ɡʔjeɬul maχʼ
χadub bose ɡʔarun kʼudijaw kaʃiʃɬun tʼamijaɬe qχurab qʼurbanaɬul meɡʔjed wa eχedeɡi borχun χʔwaɡʼjezabe ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo dur butʼaɬun
kʼudijab χiraɬiɬun rikʼkʼje ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamijaɬe qχural qʼurbanazdasan ɡʔjezije kːolel butʼabi χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurbanaɬul meɡʔjedɡi ɡʔjedinɡo χirijab sadaqʼade kʔurab boχɡi
ɡʔjeb buɡo ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi ɡʼizrailazul raqχaldasan kʔoleb daimab butʼa ɡʔjedinɡo raqʼlil qʼurbanazdasaɡi betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo ɡʔjedinal butʼabi kʔjeze kːola ɡʼizrailaz
ɡʔarunil kaʃiʃɬijaɬul partal kʔjeze buɡo ɡʔjesul naslabaz naslabazuqχe ɡʔjebɡi retʼun wa χirijab naχɡi baχun tʼamize ruɡo ɡʔjel kaʃiʃɬijalde
bitʃːante χadubkːun ɡʔjesul bakʼalda kaʃiʃɬun waqχaraw wa tʃadiraɬuwe ɬuɡʔaraw ɡʔjesul naslujaɬul ʃːiwaw tʃijas tʼotsebeseb ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeb partal tʼad retʼaraɬubɡo teze
kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamijaɬe qχurab qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔan beɬe tʃadiraɬul azbaralda
bitʃːante ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi kwanaze ɡʔjeb ɡʔan tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa ɬurab tʃʼjepaɬusa tʃedɡun tsadaqχ
ɡʔjez ʒidetsaɡo kwanaze kːola ɡʔjeb ɡʔjel qʼurbanazdaɬun ɡʔjel allaɡʔasde ɡʼaɡarɬana munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬana wa kaʃiʃɬijalde ratʼa ɡʔaruna batʼijaw tʃijasul iχtijar bukʼunaro ɡʔjeb kwine ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb allaɡʔasul kʼudijab χiraɬiɬun kːoleɬul
ɡʔjeb ɡʔanalɡi tʃadilɡi tʼokʼɬun roɡʔineɡʼan naqχe χutʼarab tsʼaduɬ buχʼje ɡʔjeb ɬitsaɡo kwine beɡʔularo allaɡʔasul χiraɬi bukʼun
ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi dutsa ɡʔabe ditsa duda maɬarabʃːinab ankʔɡo qʼo kʔje ɡʔjel ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔarijaɬul tadbiraɬe
ʃːibab qʼojaɬ munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanɬun basi qχwe ɡʔjel allaɡʔasde ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬul muradalda ɡʔjedinɡo munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurban qχwe qʼurban bakʼ batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabijaɬul muradalda wa ɡʔjelda χirijab naχɡi baχe
ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔabe qʼurban bakʼ batsʼtsʼaɬizabuleb tadbir tsinɡi qʼurban bakʼ ɬuɡʔine buɡo kʼudijab χiraɬiɬun ɡʔjelda qχwarabʃːinab ʒoɡi batsʼtsʼadabɬun ɬuɡʔine buɡo
ʃːibab qʼojaɬ qʼurbanaɬe qχwe kʼiɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjer
tsojab radal tsoɡidab baqʼanida
tʼotsebeseb kʔjeɡʼjeralda tsadaqχ bose zajtunaɬul naχul ɡinaɬul unqʼil butʼaɡun
tsoɡidab kʔjeɡʼjer batʃe baqʼanida tsadaqχ radalɡo ɡʼadinab roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡun wa qʼurban bakʼalde tʼoleb tʃaʁirɡun ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase χirijab maχʼaɬul kʼkʼuj baqχinabijaɬe tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb tsʼadul qʼurban
tʼolalɡo rukʼinesel ɡʼjelazɡi tʼobitʼize kːola ɡʔjedinab tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban betʼjerhanasda tsebe tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa ɡʔjeniw dun nuʒee zaɡʔirɬize wuɡo wa munɡun kʼaɬaze wuɡo
ɡʔjeb bakʼalda dun zaɡʔirɬize wuɡo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬe wa ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo dir χʼalkʼoɬijaɬ batʼa ɡʔaburab χirijab bakʼɬun
ditsa dirɡo χiraɬiɬun rukʼine ratʼa ɡʔarize ruɡo tʃadirɡi qʼurban bakʼɡi ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔarunɡun ɡʔjesul wasalɡi ɡʔjel dir kaʃiʃzabiɬun rukʼine
dun ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔow zaɡʔirɬize wuɡo dun wukʼine wuɡo ɡʔjezul allaɡʔɬun
ɡʔjezda ɬaze buɡo misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ʒal ratʃaraw ɡʔjezul betʼjerhan allaɡʔ dun wukʼin wa dun ɡʔjelɡun wukʼin dun wuɡo betʼjerhan ɡʔjezul allaɡʔ

akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ɡʔabe ɡʔitʼinab qʼurban bakʼ ɡʔuinmaχʼal tʼad ruχʼize
bitʃːante ɡʔjeb unqʼbokʼonab bukʼine tso natʼaɬul χalaɬiɡi ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡeb wa kʼiɡo natʼaɬul borχaɬiɡi buɡeb ɡʔjeɬul bokʼnazda tʃʼwaral ɬːurdulɡi ɡʔjebɡi tsorekʼarab ɡʔabe
batsʼtsʼadab mesed bekʔje ɡʔjeɬul tʼoɡʔaldaɡi χʔalbazdaɡi ɬːurduzdaɡi wa ɡʔjeɬul tʼadeχun raqχalda swerun mesedil tʃalu ɡʔabe
kʼiɡo mesedil ɡor ɡʔabe wa tʃalujalda ʁorkʔan kʼiɡo raqχalda tso tso rekʼinabe ɡʔjeb batʃːulel ɡʼurdul ʒanir ɬeze sanaɡʼatalda
ɡʼurdul ɡʔare akatsijaɬul tsʼulal wa mesed bekʔje ɡʔjezda tʼad
ɡʔjeb mesedil qʼurban bakʼ ɬe qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas naqχa ɬurab pardawalda tsebe munɡun dandtʃʼwaleb meχalda dun wukʼine wuɡeb tʼaɬelalda dandbitʼun kːoleduqχ
bitʃːante ɡʔarunitsa ʃːibab radal ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼize naχutʃiraqχazde naχ tʼoleb meχalda
bitʃːante markʼatʃʼudaɡi ruχʼize naχutʃiraqχazda tsʼa bakuleb meχalda bitʃːante rukʼinesel ɡʼjelazɡi kidaɡo betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɡʔjenib ɡʔuinmaχʼ buχʼize
ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tʼokʼab batʼijab ʒo buχʼuɡe ja batʼijal ɡʔuinmaχʼal ja tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban ja roɬul sadaqʼa ja qʼurban bakʼalde tʼoleb ɬamaɬi

ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼ rikʼkʼuneb meχalda bitʃːante ʃːiwas betʼjerhanase ʒindirɡo ɡʼumrujaɬuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔjeze ɡʔjeb rikʼkʼjen ɡʔabi sababɬun ɡʔjezde kinabɡʼaɡi balaɡʔ reʃːtʼintʃʼoɡo bukʼine
rikʼkʼjen ɡʔabuleb meχalda ʃːiwas kʔjeze kːola ɡʼartsul baʃːdab ʃekel betʼjerhanasul muqʼadasab bakʼalde tʃadiralda χʼaltʼizabuleb aj qʼoɡo ɡera buɡeb ʃekelaɬul baʃːdab
betʼjerhanase χʼaqʼ kʔjeze kːola qʼoɡo sonil riɡʔaldasa tʼade araw ʃːiwaw tʃijas
ɡʔjedin ʒindirɡo ɡʼumrujaɬuqχ betʼjerhanase χʼaqʼ kʔoleb meχalda betʃedaz baʃːdab ʃekelaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun kʔoɡe wa miskinazɡi ɡʔjeldasa daɡʔab kʔoɡe
ɡʼizrailazuqχa bakʼararab ɡʔjeb ɡʼarats tʃadiraɬe χʼaltʼizabe ɡʼizrailazul ɡʼumru χwasar ɡʔabijaɬul χʼaqʼ χʼisabalda bukʼina ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda tsebe

ditsa tʼasawiʃːana jaɡʔudal qʼawmaldasa χʼuril urijil was betsaliel
ditsa ɡʔjesuɬe ɬuɡʔinabuna allaɡʔasul ruχʼ ɡʼaqʼilɬi bitʃʼtʃʼi ɬaj wa kinabniɡi maχʃːeltʃiɬi
ɡʔjesuɬ maχʃːel buɡo mesedil ɡʼartsul wa mazɡarul tʼaɡʼjelal ɡʔarize
ʒawɡʔaral tsʼwakizarize wa ɡʔjel tʼaɡʼjelazda kːweze ɡʔjedinɡo tsʼulal χʼaltʼabi ɡʔarizeɡi tsoɡi bokʔarab ustarɬijaɬeɡi ɡʔunar buɡo ɡʔjesul
ɡʔjesije kumekaɬe ditsa tolew wuɡo danil qʼawmaldasa aχisamaχil was aχoliawɡi tʼolalɡo ustarzabazeɡi ditsa χasab maχʃːel kʔuna ditsa duje amru ɡʔaburabʃːinab χʼaltʼi ɡʔabize

stol wa ɡʔjelda tsadaqχab qʼaji batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul naχutʃiraqχ wa ɡʔjelda tsadaqχab qʼaji maχʼɡʔuinal ʒal ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼ
qʼurbanal ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼ wa ɡʔjeɬije χʼaʒatab tsʼaraɡʼ ɡʔumer kʼal tʃuruleb χʼjertʃ wa ɡʔjeɬul ʁorkʔtʃʼjel
kaʃiʃzabazul qχuluqχ tʼubazabuleb meχaɬ tʼad retʼuneb χasab partal kʼudijaw kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi
χirijab naχ wa χirijab bakʼalda buχʼuleb maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubaj bitʃːante ɡʔjez ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ditsa duda maɬarab qʼaɡʼidajalda ɡʔabize
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazda abe dir ʃamatqʼojal tʼoritʼje ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo ditsa nuʒerɡun wa nuʒeda χadur ratʃʼine ruɡel naslabazulɡun ɡʔaburab qʼotʼijaɬul ɡʼalamatɬun nuʒ tʼasa riʃːaraw betʼjerhan dun wukʼin nuʒeda ɬan bukʼine
ʃamatqʼojaɬul qʼanunal tʼurazare ʃamatqʼo nuʒee χasab χirijab qʼoɬun bukʼine kːola ʃamatqʼojaɬul nizam χwezaburaw ʃːiwaw tʃijase ɡʼaʒal bukʼine buɡo ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ χʼaltʼude maʃʁulɬaraw ʃːiwaw tʃi ɡʔjesul ummatalda ɡʔorkʔosa watʃaqχize wuɡo
χʼaltʼi ɡʔabize kːola anɬɡo qʼojaɬ wa ankʔabileb qʼo aj ʃamatqʼo buɡo χʼalχʔijaɬul qʼo betʼjerhanase batʼa ɡʔaburab qʼo ʃamatqʼojaɬ χʼaltʼi ɡʔaburaw tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola
bajramqʼo ɡʼadin tʼobitʼize kːola ɡʼizrailaz ʃamatqʼo naslabatsa naslabazuqχe kʔoleb daimab χirijab amru χʼisabalda
ɡʔjeb abadul abadijaɬeɡo χutʼize buɡo didaɡi ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob buɡeb qʼotʼijaɬul ɡʼalamatɬun ʃːajɡureɬul anɬɡo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanas ɡʼutsʼana zobalɡi rakʔɡi ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ paraχatalda tʃʼana wa χʼalχʔi ɡʔabuna
sinaj maɡʼarda musaɡun kʼaɬan waqχindal betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesuqχe kʔuna χirijab qʼotʼijaɬul kʼiɡo qʼono ɡʔjezda tʼad qχwaj qχwaɡʼaj ɡʔabun bukʼana betʼjerhanasul kweraɬ

maɡʼardasa tʼadwusːine musa kwatʼulew wukʼinɡi biχʔun χalqʼ bakʼarana ɡʔarunida swerun wa ɡʔjez abuna
misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire niɬ ratʃaraw dow musajeɡi ʃːib kːarabali niʒeda ɬalaro ɡʔjedinɬidal niʒee allaɡʔzabazul sipat ɡʔabe ɡʔjez niʒ tsere ratʃine rukʼine jan
ɡʔarunitsa ɡʔjezda abuna
nuʒer ɬudbuzulɡi wasal jasazulɡi ɡʼunduzdasa raqχun mesedil kʼilkʼal ʃːwezare diqχe jan
χalqʼaɬ mesedil kʼilkʼal raqχana wa ɡʔjel ɡʔaruniqχe rosana
ɡʔarunitsa ɡʔjeb kinabɡo mesedɡi biun tʼun basidul sipat ɡʔabuna ɡʔjebmeχalda χalqʼaɬ abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ ɡʔale misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire nuʒ ratʃaraw dur allaɡʔ
ɡʔjeb raɡʼarab meχaɬ ɡʔarunitsa basijalda tsebe qʼurban bakʼ bana wa χalqʼalda abuna
meter bukʼine buɡo betʼjerhanasul bajram in
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ radal tsudunɡo tʼadeɡi raqχun ɡʔjez tʼoritʼana tʼuran ruχʼulel qʼurbanalɡi raqʼlil qʼurbanalɡi ɡʔjeldasa χadub χalqʼ kwana ɡʔjeqʼeze ɡʼodob tʃʼana wa kʼudijab iχtilat kepalde bajbiχʔana

reʃːtʼa maɡʼardasa dutsa misrijaldasa qʼwatʼibe batʃarab dur χalqʼ pasatɬun buɡo
kiɡʼan χeχɡoχa muʁ reχarab ɡʔjez dir amrabazde ɡʔjez biun tʼurab basijaɬul sipat ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjelda tsere suʒdajalda tʃʼana ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ ɡʔale nuʒ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃaraw nuʒer allaɡʔ inɡi abun

amma musatsa bajbiχʔana betʼjerhanasde ʒindirɡo allaɡʔasde ɡʔardeze
waj betʼjerhan in abuna ɡʔjes ʃːaj dur ɡʔjedin tsːin baqχuneb durɡo kʼudijab qʼudrataldaɬun wa ɡutʃab kweraldaɬun misrijaldasa qʼwatʼibe batʃarab durɡo χalqʼalda
dutsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuni misrijaz abize buɡo allaɡʔas ɡʔjel misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃun rukʼun ruɡo rekʼjeɬ kweʃab pikruɡun maɡʼardeɡi ratʃun ɡʔjenir tʃʼwaze wa dunjalaldasa tʼaɡʼinarize jan ɡʔarula dur ɡʔalaɡab tsːin naqχ busːinabe ɡurχʼa bitʃːaɡe χalqʼalde balaɡʔ
rakʼalde ʃːwezare durɡo laʁzal ibraɡʔimɡi isχʼaqʼɡi ɡʼizrailɡi mun ɡʔjezije durɡo tsʼaraldaɬun ɡʔjedun wukʼindalχa ditsa nuʒee kʔjela zodir tsʼwabiɡʼan ɡʼjemeral naslabi ɡʔab kinabɡo nuʒeda biχʔizaburab rakʔɡi ditsa nuʒer naslabaze kʔjela wa abadijaɬeɡo ɡʔjeb ɡʔjezulɬun bukʼina janɡi abun
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan ɡurχʼana wa χalqʼalde bitʃːazeqχin bukʼarab balaɡʔ naqχtʃʼwana
musa kodob qʼotʼijaɬul qχwaj qχwaɡʼaj ɡʔaburab kʼiɡo ɡantʃʼil qʼonoɡun maɡʼardasa ɡʼodowe wiɬːana ɡʔjel qʼanabazul kʼijabɡo raqχalda qχwan rukʼana allaɡʔasul amrabi

kʼiɡo qʼono qʼatʃʼaj ɡantʃʼil bekʼkʼun tsere rukʼarazda reɬːaral ditsa ɡʔjezda tʼad qχwala dol tʼotseresel qʼanazda rukʼaral raɡʼabi
mun radalalde χʼadurɡo wukʼa tsudunɡo waqχun sinaj maɡʼarde waχine wa meɡʼjeraɬul tʼoɡʔiw dida tsewe waqχun tʃʼjeze
tsadaqχ ʃːiwniɡi watʃunɡe wa kiwniɡi maɡʼarda tʃiɡi wiχʔuɡe muɡʼrul aχada reqχada ɡʼi botsʼiɡitsin bukʼine beɡʔularo
