musatsa ɡʔjebsaɡʼatɡo ɡʼodob nodoɡi tsun allaɡʔase suʒda ɡʔabuna
ɡʔjes abuna
ja dir betʼjerɡʔan dutsa dida raχʼmu ɡʔabuleb batani ɡʔarula dir betʼjerɡʔan munɡo wiɬːa niʒeda tsadaqχ ɡʼasijal rakʼazul χalqʼ ɡʔab buɡoniɡi tʼasa ɬuɡʔa niʒer taqʼsiralɡun munaɡʔazdasa wa dutsaɡo durɡo ummatɬun qʼabul ɡʔare niʒ
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerɡʔanas abuna
ditsa qʼotʼi ɡʔabuleb buɡo nuʒerɡun tsebekːun rakʔalda bukʼarab tsoniɡi χalqʼalda kidaniɡi riχʔitʃʼjel χʼikmaɬabi ɡʔarila ditsa tʼolabɡo dur χalqʼalda tsere duda tsadaqχ ruɡel tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazda biχʔila ɡʔjeb wa kʼudijab χʼinqʼi reʃːtʼina ɡʔjezde duje ɡʼolo ditsa betʼjerhanas ɡʔarize ruɡel ɡʔjel iʃal riχʔidal
ditsa ʒaqʼa nuʒee bujurarabʃːinab raɡʼa rakʔande ʃːun tʼubazabe ditsa nuʒeda tseresa ɬutizarila amorijalɡi χanaanijalɡi χitijalɡi perizijalɡi χiwijalɡi wa jewusijalɡi
balaɡʔje kinabɡʼaɡi ɡʔorkʔobɬi ɡʔabuɡe nuʒ unel ruɡel rakʔazda ɡʼumru ɡʔabun ruɡel ɡʼadamazulɡun ɡuroni ɡʔjez nuʒɡi qʼosinarize ruɡo
ɡʔjezul qʼurban bakʼal riχːizare dinijal ɡantʃʼal ʁure wa aʃeral χʼubal qʼotʼje
tʃijar allaɡʔzabaze suʒda ɡʔabuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul χilipɬi χʼjeχʔolarew betʼjerhan ɡʔjele dir tsʼar χilipɬi χʼjeχʔolarew allaɡʔ
ɡʔjedinɬidal dob rakʔaɬul ɡʼadamalɡun kinabɡʼaɡi ɡʔorkʔobɬi ɡʔabuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul doz ʒiderɡo allaɡʔzabaze rokʔuqʼal ɡʼadatalɡun wa qʼurbanalɡun tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabuleb meχalda doz nuʒɡi aχʼize ruɡo ɡʔjeldeɡo wa nuʒetsaɡi ɡʔjez ɡʔaburab ɡʔabize buɡo wa ɡʔjezul qʼurbanaɬul kwen kwine kːeze buɡo
tsinɡi nuʒetsa ratʃina dozul χalqʼaɬul jasal nuʒerɡo wasaze ɬudbiɬun wa nuʒer wasalɡi tsʼaze ruɡo ɡʔjez ʒiderɡo allaɡʔzabazul rokʔuqʼal dinijal ɡʼadatazde
biun tʼun kinab bukʼaniɡi maχːɡun allaɡʔzabazul sipatal ɡʔaruɡe nuʒeeɡo
kʼodo ɡʔabe buɡʔurɡo tʃadazul bajram ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ kwanaj retʃːeb ɡʔjetʃʼjeb tʃed ditsa ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon awiw motsʼaɬul ɡʔjeɬije tʃʼjezarural qʼojazda
ebelaɬul tʼotsebeseb biχʔinɬimer dir kːola ɡʔjedinɡo nuʒer ɡʼi botsʼul ʃːibab tʼotsebeseb biχʔintʼintʃʼɡi dir kːola
χʼamil tʼotsebeseb kʼjertaɬuqχ kʔjeɡʼjer kʔje ɡʔjedin kʔjeze bokʔitʃʼoni kʼjertaɬul ɡabur beke nuʒer tʼotsere ɡʔarural wasazuqχ dije χʼaqʼ kʔje
tsoniɡi tʃi tʃʼowoɡo watʃʼunɡe dida tsewe
anɬɡo qʼojaɬ χʼaltʼje ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ χʼuχʔbaqχi ɡʔabe χʼuχʔbaqχe χur bekʔuleb wa batʃʼin bakʼaruleb zamanaldatsin
ankʔazul bajram tʼobitʼje ɬiɬari bajbiχʔarab zamanalda wa ɬaɡʼalil aχiralda tʼorʃːel bakʼarijaɬul bajram tʼobitʼje
ɬaɡʼalida ʒanib ɬabtsʼul kinalɡo biχʔinal ratʃʼine kːola χʼalkʼolew betʼjerhanasda ɡʼizrailaɬul allaɡʔasda tsere
nuʒeda tseresa χalqʼal ratʃaqχila ditsa wa ɡʼatʼid ɡʔarila nuʒer rakʔazul ɡʼorqχabi ɬitsaniɡi zaral ɡʔabize ɡʔjetʃʼo nuʒer rakʔaze ɬaɡʼalida ʒanib ɬabtsʼul nuʒ nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsere tʃʼjeze arab meχalda
dutsa qχurab qʼurbanaɬul bi qʼurbanaɬul bakʼalde tʼade bosuleb meχalda retʃːeb tʼurab tʃed bukʼine beɡʔularo ɡʔjenib pesaχaɬul bajramaɬul qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔan roɡʔineɡʼan naqχe teze beɡʔularo
ɬiɬari bajbiχʔarabɡo tsʼijab tʼorʃːalil biʃːunɡo ɬikʼab butʼa ʃːwezabe nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul roqʼobe
burutʼ ɡʔjeɬul ebelaɬul raχʔdaɬ beɬunɡe
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ditsa duda aburabʃːinaɬul qχwaj qχwaɡʼaj ɡʔabe ɡʔjel ruɡo ditsa durɡun wa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼɡun ɡʔaburab qʼotʼijaɬul ʃartʼal
kʼiqʼoɡo qʼoɡi kʼiqʼoɡo sordoɡi bana musatsa betʼjerhanɡun maɡʼarda ɡʔjebɡoʃːinab zamanajaɬ ɡʔjes ʃːibniɡi kwanatʃʼo wa ɡʔjeqʼetʃʼo ɡʔjes ɡantʃʼil qʼanazda tʼad qχwana qʼotʼijaɬul ʃartʼal antsʼɡo amru
kodob χirijab qʼotʼijaɬul kʼiɡo ɡantʃʼil qʼonoɡun sinaj maɡʼardasa reʃːtʼunew wukʼaraw musada ɬalaroan allaɡʔ ɡʔjesda kʼaɬan χadub ɡʔjesul ɡʔurmada nur baleb bukʼin
ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʼizrailazdaɡi musal kentʃʼoleb ɡʔumer biχʔidal ɡʔjel tsʼaqʼ χʼinqʼana ɡʔjesde ɡʼaɡarɬize
amma musatsa ɡʔjel askʼore aχʼana ɡʔjebmeχalda ɡʔarunɡi χalqʼaɬul kʼudijalɡi ratʃʼana ɡʔjesda askʼore wa musa ɡʔjelɡun kʼaɬana
tsinɡi χutʼaral ɡʼizrailalɡi ratʃʼana ɡʔjesda askʼore wa musatsa ɡʔjezda ritsana sinaj maɡʼarda betʼjerhanas kʔural amrabi
ɡʔjelɡun kʼaɬan waqχarawɡo musatsa ɡʔurmade pardaw batʃana
betʼjerhanasda kʼaɬaze ɡʔjesda tsewe uneb meχalda ɡʔjes pardaw tʼasa baqχulaan tʃadiraɬusa qʼwatʼiwe watʃʼineɡʼan qʼwatʼiweɡi watʃʼun ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda betʼjerɡʔanasul amru bitsuneb meχalda
ɡʔjezda biχʔulaan ɡʔjesul ɡʔurmadasa nur tʃwaχuleb bukʼin wa musatsa naqχeɡi ɡʔurmade pardaw tsʼalaan tsʼidasanɡi betʼjerhanasda tsewe ineɡʼan

musatsa ɡʼizrailaɬul tʼolɡo ʒamaɡʼat bakʼarana wa ɡʔjezda abuna
ɡʔale betʼjerhanasul amru
anɬɡo qʼojaɬ χʼaltʼje amma ankʔabileb qʼo nuʒee bukʼina χirijab qʼoɬun ɡʔjeb buɡo χʼalχʔijaɬul ʃamatqʼo betʼjerhanase batʼa ɡʔaburab qʼo ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ χʼaltʼi ɡʔaburaw tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola
nuʒetsa minabaqχ tsʼatsin bakize beɡʔularo ʃamatqʼojaɬ
musatsa ɡʼizrailazul ʒamaɡʼatalda abuna
ɡʔale betʼjerhanasul amru
nuʒer buɡoɬijaldasa betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo χasal sadaqʼabi ɡʔare bitʃːante ʒiw ʒiw tʃijas ʒindirɡo resalda reqʼon betʼjerhanase χasab sadaqʼaɬun kʔjeze χaduseb mesed ɡʼarats wa mazɡar
kantʃʼqχaχʼilab betsʼbaɡʼarab wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarab kwasul kun tʼjerenab χʼjebet wa tsʼtsʼjel kwas
baɡʼarkʔjeraɬ reɬaral ɡʼijal qʼuχʔdul tʼjerenal tsʼakal wa akatsijaɬul tsʼul
naχutʃiraqχaze zajtunaɬul naχ χirijab naχ ɡʔabijaɬe χʼaltʼizarize wa qʼurban bakʼalda buχʼuleb ʒubaj ɡʔabize maχʼɡʔuinal pitsʼalɡi χurdulɡi
efodaɬeɡi karanda baleb tsebebuχʔaɬeɡi oniks wa tsoɡidal baɡʔajal ʒawɡʔaral
nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔosa maχʃːel tʼokʼal ustarzabi rakʼare betʼjerhanas amru ɡʔaburabʃːinab wa χadub reχsarabʃːinab tʼubazabize
tʃadir ɡʔjeɬije pardaw wa tʼasan baleb pardaw ʁuntsʼbi tsʼulal ramabi wa raχal χʼubal wa ɡʔjezije ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal
qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas wa ɡʔjeɬije ɡʼurdul ʁamasaɬul tʼaɬel wa χasab pardaw
stol ɡʔjeɬije ɡʼurdul wa stolaɬul tsoɡidab tsʼaraɡʼ muqʼadasab tʃed
naχutʃiraqχ wa ɡʔjelda tsadaqχab tsʼaraɡʼ kanɬi bakulel ɡʼisintʃiraqχal naχutʃiraqχaɬe tʼoleb zajtunaɬul naχ
ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼ wa ɡʔjeɬije ɡʼurdul χirijab baχuneb naχ wa ɡʔuinmaχʼaze χʼaltʼizabuleb maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubaj tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa biʁuleb pardaw
qʼurbanal tʼad ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼ ɡʔjeɬije mazɡarul χʔuri wa ɡʔjelda tsadaqχab qʼajiɡi ɡʼurdulɡi berkʼal tʃuruleb χʼjertʃ wa ɡʔjeɬul ʁorkʔtʃʼjel
azbaraɬul pardawalɡun χʼubal wa ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal azbaraɬul kʼaltʼa biʁuleb pardaw
muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬe wa azbaraɬe kwaralɡun ʁaziqχal
muqʼadasab bakʼalda qχuluqχ ɡʔabulaɡo tʼadretʼuneb besːarab χːamil partal aj ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi kaʃiʃzabi χʼisabalda allaɡʔase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabuleb meχalda tʼadretʼuneb χirijab partal
musal χitʼabaɬuqχɡi ɡʼjenekːun ɡʼizrailal roqʼo roqʼore ana
wa ʃːiwas ʒindir rekʼjel aχʼijalda reqʼon χasal sadaqʼabi rosun ratʃʼana betʼjerhanasul tʃadiralda tsere tʃadiraɬeɡi ɡʔjenib ɡʔabuleb qχuluqχaɬeɡi kaʃiʃzabazul partalaɬeɡi χʼaʒatabʃːinab
kinatsaɡo biχʔinazɡi rutʃːabazɡi ʒiderɡo saχawatɬijalda reqʼon rosun ratʃʼunel rukʼana mesedil batʼi batʼijal tʼaɡʼjelal karanda ralel ʒal kʼilkʼal barʁitʃal wa raχsal ɡʔjez ɡʔjeb kinabɡo mesed χasab sadaqʼa χʼisabalda betʼjerhanasda tsebe bosun batʃʼana
buɡes buɡeb kʔun bosun batʃʼuneb bukʼana kantʃʼqχaχʼilab betsʼbaɡʼarab wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarab kwasul kun tʼjerenab χʼjebet tsʼtsʼjel kwas baɡʼar kʔjeraɬ reɬaral ɡʼijal qʼuχʔdul wa tʼjerenal tsʼakal
ɡʼarats jaɡi mazɡar kʔjeze bokʔaras ɡʔjeb kʔuna betʼjerhanase χasab sadaqʼaɬun wa akatsijaɬul tsʼul buɡes tsʼul kʔuna
χːam besːize wa kun durʁize baʒari buɡej ʃːijaj tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ bosun batʃʼana kantʃʼqχaχʼilab betsʼbaɡʼarab wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarab kwasul kun wa tʼjerenab χʼjebet
tsoɡidal rutʃːabaz ʒiderɡo baʒarijalda wa rekʼjel aχʼijalda reqʼon durʁuleb bukʼana tsʼtsʼjel kwas
qʼawmazul wa tuχumazul kʼudijaz efodɡi karanda baleb tsebebuχʔɡi qʼatʃʼaze oniksaɬul ʒawɡʔaralɡi tsoɡidal baɡʔa χirijal ʒawɡʔaralɡi rosun ratʃʼana
naχutʃiraqχaɬe χirijab naχuje wa ɡʔuinmaχʼazul ʒubajaɬe χʼaltʼizarize rukʼine ʒeɡi ɡʔjez ratʃʼana maχʼɡʔuinal batʼi batʼijal pitsʼalɡun χurdulɡi zajtunaɬul naχɡi
rakʼ batsʼtsʼadɡo sadaqʼa ɡʔabize bokʔaralʃːinal ɡʼizrailaz rutʃːabaz wa biχʔinaz rakʼ raziɡo betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo χirijal sadaqʼabi kʔuna ɡʔjeb kinabɡo kʔuna musaɡi ɡʔorkʔow kːun betʼjerhanas ɡʔjezda tʼadqʼarab χʼaltʼi ɡʔabun baqχinabijaɬe ɡʼolo
musatsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abuna
ɡʼjenekːe betʼjerhanas tʼasawiʃːana jaɡʔudal qʼawmaldasa χʼuril urijil was betsaliel
ɡʔjesuɬe ɬuɡʔinabuna allaɡʔasul ruχʼ ɡʼaqʼilɬi bitʃʼtʃʼi ɬaj wa kinabniɡi maχʃːeltʃiɬi
ɡʔjesuqχa baʒarula mesedil ɡʼartsul wa mazɡarul tʼaɡʼjelal ɡʔarize
ʒawɡʔaral tsʼwakizarize wa ɡʔjel tʼaɡʼjelazda kːweze ɡʔjedinɡo tsʼulal χʼaltʼabi ɡʔarizeɡi tsoɡi bokʔarab ustarɬijaɬeɡi ɡʔunar buɡo ɡʔjesul
ɡʔjesijeɡi danil qʼawmaldasa aχisamaχil was aχoliawijeɡi tsoɡidazda maɬize ɡʔunarɡi kʔun buɡo
allaɡʔas ɡʔjezije kʔuna bokʔarab χʼaltʼi ɡʔabize ɡʼaqʼlu ɡʔunar ɡʔjezda ɬala maχːul wa tsʼulal χʼaltʼabi ɡʔarize ɡʔjedinɡo tʼjerenab χʼjebtil wa kantʃʼqχaχʼilal betsʼbaɡʼaral kantʃʼbaɡʼaral kunazul χːam besːize kːoleb kuts ɡʔjel ruɡo tsʼaqʼal maχʃːeltʃaɡʼi kiɡʼan zaχʼmatabɡi ustarɬijaɬe ɡʼaqʼlu ɡʔunar buɡel

bitʃːante betsalielitsaɡi aχoliawitsaɡi wa muqʼadasab bakʼ bajaɬul muradalda betʼjerhanas maχʃːelɡi baʒariɡi kʔural ɡʔunar tʼokʼal kinalniɡi ustarzabazɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabize
musatsa aχʼana betsalielɡi aχoliawɡi wa betʼjerhanas baʒari kʔural wa ɡʔjenir χʼaltʼize ʁira buɡel kinalɡo ɡʔunar tʼokʼal ustarzabiɡi
musatsa ɡʔjezuqχe kʔuna muqʼadasab tʃadir bajaɬe ɡʼizrailaz kʔurabʃːinab ʒo χalqʼaɬin abuni qʼojidasa qʼojide ʒeɡi batʃʼuneb bukʼana
ɡʔjebmeχalda muqʼadasab bakʼalda ɡʔarulel χʼaltʼabiɡi tʃʼjezarun ustarzabi riɬːana
musaqχe wa ɡʔjez abuna
betʼjerhanas tʼadqʼaral χʼaltʼabaze χʼaʒaɬulebʃːinab ɡʼunɡi tʼokʼaɬ batʃʼuneb buɡo χalqʼaɬ in
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musatsa tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼatalda ɬazabuna ja biχʔintʃijas ja tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ tʼokʼaɬ ʃːibniɡi bosun batʃʼunɡe muqʼadasab bakʼ bajaɬe jan ɡʼadamaz ratʃʼunel rukʼaral χasal sadaqʼabi ɡʔjedin ɬalqχizaruna
ʃːajɡureɬul χʼaltʼabaze χʼaʒatabʃːinab ɡʼunɡi tʼokʼaɬ bakʼarun bukʼana
maχʃːeltʃaɡʼaz muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬe antsʼɡo pardaw ɡʔabuna tʼjerenab χʼjebtil kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunazɡi besːun ɡʔjel pardawazda tʼad maχʃːalida uɡʔana χeruwimazul sipatal
kinalɡo pardawal rukʼana tsotsazda raʃːadal qʼolo mikʔɡo natʼaɬul χalaɬiɡi unqʼɡo natʼaɬul ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡel
ʃːuɡo pardaw tsotsada buqʼun tso ɡʔabuna wa χutʼarab ʃːuɡo pardawɡi ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔabuna
tsojab pardawaɬul aχiralda buɡeb kʔjeraɬul raɡʼalkːun ruqʼana kantʃʼqχaχʼilab χːamil ʁantsʼakʼitʃʼal wa kʼiabileb pardawaɬul aχiralda buɡeb kʔjeraldaɡi ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔabuna
kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʁantsʼakʼitʃʼ buqʼana kʼijabɡo pardawaɬul aχiralda ruɡel kʔjerazul raɡʼalazdasa eχede tsotsada dandritʼun
ɡʔjedinɡo kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo mesedil ʁantsʼaɡi ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjezdaɬun tsotsada rekʼinabuna kʼijabɡo pardaw tʃadir tsorekʼarab bukʼine
tʃadiralda tʼad baze ɡʔjez ɡʔabuna tsʼtsʼjel kwasul antsʼila tso pardaw
antsʼila tsojabɡo pardawɡi bukʼana tsotsazda baʃːadab ɬeberɡo natʼaɬul χalaɬiɡi unqʼɡo natʼaɬul ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡel
ɡʔjezul ʃːuɡo pardaw tsadaqχ buqʼun tso ɡʔabuna wa χutʼarab anɬɡo pardawɡi ɡʔjedinɡo tsadaqχ buqʼana
tsojab pardawaɬul aχiriseb kʔjeraɬul raɡʼalkːun eχede ɡʔabuna kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʁantsʼakʼitʃʼ wa kʼiabileb pardawaɬul aχiriseb kʔjeraɬul raɡʼalaldaɡi ɡʔabuna kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʁantsʼakʼitʃʼ
χadub kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʁantsʼaɡi ɡʔabuna ɡʔjeb kʼijabɡo tsotsada rekʼinabun pardaw tsoɬizabize
tʃadiralda tʼasan baze pardaw ɡʔabuna baɡʼar kʔjeraɬ reɬaral ɡʼijal qʼuχʔduzul wa ɡʔjeldaɡi tʼasan baze tʼjerenal tsʼakazul
ɡʔjedinɡo tʃadiraɬul qʼedaɬe akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ramabi ɡʔaruna
ʃːibab rama bukʼana antsʼɡo natʼaɬ χalatab natʼɡun baʃːdaɬ ɡʼjebab
χːenazul aχada kʼijabɡo raqχalda tsotsada dandbitʼun kʼiɡo tsʼutʼjelɡun ɡʔaruna ɡʔjel ramabi ɡʔjedin ɡʔaruna kinalɡo ramabi
tʃadiraɬul qʼilbajaɬul raqχaɬe ɡʔabuna qʼoɡo rama
wa ɡʔjezije ɡʼartsul kʼiqʼoɡo ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi ʃːibab ramajaɬe kʼi kʼi tso tsʼutʼjelalda ʁorkʔ tso bukʼuneb χʼalalda
wa tʃadiraɬul ʃimalijab raqχaɬeɡi ɡʔabuna qʼoɡo rama
wa kʼiqʼoɡo ɡʼartsul ʁorkʔtʃʼjel ʃːibab ramajalda ʁorkʔ kʼi kʼi
tʃadiraɬul naqχiseb baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχaɬe ɡʔabuna anɬɡo rama
wa ʒeɡi kʼiɡo rama kʼijabɡo naqχiseb bokʼonaɬeɡi
ɡʔjel bokʼnazda ɬural ramabi aχadasaɡi tʼaradasaɡi tsoɬizarun rukʼana kʼijabɡo ramajaɬul tʼarada ɡoral rana ɡʔjel ʃːulaɬizarize
ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna mikʔɡo ɡor wa antsʼila anɬɡo ɡʼartsul ʁorkʔtʃʼjel ʃːibab ramajalda ʁorkʔ kʼi kʼi
ʒeɡi ɡʔjez ɡʔaruna akatsijaɬul tsʼulal raχal ramabazda tʼasan ɬeze ʃːuɡo tʃadiraɬul tsojab raqχalda ruɡel ramabazda tʼasan ɬeze
ʃːuɡo tsoɡidab raqχalda ruɡel ramabaze wa ʃːuɡo tʃadiraɬul naqχiseb baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχaɬul ramabaze
tʃadiraɬul qʼadazda tʼasan ɡʔjezul bakʔuɬan tsojab raqχaldasa tsoɡidab raqχalde ʃːwarab raχiɡi ɬuna
ramabazda tʼad mesed bekʔana wa ɡʔjezije mesedil ɡoral ɡʔaruna raχal kːweze raχazda tʼadɡi mesed bekʔana
χadub χasab pardaw besːana tʼjerenab χʼjebetɡi wa kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunalɡi χʼaltʼizarun tʼad χeruwimalɡi uɡʔun
pardaw tʼad biʁize akatsijaɬul tsʼulal unqʼɡo χʼubi ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjezda tʼad mesed bekʔana χʼubaze mesedil ʁuntsʼbiɡi ɡʼartsul unqʼɡo ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabuna
tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa biʁize pardawɡi ɡʔabuna kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunaɬul wa tʼjerenab χʼjebtil tʼad rasenalɡi uɡʔarab
wa ɡʔjeɬije ʃːuɡo χʼubi ɡʔabuna tʼad ʁuntsʼbiɡun wa aχadasaɡi tʼoɡʔisaɡi tʼad mesedɡi bekʔun wa ɡʔjezije ʃːuɡo mazɡarul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabuna

betsalielitsa ɡʔabuna akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ʁamas kʼiɡo natʼaɬul χalaɬiɡi wa natʼɡun baʃːdab ɡʼjebɬiɡi borχaɬiɡi buɡeb
ɡʔjes ɡʔjelda ʒanisanɡi tʼasanɡi mesed bekʔana wa ɡʔjelda swerunɡi mesedil tʃalu kːuna
tsinɡi mesedil unqʼɡo ɡor ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjel ɡoral ʁamasaɬul ʁorkʔijal bokʼnazda rekʼinaruna ʃːibab raqχalda kʼi kʼi
tsinɡi ɡʔaruna akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ɡʼurdul ɡʔjezda tʼadɡi mesed bekʔana
wa ʁansil kʼijabɡo raqχalda ruɡel ɡorazda ʒanire kːezaruna ɡʔjel ʁamas batʃːize sanaɡʼatab χʼalaɬ
χadub batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul tʼaɬel ɡʔabuna kʼiɡoɡun baʃːdab natʼaɬul χalaɬiɡi natʼɡun baʃːdab ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡeb
tʼaɬelaɬul raɡʼalazda kʼiɡo χeruwim ɡʔabuna mesedɡi batsʼun
tso χeruwim tso raɡʼalda wa kʼiabileb χeruwim tsoɡidab raɡʼalda ɡʔjes ɡʔjel tʼaɬelɡun tsorekʼaral ɡʔaruna
tsotsazde dande rusːaral χeruwimazul kurkʔbal ʁamasalda tʼad tʼiritʼun rukʼana wa ɡʔjezul ɡʔurmalɡi tʼaɬelalde qʼulun rukʼana
betsalielitsa ɡʔabuna akatsijaɬul tsʼulal stol kʼiɡo natʼaɬul χalaɬiɡi tso natʼaɬul ɡʼjebɬiɡi wa natʼɡun baʃːdab borχaɬiɡi buɡeb
ɡʔjelda tʼad batsʼtsʼadab mesed bekʔana wa ɡʔjelda swerun mesedil tʃalu ɡʔabuna
stolaɬul raɡʼalkːun ɡʔabuna tso qχatɡʼanaseb borχaɬi buɡeb tʼjerenab qʼed wa ɡʔjelda tʼad mesedil tʃalu kːuna
stolaɬe unqʼɡo mesedil ɡor ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjel rekʼinaruna stolaɬul bokʼnazda boχduzda tʼad
ɡoral rukʼana stolaɬul raɡʼalda stol batʃːulel ɡʼurdul ʒanire kːezarize sanaɡʼatab χʼalalda
stol batʃːulel ɡʼurdul ɡʔaruna akatsijaɬul tsʼulal wa ɡʔjezda mesed bekʔana
ʒeɡi ɡʔjes ɡʔabuna stolaɬe χʼaʒatab batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul tsʼaraɡʼ surkʼabi ɡelal ɡulɡunal ʃːurmal qʼurbanal tʼoritʼuleɬul χʼaltʼizarize rukʼine
χadub betsalielitsa ɡʔabuna batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul naχutʃiraqχ mesedɡi batsʼun ɡʔjeɬul boχɡi ɡʼarkʔjelalɡi tʼoɡʔoqʼutʃʼbiɡun tʼantʃalɡi tʼanχazul swerabiɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔabuna tsorekʼarab
naχutʃiraqχaɬul bukʼana anɬɡo ɡʼarkʔjel tso raqχalda ɬabɡo tsoɡidab raqχaldaɡi ɬabɡo
ʃːibab ɡʼarkʔjelalda bukʼana ɬab ɬab tʼoɡʔoqʼwatʃʼa mindalaɬul tʼoɡʔol tʼantʃazul sipatalda ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna naχutʃiraqχaɬul tso boχaldasa kʼijabɡo raqχalde bikʔarab anɬabɡo ɡʼarkʔjelalda
naχutʃiraqχaɬul boχalda tʼad ɡʔabuna tʼantʃazul swerabiɡi ruɡeb mindalaɬul tʼoɡʔol sipatalda ʒeɡi unqʼɡo tʼoɡʔoqʼwatʃʼa
tso tʼoɡʔoqʼwatʃʼa ɡʔabuna naχutʃiraqχaɬul boχaldasa rakːaral ɡʼarkʔalabazul tʼotsebeseb ʒutalda ʁorkʔ kʼiabileb kʼiabileb ʒutalda ʁorkʔ ɬababileb ɬababileb ʒutalda ʁorkʔ wa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna anɬabɡo ɡʼarkʔjelalda ʁorkʔ
batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul ratsʼun ɡʔarural tʼuɡʔdulɡi ɡʼarkʔalabiɡi tʃiraqχɡi tsorekʼaral rukʼana
naχutʃiraqχalda ɬeze ɡʔabuna ankʔɡo ɡʔitʼintʃiraqχɡi biltajaɬe ʁutsʼdulɡi ɡelalɡi kinabɡoɡi batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul
naχutʃiraqχaɬeɡi wa kinabɡo ɡʔjeɬul tsʼaraɡʼaɬeɡi χʼaltʼizabuna batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul tso talant
ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼɡi bana betsalielitsa akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ɡʔjeb unqʼbokʼonab ɡʔabuna tso natʼaɬul χalaɬiɡi ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡeb wa kʼiɡo natʼaɬul borχaɬiɡi buɡeb ɡʔjeɬul bokʼnazda tʃʼwaral ɬːurdulɡi ɡʔjebɡi tsorekʼarab bukʼana
batsʼtsʼadab mesed bekʔana ɡʔjeɬul tʼoɡʔibɡi χʔalbazdaɡi ɬːurduzdaɡi wa ɡʔjelda swerun mesedil tʃalu kːuna
tʃalujalda ʁorkʔjeχun tsotsada dandbitʼarab kʼiɡo raqχalda kʼiɡo mesedil ɡor ɡʔabuna ɡʔjeb batʃːize χʼaltʼizarulel ɡʼurdul ʒanire kːezarize rukʼine
ɡʼurdul ɡʔaruna akatsijaɬul tsʼulal wa ɡʔjezdaɡi mesed bekʔana
ʒeɡi ɡʔjes χʼadurana baχuneb χirijab naχɡi wa mesedil qʼurban bakʼalda buχʼuleb maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubajɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo kʼudijab maχʃːalida ɡʔabuna

betsalielitsa akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ɡʔabuna qʼurbanal ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼɡi ɡʔjeb bukʼana unqʼbokʼonab ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ χalatab ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ ɡʼjebab wa ɬabɡo natʼaɬ borχatab
ɡʔjeɬul unqʼabɡo bokʼonalda tso tso ɬːar ɡʔabuna qʼurban bakʼɡi ɬːurdulɡi tsorekʼaral ɡʔaruna wa ɡʔjeb kinaldaɡo tʼad mazɡar bekʔana
tsinɡi qʼurban bakʼaɬe χʼaʒatab kinabɡo tsʼaraɡʼɡi ɡʔabuna roqχo balel qχubi kwarχabi bi tʼolel surkʼabi ɡʔan baze ɡʼutʃʼal wa buχʼarab tʼurtʃːi ɬolel tʼabkʼal ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔabuna mazɡarul
ʒeɡi ɡʔabuna χʔuri mazɡarul ɡʔin qʼurban bakʼaɬul raɡʼalazdasa ʁorkʔjeχun ɡʔjeɬul borχaɬijaɬul baʃːaɬijalde ʃːwarab
mazɡarɡi biun tʼun χʼadurana ɡʼurduze unqʼɡo ɡor wa ɡʔjel ɡoral mazɡarul χʔurijaɬul unqʼabɡo bokʼonalda ʃːula ɡʔaruna
χadub akatsijaɬul ɡʼurdul ɡʔaruna wa ɡʔjezda tʼad mazɡar bekʔana
ɡʼurdul qʼurban bakʼaɬul kʼijabɡo raqχalda ruɡel ɡorazda ʒanire kːezaruna ɡʔjeb batʃːize sanaɡʼatab χʼalalda qʼurban buχʼuleb bakʼ ɡʔabuna qχarʃːazul ʒanisa ɡʔodorab
dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa qχuluqχ ɡʔabulel rutʃːabaz kʔural matʼabazul betsalielitsa ɡʔabuna mazɡarul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelɡi buɡeb mazɡarul kʼudijab χʼjertʃ
χadub betsalielitsa azbar ɡʼutsʼana azbaraɬul qʼilbajaɬul raqχalda ɡʔabuna nusɡo natʼaɬ χalatab tʼjerenab χʼjebtil pardaw
qʼoɡo mazɡarul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelalda tʼad eχetarab qʼoɡo χʼoboda barab χʼubazda tʼad ʁuntsʼbiɡi ɡoralɡi ɡʔaruna ɡʼartsul
ɡʔjedinɡo ʃimalijab raqχaldaɡi ɡʔabuna nusɡo natʼaɬ χalatab tʼjerenab χʼjebtil pardaw qʼoɡo mazɡarul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelalda tʼad eχetarab qʼoɡo χʼoboda barab χʼubazda tʼad ʁuntsʼbiɡi ɡoralɡi ɡʔaruna ɡʼartsul
baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχalda ɡʔabuna kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo natʼaɬ χalatab pardaw wa ɡʔjeb bana antsʼɡo ʁorkʔtʃʼjelalda tʼad eχetarab antsʼɡo χʼoboda ʁuntsʼbiɡi ɡoralɡi ɡʼartsul ɡʔaruna
baqʼbakːul raqχɡi kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo natʼaɬ χalatab bukʼana
azbaralda ʒanire ɬuɡʔuneb kʼaltʼujaɬul tsojab raqχalda ɡʔabuna antsʼila ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ χalatab pardaw ʁorkʔtʃʼjelalɡi ruɡeb ɬabɡo χʼoboda barab
wa kʼaltʼujaɬul tsoɡidab raqχaldaɡi ɡʔabuna antsʼila ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ χalatab pardaw ɡʔjedinɡo ʁorkʔtʃʼjelalɡi ruɡeb ɬabɡo χʼoboda barab
azbar swerun kːural kinalɡo pardawal ɡʔaruna tʼjerenab χʼjebtil
χʼubazul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal rukʼana mazɡarul χʼubazul ʁuntsʼbi wa ɡoral ɡʼartsul wa ɡʔjezul tʼoɡʔal ɡʼarats tʼad bekʔaral azbaraɬul kinalɡo χʼubal tsotsada ruχʔun rukʼana ritsːatal ɡʼartsul kwaraz
azbaraɬul kʼaltʼa biʁarab pardaw ɡʔabuna tʼjerenab χʼjebtil wa kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunaz besːun tʼad rasenalɡi uɡʔun ɡʔjeb bukʼana qʼoɡo natʼaɬ ɡʼjebab wa ʃːuɡo natʼaɬ borχatab azbaraɬul pardawalɡo ɡʼadin
ɡʔjeɬije ɡʔabuna mazɡarul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelalda eχetizaburab unqʼɡo χʼubi χʼubazul ʁuntsʼbiɡi ɡoralɡi ɡʔaruna ɡʼartsul wa ɡʔjezul tʼoɡʔazdaɡi ɡʼarats bekʔana
muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul wa ɡʔjelda sweruqχ buɡeb azbaraɬul kinalɡo ʁaziqχal rukʼana mazɡarul
ɡʔale muqʼadasab tʃadir aj qʼotʼijaɬul tʃadir balaɡo χʼaltʼizaburab sursataɬul sijaχʼ musal bujuruqχalda reqʼon kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunil was itamaril nuχmaɬijalda ʁorkʔ lewitaz χʼadurana ɡʔjeb sijaχʼ
jaɡʔudal qʼawmaldasa χʼuril urijil was betsalielitsa kinabɡo ɡʔabuna musaɡi ɡʔorkʔow kːun zaɡʔir ɡʔaburab betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon
ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ wukʼana danil qʼawmaldasa aχisamaχil was aχoliaw χʼalbiχʔi buɡew ustar wa maχʃːeltʃi ɡʔjedinɡo kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunazul wa tʼjerenab χʼjebetaɬul χːam besːijaɬul wa rasenal uɡʔijaɬul maχʃːel ɬalaan ɡʔjesda
muqʼadasab bakʼ ɡʼutsʼijaɬe χʼaltʼizabuna qʼolo itʃʼɡo talantɡun ankʔnusijalda ɬeberɡo ʃekel mesedaɬul
χalqʼ rikʼkʼijalda ɡʼaχʔalɬaraz batʃʼana nusɡo talantɡun azaralda ankʔnusijalda ɬabqʼojalda antsʼila ʃːuɡo ʃekel tʃadiralda χʼaltʼizabuleb ʃekel χʼisabalde bosun ɡʼaratsaɬul
χalqʼ rikʼkʼijalda ɡʼaχʔalɬarazul qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral kinalɡo biχʔinazuqχa ɡʔjedinazul kinawniɡi watana   biχʔintʃi bakʼarana ʃːiwasuqχa tso tso beka
tʃadiraɬul wa pardawazul χʼubaze ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal ɡʔarize χʼaltʼizabuna nusɡo talant
χutʼarab azaralda ankʔnusijalda ɬabqʼojalda ʃːuɡo ʃekel ɡʼaratsaɬul χʼaltʼizabuna χʼubaze ʁuntsʼbi wa ɡoral ɡʔarize χʼubazul tʼoɡʔazda bekʔize wa χʼubaze ruχʔjenal ɡʔarize
kinabniɡi ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo talantɡun kʼiazaralda unqʼnusɡo ʃekel mazɡaraɬul
ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔaruna dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼujaɬul χʼubaze ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal qʼurban bakʼ wa ɡʔjeɬije χʔuriɡi tsʼaraɡʼɡi
azbaraɬul pardawazeɡi kʼaltʼujaɬul χʼubazeɡi ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal ɡʔjedinɡo tʃadiraɬeɡi azbaraɬul pardawazeɡi kinalɡo ʁaziqχal

muqʼadasab bakʼalda qχuluqχ ɡʔabulaɡo retʼuneb kaʃiʃasul partal ɡʔabuna kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunaz besːun ɡʔarunida tʼad retʼuneb partal ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musade amru ɡʔaburab qʼaɡʼidajalda
efod ɡʔabuna tʼjerenab χʼjebtil kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunaz besːun ʁorɬe mesedil kunɡi ʒuban
tʃʼintʼizaburab mesedaɬul tʼjerenal tʼantʃalɡi ɡʔarun ɡʔjeb qʼotʼ qʼotʼana tʼjerenal kunazde wa maχʃːalida ʒubazabuna kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunazda wa tʼjerenab χʼjebtida ʁorɬe
χadub kʼiʁuʒduzda tʼad ɬolel ʒal ɡʔaruna wa ɡʔjel tseresaɡi naqχasaɡi efodalda rekʼinaruna
efodalda reɬːarab bukʼana maχʃːalida besːarab efodaɬul ratʃelɡi ɡʔjeldaɡo tsadaqχ tso χːamil kesekaɬul ɡʔaburab betʼjerhanas musada maɬuqχe ɡʔjeɬijeɡi χʼaltʼizabuna mesedil kunɡi kantʃʼqχaχʼilab betsʼbaɡʼarab wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarab kwasul kunɡi tʼjerenab χʼjebetɡi
mesedil tʼjerenkunaz χʔuχʔun maχʃːalida ɡʔarural naɡʼli ɬolel ʒalazda kːuna oniksaɬul ʒawɡʔaral wa muɡʔru bikʼuleb ɡʼadin kʼijabɡo ʒawɡʔaralda tʼad rikʼana ɡʼizrailil wasazul tsʼaral
oniksaɬul ʒawɡʔaral rekʼinaruna efodaɬul kʼiʁuʒduzda tʼad ɬolel ʒalazda ɡʼizrailil wasal rakʼaldeʃːwejaɬul ʒawɡʔaral χʼisabalda betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon
efodɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔabuna karanda baleb tsebebuχʔɡi mesedil kunɡi kantʃʼqχaχʼilab betsʼbaɡʼarab kantʃʼbaɡʼarab kwasul kunɡi wa tʼjerenab χʼjebetɡi bosun
ɡʔjeb bukʼana unqʼbokʼonab tso rokʔobaɬul χalaɬiɡi ɡʼjebɬiɡi buɡeb kʼiʁatab χːamil ɡʔaburab
ɡʔjelda ʒanib unqʼɡo kʔjer ɡʔabun ɬuna baɡʔa χirijal ʒawɡʔaral tʼotsebeseb kʔjerda ɬuna rubin topaz wa zumrud
kʼiabileb kʔjerda piruza sapfir wa almas
ɬababileb kʔjerda ɡiatsint aɡat wa ametist
unqʼabileb kʔjerda zubarʒad oniks wa jaʃma ɡʔjel ɬuna mesedil tʼjerenkunaɬ χʔuχʔaral naɡʼli ɬolel ʒalazda ʒanir
kinabniɡi antsʼila kʼiɡo ʒawɡʔar bukʼana ɡʼizrailil ʃːiwaw wasasul tsʼar rikʼkʼun ʃːibab ʒawɡʔaralda muɡʔrujalda ɡʼadin bikʼun bukʼana antsʼila kʼijabɡo qʼawmaɬul betʼjerasul tso tso tsʼar
karanda baleb tsebebuχʔalda raze batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul kʔur kʔurarab kwar ɡʼadal raχsal ɡʔaruna
mesedil tʼjerenkunaɬ χʔuχʔarab kʼiɡo naɡʼli ɬoleb ʒoɡi kʼiɡo mesedil barʁitʃɡi ɡʔabuna wa tso tso mesedil barʁitʃ rekʼinabuna tsebebuχʔaɬul kʼijabɡo bokʼonalda
kʼiɡo mesedil raχas rekʼinabuna tsebebuχʔaɬul bokʼnazda ruɡel barʁitʃazda
wa raχsazul tsoɡidal raɡʼalal naɡʼli ɬolel ʒalazda naɡʼli ɬolel ʒal efodaɬul kʼiʁuʒduzda tʼad ɬolel ʒalazul tsebeseb raqχalda
χadub kʼiɡo mesedil barʁitʃ ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjelɡi rekʼinaruna efodaɬul tsebebuχʔaɬul tsoɡidal bokʼnazda ʁorkʔijab raqχalda
χadub ʒeɡi kʼiɡo mesedil barʁitʃ ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjel rekʼinaruna efodaɬul tsebeseb raqχaɬul kʼiʁuʒduzda tʼad ɬural ʒalazul aχada efodaɬul ratʃelalda tʼadeχunisan uneb kunaɬul muqχalda askʼob
karanda baleb tsebebuχʔaɬul barʁitʃal ruχʔana kantʃʼqχaχʼilab tʃalujaɬ efodaɬul barʁitʃalɡun tsebebuχʔɡi ratʃelalda tʼadeχun kːezabun efodaldasa ɡʔjeb qχuʃːtʼulareduqχ ɡʔjedin ɡʔabejan tʼadqʼan bukʼana betʼjerhanas musada
efodalda ʁorkʔan retʼuneb riza bukʼana kantʃʼqχaχʼilab kunaɬ besːun ɡʔaburab
bakʔuɬ ɡaburɡi qʼotʼarab wa biqχunɡutʼize ɡaburalda swerun tʃʼoloɡi buqʼarab
rizajaɬul aχadasan ruqʼana kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunaɬul wa tʼjerenab χʼjebtil ɡʔarural sonojaɬul suratal
ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔo ɡʔorkʔor rekʼinaruna batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul ɡʔarural tsʼurmal
tso tsʼumur tso sonojaɬul sipat irɡa ɡʔabun ɬuna wa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna rizajaɬul tʼolabɡo aχaɬijalda ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize kːolaan kaʃiʃas tʃadiralda ʒanib qχuluqχ ɡʔabuleb meχalda ɡʔjeb tʼad retʼine bukʼine betʼjerhanas musada tʼadqʼarab kutsalda
ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi ɡʔaruna tʼjerenab χʼjebtil ɡurdal
tʼjerenab χʼjebtil χasal tʼaʁral ɡʔjeɬulɡo botʼroda ruχʔulel ʒal wa ʁorkʔan retʼunel tʼaʒal
ɡʔjedinabɡo χʼjebtil ɡʔabuna tʼad kantʃʼqχaχʼilabɡi betsʼbaɡʼarabɡi wa kantʃʼbaɡʼarabɡi kwasul kunaɬ naqʼiʃalɡi uɡʔarab ratʃel betʼjerhanas musada maɬuqχe
batsʼtsʼadab mesedɡi tʃʼintʼizabun ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔabuna χirijab taʒ wa ɡʔjelda tʼad muɡʔrujalda ɡʼadin bikʼana
χadub kantʃʼqχaχʼilab tʃalujaɬ ɡʔjeb buχʔana kaʃiʃasul tʼaʁuralda tʼad betʼjerhanas musada biχʔizaburab kutsalda
ɡʔjedin ɡʔabun raɡʼalde baqχana muqʼadasab tʃadir aj dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadir ɡʼizrailaz kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon
ɡʔjez kinabɡo musaqχe bosana tʃadirɡi ɡʔjeɬul qʼajiɡi ʁuntsʼbi ramabi raχal χʼubal wa ɡʔjezije ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal
baɡʼar kʔjeraɬ reɬaral ɡʼijal qʼuχʔduzul ɡʔarural pardawal tʼjerenal tsʼakazul ɡʔarural pardawal
qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas wa ɡʔjeɬul tʼaɬelɡun ɡʼurdul
stol wa ɡʔjeɬije χʼaʒatab tsʼaraɡʼ muqʼadasab tʃed
tʼad ɡʼisintʃiraqχazul kʔjerɡun wa ɡʔjezije χʼaʒatab tsʼaraɡʼɡun batsʼtsʼadab mesedaɬul naχutʃiraqχ kanɬi bakize naχ
mesedil qʼurban bakʼ baχuneb χirijab naχ ɡʔuinmaχʼaze maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubaj tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa baleb pardaw
mazɡarul χʔuriɡun mazɡaraɬul qʼurban bakʼ ɡʔjeɬije χʼaʒaɬuleb tsʼaraɡʼ wa ɡʼurdul berkʼal tʃuruleb χʼjertʃ wa ɡʔjeɬul ʁorkʔtʃʼjel
χʼubalɡun wa ʁorkʔtʃʼjelalɡun azbaraɬul pardawal azbaraɬul kʼaltʼa biʁuleb pardaw azbaraɬe kwaralɡi ʁaziqχalɡi muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul aj dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kinabɡo tsʼaraɡʼ
χirijab bakʼalda qχuluqχ ɡʔabulaɡo retʼuneb besːarab χːamil partal aj ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi betʼjerhanase qχuluqχ ɡʔabuleb meχalda retʼuneb χasab kaʃiʃzabazul partal
betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabuna ɡʼizrailaz kinabɡo χʼaltʼi
musatsa tʼolalɡo χʼaltʼabazul χal ʃal ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjesda biχʔana kinabɡo betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabun bukʼin musa ɡʔjelda raziɬana wa ɡʔjezije ɬikʼabʃːinab ɡʔarun duɡʼa ɡʔabuna

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
tʼotsebeseb motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ dutsa muqʼadasab tʃadir aj dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadir eχete
ɡʔjenib ʒanib ɬe qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas wa ɡʔjelda tsebe pardaw biʁe
χadub ɡʔjenibe stol bose wa ɡʔjelda tʼad kinabɡo stolaɬul tsʼaraɡʼ ɬe naχutʃiraqχɡi bose wa ɡʔjelda tʼad ɡʼisintʃiraqχal ɬe
qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamasalda tsebe ɬe ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼuleb mesedil qʼurban bakʼ χadub tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa pardaw biʁe
qʼurbanal tʼad ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼ ɬe tʃadiraɬul aj dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼujalda dandbitʼun
dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraldaɡi qʼurban buχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ɬe berkʼal tʃuruleb χʼjertʃ wa ɡʔjelda ʒanibe ɬim tʼje
tʃadiralda swerun ɡʼutsʼje azbar wa azbaraɬul kʼaltʼaɡi pardaw biʁe
bose χirijab naχ wa ɡʔjeb baχe tʃadiraldaɡi ɡʔjelda ʒanib buɡeb kinabɡo tsʼaraɡʼaldaɡi wa ɡʔjeb bukʼina allaɡʔase batʼa ɡʔaburabɬun aj χirijabɬun
ɡʔjedinɡo χirijab naχ baχe qʼurban buχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼaldaɡi kinabɡo ɡʔjeɬul tsʼaraɡʼaldaɡi ɡʔjedin allaɡʔase batʼa ɡʔabe ɡʔjeb wa ɡʔjebɡi bukʼina kʼudijab χiraɬiɬun
χirijab naχ baχe berkʼal tʃuruleb χʼjertʃaldaɡi ɡʔjeɬul ʁorkʔɬelaldaɡi wa ɡʔjelɡi allaɡʔase ratʼa ɡʔare
tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje ratʃe ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi wa ɡʔjezda tʼasan ɬim bitʃːaj
χadub ɡʔarunida tʼad χirijab partal retʼje wa ɡʔjesda χirijab naχɡi baχe ɡʔjew dir kaʃiʃɬun wukʼine
tsinɡi ɡʔjesul wasal ratʃe wa ɡʔjezda tʼad ɡurdal retʼje
insudaɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjezdaɡi χirijab naχ baχe ɡʔjelɡi dir kaʃiʃzabiɬun rukʼine ɡʔjeb χirijab naχ ɡʔjezda baχinaɬul maɡʼna kːola ɡʔjelɡi ɡʔjezul naslabiɡi daimaɬeɡo kaʃiʃɬijalde qʼabul ɡʔarun rukʼin
musatsa kinabɡo muχʼkanɡo betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabuna
kʼiabileb sonaɬul tʼotsebeseb motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ eχetizabuna muqʼadasab tʃadir
musatsa tʃadir eχetana ɡʔjeɬul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal ɬuna raqχun tʃʼjezaruna ɡʔjeɬul ramabi ɬuna raχal wa eχetizaruna χʼubal
χadub ɡʔjes tʃadiralda tʼad pardaw biʁana wa ɡʔjelda tʼasanɡi kʼiabileb pardaw tʼibitʼana betʼjerhanas maɬuqχe
musatsa rosana qʼotʼijaɬul qʼanal wa ɡʔjel ʁansida ʒanir ɬuna ɡʼurdul ʁamasaɬul ɡorazda ʒanire kːezaruna wa ɡʔjelda tʼad tʼaɬel ɬuna
χadub ɡʔjes ʁamas muqʼadasab tʃadiralda ʒanibe bosana ɡʔjelda tsebe χasab pardaw biʁana wa betʼjerhanas maɬuqχe baχtʃizabuna qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas
χadub dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub ɡʔjeb χasab pardawalda tsebeχun ʃimalijab raqχalda musatsa stol ɬuna
wa ɡʔjelda tʼad betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon muqʼadasab tʃed ɬuna
stolalda dandbitʼun tʃadiraɬul qʼilbajaɬul raqχalda ɬuna naχutʃiraqχ
wa naχutʃiraqχalda ɡʼisintʃiraqχalɡi reqʼezaruna betʼjerhanasda tsere betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon
dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda ʒanib χasab pardawalda tsebe mesedil qʼurban bakʼ ɬuna
wa ɡʔjelda tʼad ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼana betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon
χadub tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼaɡi pardaw biʁana
muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul aj dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼujalda tsebe qʼurbanal tʼad ruχʼuleb mazɡarul qʼurban bakʼ ɬuna wa ɡʔjenib tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanɡi roɬul χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi tʼoritʼana betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon
dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraldaɡi qʼurban bakʼaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ɬuna berkʼal tʃuruleb χʼjertʃ wa ɡʔjelda ʒanibe ɬim tʼuna
musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi kweralɡi χʼatʼalɡi tʃurize rukʼine
tʃadiralda ʒanire ɬuɡʔinalde jaɡi qʼurbanaɬul bakʼalda askʼore inalde tsebe betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon
aχirɡi musatsa tʃadiraldaɡi qʼurban bakʼaldaɡi sweruqχ azbar ʒanibe batʃana wa azbaraɬul kʼaltʼaɡi pardaw biʁana
ɡʔjedin ɡʔabun baqχinabuna musatsa kinabɡo χʼaltʼi
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nakʼkʼul partʃajaɬ baχtʃizabuna dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadir wa betʼjerhanasul nuraɬ tsʼjezabuna muqʼadasab bakʼ
musaqχa baʒaruleb bukʼintʃʼo tʃadiraɬuwe ʒaniwe ɬuɡʔine ʃːajɡureɬul tʃadiralda tʼad tʃʼun bukʼana nakʼkʼul partʃa wa muqʼadasab bakʼ tʼadeɡʼanasul nuraɬ tsʼjezabun bukʼana
ɡʼizrailal saparazda rukʼaɡo tʃadiraldasa nakʼkʼul partʃa naqχe indal ɡuroni nuχda raqχunaroan ɡʔjel
amma nakʼkʼul partʃa naqχe intʃʼoni ɡʔjel tʃʼaraɬurɡo rukʼunaan ɡʔjeb naqχe ineɡʼan
betʼjerhanasul nakʼkʼul partʃa tʃʼolaan tʃadiralda tʼad qʼad sardiɬ ɡʔjeb nakʼkʼul partʃaduɬ tsʼa biχʔulaan tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazda biχʔulaan ɡʔjeb ɡʔjel saparazda ruɡebɡʼan meχaɬ

betʼjerhanas musade aχʼana dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda ʒanisan wa ɡʔjes musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda kʼaɬaj wa ɡʔjezda abe betʼjerhanase qʼurban qχoleb buɡoni ɡʔjeb bukʼine kːola ruqʼaɬul χʼajwan botsʼul roχʔdoɬa jaɬuni ɡʼi tsʼanazul reqχaɬa ʒo
ɬitsa buɡoniɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe basi qχoleb buɡoni ɡʔjeb bukʼine kːola ʃːibniɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb betʼjerhanas qʼabul ɡʔabize bukʼine ɡʔjeb dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsebe batʃine kːola
bitʃːante ɡʔjes tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχoleb χʼajwanaɬul botʼroda kweral ɬeze
bitʃːante ɡʔjes basi qχweze betʼjerhanasda tsebe wa ɡʔarunil wasaz aj kaʃiʃzabaz ɡʔjeɬul biɡi bosun ɡʔjeb punqχila dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsebe ɬurab qʼurban bakʼalde ɡʔjeɬul unqʼabɡo raqχalde
tsinɡi qʼurban tʃːukʼila wa ɡʔjeɬul χamalaɡ qʼotʼ qʼotʼila
kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunil wasaz qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad tsin tsʼa bakila tsinɡi ɡʔjelda tʼade tsʼulɡi bala
χadub kaʃiʃzabaz aj ɡʔarunil wasaz qʼurban bakʼalda tsʼaduda tʼad ɬela ɡʔjeb qʼurban betʼjerɡun wa tʼatʼiɡun tsadaqχ
qʼurbanaɬul urɡʔimesɡi χʼatʼalɡi ɬetsa tʃurila wa kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeb kinabɡo qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila ɡʔjeb buɡo tsʼadudaɬun betʼjerhanase kʔoleb tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban betʼjerhanase ɡʔuinab buɡo ɡʔjeɬul maχʼ
tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe kuj jaɬuni deɡʼjen qχoleb buɡoni ɡʔjel rukʼine kːola kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjel
qʼurban ɡʔabulew tʃijas qχweze kːola ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda tsebe qʼurban bakʼaɬul ʃimalijab raqχalda kaʃiʃzabaz ɡʔarunil wasaz ɡʔjeɬul bi punqχila qʼurban bakʼalde ɡʔjeɬul ʃːibab raqχalde
tsinɡi qʼurbanaɬul qʼulaɡʼi qʼotʼ qʼotʼila wa betʼjerɡun tʼatʼiɡun tsadaqχ kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɬela qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼuleb tsʼulada tʼasan
qʼurbanaɬul urɡʔimesɡi χʼatʼalɡi ɬetsa tʃurila wa kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeb kinabɡo qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila ɡʔjeb buɡo tsʼadudaɬun betʼjerhanase kʔoleb tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban betʼjerhanase ɡʔuinab buɡo ɡʔjeɬul maχʼ
tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanɬun χʼintʃʼ kʔoleb buɡoni bitʃːante ɡʔjeb bukʼine roχʔil mikːi jaɬuni mikːidul tʼintʃʼ
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeb χʼintʃʼ qʼurban bakʼalda askʼobe bosize kːola wa ɡʔjeɬul betʼjerɡi kʔurun tʼun ɡʔjeb qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼize kːola χʼantʃʼil bi qʼurban bakʼaɬul tsojab raqχalde bitʃːaze kːola
ɡʔjeɬul muqʼurɡi χʼuliɡi kaʃiʃas qʼurban bakʼaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalde aj raqχu baleb bakʼalde reχila
bitʃːante ɡʔjes kurkʔbiɡi kːun χʼintʃʼ ɡʔakʼkʼazabize amma tʼjezabitʃʼoɡo tsadaqχɡo qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad bakarab tsʼaduɬ buχʼize ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase tsʼadudaɬun kʔoleb tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb wa ɡʔjesije maχʼ χirijab qʼurban

betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo roɬul χirijab sadaqʼa kʔoleb meχaɬ ɡʔjeb bukʼine kːola tʼasa biʃːarab roɬ χirijab sadaqʼa kʔolew tʃijas roɬuɬe zajtunaɬul naχɡi tʼjela wa tʼasan ladanɡi
wa ɡʔjeb kaʃiʃzabazuqχe aj ɡʔarunil wasazuqχe bosila kaʃiʃas ɡʔjelda tʼasa naχɡun wa kinabɡo ladanɡun tsadaqχ tso danʁura roɬul bosila wa ɡʔjeb buχʼila qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad tʼolabɡo χirijab sadaqʼajaɬul bakʼalda tʃʼoleb butʼa χʼisabalda ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase bokʔuleb maχʼaɬul tsʼadul qʼurban
roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬul χutʼarab ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi bukʼine kːola betʼjerhanasul tsʼadul sadaqʼajaɬul butʼa bukʼinaɬ ɡʔjeb buɡo kʼudijab χiraɬi
roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬe koroqχ reʒaral tʃadal kʔolel ruɡoni ɡʔjel rukʼine kːola ɬikʼab roɬul rutsaral zajtunaɬul naχuda rutsaral jaɬuni tʼad zajtunaɬul naχ baχaral buɡʔurɡo tʃadal
roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬe qʼanida tʼad beʒarab tʃed kʔoleb buɡoni ɡʔjebɡi bukʼine kːola ɬikʼab roɬul butsarab zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʒubarab retʃːebɡi ʁorɬ ɡʔjetʃʼjeb
ɡʔjeɬul ɡʼisinal motʃʼabi ɡʔare wa ɡʔjelda tʼade zajtunaɬul naχ tʼje ɡʔjeb kːola roɬul χirijab sadaqʼa
roɬul sadaqʼajaɬe ɡelalda ʒanib beʒarab tʃed kʔoleb buɡoni ɡʔjebɡi bukʼine kːola ɬikʼab roɬul zajtunaɬul naχuda butsun ɡʔaburab
ɡʔjedin χʼadurarab roɬul χirijab sadaqʼa bosize kːola betʼjerhanasul tʃadiralda tsebe tsinɡi ɡʔjeb kaʃiʃasuqχe kʔjela wa ɡʔjes qʼurban bakʼalde bosila
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeɬul tso butʼa tʼolabɡo χirijab sadaqʼajaɬul bakʼalda tʃʼoleb butʼa χʼisabalda qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase χirijal maχʼal raqχinarijaɬe tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb tsʼadul qʼurban
χirijab sadaqʼajaɬul χutʼarab ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi bukʼine kːola betʼjerhanasul tsʼadul sadaqʼajaɬul butʼa bukʼinaɬ ɡʔjeb buɡo kʼudijab χiraɬi
tʼolalɡo betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo kʔolel roɬul χirijal sadaqʼabazda tsadaqχ kinabɡʼaɡi retʃːeb bukʼine beɡʔularo ja retʃːeb ja ɡʔotsʼo betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo kʔoleb χirijab sadaqʼa χʼisabalda buχʼuɡe
dutsa ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo χirijab sadaqʼaɬun kʔjeze beɡʔula tsʼijab χʼaluqχenaɬul butʼa χʼisabalda amma qʼurban bakʼalda betʼjerhanase χirijab maχʼ baqχinabulaɡo ɡʔjeb ɡʔjenib bukʼine beɡʔularo
kinalɡo roɬul χirijal sadaqʼabazuɬe tsʼam baj ɡʔjenibe tsʼam batʃʼoɡo teze beɡʔularo ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb kːola allaɡʔasul qʼotʼijaɬul tsʼam
betʼjerhanase roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬe ɬiɬarijaɬul bajbiχʔuda tsʼijab buɡʼa roɬ kʔoleb meχaɬ tʼoraldasa batsʼtsʼadɡi ɡʔabun qχurizeɡi qχurun ɡʔjeb barsize kːola
ɡʔjelda tʼade zajtunaɬul naχɡi tʼje tʼasan ladanɡi ɬe ɡʔjeb kːola roɬul χirijab sadaqʼa
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas naχɡun wa kinabɡo ladanɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjeb ʁurarab buɡʼa roɬul tso butʼa bosize wa ɡʔjeb buχʼize tʼolabɡo χirijab sadaqʼajaɬul bakʼalda tʃʼoleb butʼa χʼisabalda ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase kʔoleb tsʼadul sadaqʼa

raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe ots jaɬuni ɡʼaka qχoleb buɡoni betʼjerhanasda tsebe batʃine kːola ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb χʼajwan
qʼurbanaɬul betʼjerɡʔanas χʼajwanaɬul betʼjeralda tʼad kwer ɬeze kːola wa dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa tsebe ɡʔjeb qχweze kːola tsinɡi ɡʔarunil wasaz aj kaʃiʃzabaz ɡʔjeɬul bi punqχize kːola qʼurban bakʼalde ɡʔjeɬul ʃːibab raqχalde
betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanɬun buχʼize bukʼine raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬul urɡʔimesaɬul tʼatʼi batʼa ɡʔabize kːola
kʼijabɡo urɡʔisalaɡi urɡʔisalabazda tʼad bukʼuneb tʼatʼiɡi tʼulal χalaseb butʼaɡi
χadub ɡʔarunil wasaz buχʼila ɡʔjeb kinabɡo qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanalda tsadaqχ ɡʔjeb buɡo tsʼadul qʼurban betʼjerhanase χirijab buɡo ɡʔjeɬul maχʼ
raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe ɡʼijaɬaʒo kʔoleb buɡoni ɡʔjeb bukʼine beɡʔula kuj jaɬuni tʃaqχu amma ɡʔjeb bukʼine kːola ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb
ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe kʔjeɡʼjer kʔoleb buɡoni ɡʔjes betʼjerhanasda tsebeɡi batʃun
ɡʔjeɬul betʼjeralda tʼad kwer ɬe wa dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsebe qχwe ɡʔjeb χadub ɡʔarunil wasaz ɡʔjeɬul bi punqχe qʼurban bakʼalde ɡʔjeɬul ʃːibab raqχalde
ɡʔjeb raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬul tʼatʼi batʼa ɡʔabize kːola betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanɬun buχʼize ratʃʼaɬul ɡʔodalɡun tsadaqχ rakʔandasa qʼotʼarab tʼolabɡo moχmoχɡi kinabɡo urɡʔimesaɬul tʼatʼiɡi
urɡʔisalabiɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjezda tʼad bukʼuneb tʼatʼiɡi tʼulal χalaseb butʼaɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo batʼa ɡʔabize kːola urɡʔisalabiɡun tsadaqχ
wa kaʃiʃas buχʼila ɡʔjeb kinabɡo qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad tsʼadudaɬun betʼjerhanase kʔoleb kwen χʼisabalda
qʼurbanaɬe tsʼtsʼje qχoleb buɡoni bitʃːante ɡʔjeɬul χwaʒainas ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda tsebe batʃine
tsin ɡʔjes tsʼtsʼjel botʼroda kwer ɬela tsinɡi dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsebe ɡʔjeb qχwela χadub ɡʔarunil wasaz ɡʔjeb tsʼtsʼjel bi punqχila qʼurban bakʼalde tʼade ɡʔjeɬul ʃːibab raqχalde
qʼurbanaɬul urɡʔimesaɬul tʼatʼi batʼa ɡʔabize kːola betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanɬun buχʼize bukʼine urɡʔimesaɬul kinabɡo tʼatʼiɡi
urɡʔisalabiɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjezda tʼad bukʼuneb tʼatʼiɡi tʼulal χalaseb butʼaɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo batʼa ɡʔabize kːola urɡʔisalabiɡun tsadaqχ
χadub kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeb kinabɡo tʼatʼi qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila ɡʔjeb buɡo ɡʔuinab maχʼaɬul tsʼadul qʼurban tʼolabɡo tʼatʼi betʼjerhanasul kːola
ɡʔale nuʒeeɡi χadusel ɡʼjelazeɡi bukʼine buɡeb abadijab qʼanun kir nuʒ ruɡoniɡi nuʒetsa ja tʼatʼi ja bi kwanije χʼaltʼizabuɡe

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
dutsa ɡʼizrailazda abe ʃːiw wukʼaniɡi toχɬukʔje munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːani wa beɡʔulareb iʃɡi ɡʔabun ɡʔjes ɬatʃʼoɡo betʼjerhanasul tsoɡʼaɡi amru χwezabuni ɡʔale ɡʔjes ɡʔabize kːoleb ʒo
ɡʔjew kʼudijaw kaʃiʃ watani wa ʒiw sababɬun χalqʼalda tʼade ɡʼajibɡi batʃun ɡʔjew munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːani bitʃːaj ɡʔjes kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb basi batʃun batʃʼine betʼjerhanasul tʃadiralda tsebe ʒindirɡo munaɡʔal tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanɬun qχweze bukʼine
bitʃːante ɡʔjes basi dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬuqχe betʼjerhanasda tsebe batʃine tsin ɡʔjeɬul betʼjeralda kwer ɬeze tsinɡi betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɡʔjeb qχweze
χadub kʼudijaw kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeb qʼurbanaɬul tsodaɡʔab bi bosize kːola dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda ʒanibe
wa biduɬ kiliʃːɡi tʃːun ɡʔjeb bi ankʔɡo nuχaɬ punqχize kːola muqʼadasab bakʼaɬul χasab pardawalda tsebe aj betʼjerhanasda tsebe
χadub ɡʔjeb bi baχine kːola dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda ʒanib betʼjerhanasda tsebe buɡeb ɡʔuinmaχʼal tʼad ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼaɬul bokʼnazda tʃʼwaral ɬːurduzdaɡi χutʼarab bi tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa buɡeb qʼurbanal tʼad ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼalda tsebe tʼjeze kːola
χadub bitʃːante kaʃiʃas batʼa ɡʔabize munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe qχurab basidul tʼolabɡo kʔaraɬi urɡʔimesaɬul tʼolabɡo tʼatʼiɡi
urɡʔisalabiɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjezda tʼad bukʼuneb tʼatʼiɡi tʼulal χalaseb butʼaɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo batʼa ɡʔabize kːola urɡʔisalabiɡun tsadaqχ
aj raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe qχural ʒalaze ɡʔabulebɡo ɡʼadin tsinɡi kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeb kinabɡo tsʼadul qʼurbanazul qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila
basidul tʼomɡi kinabɡo ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔanɡi betʼjerɡun χʼatʼalɡun urɡʔimesɡun tsadaqχ
χalqʼaɬ ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼibeχun batsʼtsʼadab bakʼalde bosize kːola wa roqχo baleb bakʼalda tsʼulɡi bakun buχʼize kːola ɡʔjeb kinabɡo buχʼize kːola roqχo baleb bakʼalda
tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬ ɬatʃʼoɡo meqʼab ʒo ɡʔabuni wa beɡʔulareb iʃɡi ɡʔabun toχɬukʔje betʼjerhanasul tsoɡʼaɡi amru χwezabuni ɡʔjebmeχaɬ χalqʼalda ɡʼajib kːola
ʒidetsa munaɡʔ ɡʔabun bukʼin ɡʼadamazda bitʃʼtʃʼidal tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬul raqχaldasan munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe tso basi kʔjeze kːola bitʃːante dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje batʃine ɡʔjeb
betʼjerhanasda tsebe ʒamaɡʼataɬul kʼudijaz ɡʔjeɬul betʼjeralda kweral ɬeze wa ɡʔjenib ɡʔjeb basi qχweze
χadub kʼudijaw kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeɬul tsodaɡʔab bi bosila dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda ʒanibe
wa biduɬ kiliʃːɡi tʃːun ɡʔjeb bi ankʔɡo nuχaɬ punqχila muqʼadasab bakʼaɬul χasab pardawalda tsebe aj betʼjerhanasda tsebe
ɡʔjeb bi baχine kːola dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda ʒanib betʼjerhanasda tsebe buɡeb ɡʔuinmaχʼal tʼad ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼaɬul bokʼnazda tʃʼwaral ɬːurduzdaɡi χutʼarab bi tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa buɡeb qʼurbanal tʼad ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼalda tsebe tʼjeze kːola
χadub basidul urɡʔimesaɬul tʼolabɡo tʼatʼi batʼa ɡʔabila wa qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔabize kːola munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe biχʔizaburab nizamalda ɡʔjedin kaʃiʃas χalqʼaldasa munaɡʔal tʃurijaɬul qʼurban tʼobitʼila wa allaɡʔ χalqʼaɬul munaɡʔazda tʼasa ɬuɡʔina
kaʃiʃasdasa tʼobitʼarab qʼurbanaɬulɡo ɡʼadin qχurab basidul χutʼarabʃːinab ʒo buχʼize kːola χalqʼaɬ ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼibeχun raqχalda ɡʔjeb kːola tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬul munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurban
kinabɡʼaɡi qʼawmaɬul jaɡi tuχumaɬul betʼjeras ɬatʃʼoɡo munaɡʔ ɡʔabuni wa beɡʔulareb iʃɡi ɡʔabun toχɬukʔje betʼjerhanasul tsoɡʼaɡi amru χwezabuni wa ɡʔjeldaɬun ʒiwɡo ɡʼajibaɬukʔje kːezawuni
ʒiwɡo munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːun wukʼin bitʃʼtʃʼidal bitʃːante ɡʔjes qʼurbanaɬe ʃːibɡo ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb deɡʼjen batʃʼine
bitʃːante ɡʔjes tsin daɡʼnil betʼjeralda kwer ɬeze wa betʼjerhanasda tsebe tʼuban ruχʼulel qʼurbanal qχoleb bakʼalda ɡʔjeb qχweze ɡʔjeb buɡo munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurban
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeɬul biduɬ kiliʃːɡi tʃːun ɡʔjeb bi baχina qʼurbanal tʼad ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼaɬul bokʼnazda tʃʼwaral ɬːurduzda wa χutʼarab bi qʼurban bakʼalda tsebe tʼjela
χadub daɡʼnil tʼolabɡo tʼatʼi qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬulɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjedin kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃijasdasa munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurban tʼobitʼila wa allaɡʔ ɡʔjesul munaɡʔalda tʼasa ɬuɡʔina
χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa kinaw wukʼaniɡi ɡʼadatijaw tʃijas ɬatʃʼoɡo munaɡʔ ɡʔabuni wa beɡʔulareb iʃɡi ɡʔabun toχɬukʔje betʼjerhanasul tsoɡʼaɡi amru χwezabuni wa ɡʔjeldaɬun ʒiwɡo ɡʼajibaɬukʔje kːezawuni
ʒiwɡo munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːun wukʼin bitʃʼtʃʼidal bitʃːante ɡʔjes qʼurbanaɬe ʃːibɡo ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb tsʼtsʼje batʃun batʃʼine
bitʃːante ɡʔjes tsin tsʼtsʼjel betʼjeralda kwer ɬeze wa tʼuban ruχʼulel qʼurbanal qχoleb bakʼalda ɡʔjeb qχweze
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeɬul biduɬ kiliʃːɡi tʃːun ɡʔjeb bi baχina qʼurbanal tʼad ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼaɬul bokʼnazda tʃʼwaral ɬːurduzda wa χutʼarab bi qʼurban bakʼalda tsebe tʼjela
χadub kaʃiʃas tsʼtsʼjel tʼolabɡo tʼatʼi batʼa ɡʔabila raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬulɡo ɡʼadin wa betʼjerhanase bokʔuleb ɡʔuinab maχʼ baqχinabizeɬun qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila ɡʔjedin kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃijasdasa munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurban tʼobitʼila wa allaɡʔ tʼasa ɬuɡʔina ɡʔjesul munaɡʔaldasa
munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe qχweze pulanaw tʃijas ɡʼijaɬaʒo batʃʼuneb buɡoni ɡʔjeb bukʼine kːola ʃːibɡo ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb tʃaqχu
bitʃːante ɡʔjes tsin tʃaqχdal betʼjeralda kwer ɬeze tsinɡi tʼuban ruχʼulel qʼurbanal qχoleb bakʼalda ɡʔjeb qχweze
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeɬul biduɬ kiliʃːɡi tʃːun ɡʔjeb bi baχina qʼurbanal tʼad ruχʼuleb qʼurban bakʼaɬul bokʼnazda tʃʼwaral ɬːurduzda wa χutʼarab bi qʼurban bakʼalda tsebe tʼjela
χadub kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeɬul tʼolabɡo tʼatʼi batʼa ɡʔabila raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe qχoleb tʃaqχdal ɡʔabulebɡo ɡʼadin tsinɡi ɡʔjeb tʼatʼi qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila betʼjerhanase ruχʼulel tsoɡidal tsʼadul qʼurbanazulɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjedin kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃijasdasa munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurban tʼobitʼila wa allaɡʔ ɡʔjesul munaɡʔalda tʼasa ɬuɡʔina

tso kinawaliɡo tʃi nuɡʼ χʼisabalda diwanχanajalde aχʼun wuɡoni wa bitʼarab ɡuroni bitsinarin ɡʔjedunɡi wukʼun χʼaqʼiqʼatalda ʒinda biχʔarabɡi raɡʼarabɡi ɡʔjes baχtʃun tani ɡʔjeɬuqχ ɡʔjew tʃi ʒawabalde tsʼaze kːola
jaɬuni pulanaw tʃi toχɬukʔje qχubab ʒojalda qχwani ʒanawaraɬul balkan bukʼa χwarab ruqʼaɬul χʼajwan bukʼa kinab bukʼaniɡi ʃuruleb ʒojaɬul balkan bukʼa ɬatʃʼoɡo qχwan wukʼun wataniɡi ɡʔjew qχubɬula wa ɡʔjesda ɡʼajib bukʼuna
jaɬuni pulanaw tʃi toχɬukʔje insanasul qχubɬijalda qχwani wa insan qχubɬizabuleb kinab bukʼaniɡi ʒojalda qχwanɡi wukʼun tsin ɡʔjeb ɡʔjesda ɬatʃʼoni amma χadub ɬani ɡʔjesda ɡʔjeɬul ɡʼajib bukʼuna
jaɬuni urʁitʃʼoɡo tʼasa masaɡo pulanaw tʃi ɡʔjedani ɬikʼab jaɡi kweʃab ʃːib bukʼaniɡi ɡʔabilin abun ɡʔjeb toχɬukʔje ɡʔjedarab ɡʔa bukʼun bataniɡi χadub ɡʔjeb ɡʔjesda bitʃʼtʃʼidal ɡʔjew ɡʼajibijaw wukʼuna
palχʼasil ɡʔjedinal ɡʼajibal kːaraw tʃi rakʼ raɡʔun mukʼurɬize kːola ʒinda pulanab ɡʼajib kːanin abun
ɡʔjedinaw tʃijas ʒinditsaɡo ɡʔaburab munaɡʔaɬuqχ ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze betʼjerhanasda tsebe tʃaqχu jaɬuni munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze tsʼtsʼje batʃun batʃʼine kːola tsinɡi kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew munaɡʔaldasa watsʼtsʼad ɡʔawila
tʃaqχu qχweze ɡʔjesul res batitʃʼoni bitʃːante ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo munaɡʔaɬuqχ betʼjerhanase kʼiɡo roχʔil mikːiɡi kʼiɡo mikːidul tʼintʃʼɡi batʃʼine tso munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe tso tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe
ɡʔjes ɡʔjel kaʃiʃasuqχe kʔjela kaʃiʃas tʼotsebe munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurban tʼobitʼila χʼantʃʼil betʼjer kʔurun bekizabila amma naqχe tʼjelaro
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeɬul bi punqχila qʼurban bakʼaɬul qʼadade wa χutʼarab bi qʼurban bakʼalda tsebe tʼjela ɡʔjeb buɡo munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurban

pulanaw tʃijasul res batitʃʼoni kʼiɡo roχʔil mikːiɡi kʼiɡo mikːidul tʼintʃʼɡi bosun batʃʼine ɡʔjedinaw tʃijas ʒindirɡo munaɡʔaɬuqχ kʔjeze kːola jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa χanʒdal amma zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʒubatʃʼoɡo ladanɡi tʼad ɬetʃʼoɡo ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurban buɡeɬul

ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi χadur reχsaral taqʼsirazul tsoniɡi ɡʔabuni ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda dande ɡʔaburab munaɡʔ kːola ʒindiqχe tsʼunize jaɡi qʼarzaɬe kʔurab ʒo kʔjetʃʼilan pulanaw tʃi tʃʼani jaɡi ɬilniɡi tso ʒo biqʼani jaɡi ɬiqχaniɡi χʼal ɡʔabun baqχani

ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazdaɡi abe ɡʔale tʼuban ruχʼulel qʼurbanazul qʼanun tʼuban buχʼize qχurab qʼurban sordo roɡʔineɡʼan qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼize kːola ɡʔjenib roɡʔineɡʼan tsʼa swine teze beɡʔularo
radal tʼad retʼun batsʼtsʼadab χʼjebtil partalɡun wa ɡʼawrat baχtʃuleb ʁorkʔan tʼaʒuɡun kaʃiʃas qʼurban bakʼalda tʼasa tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬul raqχu bakʼarila wa ɡʔjeb qʼurban bakʼalda askʼob ɡʼodob ɬela

nazrujaɬul jaɡi sunnatab qʼurban χʼisabalda raqʼlil qʼurban qχoleb buɡoni bitʃːante ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔan ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ kwanaze χutʼarab naqχiseb qʼojaɬɡi kwanaze beɡʔula
amma ɬababileb qʼojaɬɡi ɡʔan naqχe χutʼani ɡʔjeb buχʼize kːola
ɬababileb qʼojaɬɡi ɡʔjedinab raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔan kwani ɡʔjeb χʼaramɬula wa allaɡʔas ɡʔjeb qʼurban qʼabul ɡʔabularo ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb ɡʔan qχubɬun bukʼuna wa ɡʔjeb qχubab iʃ ɡʔaburaw tʃijase munaɡʔ bukʼuna
ʃːibɡʼaɡi qχubab ʒo qχwarab ɡʔanɡi qχubɬula ɡʔjeb kwanaze beɡʔularo buχʼize kːola qχubɬijalda qχwatʃʼjel ratsʼtsʼadal bokʔaral tʃaɡʼatsa kwanaze beɡʔula raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔan
amma qχubɬun wukʼinɡi ɬalaɡo betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo qχurab raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔan kwanaraw tʃi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qʼotʼize
insanasdasa batʃʼarab bukʼa χʼajwanaldasa batʃʼarab bukʼa qχubab ʒojalda qχwan jaɬuni kinab bukʼaniɡi qχubab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijalda qχwan ʒiw qχubɬun wukʼinɡi ɬalaɡo betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo qχurab raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔan kwanaraw tʃi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qʼotʼize kːola
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe botsʼul ɡʼijal wa tsʼanazul kinabɡʼaɡi tʼatʼi kwanaɡe
χwaral jaɬuni ɡʼalχul ʒanawaraɬ tʃʼwaral χʼajwanazul tʼatʼi χʼaltʼizabize beɡʔula bokʔarab bakʼalda amma kwanije χʼaltʼizabize beɡʔularo
betʼjerhanase tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanɬun qχurab χʼajwanaɬul tʼatʼi kwanaraw tʃi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qʼotʼize kːola
nuʒetsa kib ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb buɡoniɡi χʼajwanazul jaɡi χʼantʃʼazul bi kidaniɡi kwanije χʼaltʼizabuɡe
kwanije kinabɡʼaɡi bi χʼaltʼizabulew tʃi ɡʔjew ʃːiw wataniɡi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe watʃaqχize kːola
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe raqʼlil qʼurban qχolew tʃijas ɡʔjeɬul tso butʼa betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo χirijab sadaqʼaɬun kʔjeze kːola
ɡʔjes ʒinditsaɡo bosize kːola tsʼaduɬ buχʼize kːoleb butʼa qʼurban bakʼalda askʼobe aj betʼjerhanasda tsebe tʼatʼiɡi meɡʔjedɡi ɡʔjes betʼjerhanasda tsebe bosila χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurban χʼisabalda eχedeɡi borχun χʔwaɡʼjezabize
tʼatʼi kaʃiʃas qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila meɡʔjed ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul naslabazeɡi bukʼina
nuʒer raqʼlil qʼurbanazul kwaranab boχ kaʃiʃase kʔjeze kːola χirijab sadaqʼa χʼisabalda
raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬul biɡi tʼatʼiɡi qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad ʒintsa buχʼulew kaʃiʃase bukʼina ɡʔjeb boχ
ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼaɬuqχa ditsa tʼalab ɡʔarula ɡʔjezul raqʼlil qʼurbanazul χasal butʼabi χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurbanaɬul meɡʔjedɡi boχɡi wa ɡʔjel ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi kʔola ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼaɬ daim tʼubazabize kːola ɡʔjeb qʼanun
ɡʔjedinab buɡo betʼjerhanase ɡʔarulel qʼurbanazdasa ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul naslabazeɡi kːoleb butʼa betʼjerhanasul kaʃiʃzabiɬun ɡʔjel tʼamurab qʼojaldasa naqχe
χirijab naχɡi baχun ɡʔjel kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamurab qʼojaldasa naqχeɡo betʼjerhanas amru ɡʔabuna ɡʼizrailazde ɡʔjeb ɡʔjezije kʔjejan abadul abadijaɬ χisizabitʃʼoɡo tʼubazabize kːola ɡʔjeb amru
ɡʔjele qʼurbanazul qʼanun tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬulɡi roɬul χirijal sadaqʼabazulɡi munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬulɡi ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurbanaɬulɡi kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamijaɬul qʼurbanazulɡi raqʼlil qʼurbanazulɡi
sinaj salul awlaqχalda rukʼaɡo qʼurbanal qχwejan ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalde amru ɡʔaburab qʼojaɬ musaje ɡʔjel kinalɡo qʼanunalɡi zaɡʔir ɡʔaruna betʼjerhanas

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi aχʼje wa bose kaʃiʃɬijaɬul partalɡi baχuneb χirijab naχɡi munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze otsɡi kʼiɡo kujɡi buɡʔurɡo tʃadazul tʃʼjepɡi
ɡʼizrailazul tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼatɡi bakʼare dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsebe
musatsa kinabɡo betʼjerhanas maɬuqχe ɡʔabuna wa tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje χalqʼ bakʼaridal
musatsa abuna
ɡʔale betʼjerhanas dida tʼadqʼarab ʒo
tsinɡi ɡʔjes ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi tsere ratʃana wa ɡʔjezda ɬim baqχana
χadub ɡʔjes ɡʔarunida ɡurde retʼana ɡʔjelda tʼasan ratʃelɡi bana ɡurdida tʼasan riza retʼana ɡʔjeldaɡi tʼasan efod retʼana wa efodaɬul ratʃel buχʔana
ɡʔjedinɡo karanzul tsebebuχʔ retʼana wa ɡʔjenib urimɡi tummimɡi ɬuna
ɡʔarunil botʼroda χasab tʼaʁur ɬuna wa ɡʔjelda tʼasan nadalda mesedil tʼamatʃ aj χiraɬijaɬul taʒ rekʼinabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon
χadub musatsa χirijab naχ bosana wa ɡʔjeb punqχana muqʼadasab tʃadiraldeɡi ɡʔjelda ʒanib bukʼarabʃːinaldeɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo allaɡʔasul χiraɬiɬun bukʼin ɬazabize
musatsa χirijab naχ ankʔtsʼul punqχana qʼurban bakʼaldeɡi ɡʔjeɬul kinabɡo tsʼaraɡʼaldeɡi berkʼal tʃuruleb χʼjertʃaldeɡi ɡʔjeɬul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelaldeɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡoɡi allaɡʔasul χiraɬiɬun bukʼin ɬazabize
wa tsodaɡʔab χirijab naχ bosun ɡʔarunil botʼrode tʼuna ɡʔjewɡi allaɡʔas watʼa ɡʔawuraw wukʼin ɬazabize
χadub musatsa ɡʔarunil wasal aχʼana wa betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjezda kaʃiʃɬijaɬul ɡurdal retʼana ruχʔana ratʃelal wa botʼroda ɬuna χasal tʼaʁral
tsinɡi ɡʔjes tsebe batʃana munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe χʼadurarab ots ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi χʼajwanaɬul botʼroda kweral ɬuna
χadub ots qχuna wa ɡʔjeɬul biduɬ kiliʃːɡi tʃːun musatsa qʼurban bakʼaɬul bokʼnazda tʃʼwaral ɬːurduzda bi baχana qʼurban bakʼ batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabize χutʼarab bi ɡʔjes qʼurban bakʼalda tsebe tʼuna ɡʔjedin ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul nizamɡi tʼobitʼun qʼurban bakʼ allaɡʔasul χiraɬiɬun bukʼin ɬazabuna
musatsa otsol urɡʔimesaɬul kinabɡo tʼatʼi batʼa ɡʔabuna wa tʼulal χalaseb butʼaɡi urɡʔisalabiɡun wa ɡʔjezda swerun bukʼuneb tʼatʼiɡun tsadaqχ qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼana
qʼurbanaɬul tʼomɡi ɡʔanɡi urɡʔimesɡi χalqʼ reʃːtʼarab bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼibeχun buχʼana betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon
χadub tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qʼatʃʼarab kuj tsebe batʃana wa ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi ɡʔjeɬul botʼroda kweral ɬuna
ɡʔjeb qχun baqχindal musatsa ɡʔjeɬul bi punqχana qʼurban bakʼaɬul unqʼabɡo raqχalde
kujdul qʼulaɡʼi qʼotʼ qʼotʼana wa musatsa ɡʔjebɡi kujdul betʼjerɡi tʼatʼiɡi tsadaqχ buχʼana
ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔimesɡi χʼatʼalɡi ɬetsa tʃurana wa kujdul ʃːibniɡi ʒo naqχe tetʃʼoɡo musatsa ɡʔjebɡi qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼana betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjeb buɡo tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban kʼkʼujaldeɡi swerizabun allaɡʔase kʔoleb ɡʔuinab maχʼaɬul qʼurban
χadub kʼiabileb kuj tsebe batʃana kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe qχweze qʼatʃʼarab ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi ɡʔjeɬul botʼroda tsin kweral ɬuna
wa kuj qχuna musatsa ɡʔjeɬul tsodaɡʔab biɡi bosun ɡʔjeb baχana ɡʔarunil kwaranab ɡʼindaɡi kwaranab kweraɬul kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi kwaranab χʼatʼil kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi
χadub ɡʔarunil wasal tsere ratʃana wa musatsa bi baχana ɡʔjezul ʃːiwasul kwaranab ɡʼindaɡi kwaranab kweraɬul kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi kwaranab χʼatʼil kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi χutʼarab bi ɡʔjes qʼurban bakʼaɬul unqʼabɡo raqχalde punqχana
tsinɡi musatsa qʼurbanaɬul tʼatʼi batʼa ɡʔabuna moχmoχɡi urɡʔimesaɬul tʼatʼiɡi tʼulal χalaseb butʼaɡi tʼad tʼatʼiɡun urɡʔisalabiɡi ɡʔjedinɡo kujdul kwaranab boχɡi bosana
betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɬurab retʃːeb ɡʔjetʃʼjel tʃadazul tʃʼjepalda ʒanisa musatsa tso tʃedɡi tso naχuda butsarab tʃedɡi tso tʼjerenab bakariɡi bosana wa tʼatʼudaɡi kujdul kwaranab boχaldaɡi tʼad ɬuna
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔarunilɡi ɡʔjesul wasazulɡi kodobe kʔuna wa ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ musatsa ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda tsebe χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurban χʼisabalda eχede borχana
tsinɡi ɡʔjeb ɡʔarunil wa ɡʔjesul wasazul kodosaɡi bosun qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanalda tsadaqχ buχʼize ɬuna ɡʔjedinal rukʼana kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamijaɬul qʼurbanal tsʼadudaɬun betʼjerhanase χirijab ɡʔuinab maχʼ baqχinabulel χirijal sadaqʼabi
χadub musatsa kujdul meɡʔjed bosana wa eχedeɡi borχun χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurban χʼisabalda betʼjerhanasda tsebe χʔwaɡʼjezabuna betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjeb bukʼana kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamijaɬul qʼurbanaldasa musaje kːoleb butʼa
tsodaɡʔab χirijab naχɡi qʼurban bakʼalda bukʼarab biɡi bosun musatsa ɡʔjeb punqχana ɡʔarunideɡi ɡʔjesul partalaldeɡi wa ɡʔjesul wasazdeɡi ɡʔjezul partalaldeɡi ɡʔjedin ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul partalɡi wa ɡʔjesul wasalɡi ɡʔjezul partalɡi allaɡʔase ratʼa ɡʔarural rukʼin ɬazabuna
musatsa ɡʔarunida wa ɡʔjesul wasazda abuna ɡʔan beɬe dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa wa tʃʼjepalda ʒanisa tʃedɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjeb bakʼaldaɡo kwanaj ditsa nuʒede amru ɡʔabuna ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi kwanaze kːola ɡʔjeb in
naqχe χutʼarab ɡʔanɡi tʃedɡi nuʒetsa buχʼize kːola
dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼasa ankʔaɬ naqχe unɡe nuʒ kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamijaɬul zaman raɡʼalde ʃːwezeɡʼan ʃːajɡureɬul nuʒ kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼami ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ χalat baqχuna
ʒaqʼa niɬetsa ɡʔaburabʃːinab ʒo betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabuna nuʒ munaɡʔ χʼaqʼaldasa ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔarizeɬun
ankʔitsa dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa rukʼa qʼasiɡi qʼadɡi betʼjerhanase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadatɡi ɡʔabulaɡo nuʒɡo χwetʃʼoɡo rukʼine ɡʔjedinab amru batʃʼun buɡeɬul diqχe
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabuna kinabɡo

mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ musatsa ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi ɡʼizrailazul kʼudijalɡi aχʼana
musatsa ɡʔarunida abuna
munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze basiɡi bose tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze kujɡi bose ʃːibniɡi ɡʼuzru ʒideɬ ɡʔjetʃʼjel tʼasa riʃːun tsinɡi ɡʔjel betʼjerhanasda tsere ratʃe
ɡʼizrailazda abe munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze deɡʼjenɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze ɬaɡʼjel barab basiɡi kʔjeɡʼjerɡi batʃejan ʃːibɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ʒideɬ ɡʔjetʃʼjel
raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe betʼjerhanasda tsebe qχweze otsɡi kujɡi batʃejan abe zajtunaɬul naχ ʒubarab roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡun ʒaqʼa nuʒee betʼjerhanas ʒiwɡo zaɡʔirɬizawize wuɡo
musatsa bujurarabʃːinab dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje bosun batʃʼana χalqʼaɬ tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼatɡi ɡʔjenibe bakʼarana wa betʼjerhanasda tsebe baqχun tʃʼana
musatsa abuna
betʼjerhanas amru ɡʔabuna nuʒetsa ɡʔadin ɡʔabejan betʼjerhanasul qʼudrat nuʒee zaɡʔirɬize bukʼine
musatsa ɡʔarunida abuna
qʼurban bakʼalda askʼowe wiɬːa wa durɡo qʼurban qχwe munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬulɡi tʼuban buχʼulebɡi munɡoɡi χalqʼɡi munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔarize rukʼine χadub χalqʼaɬ ratʃʼaral qʼurbanalɡi tʼoritʼje betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon χalqʼ munaɡʔazdasa batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabize bukʼine
qʼurban bakʼalda askʼoweɡi wiɬːun ɡʔarunitsa ʒindirɡo basi qχuna munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurban χʼisabalda
ɡʔjesul wasaz qʼurbanaɬul bi kʔuna insuqχe wa ɡʔjes ɡʔjenib kiliʃːɡi tʃːun bi baχana qʼurban bakʼaɬul bokʼnazda tʃʼwaral ɬːurduzda χutʼarab bi qʼurban bakʼalda tsebe tʼuna
qʼurbanaɬul tʼatʼi ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔisalabi wa tʼulal χalaseb butʼa ɡʔarunitsa munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurban χʼisabalda qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼana betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon
ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔanɡi tʼomɡi ɡʔjes χalqʼaɬ ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼibeχun buχʼana
χadub ɡʔarunitsa tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban qχuna ɡʔjesul wasaz qʼurbanaɬul bi insuqχe kʔuna wa ɡʔjes ɡʔjeb bi qʼurban bakʼaɬul unqʼabɡo raqχalde punqχana
ɡʔarunil wasaz qʼurbanaɬul qʼotʼ qʼotʼarab qʼulaɡʼiɡi ɡʔjeɬul betʼjerɡi insuqχe kʔuna wa ɡʔjes ɡʔjeb qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼana
qʼurbanaɬul urɡʔimesɡi χʼatʼalɡi tʃurana wa ɡʔjebɡi kinaldaɡo tsadaqχ qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼana
χadub ɡʔjes χalqʼaɬ ratʃʼaral χʼajwanal qχuna tsin χalqʼaldasa deɡʼjen qχuna munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurban χʼisabalda wa tsebeχunɡo ɡʼadin munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul nizam tʼobitʼana
ɡʔjelda χadub tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban qχuna wa kinabɡo ɡʔabuna ɡʔjeɬije tʃʼjezaburab qʼaɡʼidajalda
roɡʔalil tsʼadul qʼurbanaɬe buχʼaralda tʼade roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬul tso danʁuraɡi bosana wa ɡʔjebɡi qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼana
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔarunitsa χalqʼaldasa raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe otsɡi kujɡi qχuna ɡʔjesul wasaz qʼurbanazul bi kʔuna insuqχe wa ɡʔjes ɡʔjeb qʼurban bakʼaɬul unqʼabɡo raqχalde punqχana
otsolɡi kujdulɡi tʼatʼi aj moχmoχɡi urɡʔimesaɬul tʼatʼiɡi urɡʔisalabiɡi tʼulal χalaseb butʼaɡi
ɡʔjes qʼurbanazul kʼijabɡo meɡʔjedalda tʼad ɬuna wa kinabɡo tʼatʼi qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼana
meɡʔjedɡi kwaranab boχɡi χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurban χʼisabalda ɡʔjes betʼjerhanasda tsebe eχede borχana musatsa maɬarab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ
tʼolalɡo qʼurbanal tʼoritʼun raqχindal munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬulɡi tʼuran ruχʼulelɡi raqʼlilɡi ɡʔarunitsa kweralɡi eχede rorχun χalqʼaɬe duɡʼa ɡʔabuna wa qʼurban bakʼaldasa ʁorkʔje reʃːtʼana
tsinɡi musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda ʒanire ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjenisa qʼwatʼire ratʃʼindal ɡʔjez naqχeɡi χalqʼaɬe duɡʼa ɡʔabuna ɡʔjebmeχaɬ χalqʼaɬeɡo betʼjerhanasul qʼudrat zaɡʔirɬana
betʼjerhanasul tsʼa reʃːtʼana wa qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad bukʼarab qʼurbanɡi tʼatʼiɡi ɡʔjeb tsʼadutsa tʼuban buχʼana ɡʔjeb biχʔarabɡo kʼudijab roχalil ɡʔarakʔɡi ɡʔabun tʼolabɡo χalqʼ suʒdajalda kːana

ɡʔarunil wasal nadawitsaɡi awiɡʔutsaɡi ʒindi ʒindir ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼuleb ʃːurun bosana amma ɡʔjenib ʒanib betʼjerhanas biχʔizabitʃʼjeb batʼijab tsʼa ɬuna tʼade maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubajɡi bana wa ɡʔjeb ɡʔjesda tsebe bosana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanasul tsʼa reʃːtʼana wa tso parajalda ʒanir ɡʔjeb tsʼajaɬ ruχʼana ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo betʼjerhanasda tsere χwana
ɡʔjeb biχʔidal musatsa ɡʔarunida abuna
ɡʔale betʼjerhanas abun bukʼarab
dide ɡʼaɡarɬulezda
ditsa dirɡo tʼadeɡʼanab batsʼtsʼaɬi biχʔizabila
tʼolabɡo χalqʼalda tsebe
dirɡo qʼudrat zaɡʔir ɡʔabila jan
ɡʔarun siχʼqʼotʼun tʃʼana
musatsa ɡʔarunil insul wats ɡʼuzielil wasal miʃaelɡi eltsafanɡi aχʼana wa ɡʔjezda abuna
askʼoreɡʼan ratʃʼa wa nuʒerɡo ɡʼaɡaral tʃaɡʼazul ʒanazabi ɡʔanisa naqχeɡi rosun χalqʼaɬ ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼire ʃːwezare
ɡʔjezda tʼad bukʼarab kaʃiʃzabazul retʼjelɡi kːun ɡʔjez musatsa abuqχe ʒanazabi χalqʼaldasa rikʼkʼadeɡʼan ʃːwezaruna
tsinɡi musatsa ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasal eleazaridaɡi itamaridaɡi abuna
χwaraze ɡʼolojan ja tʼaʁral raqχuɡe ja retʼjel biqχ biqχuɡe ɡuroni nuʒɡi χweze ruɡo tsinɡi ɡʼizrailil tʼolabɡo χalqʼaldeɡi betʼjerhanasul tsːin reʃːtʼine buɡo betʼjerhanas ruχʼun χwarazda χadub maɡʼu baqχize bitʃːante nuʒer ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬɡi tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazɡi
nuʒin abuni dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼasa kireɡo unɡe nuʒɡo χwetʃʼoɡo rukʼine ʃːajɡureɬul nuʒ betʼjerhanasul χirijab naχ baχaral tʃaɡʼi ruɡeɬul
ɡʔjez musatsa maɬarab ɡʔabuna
betʼjerhanas ɡʔarunida abuna
dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda ʒanire ɬuɡʔinalda tsebe dutsaɡi dur wasazɡi tʃaʁir jaɡi batʼijab meχtizabuleb ʒo ɡʔjeqʼoɡe nuʒɡo χwetʃʼoɡo rukʼine ɡʔjeb bukʼina nuʒee abadijab wa χisulareb qʼanunɬun
χirijabɡi ɡʼadatijabɡi batsʼtsʼadabɡi qχubabɡi nuʒeda batʼa baqχun baʒarize bukʼinaɬe
wa musadasan betʼjerhanas kʔural qʼanunal nuʒetsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda maɬize rukʼinaɬe ɡʼolo
musatsa abuna ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjesul naqχe χutʼaral wasal eleazaridaɡi itamaridaɡi
betʼjerhanase ratʃʼaral roɬul χirijal sadaqʼabazul naqχe χutʼarab bose wa ɡʔjeɬul buɡʔurɡo tʃadalɡi reʒun ɡʔjeb qʼurban bakʼalda askʼob kwanaj ɡʔjeb kʼudijab χiraɬi kːoleɬul
nuʒetsa χirijab bakʼalda kwanaze kːola ɡʔjeb ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanasul tsʼadul sadaqʼabazdasa dujeɡi dur wasazeɡi kːoleb butʼa ɡʔjedinab amru batʃʼana diqχe
χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurbanaɬul meɡʔjedɡi ɡʔjedinɡo betʼjerhanase χasab qʼurbanɬun kːoleb boχɡi ɡʔjeb kwanaze beɡʔula dur wasazɡi jasazɡi bokʔarab batsʼtsʼadab bakʼalda ɡʔjeb kːola ɡʼizrailazul tʼolalɡo raqʼlil qʼurbanazul nuʒeeɡi nuʒer ɬimalazeɡi kːoleb butʼa
tʼatʼiɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjez kʔjeze kːola χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurbanaɬe meɡʔjedɡi χasab qʼurbanaɬe boχɡi dutsa betʼjerhanasda tsere rosize rukʼine betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo durɡi dur ɬimalazulɡi kidaɡoseb butʼa ɡʔjedinab amru batʃʼana diqχe
musa ɬuɡʔana munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe χʼadurarab deɡʼjen balaɡʔize amma ɡʔjeb tsebeɡo buχʼun batana ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musal kutakalda tsːin baqχana wa ɡʔarunil χutʼaral wasal eleazaridaɡi itamaridaɡi ɡʔjes abuna
ʃːaj nuʒetsa munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔan χirijab bakʼalda kwanatʃʼjeb ɡʔjeb kʼudijab χiraɬi ɡurebiʃː nuʒee ɡurebiʃː ɡʔjeb kʔun buɡeb nuʒetsa betʼjerhanasda tsebe χalqʼ batsʼtsʼaɬizabuleb qʼurban tʼobitʼijaɬe ɡʼolo
ɡʔjeɬul biɡi muqʼadasab bakʼalde bosun bukʼintʃʼjeb meχaɬ nuʒetsa ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔan kwanaze kːolaan ditsa aburabɡi ɡʔabun
ɡʔarunitsa musada abuna
ʒaqʼa betʼjerhanase munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanɡi qχuna amma χadub niʒee ɬuɡʔarab ʒo dudaɡo ɬala ʒaqʼaɡo ditsa munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔan kwanan bukʼarabani betʼjerhanase qʼabulɬilaaniʃːχa ɡʔjeb
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musa ɡʔjesul raɡʼuda tʼadreqʼana

betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
ɡʼizrailazda abe dunjalaɬulɡo χʼajwanazda ɡʔorkʔosa ɡʔale nuʒetsa ɡʔan kwanaze beɡʔulel χʼajwanal
nuʒee batsʼtsʼadabɬun buɡo ʃːinkʼilɡi kʼikʼwekʔab wa tʃʼamun laɡʼɡi reχuleb bokʔarab χʼajwanaɬul ɡʔan
amma ʃːinkʼilɡi kʼikʼwekʔab ɡʔjetʃʼoni tʃʼamun laɡʼɡi reχuleb ɡʔjetʃʼoni ɡʔjedinal χʼajwanazul ɡʔan nuʒee ɡʔuqʼarab buɡo waranidul ɡʔan kwanaɡe ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeɬ tʃʼamun laɡʼ reχula amma ɡʔjeɬul ʃːinkʼil kʼikʼwekʔab ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjeb nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo
damanaɬul ɡʔanɡi kwanaɡe ɡʔjeɬ tʃʼamun laɡʼ reχula amma ɡʔjeɬul maɬ kʼikʼwekʔab ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjebɡi nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʼankʼɡi ɡʔjeɬɡi tʃʼamun raɡʼ reχula amma ɡʔjeɬul maɬ kʼikʼwekʔab ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjebɡi nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo
boɬonaɬul ʃːinkʼil kʼikʼwekʔab buɡo amma ɡʔjeɬ tʃʼamun laɡʼ reχularo ɡʔjebɡi nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo
ɡʔjel χʼajwanazul ɡʔan kwanaɡe wa ɡʔjezul balkanazdaɡi qχwaɡe ɡʔjel nuʒee qχubal ruɡo
ɬadaɬ rukʼunel ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬabazda ɡʔorkʔosa ɡʔjel ɡʼurul rukʼa raɬdal rukʼa nuʒetsa kwanaze beɡʔula ʁataχarab qχalɡi ɬedoleb kwatʃʼɡi buɡeb tʃːuɡʼa
amma ʁataχarab qχalɡi ɬedoleb kwatʃʼɡi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb raɬdal jaɡi ɡʼurul bokʔarab ɡʼisi biqʼinab wa tsoɡi batʼijab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo
ɡʔjel kutakalda qχubal ʒalɬun rikʼkʼje ɡʔjezul ɡʔan kwanaɡe ɡʔjezul balkanazdaɡi qχwaɡe
kinabniɡi ʒinda ʁataχarab qχalɡi ɬedoleb kwatʃʼɡi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ɬadaɬ bukʼuneb ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo
χʼantʃʼazda ɡʔorkʔosa nuʒee qχubalɬun kːola wa nuʒetsa kwanaze beɡʔularo tsʼum qχwek qχerʁu
qχartʃiʁa lutʃnuzul kinabniɡi tajpa
ʁuduzul kinabniɡi tajpa
waraniχʼintʃʼ betsːaruz tʃajka qχartʃiʁabazul kinabniɡi tajpa
ɡʔitʼinal betsːaruzal keturuz baklan ibis
pelikan sip tʃuduk
laqʼlaqʼ χʔutsʼilqχazazul kinabniɡi tajpa ɡʔudɡʔud wa ɡʼunkʼkʼχʼintʃʼ
borʒuneb unqʼɡo kwatʃʼɡi buɡeb kinabniɡi ɡʼisi biqʼinab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi nuʒee qχubabɬun kːola
amma ɡʔjedinazda ɡʔorkʔosa nuʒetsa kwanaze beɡʔula unqʼχʼatʼida kʼantsʼulel ʒal
nuʒetsa kwanaze beɡʔula kinabniɡi tajpajaɬul raqʼul ɡartsʼ akridal swertʃokal wa ɡʼisinab ɡartsʼ
amma χutʼarab borʒanqχizeɡi baʒaruleb rakʔaldasanɡi ʃuruleb kinabniɡi unqʼχʼatʼilab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo
ɡʔjedinab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi sababɬun nuʒ qχubɬula ɡʔjeb tajpajaɬul tsoniɡi χwarab ʒojalda qχwaraw tʃi baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan qχubɬun wukʼuna
ɡʔjeb kodobe bosaraw tʃijas retʼjel tʃurize kːola wa baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan ɡʔjew qχubɬun wukʼuna
ʃːankʼlal kʼikʼwekʔal amma tʃʼamun laɡʼ reχulareb kinabniɡi χʼajwan nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo ɡʔjezda qχwaraw tʃi qχubɬula
unqʼɡo kwatʃʼida biɬːuneb kinabniɡi χʼajwan nuʒee qχubab kːola ɡʔjezul balkanalda qχwaraw tʃi qʼasiɬizeɡʼan qχubɬun wukʼuna
ɡʔjezul balkanalda qχwaraw tʃijas retʼjel tʃurize kːola wa markʼatʃʼumeχ ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjew qχubɬun wukʼuna ɡʔjel kinalɡo χʼajwanal nuʒee qχubalɬun kːola
rakʔaldasan ʃurulel ɡʼisinal ʒalazul nuʒee qχubalɬun kːola betsːaɡʼunkʼkʼ ɡʼunkʼkʼ kʔintʃːazul kinabniɡi tajpa
ɡekːon waran qʼadakʔ bukʼuneb tʃːut stsink wa χameleon
rakʔaldasan ʃurulel kinalniɡi ʒalazda ɡʔorkʔor ɡʔjel kːola nuʒee qχubalɬun ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔosa tsoniɡi χwarab ʒojalda qχwaraw tʃi baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan qχubawɬun wukʼuna
ɡʔjeb tʼade bortarab ʒoɡi qχubɬula tsʼulal tsʼaraɡʼ bukʼa retʼjel bukʼa qʼoχʔol jaɬuni χʼjebtil ɡʔaburab bokʔarab ʒo bukʼa ʃːib bataniɡi ɡʔjeb ɬadaɬ ɬeze kːola qʼasiɬizeɡʼan ɡʔjeb qχubɡo bukʼina χadub batsʼtsʼaɬila
ɡʔjedinab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi ʃːaɡʼil qχabinibe kːani qχabinib ʒanib buɡebʃːinabɡi qχubɬula qχabaɡi bekize kːola
ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjedinab qχabida ʒanisa ɬim χʼaltʼizabun ɡʔaburab kwenɡi qχubɬula ɡʔjenibe ʒanibe tʼurab kinab bataniɡi ɡʔjeqʼoleb ʒoɡi qχubɬula
ɡʔjedinab χwarab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi tʼade kːarab kinabniɡi ʒo qχubɬula ɡʔjedinab qχubɬi kːani tsʼa bakuleb bakʼtsin jaɬuni korɡitsin biχːizabize kːola ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjel nuʒee qχubalɬun ɬuɡʔuna
ɡʼitsʼɡo tʃwaχuleb ɬim jaɡi ɬadal χʼawuz batsʼtsʼadabɬun χutʼula amma ɡʔjeb ɬadaɬe kːarab χwarab ʒojalda qχwaraw tʃi qχubɬula
χurib χʔaze χʼadurarab χʔonalda tʼade qχubab wa χwarab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi kːani ɡʔjeb χʔon batsʼtsʼadabɬun χutʼula
amma ɬadaɬe barab χʔonalda tʼade ɡʔjeb kːani χʔon qχubɬula
kwanije χʼalalab χʼajwan χwani ɡʔjeɬul balkanalda qχwarawʃːinaw tʃi baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan qχubɬun wukʼuna
ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔan kwaraw tʃijas retʼjel tʃurize kːola wa qʼasiɬizeɡʼan qχubɬun wukʼuna ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔjeb balkan qʼwatʼibe batʃːaraw tʃijasɡi retʼjel tʃurize kːola wa ɡʔjewɡi baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan qχubɬun wukʼuna
rakʔaldasan ʃuruleb kinabniɡi ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo ɡʔjeb kwanaze beɡʔularo
nuʒetsa kwanaɡe tʃeχʔalda jaɡi unqʼabɡo kwatʃʼida ʃuruleb kinabniɡi ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi azarχʼatʼal jaɬuni tsoɡi kinab bataniɡi χʼutʼ qχumur ɡʔjeb kinabɡo nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo
ɡʔjedinal ʒalazdaɬun nuʒɡo tʃorok ɡʔaruɡe ɡʔjel sababɬun nuʒɡo qχubɬizaruɡe
ʃːajɡureɬul dun wuɡo nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ ratsʼtsʼadɡo χʔwade wa nuʒɡo ratsʼtsʼad tsʼune dun watsʼtsʼadaw wuɡeɬul ɡʔjeb rakʔaldasan ʃuruleb ɡʼisinab χʼutʼ qχumur sababɬun nuʒɡo qχubɬize toɡe
dun wuɡo dirɡo χalqʼɬun ɡʔarijaɬe ɡʼolo nuʒ misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃaraw betʼjerhan ɡʔjedinɬidal nuʒ ratsʼtsʼadalɬun rukʼa dun watsʼtsʼadaw wuɡeɬul
ɡʔjedinab buɡo ʒanawarazulɡun ɡʼi botsʼul χʼantʃʼazul tʼolabɡo ɬadaɬ bukʼuneb ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijaɬul wa rakʔaldasan ʃurulel ʒalazul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ qʼanun
nuʒeda batʼa baqχize ɬaze kːola qχubabɡi batsʼtsʼadabɡi kwanaze beɡʔulebɡi beɡʔularebɡi

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ was ɬimer ɡʔabuni ɡʔjeldasa χadub ɡʔjej ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ qχubɬun jikʼuna χʼajizaɬul qʼojazɡo ɡʼadin
mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ wasase sunnat ɡʔabize kːola
ɡʔjej tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan ɬeberalda ɬabɡo qʼojaɬ roqʼosa qʼwatʼije jaqχine beɡʔularo ɡʼuzrujaldasa jatsʼtsʼaɬizeɡʼan tʼujan jatsʼtsʼaɬizeɡʼan ɡʔjej χirijal ʒalazda qχwaze jaɡi muqʼadasab tʃadiralde ɡʼaɡarɬize beɡʔularo
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ jas ɬimer ɡʔabuni ɡʔjej kʼiɡo ankʔaɬ qχubɬun jikʼuna χʼajizaɬul qʼojazɡo ɡʼadin wa ɬabqʼojalda anɬɡo qʼojaɬ qʼwatʼije jaqχine beɡʔularo ɡʼuzrujaldasa jatsʼtsʼaɬizeɡʼan
ɬimer ɡʔabun χadub jatsʼtsʼaɬijaɬe tʃʼjezarural qʼojal indal ɡʔjej tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje jatʃʼine kːola wa tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe roχʔil mikːiɡi jaɬuni mikːidul tʼintʃʼɡi kaʃiʃasuqχe kʔjeze kːola
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas betʼjerhanasda tsere ɡʔjel qʼurbanal tʼoritʼize ɡʔjej ɡʼadan jatsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul muradalda tsinɡi ɡʔjej ɡʼuzrujaldasa jatsʼtsʼaɬarajɬun ɬuɡʔuna ɡʔjele ɬimer ɡʔaburaj tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬul raqχaɬ qʼanun
kʔjeɡʼjer qʼurbanaɬe kʔjeze ɡʔjeɬul res batitʃʼoni bitʃːante ɡʔjeɬ kʼiɡo roχʔil mikːi jaɬuni kʼiɡo mikːidul tʼintʃʼ batʃʼine tso tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe tso munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe bitʃːante kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeɬije ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul qʼurban tʼobitʼize tsinɡi ɡʔjej jatsʼtsʼadajɬun ɬuɡʔuna

betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
insanasul tʼomalda kib bukʼaniɡi ɡʔoroj bakːani jaɡi tʼade ʒo bani jaɡi tʼankʼal rakːani wa ɡʔjeb barasaɬul unti bukʼinalda χʼinqʼi buɡoni ɡʔjew tʃi kaʃiʃ ɡʔaruniqχe jaɬuni ɡʔjesul wasazuqχe watʃine kːola
kaʃiʃas untarab bakʼaɬul χal ʃal ɡʔabila ɡʔjeb bakʼalda biʒarab ras qχaχʼɬun batani wa untarab bakʼalda ɡwend ɬuɡʔun batani ɡʔjebmeχalda ɡʔjeb baras unti
insanasul tʃerχalda qχaχʼab tʼankʼ bakːani amma ɡʔjenib ɡwend ɬuɡʔun batitʃʼoni ɡʔjelda tʼad rasɡi qχaχʼɬun ɡʔjetʃʼoni kaʃiʃas ɡʔjedinaw tʃi ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʼadamazdasa watʼa ɡʔawun tʃʼjezawize kːola
ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ kaʃiʃas naqχeɡi untarasul χal ʃal ɡʔabila wa untarab bakʼaɬul kʔjer χisun ɡʔjetʃʼoni tʼankʼ raqχ raqχalde tʼibitʼunɡi batitʃʼoni kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi ʒeɡi ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʼadamazdasa watʼa tʃʼjezawila
naqχeɡi ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjesul χal ʃal ɡʔabila wa ɡʔjeb tʼankʼaɬul kʔjer χisun bukʼin wa ɡʔjeb tʼomalda tʼibitʼuleb ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi biχʔani kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi watsʼtsʼadaw wuɡilan ɬazabize kːola ɡʔjeb buɡo ɡʼadatijab sus bitʃːante ɡʔjew tʃijas retʼjel tʃurize wa ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼaɬula
ɡʔjeldasa χadubɡi tʃerχalda tsʼijal tʼankʼal rakːani ɡʔjew tʃi naqχeɡi kaʃiʃasda wiχʔize ine kːola
kaʃiʃasda biχʔani sus tʃerχalda tʼibitʼuleb bukʼin ɡʔjew tʃi qχubaw wuɡilan ɬazabize kːola ɡʔjeb barasaɬul unti buɡo
barasaɬul unti kːaraw tʃi kaʃiʃasuqχe watʃine kːola
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjesul χal ʃal ɡʔabila wa tʼomalda ɡʔororab qχaχʼab bakʼ batani ɡʔjenib rasɡi qχaχʼɬun raɡʔaral ruʁnalɡi ɬuɡʔun ruɡoni
ɡʔjeb buɡo basrijab barasaɬul unti kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi qχubaw wuɡilan ɬazabize kːola χʼal biχʔizeɬun daɡʔal qʼojaz watʼa tʃʼjezawize kːolaro ɡʔjew rakʼtʃʼun qχubawɬun wukʼuna
baras tʃerχaldaɡo tʼibitʼani wa kaʃiʃasda biχʔulebʃːinab bakʼaldasa ɡʔjesul tʼom barasaɬ baχtʃun buɡoni
wa kaʃiʃasda biχʔani ɡʔjew tʼankʼ χutʼitʃʼoɡo barasaɬ qχaχʼɬun wukʼin ɡʔjebmeχaɬ kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi watsʼtsʼadaw wuɡilan ɬazabize kːola tʼuwanɡo qχaχʼɬaraw tʃi watsʼtsʼadaw kːola
amma raɡʔaral ruʁnal ɬuɡʔarab saɡʼatalda ɡʔjew tʃi qχubawɬun kːola
raɡʔaral ruʁnal ɬuɡʔun rukʼin biχʔarabɡo kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi qχubaw wukʼin ɬazabize kːola ʃːajɡureɬul raɡʔarab ruʁun qχubɬi kːola ɡʔjeb buɡo baras unti
amma raɡʔarab ruʁun naqχeɡi qχaχʼɬani witʃːante ɡʔjew tʃi tsʼidasan kaʃiʃasuqχe watʃʼine
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjesul χal ʃal ɡʔabila ruʁnal rutsʼtsʼun wa qχaχʼɬun rukʼin biχʔani kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼadaw wuɡilan ɬazabila

amma ɡʔjesul ruʁun bukʼarab bakʼalda ras qχaχʼɬun batitʃʼoni ɡwendɡi ɬuɡʔun ɡʔjetʃʼoni ɡʔjeɬul kʔjerɡi χisun buɡoni bitʃːante kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʼadamazdasa watʼa tʃʼjezawize
amma qχaχʼab tʼankʼ kʼodoɬuleb buɡoni kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi qχubaw wuɡilan ɬazabize kːola ɡʔjeb buɡo kweʃab baχuneb unti
qχaχʼab tʼankʼ χisulebɡi kʼodoɬulebɡi ɡʔjetʃʼoni tsebe bukʼarab ruʁunaɬul ɡʼuʒ bukʼuna ɡʔjeb ɡʔjedinɬidal kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi watsʼtsʼadaw wuɡilan ɬazabize kːola

amma qχaχʼab tʼankʼ χisitʃʼoɡo buɡoni ɡʔjeb tʼomalda tʼibitʼulebɡi ɡʔjetʃʼoni kʔjerɡi χisun buɡoni ɡʔjeb kːola buχʼun bukʼinaɬ ɡʔororab bakʼ kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi watsʼtsʼadaw wuɡilan ɬazabize kːola buχʼarab bakʼalda χutʼarab ɡʼuʒ tun batʼijab ʒo ɡureɬul ɡʔjeb
naɡaɡʔ biχʔintʃijasul jaɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬul botʼroda jaɬuni niɬalda tʼjeχʼ bani

bitʃːante ɡʔjew tʃijas ras kʼkʼwaze ɡʼitsʼɡo untaral bakʼalɡi ʒalɡo tun tsinɡi kaʃiʃas ʒeɡi ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ watʼa tʃʼjezawila ɡʔjew
ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ kaʃiʃas tʼjeχʼ barab bakʼaɬul naqχeɡi χal ʃal ɡʔabila wa ɡʔjeb kʼodoɬunɡi ʁwariɬunɡi ɡʔjetʃʼjebɬi biχʔani kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi watsʼtsʼadaw wuɡilan ɬazabila ɡʔjew tʃijas retʼjel tʃurila wa ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼadaw wukʼina

amma tʃurun χadub χːamil wa qʼoχʔol ʒojaldasa kːal tʼasa ani ɡʔjeb kʼiabileb nuχaɬɡi tʃurila wa χadub batsʼtsʼadabɬun ɬuɡʔina
