betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔale barasaɬ untunɡi wukʼun saχɬaraw tʃijas ʒiwɡo watsʼtsʼaɬize ɡʼolo ɡʔabize kːoleb ʒo ɡʔjedinaw tʃi kaʃiʃasuqχe watʃine kːola
χalqʼaɬ ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bakʼaldasa aj rosuɬa jaɡi ʃaɡʔaraldasa qʼwatʼiwe ine kːola kaʃiʃ ɡʔjew wiχʔize kaʃiʃasda ɡʔjew tʃi barasaldasa saχɬun wukʼin biχʔani
kaʃiʃas ɬazabize kːola ɡʔjew tʃijase kʼiɡo χʼalalab χʼintʃʼɡi tso kedraɬul qχwalχʔjenɡi baɡʼarab kwasul kunɡi isːopaɬul kwatsʼiɡi bosun batʃʼajan
kaʃiʃas tsojab χʼintʃʼ qχwezabize kːola itsːuqχa ɬadal tsʼurab ʃːaɡʼil qχabajalda tʼadeɡi kːun
χadub kaʃiʃas bosila tʃʼaɡojab χʼintʃʼɡi kedraɬul tso qχwalχʔjenɡi baɡʼarab kwasul kunɡi isːopaɬul kwatsʼiɡi wa itsːuqχa ɬimɡun ʒubarab χʼintʃʼaɬul biduɬ tʃːula ɡʔjeb kinabɡo
χadub kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeb bi punqχize kːola barasaɬ untun wukʼaraw tʃijasde ankʔɡo nuχaɬ wa ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼaɬun wuɡilan ɬazabize kːola tʃʼaɡojab χʼintʃʼ ɡʼatʼidab awlaqχaldeɡi bosun ɡʔjenib bitʃːan teze kːola
χadub ɡʔjew tʃijas ʒindirɡo retʼjelɡi tʃurila tʼolabɡo rasɡi kʼkʼwala tʃerχɡi tʃurila tsinɡi ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼadawɬun wukʼina ɡʔjeldasa χadub ɡʔjew χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔowe ine beɡʔula amma ʒeɡi ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ʒindirɡo tʃadiralda ʒaniwe ɬuɡʔine beɡʔularo
ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjes naqχeɡi tʼolabɡo ras kʼkʼwala aj betʼjerɡi miqχ meɡeʒɡi kʔunsrulɡi wa tʃurila retʼjelɡi tʃerχɡi ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼaɬila
mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjes qʼurbanaɬe qχweze kʼiɡo biχʔinab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi tso tsʼujab ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi batʃʼine kːola ʃːibɡo ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjel tʼasa riʃːun ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬe batʃʼine kːola jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun ɬabɡo butʼa χanʒdal zajtunaɬul naχɡi tʼade tʼun ɡʔjedinɡo tso loɡ
bitʃːante ɡʔjesul raqχaɬ ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul qʼurban tʼobitʼulew kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi ɡʔjesul qʼurban sadaqʼaɡun tsadaqχ betʼjerhanasul dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsewe waqχun tʃʼjezawize
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas tso biχʔinab kʔjeɡʼjer ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurbanɬun ɡʔabize ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ tso loɡ tsʼurab zajtunaɬul naχɡi ɬun ɡʔjes ɡʔjeb eχedeɡi borχun betʼjerhanasda tsebe χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurban χʼisabalda χʔwaɡʼjezabila
kʔjeɡʼjer qχweze kːola munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬulɡi tʼuban buχʼulebɡi qʼurban qχoleb bakʼalda aj muqʼadasab bakʼalda munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬulɡo ɡʼadin ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔanɡi kaʃiʃase bukʼuna ɡʔjeb kutakalda χirijab ʒo kːola
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurbanaɬul bi bosize wa ɡʔjeb baχine watsʼtsʼad ɡʔawulew tʃijasul kwaranab ɡʼindaɡi kwaranab kweraɬul kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi kwaranab χʼatʼil kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi
χadub kaʃiʃas zajtunaɬul naχ bosila wa kweɡʼab qχatinibe tʼjela
ɡʔjelda ʒanib kwaranab kweraɬul surtʼinkiliʃːɡi tʃːun ɡʔjeb naχ ankʔtsʼul punqχila betʼjerhanasda tsebe aj tʃadiraldeχun balaɡʔizabun
qχatinib χutʼarab naχ baχine kːola watsʼtsʼad ɡʔawulew tʃijasul kwaranab ɡʼindaɡi kwaranab kweraɬul kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi kwaranab χʼatʼil kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi ɡʼajib batsʼtsʼuneb bi baχarab bakʼalda tʼasan
χutʼarab naχ kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃijasul betʼjeralde tʼjeze kːola ɡʔjedin tʼobitʼila kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃijase ratsʼtsʼaɬizaruleb nizam
bitʃːante χadub kaʃiʃas munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurban tʼobitʼize ɡʔjew qχubɬijaldasa watsʼtsʼad ɡʔawizeɬun ɡʔjeldasa χadub tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban qχweze kːola
tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanɡi roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi kaʃiʃas qʼurban bakʼalda tʼade bosila ɡʔjedin watsʼtsʼad ɡʔawila kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi wa ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼaɬila
amma ɡʔjew resuqʼaw tʃi watani wa ɡʔjedinal qʼurbanal qχweze ɡʔjesul res batitʃʼoni ɡʔjes ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze tso biχʔinab kʔjeɡʼjer batʃʼani ɡʼola ɡʔjebɡo bukʼina χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurbanɬunɡi kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi watsʼtsʼad ɡʔawize wukʼinaɬe ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬe batʃʼina jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa
kʼiɡo roχʔil mikːi jaɬuni kʼiɡo mikːidul tʼintʃʼ ɡʔjesul resaɬuqχ balaɡʔun tso χʼintʃʼ munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe bukʼina kʼiabileb χʼintʃʼ tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe
bitʃːante ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul qʼojazul mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeb kinabɡoɡi tsadaqχ bosun ɡʔjew tʃi kaʃiʃasuqχe watʃʼine wa dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa betʼjerhanasda tsewe tʃʼjeze
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas bosize ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze batʃʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi zajtunaɬul naχɡi wa χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurban χʼisabalda ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda tsebe eχede borχize
tsinɡi qʼurban qχwela wa kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeɬul bi baχina watsʼtsʼad ɡʔawulew tʃijasul kwaranab ɡʼindaɡi kwaranab kweraɬul kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi kwaranab χʼatʼil kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi
χadub kaʃiʃas zajtunaɬul naχ bosila wa ʒindirɡo kweɡʼab qχatinibe tʼjela
ɡʔjelda ʒanib kwaranab kweraɬul surtʼinkiliʃːɡi tʃːun ɡʔjeb naχ ankʔtsʼul punqχila betʼjerhanasda tsebe
χadub zajtunaɬul naχ baχine kːola watsʼtsʼad ɡʔawulew tʃijasul kwaranab ɡʼindaɡi kwaranab kweraɬul kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi kwaranab χʼatʼil kʼudijab kilʃːidaɡi ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurbanaɬul bi baχarab bakʼalda tʼasan
qχatinib χutʼarab naχ kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃijasul betʼjeralde tʼjeze kːola ɡʔjedin tʼobitʼila kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃijase ratsʼtsʼaɬizaruleb nizam
bitʃːante χadub ɡʔjes χʼantʃʼi qʼurban ɡʔarize roχʔil makːal jaɬuni mikːidul tʼantʃʼi ɡʔjesul resalda reqʼon
tsojab munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe tsoɡidab tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe ɡʔjedin watsʼtsʼad ɡʔawila kaʃiʃas ɡʔjew tʃi betʼjerhanasda tsewe
ɡʔale barasaɬul untudasa saχɬaral tʃaɡʼi ratsʼtsʼaɬizarijaɬe qχwaral qʼanunal wa ɡʔjedinɡo resuqʼal tʃaɡʼaze tʃʼjezarural qʼanunal
betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
nuʒ ditsa nuʒee kʔurab χanaanaɬul rakʔalde ɬuɡʔindal wa ditsa nuʒer ɬil bukʼaniɡi minajalde kːal bitʃːajdal
minajaɬul χwaʒain kaʃiʃasuqχe ine kːola wa ɡʔjes abize kːola dir minajalda ʒanir kːalaɬul ɡʼadinal tʼankʼal ɬuɡʔun ruɡo jan
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeniwe watʃʼinalda tsebe minajalda ʒanib buɡebʃːinab qʼaji tsʼa qʼwatʼibe bosejan ɬazabize ɡʔjeb kinabɡoɡi qχubabɬun ɬazabize kːetʃʼoɡo bukʼine ɡʔjeldasa χadub kaʃiʃ watʃʼina wa minajaɬul χal ʃal ɡʔabila
ɡʔjew balaɡʔila qʼadazda ɬuɡʔaral tʼankʼazuqχ ɡʔjel ɡʼurtʃːinkːarab jaɡi baɡʼarkːarab kʔjeraɬul ratani wa ɡwendaχaral ruɡoni
kaʃiʃ ɡʔjenisa qʼwatʼiwe wiɬːine kːola wa ɡʔjeb mina raχaze kːola ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ
ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ naqχeɡi minajaɬul χal ʃal ɡʔabize watʃʼaraw kaʃiʃasda qʼadazda ɡʔjel tʼankʼal tʼadeɡi ɡʼjemerɬun ratani
ɡʔjes qʼadazul kːal tʃʼwaralʃːinal bakʼazda ruɡel ɡantʃʼal raqχun ʃaɡʔar tun qʼwatʼire qχubab bakʼalde reχejan ɬazabize kːola
minajaɬul ʒanisa qʼadazdasa tʼolabɡo χʼarʃːɡi qχatʃaze kːola wa ɡʔjebɡi ʃaɡʔaraldasa qʼwatʼibeχun qχubab bakʼalde naqχe baze kːola
bitʃːante basrijal ɡantʃʼazul bakʼalda tsʼijal ɬeze wa qʼadazda tsʼidasan χʼarʃː ʒuʒaze
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔabun χadub aj ɡantʃʼalɡi χisun basrijab χʼarʃːɡi naqχe qχatʃan wa tsʼidasan χʼarʃːɡi tʃʼwan χadub naqχeɡi minajaɬul qʼadazda kːalaɬul tʼankʼal rakːani
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ naqχeɡi kaʃiʃ watʃʼina wa minajaɬul χal ʃal ɡʔabila ɡʔjesda biχʔani tʼankʼal qʼadazda ɡʼjemerɬun rukʼin ɡʔjeb minajalda kweʃab barasaɬul kːal tʃʼwan bukʼin ɬala wa mina qχubɬun bukʼin ɬazabila
ɡʔjedinab mina biχːizabize kːola ɡʔjeɬul ɡantʃʼalɡi tʃʼalabiɡi χʼarʃːɡi ʃaɡʔaraldasa qʼwatʼibeχun qχubab bakʼalde naqχe baze kːola
kaʃiʃas ɡʔuqʼun χadub ɡʔjeb minajalda ʒaniwe ɬuɡʔaraw ʃːiwaw tʃi qχubawɬun wukʼuna baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan
ɡʔjeb minajalda ʒaniw kʔiʒaraw tʃijas ʒindirɡo tʼad bukʼarab retʼjel tʃurize kːola ɡʔjenib ʒanib kwen kwanarasɡi tʃurize kːola tʼad bukʼarab retʼjel
amma ɡantʃʼalɡi χisun qʼadazdasa basrijab χʼarʃːɡi naqχe qχatʃan tsʼidasan χʼarʃːɡi ʒuʒan χadub minajaɬul χal ʃal ɡʔabize watʃʼaraw kaʃiʃasda biχʔani tʼokʼaɬ tʼankʼal rakːulel ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi ɡʔjes ɡʔjeb mina batsʼtsʼadab buɡilan ɬazabila kːal tʼuban naqχe un buɡeɬul
ɡʔjeb mina batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabijaɬul nizam tʼobitʼijaɬe χwaʒainas bosize kːola kʼiɡo χʼintʃʼɡi tso kedraɬul qχwalχʔjenɡi baɡʼarab kwasul kunɡi isːopaɬul kwatsʼiɡi
tsojab χʼintʃʼ qχwela itsːuqχa ɬadal tsʼurab ʃːaɡʼil qχabajalda tʼadeɡi kːun
χadub kaʃiʃas bosila kedraɬul qχwalχʔjenɡi isːopaɬul kwatsʼiɡi baɡʼarab kwasul kunɡi tʃʼaɡojab χʼintʃʼɡi wa ɡʔjeb kinabɡo itsːuqχa ɬimɡun ʒubarab χʼintʃʼaɬul biduɬ tʃːun baqχila wa ɡʔjeb punqχila minajalde ankʔɡo nuχaɬ
ɡʔjedin χʼantʃʼil biɡi itsːul ɬimɡi tʃʼaɡojab χʼintʃʼɡi kedraɬul qχwalχʔjenɡi isːopaɬul kwatsʼiɡi baɡʼarab kwasul kunɡi χʼaltʼizabun kaʃiʃas mina batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabila
tʃʼaɡojab χʼintʃʼ ʃaɡʔaraldasa qʼwatʼibeχun ɡʼatʼidab awlaqχalda bitʃːan teze kːola ɡʔjedin kaʃiʃas batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabila ɡʔjeb mina wa ɡʔjeb batsʼtsʼaɬila
ɡʔjedinal ruɡo barasaɬul untabazul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ qʼanunal botʼroda barab tʼjeχʼ
ratʼlida jaɬuni minajalda tʃʼwarab kːal tʃerχaɬul kinab bukʼaniɡi bakʼ ɡʔoroj tʼomalde barab sus jaɡi qχaχʼal tʼankʼal ʃːib ɡʔjeb bataniɡi
ɡʔjel qʼanunazdaɬun ɬala nuʒeda qχubabɡi batsʼtsʼadabɡi batʼa ɡʔabize ɡʔjele barasaɬul raqχaɬ qʼanunal

betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɬazabe naɡaɡʔ biχʔintʃijasul tʃerχaldasa qʼwatʼibe ɬamaɬi batʃʼuneb buɡoni ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjew qχubɬizawula
batʼaɬi ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjeb ʒeɡi batʃʼuneb bukʼa ɡʔorkʔob qʼotʼun bukʼa ɡʔjew qχubaw kːola
ɡʔjedinaw biχʔintʃi tʼad kʔiʒarab busen qʼaj qχubɬula wa ɡʔjew ɡʼodow tʃʼarabʃːinab bakʼɡi qχubɬula
ɡʔjesul busen qʼajalda qχwarawʃːinaw tʃijas ʒindirɡo tʃerχɡi tʼad bukʼarab retʼjelɡi tʃurize kːola wa baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan qχubawɬun wukʼuna
ɬamaɬi batʃʼunew tʃi wukʼarab bakʼalda ɡʼodow tʃʼarasɡi tʃerχɡi tʼad bukʼarab retʼjelɡi tʃurize kːola ɡʔjewɡi baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan qχubawɬun wukʼuna
ɬamaɬi batʃʼunew tʃijasda qχwarasɡi tʃurize kːola tʼad bukʼarab retʼjelɡi ʒindirɡo tʃerχɡi ɡʔjewɡi qʼasiɬizeɡʼan qχubawɬun wukʼuna
ɡʔjes ɬideniɡi tuni ɡʔjesɡi tʃurize kːola tʼad bukʼarab retʼjel tʃerχalda ɬimɡi baqχize kːola wa baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan ɡʔjewɡi qχubɬun wukʼuna
ɬamaɬi batʃʼunew tʃi tʼad rekʼarab kinab bataniɡi kʔiliɡi qχubɬula
ɡʔjesda ʁorkʔ bukʼarab ʃːibniɡi ʒojalda qχwaraw tʃiɡi ɡʔjeb kodobe bosaraw tʃiɡi qʼasiɬizeɡʼan qχubawɬun wukʼuna ɡʔjesda tʼad bukʼarab retʼjelɡi tʃurize kːola tʃerχalda ɬimɡi baqχize kːola wa ɡʔjew qʼasiɬizeɡʼan qχubawɬun wukʼuna
ɬamaɬi batʃʼunew tʃi kweralɡi tʃuritʃʼoɡo tsoɡi tʃijasda qχwani ɡʔjesɡi tʃurize kːola ʒindirɡo retʼjel tʃerχalda ɬimɡi baqχize kːola ɡʔjewɡi markʼatʃʼumeχ ʃːwezeɡʼan qχubawɬun wukʼuna
ɡʔjew tʃi ʃːaɡʼil tsʼaraɡʼalda qχwani ɡʔjeb bekize kːola ɡʔjeb tsʼulal tsʼaraɡʼ bukʼun batani ɬetsa tʃurize kːola
ɡʔjew tʃijasul ɬamaɬi batʃʼin qʼotʼarab meχaɬ ankʔɡo qʼojaɬɡi tʃʼun bitʃːante ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo retʼjel tʃurize wa tʃerχalda itsːul jaɡi tʃwaχuleb ɬaral ɬim baqχize tsinɡi ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼaɬila
bitʃːante mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjew tʃi kʼiɡo roχʔil mikːiɡi jaɬuni kʼiɡo mikːidul tʼintʃʼɡi bosun dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsewe watʃʼine wa ɡʔjes ɡʔjeb kaʃiʃasuqχe kʔjeze
kaʃiʃas tsojab χʼintʃʼ munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe tsoɡijab tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχwela wa ɡʔjedin betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɡʔjesul raqχaɬ qʼurbanalɡi tʼoritʼun ɡʔjew qχubɬijaldasa watsʼtsʼad ɡʔawila
biχʔintʃijasul mani batʃʼani ɡʔjes tʃerχalda ɬim baqχize kːola wa qʼasiɬizeɡʼan ɡʔjew qχubawɬun wukʼuna
mani tʼade arab kinab bataniɡi ʒo jaɡi retʼjel ɡʔjeb tʃurize kːola wa qʼasiɬizeɡʼan ɡʔjeb qχubabɬun rikʼkʼuna
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan rosasda askʼoj jjeɡani wa ɡʔjesul mani batʃʼani ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ ɡʔjeɬɡi tʃerχalda ɬim baqχize kːola wa qʼasiɬizeɡʼan kʼijalɡo qχubalɬun rukʼuna
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬul tʃerχaldasa bi batʃʼuneb buɡoni wa ɡʔjeb ɡʼadatijab χʼajiz batani ɡʔjej ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ qχubajɬun jikʼuna ɡʔjelda qχwarawʃːinaw tʃiɡi qʼasiɬizeɡʼan qχubawɬun rikʼkʼuna
ʒindirɡo χʼajizaɬul qʼojaz ɡʔjej tʼad jjeɡarabʃːinab wa ɡʼodoj tʃʼarabʃːinab bakʼɡi qχubɬula
ɡʔjeɬul busada qχwaraw tʃijas tʼad bukʼarab retʼjelɡi ʒindirɡo tʃerχɡi tʃurize kːola ɡʔjewɡi markʼatʃʼumeχ ʃːwezeɡʼan qχubawɬun rikʼkʼuna
ɡʔjej ɡʼodoj tʃʼun jikʼarab bakʼalda qχwaraw tʃijasɡi ʒindirɡo retʼjelɡi tʃerχɡi tʃurize kːola ɡʔjewɡi qʼasiɬizeɡʼan qχubawɬun rikʼkʼuna
ɡʔjeɬul busada bukʼarab jaɬuni ɡʔjej ɡʼodoj tʃʼoleb bakʼalda bukʼarab kinabniɡi ʒojalda qχwaraw tʃiɡi qʼasiɬizeɡʼan qχubaw wukʼuna
ɡʔjeɬul χʼajizaɬul qʼojaz ros ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡani ɡʔjeɬul χʼajizaɬul qχubɬi ɡʔjesde batʃʼuna wa ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔjewɡi qχubawɬun rikʼkʼuna tsinɡi ɡʔjew tʼad weɡarab busen qʼajɡi qχubɬula
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬul tʃerχaldasa ɡʼjemeral qʼojaz bi batʃʼuneb buɡoni ɡʔjeb ɡʼadatijab χʼajizɡi batitʃʼoni jaɬuni χʼajiz χalat baqχuneb buɡoni ɡʔjebmeχaɬɡi χʼajizaɬul qʼojazɡo ɡʼadin bi batʃʼunelʃːinal qʼojaz ɡʔjej qχubajɬun jikʼuna
χʼajizaɬul qʼojazɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjej ɡʼadan tʼad jeɡarabʃːinab busen qʼajɡi qχubɬula ɡʔjej ɡʼodoj tʃʼarabʃːinab bakʼɡi qχubɬula
ɡʔjel ʒalazda qχwaraw tʃiɡi qχubɬula ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo retʼjelɡi tʃerχɡi tʃurize kːola ɡʔjewɡi qʼasiɬizeɡʼan qχubawɬun wukʼuna
bi qʼotʼarab meχaɬ tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan ʒeɡi ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ tʃʼjeze kːola tsinɡi ɡʔjej jatsʼtsʼaɬula
mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ kʼiɡo roχʔil mikːiɡi jaɬuni kʼiɡo mikːidul tʼintʃʼɡi bosun ɡʔjej ɡʼadan dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsee jatʃʼina wa ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjeb kaʃiʃasuqχe kʔjela
kaʃiʃas tsojab χʼintʃʼ munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe tsoɡidab tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχwela wa ɡʔjedin betʼjerhanasda tsere ɡʔjeɬul raqχaɬ qʼurbanalɡi tʼoritʼun ɡʔjej qχubɬijaldasa jatsʼtsʼad ɡʔajila
nuʒetsa ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼ qχubɬijaldasa tsʼune ʒindirɡo qχubɬijaldaɬun ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔob buɡeb dir tʃadirɡi qχubɬizabun ɡʔjel χwezarize kːetʃʼoɡo rukʼine
ɡʔjele ɬamaɬi batʃʼunew jaɡi mani batʃʼaraw wa ɡʔjeldaɬun qχubɬaraw biχʔintʃijase qχwaral qʼanunal
ɡʔjedinɡo bi batʃʼinaɬ qχubɬaraj tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬeɡi palχʼasil qχubɬaraw biχʔintʃijaseɡi qχubɬaraj tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬeɡi tsoɡo qʼanun bukʼina ɡʔjedinɡo qχubɬaraj ɬaduda askʼow weɡaraw rosaseɡi

betʼjerhanasda tsere ɡʔarunil wasal χun χadub betʼjerhan kʼaɬana musada
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
durɡo wats ɡʔarunida abe bokʔa bokʔarab meχaɬ watʃʼine beɡʔularin χasab pardawalda naqχa buɡeb biʃːunɡo muqʼadasab bakʼalda ʒaniwe wa ɡʔjenib buɡeb qʼotʼijaɬul ʁansil tʼaɬelalda tsewe ɡuroni ɡʔjew χweze wuɡin ɡʔjenib nakʼkʼul partʃaduɬ ditsa dunɡo zaɡʔir ɡʔawize wuɡeɬul
biʃːunɡo muqʼadasab bakʼalde ɬuɡʔinalda tsebe ɡʔarunitsa munaɡʔal tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze otsɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze kujɡi batʃʼine kːola
bitʃːante ɡʔjes tsin tʃerχalda ɬim baqχize wa kaʃiʃzabazul χirijab retʼjel tʼad retʼine batsʼtsʼadab χʼjebtil kaʃiʃasul ɡurdeɡi ɡʼawrat baχtʃuleb batsʼtsʼadab χʼjebtil tʼaʒuɡi ɡʔjedinabɡo χʼjebtil ratʃelɡi botʼroda χʼjebtil tʼaʁurɡi ɬe
ɡʼizrailazul ʒamaɡʼataɬuqχa ɡʔjes qʼabul ɡʔabize kːola munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze kʼiɡo deɡʼjenɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze kujɡi
bitʃːante ʒindirɡo raqχaldasan munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe qʼatʃʼarab ots qχweze ɡʔarunitsa ʒindasaɡoɡi ʒindirɡo qχizan qʼajaldasaɡi munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬize rukʼine
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔjes kʼijabɡo deɡʼjenɡi batʃine kːola betʼjerhanasda tsebe dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje
wa moʒoro reχize kːola ɡʔjezul kinab betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo qχweze buɡeb kinab azazelaɬe
ɡʔarunitsa batʃina moʒorojaɬ betʼjerhanase biχʔizaburab deɡʼjen wa munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe qχwela
moʒorojaɬ azazelaɬe biχʔizaburab deɡʼjen betʼjerhanasda tsebe tʃʼaɡo batʃina χalqʼ munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul nizam tʼobitʼize wa χadub ɡʼalaχalde azazelaɬe bitʃːan teze bukʼine
munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe χʼadurarab ʒindirɡo ots qχun χadub wa ʒindasaɡi ʒindirɡo qχizan qʼajaldasaɡi munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul qʼurban tʼobitʼun χadub
ɡʔarunitsa bosila ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼuleb ʃːurun qʼurban bakʼalda tʼasa buχʼuleb tʼurtʃːiɡi ʒanib ɬun wa danʁura tsʼurab ɡʔuinmaχʼazul ʒubajɡi bosun χasab pardawalda naqχe ina
ɡʔjenib betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɡʔjes ɡʔuinmaχʼazul ʒubaj tʼurtʃːijalda tʼade bala wa qʼotʼijaɬul ʁansil tʼaɬel kʼkʼujaɬ baχtʃizabila ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize kːola ɡʔjew χwetʃʼoɡo χutʼize
ɡʔjeldasa χadub bitʃːante ɡʔjes otsol bi bosize wa biduɬ kiliʃːɡi tʃːun bi punqχize ʁansil tʼaɬelaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalde wa ankʔɡo nuχaɬ tʼaɬelalda tsebeseb raqχalde
χadub ɡʔarunitsa tʼolabɡo χalqʼaldasa munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe deɡʼjen qχwela wa ɡʔjeɬul biɡi bosun χasab pardawalda naqχe ina otsol biɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjebɡi punqχila qʼotʼijaɬul ʁansil tʼaɬelalda tʼade wa tʼaɬelalda tsebeseb raqχalde
ɡʔjedin batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabila ɡʔarunitsa biʃːunɡo muqʼadasab bakʼ χalqʼaɬul qχubɬijaldasaɡi ɡʔjezul taqʼsirazdasaɡi ɡʔjezul munaɡʔazdasaɡi ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔabize kːola dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬeɡi ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʼadamazda ɡʔorkʔob buɡeɬul ɡʔjeb ɡʔjezul qχubɬijaɬ swerunɡi kːun
munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul nizam tʼobitʼizeɬun ɡʔarun ɡʔjeniwe ʒaniwe araldasa naqχe ɡʔjew qʼwatʼiwe watʃʼineɡʼan dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda ʒaniw tsoniɡi tʃi wukʼine beɡʔularo ɡʔjedin ɡʔarunitsa munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬizarila ʒiwɡoɡi ʒindirɡo qχizan qʼajɡi tʼolabɡo χalqʼɡi
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔabun χadub ɡʔjew betʼjerhanasda tsebe buɡeb mesedil qʼurban bakʼalda askʼowe ina wa ɡʔjelda tʼadɡi ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul nizam tʼobitʼila otsolɡi daɡʼnilɡi biɡi bosun ɡʔjeb baχina qʼurban bakʼaɬul unqʼabɡo bokʼnida tʃʼwaral ɬːurduzda
wa ɡʔjebɡo bi punqχila qʼurban bakʼalda tʼade ankʔɡo nuχaɬ ɡʔjedin batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabila ɡʔjeb ɡʼizrailazul qχubɬijaldasa wa ɡʔjeb muqʼadasabɬun bukʼina
biʃːunɡo muqʼadasab bakʼɡi dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadirɡi qʼurban bakʼɡi batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabun χadub ɡʔarunitsa tʃʼaɡojab deɡʼjen betʼjerhanasda tsebe batʃina
kʼijabɡo kwerɡi daɡʼnil botʼroda ɬun ɡʔjes ɡʼizrailazul kinabniɡi munaɡʔ χʼaqʼ reχsela ɡʔjeb daɡʼnitsa batʃːize bukʼine χadub ɡʔjeb deɡʼjen ɡʼalaχalde bitʼila ɡʔjeb batʃun tso tʃiɡi ina
wa ɡʔjeb daɡʼnitsa rikʼkʼadab meɡʼjer ɡʼalaχalde rosun ina χalqʼaɬulɡo munaɡʔal ɡʔjenib deɡʼjenɡi bitʃːan tela
ɡʔjeldasa χadub ɡʔarun dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬuwe ɬuɡʔina wa biʃːunɡo muqʼadasab bakʼalde ɬuɡʔinalda tsebe ɡʔjes retʼarab batsʼtsʼadab χʼjebtil retʼjel tʼasa baqχina wa ɡʔjenib tela
bitʃːante ɡʔjes muqʼadasab bakʼalda tʃerχaldasa ɬimɡi baqχun tsoɡidab retʼjel tʼad retʼine tsinɡi ɡʔjew tʃadiraɬusa qʼwatʼiwe watʃʼina wa ʒindasaɡoɡi χalqʼaldasaɡi tʼuran ruχʼulel qʼurbanal tʼoritʼila wa ʒiwɡoɡi χalqʼɡi ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔarila
munaɡʔal tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬul tʼatʼi qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼize kːola
azazelaɬul deɡʼjen batʃun un wukʼaraw tʃijas ʒindirɡo retʼjelɡi tʃerχɡi tʃurize kːola tsinɡi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔowe tʼad wusːine beɡʔula
munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe qχurab otsɡi deɡʼjenɡi ʃaɡʔaraldasa qʼwatʼibe bosize kːola ɡʔjezul tʼomɡi ɡʔanɡi kinabɡo urɡʔimesɡi ɡʔjenib buχʼize kːola ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjezul bi munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul nizam tʼobitʼijaɬe biʃːunɡo muqʼadasab bakʼalde bosun bukʼindal
ɡʔjeb buχʼaraw tʃijasɡi ʒindirɡo retʼjelɡi tʃerχɡi tʃurize kːola χadub ɡʔjew χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔowe tʼad wusːine beɡʔula
nuʒee abadijab qʼanunɬun ɬazabuleb buɡo ankʔabileb motsʼaɬul antsʼabileb qʼojaɬ aj kipurimaɬul qʼojaɬ kʼal kːwe wa ʃːiwniɡi tʃi χʼaltʼuɡe ja ɡʼizrailaw ja nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼaraw qʼwatʼisa tʃi
ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ kaʃiʃas munaɡʔazdasa χwasarɬijaɬul nizam tʼobitʼula nuʒeqχa kːaral tʼolalɡo munaɡʔazdasa betʼjerhanasda tsere nuʒ ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔarize
ɡʔjeb qʼo nuʒee χʼalχʔijaɬul wa allaɡʔase mutʼiɡʼɬijaɬul qʼoɬun bukʼine kːola ɡʔjeb qʼanun bukʼina nuʒee abadijaɬeɡo
munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul qʼurban tʼobitʼize kːola χirijab naχɡi baχaraw wa umumuzdasa kaʃiʃɬijaɬul irsɡi bosaraw kʼudijaw kaʃiʃas bitʃːante ɡʔjes batsʼtsʼadab χʼjebtil χasab retʼjel tʼad retʼine
wa biʃːunɡo muqʼadasab bakʼɡi dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadirɡi qʼurban bakʼɡi batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabize ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔjes ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔarila kaʃiʃzabiɡi tʼolabɡo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼɡi
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ tʼolalɡo munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬe tʃʼjezaburab qʼanun abadijaɬeɡo buɡeb qʼanun buɡo ɬaɡʼalida ʒanib tso nuχaɬ tʼubazabe ɡʔjeb
ɡʔjez kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musada abuqχe

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazdaɡi ɡʼizrailil tʼolabɡo χalqʼaldaɡi abe betʼjerhanas ɡʔadinab amru ɡʔabunin
ɡʼizrailazul ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi botsʼul ɡʼijal jaɬuni tsʼanazul reqχaɬa ʒo dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa betʼjerhanasul muqʼadasab bakʼalda tsebe qʼurbanaɬeɡi qχwetʃʼoɡo batʼijab bakʼalda ʒindijeɡo bokʔuqχe qχuni
ɡʔabsaɡʼat ɡʼizrailaz awlaqχalda qχolel ruɡel χʼajwanal ritʃːante ɡʔjez betʼjerhanasda tsere dandtʃʼwajaɬul kʼaltʼje kaʃiʃasuqχe ratʃun ratʃʼine wa ɡʔjenir betʼjerhanase raqʼlil qʼurbanal χʼisabalda qχweze
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas qʼurbanaɬul bi punqχize dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa buɡeb betʼjerhanasul qʼurban bakʼalde wa ɡʔjeɬul tʼatʼi buχʼize betʼjerhanase χirijab maχʼaɬul kʼkʼuj baqχinabize
amma dora daɡʼnil sipataɬul ʃajtʼabaze qʼurbanalɡi qχun ɡʔjezije laʁɬiɡi ɡʔabun tʼokʼaɬ allaɡʔase χilipɬuɡejan
dutsa ɡʔjezda abe ɡʼizrailazul jaɬuni qʼwatʼisa ratʃʼun nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor ɡʼumru ɡʔabulezul ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb jaɡi raqʼlil qʼurban ɡʔabuni
amma dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa betʼjerhanase ɡʔaburab qʼurban ɡʔjeb batitʃʼoni ɡʔjedin ɡʔaburaw tʃi tʼaɡʼinawize kːola ɡʔjesul tsʼarɡi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qχwaɡʼaze kːola
ɡʼizrailazul jaɬuni qʼwatʼisa ratʃʼun nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabulezul ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi kwanije bi χʼaltʼizabuleb buɡoni ɡʔjew tʃijasde dir ɡʔalaɡab tsːin reʃːtʼine buɡo wa ditsa ɡʔjew tʼaɡʼinawize wuɡo ɡʔjesul tsʼarɡi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qχwaɡʼaze buɡo
tʃʼaɡojab ʒojaɬul ruχʼ ɡʔjeɬul biduɬ bukʼuna ɡʔjedinɬidal ditsa nuʒede amru ɡʔabuna bi qʼurban bakʼalde punqχejan nuʒerɡo ruχʼal χwasarɬize rukʼine nuʒee ɡʼolo ɡʼodobe tʼurab ɡʔjeb bijaɬ nuʒer ɡʼumru χwasar ɡʔabula ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʼumru biduɬ bukʼuneɬul
ɡʔjedinɬidalin ditsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɬazabuleb buɡeb tsoniɡi tʃijas bi kʼaldib qχwaɡe ɡʔjedinɡo qʼwatʼisa ratʃʼun nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor tʃʼaral ɡʼadamazɡi bi kwanije χʼaltʼizabuɡe
ɡʼizrailas jaɬuni qʼwatʼisa watʃʼun nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔow tʃʼaraw tsoɡi tʃijas tʃanaweɡi un kwanaze beɡʔuleb ɡʼalχul tʃan jaɬuni χʼintʃʼ kːuni ɡʔjes tʃanil kinabɡo bi bitʃːaze kːola χadub bijalda tʼade rakʔɡi qχwaze kːola
ʃːajɡureɬul tʃʼaɡojabʃːinab ʒojaɬul ruχʼ ɡʔjeɬul biduɬ bukʼuna bi ɡʔjeb kːola ɡʼumru ɡʔjedinɬidalin ditsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɬazaburab kinab buɡoniɡi ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijaɬul bi ɡʔjeqʼoɡejan ʃːibab tʃʼaɡojabʃːinab ʒojaɬul ruχʼ ɡʔjeɬul biduɬ bukʼuneɬul bi ɡʔjeqʼolew tʃi tʼaɡʼinawize wuɡo
ɡʼizrailas jaɬuni qʼwatʼisa watʃʼun nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔow tʃʼaraw tsoɡi tʃijas χwarab jaɬuni ʒanawaraz tʃʼwarab χʼajwanaɬul ɡʔan kwanan batani ɡʔjes retʼjelɡi tʃerχɡi tʃurize kːola wa baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan ɡʔjew qχubɬun wukʼuna tsinɡi watsʼtsʼaɬula
amma ɡʔjes retʼjelɡi tʃerχɡi tʃuritʃʼoni ɡʔjew ɡʼajibaɬukʔje kːeze wuɡo

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼalda abe dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
nuʒetsa naqχa tarab misrijaɬul χalqʼaldaɡi ditsa nuʒ ratʃunel ruɡeb χanaanaɬul χalqʼazdaɡi reɬun χʔwaduɡe wa ɡʔjezul ɡʼadatazda naqχ riɬːunɡe
dir amrabi tʼurazare dir qʼanunal tsʼune wa ɡʔjezda reqʼon χʔwade dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
dir qʼanunalɡi dir amrabiɡi tʼurazare ɡʔjel tʼurazarijaldaɬun tʃʼaɡo wukʼina insan dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
tseesej ɡʼaɡaraj tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanalda qχwaɡe ɡʔjejɡun weɡize muradɡun dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
durɡo ebelalda askʼowɡi weɡun insul tʼaʁuralde roɡʔo batʃunɡe ɡʔjej dur ebelɬidal ɡʔjej inʒit ɡʔajuɡe
durɡo insul batʼijaj ɬaduda askʼowɡi weɡuɡe emenɡi χʼaqʼir ɡʔawun
kinaj jataniɡi durɡo jatsalda askʼow weɡuɡe ɡʔjej ementsadaqχaj jataniɡi ebeltsadaqχaj jataniɡi munɡun tso minajalda ɡʼuraj jaɬuni batʼaɡo ɡʼuraj jataniɡi
durɡo wasasul jasaldaɡi jasaɬul jasaldaɡi qχwaɡe qχubal qʼasdalɡun ɡʔjeb munɡo basra ɡʔawi kːola
durɡo insuje batʼijaj tʃʼuʒujaɬ ɡʔajuraj jasalda askʼow weɡuɡe ɡʔjej dur jats kːola ɡʔjej inʒit ɡʔajuɡe
durɡo insul jatsalda askʼow weɡuɡe ɡʔjej dur insul tʼul bikʔaraj jatsɬidal
ɡʔjedinɡo durɡo ebelaɬul jatsalda askʼowɡi weɡuɡe ɡʔjej dur ebelaɬul tʼul bikʔaraj jatsɬidal
durɡo insul watsasul tʼaʁuralde roɡʔo batʃunɡe qχubal qʼasdalɡun ɡʔjesul ɬaduda askʼowe ɬuɡʔunɡe ɡʔjej dur insul watsasul ɬadiɬidal
durɡo nusalda askʼow weɡuɡe ɡʔjej dur wasasul ɬadiɬidal ɡʔjej inʒit ɡʔajuɡe
durɡo watsasul ɬaduda askʼow weɡuɡe durɡo wats basra ɡʔawi kːola ɡʔjeb
mun tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanalda tsinɡi ɡʔjeɬul jasaldaɡi askʼow weɡize beɡʔularo tʃʼuʒujaɬul jasalda jaɡi ɡʔjeɬul jasaɬulɡi wasasulɡi jasalda mun qχwaɡe ɡʔjeldaɬun tʃʼuʒu inʒit ɡʔajuɡe ɡʔjeb kʼudijab qʼabiχʼɬi buɡo
durɡo ɬadul jats jatʃunɡe ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔob qʼetsɡi kːezabun durɡo ɬadiɡi tʃʼaɡo jikʼaɡo ɡʔjeɬul jatsalda askʼow weɡuɡe
tʃʼuʒujaɬul χʼajizaɬul qʼojaz aj ɡʔjej qχubɬun jikʼaɡo ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡuɡe
tʃijar tʃʼuʒujalda askʼow weɡuɡe wa munɡo qχubɬizawuɡe
durɡo ɬimal moloχije
biχʔintʃijasda askʼow tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanalda askʼow ɡʼadin weɡuɡe ɡʔjeb kʼudijab qʼabiχʼɬi buɡo
ɡʔjedinɡo χʼajwanalɡun qχubal ʒal ɡʔaruɡe munɡoɡi qχubɬizawun ɡʔjedinɡo tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanɡi χʼajwanalda ʁorkʔ jjeɡuɡe ɡʔjeb kʼudijab qʼabiχʼɬi buɡo
ɡʔjel kinalɡo tʃorokal ʒalazdaɬun nuʒɡo qχubɬizaruɡe ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔabula ditsa nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔaldasa naqχe qχamize ruɡel χalqʼaz
ɡʔjel sababɬun ɡʔjeb rakʔɡo qχubɬana wa ditsa ɡʔjezije ʒaza ɡʔabize χʼukmu qʼotʼana ɡʔjedinɬidal rakʔaɬɡi ɡʔjel χalqʼal qʼwatʼire tun ralaɡʔizaruna
nuʒetsajin abuni dir qʼanunalɡi dir amrabiɡi tʼurazare ɡʼizrailazul tsoniɡi tʃijas jaɡi qʼwatʼisa watʃʼun nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼaras ɡʔjel qʼabiχʼal ʒal ɡʔaruɡe
ʃːajɡureɬul nuʒeda tsere ɡʔab rakʔalda rukʼaral χalqʼaz ɡʔjel riχaral iʃal ɡʔaruna wa ɡʔjeb sababɬun rakʔɡi qχubɬana
ɡʔjedinal iʃal ɡʔarize ɬuɡʔani nuʒetsaɡi qχubɬizabila ɡʔab rakʔ tsinɡi nuʒɡi qʼwatʼire tun ralaɡʔizarila ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔanir rukʼaral χalqʼalɡo ɡʼadin
ɡʔjedinal iʃal ɡʔarurawʃːinaw tʃi tʼaɡʼinawize wuɡo wa ɡʔjesul tsʼarɡi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qχwaɡʼaze buɡo
dir amrabiɡi aχʼkamalɡi tʼurazare ɡʔanir rukʼaral χalqʼazul qʼabiχʼal ɡʼadatazda naqχriɬːunɡe wa nuʒɡo qχubɬizaruɡe dun wuɡo betʼjerhan

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil tʼolabɡo χalqʼalda ɬazabe nuʒ ratsʼtsʼadɡo χʔwade ʃːajɡureɬul dun wuɡo watsʼtsʼadaw betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
ebelaɬulɡi insulɡi adab qχatir ɡʔabe wa dir ʃamatazul ʃurutʼal tʼurazare dun wuɡo nuʒer betʼjerhan
pajda ɡʔjetʃʼjel ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔzabazde rusːunɡe biun tʼun maχːɡun allaɡʔzabazul sipatal ɡʔaruɡe dun wuɡo nuʒer betʼjerhan
betʼjerhanase raqʼlil qʼurbanal qχoleb meχaɬ ɡʔjew raziɬuleb χʼalaɬ ɡʔabe kinabɡo
ɡʔjezul ɡʔan kwanaj ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬɡi naqχiseb qʼojaɬɡi ɬababileb qʼojaɬ naqχe χutʼarab ɡʔan buχʼize kːola
amma ɬababileb qʼojaɬɡi nuʒ ɡʔjeb ɡʔan kwanaze ɬuɡʔani nuʒer qʼurban allaɡʔas naqχtʃʼwala maχʼ kʼutʼarab ɡʔan nuʒetsa kwanaraɬuqχ
ɡʔjedinab iʃ ɡʔaburaw tʃijase χʼaqʼ bukʼuna ʃːajɡureɬul betʼjerhanas χirijabɬun ɡʔaburab ʒo ɡʔjes qχubɬizabun bukʼun ɡʔjew tʃi tʼaɡʼinawize kːola ɡʔjesul tsʼarɡi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qχwaɡʼaze kːola
χurir ɬiɬaruleb meχaɬ χʼaluqχen raɡʼa rakʔande ʃːun bakʼaruɡe wa ɡʼodore rortaral tʼoralɡi riʃːuɡe
ɡʔjedinɡo tsʼolbol aχikʔa naqχe ʒo tetʃʼoɡo piqχ bakʼaruɡe ɡʼodobe bortarab ɡʔjenibɡo te miskinzabazeɡi tʃijar rakʔazdasa ratʃʼarazeɡi bukʼine te ɡʔjeb dun wuɡo nuʒer betʼjerhan
tsʼoɡʔ ɡʔabuɡe
ɡʔjeresi bitsunɡe
tsotsaje χʼilla makru ɡʔabuɡe
dir tsʼarɡi reχson ɡʔjeresijab ɡʔa baɡe allaɡʔasul tsʼar surizabuɡe dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
tsoɡidasuqχa ʃːibɡo baqχuɡe wa tsʼoɡʔ ɡʔabuɡe
χʼaltʼuqχanase kːoleb χarʒ qʼasiɡo kʔje roɡʔineɡʼan toɡe
ɡʼinqʼase naɡʼana kʔoɡe betsːasda tsebe χʼjetʼje ɬoɡe durɡo allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼa dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
diwanχanajalda ritʼuqχab χʼukmu qʼotʼje betʃedaw wuɡin jaɬuni miskinaw wuɡin abun ɡʔjesul ɡʔurmaqχ balaɡʔuɡe diwan ritʼuqχɡo qʼotʼje
ɡʼadamazda ɡʔorkʔor matsʼal ɡʔaruɡe
tsoɡidaw tʃijasul ɡʼumrujaɬe χʼinqʼi kːoleb ʒo ɡʔabuɡe dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
ɬideχun bukʼaniɡi rekʼjeɬ tsːin χʔiχʔuɡe dur χalqʼtsojas meqʼab iʃ ɡʔabuni ɡʔjesda badibe abe ɡʔjesul ɡʼajib dujeɡi ɡʼaχʔalɬitʃʼoɡo bukʼine
durɡo χalqʼtsojasdasa retsʼjel bosuɡe wa ɡʔjesde tsːidaχun wukʼunɡe durɡo ruχʼɡʼan wokʔa duje duda askʼow wuɡew tsoɡidaw tʃiɡi dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
dir qʼanunal tʼurazare
batʼi batʼijab tajpajaɬul χʼajwanal dande ratʃunɡe
kʼiɡo batʼijab χʔon tso χurib bekʔuɡe
batʼi batʼijab tajpajaɬul χːamazul ɡʔaburab retʼjel retʼunɡe
tʃijae kʔjeze qʼotʼi ɡʔaburaj laʁalda askʼow pulanaw tʃi weɡani amma ɡʔjeɬuqχ ʒeɡi muχʔ kʔun bukʼun ɡʔjetʃʼoni wa ɡʔjej erken ɡʔajunɡi jikʼun jatitʃʼoni ɡʔjesije tamiχʼ ɡʔabize kːola amma ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo tʃʼwaze beɡʔularo ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjej ʒeɡi erkenɬun jikʼintʃʼjeɬul
bitʃːante ɡʼajibijaw biχʔintʃijas ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze kuj batʃun batʃʼine betʼjerhanasda tsebe dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje
kaʃiʃas betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɡʔjew χwasarɬijaɬe ɡʼolo ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurban tʼobitʼila wa allaɡʔ ɡʔjesul munaɡʔalda tʼasa ɬuɡʔina
nuʒerɡo rakʔalde ʃːwedal nuʒetsa ɡʔjenir piqχil ʁutʼbi tʃʼjela amma tʼotsebeseb ɬabɡo sonaɬ nuʒetsa ɡʔjel ʁutʼbuzdasa piqχ kwanaɡe
unqʼabileb sonaɬ ɡʔjel ʁutʼbuzda biʒarab piqχ χirijabɬun aj betʼjerhanase kʔoleb retsː baqʼaɬul sadaqʼaɬun kːola
ʃːuabileb sonaɬ nuʒetsa ɡʔjezdasa piqχ kwanaze beɡʔula tsinɡi ɬaɡʼalidasa ɬaɡʼalide ɡʔjezda piqχ ɡʔarzaɬila dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
biɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔan kwanaɡe
pal tʼamuɡe siχʼrutʃiɬi ɡʔabuɡe
qʼunʃːbuzdasa ras kʼkʼwaɡe wa meɡeʒaɬul raɡʼal qʼuntsʼuɡe
χwarasda maɡʼu baqχuleɬul tʃerχalda nusal tʃʼwaɡe wa kinal rukʼaniɡi ɡʼuʒal ɬoɡe
nuʒerɡo jasal qχubɬizaruɡe qχaχʼbaɬijaldeɡi kʔun
dir ʃamatazul ʃurutʼal tʼurazare wa dir muqʼadasab bakʼaɬul adab χʼurmat ɡʔabe dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
χwarazul ruχʼazda kʼaɬalel jaɡi baɬɡoɬi bitsunel ɡʼadamazuqχe unɡe wa ɡʔjel tsʼjeχoɡe ɡʔjel sababɬun nuʒɡo qχubɬitʃʼoɡo rukʼine dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
kʼudijasda tsewe tʼade waqχa χeraw tʃijasul adab ɡʔabe allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼa dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob tʃʼjel ɡʔaburaw qʼwatʼib rakʔaldasa tʃi qʼwarid ɡʔawuɡe
nuʒerɡo rakʔtsojasdeχun ɡʼadab berbalaɡʔi ɡʔabe ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasdeχunɡi durɡo ruχʼɡʼan wokʔa ɡʔjewɡi nuʒɡoɡi rukʼindal tʃijar χalqʼ χʼisabalda misrijalda ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
ɡʔarulel iʃal rakʼbatsʼtsʼadɡo ɡʔare diwan ritʼuqχɡo qʼotʼje wa tsʼadirabazdaɬun jaɡi rotsenaɬe χʼaltʼizabuleb tsoɡi batʼijab tsʼaraɡʼaldaɬun χʼaram ɡʔabuɡe
bitʃːante nuʒer kinalɡo tsʼadirabiɡi jefaɡi ɡinɡi ritʼaral durusal rukʼine
dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃaraw nuʒer allaɡʔ
dir qʼanunalɡi dir χʼukmabiɡi tsʼune wa ɡʔjezda reqʼon χʔwade dun wuɡo betʼjerhan

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe ɡʼizrailazul tsoniɡi tʃijas jaɬuni nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼaral qʼwatʼib rakʔaldasa ratʃʼaral ɡʼadamazul ɬitsaniɡi moloχije ʒindirɡo ɬimer qʼurban ɡʔabuni ɡʔjew tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola ʒamaɡʼataɬ ɡantʃʼalɡi retʃʼtʃʼun tʃʼwaj ɡʔjew tʃi
dir tsːin reʃːtʼine buɡo ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasde ɡʔjew tʼaɡʼinawize wuɡo wa χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qʼotʼize wuɡo dir χirijab tsʼaralda wa muqʼadasab bakʼalda tʼade roɡʔoɡi batʃun ɡʔjes ɬimer moloχije kʔuraɬuqχ
ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi ɬimer moloχije qʼurban ɡʔabuni wa χalqʼaɬ ɡʔjeb iʃ kʼwar kʔjetʃʼoɡo tani wa ɡʔjew tʃi tʃʼwatʃʼoni
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsa ʒaza ɡʔabize buɡo ɡʔjesijeɡi ɡʔjesul ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬeɡi ditsa tʼaɡʼinawila ɡʔjewɡi ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ moloχije ɡʼolo qχubal iʃal ɡʔarural kinalɡoɡi ɡʔjezul tsʼaralɡi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qχwaɡʼala
χwarazul ruχʼazda kʼaɬalel baɬɡoɬi bitsunel wa ɡʔjezulɡun buχʔjen ɡʔaburalʃːinal tʃaɡʼaze ditsa ʒaza ɡʔabize buɡo ɡʔjedinal tʃaɡʼi tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡo wa χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qχwaɡʼaze ruɡo
dinijab ratsʼtsʼaɬi tsʼune munaɡʔal ɡʔaruɡe dun wuɡeɬul betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
dir qʼanunal muχʼkanɡo tʼurazare dun wuɡo betʼjerhan dirɡo χalqʼɬun nuʒ ratʼa ɡʔaruraw
ebel emen χʼaqʼir ɡʔarun kʼaɬaraw tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjes ebel insuje naɡʼana kʔun batani ʒiwɡo tʃʼwajaɬul ɡʼajib ɡʔjesda ʒindaɡo tʼade kːola
biχʔintʃijas zina ɡʔabuni wa tʃijar ɬadiɡun weɡani tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjewɡi ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ zina ɡʔaburaj tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanɡi
ʒindirɡo insul ɬaduda askʼow biχʔintʃi weɡani emen χʼaqʼir ɡʔawi buɡo ɡʔjeb ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo zinatʃaɡʼi tʃʼwaze kːola ʒalɡo tʃʼwajaɬul ɡʼajib ɡʔjezda ʒidedaɡo bukʼina
ʒindirɡo nusalda askʼow wakʔad weɡani ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjeb kutakalda qʼabiχʼab iʃ buɡo ʒalɡo tʃʼwajaɬul ɡʼajib ɡʔjezda ʒidedaɡo bukʼina
biχʔintʃi tsoɡi biχʔintʃijasda askʼow tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanalda askʼow kiniɡin weɡani ɡʔjeb kutakalda pasiqʼab iʃ buɡo ɡʔjel tʃʼwaze kːola ʒalɡo tʃʼwajaɬul ɡʼajibijal ɡʔjel ʒalɡo rukʼina
biχʔintʃijas jasɡi tsinɡi ɡʔjeɬul ebelɡi ɬudbiɬun ratʃani ɡʔjeb pasiqʼɬi buɡo ɡʔjewɡi ɡʔjej kʼijajɡo ɡʼadanɡi ruχʼize kːola ɡʔjedinab pasiqʼɬi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔobe bitʃːatʃʼoɡo bukʼine
χʼajwanɡun qχubal ɡʔorkʔorɬabi ɡʔaruraw biχʔintʃi tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjeb χʼajwanɡi tʃʼwaze kːola
ɡʔjedinɡo tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬɡi χʼajwanɡun qχubal ɡʔorkʔorɬabi ɡʔaruni ɡʔjejɡi ɡʔjeb χʼajwanɡi tʃʼwaj ɡʔjel tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjel tʃʼwajaɬul ɡʼajibɡi ɡʔjezda ʒidedaɡo buɡo
ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi ʒindirɡo ementsadaqχaj jaɬuni ebeltsadaqχaj jats jatʃani wa ɡʔjel tsotsada askʼor reɡani wa tsotsazul ɡʼitsʼɬi ɡʔjezda biχʔani ɡʔjeb buɡo kʼudijab nitʃ ɡʔjel χalqʼaldaɡo riχʔun tʼaɡʼinarize kːola wa χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qχwaɡʼaze kːola ɡʔjew tʃijas ʒindirɡo jats basra ɡʔajuna ɡʔjeɬuqχ ɡʔjesije ʒaza ɡʔabize kːola
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬul χʼajizaɬul qʼojaz ros ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡani ɡʔjez kʼijazɡo ɡʔjeɬul χʼajizaɬul bi qʼwatʼibe zaɡʔir ɡʔabuna ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjel χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe tʼaɡʼinarize kːola
ebelaɬul jaɡi insul jatsalda askʼow biχʔintʃi weɡuɡe ɡʔjedinab iʃ ɡʔaburaw tʃijas ʒindirɡo tsebeseb ɡʼaɡarɬi inʒit ɡʔabuleb buɡo ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo ɡʼajibijal rukʼina
insul jaɡi ebelaɬul jatsalda askʼow weɡaraw tʃijas ɡʔjeɬul ros inʒit ɡʔawulew wuɡo ɡʔjedinɬidal kʼijalɡo zinatʃaɡʼaze ʒaza bukʼina ɡʔjel ɬimalɡi ɡʔaritʃʼoɡo χwela
watsasul ɬadi ʒindijeɡo jatʃin qχubab iʃ buɡo wats inʒit ɡʔawi kːola ɡʔjeb ɡʔjezije ɬimal ɡʔarize ɡʔjetʃʼo
muχʼkanɡo tʼurazare tʼolalɡo dir qʼanunalɡi χʼukmabiɡi ditsa nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔaɬ nuʒɡoɡi qʼwatʼire tun ralaɡʔizaritʃʼoɡo rukʼine
nuʒeda tseresa ditsa naqχe qʼotʼulel ruɡel χalqʼazul ɡʼadatal rosuɡe ɡʔjedinal iʃal ɡʔaruraɬuqχ dir ɡʔalaɡab tsːin reʃːtʼana ɡʔjezde
ditsa nuʒeda abuna ɡʔjezul rakʔaɬul betʼjerɡʔabiɬun nuʒ rukʼine ruɡin wa ditsa nuʒee kʔjeze buɡin raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb ɡʔjeb rakʔ dun wuɡo betʼjerhan tsoɡidal χalqʼazdasa nuʒ ratʼa ɡʔaruraw nuʒer allaɡʔ
nuʒetsa batʼa ɡʔabize kːola batsʼtsʼadabɡi qχubabɡi χʼajwan ɡʔjedinɡo batsʼtsʼadabɡi qχubabɡi χʼintʃʼ ditsa nuʒee qχubabɬun biχʔizaburab χʼajwanaldaɬun χʼantʃʼidaɬun jaɬuni rakʔaldasa ʃuruleb ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijaldaɬun nuʒɡo qχubɬizaruɡe
dida tsebe batsʼtsʼadab ɡʼumru ɡʔabe dun wuɡeɬul watsʼtsʼadaw betʼjerhan ditsa nuʒ tsoɡidal χalqʼazdasa ratʼa ɡʔaruna nuʒ dir kːola
χwarazul ruχʼazda kʼaɬalel wa baɬɡoɬi bitsunel biχʔinalɡi rutʃːabiɡi tʃʼwaze kːola ɡantʃʼalɡi retʃʼtʃʼun tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjel ɡʔjel tʃʼwajaɬul ɡʼajib ɡʔjezda ʒidedaɡo bukʼina

betʼjerhanas musada abuna kaʃiʃzabazda ɡʔarunil wasazda abe ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬul tʃi χun wuɡoni kaʃiʃ ɡʔjesul ʒanazajalda qχwaze beɡʔularo ɡʔjeb sababɬun ʒiwɡo qχubɬitʃʼoɡo wukʼine
amma ɡʔjesul biʃːun tseresel tʃaɡʼi χun ruɡoni ebel emen was jas wats
jaɡi rosase intʃʼjej wa ɡʔjesul minajalda ɡʼumru ɡʔabun jikʼaraj jats ɡʔjezije ɡʼolo kaʃiʃase iχtijar buɡo qχubɬuleb ʒo ɡʔabize
riɡʔnal ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬul tsoniɡi tʃijase ɡʼolo ɡʔjes ʒiwɡo qχubɬuleb ʒo ɡʔabize beɡʔularo
kaʃiʃzabaz beɡʔularo betʼjer kʼkʼwaze meɡeʒaɬul raɡʼal qʼuntsʼize wa tʃerχalda ɡʼuʒal ɬeze
ɡʔjel rukʼine kːola allaɡʔase ratʼa ɡʔaruralɬun wa ratsʼtsʼadalɬun allaɡʔasul tsʼaraɬul adab reχarab ʒo ɡʔjez ɡʔabize beɡʔularo betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanal tʼoritʼuleɬul aj ʒindirɡo allaɡʔase χirijab niɡʼmat sadaqʼa ɡʔabuleɬul ɡʔjel ratsʼtsʼadɡo rukʼine kːola
kaʃiʃas ɬadiɬun jatʃine beɡʔularo qχaχʼbaɬi ɡʔaburaj jaɡi batʼijaw biχʔintʃi qχwaraj jaɡi rosasdasa jatʼaɬaraj ɡʼadan ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjew allaɡʔase watʼa ɡʔawuraw wa watsʼtsʼadaw kːoleɬul
allaɡʔase qχuluqχaɬe tʃʼaraw wa qʼurban bakʼalda allaɡʔase χirijab niɡʼmat kʔolew tʃi wuɡeɬul kaʃiʃ nuʒetsa ɡʔjesul adab ɡʔabize kːola ratsʼtsʼadalɬun rukʼina ɡʔjel nuʒee ʃːajɡureɬul dun wuɡeɬul watsʼtsʼadaw betʼjerhan nuʒer ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul itsː
kaʃiʃasul jasaɬ qχaχʼbaɬi ɡʔabuni wa ʒijɡo qχubɬizajuni ɡʔjeldaɬun emenɡi qχubɬula ɡʔjedinaj jas juχʼize kːola
kʼudijaw kaʃiʃas aj χirijab naχɡi baχaraw χasab kaʃiʃɬijaɬul retʼjelɡi retʼunew kʼudijaw kaʃiʃas betʼjer ɡʔurʃːun bitʃːaze beɡʔularo wa tʼad buɡeb retʼjel biqχ biqχize beɡʔularo
ʒanaza buɡeb bakʼaldeɡi ɡʔjew ɬuɡʔine beɡʔularo ʒindirɡo ebel jaɡi emen χun ruɡoniɡitsin ʒiwɡo qχubɬize witʃːaze beɡʔularo
kʼudijaw kaʃiʃ muqʼadasab bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼiwe ine beɡʔularo allaɡʔasul muqʼadasab bakʼ qχubɬizabitʃʼoɡo bukʼine ʃːajɡureɬul χasab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ watʼaɡi ɡʔawun allaɡʔasul χirijab naχ baχun buɡeɬul ɡʔjesda dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
ɡʔjes ɬadiɬun jasɡʼadan ɡuroni jatʃine beɡʔularo
ɡʔjes jatʃine beɡʔularo qʼorolaj jaɡi rosasdasa jatʼaɬaraj qχaχʼbaɬi ɡʔaburaj jaɬuni batʼijaw biχʔintʃi qχwaraj ɡʼadan ɡʼitsʼɡo ʒindirɡo ɡʼaɡarɬijaldasa jasɡʼadan ɡuroni
ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjesul naslu batsʼtsʼadab bukʼine kːola dun wuɡeɬul betʼjerhan ɡʔjesul ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul itsː
χadub betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔarunida ɬazabe ɡʔjesul naslujaldasa tʃerχalda kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi buɡew tʃi wuɡoni ɡʔjesul iχtijar ɡʔjetʃʼo qʼurban bakʼalde tʼade allaɡʔase χirijab niɡʼmat bosize
tʃerχalda ɡʼuzru buɡew ʃːiwniɡi tʃijasul iχtijar ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjeb χirijab niɡʼmatalda askʼowe ɡʼaɡarɬize betsːaw reqʼaw ɡʔurmada ɡʼuʒ ɬuraw χʼjetʼje kwer ɡʼajibaw
boχ jaɡi ʁeʒ bekaraw
qʼularaw tʃʼintʃʼiqʼaw ber ɡʼajibaw tʃerχalda qχiris jaɬuni tʃanqχ baraw biχʔinɬi ʒaʁalɬaraw
kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunil naslujaldasa tʃorχoɬ ʒaʁalɬi buɡew tsoniɡi tʃijas betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanal tʼoritʼize beɡʔularo ɡʔjedinaw tʃijas qʼurban bakʼalde tʼade allaɡʔase χirijab niɡʼmat bosize beɡʔularo
ɡʔjes kwanaze beɡʔula allaɡʔasul χirijab niɡʼmat χirijabɡi biʃːunɡo χirijabɡi
amma ɡʔjesul tʃerχalda ɡʼuzru bukʼinaɬ ɡʔjew pardawalda askʼowe watʃʼine wa qʼurban bakʼalde ɡʼaɡarɬize beɡʔularo ɡʔjeldaɬun dir muqʼadasab tʃadir qχubɬizabitʃʼoɡo bukʼine dun wuɡo betʼjerhan ɡʔjezul ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul itsː
musatsa ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazdaɡi tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazdaɡi bitsana

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazdaɡi ɬazabe ɡʼizrailaz dije ratʃʼaral χirijal sadaqʼabi kʼudijab adab qχatiralda qʼabul ɡʔarejan wa kaʃiʃzabazul ɡʼajibaldaɬun dir χirijab tsʼaraɬul adab reχuleb ʒo kːeze bitʃːaɡejan dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
ɡʔjezda ɡʔadin abe nuʒer naslujaldasa wa ɡʔjeb naslujaɬul tʼolalɡo ɡʼjelazdasa ʃːiwniɡi tʃi ʒiw qχubɬun wukʼinɡi ɬalaɡo ɡʼizrailaz dije ratʃʼaral dir χirijal ʒalazda askʼowe watʃʼani ɡʔjew naqχe qʼotʼize wuɡo wa tʼokʼaɬ dida tsewe watʃʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
ɡʔarunil naslujaldasa baras unti buɡew jaɡi tʃerχaldasa ɬamaɬi batʃʼunew ʃːiwniɡi tʃijas kwanaze beɡʔularo qʼurban bakʼalde batʃʼarab χirijab sadaqʼa ʒiwɡo watsʼtsʼaɬizeɡʼan ɡʔjedinɡo χwaraw tʃijasda qχwaraw mani batʃʼaraw
qχubab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijalda qχwaraw qχubɬaraw tʃijasda qχwaraw tʃi ʃːib sababɬun ɡʔjew qχubɬun wataniɡi
ɡʔjedinaw tʃi baqʼ tʼjerχʔineɡʼan qχubɬun wukʼina ɡʔjew tʃijasul iχtijar ɡʔjetʃʼo χirijab sadaqʼa kwanaze tsin ɡʔjes tʃerχalda ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬim baqχize kːola
wa baqʼ tʼjerχʔun χadub ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼadawɬun wukʼina ɡʔjeldasa χadub ɡʔjes χirijab sadaqʼa kwanaze beɡʔula ɡʔjeb buɡeɬul ɡʔjesije kːoleb napaqʼa
χwarab jaɬuni ʒanawaraz tʃʼwarab χʼajwanaɬul ɡʔan ɡʔjes kwanaze beɡʔularo ʒiwɡo qχubɬitʃʼoɡo wukʼine dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
bitʃːante ɡʔjez dir amrabi tʼurazarize ʒalɡo munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːetʃʼoɡo rukʼine ɡuroni ɡʔjel χweze ruɡo allaɡʔasul χirijabɬun ɡʔaburab ʒo qχubɬizaburaɬuqχ dun wuɡo betʼjerhan ɡʔjezul ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul itsː
ʃːiwniɡi batʼijaw tʃijas χirijal sadaqʼabazul kwen kwanaze beɡʔularo kaʃiʃasul χʼaltʼuqχanasɡi ɡʔjeb kwanaze beɡʔularo
amma ʒindirɡo ɡʼaratsɡi kʔun witʃun wosaraw kaʃiʃasul laʁas ɡʔjeb kwanaze beɡʔula ɡʔjedinɡo kaʃiʃasul roqʼow ɡʔawuraw bokʔaraw tʃijasɡi kwanaze beɡʔula ɡʔjeb kwen
kaʃiʃasul jas kaʃiʃzabazul ɡurew tʃijasda jiɡoni ɡʔjeɬ kwanaze beɡʔularo qʼurban bakʼalde batʃʼarab kinab bataniɡi χirijab sadaqʼa
amma kaʃiʃasul jas qʼorolɬani jaɡi jatʼaɬani ɡʔjeɬul ɬimalɡi ɡʔjetʃʼoni ɡʔjej ɡʔitʼinab meχaɬɡo ɡʼadin naqχeɡi insul roqʼoj ɡʼumru ɡʔabunɡi jiɡoni ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjeɬ kwanaze beɡʔula insutsa kwanaleb χirijab kwen amma tsoniɡi tʃijar tʃijas ɡʔjeb kwanaze beɡʔularo
ɬatʃʼoɡo χirijab kwen kwanaraw batʼijaw tʃijas ɡʔjeb kwenaɬul baɡʔajab ɡʼarats kʔjeze kːola kaʃiʃase ɡʔjeb baɡʔajaɬul ʃːujil butʼaɡi tʼade ʒuban
kaʃiʃzabaz bitʃːaɡe betʼjerhanasul roqʼore ratʃʼunel ɡʼizrailazul χirijal sadaqʼabazul qʼimat χwezabize
batʼijal tʃaɡʼaz χirijab kwen kwanaze bitʃːaɡe ɡʔjeb sababɬun munaɡʔɡi tʼade kːun allaɡʔasda tsebe ɡʔjeɬul ʒawab kʔjeze kːetʃʼoɡo bukʼine dun wuɡo betʼjerhan ɡʔjezul ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul itsː
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazdaɡi tʼolabɡo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaldaɡi abe ɡʼizrailazul tsojas jaɬuni tʃijar χalqʼaɬul tʃijas sunnatab jaɡi nazrujaɬul qʼurban χʼisabalda tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban qχoleb buɡoni
ɡʔjeɬije batʃine kːola ʃːibɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ots kuj jaɡi deɡʼjen
ʃːibniɡi ʒaʁalɬi buɡeb χʼajwan qʼurbanaɬe qχoɡe ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb qʼabulɬularo
botsʼul roχʔdoɬa jaɬuni ɡʼi tsʼanazul reqχaɬa batʃun ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi sunnatab jaɬuni nazrujaɬul raqʼlil qʼurban qχoleb buɡoni qʼurban qʼabulɬize kːani χʼajwan ʃːibniɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb bukʼine kːola
betʼjerhanase qʼurban ɡʔaruɡe betsːal reqʼal ɬuqʼaral rakʔa bekaral tʼomol untabi ruɡel χʼajwanal betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurban χʼisabalda ɡʔjedinal χʼajwanal qʼurban bakʼalda tʼade rosuɡe
tsʼaqʼɡo χalatal jaɡi tsʼaqʼɡo qʼoqʼal boχdul ruɡeb ots jaɡi ɡʼijaɬoʒo qχweze beɡʔula sunnatab qʼurbanaɬe amma nazrujaɬul qʼurbanaɬe ɡʔjedinab χʼajwan jaraɡʔunaro
χʼanal qʼarab jaɬuni ɡʔjel naqχe raqχarab jaɡi ɡʔjel ɬuqʼarab χʼajwan betʼjerhanase qʼurban ɡʔabize beɡʔularo nuʒer rakʔalda kidaniɡi ɡʔjedinab ʒo ɡʔabuɡe
tʃijar χalqʼaɬul tʃijasuqχaɡi qʼabul ɡʔabuɡe ɡʔjedinab χʼajwan wa betʼjerhanasul χirijab niɡʼmat χʼisabalda ɡʔjedinab qʼurban qʼurban bakʼalde tʼade bosuɡe ɡʔjeb ɡʼaʒizab wa ʒaʁalab buɡeɬul ɡʔjedinab nuʒer qʼurban qʼabulɬize ɡʔjetʃʼo
wa betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼakdal tʃaqχdal jaɡi tsʼtsʼjel tʼintʃʼ ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ebelalda askʼob teze kːola mikʔabileb qʼojaldasa naqχe ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanɬun qχweze beɡʔula
amma ɡʔjeb ɡʔjeɬul ebelɡun tsadaqχ tsoɡo qʼojaɬ qχweze beɡʔularo ɡʔjeb qʼanun bukʼine buɡo botsʼujeɡi ɡʼi tsʼanazeɡi
betʼjerhanase barkalajaɬul qʼurban qχweze bokʔarab meχalda ɡʔjeb qʼabulɬuleb qʼaɡʼidajalda ɡʔabe kinabɡo
ɡʔjeb kwanaze kːola ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ radalalde ʃːibɡo naqχe teze beɡʔularo dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
dir amrabi tsʼune wa ɡʔjel tʼurazare dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
betʼjerhanasul tsʼar χʼaqʼir ɡʔabuɡe tsinɡi ditsaɡi ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔob dirɡo qʼudrat zaɡʔir ɡʔabize buɡo dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul itsː
dun wuɡo nuʒ misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃaraw wa dirɡo χalqʼɬun nuʒ ratʼa ɡʔaruraw allaɡʔ dun wuɡo betʼjerhan

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe ɡʔale betʼjerhanasul χirijal qʼojal ɡʔjel qʼojaz nuʒetsa dinijab dandeɬi aχʼize kːola ɡʔjel ruɡo ditsa tʃʼjezarural dinijal bajramqʼojal
anɬɡo qʼojaɬ χʼaltʼje ankʔabileb qʼo ʃamat
ɡʔale betʼjerhanasul χirijal bajramqʼojal ɡʔjel qʼojaz nuʒetsa dinijab dandeɬi aχʼila ɡʔjezije biχʔizaburab zamanalda
tʼotsebeseb motsʼaɬul antsʼila unqʼabileb qʼojaɬ markʼatʃʼul ɡʼuʒalda bajbiχʔula betʼjerhanasul pesaχ bajram
ɡʔjebɡo motsʼaɬul antsʼila ʃːuabileb qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanasul buɡʔurɡo tʃadazul bajram ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ nuʒetsa retʃːeb ɡʔjetʃʼjeb tʃed kwanaze kːola
bajramaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ nuʒetsa dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ kinabɡʼaɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe
ankʔabɡo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanal ɡʔare ankʔabileb qʼojaɬɡi dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬɡi kinabɡʼaɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe ditsa nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔalde ʃːwedal wa nuʒetsa ɡʔjenib tʼorʃːel bakʼarize bajbiχʔidal tʼorʃːalil tʼorazul tʼotsebeseb ɡul kaʃiʃasuqχe bose
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeb tʼorʃːalil ɡul betʼjerhanasda tsebe eχede borχun χʔwaɡʼjezabila nuʒedasa ɡʔjew razijab sadaqʼa χʼisabalda bitʃːante kaʃiʃas ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize ʃamatqʼojalda χaduseb qʼojaɬ
ɡʔjeb nizam tʼobitʼuleb qʼojaɬ nuʒetsa tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze kːola ʃːibniɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjer
ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi bukʼine kːola tsʼadudaɬun betʼjerhanase χirijab maχʼ baqχinabijaɬe zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʒubarab jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun kʼiɡo butʼa roɬul wa ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ qʼurban bakʼalda tʼade tʼjeze ɡinaɬul unqʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa tʃaʁirɡi bukʼine kːola
nuʒetsa tsʼijab roɬul tʃed jaɬuni tʃʼjer jaɡi tsʼijab buɡʼa roɬ kwanaze beɡʔularo nuʒerɡo allaɡʔasda tsebe qʼurbanɡi χirijab sadaqʼaɡi ɡʔabizeɡʼan kir nuʒ rukʼaniɡi ɡʔjeb buɡo nuʒer χadusel ɡʼjelazeɡi bukʼine buɡeb abadijab qʼanun
ʃamatqʼojalda χaduseb aj tʼorʃːalil tʼotsebeseb ɡul eχede borχarab qʼojalda χaduseb qʼojaldasa bajbiχʔun ankʔɡo ankʔ rikʼkʼje
kʼiqʼojalda antsʼabileb qʼojaɬ aj ankʔabileb ʃamatqʼojalda χaduseb qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanase tsʼijab roɬul χirijab sadaqʼa ɡʔabe
kir nuʒ ruɡoniɡi χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb sadaqʼa χʼisabalda betʼjerhanasda tsebe kʼiɡo betʃːarab tʃed bose ʃːibab tʃadije χʼaltʼizabe jefa tsʼurab ɬikʼab χanʒdal antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa ɡʔjeb buɡo tsʼijab tʼorʃːalidasa betʼjerhanasda tsebe bosize kːoleb χirijab sadaqʼa
tʃadil χirijab sadaqʼajalda tsadaqχ qʼurbanaɬe qχwela ʃːibniɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ankʔɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi tso otsɡi kʼiɡo kujɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo bukʼina tʃedɡun wa tʃaʁirɡun tsadaqχ betʼjerhanase kʔoleb tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanɬun aj betʼjerhanase χirijab maχʼ baqχinabuleb tsʼadul qʼurbanɬun
ɡʔjedinɡo munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe tso deɡʼjen qχwela kʼiɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjer raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬeɡi qχwela
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurban χʼisabalda tsʼijab tʼorʃːalidasa roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi kʼiɡo kʔjeɡʼjerɡi betʼjerhanasda tsebe eχedeɡi borχun χʔwaɡʼjezabize
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje nuʒetsa ʃːibniɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeb buɡo kir nuʒ rukʼaniɡi nuʒeeɡi χadusel ɡʼjelazeɡi bukʼine buɡeb abadijab qʼanun
nuʒerɡo aχikʔa jaɡi χurisa χʼaluqχen bakʼarulaɡo ɡʔjeb raɡʼa rakʔande ʃːun bakʼaruɡe ɡʼodore rortaral tʼoralɡi riʃːuɡe ɡʔjeb miskinaseɡi qʼwatʼisa tʃijaseɡi bukʼine te dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ

ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ nuʒerɡo χʼaltʼabi ɡʔaruɡe betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanal ɡʔare

ankʔabileb motsʼaɬul antsʼabileb qʼo bukʼina kipurimaɬul qʼo
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ nuʒerɡo χʼaltʼabi ɡʔaruɡe ʃːajɡureɬul kipurimaɬul qʼo buɡeɬul ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda tsebe nuʒedasa χasab qʼurban tʼobitʼuleb wa nuʒ munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬuleb qʼo
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ allaɡʔase mutʼiɡʼɬun kʼal kːwetʃʼjew tʃi ʃːiw ɡʔjew wataniɡi tʼaɡʼinawila wa χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qχwaɡʼala
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ χʼaltʼi ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔarawʃːinaw tʃi ditsa χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼaɡʼinawize buɡo
kinab bataniɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeb buɡo kir nuʒ rukʼaniɡi nuʒeeɡi χadusel ɡʼjelazeɡi bukʼine buɡeb abadijab qʼanun
ɡʔjeb qʼo bukʼina allaɡʔase mutʼiɡʼɬi zaɡʔir ɡʔabun nuʒetsa tʼobitʼuleb χʼalχʔijaɬul ʃamatqʼoɬun ɡʔjeb motsʼaɬul itʃʼabileb qʼojaɬul baqʼtʼjerχʔul ɡʼuʒaldasa bajbiχʔun naqχiseb qʼojaɬul baqʼtʼjerχʔul ɡʼuʒalde ʃːwezeɡʼan nuʒ χʼalχʔijalda rukʼine kːola

ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe ankʔabileb motsʼaɬul antsʼila ʃːuabileb qʼojaɬ qχoʃazul bajram bajbiχʔila wa ɡʔjeb tʼobitʼila ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ χalat baqχun
bajramaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje wa ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ kinabɡʼaɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe
ankʔabɡo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanal ɡʔare mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ naqχeɡi dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje wa betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanal ɡʔare ɡʔjeb kːola bajramaɬul aχiriseb qʼo ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬɡi ʃːibniɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe
ɡʔjele betʼjerhanas riχʔizarural χirijal bajramqʼojal ɡʔjel qʼojaz nuʒetsa dinijab dandeɬi aχʼize kːola wa betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanalɡi χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi ɡʔarize kːola tʼuran ruχʼulel qʼurbanalɡun roɬul χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi tsoɡidal qʼurbanalɡun tʃaʁiraɬul χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi ʃːibab qʼojaɬe tʃʼjezaburab qʼaɡʼidajalda
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo tʼubazabize kːola tsoɡidal qʼurbanazda tʼade aj betʼjerhanasul ʃamatqʼoɡi tsoɡidal χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi betʼjerhanase ɡʔarulel sunnatal wa nazrujaɬul χirijal sadaqʼabiɡun qʼurbanalɡi rikʼkʼintʃʼoɡo
palχʼasil ankʔabileb motsʼaɬul antsʼila ʃːuabileb qʼojaɬ nuʒerɡo χʼaluqχen roqʼobe bakʼarun χadub ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanase bajram tʼobitʼje bitʃːante tʼotsebeseb wa mikʔabileb qʼo χʼalχʔijaɬul qʼoɬun bukʼine
tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ biʃːun ɬikʼab piqχɡi bosun wa palʔmajaɬulɡi biɡʔarodulɡi ritsʼilɡi ɡʼarkʔalabiɡi rosun ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsere iχtilatalda rukʼa
ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasul bajram tʼobitʼje ʃːibab sonaɬ ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ χalat baqχun ɡʔjeb buɡo nuʒeeɡi χadusel ɡʼjelazeɡi bukʼine buɡeb abadijab qʼanun ʃːibab sonaɬul ankʔabileb motsʼaɬ tʼobitʼje ɡʔjeb bajram
bajramaɬul ankʔabɡo qʼojaɬ qχoʃazda ʒanir rukʼa ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailal ɡʔjel qʼojaz qχoʃazda ʒanir tʃʼjeze kːola
nuʒer naslujalda ɬan bukʼine ditsa nuʒ misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃarab meχalda nuʒ qχoʃazda ʒanir ɡʼumru ɡʔabun rukʼarabɬi dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
