ɡʼizrailazda ɬazabe naχutʃiraqχaɬe χʼaltʼizabize batsʼtsʼadab zajtunaɬul naχ duqχe bosejan kidaɡo naχutʃiraqχ bakun bukʼine
muqʼadasab tʃadiralda ʒanir betʼjerhanasul qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas naqχa ɬurab pardawalda tsere ruɡel naχutʃiraqχal ɡʔarunitsa rakize kːola kidaɡo baqʼtʼjerχʔul ɡʼuʒalda wa roɡʔineɡʼan ɡʔjenib kanɬi swine bitʃːaze beɡʔularo ɡʔjeb buɡo nuʒeeɡi χadusel ɡʼjelazeɡi bukʼine buɡeb abadijab qʼanun
batsʼtsʼadab mesedil naχutʃiraqχalda tʼad ruɡel ɡʼisːintʃiraqχazda ʒanib naχ tʃʼjezabize kːola ɡʔjes kidaɡo betʼjerhanasda tsebe
ɬikʼab roɬɡi bosun antsʼila kʼiɡo tʃed beʒe ʃːibab tʃadije χʼaltʼizabe jefa tsʼurab χanʒdal antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun kʼiɡo butʼa
ɡʔjel tʃadal ɬe betʼjerhanasda tsere batsʼtsʼadab mesedil stolalda tʼad anɬ anɬ tʃed ɬurab kʼiɡo si ɡʔabun
ʃːibab sijalda askʼob batsʼtsʼadab ladanɡi ɬe tʃadazdasa tsʼadul qʼurbanaɬul ɡʼadab χirijab maχʼ baqχinabize ɡʔjeb bukʼina betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɬoleb χirijab sadaqʼaɬun
kidaɡo ʃːibab ʃamatqʼojaɬ betʼjerhanasda tsebe tsʼijab tʃed ɬeze kːola ɡʔjeb bukʼina tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazul raqχaɬ dirɡun buɡeb abadijab qʼotʼijaɬul ɡʼalamatɬun
ɡʔjel tʃadal ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi rukʼina wa ɡʔjez ɡʔjel χirijab bakʼalda kwanaze kːola ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb buɡo kʼudijab χiraɬi betʼjerhanasul χirijal sadaqʼabazdasa ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul naslujaɬeɡi abadijaɬeɡo kʔurab butʼa
ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔow wukʼana tso tʃi ɡʔjesul ebel ɡʼizrailaj emen misrijaw wukʼana tso nuχaɬ ɡʼizrailazul tsoɡi tʃiɡun waʁize kːana ɡʔjew
wa ɡʔjeb bakʼalda betʼjerhanasul tsʼarɡi qʼabiχʼ ɡʔabun χʔandeze ɬuɡʔana ɡʼizrailaɬul was ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjew tʃi musaqχe watʃana ɡʔjesul ebelalda tsʼar ʃelomit bukʼana wa ɡʔjej danil qʼawmaldasa diwril jas kːolaan
ɡʔjew tʃi betʼjerhanasul χʼukmu ɬazeɡʼan ʒaniw tʼamuna
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas musada abuna
bitʃasul tsʼar qʼabiχʼ ɡʔaburaw ɡʔjew tʃi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe watʃe bitʃːante ɡʔjesul kʼal raɡʼarawʃːinaw tʃijas tsin ɡʔjesul botʼroda kweral ɬeze wa tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬ ɡʔjew ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwaze
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe ʃːiwniɡi tʃi allaɡʔasul tsʼar qʼabiχʼ ɡʔabun kʼaɬani ɡʔjesije ʒaza bukʼine buɡo
betʼjerhanasul tsʼar qʼabiχʼ ɡʔaburaw tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola bitʃːante ɡʔjedinaw tʃi tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬ ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwaze ɡʔjew ʃːiw wataniɡi ɡʼizrailaw wukʼa tʃijar χalqʼaɬul tʃi wukʼa bitʃasul adab reχun kʼaɬaraw tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola
ɡʔjedinɡo ɬitsaniɡi tʃi tʃʼwani ɡʔjewɡi tʃʼwaze kːola
kinab bataniɡi χʼajwan tʃʼwaraw tʃijas ɡʔjeb betsʼize kːola ɡʼumrujaɬuqχ ɡʼumru
tsoɡidaw tʃi ɡʼaʒiz ɡʔawuraw tʃijaseɡi ɡʔjebɡo ɡʔabize kːola
bekarab bakʼaɬuqχ bekarab bakʼ beraɬuqχ ber ɡʼusaɬuqχ ɡʼus kinab ʁaja insanas tsoɡidase ɡʔabun bataniɡi ɡʔjedinabɡo ɡʔjesijeɡi ɡʔabize kːola
χʼajwan tʃʼwaras ɡʔjeb betsʼize kːola insan tʃʼwaraw tʃʼwaze kːola
nuʒee kinazeɡo tso qʼanun bukʼine buɡo ɡʼizrailazeɡi tʃijar χalqʼaɬul tʃaɡʼazeɡi dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
musatsa ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʼizrailazda bitsana wa bitʃasul tsʼar qʼabiχʼ ɡʔabun kʼaɬaraw tʃi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa doweɡʼanɡi watʃun ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwana ɡʼizrailaz kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon

sinaj maɡʼarda betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe ditsa nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔalde ʃːwedal ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬɡi betʼjerhanasul ʃamat tʼubazabize kːola
anɬɡo sonaɬ χurɡi bekʔje tsʼolbol ʁabuɡi kʼure χʼaluqχenɡi bakʼare
ankʔabileb sonaɬ bitʃːante rakʔaɬ χʼuχʔbaqχize ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanasul ʃamataɬul son χurɡi bekʔuɡe tsʼolbol ʁabuɡi kʼuruɡe
χurib ʒibɡo biʒarab ʒojaɬulɡi kʼuritʃʼjeb ʁabujalda biʒarab tsʼolbolɡi χʼaluqχen bakʼaruɡe rakʔaɬ χʼuχʔbaqχize bitʃːaj
χʼalχʔijaɬul sonaɬ rakʔalda ʒibɡo biʒarabʃːinab niɡʼmat nuʒee kwen tʼjeχaɬe bukʼina nuʒeeɡi nuʒer laʁzaderijeɡi nuʒer χʼaltʼuqχabazeɡi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel tʃijar χalqʼaɬul ɡʼadamazeɡi
nuʒer ɡʼi botsʼujeɡi ɡʼalχul ʒanawarazeɡi rakʔalda ʒibɡo biʒarabʃːinab ʒo kwanaze beɡʔula
ɡʔjedinab ankʔɡo ʃamataɬul son rikʼkʼje aj ankʔɡo nuχaɬ ankʔɡo son ankʔɡo ʃamataɬul sonalda ʒanib kinabniɡi kʼiqʼojalda itʃʼɡo son kːoleb χʼalaɬ
ankʔabileb motsʼaɬul antsʼabileb qʼojaɬ aj kipurimaɬul qʼojaɬ tʼolabɡo ulkajalda raɡʼizabun sur puj
wa kʼiqʼojalda antsʼabileb son χirijab sonɬun ɬazabe ɡʔjeb sonaɬ ulkajaɬul tʼolalɡo ɡʼadamaze erkenɬi ʃːwela ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo jubilejaɬul son ɡʔjeb sonaɬ ʃːiwaw tʃijasuqχe tʼadbusːina ʒindirɡo umumuzul irs wa ʃːiwaw tʃi ʒindirɡo qχizan kulpataɬuqχeɡi naqχwusːina
bitʃːante kʼiqʼojalda antsʼabileb son nuʒee jubilejaɬul sonɬun bukʼine χurɡi bekʔuɡe ʒibɡo biʒarab buɡʼa roɬulɡi kʼuritʃʼjeb ʁabujalda biʒarab tsʼibilaɬulɡi χʼaluqχenɡi bakʼaruɡe
ɡʔjeb jubilejaɬul son buɡeɬul ɡʔjeb χirijab sonɬun bukʼa nuʒee wa ɡʔjeb sonaɬ kwanaj ʒibɡo biʒarab niɡʼmat
jubilejaɬul sonaɬ ʃːiwaw tʃijasuqχe tʼadbusːina ɡʔjesul umumuzul mulk
naɡaɡʔ ɬitsaniɡi ʒindirɡo mulk bitʃuleb jaɬuni bitʃun bosuleb buɡoni ɡʔjelda ɡʔorkʔob χʼilla ɡʔabuɡe
bitʃun rakʔ bosuleb buɡoni jubilejaɬul sonaldasa naqχe tʃan son arabali χʼisabaldeɡi bosun ɡʔabe daran bitʃulew tʃijasɡi batʃʼin bakʼarulel sonazul tʃan son χutʼun buɡebali χʼisabaldeɡi bosun ɡʔabize kːola rakʔaɬul baɡʔa
tsʼikʼkʼun sonal χutʼaralɡʼan rakʔaɬul baɡʔaɡi tsʼikʼkʼuna daɡʔal χutʼaralɡʼan baɡʔaɡi daɡʔɬula ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjenisa ʃːoleb χʼaluqχenɬidal ɡʔjes bitʃuleb buɡeb
tsotsaje rekʼkʼ ɡʔabuɡe allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼa dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
dir qʼanunal tsʼune dir amrabi tʼurazare ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuni nuʒerɡo ulkajalda ɬikʼab χʼinqʼi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ɡʼumru bukʼina nuʒee
rakʔaɬ ɡʔarzaɡo χʼaluqχenɡi kʔjela ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwanaze niɡʼmatɡi bukʼina wa paraχatab χʼinqʼi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ɡʼumruɡi bukʼina nuʒee
nuʒetsa tsʼjeχeze beɡʔula χurɡi bekʔitʃʼoni χʼaluqχenɡi bakʼaritʃʼoni ʃːib niʒetsa kwanaze buɡeb ankʔabileb sonaɬ in
anɬabileb sonaɬ ditsa nuʒede kʼudijab barakat reʃːtʼinabila wa ɡʔjeb sonaɬ nuʒee ɬabɡo sonaɬul qʼadaralda χʼaluqχen biʒizabila
mikʔabileb sonaɬ χurib χʔon χʔaleb meχalda ʒeɡi basrijab χʼaluqχen kwanalel rukʼina nuʒ wa itʃʼabileb sonaɬ tsʼijab tʼorʃːel bakʼarizeɡʼanɡi ɡʔjeɬ χʔiχʔila nuʒ
rakʔ abadijaɬeɡo bitʃize beɡʔularo ʃːajɡureɬul rakʔ dir kːola nuʒin abuni ruɡo ditsa reɡa raqχine bakʼ kʔural ɡʔalbal zamanaɬ ratʃʼaral aparaɡzabi
nuʒer ulkajalda rakʔ bitʃun bosulew ʃːiwaw tʃijas ɡʔjeɬul χwaʒainase iχtijar kʔjeze kːola ɡʔjeb naqχe bitʃun bosize
dur rakʔtsojaw miskinɬani wa ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo umumuzul rakʔul tso butʼa bitʃani witʃːante ɡʔjesul tsewesew ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi watʃʼine wa ɡʔjeb naqχe bitʃun bosize
ɡʔjedinaw ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi watitʃʼoni amma bitʃun bukʼarab rakʔ naqχe bosize ɡʼurab ɡʼarats ɡʔjesul ʒindirɡo batani
bitʃːante ɡʔjes rakʔ bitʃaraldasa naqχe aral sonal rikʼkʼine wa χutʼaral sonazuqχ ɡʼaratsɡi kʔun ɡʔjeb naqχe bosize
amma ɡʔjeb naqχe bitʃun bosize rakʔul χwaʒainasul res batitʃʼoni bitʃun bosaraw tʃijasuqχ χutʼila ɡʔjeb jubilejaɬul son tʼade ʃːwezeɡʼan jubilejaɬul sonaɬ rakʔ naqχe kʔjela ɡʔjeb ɡʔjeɬul tsewesew χwaʒainasuqχe tʼadbusːina
swerun qʼarab ʃaɡʔaralda ɬitsaniɡi ʒindirɡo mina bitʃani ɡʔjeb bitʃaraldasa naqχe ɬaɡʼalil bolʒalalda ʒanib ɡʔjeb naqχe bitʃun bosize iχtijar bukʼuna ɡʔjesul ɡʔjebɡoʃːinab meχaɬ mina tʼadbusːinabize res bukʼuna
swerun qʼarab ʃaɡʔaralda buɡeb ɡʔjeb mina bitʃaraw tʃijas ɬaɡʼalida ʒanib ɡʔjeb naqχe bitʃun bositʃʼoni ɡʔjeb abadijaɬɡo χutʼula bosaraw tʃijaseɡi ɡʔjesul naslabazeɡi jubilejaɬul sonaɬɡi ɡʔjeb naqχe kʔolaro
amma rosabaɬ ruɡel minabi rakʔaɬul butʼaɬun kːola ɡʔjel naqχe ritʃun rosize beɡʔula wa jubilejaɬul sonaɬ ritʃaral tʃaɡʼazuqχe naqχe kʔjeze kːola
lewijilazul iχtijar buɡo ɡʔjezul swerun qʼaral ʃaɡʔarazda ruɡel ʒiderɡo minabi bokʔarab meχalda naqχe ritʃun rosize
ɡʔjel tsoɡidal lewitaze ritʃun rukʼun rataniɡi lewijilazul ʃaɡʔaralda bitʃarab mina jubilejaɬul sonaɬ naqχe kʔjeze kːola ʃːajɡureɬul lewitazul ʃaɡʔarazda ruɡel minabi ɡʼizrailazul tsoɡidal qʼawmazda ɡʔorkʔob lewijil naslabaze kʔurab irsɬun kːola
ɡʔjezul ʃaɡʔarazda swerun buɡeb botsʼi χʔiχʔuleb meʁ rakʔɡi bitʃize beɡʔularo ɡʔjeb lewitazul abadijab irs kːola
dur ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi miskinɬani wa jaziqχɬani ɡʔjesije kumek ɡʔabe wa duqχeɡo watʃe ɡʔjew bitʃːante ɡʔjes qʼwatʼisa watʃʼaraw ɡʔobol jaɬuni aparaɡ χʼisabalda duda tsadaqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabize
dur ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi duda askʼow tʃʼjeze te ɡʔjesuqχa χajir bosuɡe durɡo allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼa
dujeɡo tʼade χajir ʃːwezeɬun ɡʔjesuqχe qʼarzaɬe ɡʼaratsɡi kʔoɡe ɡʔjesije tʃed χinkʼɡi bitʃuɡe
dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ ditsa misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃana nuʒ χanaanaɬul rakʔ nuʒee kʔjeze wa nuʒ dirɡo χalqʼɬun rukʼinaɬe ɡʼolo
dur rakʔtsojaw miskinɬani wa ʒiwɡo ʒintsaɡo duje witʃani laʁ ɡʼadin χʼaltʼizawuɡe ɡʔjew
bitʃːante ɡʔjew qʼwatʼisa kːun watʃaraw χʼaltʼuqχan χʼisabalda jubilejaɬul son tʼade ʃːwezeɡʼan duje χʼaltʼize
ɡʔjeb sonaɬ ɡʔjew erkenɬila wa tsadaqχ ɬimalɡun ʒindirɡo qχizan kulpatalde wa umumuzul rakʔalde tʼadwusːina
kinalɡo ɡʼizrailal ditsa misrijaɬul laʁɬijaldasa naqχe ratʃaral dir laʁzal kːola wa ɡʔjel naqχeɡi laʁɬijalde ritʃize beɡʔularo
ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasda tʼad zulmutʃiɬun wukʼunɡe durɡo allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼa
duje laʁzal qʼwariɡʼarab meχaɬ nuʒeda sweruqχ ruɡel qʼwatʼisa χalqʼazuqχa ritʃun rose laʁzalɡi ʁarawaʃalɡi
ɡʔjedinɡo nuʒetsa ɡʔjel ritʃun rosize beɡʔula nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor ɡʼumru ɡʔabun ruɡel tʃijar χalqʼazul tʃaɡʼazuqχa wa nuʒer rakʔalda ɡʔarural ɡʔjezul naslabazuqχa wa ɡʔjel rukʼina nuʒer mulkɬun
ɡʔjel rukʼina nuʒer mulkɬun nuʒer ɬimalazeɡi abadijab irsɬun ritʃːante ɡʔjel rukʼine nuʒee laʁzalɬun amma nuʒerɡo χalqʼalda aj ɡʼizrailazda tʼad zulmu ɡʔabuɡe
nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabulew tʃijar rakʔaɬul tʃi betʃeɬani dur χalqʼtsojawin abuni miskinɬani wa tʃijarase jaɡi ɡʔjesul χalqʼaɬul tsoɡi tʃijase laʁɬijalde ɡʔjes ʒiwɡoɡi witʃani
ɡʔjew naqχe witʃun wosize beɡʔula ɡʔjesul ɡʼaɡaraw tʃijas witʃun wosize beɡʔula ɡʔjew
insul jaɡi ebelaɬul watsas jaɡi tsoɡi bokʔaraw ɡʼaɡaraw tʃijas jaɬuni ɡʔjesije ʒindijeɡo ɡʼurab ɡʼarats ʃːun buɡoni ʒinditsaɡo ʒiwɡo erken ɡʔawizeɡi beɡʔula
bitʃːante ɡʔjew witʃun wosaraw tʃijasɡi ɡʔjesɡi jubilejaɬul sonalde ʃːwezeɡʼan χutʼaral sonal rikʼkʼine ɡʔjesul baɡʔa ɡʔabize kːola ɡʔjel sonalɡi kːun watʃaraw χʼaltʼuqχanase ɡʔjel sonazuqχ kːoleb muχʔɡi χʼisabalde bosun
jubilejaɬul son ʃːweze ʒeɡi ɡʼjemeral sonal χutʼun ruɡoni ʒiwɡo witʃuleɬul ɡʔjesije ʃːun bukʼarab ɡʼartsul tsʼikʼkʼaraseb butʼa naqχe kʔjeze kːola ɡʔjes
ɡʔjedinɡo jubilejaɬul son ʃːweze daɡʔal sonal χutʼun ratani ɡʔjel sonazda reqʼon kʔjeze kːola ʒiwɡo erken ɡʔawijaɬuqχ muχʔ
χwaʒainase ɡʔjew wukʼine kːola kːun watʃaraw χʼaltʼuqχan χʼisabalda ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasda tʼad zulmu χʼal ɡʔabize bitʃːaze beɡʔularo nuʒetsa
witʃun wosaraw tʃi erken ɡʔawun ɡʔjetʃʼoni jubilejaɬul sonaɬ erkenɬula ɡʔjewɡi ɡʔjesul ɬimalɡi
tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailal dir laʁzal ruɡeɬul ɡʔjel ruɡo ditsa misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃaral dir laʁzal dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ

nuʒeeɡo ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔzabi ɡʔaruɡe ʒidee suʒda ɡʔabizeɬun kinalɡʼaɡi suratal muqʼadasal χʼubal jaɬuni rekʼkʼaral ɡantʃʼazul sipatal nuʒerɡo rakʔalda eχetuɡe wa ɡʔjezije laʁɬi ɡʔabuɡe dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
dir ʃamatqʼojal tʼurazare wa dir muqʼadasab ruqʼaɬul adab ɡʔabe dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
dir qʼanunal tʼurazaruni wa dir amrabazda reqʼon χʔwadani
ditsa nuʒee ʒindir zamanalda tsʼad bazabila rakʔaɬ χʼaluqχenɡi ɡʔarzaɡo kʔjela ʁutʼbuzda piqχɡi ɡʼjemerab biʒila
tsʼibil barʃːuleb zamanaldaɡi lal tʼami ɬuɡʼilaro rekʔari bajbiχʔizeɡʼanɡi bakʼarize tsʼibil bukʼina ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔarzaɡo kwanaze kwenɡi χʼinqʼi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb paraχatab ɡʼumruɡi bukʼina nuʒee
ditsa raqʼlilab ɡʼumru kʔjela nuʒer ulkajaɬe nuʒ paraχatɡo kʔiʒila wa sardil χʼinqʼi nuʒee bukʼinaro ditsa nuʒer rakʔaldasa ɡʼalχul ʒanawaral naqχe ratʃaqχila wa tuʃmanasul χetʃ nuʒer rakʔalde ɡʼuntʼilaro
tuʃbabi nuʒeqχa ɬutila wa nuʒer χwaltʃabazdaɬun ʃːapila
ʃːuɡojas nusɡo tʃʼwala nusɡojas antsʼazarɡo tʃʼwala nuʒer χwaltʃabaz tʃʼwan ɡʼodor ɬela nuʒer tuʃbabi
tsinɡi dun nuʒeqχ walaɡʔila ɬikʼɬijaɬe ɬimal ɡʼjemeral kʔjela wa nuʒerɡun ɡʔaburab dirɡo qʼotʼi tʼubazabila
tsʼijab χʼaluqχen bakʼarize meχ ʃːwela amma arab sonaɬ biʒarab ʒeɡi ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwanaze ɡʼurab bukʼina nuʒee ɡʼjemerɬijaɬ ɡʔjeb naqχe baze kːeze buɡo
ditsa dirɡo muqʼadasab ruqʼ bala nuʒ ruɡeb bakʼalda wa nuʒ reχun telaro
dun nuʒɡun wukʼina nuʒer allaɡʔɬun nuʒ dir χalqʼɬun rukʼina
dun wuɡo betʼjerhan misrijaɬul laʁɬijaldasa tarqχan ɡʔarun ɡʔjenisa nuʒ naqχe ratʃaraw nuʒer allaɡʔ nuʒer ɡorboda ban bukʼarab bakʼab laʁɬijaɬul rukʔ bekana ditsa wa nuʒ borχatɡo betʼjerɡi kːun χʔwadulelɬun ɡʔaruna
amma nuʒ diqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼoni wa kinalɡo ɡʔjel amrabi tʼurazaritʃʼoni
nuʒetsa dir qʼanunal naqχ tʃʼwani wa dir tʼadqʼajal ɡʼadaqχ rositʃʼoni nuʒetsa dir tʼolalɡo amrabi tʼurazaritʃʼoni wa dir qʼotʼi χwezabuni
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsa nuʒee ɡʔabulebɡi ɬaj ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsa nuʒeda tʼade kʼudijab χʼinqʼi reʃːtʼinabila berzul kanɬi bosuleb wa tʃorχoje ɡʼazab kʔoleb karanzul untiɡi tsʼadul untiɡi bitʃːala nuʒetsa χur bekʔila amma ɡʔjeb ɡʼadada kːela ɡʔjenisa χʼaluqχen nuʒer tuʃbabaz kwanala
ditsa diwan qʼotʼila nuʒee wa tuʃbabaz nuʒeda tʼad berɡʔjenɬi bosila nuʒ riχaraz nuʒeda tʼad kwerʃːel ɡʔabila wa χʼinqʼi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb bakʼaldaɡitsin ɬutanqχilel rukʼina nuʒ
ɡʔjebmeχaldaɡi nuʒ dije mutʼiɡʼɬitʃʼoni ditsa ʒeɡi ankʔɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼun ʒaza ɡʔabila nuʒee
ditsa nuʒer tʃʼuχʼijaɬul ɡabur bekila ditsa nuʒeda tʼad zobal paχʔude swerizarila rakʔ mazɡaralde swerizabila
tʼolabɡo nuʒer qʼuwatɡi ɡʔorodaqχ ina nuʒer χurzabaqχ ʃːibɡo biʒilaro ʁutʼbuz piqχɡi kʔjelaro
ɡʔjebmeχaɬɡi dida dande tʃʼani wa dije mukʼurɬize bokʔitʃʼoni ditsa ʒeɡi ankʔɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼun ʒaza ɡʔabila nuʒee
ditsa ɡʼalχul ʒanawaral ritʃːala nuʒeda tʼade wa ɡʔjez tʃʼwala nuʒer ɬimalɡi ɡʼi botsʼiɡi nuʒɡi tʼadejaldasa tʼade daɡʔɬila nuʒer nuχalɡi tʃʼuntila
ɡʔjebmeχaɬɡi nuʒ kantʼitʃʼoni wa dida dande tʃʼun χʔwadani
dunɡi tʃʼjela nuʒeda dande ditsa ʒeɡi ankʔɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼun ʒaza ɡʔabila nuʒee
dir qʼotʼi χwezaburaɬuqχ ditsa qʼisasaɬul χwaltʃen bitʃːala nuʒeda tʼade ʃaɡʔarazda ʒanir raχtʃilin nuʒ ɬuɡʔani ditsa kweʃab χwalil unti bitʃːala nuʒeda tʼade wa tuʃmanas kwerde rosila nuʒ
ditsa nuʒee tʃed muqʼsanɬizabila antsʼɡo tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬe tso kor ɡʼjeze buɡo kinabɡo tʃed beʒize tsʼadirabazdaɡi tsʼan kʔjela nuʒee tʃadil keskal nuʒetsa tʃed kwanala amma nuʒ ɡʔjeɬ ɡʼortsʼilaro
ɡʔjebmeχaɬɡi nuʒ diqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼoni wa dida dande tʃʼun χʔwadani
dunɡi tʃʼjela nuʒeda dande ɡʔalaɡab tsːidaɬ wa ʒeɡi ankʔɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼun ʒaza ɡʔabila ditsa nuʒee
nuʒerɡo ɬimalazul ɡʔan kwanaze buɡo nuʒetsa
ditsa nuʒer rorχaɬabazul muqʼadasal bakʼal riχːizarila jasikʼo allaɡʔzabaze ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼulel bakʼal ʁurila wa rekaral jasikʼo allaɡʔzabazda tʼade nuʒer ʒanazabiɡi reχila nuʒedasa dir rakʼɡi busːina
ditsa ʃːuʃːaqχ rala nuʒer ʃaɡʔaral nuʒer muqʼadasal bakʼal tʃʼuntizarila wa nuʒer tsʼadul qʼurbanazul ɡʔuinab maχʼ tʼokʼaɬ qʼabul ɡʔabilaro
ditsa tʃʼoboɡoɬizabila nuʒer rakʔ ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabize ratʃʼaral nuʒer tuʃbabitsin riχːun χutʼuleb χʼalaɬ
ditsa χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔor rikʔ rikʔizarila wa dirɡo χwaltʃadaɬun tsere qʼotʼila nuʒ nuʒer ulka tʃʼoboɡoɬila ʃaɡʔaralɡi tʃʼwadnazde swerila
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ rakʔaɬ ʃamataɬul sonazul lazat bosila nuʒ tuʃbabazul rakʔalda ruɡebɡʼan zamanaɬ tʃʼoboɡoɬarab nuʒer rakʔaɬe χʼalχʔi ʃːwela wa ɡʔjeɬ ʃamataɬul sonazul lazat bosila
nuʒetsa ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bukʼarab meχalda tʼurazaritʃʼjelʃːinal ʃamatazul sonal rikʼkʼun χʼalχʔijalda bukʼina rakʔ tʃʼoboɡo χutʼarabɡʼan meχaɬ
tʃijar rakʔalde kːaral nuʒer tʃʼaɡo χutʼarazul rekʼjeɬe ditsa batʃʼinaburab χʼinqʼijaɬ ɡʔuri purab meχaɬ ʃurarab tʼanχil ɡʔarkʔiqχatsin tʼurila ɡʔjel χwaltʃakʔa kiniɡin ɬutila ɡʔjel wa ɡʼodor kːela ɡʔjezda χaduw ʃːiwɡo ɬuɡʔun ɡʔjetʃʼjeb meχaɬɡi
tsotsada tenkelaɡo ɬutila ɡʔjel χwaltʃakʔa χwasarɬize ɬutulel tʃaɡʼi kiniɡin wiχʔuda tuʃman ɡʔjetʃʼoniɡi tuʃbabazda dande tʃʼjeze ɡʼurab qʼuwat nuʒeɬ bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo
ɡʔjedin χwela nuʒ tʃijar χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔor nuʒer tuʃbabazul rakʔalda tʼaɡʼina nuʒ
naqχe χutʼarazul daɡʔabɡo qʼadar tuʃbabazul rakʔalda tʃʼaɡoɡo turila ʒiderɡoɡi umumuzulɡi munaɡʔal sababɬun
bukʼaniɡi ʒiderɡoɡi umumuzulɡi munaɡʔaze wa ʒidetsaɡo dida dande ɡʔarural taqʼsirazeɡun tʼjeqʼɬabaze ɡʔjel mukʼurɬize beɡʔula
ɡʔjeb sababɬunɬidal dir ɡʔjezda tsːin baqχarab wa ɡʔjel tuʃbabazul rakʔalde tʼurizarural ɡʔjezul ritsːatal rakʼal
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsa rakʼalde ʃːwezabila jaqʼubilɡun ɡʔaburab dirɡo qʼotʼi isχʼaqʼilɡun ɡʔaburab dirɡo qʼotʼi wa ibraɡʔimilɡun ɡʔaburab dirɡo qʼotʼi wa ɡʔab rakʔɡi rakʼalde ʃːwezabila
ɡʔab rakʔ tʃʼoboɡoɬarab wa χalqʼ ɡʔanisa naqχe qʼotʼarab meχaɬ rakʔaɬ lazat bosize buɡo ɡʔorkʔor ritʃːan rukʼaralʃːinal ʃamataɬul sonazul χʼuχʔ baqχijaldasa tʃʼaɡo χutʼaral ɡʼadamaz ʒiderɡo ɡʼajib batʃːize buɡo dir amrabi naqχtʃʼwaraɬuqχ wa dir qʼanunal ɡʼadaqχ rositʃʼoɬijaɬuqχ
amma ɡʔjeb meχaldaɡi tuʃbabazul rakʔalda ditsa ɡʔjel reχun telaro tʼuran naqχtʃʼwalaro wa tʼaɡʼinarilaro ɡʔjezulɡun ɡʔaburab dirɡo qʼotʼi χweze telaro dun wuɡo betʼjerhan ɡʔjezul allaɡʔ
dirɡo χalqʼɬun rukʼine batʼijal χalqʼazdaɡi riχʔulaɡo misrijaldasa ditsa naqχe ratʃaral ɡʔjezul umumuzulɡun ɡʔaburab qʼotʼi rakʼalde batʃʼina dida dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
ɡʔjele betʼjerhanas ʒindidaɡoɡi ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔor ɡʔarural wa sinaj maɡʼarda musadasan reʃːtʼaral qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi maɬa qχwajalɡi

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazda kʼaɬaj wa ɡʔjezda abe ɬitsaniɡi ʒiwɡo jaɡi tsewesew tʃi betʼjerhanase nazru ɡʔawize beɡʔula ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasuqχ kʔjeze kːoleb χʼaqʼɡi kʔun
ɡʔjew qʼoɡojaldasa tʼade arab wa ɬabqʼoɡo sonaldasa tʼade intʃʼjeb riɡʔaɬul biχʔintʃi wuɡoni ɡʔjesuqχ kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ɡʼartsul ʃekel kʔjeze kːola muqʼadasab tʃadiralda χʔwaduleb ʃekel
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬuqχ ɬeberɡo ɡʼartsul ʃekel
ʃːuɡojaldasa tʼade arab wa qʼoɡo sonaldasa tʼade intʃʼjeb riɡʔaɬul wasasuqχ qʼoɡo ʃekel jasaɬuqχ antsʼɡo ʃekel
tso motsʼaldasa tʼade arab wa ʃːuɡo sonaldasa tʼade intʃʼjeb riɡʔaɬul ɬimaduqχ wasasuqχ ʃːuɡo ʃekel ɡʼartsul jasaɬuqχ ɬabɡo ʃekel ɡʼartsul
ɬabqʼoɡo sonaldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul biχʔintʃijasuqχ antsʼila ʃːuɡo ʃekel tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬuqχ antsʼɡo ʃekel
amma nazru ɡʔaburaw tʃi tsʼaqʼɡo resuqʼaw wuɡoni wa ɬazaburab qʼadaralda χʼaqʼ kʔjeze ɡʔjesul res batitʃʼoni ɡʔjew kaʃiʃasda tsewe watʃine kːola ɡʔjesul buɡoɬiɡi χʼisabalde bosun kaʃiʃas ɡʔjesul baɡʔa tʃʼjezabize bukʼine
ɡʼi botsʼul raqχaɬ nazru ɡʔabun bukʼun kinabɡʼaɡi qʼurbanaɬe jaraɡʔuneb χʼajwan betʼjerhanase kʔoleb buɡoni ɡʔjeb χʼajwan betʼjerhanasul χiraɬiɬun kːola
ɡʔjeb χʼajwan χisun tsoɡi χʼajwan kʔjeze beɡʔularo χʼalaqʼab χʼajwanaɬuqχ kʔarijabɡi χisize beɡʔularo kʔarijab χʼajwanaɬuqχ χʼalaqʼabɡi χisize beɡʔularo amma nazru ɡʔaburaw tʃijas ɡʔjeb χʼajwan tsoɡidaɬuqχ χisani ɡʔjeb kʼijabɡoɡi betʼjerhanasul χiraɬiɬun kːola
betʼjerhanas qχubabɬun ɬazaburab wa qʼurban ɡʔabize ɡʔuqʼarab χʼajwan kʔjeze ɬitsaniɡi nazru ɡʔabun buɡoni ɡʔjeb kaʃiʃasda tsebe batʃine kːola
wa kaʃiʃas ɡʔjelda reqʼarab baɡʔa tʃʼjezabize kːola ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔa kaʃiʃas abuqχe bukʼina
χʼajwanaɬul χwaʒainase ɡʔjeb χʼajwan ʒindijeɡo teze bokʔani bitʃːante ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔjeze ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔajalda tʼade ʃːujil butʼaɡi ʒuban
ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi betʼjerhanase ʒindirɡo mina nazru ɡʔabuni minajaɬul χal ʃalɡi ɡʔabun kaʃiʃas ɡʔjelda reqʼarab baɡʔa tʃʼjezabila ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔa kaʃiʃas abuqχe bukʼina
minajaɬul χwaʒainase mina ʒindijeɡo teze bokʔani bitʃːante ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔjeze ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔajalda tʼade ʃːujil butʼaɡi ʒuban wa mina ɡʔjesije χutʼila
ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi ʒindirɡo umumuzul irsɬun kːoleb χur betʼjerhanase nazru ɡʔabuni ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔa ɡʔabize kːola kiɡʼan χʔon χʔaleb χur ɡʔjeb buɡebali χʼisabaldeɡi bosun ɡʔjenibe χʔarab ʃːibab purtʃʼinadul χomeraɬuqχ
jubilejaɬul sonaɬ ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi ʒindirɡo χur betʼjerhanase nazru ɡʔabuni ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔa χisularo
amma jubilejaɬul son un χadub pulanaw tʃijas χur betʼjerhanase nazru ɡʔabuni ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔa ɡʔabize kːola tʼasijab jubilejaɬul son ʃːwezeɡʼan tʃan son χutʼun buɡebali χʼisabaldeɡi bosun aral sonazuqχ baɡʔaɡi tʼasa baqχun
ɡʔjew tʃijase χur ʒindijeɡo teze bokʔani bitʃːante ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔjeze ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔajalda tʼade ʃːujil butʼaɡi ʒuban tsinɡi χur ɡʔjesije χutʼila
amma ɡʔjeɬuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔun bukʼun batitʃʼoni wa tsoɡi tʃijase ɡʔjeb χur bitʃani tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔjeb tʼad busːinabize res bukʼunaro
nazru ɡʔaburab amma χʼaqʼ kʔjetʃʼjeb χur jubilejaɬul sonaɬ χwaʒainasuqχe tʼadbusːunaro ɡʔjeb tʼuban betʼjerhanase batʼa ɡʔaburab ɡʔjesul χiraɬiɬun χutʼula wa daimɡo kaʃiʃasul mulkɬun ɬuɡʔuna
tʃijaqχa bitʃun bosarab wa ʒindirɡo umumuzul ɡureb χur ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi betʼjerhanase nazru ɡʔabuni
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔa ɡʔabize jubilejaɬul son ʃːwezeɡʼan χutʼaral sonalɡi χʼisabalde rosun ɡʔjew tʃijas ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeɬuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔjeze kːola ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasul χiraɬiɬun kːola
jubilejaɬul sonaɬ ɡʔjeb χur ʒindirɡo umumuzul irsɬun ɡʔjeb kːolew tʼotsewesew χwaʒainasuqχe tʼadbusːinabize kːola
kinabɡo ʒojaɬul baɡʔa tʃʼjezabize kːola tʃadiralda χʼaltʼizabuleb aj qʼoɡo ɡera buɡeb ʃekelɡi χʼisabalde bosun
ɡʼi botsʼul tʼotsebe ɡʔaburab tʼintʃʼ nazru ɡʔabize beɡʔularo ɡʔjeb ɡʔadinɡoɡi betʼjerhanasul buɡo betʃe bataniɡi kʔjeɡʼjer jaɡi burutʼ bataniɡi ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasul kːola
amma ɡʔjeb qχubab χʼajwanaɬul tʼintʃʼ buɡoni ɡʔjeɬuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔjeze beɡʔula ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔajalda tʼade ʃːujil butʼaɡi ʒuban ɡʔjeɬuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔun ɡʔjetʃʼoni ɡʔjeb tʃʼjezaburab baɡʔajalda bitʃila
ɬilniɡi iχtijar ɡʔjetʃʼo ʒindirɡo buɡoɬijaldasa betʼjerhanase χerem
insan χerem ɡʔawun wuɡoni ɡʔjew χʼaqʼɡi kʔun erken ɡʔawize beɡʔularo ɡʔjew tʃʼwaze kːola
tʼolabɡo χʼaluqχenaɬul aj χurisa ʃːwarab tʼorʃːalilɡi aχikʔa bakʼararab piqχilɡi antsʼil butʼa
antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa ʒindijeɡo teze bokʔaraw tʃijas ɡʔjeɬuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔjeze kːola ɡʔjeɬul baɡʔajalda tʼade ʃːujil butʼaɡi ʒuban
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʼi botsʼul antsʼil butʼaɡi weχʔasul tʼil kʼutʼarab ʃːibab antsʼabileb χʼajwan ɡʔjebɡi betʼjerhanasul χiraɬiɬun kːola
antsʼil butʼajaɬul χʼajwan ɬikʼabiʃː kweʃabiʃː balaɡʔize kːolaro wa tsotsazuqχ χisize beɡʔularo naɡaɡʔ ɬitsaniɡi ɡʔjeb χisani kʼijabɡo betʼjerɡʔanasul kːola χisarab χʼajwanɡi χʼaqʼɡi kʔun naqχe bosize beɡʔularo
ɡʔjele betʼjerhanas sinaj maɡʼarda musadasan ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalde reʃːtʼaral amrabi

misrijaldasa ɡʼizrailal qʼwatʼire raqχun kʼiabileb sonaɬul kʼiabileb motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ rikʼkʼje ʃːibab qʼawmkːun wa tuχumkːun sijaχʼ ɡʔabun ʃːiwaw biχʔintʃijasul tsʼarɡi qχwan
raʁuje jaraɡʔunel qʼoɡo sonaldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul ɡʼizrailal rikʼkʼje wa ɡʔjezul qʼoqʼabi ɡʔarun tsʼaral qχwaj
ʃːibab qʼawmaɬul kʼudijazda ɡʔorkʔosa tso tso tʃi nuʒee χʼalaje wukʼine te
ɡʔale nuʒee kumek ɡʔabize ruɡel tʃaɡʼazul tsʼaral
ruwimil qʼawmaldasa ʃedeuril was elitsur
ʃimeonil qʼawmaldasa tsuriʃadajil was ʃelumiel
jaɡʔudal qʼawmaldasa ɡʼaminadawil was naχʼʃon
isːaχaril qʼawmaldasa tsuaril was netaniel
zewulunil qʼawmaldasa χelonil was eliaw
jusupil qʼawmaldasa
jefraimil qʼawmaldasa ammiɡʔudil was eliʃamaɡʼ
manasːil qʼawmaldasa pedatsuril was ɡamliel
bunjaminil qʼawmaldasa ɡideonil was awidan
danil qʼawmaldasa amiʃadajil was aχijezer
aʃeril qʼawmaldasa oχranil was paɡiel
ɡadil qʼawmaldasa deɡuelil was elijasaf
naftalil qʼawmaldasa jenanil was aχir
ɡʔal kːola ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼaɬul qʼawmazul tʼasa riʃːaral kʼudijal ɡʼizrailaɬul butʼrul
musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi tsʼar tsʼarkːun reχsaral ɡʔjel tʃaɡʼiɡun tsadaqχ
χalqʼaɬul dandeɬi aχʼana kʼiabileb motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ ɡʼizrailazul ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi reχson qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral kinalɡo biχʔinal rikʼkʼana
betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjedin rikʼkʼjen ɡʔabuna ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬul sinajaɬul salul awlaqχalda ɡʔjel rukʼaɡo
ɡʼizrailil tʼotsewesew was ruwimil qʼawmaldasa qʼoɡo sonaldasa aral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
ruwimil qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
ʃimeonil qʼawmaldasa qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
ʃimeonil qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
ɡadil qʼawmaldasa qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
ɡadil qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
jaɡʔudal qʼawmaldasa qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
jaɡʔudal qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
isːaχaril qʼawmaldasa qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
isːaχaril qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
zewulunil qʼawmaldasa qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
zewulunil qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
jusupil wasazul aj jefraimil wa manasːil qʼawmazdasa qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul qχizanɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
jefraimil qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
manasːil qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
bunjaminil qʼawmaldasa qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
bunjaminil qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
danil qʼawmaldasa qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
danil qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
aʃeril qʼawmaldasa qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
aʃeril qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
naftalil qʼawmaldasa qʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun son baral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel kinalɡo biχʔinal reχsana irɡadal tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
naftalil qʼawmaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   tʃi
ɡʔjel ruɡo musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʼizrailaɬul antsʼila kʼijabɡo qʼawmaɬul ʃːibaldasa tso tso tʼasa riʃːaral kʼudijazɡi rikʼkʼaral biχʔinal
qʼoɡo sonaldasa aral wa raʁuje jaraɡʔunel tʼolɡo ɡʼizrailal rikʼkʼana ɡʔjezul ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
ɡʔjezul kinawniɡi watana   tʃi
amma ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ rikʼkʼintʃʼo lewijil qʼawmaɬul naslabi
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
lewijil qʼawm rikʼkʼunɡe wa tsoɡidal ɡʼizrailazul sijaχʼalda ʁorɬ ɡʔjezul tsʼaral qχwaɡe
muqʼadasab tʃadirɡi ɡʔjeɬul kinabɡo qʼajiɡi kinabɡo ɡʔjelda χurχarab ʒoɡi lewijilazda tʼadqʼaj bitʃːante ɡʔjez tʃadir batʃːize wa ɡʔjeɬulɡi ɡʔjeɬul qʼaji tsʼajaɬulɡi tʼalabɡi ɡʔabize ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bakʼɡi ɡʔjez tʃadiralda sweruqχ ɡʼutsʼize kːola
nuχda raqχuneɬul muqʼadasab tʃadir biχːize wa tʼatʼala ɬeze buɡo lewitaz wa tʃʼjel ɡʔaburab bakʼalda ɡʔjezɡo eχetizeɡi bakʼarizeɡi buɡo ɡʔjel ɡurel batʼijaw tʃi tʃadiralda askʼowe ɡʼaɡarɬani ɡʔjew tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola
bitʃːante χutʼaral ɡʼizrailazul qʼawmaz ʒiderɡo tʃadral tʃʼwaze ʃːibab qʼawmaɬe biχʔizaburab bakʼalda ʃːibab askaraɬ ɡʔjenib ʒindirɡo bajraqχɡi tʃʼwaze bitʃːante
amma lewitazul tʃadral rukʼine kːola qʼotʼijaɬul tʃadiralda sweruqχ ɡʼizrailaɬul χalqʼ allaɡʔasul tsːidakʔa tsʼunun bukʼine lewijilal rukʼine ruɡo qʼotʼijaɬul tʃadiraɬul qχarawulzabiɬun
ɡʼizrailaz kinabɡo tʼubazabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon

betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
bitʃːante ɡʼizrailaz tʃadral tʃʼwaze dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda sweruqχ ɡʔjeldasa daɡʔaɬ rikʼkʼadeɡʼan ʒide ʒider qʼawmaɬul wa insul aɡʔlujaɬul bajraqχɡi tʃʼwan
bitʃːante jaɡʔudal askaraɬul bajraqχ tʃʼwaze baqʼbakːul raqχaldeχun ɡʔjenib ɡʔjez tʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabize jaɡʔudal qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw ɡʼaminadawil was naχʼʃon
naχʼʃonil bojalda   biχʔintʃi
bitʃːante ɡʔjesda χaduseb bakʼalda isːaχaril qʼawmaɬ tʃʼjel ɡʔabize isːaχaril qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw tsuaril was netaniel
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
ɡʔjezdasa dobeχun tʃʼjel ɡʔabila zewulunil qʼawmaɬ zewulunil qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw χelonil was eliaw
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
jaɡʔudal askaralda ʃːibab bo rikʼkʼun kinawniɡi   biχʔintʃi biʃːunɡo tsere saparazde ɡʔjel raqχine ruɡo
bitʃːante qʼilbajaɬul raqχalda ruwimil askaraɬul bajraqχ tʃʼwaze wa ɡʔjezul bojaz ɡʔjenib tʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabize ruwimil qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw ʃedeuril was elitsur
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
ɡʔjezda dobeχun tʃʼjel ɡʔabila ʃimeonil qʼawmaɬ ʃimeonil qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw tsuriʃadajil was ʃelumiel
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
ɡʔjesdasaɡi dobeχun tʃadral tʃʼwala ɡadil qʼawmaɬ ɡadil qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw deɡuelil was elijasaf
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
ruwimil askaralda ʃːibab bo rikʼkʼun kinawniɡi   tʃi saparazde raqχunezda ʁorɬ ɡʔjel rukʼine ruɡo kʼiabilelɬun
dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadirɡun tsadaqχ lewital rukʼina tsoɡidal qʼawmazda bakʔuɬ ɡʼizrailal saparazde raqχine ruɡo tʃʼjel ɡʔaburab bakʼaɬul tartibɡi tsʼunun tsotsada χadur ʃːiwaw tʃi ʒindirɡo askarɡun wa ʒindirɡo bakʼalda
bitʃːante baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχalda tʃadral tʃʼwaze jefraimil askaraɬ ʒindirɡo bajraqχɡun jefraimil qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw ammiɡʔudil was eliʃamaɡʼ
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
ɡʔjezda χadub bukʼina manasːil qʼawm manasːil qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw pedatsuril was ɡamliel
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
ɡʔjezda dobeχun bukʼina bunjaminil qʼawm bunjaminil qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw ɡideonil was awidan
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
jefraimil askaralda ʃːibab bo rikʼkʼun kinawniɡi   tʃi saparazde raqχunezda ʁorɬ ɡʔjel rukʼine ruɡo ɬababilelɬun
bitʃːante ʃimalijab raqχalda tʃadir tʃʼwaze danil askaraɬ ʒindirɡo bajraqχalda ʁorkʔ danil qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw amiʃadajil was aχijezer
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
ɡʔjezdaɡi χadur tʃadral tʃʼwaze ruɡo aʃeril qʼawmaɬ aʃeril qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw oχranil was paɡiel
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
ɡʔjezdasa dobeχun qʼaji tʃʼwaze buɡo naftalil qʼawmaɬ naftalil qʼawmaɬul kʼudijaw jenanil was aχir
ɡʔjesul bojalda   biχʔintʃi
danil askaralda kinawniɡi   biχʔintʃi ɡʔjel saparalde raqχine ruɡo biʃːun aχiralda ʒiderɡo bajraqχalɡun
ɡʔale ʃːiwasul tuχumɡi qʼawmɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun ɡʼizrailazul ɡʔaburab sijaχʼ kinalɡo askaralɡi ɡʔjezul bojalɡi dande ratʃun kinawniɡi ɡʼuna   biχʔintʃi
betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon ɡʼitsʼɡo lewital rikʼkʼintʃʼo tsoɡidal ɡʼizrailazda tsadaqχ
ɡʼizrailaz kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon biχʔizaburab tartibalda tʃʼwalaan ɡʔjez tʃadral ʒide ʒider bajraqχalɡun wa ɡʔjedinabɡo tartibalda saparazdeɡi raqχunaan ʃːiwaw ʒindirɡo qʼawmɡun wa qχizan aɡʔluɡun tsadaqχ

ɡʔale sinaj maɡʼarda musaɡun betʼjerhan kʼaɬarab zamanalda ɡʔarunilɡi musalɡi rukʼaral naslabi
ɡʔarunil wasazul tsʼaral nadaw tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw awiɡʔu eleazar wa itamar
ɡʔjel rukʼana dinijab qχuluqχaɬe ratʼa ɡʔarural wa χirijab naχɡi baχun kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼamural ɡʔarunil wasal
amma nadawɡi awiɡʔuɡi χwana betʼjerhanasul muqʼadasab bakʼalda sinaj salul awlaqχalda rukʼaɡo beɡʔulareb tʃijarab tsʼaɡi bosun betʼjerhanasda tsere ratʃʼarab meχaɬ ɡʔjezul ɬimal rukʼintʃʼjeɬul ɡʔjezul emen ɡʔarunɡun tsadaqχ ɡʼitsʼɡo ɡʔjezul watsal eleazarɡi itamarɡi rukʼana kaʃiʃalɬun
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
lewijil qʼawm batʃe ɡʔarunida tsebe ɡʔjesije kumekaɬe bukʼine
dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda qχuluqχalda rukʼine ruɡo ɡʔjel wa ɡʔjenib ɡʔarunijeɡi χalqʼaɬeɡi χʼaʒatabʃːinaɬul tʼalabɡi ɡʔabize buɡo ɡʔjez
ɡʔjez ʒawab kʔjeze kːola tʃadiraɬul tʼolabɡo qʼaji tsʼajaɬul wa ɡʼizrailazul raqχaɬ muqʼadasab bakʼalda qχuluqχɡi ɡʔabize kːola
ɡʔarunilɡi ɡʔjesul wasazulɡi iχtijaralde kʔje lewijilal ɡʼizrailazul tʼolɡo qʼawmazda ɡʔorkʔosa ɡʔjel riʃːun ruɡo ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi kumekaɬe rukʼine
wa ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi kaʃiʃɬijalde tʼame tsoɡi batʼijaw tʃi tʃadiralda askʼowe watʃʼani ɡʔjew tʃʼwaze kːola
ʒeɡi abuna betʼjerhanas musada
kinalɡo qʼawmazda ɡʔorkʔosa ditsa lewijilal ratʃana dijeɡo ɡʼizrailazul tʼotsere ɡʔarural wasazul bakʼalda lewijilal dir kːola
ʃːajɡureɬul ʃːibab tʼotsebeseb was ɬimer dir kːoleɬul misrijalda ditsa dozul kinalɡo tʼotseresel ɬimal χwezarurab meχalda ditsa ɡʼizrailazul tʼotseresel ɬimalɡi χʼajwanazul tʼotseresel tʼantʃʼiɡi dijeɡo ratʼa ɡʔaruna ɡʔjel dir kːola dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
sinajaɬul salul awlaqχalda betʼjerhanas musada abuna
lewijilal rikʼkʼje ɡʔjezul ʃːiwasul insul aɡʔluɡi tuχum kʔibilɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun motsʼaldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul kinalɡo biχʔinal rikʼkʼje
betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon musatsa ɡʔjel rikʼkʼana
ɡʔale lewijil wasazul tsʼaral
ɡerʃon keχat wa merari
ɡʔale ʒidedasa kʼudijal tuχumal ɬuɡʔaral ɡerʃonil wasazul tsʼaral
liwni wa ʃimɡʼi
ɡʔale ʒidedasa kʼudijal tuχumal ɬuɡʔaral keχatil wasal
amram itsχar χewron wa ɡʼuziel
ɡʔale ɡʔjedinɡo ʒidedasa kʼudijal tuχumal ɬuɡʔaral meraril wasazul tsʼaral maχʼli wa muʃi
ɡʔjele lewijil wasal wa ɡʔjezul naslabi
ɡerʃonidasan ɬuɡʔana liwnilɡi ʃimɡʼilɡi tuχumal ɡʔjel ruɡo ɡerʃonilazul tuχumal
ɡʔjezul wukʼana motsʼaldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul ankʔazaralda ʃːunusɡo tʃi
ɡerʃonilaz tʃʼjel ɡʔabize kːolaan muqʼadasab tʃadiralda naqχa baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχalda
ɡerʃonilazul kʔibilazul kʼudijawɬun wukʼana laelil was elijasaf
ɡʔjezul tʼalabalde kʔuna muqʼadasab tʃadirɡi ɡʔjelda tʼad ralel pardawalɡi tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa baleb pardawɡi
bakʔuɬ tʃadirɡi qʼurban bakʼɡi ɬurab azbaralda sweruqχ wa ɡʔjeɬul kʼaltʼa ralel pardawalɡi kwaralɡi wa ɡʔjeb kinaldaɡo χurχaral χʼaltʼabiɡi
keχatidasan ɬuɡʔana amramilazulɡi itsχarilazulɡi χewronilazulɡi wa ɡʼuzielilazulɡi kʔibilal ɡʔjel ruɡo keχatilal
ɡʔjezul wukʼana motsʼaldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul mikʔazaralda anɬnusɡo tʃi ɡʔjezda tʼadqʼana muqʼadasab bakʼ
keχatil naslabaz tʃʼjel ɡʔabize kːolaan muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul qʼilbajaɬulab raqχalda
ɡʔjezul kʔibilazul kʼudijawɬun wukʼana ɡʼuzielil was elitsafan
ɡʔjezda tʼad qʼana qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamasɡi stolɡi naχutʃiraqχɡi mesedil qʼurban bakʼɡi muqʼadasab bakʼaɬul tsʼaraɡʼɡi χasab pardawɡi ɡʔjeb kinaldaɡo χurχaral χʼaltʼabiɡi
lewijilazul kʼudijazulɡi kʼudijawɬun wukʼana eleazar kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunil was ɡʔjew wukʼana muqʼadasab bakʼaɬul tʼalab ɡʔabulezul betʼjerawɬun
meraridasan ɬuɡʔana maχʼlilɡi muʃilɡi kʔibilal ɡʔjel kːola meraril naslabi
ɡʔjezul wukʼana motsʼaldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul anɬazaralda kʼinusɡo biχʔintʃi
meraril naslabazul kʼudijawɬun wukʼana tsuriel awiχajilil was ɡʔjez tʃʼjel ɡʔabize kːolaan muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul ʃimalijab raqχalda
meraril naslabazda tʼadqʼana muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul ramabiɡi raχalɡi χʼubalɡi ʁorkʔtʃʼjelalɡi wa ɡʔjezda χurχaral χʼaltʼabiɡi
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔjez ʒawab kʔjeze kːolaan azbaralda sweruqχ ruɡel χʼubazulɡi ɡʔjezul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelazulɡi tʃadiraɬul ʁaziqχazulɡi kwarazulɡi
musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi wa ɡʔjezul wasazɡi tʃʼjel ɡʔabize kːolaan dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda tʃadiralda tsebe ɡʔjez muqʼadasab bakʼalda allaɡʔase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize kːolaan tʼolabɡo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬul raqχaldasan ɡʔjeniwe ɡʼaɡarɬaraw tsoniɡi batʼijaw tʃi tʃʼwaze kːolaan
betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi lewital rikʼkʼana ɡʔjezul ʃːiwasul qχizan aɡʔluɡi χʼisabalde bosun motsʼaldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul kinawniɡi watana qʼolo kʼiazarɡo biχʔinaw
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazul tʼotsere ɡʔarural wasal rikʼkʼje motsʼaldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul wa ɡʔjezul tsʼarazul sijaχʼ ɡʔabe
dun wuɡo betʼjerhan ɡʼizrailazul tʼotsere ɡʔarural wasazul bakʼalda dije lewital ratʼa ɡʔare wa ɡʼizrailazul ɡʼi botsʼul tʼotseresel tʼantʃʼazul bakʼalda lewitazul tʼolabɡo botsʼiɡi batʼa ɡʔabe
betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon musatsa rikʼkʼana ɡʼizrailazul tʼotsere ɡʔarural wasal
motsʼaldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul tsʼar tsʼarkːun reχsarazul kinawniɡi watana   tʃi
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazul tʼotsere ɡʔarural ɬimalazul bakʼalda lewital ratʃe wa ɡʔjezul botsʼul bakʼalda lewitazul tʼolɡo botsʼiɡi batʃe lewijilal dir kːola dun wuɡo betʼjerhan
ɡʼizrailazul tʼotsere ɡʔarurazul lewitazul qʼadaralda dande kːun  tʃi tsʼikʼkʼun wuɡeɬul
ɡʔjel tʼokʼɬaral wasazuqχa χʼaqʼ bakʼare ʃːiwasuqχa ʃːu ʃːu tʃadiralda χʼaltʼizabuleb ʃekel qʼo qʼo ɡeraɬul tsʼaji buɡeb
ɡʔjeb χʼaqʼ aj ɡʔjezuqχa bosarab ɡʼarats kʔje ɡʔaruniqχeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazuqχeɡi
musatsa bakʼarana lewitazdaɬun χisize res ʃːwetʃʼjel tʼotsere ɡʔarural ɡʼizrailazuqχa
 ʃekel ɡʼartsul
betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon musatsa ɡʔjeb ɡʼarats ɡʔaruniqχeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazuqχeɡi kʔuna

betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
lewijil was keχatidasan ɬuɡʔaral naslabazul sijaχʼ ɡʔabe ɡʔjezul ʃːiwasul tuχum kʔibilɡi insul aɡʔluɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
nuʒetsa rikʼkʼje dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda qχuluqχ ɡʔabize jaraɡʔunel ɬeberɡojaldasa kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡojalde ʃːwezeɡʼan sonazul riɡʔalda ruɡel kinalɡo biχʔinal
ɡʔale keχatil naslabaz dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub ɡʔabize kːoleb qχuluqχ ɡʔjez tʼalab ɡʔabize kːola muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul biʃːunɡo χirijab qʼajijaɬul
tʼolabɡo χalqʼ saparalde baqχuneb meχalda ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi χasab pardaw naqχe baqχila wa ɡʔjeb qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamasalda tʼad bala
χasab pardawalda tʼasan tʼjerenal tsʼakazul ɡʔaburab pardaw baze kːola ɡʔjeldaɡi tʼasan qχaχʼilab pardaw ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔabun χadub ʁamas batʃːulel ɡʼurdul ɡorazda ʒanire kːezarila
muqʼadasab tʃed ɬoleb stolalda tʼad ɡʔjez tʼamila kantʃʼqχaχʼilab pardaw wa ɡʔjelda tʼad sokʼkʼina surkʼabiɡi ɡelalɡi ɬamaɬi tʼolel ʃːurmalɡi ɡulɡunalɡi stolalda tʼad bukʼuneb muqʼadasab tʃedɡi bitʃːante ɡʔjenibɡo bukʼine
ɡʔjezda tʼasan ɡʔjez tʼamila bilbaɡʼarab pardaw ɡʔjeldaɡi tʼasan tʼamila tʼjerenal tsʼakazul ɡʔaburab pardaw wa stol batʃːulel ɡʼurdul ɡorazda ʒanir ɬela
tsinɡi ɡʔjez bosila kantʃʼqχaχʼilab pardaw wa ɡʔjeb bala kʼudijab naχutʃiraqχaldaɡi kinabɡo ɡʔjeɬul tsʼaraɡʼaldaɡi tʼad ɡʼisinal tʃiraqχazda bilta batsʼtsʼunel ʁuntsʼbuzda bilta batsʼtsʼarab laχʼ ɬolel surkʼabazda wa tʃiraqχaɬul naχ tʼoleb tʼolabɡo tsʼaraɡʼalda tʼad
χadub ɡʔjeb kinabɡo tsadaqχ ʒemila tʼjerenal tsʼakazul ɡʔaburab pardawaɬuɬ wa moloda tʼad ɬela
bitʃːante ɡʔjez mesedil qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad kantʃʼqχaχʼilab pardawɡi ɡʔjelda tʼasan tʼjerenal tsʼakazul ɡʔaburab pardawɡi tʼamize wa ɡʔjeb batʃːulel ɡʼurdul ɡorazda ʒanir ɬeze
muqʼadasab bakʼalda qχuluqχ ɡʔabijaɬe χʼaʒaɬuleb kinabɡo qʼajiɡi bakʼarun ɡʔjeb ʒemila kantʃʼqχaχʼilab pardawaɬuɬ ɡʔjelda tʼasan tʼamila tʼjerenal tsʼakazul ɡʔaburab pardaw wa ɡʔjebɡi ɬela moloda tʼad
mazɡarul qʼurban bakʼalda tʼasa roqχoɡi ɬuχʔun ɡʔjelda tʼad ɡʔjez tʼamila baɡʼarab pardaw
wa ɡʔjelda tʼad ɬela qʼurban buχʼijaɬe χʼaʒaɬuleb kinabɡo tsʼaraɡʼ buχʼarab tʼurtʃːi ɬolel tʼabkʼal ɡʼutʃʼal raqχubaqχal wa bi ʒanibe tʼolel ʃːurmal ɡʔjeb kinaldaɡo tʼasan tʼamila tʼjerenal tsʼakazul pardaw wa qʼurban bakʼ batʃːulel ɡʼurdul ɡorazda ɬela
saparalde raqχine χʼadurɬuleɬul bitʃːante tsin ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi muqʼadasab bakʼaɬul kinabɡo qʼaji pardawazuɬ ʒemize tsinɡi keχatilal ratʃʼina ɡʔjeb kinabɡo bosize amma ʒibɡo muqʼadasab tsʼaraɡʼalda keχatilaz kwer qχwaze beɡʔularo qχwani ɡʔjel χweze ruɡo ɡʔjeb kinabɡo dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul tsʼaraɡʼ batʃːize kːola ɡʔjez
kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunil was eleazaritsa tʼalab ɡʔabize kːola naχutʃiraqχaɬe χʼaʒaɬuleb naχulɡi ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼize χʼaltʼizabuleb maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubanʒojaɬulɡi qʼojil allaɡʔase ɡʼolo ɡʔabuleb roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬulɡi baχuneb χirijab naχulɡi ɡʔjedinɡo muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬulɡi ɡʔjelda ʒanib bukʼuneb kinabɡo qʼaji tsʼajaɬulɡi ʒawab kʔjeze kːola ɡʔjes
betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
woreɡi keχatil naslabi tʼaɡʼine ritʃːaɡe lewijil qʼawmaldasa ɡʔjel naqχe qχwaɡʼaze toɡe
muqʼadasab qʼaji tsʼajalde ɡʼaɡarɬulaɡo ɡʔjel χunɡutʼize ɡʔadin ɡʔabe bitʃːante ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazɡi ʒidetsaɡo biχʔizabize keχatilazda ɡʔjezul ʃːiwasul qχuluqχɡi ɡʔjesul ratʃːiɡi

ɡerʃonil naslabazulɡi sijaχʼ ɡʔabe ʃːiwasul insul aɡʔluɡi tuχum kʔibilɡi χʼisabaldeɡi bosun
dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda qχuluqχ ɡʔabize beɡʔulel ɬeberɡojaldasa kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡojalde ʃːwezeɡʼan sonazul riɡʔalda ruɡel kinalɡo biχʔinal maɬːe
ɡʔale ɡerʃonilazul naslabaz ɡʔabize kːoleb χʼaltʼi wa ɡʔjez batʃːize kːoleb qʼaji
ɡʔjez ratʃːize kːola muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul aj dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul pardawalɡi ɡʔjelda tʼasan baleb pardawɡi ɡʔjeldaɡi tʼasan baleb tʼjerenal tsʼakazul pardawɡi tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa biʁuleb pardawɡi
tʃadirɡi mazɡarul qʼurban bakʼɡi ʒanib ɬoleb azbaraɬul pardawalɡi azbaraɬul kʼaltʼa baleb pardawɡi kwaralɡi pardawazda tsadaqχ bukʼunebʃːinab qʼajiɡi ɡʔjeb kinaldaɡo χurχaral χʼaltʼabiɡi ɡʔarize kːola ɡʔjez
ɡerʃonilaz kinalɡo χʼaltʼabi ɡʔarize kːola ɡʔarunilɡi ɡʔjesul wasazulɡi nuχmaɬijalda ʁorkʔ nuʒetsa biχʔizabe ɡʔjezda ɡʔjez batʃːize kːoleb qʼajiɡi ɡʔjelda sweruqχ ɡʔabize kːoleb χʼaltʼiɡi
ɡʔjedinab bukʼine buɡo ɡerʃonilazul naslabaz dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub ɡʔabuleb qχuluqχ bitʃːante ɡʔjez ʒideda tʼadab qχuluqχ tʼubaze kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunil was itamaril nuχmaɬijalda ʁorkʔ

ɬeberɡojaldasa kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡojalde ʃːwezeɡʼan sonazul riɡʔalda ruɡel wa dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub qχuluqχ ɡʔabize beɡʔulel kinalɡo biχʔinal maɬe
ɡʔale dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub ɡʔjezda tʼaɬulel qχuluqχal ɡʔjez ratʃːize kːola muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul ramabi raχal χʼubal wa ɡʔjezul ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal
azbaraɬul χʼubalɡun ʁorkʔtʃʼjelal ʁaziqχalɡun kwaral wa ɡʔjeb kinaldaɡo tsadaqχ qʼwariɡʼunebʃːinab tsoɡidab qʼaji alat tsʼar tsʼarkːun ʒiw ʒiwasda biχʔizabe ɡʔjesda tʼadab ʃːiwas ʒawab kʔjeze kːoleb ɡʔjezul ratʃːi
ɡʔjedinab buɡo meraril naslabaz kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunil was itamaril nuχmaɬijalda ʁorkʔ dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub ɡʔabize kːoleb qχuluqχ

ɬeberɡojaldasa kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡojalde ʃːwezeɡʼan sonazul riɡʔalda ruɡel wa dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub qχuluqχ ɡʔabize jaraɡʔunel ɡʔjedinɡo tʃadir batʃːize baʒarulel

ɡʔjedinal tʃaɡʼi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe ritʼje biχʔinal rukʼa rutʃːabi rukʼa χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔob dun zaɡʔirɬuleb bakʼ qχubɬizabitʃʼoɡo bukʼine
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬ ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna χalqʼ tʃʼarab bakʼ tun qʼwatʼire ritʼana ɡʔjedinal tʃaɡʼi ɡʼizrailaz ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon

ɡʼizrailazda abe naɡaɡʔ biχʔintʃijas jaɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ tsoɡidaw tʃijase zaral ɡʔabuni ɡʔjeb kːola betʼjerhanasda dande ɡʔaburab taqʼsir ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjedinal tʃaɡʼiɡi ɡʼajibijalɬun rikʼkʼuna
ɡʔjel rakʼraɡʔun mukʼurɬize kːola ʒidetsa munaɡʔ ɡʔabijalda wa ʒidetsaɡo ɡʔaburab zaral betsʼize kːola kːarab zaralaɬul ʃːujil butʼa tʼadeɡi ʒuban ɡʔjeb kʔjeze kːola ʒidetsa kweʃɬi ɡʔaburaw tʃijase
naɡaɡʔɬun ɡʔjew tʃi χwani wa ɡʔjeb kʔjeze ɡʔjesul ɡʼaɡaraw tʃiɡi watitʃʼoni retsʼjel kːola betʼjerhanasul mulkɬun wa munaɡʔaldasa ratsʼtsʼaɬizaruleb qʼurbanaɬul kujɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjeb kʔjeze kːola kaʃiʃasuqχe

ɡʼizrailazda kʼaɬaj wa ɡʔjezda abe naɡaɡʔ ɬadi rosase χilipɬani
rosasdasa baɬɡo ɡʔjej tsoɡidaw tʃiɡun busada jeɡani amma rosas ɡʔjej tʼad kːun ɡʔjetʃʼoni wa nuɡʼ ɡʔjetʃʼoɬijalda ban ɡʔjej tʼatinajunɡi ɡʔjetʃʼoni
amma zina ɡʔaburaj tʃʼuʒujalda ros ʃːakdarize bajbiχʔani jaɬuni ɡʼajibɡo ɡʔjetʃʼjej ɬaduda ɡʔjew ʃːakdarize bajbiχʔani
bitʃːante rosas ɬadi kaʃiʃasuqχe jatʃine ɡʔjes kaʃiʃasuqχe bosize kːola jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjej betʼjerhanasda tsee jatʃina
bitʃːante ɡʔjes ʃːaɡʼil ɡʼortojaɬube duɡʼadul ɬim tʼjeze wa tʃadiraɬul tʃʼabaraldasa bosun ɡʔjenibe tsodaɡʔab rakʔɡi baze
betʼjerhanasda tseeɡi tʃʼjezajun kaʃiʃas ɡʔjej tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬul ras ɡʔurʃːizabila wa ɡʔjeɬul kodob ɬela taqʼsir tʼatinabijaɬul roɬul sadaqʼa aj ʃakdarijaɬul χanʒdal sadaqʼa wa ʒinditsaɡo kodob kːwela naɡʼana kʔjejaɬul kʔoɡʼab ɬim
tsinɡi kaʃiʃas tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan ɡʔjedize tʼamila ɡʔadinɡi abun duda askʼow tʃijar biχʔintʃi weɡun watitʃʼoni wa rosase χilipɬun zinaɡi ɡʔabun mun qχubɬun jatitʃʼoni ɡʔab naɡʼana kʔjejaɬul kʔoɡʼab ɬetsa duje kinabɡʼaɡi zaral ɡʔabuɡeɡi
wa amma rosaseɡi χilipɬun dutsa munɡo qχubɬizajun jatani ros ɡurew batʼijaw tʃijasda askʼoj jeɡunɡi jatani
ɡʔjeb bakʼalda kaʃiʃas naɡʼanaɡi kʔun tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan ɡʔjedize tʼamila wa abila betʼjerhanas naɡʼana kʔjela duje wa χalqʼalda surizajila mun ɬimal ɡʔarularejɬun ɬuɡʔina wa dur urɡʔimes ɡʔorola
wa bitʃːante ɡʔab naɡʼana kʔjejaɬul kʔoɡʼab ɬim dur urɡʔibe ine wa dur urɡʔimes ɡʔodorɬun mun ɬimal ɡʔarularejɬun ɬuɡʔine
tsinɡi bitʃːante tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ amin amin an abize
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas ɡʔjel raɡʼabi kaʁtidaɡi qχwan kʔoɡʼab ɬadaɬ tʃurize

tsin kaʃiʃas ɡʔjelda kodosa bosila ʃːakdarijaɬul roɬul sadaqʼa wa betʼjerhanasda tsebeɡi χʔwaɡʼjezabun qʼurban bakʼalde bosila
ɡʔjes roɬul sadaqʼajalda tʼasa bosun danʁura tsʼurab ʒo ɡʔjeɬul χasab butʼa χʼisabalda qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila tsinɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanalda ɬim ɡʔjeqʼezabila
ɡʔjeɬ rosaseɡi χilipɬun ʒijɡo qχubɬizajun jatani naɡʼana kʔjejaɬul kʔoɡʼab ɬim ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ina ɡʔjeɬije ɡʼazabaɬe ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔimes ɡʔorola ɡʔjej ɬimal ɡʔarularejɬun ɬuɡʔina wa χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔoj surarajɬun jikʼina
amma tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ zina ɡʔabun batitʃʼoni wa ɡʔjej jatsʼtsʼadaj jiɡoni ɡʔjeɬije zaral kːelaro ɡʔjeɬije ɬimalɡi kʔjela

betʼjerhanase ɡʼumru nazru ɡʔabun buɡebɡʼan zamanalda ɡʔjesije ɡʔuqʼarab buɡo ʒanazajalda askʼowe qʼaze
ɡʔjesul emen ebel wats jaɡi jats χwaniɡitsin ɡʔjel sababɬun ʒindir botʼrol ras qχubɬizabize beɡʔularo ɡʔjes ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb buɡo ɡʔjesul ɡʼumru betʼjerhanase nazru ɡʔabijaɬul ɡʼalamat

mikʔabileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjes kaʃiʃasuqχe dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje batʃʼine kːola kʼiɡo roχʔil mikːi jaɡi kʼiɡo mikːidul tʼintʃʼ
kaʃiʃas tso χʼintʃʼ qʼabul ɡʔabila munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanɬun wa tsoɡidab tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanɬun ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjew ʒanazajalda askʼowɡi wukʼun qχubɬun wuɡeɬul ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔjes tsʼi ɡʔabize kːola nazorejɬi tʼade bosijaɬul nijat
bitʃːante ɡʔjes tsʼidasan betʼjerhanase ɡʼumru nazru ɡʔabize wa ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjer kʔjeze
ɡʔjezul nazorejɬijaɬul aral qʼojal rikʼkʼunaro ʃːajɡureɬul nazorejɬi qχubɬun bukʼindal
ɡʔale nazorejɬijaɬul qʼanun ɡʔjesul nazorejɬijaɬul zaman aχiralde ʃːwarab meχalda ɡʔjew watʃine kːola dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje
bitʃːante ɡʔjes betʼjerhanase qʼurbanaɬe batʃʼine tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ɬaɡʼarab biχʔinab kʔjeɡʼjer munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ɬaɡʼarab tsʼujab kʔjeɡʼjer raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb kuj
ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ bukʼine kːola roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi qʼurban bakʼalde tʼoleb tʃaʁirɡi ɡʔjedinɡo zajtunaɬul naχuda rutsaral biʃːunɡo ɬikʼab roɬul χanʒdal ɡʔarural buɡʔurɡo tʃadazul tsʼurab tʃʼjepɡi tʼad naχ baχaral retʃːeb ʒubatʃʼjel bakarabiɡi
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjel χirijal sadaqʼabi betʼjerhanasda tsere rosila wa munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanɡi tʼobitʼila
χadub betʼjerhanasda tsebe raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe tso kuj qχwela ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ retʃːeb ɡʔjetʃʼjel tʃadazul tʃʼjepɡi bukʼine kːola ɡʔjedinɡo kaʃiʃas roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi qʼurban bakʼalde tʼolel ʒalazul sadaqʼaɡi qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad buχʼila
dandtʃʼwajaɬul kʼaltʼa qʼuntsʼize kːola nazorejas ʒindirɡo nazorejɬijaɬul ras tsinɡi ɡʔjeb ras reχize kːola raqʼlil qʼurban buχʼuleb tsʼaduɬe
nazorejas ʒindirɡo ras qʼuntsʼun χadub kaʃiʃas ɡʔjesuqχe kodobe kʔjela kujdul beɬarab buɡʔnalaɡaɡi naχuda butsarab retʃːeb ɡʔjetʃʼjeb tʃedɡi tʼad naχ baχarab retʃːeb ɡʔjetʃʼjeb bakariɡi
kaʃiʃas ɡʔjel eχedeɡi rorχun χʔwaɡʼjezarila betʼjerhanasda tsere χasab χirijab sadaqʼa χʼisabalda ɡʔjel χirijalɬun kːola wa ɡʔjelɡi meɡʔjedɡi kujdul boχɡi kaʃiʃase rukʼine kːola ɡʔjeldasa χadub nazorejas tʃaʁir ɡʔjeqʼeze beɡʔula
ɡʔjedinal ruɡo betʼjerhanase ɡʼumru nazru ɡʔaburaw nazorejasda tʼadal iʃal bitʃːante ɡʔjelde tʼadeɡi ɡʔjes sadaqʼa ɡʔabize ʒindirɡo buɡoɬijalda reqʼon ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo nijat tʼubazabize kːola nazorejɬijaɬul qʼanunalda reqʼon
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazdaɡi abe ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬe duɡʼa ɡʔabe ɡʔadinal raɡʼabazdaɬun
betʼjerhanas barakat buɡelɬun ɡʔareɡi nuʒ wa
kweʃabʃːinaldasa tsʼunaɡi
betʼjerhanasul sipataɬul nur qʼaɬaɡi nuʒeda tʼad
wa ɡʔjew ɡurχʼaɡi nuʒeda
betʼjerhanase χiraɬaɡi nuʒ
wa saχ salamatab ɡʼumru kʔjeɡi nuʒee
ɡʔjedin dir tsʼarɡi reχson ɡʼizrailaze duɡʼa ɡʔabila ɡʔjez wa ditsa ɬikʼabʃːinab kʔjela ɡʔjezije

musatsa muqʼadasab tʃadir eχetizaburab meχalda ɡʔjes ɡʔjeldaɡi ɡʔjelda ʒanib buɡeb qʼaji qʼonojaldaɡi qʼurban bakʼaldaɡun ɡʔjeɬul tsʼaraɡʼaldaɡi χirijab naχɡi baχun ɡʔjeb kinabɡo betʼjerɡʔanase batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabuna ɡʔjeb kinaldaɡo ɡʔjes χirijab naχ baχana ɡʔjeb muqʼadasabɬun bukʼine
wa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬul butʼruz qʼawmazul kʼudijaz aj χalqʼaɬul sijaχʼ ɡʔabijaɬul ʒawabtʃiɬi ʒideda tʼadal qʼawmazul butʼruz ʒiderɡo raqχaɬ χirijal sadaqʼabi rosun ratʃʼana
ɡʔjez tʃadiralda tsere ɬuna betʼjerhanase χirijab sadaqʼa χʼisabalda tʼadqχel buɡeb anɬɡo ɡʔokoɡi antsʼila kʼiɡo otsɡi ʃːibab qʼawmaɬul betʼjeras tso tso ots wa kʼi kʼijas tsadaqχ tso tso ɡʔoko ɡʔjeb kinabɡo muqʼadasab tʃadiralda tsebe ɬuna
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
qʼabul ɡʔare ɡʔjezuqχa ɡʔakalɡi otsalɡi dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda χʼaltʼizarize rukʼine ɡʔjel lewitazuqχe kʔje ɡʔjez tʼubaleb qχuluqχalda reqʼon
musatsa ɡʔakalɡi otsalɡi lewitazuqχe kʔuna
kʼiɡo ɡʔokoɡi unqʼɡo otsɡi ɡerʃonil naslabazuqχe kʔuna ɡʔjezul qχuluqχalda reqʼon
wa unqʼɡo ɡʔokoɡi mikʔɡo otsɡi meraril naslabazuqχe kʔuna ɡʔarunil was itamaril nuχmaɬijalda ʁorkʔ ɡʔjez ɡʔabuleb qχuluqχalda reqʼon
amma keχatil naslabazuqχe musatsa ʃːibniɡi kʔjetʃʼo ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjez tʃadiraɬul biʃːun muqʼadasab qʼaji batʃːize kːolaan ʒiderɡo kʼiʁuʒduzdaɡi ɬun
qʼurban bakʼalda χirijab naχ baχun baqχindal χalqʼaɬul butʼruz ʒiderɡo raqχaldasan χirijal sadaqʼabi kʔuna wa ɡʔjeldaɬun kʼodo ɡʔabuna qʼurbanal ruχʼize bajbiχʔi ɡʔjel sadaqʼabiɡi qʼurban bakʼalda tsere ʃːwezaruna
betʼjerhanas musada abuna bitʃːante ɡʔjez irɡadal ʃːibab qʼojaɬ tso betʼjeras qʼurban bakʼalda qʼurbanal ruχʼize bajbiχʔi kʼodo ɡʔabun ʒindirɡo raqχaldasan qʼurbanalɡun χirijal sadaqʼabi ratʃʼine
tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi ratʃʼana jaɡʔudal tuχumaldasa ɡʼaminadawil was naχʼʃonitsa
ɡʔjes batʃʼana nusijalda ɬeberɡo ʃekelaɬul
ɡʔuinmaχʼaze χʼaltʼizabuleb maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubanʒoɡi ʒanib ɬun antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul
basiɡi kujɡi ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe
munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe deɡʼjen
raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe kʼiɡo otsɡi ʃːuɡo kujɡi ʃːuɡo deɡʼjenɡi ʃːuɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi
ɡʔjedinal rukʼana ɡʼaminadawil was naχʼʃonil qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi
kʼiabileb qʼojaɬ qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi ratʃʼana isːaχaril qʼawmaɬul betʼjer tsuaril was netanielitsa
ɡʔjes batʃʼana nusijalda ɬeberɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb ɡʼartsul ʁadaro wa ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb ɡʼartsul ʃːurun ɡʔjezda ʒanib bukʼana roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬe χʼadurarab zajtunaɬul naχɡun ʒubazaburab biʃːun ɬikʼab roɬul χanʒu
antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb mesedil ɡel ɡʔuinmaχʼaze χʼaltʼizabuleb maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubanʒoɡi ʒanib ɬun
basiɡi kujɡi ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe
munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe deɡʼjen
raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe kʼiɡo otsɡi ʃːuɡo kujɡi ʃːuɡo deɡʼjenɡi ʃːuɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi
ɡʔjedinal rukʼana tsuaril was netanielil qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi
ɬababileb qʼojaɬ qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi ratʃʼana zewulunil qʼawmaɬul betʼjer χelonil was eliawitsa
ɡʔjes batʃʼana nusijalda ɬeberɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb ɡʼartsul ʁadaro wa ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb ɡʼartsul ʃːurun ɡʔjezda ʒanib bukʼana roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬe χʼadurarab zajtunaɬul naχɡun ʒubazaburab biʃːun ɬikʼab roɬul χanʒu
antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb mesedil ɡel ɡʔuinmaχʼaze χʼaltʼizabuleb maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubanʒoɡi ʒanib ɬun

ɡʔjedinal rukʼana χelonil was eliawil qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi
unqʼabileb qʼojaɬ qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi ɡʔaruna ruwimil qʼawmaɬul betʼjer ʃedeuril was elitsuritsa
