antsʼabileb qʼojaɬ qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi ɡʔaruna danil qʼawmaɬul betʼjer amiʃadajil was aχijezeritsa
ɡʔjes batʃʼana nusijalda ɬeberɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb ɡʼartsul ʁadaro wa ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb ɡʼartsul ʃːurun ɡʔjezda ʒanib bukʼana roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬe χʼadurarab zajtunaɬul naχɡun ʒubazaburab biʃːun ɬikʼab roɬul χanʒu
antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb mesedil ɡel ɡʔuinmaχʼaze χʼaltʼizabuleb maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubanʒoɡi ʒanib ɬun
basiɡi kujɡi ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe
munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe deɡʼjen
raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe kʼiɡo otsɡi ʃːuɡo kujɡi ʃːuɡo deɡʼjenɡi ʃːuɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi
ɡʔjedinal rukʼana amiʃadajil was aχijezeril qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi
antsʼila tsoabileb qʼojaɬ qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi ɡʔaruna aʃeril qʼawmaɬul betʼjer oχranil was paɡielitsa
ɡʔjes batʃʼana nusijalda ɬeberɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb ɡʼartsul ʁadaro wa ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb ɡʼartsul ʃːurun ɡʔjezda ʒanib bukʼana roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬe χʼadurarab zajtunaɬul naχɡun ʒubazaburab biʃːun ɬikʼab roɬul χanʒu
antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb mesedil ɡel ɡʔuinmaχʼaze χʼaltʼizabuleb maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubanʒoɡi ʒanib ɬun
basiɡi kujɡi ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe
munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe deɡʼjen
raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe kʼiɡo otsɡi ʃːuɡo kujɡi ʃːuɡo deɡʼjenɡi ʃːuɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi
ɡʔjedinal rukʼana oχranil was paɡielil qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi
antsʼila kʼiabileb qʼojaɬ qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi ɡʔaruna naftalil qʼawmaɬul betʼjer jenanil was aχiritsa
ɡʔjes batʃʼana nusijalda ɬeberɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb ɡʼartsul ʁadaro wa ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb ɡʼartsul ʃːurun ɡʔjezda ʒanib bukʼana roɬul χirijab sadaqʼajaɬe χʼadurarab zajtunaɬul naχɡun ʒubazaburab biʃːun ɬikʼab roɬul χanʒu
antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb mesedil ɡel ɡʔuinmaχʼaze χʼaltʼizabuleb maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubanʒoɡi ʒanib ɬun
basiɡi kujɡi ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe
munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe deɡʼjen
raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe kʼiɡo otsɡi ʃːuɡo kujɡi ʃːuɡo deɡʼjenɡi ʃːuɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi
ɡʔjedinal rukʼana jenanil was aχiril qʼurbanalɡun sadaqʼabi
qʼurban bakʼalda χirijab naχ baχin kʼodo ɡʔabun ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬul butʼruz muqʼadasab bakʼalde kʔuna antsʼila kʼiɡo ɡʼartsul ʁadaroɡi antsʼila kʼiɡo ɡʼartsul ʃːurunɡi antsʼila kʼiɡo mesedil ɡelɡi
ʃːibab ɡʼartsul ʁadarojalda bukʼana nusijalda ɬeberɡo ʃekel tsʼaji wa ʃːibab ʃːurmida ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʃekel ɡʔjezul kinazulɡo ɡʼammab bakʼɬi bukʼana kʼiazaralda unqʼnusɡo ʃekel
maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubanʒo ʒanib ɬurab antsʼila kʼiɡo mesedil ɡel bukʼana ʃːibalda antsʼɡo ʃekelaɬul tsʼaji buɡeb wa ɡʔjezul ɡʼammab bakʼɬi bukʼana nusijalda qʼoɡo ʃekel
tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe kinabniɡi batʃʼana antsʼila kʼiɡo basiɡi antsʼila kʼiɡo kujɡi antsʼila kʼiɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi wa ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ rukʼine kːolel roɬul χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi
raqʼlil qʼurbanaɬe kinabniɡi batʃʼana qʼolo unqʼɡo otsɡi ɬabqʼoɡo kujɡi ɬabqʼoɡo deɡʼjenɡi ɬabqʼoɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi ɡʔjedinal rukʼana qʼurban bakʼalda χirijab naχ baχun χadub ɡʔjeb kʼodo ɡʔabijaɬe ratʃʼaral qʼurbanalɡun χirijal sadaqʼabi
betʼjerhanasda tsewe dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬuwe musa ɬuɡʔanʃːinaqχe musada ɡʔjesul ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼulaan qʼotʼijaɬul ʁansil tʼaɬelalda tʼad buɡeb kʼiɡo χeruwimalda ɡʔorkʔosan ɡʔjedin kʼaɬalaan betʼjerhan musaɡun

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔarunida ɬazabe dutsa naχutʃiraqχalda ankʔɡo ɡʔitʼintʃiraqχ reqʼezabuleb meχalda ɡʔjel tʃiraqχal ɬe ɡʔjezda tsebeseb raqχ ɡʔjez ɡwanʁizabuleb kutsaɬ in
ɡʔarunitsa kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon ɡʼisintʃiraqχal ɬuna tsebeseb raqχ ɡwanʁizabuleb kutsalda
naχutʃiraqχ ɡʔabuna ratʃitʼa mesedɡi buχun aχaɬijaldasa baqχarab tʼadeχun ruɡel mesedil tʼuɡʔduzul sipatazde ɡʼuntʼun kinabɡo betʼjerhanas musada biχʔizaburab sipatalda reqʼon
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
lewijil naslabi tsoɡidal ɡʼizrailazdasa ratʼa ɡʔare wa ɡʔjel ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔare
ɡʔjel ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔare χaduseb qʼaɡʼidajaɬ ɡʔjezde dinijab ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬim punqχizabe wa bitʃːante ɡʔjez tʼolɡo tʃerχaldasa ras kʼkʼwaze wa ʒiderɡo partal tʃurize tsinɡi ɡʔjel ratsʼtsʼadalɬun ɬuɡʔina
χadub bitʃːante ɡʔjez batʃʼine tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze tso basi tsadaqχ bukʼine kːoleb roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡun aj zajtunaɬul naχɡun ʒubarab biʃːun ɬikʼab χanʒuɡun wa tsoɡi basi munaɡʔal tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe
tsinɡi lewijilal lewital dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsere aχʼje ɡʼizrailazul tʼolɡo ʒamaɡʼatɡi ɡʔjenibe bakʼarun
lewijil naslabi betʼjerhanasda tsere tʃʼjezare wa bitʃːante ɡʼizrailaz ɡʔjezda tʼad kweral ɬeze
ɡʔarunitsa ratʃine kːola lewital betʼjerhanasda tsere ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬul raqχaldasan ɡʔjesije kʔoleb χasab sajʁat χʼisabalda ɡʔjeldasa naqχe ɡʔjel betʼjerhanase qχuluqχaɬe rukʼine
tsinɡi bitʃːante lewijil naslabaz otsazul butʼruzda kweral ɬeze wa tso ots betʼjerhanase munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurbanaɬe kʼiabileb ots tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχweze ɡʔjel qʼurbanazdaɬun ratsʼtsʼaɬila lewital
dutsa lewijil naslabi ɡʔarunidaɡi ɡʔjesul wasazdaɡi tsere ratʃe wa ɡʔjezul nuχmaɬijalde kʔje betʼjerhanase kʔoleb χasab sajʁat χʼisabalda
ɡʔjedin dutsa lewital ratʼa ɡʔarila tsoɡidal ɡʼizrailazdasa ɡʔjel diralɬun rukʼinaɬe ɡʼolo
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔabun χadub aj dutsa ɡʔjel ratsʼtsʼadɡi ɡʔarun χasab sajʁatɬun betʼjerɡʔanase kʔun χadub lewijil naslabi dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬure ɬuɡʔine beɡʔula ɡʔjenir qχuluqχaɬe tʃʼjeze
ɡʼitsʼɡo ɡʔjel ruɡo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼuranɡo dije kʔjeze ratʼa ɡʔarural ɡʼizrailal ditsa ɡʔjel dijeɡo ratʃana χutʼaral ɡʼizrailazul tʼotsere ɡʔarural biχʔinɬimalazul bakʼalda
ɡʼizrailalda ɡʔaburab tʼotsebeseb biχʔinɬimer dir kːola ɡʔjedinɡo χʼajwanaɬul tʼotsebeseb tʼintʃʼɡi kːola dir misrijaɬul tʼolalɡo tʼotsere ɡʔarural ɬimal χwezarurab qʼojaɬ ditsa ɡʼizrailazul tʼotsere ɡʔarural ɬimal dijeɡo ratʼa ɡʔaruna
ɡʔanʒejan abuni ditsa tsoχʼo lewijil tʼolalɡo naslabi rosana dijeɡo ɡʼizrailazul kinalɡo tʼotsere ɡʔarural biχʔinɬimalazul bakʼalda
ditsa lewital ratʼa ɡʔaruna ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa wa ɡʔarunijeɡi ɡʔjesul wasazeɡi sajʁatɬun kʔuna ɡʔjel dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazul bakʼalda qχuluqχ ɡʔabize kːola ɡʔjez ɡʔjel rukʼine ruɡo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬuqχ bosarab χʼaqʼɬun tsinɡi ɡʼizrailal muqʼadasab bakʼalde ɡʼaɡarɬilaro wa kweʃab unti jaɡi balaɡʔ batʃʼinaldasa tsʼunun rukʼina
musatsaɡi ɡʔarunitsaɡi wa ɡʼizrailaɬul tʼolɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬɡi kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon
lewijilaz ratsʼtsʼaɬi ɡʔabuna wa partal tʃurana ɡʔarunitsa ɡʔjel betʼjerhanasda tsere ratʃana ɡʔjesije kʔoleb χasab sajʁat χʼisabalda wa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul nizam tʼobitʼana kinab bataniɡi munaɡʔ χʼaqʼaldasa ɡʔjel ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔarizeɬun
ɡʔjeldasa χadub lewital ɡʔarunilɡi ɡʔjesul wasazulɡi nuχmaɬijalda ʁorkʔ dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬur qχuluqχ ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔana lewijilaze kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔale lewitazul raqχaɬ qʼanun qʼolo ʃːuɡo sonil riɡʔalde waχaraw ʃːiwaw tʃijas bajbiχʔize kːola dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub qχuluqχ ɡʔabize
amma kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo son barab meχalda ɡʔjez qχuluqχ teze kːola ɡʔjeldasa χadub ɡʔjez tʼokʼaɬ qχuluqχ ɡʔabize kːolaro
ɡʔjez kumek ɡʔabize beɡʔula dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub qχuluqχ ɡʔabulel ʒiderɡo watsaze amma ʒidetsaɡo qχuluqχ ɡʔabize kːolaro ɡʔjezda tʼadab qχuluqχaɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ ɡʔjedin ɬazabe lewitazda

misrijaldasa qʼwatʼibe ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ baqχun kʼiabileb sonaɬul tʼotsebeseb motsʼalda
bitʃːante ɡʼizrailaz pesaχ bajram tʼobitʼize ɡʔjeɬije biχʔizaburab zamanɡi χʼisabalde bosun
pesaχ tʼobitʼje ɡʔab motsʼaɬul antsʼila unqʼabileb qʼojaɬ baqʼanil ɡʼuʒalda qʼo rukʼkʼinalde tsebe kinalɡo pesaχaɬul tʼadqʼajalɡi nizamalɡi tsʼunun
ɡʔjedinɬidal musatsa ɡʼizrailazde amru ɡʔabuna pesaχaɬul bajram kʼodo ɡʔabejan
wa tʼotsebeseb motsʼaɬul antsʼila unqʼabileb qʼojaɬ baqʼanil ɡʼuʒalda qʼo rukʼkʼinalde tsebe sinaj aburab salul awlaqχalda ɡʔjez pesaχaɬul bajram tʼobitʼana ɡʼizrailaz kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon
amma ɡʔjezul tso tsojazuqχa baʒaritʃʼo pesaχaɬul bajramalda ɡʼaχʔalɬize ʃːajɡureɬul ʒanazajalda qχwaze kːun ɡʔjel qχubɬun rukʼana ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔjel musaqχeɡi ɡʔaruniqχeɡi ratʃʼana
wa ɡʔjez musada abuna
niʒ qχubɬun ruɡo ʒanazajalda qχwaze kːun rukʼun amma ʃːaj niʒ maχʼrum ɡʔarulel tʃʼjezaburab zamanalda ɡʼizrailazda tsadaqχ betʼjerhanase qʼurban ɡʔabijaldasa
musatsa ɡʔjezije ʒawab kʔuna
ɡʔanir tʃʼa betʼjerhanas nuʒer raqχaɬ kinab amru batʃʼunebali ditsa ɬazabizeɡʼan
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazda abe ʒanazajalda qχwan qχubɬaraw jaɡi rikʼkʼadab saparalde kːun ɡʔjeɬije biχʔizaburab zamanalda pesaχaɬul bajram kʼodo ɡʔabize res ʃːwetʃʼjew tʃijasɡi tʼobitʼize kːola betʼjerhanas tʃʼjezaburab pesaχaɬul bajram
ɡʔjedinaw tʃijas pesaχ kʼodo ɡʔabize bitʃːante kʼiabileb motsʼaɬul antsʼila unqʼabileb qʼojaɬul baqʼanida qʼurbanaɬul kʔaɡʼril ɡʔan kwanaze kːola ɡʔjes buɡʔurɡo tʃedɡun wa kʔoɡʼal χurdulɡun tsadaqχ
roɡʔinalde ʃːibɡo ʒo naqχe tetʃʼoɡo wa tsoniɡi rakʔa bekitʃʼoɡo pesaχaɬul bajram tʼobitʼuleɬul ɡʔjeɬije tʃʼjezarural bitʃasul χʼukmabi raɡʼa rakʔande ʃːun tʼurazarize kːola ɡʔjes
amma tʃerχɡi qχubɬitʃʼjew saparaldeɡi kːetʃʼjew tʃijas pesaχaɬul bajramaɬul kʼwar ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo tani ɡʔjew χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe qʼotʼize wuɡo ɡʔjes tʃʼjezaburab zamanalda betʼjerhanase qʼurban ɡʔabitʃʼoɬi sababɬun ɡʔjesije ʒaza ɡʔabize kːola
nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabulew tʃijar rakʔaldasa tʃijase bokʔani betʼjerhanas tʼad ɬurab pesaχaɬul bajram kʼodo ɡʔabize ɡʔjesdaɡi tʼaɬula ɡʔjeb bajramaɬe riχʔizarural bitʃasul kinalɡo χʼukmabiɡi nizamɡi tsʼunize ɡʔab ulkajalda ɡʔawuraseɡi tʃijar rakʔaldasa watʃʼun ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleseɡi tsoɡojab nizam bukʼine kːola
muqʼadasab aj dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadir eχetizaburab qʼojaɬɡo nakʼkʼul partʃajaɬ baχtʃizabuna sordo roɡʔineɡʼan ɡʔjeb tsʼadul partʃaduɬ buɡeb ɡʼadin biχʔulaan
ɡʔjeldasa naqχe ɡʔjedin bukʼana kidaɡo qʼad tʃadiralda tʼad nakʼkʼul partʃa tʃʼolaan wa qʼasi ɡʔjeb tsʼaduda reɬːunaan
tʃadiraldasa nakʼkʼul partʃa tʼade bosarab meχaɬ ɡʼizrailal saparaɬ raqχunaan nakʼkʼul partʃa ɬalqχarab bakʼalda ɡʼizrailaz qʼajiɡi tʃʼwalaan
betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʼizrailal saparalde raqχunaan wa ɡʔjesulɡo amrujalda reqʼon tʃʼjelɡi ɡʔabulaan tʃadiralda tʼad nakʼkʼul partʃa biʁarabɡʼan zamanalda ɡʔjel tʃʼarab bakʼaldaɡo rukʼunaan
tʃadiralda tʼad nakʼkʼul partʃa ɡʼjemerab zamanaɬ tʃʼaniɡi ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ betʼjerhanase mutʼiɡʼɬulaan wa saparalde baqχunaroan
tʃadiralda tʼad nakʼkʼul partʃajaɬ tso tʃanɡo qʼo ɡuroni batʃʼoniɡi ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔabulaan ɡʼitsʼɡo betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon qʼaji tʃʼwalaan wa ɡʔjesul amrujalda reqʼon saparaldeɡi raqχunaan
tso tso meχalda nakʼkʼul partʃa tʃadiralda tʼad tʃʼolaan sordo roɡʔineɡʼan wa radal partʃa tʼade borχun biχʔani ɡʔjezɡi saparalde bajbiχʔulaan qʼad bukʼa qʼasi bukʼa nakʼkʼul partʃa tʼade borχun biχʔarabɡo ɡʔjel saparaɬ raqχunaan
kʼiɡo qʼojaɬ jaɡi motsʼaɬ jaɡi ʒeɡi tsʼikʼkʼun kiɡʼan zamanajaɬ muqʼadasab tʃadiralda tʼad nakʼkʼul partʃa tʃʼaniɡi ɡʼizrailal tʃʼarab bakʼaldasa raqχunaroan aj nakʼkʼul partʃa baʁarizeɡʼan ɡʔjel nuχde raqχunaroan nakʼkʼul partʃa tʼasa bosidal χalqʼaɬɡi saparalde bajbiχʔulaan
betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjez qʼajiɡi tʃʼwalaan wa ɡʔjesulɡo amrujaldaɬun saparaldeɡi raqχunaan betʼjerhanas musadasan kʔurab amru ɡʔjedin tʼubazabulaan ɡʼizrailaz

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ratʃitʼa ɡʼaratsɡi buχun kʼiɡo ɡʼartsul sur ɡʔabe ɡʔjel χʼaltʼizare χalqʼaɬul dandeɬi aχʼize wa χalqʼalda nuχda raqχine kːolebɬi ɬazabize
kʼijabɡo sur puleb ɡʔarakʔ baqχarab meχaɬ tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼat duda tsebe dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje bakʼarize kːola
tso sur puleb ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼidal duqχe χalqʼaɬul kʼudijal aj ɡʼizrailil qʼawmazul butʼrul rakʼarize kːola
ɡʔorkʔor qʼotʼ qʼotʼaral qʼoqʼal ɡʔarkʔal ɡʔarun sur purab meχalda saparalde raqχine kːola baqʼbakːul raqχalda tʃʼjel ɡʔabural qʼawmal
ɡʔjedinabɡo χʼalalda kʼiabileb nuχaɬ sur purabɡo saparalde raqχine kːola qʼilbajaɬul raqχalda tʃʼaral qʼawmal ɡʔjeb aχʼi bukʼine buɡo saparalde raqχine kːejaɬul bitsuneb ɡʼalamatɬun
dandeɬi aχʼize kːani sur puj tso χalatbaqχarab aχʼijaldaɬun
sural pujze ruɡo kaʃiʃzabaz ɡʔarunil wasaz ɡʔjeb buɡo nuʒeeɡi rukʼinesel naslabazeɡi daimab amru
nuʒ nuʒerɡo rakʔalda rukʼaɡo tuʃman tʼade kʼantsʼani wa raʁ kːani kʼwarab χʼalaɬ sural puj ɡʔjebmeχalda nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda nuʒer aχʼi raɡʼila wa tuʃmanasdasa nuʒ χwasar ɡʔarila
ɡʔjedinɡo roχalil qʼojazɡi bajramqʼojazɡi ʃːibab motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬɡi tsʼadulɡi raqʼlilɡi qʼurbanal ɡʔaruleb meχaɬ ɡʼartsul sural puj ɡʔjeb bukʼina betʼjerhanasda nuʒ rakʼalde ʃːwezarijaɬul ɡʼalamatɬun dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ
qʼotʼijaɬul tʃadiralda tʼad tʼuparab nakʼkʼul partʃa tʼade borχana kʼiabileb motsʼaɬul qʼoabileb qʼojaɬ wa
sinaj aburab salul awlaqχɡi tun ɡʼizrailal saparaɬ raqχana paran aburab salul awlaqχalde ʃːwedal nakʼkʼul partʃa ɬalqχana
ɡʔjeb bukʼana ɡʔjezul musadasan batʃʼarab betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon nuχda raqχarab tʼotsebeseb sapar
tʼotsebe saparalde baqχana jaɡʔudal askar qʼoqʼajalda χadub qʼoqʼa ɡʔabun ɡʔjezul betʼjerɬuda wukʼana ɡʼaminadawil was naχʼʃon
tsuaril was netaniel wukʼana isːaχaril qʼawmaɬul betʼjerɬuda
wa χelonil was eliaw zewulunil qʼawmaɬul betʼjerɬuda
χadub muqʼadasab tʃadir biχːana wa sokʼkʼana wa batʃːun tʃadirɡun ɡerʃonilɡi merarilɡi tuχumal saparalde raqχana
ɡʔjezda χadub biɬːana ruwimil askar qʼoqʼabi ɡʔarun ɡʔjezul betʼjerɬuda wukʼana ʃedeuril was elitsur
ʃimeonil qʼawmaɬul betʼjerɬuda wukʼana tsuriʃadajil was ʃelumiel
wa ɡadil qʼawmaɬul betʼjerɬuda deɡuelil was elijasaf
ɡʔjezda χadub saparalde baqχana keχatil tuχum batʃːun muqʼadasab qʼajiɡun ɡʼizrailal tsʼijab bakʼalde ʃːwelalde ɡʔjenib muqʼadasab tʃadir tʃʼwan bukʼine kːolaan
ɡʔjezda χadub saparalde baqχana jefraimil askar qʼoqʼabi ɡʔarun ɡʔjezul betʼjerɬuda wukʼana ammiɡʔudil was eliʃamaɡʼ
manasːil qʼawmaɬul betʼjerɬuda wukʼana pedatsuril was ɡamliel
wa bunjaminil qʼawmaɬul betʼjerɬuda ɡideonil was awidan
biʃːun aχiralda saparalde baqχana danil askar qʼoqʼabi ɡʔarun ɡʔjezul betʼjerɬuda wukʼana amiʃadajil was aχijezer
aʃeril qʼawmaɬe betʼjerɬi ɡʔabuleb bukʼana oχranil was paɡielitsa
wa naftalil qʼawmaɬe jenanil was aχiritsa
ɡʔjedinab bukʼana saparalde raqχulel ɡʼizrailazul qʼawmazul tartibɡun nizam
musatsa abuna ʒindirɡo wakʔad wasasda aj midjanijaw reɡuelil was χowawida niʒ unel ruɡo betʼjerhanas niʒee kʔjelin aburab rakʔalde wiɬːa niʒeda tsadaqχ dujeɡi niʒeeɡo ɡʼadin iqʼbal bukʼina ʃːajɡureɬul betʼjerhanas ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬe ɬikʼɬi ɡʔabize raɡʼi kʔun buɡeɬul in
amma ɡʔjes ʒawab kʔuna dun wiɬːinaro nuʒɡun dirɡo rakʔalde wa dirɡo ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬuqχe tʼadwusːin ɬikʼ dije jan
amma musatsa naqχeɡi abuna ɡʔarula duda reχun toɡe niʒ duda ɬikʼ ɬala salul awlaqχalda qʼaji tʃʼwaze sanaɡʼatal bakʼal niʒeda nuχ maɬulew tʃiɬun wukʼa
mun niʒeda tsadaqχ wiɬːani niʒetsa dujeɡi baʃːad ɡʔabila betʼjerhanas niʒee kʔurabʃːinab riqʼzi jan
tsinɡi betʼjerhanasul maɡʼardasa ɡʔjel saparalde raqχana wa ɡʔjez ɬabɡo qʼo nuχda bana ɬababɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔjezda tsebe tsebe uneb bukʼana betʼjerhanasul qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamasɡi ɡʔjezda χʼuχʔbaqχijaɬe bakʼɡi biχʔizabulaɡo
qʼad saparaɬ uneb meχalda betʼjerhanasul nakʼkʼul partʃaɡi bukʼunaan ɡʔjezda tʼasan borʒuneb
saparalde raqχine ʁamas borχuleɬul musatsa abulaan
waqχa tsewe ja betʼjerhan
riχː riχːun aɡi dur tuʃbabi
duda tseresa ɬutun aɡi mun riχaral
ʁamas ɬalqχarab meχalda ɡʔjes abulaan
ɬalqχe betʼjerhan
rikʼkʼun χʼalkʼolarel ɡʼizrailalɡun

zaχʼmaɬi χʼjeχʔjeze bokʔitʃʼoɡo ziɡardize ɬuɡʔana χalqʼ tso qʼojaɬ wa ɡʔjezul raziɡʔjetʃʼoɬijaɬul qʼulqʼudiɡi raɡʼun betʼjerhanasul kutakalda tsːin baqχana ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanasul tsʼa reʃːtʼana ɡʔjezde wa ɡʔjeɬ buχʼize bajbiχʔana χalqʼaɬ tʃʼjel ɡʔaburab bakʼaɬul raɡʼal
χalqʼ kumekaɬe musade aχʼi baze ɬuɡʔana musatsa betʼjerhanasde duɡʼa ɡʔabun χadub tsʼa swana
ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tawera
tso zamanalda ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔor rukʼaral batʼijal χalqʼazul ɡʼadamaz tʼalab ɡʔabize bajbiχʔana ɬikʼa ɬikʼab kwen ɡʔjezdaɡo tsadaqχ ziɡardize ɬuɡʔana ɡʼizrailalɡi ɡʔjez abuleb bukʼana
niʒee ɡʔan kʔolew tʃi kisa ʃːolew
rakʼalda buɡiʃː misrijalda tʃʼoboɡo kwanaleb bukʼarab tʃːuɡʼaɡi oχtserɡi pastʼanɡi purtʃːɡi perɡi raʒiɡi
ɡʔanʒejan abuni tʃerχalda ruχʼtsin χutʼun ɡʔjetʃʼo ʃːibniɡi ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul kwanaze ɡʼitsʼɡo manna ɡuroni badisan bakːun buɡo ɡʔjebɡi
manna bukʼana ʁaranχeraɬul χʔonalda reɬːarab qχaχʼab kʔjeraɬul zobalazul niɡʼmat
χalqʼaɬ ɡʔjeb bakʼarulaan wa χadub kwerzul ɡʔabida χːenolaan jaɡi tʃuχʼulaan χadub ɡʔjeb qχabajaɬub beɬunaan jaɡi ɡʔjeɬul bakarabi reʒulaan zajtunaɬul naχuɬ butsun beʒarab tʃadil ɡʼadinab tʼaɡʼamɡi bukʼana ɡʔjeɬul
qʼasi ʃːub kːarab meχalda ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ reʃːtʼunaan mannaɡi
musada raɡʼana χalqʼaɬul ɡʼodi ʃːibab qχizan qʼaj ɡʼoduleb bukʼana ʒiderɡo tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼaɡi tʃʼun ɡʔjebmeχalda betʼjerhanasul tsːin ɡʔjeleɡʔana musalɡi ɡʔjeɬ kutakalda rakʼbaqʼwana
ɡʔjes betʼjerhanasda abuna
ʃːaj dutsa dije ɡʔab ɡʼazab kʔoleb buɡeb ʃːib ɡʔabun ditsa dur tsːin baqχinaburab ɡʔab tʼolabɡo χalqʼ dida batʃːizabize kːani
dun ɡʔazul emeniʃː wuɡew didasan biʒarab χalqʼiʃː ɡʔab buɡeb ʃːaj dutsa ʒib χʔiχʔulej ɡʼadanaɬ ɬimer kiniɡin dida karandaɡi ɬun ɡʔjezije kʔjelin abun ɡʔjezul umumuze dutsa raɡʼi kʔurab rakʔalde ʃːwezeɡʼan dida batʃːizabuleb buɡeb ɡʔab χalqʼ
kisa ditsa ɡʔab ɡʼalamaɬe ɡʼurab ɡʔan balaɡʔileb ɡʔan kʔje niʒee kwanaze jan ɡʼodulel ruɡeɬul ɡʔjel dida tsere
tsoχʼo dida baʒarularo ɡʔab χalqʼ batʃːun ɡʔjeb tsʼaqʼɡo zaχʼmatab iʃ buɡo dije
χadubkːunɡi dije ɡʔadinabɡo qʼismat dutsa qχwan batani dur tsʼobaɬe mustaχʼiqʼawɡi dun watani ɡʔarula ɡʔabsaɡʼatɡo tʃʼwaj dun ɡʔab balaɡʔaɬukʔa wortʃʼize wukʼine
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazul kʼudijazda ɡʔorkʔosa ɡʼaqʼlu ɡʔunar buɡel butʼrul χʼisabalda duda ɬikʼ ɬalel tʃaɡʼi rakʼare dida tsere kinawniɡi ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo tʃi ritʃːante ɡʔjel ratʃʼine dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje wa duda askʼor tʃʼjeze
ɡʔjeniw dun kʼaɬaze wuɡo duda duda ɬurab ruχʼaldasaɡi bosun ɡʔjezdaɡi ɬela ditsa ɡʔjeb ɡʔjel χʼalaje raqχina duje ɡʔjeb bakʼab ɡʔir batʃːijaɬe tsoχʼo dutsaɡo batʃːitʃʼoɡo bukʼine
χalqʼalda abe ratsʼtsʼaɬi ɡʔabe meteralde χʼadurɬun rukʼine meter nuʒetsa ɡʔan kwanaze buɡo betʼjerhanasda raɡʼun buɡeɬul nuʒer ɡʼodiɡi niʒee ɡʔan kʔolew tʃi kisa ʃːolew misrijaldaɡo ɬikʼ bukʼana aburab nuʒer qʼulqʼudiɡi betʼjerhanas kʔjeze buɡo nuʒee ɡʔan
nuʒetsa ɡʔjeb kwanaze buɡo tso kʼiɡo ʃːuɡo antsʼɡo qʼoɡo qʼojaɬ ɡureb
nuʒetsa ɡʔjeb kwanaze buɡo tʼubarab motsʼaɬ nuʒer maɡʼarzuqχan batʃʼineɡʼan wa nuʒeda ɡʔjeb riχineɡʼan nuʒetsa nuʒedaɡo ɡʔorkʔowɡi wuɡew betʼjerhanasde muʁɡi reχun ɡʔjesda tsere ʃːaj niʒ misrijaldasa naqχe aral in abun nuʒ ziɡardaraɬuqχ
musatsa abuna
ɡʔaniw tsin anɬnusazarɡo raʁuqχan wuɡo wa dutsa abuleb buɡo tʼubarab motsʼaɬ ditsa ɡʔjezda ɡʔan kwanazabize buɡo jan
buɡebʃːinab ɡʼi botsʼi qχuniɡi ɡʼolebiʃː ɡʔjezije kinazeɡo ɡʔan jaɬuni raɬdaɬ buɡeb tʼolɡo tʃːuɡʼa kːuniɡi kinazeɡo ɡʼjeliʃː ɡʔjeb
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
betʼjerhanasul χʼal daɡʔɬuniʃː buɡeb ɡʔabsaɡʼat dudaɡo biχʔila ditsa duje kʔurab raɡʼi tʼubaliʃːali
musa χalqʼaɬuqχe wiɬːana wa betʼjerhanas aburab ʒo bitsana ɡʔjes χalqʼaɬul kʼudijazul ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo tʃi askʼowe aχʼana wa ɡʔjel tʃadiralda sweruqχ tʃʼjezaruna
ɡʔjebmeχalda betʼjerhan nakʼkʼul partʃaduɬ reʃːtʼana wa musaɡun kʼaɬana musada tʼad ɬurab ruχʼaldasa bosun ɡʔjenire rakʼararal kʼudijazdeɡi reʃːtʼinabuna ɡʔjeb ruχʼ ɡʔjezda tʼade ruχʼ reʃːtʼindal ɡʔjez bajbiχʔana aχʼunɡo aχʼun ʃawqʼalda allaɡʔasul amrabi zaɡʔir ɡʔarize amma χadubkːun tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔjedin ɡʔabitʃʼo
kʼiɡojal rukʼana ɡʔjenire ratʃʼintʃʼoɡo χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔorɡo tʃʼun tsojasda tsʼar bukʼana eldad kʼiabilesda medad amma ɡʔjezdeɡi reʃːtʼana ruχʼ ɡʔjelɡi rukʼindal kʔolbol kʼudijazul sijaχʼalda reχson tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje intʃʼoniɡi ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjelɡi ɬuɡʔana allaɡʔasul amrabi zaɡʔir ɡʔarun kʼaɬaze
tso ɡʼoloqχantʃi wekerun watʃʼana musaqχe wa ɡʔjes abuna
eldaditsaɡi medaditsaɡi allaɡʔasul amrabi ritsunel ruɡo jan
ɡʔitʼinab qʼojaldasaɡo musal kumektʃiɬun wukʼaraw nunil was jeɡʔoʃuatsa abuna
musa betʼjertʃʼaqχad tʃʼjezare ɡʔjel in
amma musatsa ʒawab kʔuna
dun tsʼunizejiʃː mun waqχaraw dije bokʔilaan betʼjerhanasul χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa kinazeɡo awaraɡzabazul karamaɬi ʃːweze wa betʼjerhanas ɡʔjezul ʃːiwasde ʒindirɡo illaɡʔijab ruχʼ reʃːtʼinabize jan
tsinɡi musaɡi kʔolbol kʼudijalɡi ʒide ʒider tʃadrazuqχe tʼadrusːana
tsinɡi betʼjerhanasul χʼalkʼoɬijaldaɬun kutakab ɡʔuri baqχana wa ɡʔjeɬ raɬdaqχan tʃʼorolabi ratʃun ratʃʼana χalqʼ tʃʼarab bakʼalda sweruqχ kisa kibeɡo tso qʼojaɬul saparaɬul manzilalda ɡʔjez rakʔ baχtʃizabuna kʼiɡo natʼaɬul borχaɬijalda
χalqʼ tʃʼorolabi rakʼarize ɬuɡʔana tʼubarab qʼojaɬɡi qʼasi roɡʔineɡʼanɡi wa χaduseb qʼojaɬɡi rakʼarana ɡʔjel wa ʃːiwas bakʼarana tso χomeraldasa
ʒeɡi ɡʔjezul kʼaldib ɡʔan bukʼaɡo betʼjerhanasul tsːin reʃːtʼana χalqʼalde wa ɡʔjes ɡʔjezde kutakab unti bitʃːana
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjeb bakʼalda kiwrot ɡʔataawa
kiwrot ɡʔataawajaldasa χalqʼ baʁarana χatserotalde wa ɡʔjenib ɬalqχana

marjamɡi ɡʔarunɡi ɬuɡʔana musada badibtʃʼwaj ɡʔabize ɡʔjes kuʃaldasa ɡʼadan jatʃunin abun
ɡʔjez abuleb bukʼana
ɡʼitsʼɡo musada ɡuroni kʼaɬatʃʼjewiʃː betʼjerhan niʒedaɡi ɡuriʃː ɡʔjew kʼaɬaraw in
wa ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasda raɡʼana
ʒiwɡo musajin abuni kutakalda χʼalimaw dunjalaldaɡo biʃːun χʼalimaw tʃi wukʼana
tsindaɡo betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi marjamidaɡi abuna
nuʒ ɬabalɡo dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsere riɬːa jan ɡʔjel ɬabalɡo ɡʔjenire riɬːana
tsinɡi betʼjerhan reʃːtʼana nakʼkʼul χʼubiɬun tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje wa ɡʔjes ɡʔarunɡi marjamɡi aχʼana ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo tsereɡʼan riɬːana
wa betʼjerhanas abuna
ɡʼintʼame diqχ
nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔow wuɡew betʼjerhanasul awaraɡase
dun zaɡʔirɬula tseretʼamijazuɬ
kʼaɬala ɡʔjewɡun makʔabazuɬ
amma dir laʁ musaɡun ɡʔjedin ɡurebχa bukʼuneb
dir roqʼow ɡʔjew sunduɬɡoɡi dije ritʼuqχaw wuɡo
ɡʔjewɡun dun kʼaɬala badisa badiwe raɡʔun
kitsi bitsenazdaɬun ɡurew
ɡʔjesda biχʔula betʼjerhanasul sipat
kinχa nuʒ χʼinqʼitʃʼjel
dir laʁ musada dande raqχun kʼaɬaze
betʼjerhanasul ɡʔjezda kutakab tsːin baqχana wa ɡʔjew naqχe ana
tʃadiraldasa batʼaɬun nakʼkʼul partʃa eχede bosarab saɡʼataɬ marjamil tʃerχ baras untijaɬ tsʼuna ɡʔjeɬul tʼom ɡʼazu ɡʼadin qχaχʼɬana ɡʔarun ɡʔjeldeχun wusːindal ɡʔjesda biχʔana ɡʔjelde barasaɬul unti baχun buɡebɬi
wa ɡʔjes musada abuna
betʼjertʃʼaqχad ɡʔarula ɡʔabuɡe niʒee tamiχʼ ɡʼaqʼlu ɡʔjetʃʼjel niʒetsa ɡʔaburab munaɡʔaɬuqχ
ɡʔarula duda ebelaɬul urɡʔisa batʃʼarabɡo χwarab wa baʃːdab tʃerχ turarab ɬimada reɬːine toɡe marjam
tsinɡi musatsa betʼjerhanasde duɡʼa ɡʔabuna
ja dir allaɡʔ saχɬizaje marjam in
amma betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔjeɬul badibe insutsa χʼatsʼu turabani ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ roɡʔo batʃːize kːeze ɡuriʃː ɡʔjeɬ bukʼarab ɡʔjej χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe jitʼje ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ χaduj tʼadjusːine jitʃːante
marjam ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe jitʼana wa ɡʔjej tʼadjusːineɡʼan χalqʼɡi buɡeɬubɡo tʃʼun bukʼana

χadub χalqʼ χatserotaldasa saparaɬ baqχana wa paran salul awlaqχalde ʃːwedal ɡʔjenib ɬalqχi ɡʔabuna
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ditsa ɡʼizrailaze kʔoleb buɡeb χanaanaɬul rakʔaɬul tsʼjeχ reχ ɡʔabize ʒasusal ritʼje ʃːibab qʼawmaɬul tsereqχabazda ɡʔorkʔosa tso tso tʃi
musatsa ɡʔjel ritʼana paran aburab salul awlaqχaldasa betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjel kinalɡo rukʼana ɡʼizrailazul qʼawmazul tsereqχabazda ɡʔorkʔosa tʃaɡʼi
ɡʔale ɡʔjezul tsʼaral
ruwimil qʼawmaldasa zakːuril was ʃammua
ʃimeonil qʼawmaldasa χʼoril was ʃafat
jaɡʔudal qʼawmaldasa jefunnil was χalew
isːaχaril qʼawmaldasa jusupil was iɡal
jefraimil qʼawmaldasa nunil was ɡʔoʃea
bunjaminil qʼawmaldasa raful was palti
zewulunil qʼawmaldasa sodil was ɡʔadiel
jusupil qʼawmaldasa ɡʔjesul was manasːil naslujaldasa susijil was ɡʔadij
danil qʼawmaldasa ɡemalijil was ammiel
aʃeril qʼawmaldasa mikaɡʼilil was setur
naftalil qʼawmaldasa wafsil was naχbi
ɡadil qʼawmaldasa maχil was ɡeuel
ɡʔjel ruɡo musatsa rakʔazul tsʼjeχ reχ ɡʔabize ritʼaral ɡʼadamazul tsʼaral nunil was ɡʔoʃeaje
χanaanaɬul tsʼjeχ reχ ɡʔabize ɡʔjel ritʼulaɡo musatsa abuna
nuʒ neɡew qʼotʼun muɡʼrul ʃːobazde a
χalɡʔabe kinab rakʔ ɡʔjeb buɡebali ɬazabe kinab χalqʼaɬ ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabun buɡebali qʼuwatabiʃː zaɡʼipabiʃː ɡʔjeb buɡeb daɡʔal tʃaɡʼijiʃː jaɬuni kʼudijab ɡʼalamiʃː ɡʔjezul buɡeb
ɡʔjeb χalqʼaɬ ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb rakʔ kinab buɡeb ɡʔarzajabiʃː muqʼsanabiʃː kinal ruɡel ɡʔjezul ʃaɡʔaral tʃadrazuqχiʃː ɡʔjez ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb buɡeb jaɡi swerun qʼadalɡi raral ʃːula ɡʔarural ʃaɡʔarazuqχiʃː
kinab rakʔ buɡeb ɡʔjenib beenabiʃː jaɡi qχartsinabiʃː ruɡiʃː ɡʔjenir ʁutʼbi ɡʔjetʃʼiʃː nuʒ sunkʔaɡo χʼinqʼuɡe ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬul piqχɡi bose tsʼibil barʃːuleb zaman ʃːun bukʼana
ɡʔjel ana wa ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬul χal ʃal ɡʔabuna tsin aburab salul awlaqχaldasa baqχarab bitʼaqχe lewo χamatalda askʼob buɡeb reχowalde ʃːwezeɡʼan
neɡewɡi naqχa tun ɡʔjel ʃːwana χewronalde anakil naslujaɬul aχʼimanitsaɡi ʃeʃajitsaɡi talmajitsaɡi ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bukʼana ɡʔjenib χewron bukʼana misrijaɬul ʃaɡʔar tsoanaldasa ankʔɡo sonaɬ tsebe barab ʃaɡʔar
eʃkol aburab rasaɬijalde ʃːwedal ɡʔjez tso tsʼolbol χʔop tʼad buɡeb ʁabujaɬul ɡʼarkʔjel qʼotʼana wa ɡʼjeraldaɡi ban ɡʔjezul kʼiɡojas batʃːana ɡʔjeb ɡʔjedinɡo sonoɡi inʒirɡi bosana ɡʔjenisa
ɡʔjeb bakʼalda tsʼar ɬuna eʃkolaɬul
kʼiqʼoɡo qʼojaldasan ɡʔjel saparaldasa tʼadrusːana
wa ɡʔjel ratʃʼana paran aburab salul awlaqχalda buɡeb kadeʃalde musaqχeɡi ɡʔaruniqχeɡi ɡʼizrailazul ʒamaɡʼataɬuqχeɡi ɡʔjenib ɡʔjezdaɡi χalqʼaldaɡi tsebe ɡʔjez biχʔa taraɬul jaqʼinab bajan kʔuna wa ɡʔjenisa bosun batʃʼarab piqχ biχʔizabuna
ɡʔjez musada abuna
niʒ ana dutsa ritʼarab rakʔalde χʼaqʼiqʼataldaɡi raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb rakʔ buɡoan dob ɡʔale ɡʔjenisa piqχ
amma doba ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb χalqʼ tsʼaqʼ qʼuwatab buɡo ɡʔjezul ʃaɡʔaralɡi ʃːula ɡʔarural wa tsʼaqʼɡo kʼudijal ruɡo niʒeda dora anakil naslabitsin riχʔana
amalekijaz ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb buɡo neɡewalda χitijazɡi jewusijazɡi amorijazɡi muɡʼruzda χanaanijaz raɬdal raɡʼalɬijaldaɡi iordan ɡʼurul raɡʼalɬijaldaɡi
χalewitsa χʼalbiχʔana musada tsebe χalqʼ ɡʼodobusːinabize wa ɡʔjes abuna
riɬːa ɡʔjeb rakʔ kwerde bosize niɬeqχa baʒarilaɡuriʃː ɡʔjeb
amma ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ rukʼaraz abuna
niɬeqχa baʒarularo dob χalqʼɡun raʁize dob niɬedasa qʼuwatab χalqʼ buɡo jan
ʒidedaɡo biχʔarab rakʔaɬul raqχaɬ χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔor kweʃal χarbal tʼiritʼizarize ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjel
ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabize ratʃʼaral tʃaɡʼi kwanaleb rakʔ buɡo ɡʔjeb niʒeda ɡʔjenir riχʔaral kinalɡo ɡʼadamal rukʼana nartal ɡʼadal tʃʼaχʼijal
niʒeda ɡʔjenir nefilimalɡi riχʔana anakil naslabi nefilimidasan ɬuɡʔaral kːola ɡʔjezda askʼor niʒ niʒedaɡo ɡartsʼalin kːolel rukʼana wa ɡʔjezdaɡi niʒ ɡartsʼalɬun riχʔulel rukʼana

ɡʔjebmeχaɬ χalqʼaɬ aχʼi χʼur baqχinabuna tʼubarab sordojaɬ ɡʼodana ɡʔjel ritʃːan ɡʔarkʔalɡun wa
musajeɡi ɡʔarunijeɡi badirtʃʼwajal ɡʔarize ɬuɡʔana tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ ɡʔjezda abuleb bukʼana
unɡo misrijaldaɡo χwaral aniʃː niʒ jaɡi ɡʔanir salul awlaqχalda χun rukʼaral aniʃː
ʃːaj betʼjerhanas niʒ ɡʔjeb rakʔalde ratʃunel ruɡel ɡʔjenir niʒ χwaltʃatsa tʃʼwaze rukʼinejiʃː tsinɡi niʒer ɬudbiɡi ɬimalɡi asirɬude kːela misrijaldeɡo tʼadrusːani ɬikʼ bukʼina niɬee
ɡʔjez tsotsazda abuleb bukʼana
ratʃʼa niɬetsa tsoɡi betʼjer tʼasa wiʃːize wa misrijalde tʼadrusːine jan
ɡʔjebmeχalda musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi ɡʼizrailaɬul ʒamaɡʼatalda tsere nakabazda tʃʼana
rakʔazul χal ʃal ɡʔabize arazda ɡʔorkʔor rukʼaral nunil was jeɡʔoʃuatsaɡi jefunnil was χalewitsaɡi tʃara buχʼun ʒidedaɡo tʼad bukʼarab partal biqχ biqχana
wa ɡʔjez ɡʼizrailazul ʒamaɡʼatalda abuna
niɬetsa χal ʃal ɡʔaburab rakʔ kutakalda ɬikʼab buɡo
betʼjerhan niɬeda ɡurχʼulew watani ɡʔjes ratʃineɡi ratʃun niɬee kʔjela raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb dob rakʔ
amma betʼjerhanasda dande raqχunɡe wa dob rakʔaɬul ɡʼadamazukʔa χʼinqʼuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul niɬetsa biɡʔaɡo qʼezarila dol dozije kumek ɡʔjetʃʼo niɬɡunin abuni betʼjerhan wuɡo χʼinqʼuɡe dozukʔa jan
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ χalqʼaɬ ɡʔjel ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwazeqχin rukʼana amma tsindaɡo kinazdaɡo biχʔun betʼjerhanasul qʼudrat zaɡʔirɬana dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
kidalɬizeɡʼan ɡʔab χalqʼaɬ dun naqχtʃʼwaze wuɡew kidalɬizeɡʼan ɡʔjel dida boʒilarel ditsa ʒideda ɡʔorkʔor ɡʔaruralʃːinal ɡʼalamatalɡi ɡʼjetʃʼoɡo
kweʃab untiɡi tʼade bitʃːan tʼaɡʼinabila ditsa ɡʔab χalqʼ wa dudasan biʒizabila ɡʔaldasaɡi tsʼikʼkʼarab wa qʼuwatab χalqʼ
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ musatsa betʼjerhanasda abuna
tsinɡi ɡʔjeb χabar raɡʼila dutsa durɡo qʼuwataldaɬun ʒider kwerʃːalikʔa ɡʔab χalqʼ χwasar ɡʔabural misrijazda
misrijaz kinabɡo bitsina ɡʔab rakʔaɬul χalqʼazda oɡʔ dir betʼjerhan ɡʔjel χalqʼazda raɡʼun buɡeɬul mun dur χalqʼalda tsadaqχ wukʼunewɬi wa dutsa badisa badiwe munɡo wiχʔize tolebɬi ja betʼjerhan χanaanijazda ɬala dur nakʼkʼul partʃa ɡʼizrailazda tʼad buɡebɬi wa mun ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ qʼad nakʼkʼul χʼubiɬun qʼasi tsʼadul χʼubiɬun unew wuɡebɬiɡi
tso tʃi tetʃʼoɡo dutsa ɡʔab χalqʼ tʼaɡʼinabuni dur χʼalkʼoɬijaɬul χabar raɡʼaral χalqʼaz abize buɡo
betʼjerhanasuqχa baʒaritʃʼo dozije kʔjeze amru ɡʔaburab rakʔalde dob χalqʼ batʃine ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjes dol salul awlaqχalda tʃʼwan ruɡo jan
bitʃːante ɡʔanʒe zaɡʔirɬun bukʼine betʼjerɡʔanasul χʼalkʼoɬi dutsaɡo aburab kutsalda
betʼjerhanasul sabru χalatab ɡʔjesul raχʼmu tsʼob ɡʼatʼidab ɡʔjew munaɡʔ χʼaqʼaldasaɡi tʼasaɬuɡʔuna amma ɡʼajibijal tamiχʼalde tsʼala umumuzul munaɡʔazuqχ ɬababileb wa unqʼabileb naslujalde ʃːwezeɡʼanɡi ɬimalazul ɬimalazeɡi tamiχʼ ɡʔabula jan
dur tʼadeɡʼanab raχʼmu tsʼobaɬe ɡʼolo tʼasaɬuɡʔa ɡʔab χalqʼaɬul munaɡʔaldasa misrijaldasa raqχaraldasa naqχe ʒaqʼa qʼojalde ʃːwezeɡʼanɡi tʼasaɬuɡʔunew wukʼarawɡo ɡʼadin
betʼjerhanas ʒawab kʔuna
dur ɡʔarijaɬe ɡʼolo tʼasaɬuɡʔina dun ɡʔjeb χalqʼaldasa
amma dirɡo tsʼaralχʼaɡi wa dunijalɡo tsʼjezaburab dirɡo retsːalχʼaɡi
dir qʼudratɡi biχʔaral misrijalda wa salul awlaqχalda ditsa ɡʔarural χʼikmatal iʃalɡi riχʔaral amma ɡʔjebɡi ɡʼjetʃʼoɡo tʼokʼaɬ tʃʼjetʃʼoɡo dir χʼalalɡi riχʔun dije mutʼiɡʼɬitʃʼjel tʃaɡʼazda
biχʔize ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjezije kʔjeze buɡin abun ɡʔjezul umumuze dun ɡʔjedarab rakʔ dun riχaraw tsoniɡi tʃijasda ɡʔjeb biχʔilaro
amma dir laʁ χalew ɡʔjezda reɬːaraw ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjew rakʼ rakʼaɬ dida boʒaraw wuɡo ɡʔjeɬuqχ ditsa ɡʔjew ʃːwezawila ɡʔjesda biχʔarab rakʔalde wa ɡʔjesul naslabi rukʼina ɡʔjeɬul betʼjerɡʔabiɬun
ɡʼatʼirakʔalda amalekijalɡi χanaanijalɡi ruɡo ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel ɡʔjedinɬidal meter nuʒ tʼadrusːa wa baɡʼarab raɬdaqχe uneb nuχkːun salul awlaqχalde a
betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
kidalɬizeɡʼan dida dande ɡʼarzaqχdize buɡeb ɡʔab tsːidal tsʼurab χalqʼ ɡʔjezul raziɡʔjetʃʼoɬijaɬul qʼulqʼudi raɡʼuleb buɡo dida
ɡʔjezda abe dirɡo tsʼaralχʼaɡi jan abuleb buɡin betʼjerhanas nuʒetsa bitsaralda reqʼon ɡʔabila ditsa nuʒee
nuʒer ʒanazabi ɡʔab salul awlaqχalda χutʼila χalqʼaɬul sijaχʼalda qχwaraw qʼoɡojaldasa tʼade son baraw wa dide qʼulqʼudulew wukʼaraw ʃːiwaw tʃijasul ʒanaza ɡʔab awlaqχalda χutʼila
nuʒer tsoniɡijas χʼjetʼje tʃʼjelaro ditsa nuʒer ulkaɬun ɡʔabize raɡʼi kʔun bukʼarab rakʔalda jefunnil was χalewitsaɡi nunil was jeɡʔoʃuatsaɡi ɡuroni
nuʒerɡo ɬimal asirɬude kːeze ɡurin χʼinqʼun rukʼana nuʒ ɡʔjele ɡʔjel ratʃina ditsa nuʒetsa inkar ɡʔaburab rakʔalde
amma nuʒer ʒanazabi ɡʔab salul awlaqχalde reχun tela
nuʒer ɬimal rukʼina kʼiqʼoɡo sonaɬ ɡʔab awlaqχalda ɡʼuχʔbi kiniɡin nuʒer pasiqʼɬijaɬuqχ ɡʼaqʼuba tʃʼamulel nuʒer aχirisew tʃi χwezeɡʼan
kʼiqʼoɡo sonaɬ nuʒetsa dob χanaanaɬul tsʼjeχ reχ ɡʔabulaɡo barab kʼiqʼoɡo qʼojaɬul ʃːibab qʼojaɬuqχ tso tso son rikʼkʼun nuʒ rukʼina ɡʼazabalda nuʒerɡo munaɡʔal sababɬun wa ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɬala nuʒeda dirɡun tuʃmanɬi ɡʔabijaɬul kʔoɡʼɬi
ditsa betʼjerhanas abuleb buɡo ɡʔjedin ditsa tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo ɡʔjedin ɡʔabila dida dande baqχarab tʼolabɡo ɡʔab tsːidal tsʼurab χalqʼaɬe ɡʔab salul awlaqχalda tʼaɡʼina ɡʔjel ɡʔjel kinalɡo χweze ruɡo ɡʔanir
musatsa dob rakʔaɬul tsʼjeχ reχ ɡʔabize ritʼun rukʼaral tʃaɡʼaz ɡʔjenisa tʼadrusːun χadub kweʃal χarbal tʼiritʼizarize ɬuɡʔana wa tʼolabɡo χalqʼɡi ɡʔjezda reqʼon musada dande qʼulqʼudana
ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ χʼinqʼaral χarbal tʼiritʼizaruraɬuqχ ɡʔjel kinalɡo kweʃab untiɡi kːun χwana betʼjerhanas ʒaza ɡʔabuna ɡʔjezije
rakʔaɬul χal ʃal ɡʔabize un rukʼarazda ɡʔorkʔosa tʃʼaɡo χutʼana ɡʼitsʼɡo nunil was jeɡʔoʃuaɡi jefunnil was χalewɡi
musatsa betʼjerɡʔanasul raɡʼi ɡʼizrailazda bitsarab meχaɬ tʼolabɡo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ ɡʼjek ɡʼjekijalda ɡʼodana
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ tsudunɡo tʼadeɡi raqχun ɡʔjel muɡʼruzdeχun qʼoqʼana
niʒetsa munaɡʔ ɡʔabuna jan abuleb bukʼana ɡʔjez bukʼaniɡi ɡʔanʒe niʒ ina betʼjerhanas aburab bakʼalde
amma musatsa abuna
ʃːaj nuʒetsa betʼjerhanasul amru tʼubazabulareb ɡʔjeb iʃaɬul nuʒee ɬikʼab χʼasil kːolaro
kireɡo unɡe nuʒeda tsadaqχ betʼjerhan ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul ɡʔanʒe ani tuʃbabatsa ʃːuʃːaqχ riχːizarize ruɡo nuʒ
nuχda nuʒeda dande raʁila amalekijalɡi χanaanijalɡi wa ɡʔjez tʃʼwala nuʒ nuʒetsa betʼjerhanasde muʁ reχana ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjesul kwerbaqʼi bukʼunaro nuʒee jan
amma ʒidedaɡo rakʼtʃʼun muɡʼruzdeχun ralaɡʔun nuχda raqχana ɡʔjel tʃaɡʼi betʼjerhanasul qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamasɡi musaɡi ruɡeɬurɡo tʃʼana
tsinɡi muɡʼruzda tʃʼaral amalekijazɡi χanaanijazɡi ɡʔjezda dandeɡi ratʃʼun ɡʔjel ʃːuʃːaqχ riχːizaruna wa χormajalde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɬutizaruna

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazda ɬazabe ditsa nuʒee watʼanɬun kʔurab rakʔalde ʃːwarab meχalda
wa nuʒetsa betʼjerhanase ɡʼi botsʼijaldasa qʼurban ɡʔabuleb meχalda tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban nazrujaɬul qʼurban raqʼlil qʼurban jaɡi bokʔarab χirijab bajram kʼodo ɡʔabijalda χurχarab qʼurban wa nuʒetsa betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔuinab maχʼ baqχinabuleb meχalda
ɡʔjelda tsadaqχɡo roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi bukʼine kːola zajtunaɬul naχul ɡinaɬul unqʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼaɡi
tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe jaɡi batʼijab qʼurbanaɬe batʃʼuneb ʃːibab kʔjeɡʼjeralda tsadaqχ ɡʔjedinɡo batʃʼine kːola ɡinaɬul unqʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa
kujalda tsadaqχ batʃʼine kːola ɡinaɬul ɬabɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʒubarab jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun kʼiɡo butʼa biʃːun ɬikʼab χanʒdal wa
ɡinaɬul ɬabɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa tʃaʁirɡi ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo betʼjerhanase χirijab maχʼ baqχinabijaɬe
betʼjerhanase basi qʼurbanɬun ɡʔabuleb buɡoni tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban jaɡi nazrujaɬul qʼurban jaɡi raqʼlil qʼurban
ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ bukʼine kːola roɬul χirijab sadaqʼa baʃːdab ɡin zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʁorɬ ʒubarab jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun ɬabɡo butʼa biʃːun ɬikʼab χanʒdal
qʼurban bakʼalda tʼade tʼjeze tʃaʁiraɬul baʃːdab ɡinɡi bukʼine kːola ɡʔjeb bukʼina tsʼadudaɬun betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo kʔoleb sadaqʼa ɡʔjesije χirijab buɡo ɡʔjeɬul maχʼ
ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize kːola qʼurbanaɬe batʃʼuneb ʃːibab basiɡun kujɡun kʔjeɡʼjerɡun jaɡi burutʼɡun tsadaqχ
qʼurbanazul qʼadar kinab bukʼaniɡi ʃːibab qʼurbanaɬe ɡʔjedin ɡʔabe
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬul ʃːiwaw tʃijas ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize kːola betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo χirijal sadaqʼabi ɡʔarulaɡo wa qʼurban buχʼijaldaɬun ɡʔjesije χirijab maχʼ baqχinabulaɡo
tʃijar rakʔaldasa watʃʼaraw wa nuʒeda ʁorɬ ɡʼumru ɡʔabulew tsoɡidaw tʃijase bokʔani betʼjerhanase χirijab maχʼ baqχinabizeɬun tsʼadul qʼurban ɡʔabize ɡʔjesɡi kinabɡo ɡʔabize kːola nuʒetsaɡo ɡʼadin
nuʒeeɡi nuʒeda tsadaqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel tʃijar rakʔazdasa ɡʼadamazeɡi tso qʼanun bukʼine kːola ɡʔjedinab buɡo rukʼinesel naslabazeɡi daimab amru nuʒɡi qʼwatʼisa ratʃʼaral ɡʼadamalɡi betʼjerhanasda tsere raʃːadal ruɡo
nuʒeeɡi nuʒeda tsadaqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel tʃijar χalqʼazul ɡʼadamazeɡi tso qʼanun wa tso nizam
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔadin abe ditsa ratʃunel ruɡeb rakʔalde nuʒ ʃːwaralɡo
wa nuʒetsa ɡʔjeɬul niɡʼmat kwanalaɡo ɡʔjeldasa butʼa betʼjerhanase χirijab sadaqʼaɬun kʔje
tʼotsebe χːarab χanʒdal ɡʔaburab tʃed χirijab sadaqʼaɬun kʔjeze kːola ɡʔjeb ʃːwezabe ɡʔotsʼib lal reχuleb meχaɬ kʔoleb χirijab sadaqʼa χʼisabalda
tʼotsebe χːarab χanʒdal χirijab sadaqʼa kinalɡo rukʼinesel naslabaz betʼjerhanasul roqʼobe kʔjeze kːola daimɡo
betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔarural amrabi naɡaɡʔ nuʒeqχa tʼurazaritʃʼoɡo χutʼani
betʼjerhanas musadasan tʼalab ɡʔarural kinalɡo amrabiɡi χʼisabalde rosun betʼjerhanas tʼotsebe amru ɡʔaburab qʼojaldasa baqχarab ɡʔanʒeɡi nuʒer χadusel ɡʼjelazɡi ɡʔadin ɡʔabe
ɡʔjeb χalqʼaɬuqχa ɬatʃʼoɡo kːarab ʁalatʼ batani tʼolɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬul raqχaldasan tʼuban buχʼuleb wa betʼjerhanase χirijab maχʼ baqχinabuleb qʼurbanaɬe kʔjeze kːola basi wa ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ bukʼine kːola roɬul sadaqʼaɡi qʼurban bakʼalda tʼade tʼoleb ʒoɡi munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe tso deɡʼjenɡi qχweze kːola
bitʃːante kaʃiʃas tʼobitʼize ɡʼizrailaɬul tʼolɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬul munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurban χalqʼ munaɡʔaldasa batsʼtsʼaɬize bukʼine ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb χalqʼaɬuqχa ɬatʃʼoɡo kːarab ʁalatʼɬidal bukʼarab ɡʔjeb ʁalatʼaɬuqχ χalqʼaɬ betʼjerhanase qʼurbanɡi ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ kʔjeze kːolel sadaqʼabiɡi kʔjela betʼjerhanasda tsebe munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanɡi qχwela
ɡʼizrailaɬul tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬulɡi wa ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔor ruɡel tʃijar χalqʼazul ɡʼadamazulɡi munaɡʔaldasa allaɡʔ tʼasaɬuɡʔina ʃːajɡureɬul χalqʼaɬuqχa ɬatʃʼoɡo kːarab munaɡʔ bukʼindal ɡʔjeb
ɡʔjedinab munaɡʔ tso tʃijas ɡʔabun buɡoni munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe ɡʔjes kʔjeze kːola ɬaɡʼarab tsʼtsʼje
kaʃiʃas betʼjerhanasda tsebe tʼobitʼila toχɬukʔje munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːaraw tʃi watsʼtsʼaɬijaɬe qʼurban wa ɡʔjesul munaɡʔazdasa tʼasa ɬuɡʔina
tsoɡo nizam bukʼine kːola toχɬukʔje munaɡʔ ɡʔaburaw ʃːiwaw tʃijase ɡʼizrailaseɡi tʃijar χalqʼaɬul tʃijaseɡi
amma tsoniɡi tʃijas ɡʼizrailaw wukʼa ɡotʃun watʃʼaraw wukʼa urʁunɡo munaɡʔ ɡʔabuni ɡʔjeb kːola betʼjerhan χʼaqʼir ɡʔawi ɡʔjedinaw tʃi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔow teze beɡʔularo naqχe ʁeze kːola
ɡʔjes betʼjerhanasul raɡʼul san ɡʔabitʃʼo ɡʔjes ɡʔjesul amru χwezabuna ɡʔjew tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa watʃaqχize kːola ɡʔjesije ʒaza ɡʔabize kːola
ɡʼizrailal salul awlaqχalda rukʼaɡo ɡʔjezda wiχʔana tso tʃi ʃamatqʼojaɬ tsʼul bakʼarulew
ɡʔjedin ɡʔjew wiχʔaral ɡʼadamaz ɡʔjew watʃana musaqχeɡi ɡʔaruniqχeɡi tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼataɬuqχeɡi
ɡʔjew ʒaniw tʼamuna qχarawulzabiɡi tana ʃːajɡureɬul ɬaleb bukʼintʃʼo ʃːib ɡʔjesije ɡʔabilebali
ɡʔjebmeχalda betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔjew tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ χalqʼ reʃːtʼarab bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼiweɡi watʃun ɡʔjew ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwaze
tsinɡi χalqʼaɬ ɡʔjew χalqʼ tʃʼarab bakʼaldasa doweɡʼanɡi watʃun betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔadin abe kunazul ɡʼjertelal ruqʼe nuʒerɡo ratʼlil aχada ʃːibab ɡʼjertelalde kantʃʼqχaχʼilab kʔjeraɬul kunɡi ʒubaj rukʼinesel ɡʼjelazɡi daim ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize kːola
ɡʔjel ɡʼjertelazuqχ balaɡʔun nuʒeda rakʼalde ʃːwela betʼjerhanasul kinalɡo amrabi wa napsaɬɡi berazɡi tʼalab ɡʔabulelda χadur intʃʼoɡo nuʒetsa ɡʔjel amrabi tʼurazarila
tsinɡi nuʒeda kʼotʃon telaro dir amrabi nuʒ ɡʔjezda reqʼon χʔwadila wa allaɡʔasda tsere ratsʼtsʼadalɬun rukʼina
dun wuɡo misrijaldasa nuʒ qʼwatʼire ratʃaraw nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ dun wuɡo betʼjerhan nuʒer allaɡʔ

lewijil qʼawmaldasa keχatil itsχaril was qʼoraχʼɡi ruwimil qʼawmaldasa eliawil wasal datanɡun awiramɡi peletil was onɡi
musada dande tʃʼana ɡʔjezul raqχ kːuna kʼinusijalda kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo tʃijas ɡʔjel kinalɡo rukʼana ɡʼizrailazul tsereqχabi raɡʼi biɬːaral qʼadrujal tʃaɡʼi
ɡʔjez swerun kːuna musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi wa ɡʔjezda kʼalɡʔiqʼize ɬuɡʔana
ɡʼjela tsʼaqʼɡo tʼasan kːolel ruɡo nuʒ tʼolabɡo χalqʼɡi batsʼtsʼadab buɡo χalqʼɡunɡi betʼjerhan wuɡo ʃːajχa nuʒetsa nuʒɡo betʼjerhanasul tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼataldasa tʼadeɡʼanalɬun ɡʔarulel
ɡʔjeb raɡʼidal musa tʃʼarbida nakabazde kːana

meter radal betʼjerhanas ʒinditsaɡo biχʔizabila ʃːiw ɡʔjesul kːolewaliɡi ʃːiw watsʼtsʼadaw wuɡewaliɡi ɬije ɡʔjes ʒinde ɡʼaɡarɬize iχtijar kʔolebaliɡi ɡʔjes tʼasa wiʃːaraw tʃijase res bukʼina ɡʔjesde ɡʼaɡarɬize

wa meter ɡʔjezda ʒanib ɬe tsʼa rekʼarab tʼurtʃːiɡi tʼurtʃːijalda tʼade baj χirijab ɡʔuinmaχʼaɬul ʒubanʒoɡi tsinɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɬe betʼjerhanas tʼasa wiʃːaraw wukʼina watsʼtsʼadawɬun ɡʼjela ɡʔanʒe nuʒee lewijil naslabi

ɡʼjenekːeja lewijil naslu

munɡi dur watsal lewitalɡi ɡʔjes ʒindeɡo ɡʼaɡarɬize ɡʔaruna nuʒetsajin abuni ɡʔjelda tʼadeɡi nuʒeeɡo kaʃiʃɬiɡi tʼalab ɡʔabuleb buɡo
munɡi dur iʃtsojalɡi betʼjerhanasda dande tʃʼun ruɡo ɡʔarunitsa ʃːib ɡʔabun buɡeb nuʒetsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔjew kakize kːani

niʒ ratʃʼinaro

dutsa niʒ ratʃintʃʼo raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb rakʔalde kʔjetʃʼo niʒee χurzalɡi tsʼolbol aχalɡi duda ɡʼadamal betsːal ruɡilaniʃː kːoleb niʒ ratʃʼinaro duqχe

munɡi dur iʃtsojalɡi meter betʼjerhanasda tsere tʃʼjeze kːola munɡi dolɡi ɡʔarunɡi

kinatsaɡo rosana ʒiderɡo ʃːurmal ɬuna ɡʔjezda ʒanib buχʼarab tʼurtʃːiɡi χirijab maχʼɡʔuinab ʒubanʒoɡi wa musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi askʼor dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa eχetana kinalɡo
qʼoraχʼitsa dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje bakʼarana musada dande tʃʼarazul tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼat ɡʔjebmeχalda kinabɡo χalqʼaɬe betʼjerhanasul qʼudrat zaɡʔirɬana

ɡʔjes χalqʼalda ɬazabuna
ɡʔal munapiqʼazul tʃadirazdasa rikʼkʼadeɡʼan a ɡʔjezul qʼaji qʼonojalda kwerɡi qχwaɡe ɡuroni ɡʔjezul munaɡʔ sababɬun nuʒɡi χweze ruɡo jan
χalqʼ qʼoraχʼilɡi datanilɡi wa awiramilɡi tʃadiraldasa rikʼkʼadeɡʼan ana datanɡi awiramɡi ʒiderɡo ɬudbiɡun ɬimalɡun wa χaχulel ɡʔitʼitʃalɡun ʒiderɡo tʃadirazul kʼaltʼa eχetun tʃʼana
tsinɡi musatsa abuna
ɡʔanʒe nuʒeda biχʔila ditsa kinabɡo dijeɡo bokʔun ɡureb betʼjerhanasul amrujaldaɬun ɡʔabuleb bukʼin
naɡaɡʔɬun tsoɡidal ɡʼadamalɡo ɡʼadin ɡʼadatijab χwel reʃːtʼun ɡʔjel χwani dun betʼjerhanas witʼaraw tʃi kːolaro
amma betʼjerhanas ɡʼaʒaibab ɬuɡʔa baqχinaldaɬun rakʔɡi qχwalχʔun ɡʔjelɡi ɡʔjezul kinabɡo mulkɡi tsadaqχɡo rakʔuɬe tʼjerχʔinabuni wa ɡʔjel tʃʼaɡoɡo barzaχalde ani nuʒeda ɬan bukʼa ɡʔjel betʼjerhanasda dande tʃʼaral rukʼaralɬi
musa kʼaɬan waqχinalde ɡʔjezda ʁorkʔ bukʼarab rakʔ kʔwatʼun ana
rakʔaɬ kʼal ɡʔakʼkʼana wa ɡʔjel ʒalɡoɡi ɡʔjezul qχizan qʼajɡi qʼoraχʼil aɡʔluɡi ɡʔjezul bukʼarabʃːinab maɡʼiʃatɡi rakʔuɬe tʼjerχʔun ana
ɡʔjel tʃʼaɡoɡo ana barzaχalde ʒider tʼolabɡo maɡʼiʃatɡun tsadaqχ ɡʔjezda tʼad rakʔ dande ana wa ɡʔjelɡi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼaɡʼana

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunil was eleazarida abe ruχʼarazul ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼulel ʃːurmalɡi rakʼarun ɡʔjezda ʒanisa tʼurtʃːi naqχe bajilan
ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjel ruɡo munapiqʼazul ɡʼumruɡi kʔun muqʼadasalɬun ɬuɡʔaral ʃːurmal ratʃitʼaɡi ruχun ɡʔjezul tʼantʃal ɡʔare qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad kːweze betʼjerhanasda tsere rosun rukʼinaɬ ɡʔjel ʃːurmal muqʼadasalɬun ɬuɡʔana bitʃːante ɡʔjeb χutʼize ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ tsʼodorɬijaɬe ɡʼalamatɬun in
kaʃiʃ eleazaritsa rakʼarana tsʼadutsa ruχʼarazuqχ rukʼaral mazɡarul ʃːurmal wa ɡʔjezul tʼantʃal ɡʔaruna qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad kːweze
musade betʼjerhanas ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjel qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad kːural mazɡarul tʼantʃaz ɡʼizrailazda daimɡo rakʼalde ʃːwezabize bukʼana betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼize ɡʔarunilɡi ɡʔjesul naslabazulɡi ɡuroni iχtijar ɡʔjetʃʼjebɬi qʼoraχʼilɡi ɡʔjesul iʃtsojazulɡi ɡʼadinab qʼismat ɬilniɡi bukʼunɡutʼize
χaduseb qʼojaɬ ɡʼizrailazul tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼat ɬuɡʔana razi ɡʔjetʃʼoɬi zaɡʔir ɡʔabun musadeɡi ɡʔarunideɡi qʼulqʼudize nuʒetsa tʃʼwana betʼjerhanasul χalqʼ in abuleb bukʼana ɡʔjez
amma kinabɡo χalqʼ musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi dandeɡi baqχun dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraldeχun balaɡʔidal χalqʼalda biχʔana tʃadiralda tʼad nakʼkʼul partʃa tʃʼun betʼjerhanasul qʼudrat zaɡʔirɬana
musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje ʃːwaralɡo

tsinɡi ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo kʼalaʁorkʔje nakabazde kːana
musatsa ɡʔarunida abuna
bose χeχɡo ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼuleb ʃːurunɡi ɬe ɡʔjelda ʒanib qʼurban bakʼaldasa bosun ɡʔjeleɡʔarab tʼurtʃːiɡi ɡʔuinmaχʼazul ʒubanʒoɡi wa ɡʼjedeɡʼje χalqʼaɬuqχe ɡʔjel munaɡʔaldasa ratsʼtsʼad ɡʔarize betʼjerhanasul tsːin reʃːtʼun buɡo wa χalqʼalde kweʃab χwalil unti bitʃːan buɡo jan
ɡʔarunitsa musatsa maɬuqχe ɡʔabuna wa χalqʼaɬuqχe ɡʼjedeɡʼana ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔob χwalil unti bajbiχʔun bukʼana ʒindirɡo ʃːurminib χirijab ɡʔuinmaχʼazul ʒubanʒoɡi ɬun ɡʔarun χalqʼ batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔana
ɡʔjew χwarazdaɡi tʃʼaɡojazdaɡi ɡʔorkʔow eχetana wa χwalil unti qʼotʼana
amma ɡʔjeb untutsa χwana   tʃi qʼoraχʼ sababɬun χwaral rikʼkʼintʃʼoɡo
χwalil unti ɬuɡʼidal ɡʔarun dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa tʃʼun wukʼaraw musaqχe tʼadwusːana

tsinɡi betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailalɡun kʼaɬaj wa ɡʔjezuqχa antsʼila kʼiɡo ɡʼansa bose ʃːibab qʼawmaɬuqχa tso tso ɡʔjezul kʼudijazul ɡʼunsbi ʃːibab ɡʼansajalda tʼad qʼawmaɬul betʼjerasul tsʼarɡi qχwaj
lewijil ɡʼansajalda tʼad ɡʔarunil tsʼar qχwaj ʃːibab qʼawmaɬul kʼudijasuqχa tso tso ɡʼansa bosize kːola
ɡʔjel ɡʼunsbi ɬe dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda ʒanir dun munɡun dandtʃʼwaleb bakʼalda qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamasalda tsere
ditsa tʼasawiʃːaraw tʃijasul ɡʼansajalda tʼad tʃʼoral kʼantsʼize ruɡo wa ɡʔjedin ditsa ɡʔorkʔob qʼotʼizabize buɡo ɡʼizrailazul nuʒedasa raziɡʔjetʃʼoɬijaɬul ɬuɡʼjel ɡʔjetʃʼjeb qʼulqʼudi
musatsa ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʼizrailazda bitsana wa ɡʔjezul kʼudijaz antsʼila kʼiɡo ɡʼansa ɡʔjesuqχe kʔuna ʃːibab qʼawmaldasa tso tso ɡʼansa
tsinɡi musatsa ɡʔjel dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬur betʼjerhanasul qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamasalda tsere ɬuna
χaduseb qʼojaɬ musa tʃadiraɬuwe wiɬːana wa ɡʔjesda biχʔana ɡʔarunil ɡʼansajalda aj lewijil qʼawmaɬul ɡʼansajalda tʃʼoral kʼantsʼun ruɡebɬi ɡʔjelda bukʼdulɡi rakːun tʼjeɡʔɡi ban mindalʔɡi barʃːun batana
musatsa kinalɡo ɡʼunsbi betʼjerhanasda tseresa qʼwatʼireɡi rosun ɡʼizrailazda riχʔizaruna ɡʔjel ɡʔjezuqχ ralaɡʔana tsinɡi ʃːiwas ʒindi ʒindir ɡʼansa naqχe bosana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔarunil ɡʼansa ɬe qʼotʼijaɬul ʁansida tsebe bitʃːante ɡʔjeb bukʼine mutʼiɡʼɬulareze rakʼaldeʃːwejaɬul ɡʼalamatɬun ɡʔjedin dutsa aχir ɬela dida dande ɡʔjezul qʼulqʼudijaɬe wa ɡʔjelɡi χwetʃʼoɡo χutʼila

betʼjerhanas ɡʔarunida abuna
dutsaɡi dur wasazɡi tʼolabɡo dur ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬɡi ʒawab kʔjeze buɡo muqʼadasab bakʼalda ʃːibɡʼaɡi munaɡʔ kːejaɬul ɡʔjelda tʼadeɡi kaʃiʃzabazul qχuluqχalda ʒanib ʃːibɡʼaɡi munaɡʔ χatʼa kːani ɡʔjeɬulɡi ʒawab kʔjeze buɡo dutsaɡi dur wasazɡi
lewijil aj dur umumuzul qʼawmaldasa durɡo watsalɡi aχʼje duqχeɡo dutsaɡi dur wasazɡi qʼotʼijaɬul tʃadiralda tsebe tʼaɡʼat ɡʔabuleb meχalda ɡʔjel kidaɡo duje kumekaɬe rukʼine
ɡʔjel rukʼine ruɡo dur nuχmaɬijalda ʁorkʔ wa tʃadiralda ʒanib χʼaʒatab kinabɡo χʼaltʼi ɡʔabize buɡo ɡʔjez amma ɡʔjezije ɡʔuqʼun buɡo ja muqʼadasab tsʼaraɡʼalda ja qʼurban bakʼalda kwer qχwaze ɡuroni χweze ruɡo ɡʔjelɡi ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ nuʒɡoɡi
ɡʼitsʼɡo lewital rukʼine ruɡo duda tsadaqχ dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub duje kumek ɡʔabijaɬe wa ɡʔjenir ɡʔarize kːolelʃːinal χʼaltʼabiɡi ɡʔjez tʼurazarize ruɡo amma tsoɡi batʼijal tʃaɡʼi nuʒeda askʼore qʼazetsin beɡʔularo
nuʒetsa muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬulɡi qʼurban bakʼaɬulɡi tʼalab ɡʔabize kːola χadubkːunɡi ɡʼizrailazda dir tsːin baqχintʃʼoɡo bukʼine
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosaɡi ratʃun ditsaɡo kʔuna nuʒee kumekaɬe lewital ɡʔjel rukʼine ruɡo nuʒee dir sajʁatɬun ɡʔjel betʼjerhanase ratʼa ɡʔaruralɬun kːola dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda χʼaltʼize rukʼine
amma ɡʼitsʼɡo dutsaɡi dur wasazɡi ɡuroni tʼubaze beɡʔularo qʼurban bakʼalda wa tʃadiralda ʒanibeχun pardawalda naqχa buɡeb bakʼalda χurχarab kinabɡʼaɡi kaʃiʃzabazul qχuluqχ ɡʔjeb nuʒeda tʼadab qχuluqχ kːola ditsa nuʒee sajʁatɬun kʔoleb buɡo kaʃiʃɬi ɡʔjeb tʼade bosize ɬuɡʔaraw ʃːiwaw batʼijaw tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola
betʼjerhanas ɡʔarunida abuna
ditsa dur iχtijaralde kʔuna χalqʼaɬ dir muqʼadasab bakʼalde ratʃʼunel tʼolalɡo χirijal sadaqʼabi ɡʼizrailaz dije ɡʼolo batʃʼunebʃːinab χirijab sadaqʼa ditsa kʔoleb buɡo duje wa dur naslabaze daim nuʒee bukʼine kːoleb butʼa χʼisabalda
χalqʼaɬ ɡʔarulel biʃːunɡo χirijal qʼurbanal wa χirijal sadaqʼabi roɬul χirijal sadaqʼabi munaɡʔ tʃuruleb qʼurban wa ɡʼajib betsʼuleb qʼurban ɡʔjel kːola kutakalda χirijal ʒal wa ɡʔjezul ruχʼularel butʼabi duje rukʼine kːola ɡʔjeb kːola durɡi dur naslabazulɡi butʼa
ɡʔjeb kwanaj tʼadeɡʼanab χiraɬijaɬul sadaqʼa χʼisabalda ɡʔjeb kwanaze beɡʔula dur naslujaɬul ʃːiwaw biχʔintʃijas ɡʔjeb χirijab ʒo bukʼin kʼotʃonɡe
ɡʔale ʒeɡi duje bukʼine kːoleb ʒo ɡʼizrailaz ratʃʼunel kinalɡo χʔwaɡʼjezarulel qʼurbanal ditsa dujeɡi dur wasal jasazeɡi daim nuʒee bukʼine kːoleb butʼaɬun kʔolel ruɡo dur ruqʼaɬul ʃːiwaw watsʼtsʼadaw tʃijas kwanaze beɡʔula ɡʔjeb butʼa
ɬiɬarijaɬul awalalda betʼjerhanase χirijab sadaqʼa χʼisabalda batʃʼuneb biʃːun ɬikʼab zajtunaɬul naχɡi tsʼijab tʃaʁirɡi tʼorʃːelɡi ditsa duje kʔoleb buɡo
rakʔaldasa ʃːwarab wa dir muqʼadasab bakʼalde batʃʼuneb kinabniɡi tʼotsebeseb niɡʼmat bukʼine buɡo durɬun dur ruqʼaɬul ʃːiwaw watsʼtsʼadaw tʃijas kwanaze beɡʔula ɡʔjeb
ɡʼizrailalda ɬitsaniɡi betʼjerhanase nazru ɡʔaburab kinabniɡi ʒo duje bukʼine buɡo
betʼjerhanase kʔjeze kːoleb ebelaɬul tʼotsebeseb biχʔintʼintʃʼɡi insanasulɡi χʼajwanaɬulɡi ɡʔjebɡi dur kːola amma ɡʼadamazul tʼotsere ɡʔarural biχʔinɬimal ɡʔjezuqχ χʼaqʼɡi bosun erken ɡʔarize kːola wa batsʼtsʼadab ɡureb χʼajwanaɬ ɡʔaburab tʼintʃʼaɬuqχɡi χʼaqʼ kʔjeze kːola
tʼotseresel biχʔinɬimalazuqχ χʼaqʼ bose ɡʔjez motsʼ barab zamanalda ʃːuɡo ʃekel ɡʼartsul
amma ɡʼatʃijazul ɡʼijazul jaɡi tsʼtsʼanazul tʼotsebeseb qʼinɬi betʼjerɡʔanasul kːola ɡʔjezuqχ χʼaqʼ kʔolaro ɡʔjezul bi punqχizabe qʼurban bakʼalde wa ɡʔjenib ɡʔjezul tʼatʼiɡi buχʼje betʼjerhanase tsʼadul qʼurbanɬun ɡʔjew razijab kʼkʼujdul maχʼ baqχinabizeɬun
ɡʔjezul ɡʔan duje bukʼina χʔwaɡʼjezabuleb qʼurbanaɬul meɡʔjedɡi kwaranab boχɡi ɡʼadin
ɡʼizrailaz betʼjerhanase ratʃʼunel kinalɡo χirijal sadaqʼabi ditsa dujeɡi dur ɬimalazeɡi kʔolel ruɡo nuʒer daimab butʼa χʼisabalda ɡʔjeb buɡo daimab betʼjerhanasdaɡi durɡun dur naslujaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔaburab kidaniɡi biχːulareb abadijab tsʼamul
betʼjerhanas ɡʔarunida abuna
ɡʼizrailalda dur bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo kinabɡʼaɡi irs wa rakʔaɬul kinabɡʼaɡi butʼa dunɡo wukʼina ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔow dur butʼaɬunɡi dur irsɬunɡi
dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda qχuluqχ ɡʔabijaɬuqχ lewijil naslabaze irsaɬe ditsa kʔola ɡʼizrailazul kinalɡo antsʼil butʼabi
ɡʼizrailal tʼokʼaɬ dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralde ɡʼaɡarɬize beɡʔularo naɡaɡʔ ɡʼaɡarɬani ɡʔjel munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːeze ruɡo wa ɡʔjeb sababɬun ɡʔjezije ʒaza ɡʔabize buɡo
bitʃːante dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub χʼaltʼi ɡʔabize ɡʼitsʼɡo lewitaz wa qχubɬijaldasa ɡʔjeb tsʼunijaɬul ʒawabɡi ɡʔjezdasa tʼalab ɡʔabize ɡʔjeb buɡo daimab tʼadqʼaj nuʒer tʼolalɡo naslabaz tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo tʼubazabize kːoleb amma ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔjezije rakʔaɬul irs bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo
ɡʔjeɬul bakʼalda ditsa lewitaze irsɬun kʔolel ruɡo ɡʼizrailaz betʼjerhanase ratʃʼunel ɡʔjezul botsʼi riqʼzijaɬul antsʼil butʼabi ɡʔjedinɬidalin ditsa aburab ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔjezije rakʔaɬul butʼa bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼin abun
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
lewijilazda abe ditsa nuʒee irsɬun kʔural antsʼil butʼabi ɡʼizrailaz nuʒeqχe rosun ratʃʼarab meχalda nuʒetsa dije batʼa ɡʔabun kʔjeze kːola ɡʔjezulɡi antsʼil butʼa antsʼil butʼajaɬul antsʼil butʼa
ɡʔjeb nuʒer sadaqʼa rikʼkʼine buɡo tsoɡidal ɡʼadamaz ratʃʼaral sadaqʼabazda baʃːadabɬun ɡʔotsʼisa tʼorʃːelalda jaɡi tʃanaɬusa bosarab tsʼijab baqχarab tʃaʁiralda baʃːadabɬun
nuʒetsa betʼjerhanase ɡʔjedinal antsʼil butʼabi kʔje ɡʼizrailaz ratʃʼaral kinalɡo antsʼil butʼabazdasa ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasul butʼa kːola kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunije kʔjeze kːola ɡʔjeb
nuʒee batʃʼarab butʼajaldasa biʃːunɡo ɬikʼab wa biʃːunɡo χirijab tʼasa biʃːun betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo χirijab sadaqʼaɬun kʔje
ɡʔjedinɡo lewijilazda abe nuʒetsa antsʼil butʼabazdasa biʃːunɡo ɬikʼab butʼa allaɡʔase kʔurab meχalda χutʼarab nuʒer kːola nuʒerɡo ɡʔotsʼisa ʃːwarab buɡʼa roɬ jaɬuni nuʒerɡo tʃanalda ʒanib tsʼtsʼurab tsʼijab tʃaʁir kiniɡin
nuʒetsaɡi nuʒer ruqʼaɬul aɡʔlujaɬɡi ɡʔjeb bokʔarab bakʼalda kwanaze beɡʔula ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb buɡo dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub nuʒetsa ɡʔaburab qχuluqχaɬuqχ nuʒee χʼalalab muχʔ
ɡʔjeb kwananilan nuʒeda ɡʼajib bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjeldasa batʼaɡi ɡʔabun biʃːunɡo ɬikʼab butʼa nuʒetsa allaɡʔase kʔun buɡeɬul kʼotʃonɡe ɡʔjeb ɡʼizrailazul χirijab sadaqʼa bukʼin nuʒɡo χwetʃʼoɡo rukʼine

betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
ɡʔale ditsa betʼjerhanas nuʒee tʃʼjezabuleb qʼanun ɡʼizrailazda abe kidaniɡi rukʔaldaɡi batʃʼjeb wa kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬiɡi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb baɡʼarab ɡʼatʃʼar duqχe batʃejan abun
ɡʔjeb kʔje kaʃiʃ eleazariqχe χadub bitʃːante ɡʔjeb batʃine χalqʼaɬ qʼaji tʃʼwarab bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼibeχun wa kaʃiʃasda tsebe qχweze
kaʃiʃ eleazaritsa ɡʼatʃʼral biduɬ ʒindirɡo kiliʃːɡi tʃːun ɡʔjeb bi ankʔtsʼul punqχizabe dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraldeχun
ɡʔjeb ɡʼatʃʼar buχʼize kːola ɡʔjesdaɡi biχʔun ɡʼatʃʼaraɬul tʼomɡi ɡʔanɡi biɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo tsadaqχ ɡʔjeɬul qχubɬiɡun buχʼize kːola
tsinɡi kaʃiʃas bosila kedraɬul qχwalχʔjenɡi isːopaɬul kwatsʼiɡi wa baɡʼarab kwasɡi wa ɡʔjeb kinabɡo reχila ɡʼatʃʼar buχʼuleb tsʼaduɬe
ɡʔjeldasa χadub kaʃiʃas ʒindirɡo retʼjelɡi tʃurila tʃerχaldasa ɬimɡi baqχila wa ɡʔjenisa tʼadwusːina ɡʔjew markʼatʃʼumeχ ʃːwezeɡʼan qχubawɬun wukʼina
ɡʼatʃʼar buχʼaraw tʃijasɡi tʃurila ʒindirɡo retʼjel wa tʃerχaldasa ɬimɡi baqχila ɡʔjewɡi qχubawɬun wukʼina markʼatʃʼumeχ ʃːwezeɡʼan
watsʼtsʼadɡo wuɡew tʃijas bakʼarila ɡʼatʃʼaraɬul roqχo wa ɡʔjeb ɬela qʼwatʼibeχun batsʼtsʼadab bakʼalda ɡʔjeb roqχo tsʼunize kːola ɡʼizrailaɬul χalqʼaɬe ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬim χʼadurijaɬe ɡʔjeb buɡo ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul qʼurban
ɡʼatʃʼaraɬul roqχo bakʼararaw tʃijasɡi tʃurize kːola ʒindirɡo retʼjel ɡʔjewɡi qχubawɬun wukʼuna markʼatʃʼumeχ ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʼizrailazeɡi ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel tʃijar rakʔaɬul ɡʼadamazeɡi ɡʔjebɡo nizam bukʼine buɡo daimabɬun
insanasul ʒanazajalda qχwaraw ʃːiwaw tʃi ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ qχubawɬun rikʼkʼuna
ɡʔjesde ɡʔjeb ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬim punqχize kːola ɬababileb wa ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ tsinɡi ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼaɬula amma ɡʔjesde ɬababilebɡi ankʔabilebɡi qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeb ɬim punqχitʃʼoni ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼaɬularo
insanasul ʒanazajalda qχwaraw wa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul nizam ɡʔabitʃʼjew tʃijas dir tʃadir qχubɬizabula ɡʔjedinaw tʃi ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔow teze beɡʔularo naqχe watʃaqχize kːola ɡʔjesde ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬim punqχizabitʃʼoni ɡʔjew qχubaw kːola ɡʔjesul qχubɬi ɡʔjesda tʼadɡo χutʼula
ɡʔale tʃadiralda ʒaniw tʃi χwani bukʼuneb qʼanun ʒanaza buɡeb tʃadiralda ʒaniwe ɬuɡʔaraw wa ɡʔjelda ʒaniw wuɡewɡi bokʔaraw tʃi qχubawɬun rikʼkʼuna ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ
wa ɡʔjeb tʃadiralda ʒanib buɡeb tʼad tʼaɬel ɡʔjetʃʼjeb bokʔarab tsʼaraɡʼɡi qχubɬula
awlaqχalda tʃʼwaraw jaɡi allaɡʔasul qʼadar ʃːun χwaraw tʃijasul ʒanazajalda jaɡi insanasul rakʔajalda jaɡi χobalda kwer qχwaraw bokʔaraw tʃi qχubawɬun wukʼuna ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ
ɡʔjedinaw tʃi watsʼtsʼadawɬun ɡʔawize qχabinibe baj ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe buχʼarab ʒojaɬul roqχo wa tʼade tʼje tʃwaχuleb bakʼaldasa bosarab batsʼtsʼadab ɬim
bitʃːante watsʼtsʼadɡo wuɡew tʃijas isːopaɬul kwatsʼi bosize wa ɡʔjebɡi ɬadaɬ tʃːun ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬim punqχize tʃadiralde ɡʔjenib buɡeb qʼajijalde wa ɡʼadamazde ɡʔjedinɡo insanasul rakʔajalda χobalda tʃʼwarasul jaɡi qʼadar ʃːun χwarasul ʒanazajalda qχwaraw tʃijasde
watsʼtsʼadɡo wuɡew tʃijas qχubɬaraw tʃijasde ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬim punqχizabe ɬababileb qʼojaɬ wa naqχeɡi ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ watsʼtsʼaɬaras tʃurila ʒindirɡo retʼjel wa tʃerχaldasa ɬim baqχila markʼatʃʼumeχalde ɡʔjew watsʼtsʼaɬila
amma pulanaw tʃi qχubɬani wa ɡʔjes ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul nizam ɡʔabitʃʼoni ɡʔjew χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa watʃaqχize kːola ɡʔjes betʼjerhanasul tʃadir qχubɬizaburaɬuqχ ɡʔjesde ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬim punqχitʃʼjeɬul ɡʔjew qχubawɬun χutʼula
ɡʔab nizam bukʼina nuʒee daimabɬun ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬim tsoɡidasde punqχizaburaw tʃijasɡi tʃurize kːola ʒindirɡo retʼjel ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬeda qχwaraw ʃːiwaw tʃi markʼatʃʼumeχ ʃːwezeɡʼan qχubawɬun wukʼuna
qχubaw tʃijas kwer qχwarabʃːinab ʒoɡi qχubɬula wa ɡʔjesda qχwarawɡi markʼatʃʼumeχ ʃːwezeɡʼan qχubɬun wukʼuna

tʼotsebeseb motsʼalda
χalqʼaɬe ɡʼurab ɬim bukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjenib ɡʔjeb sababɬun musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi dande tʃʼana ɡʼadamal
ɡʔjez bajbiχʔana musada kʼalal ɡʔiqʼize
niʒɡi ʃːaj χwetʃʼjel betʼjerhanasda tsere niʒer watsal χwarab qʼojaɬ
ʃːaj nuʒetsa ɡʔab salul awlaqχalde batʃarab betʼjerhanasul χalqʼ niʒɡi niʒer botsʼiɡi ɡʔanir χweze rukʼinejiʃː
ʃːaj nuʒetsa niʒ misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃaral wa ɡʔab barakat baqχarab ʃːibɡo biʒulareb bakʼalde ʃːwezarural ɡʔanib ja inʒir ja tsʼibil ja sono ɡʔjetʃʼo qʼetʃ χʔjezabize ɬimɡitsin ɡʔjetʃʼo
musaɡi ɡʔarunɡi bakʼararab χalqʼɡi ʒibɡo tun tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje riɬːana wa ɡʔjenir allaɡʔasda tsere nakabazde kːana wa ɡʔjebsaɡʼataldaɡo ɡʔjezije betʼjerhanasul qʼudrat zaɡʔirɬana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔjeb ɡʼansaɡi bose durɡo wats ɡʔarunida tsadaqχ ʒamaɡʼataɬul dandeɬi aχʼje χadub ɡʔjel kinazdaɡo tsebe buɡeb dob kʔurujalde amru ɡʔabe ɬim kʔjejan ɡʔjedin dutsa kʔuruɬan ɬim batʃʼinabila wa χalqʼɡi botsʼiɡi ɡʔjeqʼezabila jan
betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon musatsa ɡʔjesda tsebe bukʼarab ɡʼansa bosana
ɡʔarunɡun tsadaqχ kʔurujalda tsebe χalqʼɡi bakʼarun musatsa abuna
ɡʼjenekːeja pitnatʃaɡʼi ɡʔab kʔuruɬa baqχuniʃː niʒetsa nuʒee ɬim kʔjeze kːoleb in
tsinɡi musatsa ʒindirɡo ɡʼansa kʔurujalda kʼitsʼul kʔabuna tʃwaχun batʃʼana kʔuruɬa ɬim wa kinabɡo χalqʼaɬɡi botsʼutsaɡi ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan ɡʔjeqʼana
amma betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
nuʒ dida boʒitʃʼjeɬul wa nuʒetsa ɡʼizrailazda tsebe dir tʼadeɡʼanab batsʼtsʼaɬiɡi biχʔizabitʃʼjeɬul nuʒetsa batʃine ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔanʒe ɡʔab χalqʼ ditsa ɡʔjezije kʔjelin aburab rakʔalde
wa ɡʔjeb itsːalda tsʼar ɬuna meriwajaɬul
kadeʃaldasa edomaɬul patʃajasuqχe tʃaparzabi ritʼana musatsa ɡʔadinab χabarɡun
niʒ ruɡo dur watsal ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ duda ɬala niʒetsa χʼjeχʔjeze kːaral kinalɡo zaχʼmaɬabi
niʒer umumul ɡotʃana misrijalde wa ɡʼjemeral sonaz ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabuna niʒetsa misrijaz zulmu ɡʔabuleb bukʼana niʒeeɡi niʒer umumuzeɡi
amma niʒ betʼjerhanasde ɡʔardedal ɡʔjesda niʒer ɡʔari raɡʼana wa niʒeqχe witʼana misrijaldasa niʒ naqχe ratʃaraw malaik
ɡʔanʒe niʒ ʃːun ruɡo kadeʃalde dur rakʔaɬul raɡʼalda buɡeb ʃaɡʔaralde
ɡʔarula iznu kʔje niʒee dur ulkajaɬul rakʔaldasan buɡeb nuχkːun ine dur χurzabaqχanɡi tsʼolbol aχakʔanɡi inaro niʒ wa dur ʁujazuqχa ɬimɡi ɡʔjeqʼelaro niʒ ina χanzabazul nuχkːun ja kwaranab ja kweɡʼab raqχaldeχun kʔuritʃʼoɡo dur rakʔal naqχa tezeɡʼan
amma edomitsa ʒawab kʔuna
nuʒ dir rakʔaldasan inaro ine χʼalbiχʔani niʒ nuʒeda dande χwaltʃabiɡun raqχina jan
ɡʼizrailaz abuna
niʒ aslijab ʃaɡʔrakːun ina wa naɡaɡʔ niʒetsa jaɡi niʒer botsʼutsa nuʒer ʁujazuqχa ɬim ɡʔjeqʼani niʒetsa ɡʔjeɬuqχ muχʔ kʔjela niʒee bokʔun buɡo ɡʼitsʼɡo dur ulkajaɬul nuχkːun ine tʼokʼaɬ ʃːibniɡi qʼwariɡʼun ɡʔjetʃʼo jan
ɡʔjez ʒawab kʔuna
nuʒ ine ɡʔjetʃʼo niʒer rakʔaldasan in
tsinɡi kʼudijab qʼuwatab askarɡun ɡʔjezda dande waqχana edom
edomitsa ritʃːatʃʼo ɡʔjel ʒindirɡo rakʔaldasan ine wa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ ɡʔjenisa batʼijab raqχaldeχun swerana
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ kadeʃaldasa qʼwatʼibe baqχana ɡʔor aburab maɡʼardeχun balaɡʔun
edomaɬul ɡʼorqχoda buɡeb ɡʔor maɡʼarde ʃːwedal betʼjerhanas musadaɡi ɡʔarunidaɡi abuna
ɡʔarunije zaman ʃːwana abadijab roqʼowe ine wa ʒindirɡo umumulɡun tsoɬize ɡʔjew ɬuɡʔine ɡʔjetʃʼo ditsa ɡʼizrailaze kʔjelin χʼukmu ɡʔaburab rakʔalde ʃːajɡureɬul meriwa itsːuqχ ditsa ɡʔaburab amru nuʒetsa kʼijazɡo batsʼtsʼadɡo tʼubazabitʃʼo
ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjesul was eleazarɡi ɡʔor maɡʼarde aχʼje
ɡʔjenib ɡʔarunidasa kaʃiʃɬijaɬul retʼjelɡi baqχun ɡʔjeb ɡʔjesul was eleazarida retʼje ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeniw ɡʔarun χweze wuɡo wa ʒindirɡo umumulɡun tsoɬize wuɡo
musatsa betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabuna tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼatalda tsere ɡʔjel ɡʔor maɡʼarde raχana
ɡʔjenib musatsa ɡʔarunida tʼasa kaʃiʃɬijaɬul retʼjel baqχana wa ɡʔjeb retʼana ɡʔjesul was eleazarida wa ɡʔjeniw meɡʼjeraɬul tʼoɡʔiw χwana ɡʔarun musaɡi eleazarɡi maɡʼardasa ʁorkʔje ratʃʼindal
tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼatalda bitʃʼtʃʼana ɡʔarun χwarawɬi wa kinalɡo ɡʼizrailaz ɬeberɡo qʼojaɬ maɡʼu tʼuna ɡʔjesda χadub

χanaanaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda buɡeb arada ʃaɡʔaraɬul χanasda atarimaɬul nuχdasan ɡʼizrailal unel ruɡin raɡʼarab meχaɬ ɡʔjew ɡʔjezda tʼade kʼantsʼana wa ɡʔjezul tso tsojal asirɬude ratʃana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʼizrailaz kumek ɡʔarun betʼjerhanasde duɡʼa ɡʔabuna ɡʔadinab ɡʔaɡi ban
dutsa niʒee dob χalqʼalda tʼad berɡʔjenɬi kʔuni niʒetsa dozul ʃaɡʔaral duje χerem ɡʔarila
betʼjerhanas ɡʼizrailazul ɡʔa qʼabul ɡʔabuna χanaanijal ɡʔjezul kwerʃːalikʔje kʔuna ɡʔjezɡi χʼur ɡʔabuna ɡʔjezulɡi ɡʔjezul ʃaɡʔarazulɡi ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjeb bakʼalda χorma
ɡʔor aburab maɡʼardasa ɡʔjel saparaɬ raqχana baɡʼarab raɬdaqχe uneb nuχkːun edomaɬul rakʔalda χʼjetʼje tʃʼolareduqχ amma nuχda χalqʼaɬul jaχʼ χwana
ɡʼadamal naqχeɡi betʼjerhanasdaɡi musadaɡi dande razi ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo qʼulqʼudize ɬuɡʔana
ʃːaj nuʒetsa misrijaldasa niʒ naqχe ratʃaral ja kwen ɡureb ja ɬim ɡureb ɡʔab salul awlaqχalda χwezeɬuniʃː ɡʔab tʃʼamutʃʼab kwenɡi badisan bakːun buɡo niʒeda
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanas ɡʔjezda tʼade zaɡʔrujal borχʔal ritʃːana wa ɡʔjez χʼantʃʼun ɡʼizrailazul ɡʼjemeraw tʃi χwana
tsinɡi χalqʼ musaqχe batʃʼana wa ɡʔjez abuna
niʒetsa munɡi betʼjerhanɡi kakun niʒ munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːana ɡʔare betʼjerhanasda niʒedasa borχʔal tʼasa rosejan
musatsa χalqʼaɬe ɡʼolo betʼjerhanasda ɡʔarana
wa betʼjerhanas musada abuna
borχʔil sipat ɡʔabe wa ɡʼjeraldaɡi ban ɡʔjeb eχede borχizabe borχʔitsa χʼantʃʼarawʃːinaw tʃi ɡʔjeɬuqχ walaɡʔila wa tʃʼaɡo χutʼila jan
musatsa paχʔul boroχʔ ɡʔabuna wa ɡʼjeraldaɡi ban ɡʔjeb eχede borχinabuna borχʔitsa ɬidaniɡi χʼantʃʼani ɡʔjew tʃi paχʔul borχʔiqχ walaɡʔulaan wa tʃʼaɡo χutʼulaan
ɡʔjenisanɡi tsere un ɡʼizrailaz owot aburab bakʼalda tʃʼjel ɡʔabuna
owotaldasaɡi raqχun ɡʔjel ʃːwana ijje awarimalde wa ɡʔjenir ɬalqχana moɡʼawaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχaɬul ɡʼorqχoda askʼob buɡeb salul awlaqχalda
ɡʔjenisaɡi un ɡʔjel ʃːwana zaredalde wa ɡʔjenir ɬalqχana
ɡʔjenisa nuχde raqχaral ɡʔjel ʃːwana arnon ɡʼurul dob tsojab raɡʼalda buɡeb amorijazul ɡʼorqχode ɡʼuntʼuleb salul awlaqχalde arnon kːola moɡʼawaldaɡi amorijazul rakʔaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob buɡeb ɡʼorqχi
ɡʔjele ɡʔjedinɬidalin betʼjerhanasul raʁazul tʼjeχʔalda bitsuneb buɡeb
sufajalda waχewɡi arnonaɬul ɬaramuqχalɡi
ar aburab bakʼalde ʃːwezeɡʼan ruɡel kʼkʼalazul ʁuldulɡi
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼorqχoda buɡo
ɡʔjenisanɡi ɡʔjel riɬːana beeraɬuqχe aj ʁujaɬuqχe
χalqʼ bakʼare ditsa kʔjela ɡʔjezije ɬim an
dob meχalda ɡʼizrailaz ɡʔab ketʃʼ aχʼana
ʁuj ɬetsa tsʼje abe
aχʼje ɡʔjeɬij ketʃʼ
χalqʼaɬul kʼudijaz ʒib buqχarab ɡʔjezul
qʼadru kʼodoɬijaɬul ɡʼalamatɬun kːolel ɡʼunsbuzdaɬun buqχarab
salul awlaqχaldasa ɡʔjel ana mattanalde
mattanaldasa naχalielalde naχalielaldasa bamotalde
wa bamotaldasa moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalde salul awlaqχalda tʼade balaɡʔarab fasɡa aburab meɡʼjeraɬul tʼoɡʔire uneb bakʼalde
ɡʼizrailaz wakilzabi ritʼana amorijazul patʃa siχoniqχe ɡʔadinab χabarɡun
iznu kʔje niʒee dur ulkajaɬul rakʔaldasan buɡeb nuχkːun ine ja χurzabaqχe ja tsʼolbol aχikʔje niʒ qʼalaro ɡʔjeqʼelaro dur ʁujazuqχa ɬimɡi niʒ χanzabazul nuχdasan ina dur ulkajaɬul rakʔal naqχa tezeɡʼan
amma siχonitsa ɡʼizrailaze iznu kʔjetʃʼo ʒindirɡo ulka qʼotʼun ine ɡʔjes tʼolabɡo ʒindirɡo askar bakʼarana wa askarɡun ɡʼizrailazda dande salul awlaqχalde waqχana wa jaχatsalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ ɡʔjes ɡʼizrailazda dande raʁ ɡʔabuna
amma ɡʼizrailaz ɡʔjesul bo ʃːuʃːaqχ biχːizabuna wa arnonaldasa jabbokalde ammonijazul ɡʼorqχode ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjesul rakʔalɡi raqχana ammonijazul ɡʼorqχabi ɬikʼ ʃːula ɡʔarun rukʼana
amorijazul kinalɡo ʃaɡʔaral kwerde rosana ɡʼizrailaz χeʃbonɡi ɡʔjelda sweruqχ ruɡel rosabiɡi rikʼkʼun wa ʒalɡoɡi ɡʔjenir ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼana
χeʃbon bukʼana amorijazul patʃa siχonil ʃaɡʔar tsewekːun moɡʼawaɬul wukʼaraw patʃajasulɡun raʁɡi ɡʔabun arnonalde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjesul tʼolalɡo rakʔal siχonitsa raqχun rukʼana
ɡʔjedinɬidal qʼisabi ritsunel ɡʼadamaz abula
ratʃʼa χeʃbonalde tsʼidasan baj ɡʔjeb
ʃːula ɡʔabe siχonil ʃaɡʔar
χeʃbonaldasa tsʼa ɡʔjeleɡʔana
siχonil ʃaɡʔaraldasa tsʼadul matsʼal ratʃʼana
ɡʔjeɬ kʼkʼun ana moɡʼawaɬul ar ʃaɡʔar
wa arnonil borχaɬabazul betʼjerɡʔabi
balaɡʔ reʃːtʼana dude moɡʼaw
ɬuɡʼana mun kemoʃil χalqʼ
riʒarab rakʔɡi reχun tun ɬutana dur wasal
amorijazul patʃa siχonil asirɬude kːana dur jasal
niʒetsa tʃʼoral retʃʼtʃʼana
wa tʼaɡʼana χeʃbonaldasa baqχarab diwonalde ʃːwezeɡʼan kinabɡo
niʒetsa talawur ɡʔabuna
nofaχaldasa baqχarab medewalde ʃːwezeɡʼan kinabɡo ʃːibɡo ɡʔorkʔob tetʃʼoɡo
ɡʔjedin ɡʼizrailal tʃʼana amorijazul rakʔalda
χadub musatsa jazer ʃaɡʔaraɬul χal ʃal ɡʔabize tʃaɡʼi ritʼana wa ɡʔjebɡi ɡʔjelda sweruqχ rukʼaral rosabiɡi raqχana ɡʔjenir rukʼaral amorijalɡi naqχe ratʃaqχana
ɡʔjenisan ʃimalijab raqχaldeχunɡi swerun ɡʼizrailal ana baʃanalde uneb nuχdasan amma baʃanaɬul patʃa oɡ waqχana ɡʔjezda dande tʼolabɡo ʒindirɡo askarɡun wa edrei ʃaɡʔaralda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ ɡʔjezda dande raʁ ɡʔabuna
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
χʼinqʼuɡe ɡʔjesukʔa ditsa dur kwerʃːalikʔje kʔolew wuɡo ɡʔjewɡi ɡʔjesul tʼolabɡo askarɡi ɡʔjesul rakʔalɡi χeʃbonalda χanɬuda wukʼaraw amorijazul patʃa siχonije ɡʔaburab ɡʔabe dutsa ɡʔjesijeɡi
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʼizrailaz tʃʼwana ɡʔjewɡi ɡʔjesul wasalɡi ʁurana tʼolabɡo ɡʔjesul askarɡi tsoniɡi tʃi naqχe tetʃʼo ɡʔjesul tʼolalɡo rakʔalɡi ɡʼizrailazul kwerʃːalikʔje kːana

kwatʼitʃʼoɡo ɡʼizrailal naqχeɡi saparalde raqχana moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔaldeχun balaɡʔun wa jeriχon ʃaɡʔaralda dandbitʼarab iordan ɡʼurul raɡʼalda ɬalqχana
tsiporil was balakida raɡʼana ɡʼizrailaz amorijaze ɡʔaburabʃːinaɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ
kutakalda χʼinqʼana moɡʼawaɬul χalqʼ ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼaɬul kʼodoɬi biχʔun ɡʼizrailazukʔa χʼinqʼun soroduleb bukʼana tʼolabɡo moɡʼaw
moɡʼawijaz midjanaɬul kʼudijazda abuna
ɡʔab χalqʼaɬul rukːelaɬ niɬeda sweruqχ buɡebʃːinab kwanaleb buɡo maʁiɬ buʁitsa χer ɡʼadin
tsinɡi dob zamanalda moɡʼawaɬul patʃaɬun wukʼaraw tsiporil balakitsa
tʃaparzabi ritʼana beoril was bilɡʼamiqχe jefrat ɡʼuruqχ buɡeb petor ʃaɡʔaralde ɡʔadinab ruɡʔjelɡun
misrijaldasa batʃʼarab χalqʼaɬ tsʼjezabun buɡo rakʔaɬul ɡʔumerɡo wa ɡʔjeb χalqʼ reʃːtʼun buɡo dida askʼob
ɡʔarula duda watʃʼa naɡʼana reʃːtʼinabe ɡʔab χalqʼalde ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔabsaɡʼat ɡʔjel didasa ɡʼjemerɡo qʼuwatal ruɡo tsinɡi diqχa baʒarize beɡʔula ɡʔjel ʁurize wa dir rakʔaldasa naqχe ratʃaqχize dida ɬaleɬul dutsa barakataɬul duɡʼa ɡʔaburasde barakat reʃːtʼunebɬi wa dutsa naɡʼana kʔuraw balaɡʔaɬukʔje kːolewɬi
moɡʼawaɬulɡi midjanaɬulɡi kʼudijal ratʃʼana bilɡʼamiqχe ɡʔjesije kʔjeze ɡʼaratsɡi tsadaqχ bosun wa balakil murad ɡʔjesda bitsana
sordo ɡʔanib baj in abuna ɡʔjezda bilɡʼamitsa radal bitsina ditsa nuʒeda betʼjerhanasul ʒawab moɡʼawaɬul kʼudijal roɡʔineɡʼan ɡʔjesuqχ tʃʼana
allaɡʔ zaɡʔirɬana bilɡʼamije wa ɡʔjesda tsʼjeχana
ɡʔal duqχ ruɡel ɡʼadamal ʃːal in
bilɡʼamitsa allaɡʔase ʒawab kʔuna moɡʼawaɬul patʃa tsiporil balakitsa ritʼun ratʃʼun ruɡo ɡʔjel diqχe ɡʔadinab ruɡʔjelɡi bosun
misrijaldasa batʃʼarab χalqʼaɬ dunjal tsʼjezabun buɡo ɡʔarula watʃʼa naɡʼana kʔje ɡʔjeb χalqʼaɬe ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔabsaɡʼat ɡʔjel didasa ɡʼjemerɡo qʼuwatal ruɡo tsinɡi diqχa baʒarize beɡʔula ɡʔjel ʁurize wa dir rakʔaldasa naqχe ratʃaqχize jan
allaɡʔas bilɡʼamida abuna
unɡe ɡʔjelɡun kʔoɡe naɡʼana ɡʔjeb χalqʼaɬe ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb buɡo barakat ɬurab χalqʼ
χaduseb qʼojaɬ bilɡʼamitsa balakil wakilzabazda abuna
tʼadrusːa nuʒerɡo rakʔalde betʼjerhanas iznu kʔjetʃʼo dije nuʒɡun ine jan
moɡʼawaɬul tsereqχabi balakiqχe tʼadrusːana wa ɡʔjesda bitsana
bilɡʼamitsa inkar ɡʔabuna niʒɡun wiɬːine jan
balakitsa naqχeɡi wakilzabi ritʼana tserekːun ritʼarazdasaɡi tsʼikʼkʼun wa ɡʔjezdasaɡi qʼadrujal
ɡʔjel ratʃʼana bilɡʼamiqχe wa ɡʔjez abuna
tsiporil was balakitsa ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo inkar ɡʔabuɡe diqχe watʃʼine
kʼudijab χʼurmatɡun qʼabul ɡʔawila ditsa mun wa duje bokʔarabʃːinabɡi kʔjela watʃʼa ɡʔab χalqʼaɬe naɡʼana kʔjeze jan
amma bilɡʼamitsa balakil wakilzabaze ɡʔadinab ʒawab kʔuna
ɡʼartsulɡi mesedaɬulɡi tsʼurab ʒindirɡo kʼalɡʼa balakitsa dije kʔuniɡi dirɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrujalda reqʼon kːolareb ʃːibniɡi ʒo ɡʔabize kʼolaro dida ja kʼudijab ja ɡʔitʼinab
amma nuʒetsaɡi sordo baj ɡʔanib dun balaɡʔilin ʃːib betʼjerhanas abulebali
ɡʔjeb sordojaɬɡi allaɡʔ zaɡʔirɬana bilɡʼamije wa ɡʔjes abuna
mun aχʼize ɡʔjel ɡʼadamal ratʃʼun ruɡeɬul ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ a amma ɡʼitsʼɡo ditsa duda maɬarab ʒo ɡuroni ɡʔabuɡe
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ radal bilɡʼamitsa ʒindirɡo χʼama kʔolona wa moɡʼawaɬul tʃʼuχʼbi χʼakimzabiɡun tsadaqχ saparalde waqχana
wa ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ nuχda unew wukʼaɡo allaɡʔasul kweʃɡo tsːin baqχana bilɡʼamida wa betʼjerhanasul malaik eχetana ɡʔjesda tsewe nuχ bakʔuɬ bilɡʼam wukʼana χʼamida rekʼun ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ ɡʔjesul kʼiɡo tsewetelɡi wukʼana
χʼamida wiχʔana kodob ɬalinisa baqχarab χwaltʃenɡun nuχda tʃʼaraw betʼjerhanasul malaik ɡʔjedinɬidal nuχdasa ɡʔjeb χuribeχun swerana bilɡʼamitsa bajbiχʔana ɡʔjeb buχize wa nuχdeχun swerizabize
ɡʔjebmeχalda betʼjerhanasul malaik tʃʼana tsʼolbol kʼiɡo aχalda ɡʔorkʔob buɡeb qʼwaridab suqχmaqχnuχda nuχlul kʼijabɡo raqχalda qʼadalɡi rukʼana
betʼjerhanasul malaik wiχʔarab χʼama qʼadadeɡʼan qʼana wa bilɡʼamil χʼjetʼje qʼadada dande bazabuna ɡʔjesɡi tsʼidasan χʼama buχana
tsinɡi betʼjerhanasul malaik daɡʔawɡi tseweɡʼanɡi un kwaranide jaɡi kweɡʼide swerize res ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ʒeɡi qʼwaridab bakʼalda tʃʼana
betʼjerhanasul malaik wiχʔarab χʼama beɡana bilɡʼamida ʁorkʔ tsinɡi bilɡʼamil kweʃɡo tsːin baqχana wa ɡʔjes naqχeɡi tʼilitsa buχana χʼama
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanas χʼamije kʼaɬaze ɡʔunar kʔuna wa ɡʔjeɬ bilɡʼamida abuna
ʃːib kweʃɬi ditsa duje ɡʔaburab dutsa ɬabtsʼul dun buχize kːani jan
bilɡʼamitsa ʒawab kʔuna
dun ɡʼabdal ɡʔawize ɬuɡʔun buɡoɡuri mun diqχ kodob χwaltʃen bukʼarabani ɡʔabsaɡʼatɡo tʃʼwalaan ditsa mun
amma χʼamitsa bilɡʼamida abuna
ʒaqʼa qʼojalde ʃːwezeɡʼanɡi ɡʼumrujaɬɡo mun watʃːarab dur χʼama ɡuriʃː dun buɡeb bukʼaniʃː dir kidaniɡi ɡʔadinab ɡʼamal
bukʼintʃʼo jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjes
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas raɡʔizaruna bilɡʼamil beral wa ɡʔjesda wiχʔana ɬalinisa baqχarab χwaltʃenɡun nuχda tʃʼaraw betʼjerhanasul malaik bilɡʼam kʼalaʁorkʔje kːana wa ɡʼodob nodoɡi tsun nakabazda tʃʼana
betʼjerhanasul malaikas ɡʔjesda abuna
sunduqχ dutsa ɬabtsʼul tʼatʼala χʼama buχarab dun watʃʼun wuɡo duda dande mun tʃʼjezawize ʃːajɡureɬul dur saparaɬul muradaldasa razi ɡʔjetʃʼo dun
χʼamida dun wiχʔana wa ɬabɡo nuχaɬ ɡʔjeb didasa swerun ana ɡʔjeb sweritʃʼjebani ditsa mun tʃʼwaze wukʼana χʼama tʃʼaɡo teze bukʼana
bilɡʼamitsa betʼjerhanasul malaikasda abuna
dida ɡʼajib kːana dida ɬaleb bukʼintʃʼjeɬul mun dir nuχda tsewe tʃʼun wuɡewɬi amma ɡʔanʒe mun razi ɡʔjetʃʼjew watani dun tʼadwusːina
tsinɡi betʼjerhanasul malaikas bilɡʼamida abuna
mun ine beɡʔula ɡʔjel ɡʼadamazda tsadaqχ amma ɡʼitsʼɡo ditsa maɬarab ɡʔabe jan
wa bilɡʼam ana balakil tsereqχabazda tsadaqχ
bilɡʼam watʃʼunew wuɡin raɡʼidal balak watʃʼana ɡʔjesda dande arnon ɡʼuruqχ buɡeb moɡʼawijazul ʃaɡʔaralde ʒindirɡo ulkajaɬul ɡʼorqχode ʃːwezeɡʼan
balakitsa bilɡʼamida abuna
ditsa tsereɡo ɡuriʃː ritʼun rukʼaral duda χadur ɡʼadamal ɡʔab tsʼaqʼ kʼwar buɡeb iʃ buɡilanɡi abun ʃːajχa mun watʃʼunaroɡo wukʼaraw duje mustaχʼiqʼab adab χʼurmat ɡʔabun baʒarularew tʃijiʃː dun
ɡʔale watʃʼun wuɡoɡuri dun duqχe jan ʒawab kʔuna bilɡʼamitsa amma kʼolebdaj dida dijeɡo bokʔarab bitsine dir kʼaldib betʼjerhanas ɬurab raɡʼi ɡʔjele ɡʔjeb bitsina ditsa
tsinɡi balakida tsadaqχ kirjat χutsot ʃaɡʔaralde ana bilɡʼam
ɡʔjenib balakitsa qʼurbanaɬe botsʼiɡi ɡʼiɡi qχuna wa ɡʔanal butʼabi kʔuna bilɡʼamijeɡi ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ rukʼaral kʼudijazeɡi
χaduseb qʼojaɬ radal balakitsa bilɡʼam watʃana baɡʼalaɬul biʃːun borχatab bakʼalde wa ɡʔjenisan ɡʔjesda biχʔana ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ tʃʼarab bakʼ

bilɡʼamitsa balakida abuna
ɡʔanib ankʔɡo qʼurban bakʼ baj dije wa qʼurbanaɬe qχweze ankʔɡo otsɡi ankʔɡo kujɡi χʼadure jan
bilɡʼamitsa maɬuqχe ɡʔabuna balakitsa wa ɡʔjez kʼijazɡo tso tso otsɡi tso tso kujɡi buχʼana ʃːibab qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad
bilɡʼamitsa balakida abuna
mun ɡʔaniw dutsaɡo ruχʼaral qʼurbanazda askʼow tʃʼa dun doweɡʼan ina ʃːib ɬaleb betʼjerhan watʃʼine beɡʔula dunɡun dandtʃʼwaze ditsa duda bitsina dos dije zaɡʔir ɡʔaburab kinabɡo ʒo
wa ɡʔjew tso ɡʼitsʼab borχaɬijalde waχana
ɡʔjeniw allaɡʔ watʃʼana ɡʔjesda dande wa bilɡʼamitsa abuna
ditsa ankʔɡo qʼurban bakʼ bana wa ʃːibalda tʼad tso tso qʼurbanaɬul otsɡi kujɡi qʼurbanaɬe buχʼana jan
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas bilɡʼamida maɬana balakida abize kːoleb raɡʼi
balakiqχe tʼadwusːa wa ɡʔjedin abe dosda jan abuna ɡʔjes
ɡʔjew balakiqχe tʼadwusːana balak ʒintsaɡo ruχʼaral qʼurbanazda askʼow tʃʼun wukʼana wa ɡʔjesda askʼor moɡʼawaɬul kinalɡo tsereqχabiɡi rukʼana
tsinɡi bilɡʼamitsa abuna
sirijaldasa watʃana dun ɡʔaniwe balakitsa
moɡʼawaɬul patʃajas watʃana dun baqʼbakːul muɡʼruzdasa
watʃʼa dije ɡʼolo naɡʼana kʔje jaqʼubije
watʃʼa balaɡʔ batʃe ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalde janɡi abun
kin ditsa naɡʼana kʔjeleb allaɡʔas naɡʼana kʔolareb χalqʼaɬe
kin ditsa balaɡʔ batʃineb betʼjerhanas balaɡʔ batʃunareb χalqʼalde
dida biχʔula ɡʔjeb kʔurabazul borχaɬijaldasan
dun walaɡʔula ɡʔjeɬuqχ ɡoχʼal ʃːobazdasan
dida biχʔula χalqʼ kinazdasaɡo batʼa tʃʼun ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb
tsoɡidal χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔob ʒib χasabɬun kːoleb
ɬiqχa rikʼkʼun baʒaruleb raɬdal sali
ɡʔjediɡʼan ɡʼjemerab jaqʼubil naslu
ɬiqχa rikʼkʼun baʒaruleb ɡʼizrailaɬul unqʼil butʼatsin
bitʃːante allaɡʔasul aɡʔlujaɬul χwel dijeɡi nasibɬize
wa dir ɡʼumrudul aχirɡi ɡʔjezul ɡʼadinab bukʼine
balakitsa bilɡʼamida abuna
dutsa dije ɡʔabuleb ʃːib ditsa mun watʃana dir tuʃbabaze naɡʼana kʔjezejan abun dutsajin abuni ɡʔjezije barakatab duɡʼa ɡʔabuleb buɡo
ɡʔjes ʒawab kʔuna
betʼjerhanas dir matsʼalda ɬurab raɡʼi abize tʼadab ɡʔjetʃʼiʃː dida jan
tsinɡi balakitsa ɡʔjesda abuna
wiɬːa dida tsadaqχ tsoɡi bakʼalde ɡʔjenisan duda kinalɡo riχʔize ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjel tʃʼarab bakʼaɬul tso ɡʔitʼinabɡo raɡʼal ɡuroni ɡʔjele ɡʔjenisan kʔje ɡʔjezije naɡʼana tʼubazabe dir ɡʔari
balakitsa bilɡʼam watʃana fasɡa aburab meɡʼjeraɬul tʼoɡʔib buɡeb qχarawulzabazul rasaɬijalde ɡʔjenib bana ankʔɡo qʼurban bakʼ wa ʃːibalda tʼad tso tso qʼurbanaɬul otsɡi kujɡi buχʼana
bilɡʼamitsa balakida abuna
mun ɡʔaniw durɡo qʼurbanazda askʼow wukʼa dun dowɡun dandtʃʼwaze ina jan
betʼjerhan watʃʼana bilɡʼamida dande wa abize kːoleb ʒo ɡʔjesda maɬana
tʼadwusːa balakiqχe wa ɡʔadin abe dosda jan abuna ɡʔjes
ɡʔjew balakiqχe tʼadwusːana balak ʒintsaɡo ruχʼaral qʼurbanazda askʼow tʃʼun wukʼana wa ɡʔjesda askʼor moɡʼawaɬul tʼolɡo tsereqχabiɡi rukʼana
ʃːib aburab betʼjerhanas in tsʼjeχana balakitsa
tsinɡi bilɡʼamitsa abuna
tʼade waqχa balak ɡʼjenekːe diqχ ɡʼintʼame dutsa tsiporil was
allaɡʔ insan ɡuro ɡʔjersal ritsine
ɡʼadamaz ɡʼadin tsin bitsarab amru χisizabularo ɡʔjes
aburab ʒo ɡʔjes ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo tolebdaj
kʔurab raɡʼi ɡʔjes tʼubatʃʼoɡo χutʼulebdaj
diqχe amru batʃʼana ɡʔjezije barakatab duɡʼa ɡʔabejan
dosin barakat ɬoleb dun ɡʔjeb χisizabulew tʃi ɡuro
ɡʔjetʃʼo jaqʼubil χalqʼaɬe balaɡʔ
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬe qʼwariɬi ɡʔjetʃʼo biχʔuleb
ɡʔjelɡun wuɡo betʼjerhan ɡʔjezul allaɡʔ
ɡʔjez ʒiderɡo patʃaɬun ɬazawuraw
misrijaldasa ɡʔjel naqχe ratʃana allaɡʔas
ɡʼalχul buʁil ɡʼadab qʼuwat ɡutʃɡi ɡʔjezuɬ
jaqʼubil χalqʼalda dande χʼaltʼuleb χʼilla makru balaɡʔun baʒarularo
ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda dande χʼaltʼuleb siχʼruɡi
ɡʔanʒe jaqʼubilɡi ɡʼizrailaɬulɡi χʼaqʼaɬuɬ bitsine buɡo
balaɡʔjeja betʼjerhanasul χʼalkʼoɬi biχʔize janɡi abun
ebelab ʁalbatsʼ ɡʼadin qʼuwatab buɡo ɡʔjeb χalqʼ
biχʔinab ʁalbatsʼ ɡʼadin baʁula ɡʔjeb
ɡʔjeɬ χʼuχʔbaqχularo dawla kwanatʃʼoɡo
wa ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan tuʃmanasul bi ɡʔjeqʼetʃʼoɡo
ɡʔjebmeχalda balakitsa bilɡʼamida abuna
ja naɡʼana kʔoɡe ɡʔjezije ja barakat ɬoɡe ɡʔjezda jan
bilɡʼamitsa ʒawab kʔuna
ditsa duda abun bukʼintʃʼiʃː betʼjerhanas aburab ɡʔabize buɡo ditsajan
tsinɡi balakitsa bilɡʼamida abuna
wiɬːa ditsa mun batʼijab bakʼalde watʃina ʃːib ɬaleb betʼjerhanas duje iznu kʔjeze beɡʔula ɡʔjenisanɡʼaɡi dir muradɡi tʼuban ɡʔjezije naɡʼana kʔjeze jan
balakitsa bilɡʼam watʃana salul awlaqχalda tʼade balaɡʔarab peor maɡʼarde
ɡʔjenib naqχeɡi bilɡʼamitsa balakida abuna
ɡʔanib ankʔɡo qʼurban bakʼ baj dije wa qʼurbanaɬe qχweze ankʔɡo otsɡi ankʔɡo kujɡi χʼadure jan
balakitsa bilɡʼamitsa maɬuqχe ɡʔabuna wa ʃːibab qʼurban bakʼalda tso tso qʼurbanaɬul otsɡi kujɡi qʼurbanaɬe buχʼana

betʼjerhanasul amru ɬazabizejan abun bilɡʼam kiweniɡi intʃʼo ɡʔanʒesala ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjesda bitʃʼtʃʼun bukʼana betʼjerhanase ɡʼizrailazul χalqʼalda barakat ɬeze bokʔun bukʼin ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjew watʃʼinaqχeɡo salul awlaqχaldeχun walaɡʔana
wa ɡʔjesda biχʔana qʼawmalkːun tartibalda ɡʔjenib reʃːtʼarab ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ ɡʔjebmeχaɬ bilɡʼamide allaɡʔasul ruχʼ reʃːtʼana

χalqʼaɬul kinalɡo butʼrul rakʼare wa tʼolabɡo χalqʼalda biχʔun dida tsere tʃʼwaj ɡʔjel ɡʼizrailazda baqχarab dir ɡʔaldoleb tsːin swine bukʼine
tsinɡi musatsa χalqʼaɬul diwantʃaɡʼazda abuna

ɡʔjebmeχalda dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsereɡi rakʼarun ɡʼodulel rukʼaral ɡʼizrailazdaɡi musadaɡi tseesan pulanaw tʃijas ʒindirɡo roqʼoje ʒanije jatʃun ana midjanijaj
ɡʔjeb biχʔaraw kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunil eleazaril was pinχasitsa ʒamaɡʼataɬul dandeɬi tana wa χetʃɡi bosun
ɡʔjew tʃijasda χaduw ɡʔjesul tʃodroniwe wiɬːana ɡʔjes tso qʼazaburab χotʃotsa ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo tʃʼwana ɡʼizrailawɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanɡi ɡʔjebmeχaɬ qʼotʼana ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔob baʁarun bukʼarab kweʃab baχuneb unti
amma ɡʔjeb untijaɬ qʼolo unqʼazarɡo tʃi tʃʼwana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunil eleazaril was pinχasitsa swinabuna ɡʼizrailazde baqχun bukʼarab dir tsːidal ɡʔalaɡab tsʼa ɡʔjes χʼjeχʔjetʃʼo ditsaɡi χʼjeχʔolarel ɡʔjezul qʼabiχʼal iʃal ɡʔjedinɬidal ditsa tʼuran tʼaɡʼinaritʃʼoɡo tana ɡʼizrailal

ɡʔjesulɡun wa ɡʔjesul naslabiɡun ɡʔabuleb buɡo daimab kaʃiʃɬijaɬul qʼotʼi ʃːajɡureɬul ʒindirɡo allaɡʔase ɡʼolo pinχasitsa χʼjeχʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjezul inʒitɬi wa tʃurana ɡʼizrailazul munaɡʔ
midjanaɬul ɡʼadanɡun tsadaqχ tʃʼwaraw ɡʼizrailasda tsʼar bukʼana zimri salul was ɡʔjew wukʼana ʃimeonil qʼawmaɬul tso tuχumaɬul betʼjer
tʃʼwaraj ɡʼadanalda tsʼar bukʼana kozbi ɡʔjej jikʼana midjanaɬul tso kʔibilaɬul betʼjer tsuril jas

ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjez nuʒee ɡʔabuna tuʃmanase ɡʔabuleb ʒo ɡʔjez nuʒee peoraɬul qʼor ʁuna wa peor sababɬun kweʃab unti baʁararab meχalda tʃʼwaraj midjanijazul tseweqχanasul jas kozbil qʼorikʔje kːezaruna nuʒ
