keχatil wukʼana amram aburaw was
amramil tʃʼuʒujalda tsʼar bukʼana joχewed ɡʔjej jikʼana misrijalda ɡʔajuraj lewijil jas amramije joχeweditsa ɡʔaruna ɡʔarunɡi musaɡi ɡʔjezul jats marjamɡi
ɡʔarunije ɡʔaruna nadawɡi awiɡʔuɡi eleazarɡi itamarɡi
nadawɡi awiɡʔuɡi χwana betʼjerhanasda tsere beɡʔulareb tʃijarab tsʼaɡi bosun ratʃʼindal
lewijilazul motsʼ baraldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul kinawniɡi wukʼana   biχʔinaw ɡʔjezul tsʼaral qχwan rukʼintʃʼo tsoɡidal ɡʼizrailazul sijaχʼalda ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjezije kʔjeze kːolaroan rakʔaɬul butʼa
ɡʔjedinab bukʼana musatsaɡi kaʃiʃ eleazaritsaɡi moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalda iordan ɡʼurul raɡʼalda jeriχon ʃaɡʔaralda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ rukʼaɡo ɡʼizrailalɡi rikʼkʼun ɡʔaburab sijaχʼ
sinaj salul awlaqχalda rukʼaɡo musatsaɡi kaʃiʃ ɡʔarunitsaɡi ɡʔaburab tsebeseb sijaχʼalda reχsarazul tsoniɡi tʃi wukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔow
betʼjerhanas abun bukʼindal ɡʔjel kinalɡo salul awlaqχalda χweze ruɡin abun ɡʼitsʼɡo jefunnil was χalewɡi nunil was jeɡʔoʃuaɡi χutʼizeɡʼan

manasːil was maχir maχiril was ɡilɡʼad ɡilɡʼadil was χefer χeferil was tselofχad ɡʔjew tselofχadil jikʼana ʃːuɡo jas maχla noɡʼa χoɡla milka wa tirza jusupil was manasːil qʼawmaɬul tʃaɡʼi kːolaan ɡʔjel
ɡʔjel ratʃʼana dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼje musadaɡi kaʃiʃ eleazaridaɡi χalqʼaɬul kʼudijazdaɡi tʼolɡo ʒamaɡʼataldaɡi tsereɡi tʃʼun ɡʔjez abuna
awlaqχalda niɬ rukʼaɡo niʒer emen χwana ɡʔjew wukʼintʃʼo betʼjerhanasda dande waqχaraw qʼoraχʼil ɡʔalmaʁzabazda ɡʔorkʔow ɡʔjew χwana ʒindirɡo munaɡʔazuqχ [aj ɡʼadatijab χwelaldaɬun] wasalɡi naqχa tetʃʼoɡo
ʃːajχa niʒer insul tsʼar kʼotʃene teze kːoleb ɡʔjesul tuχumalda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔjesul wasal ɡʔjetʃʼinɡi abun kʔje niʒeeɡi niʒer insul watsaze kʔolebɡʼanaseb rakʔaɬul butʼa jan
musatsa ɡʔjezul sual betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɬuna
wa betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesda abuna
tselofχadil jasaz bitʼarab bitsuneb buɡo tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo kʔje ɡʔjezije ɡʔjezul insul watsazda baʃːadab rakʔaɬul butʼa wa ɡʔjeb kʔje ɡʔjezije irsaɬe ʃːwarab ɡʔjezul insul butʼa χʼisabalda
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abe naɡaɡʔ was ɡʔjetʃʼjew tʃi χwani ɡʔjesul rakʔaɬul butʼa jasaɬe kʔje
ɡʔjesul jasɡi jatitʃʼoni ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬul butʼa ɡʔjesul watsaze kʔje
ɡʔjesul watsal ratitʃʼoni ɡʔjeb ɡʔjesul insul watsaze kʔje
ɡʔjesul insulɡi watsal rukʼun ratitʃʼoni ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬul butʼa kʔje ɡʔjesul tuχumaɬul biʃːun tsewesew ɡʼaɡaraw tʃijase ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo ɡʼizrailaze tʃʼjezaburab daimab qʼanunɬun ɡʔjedinab amru ɡʔabuleb buɡo musadasan betʼjerhanas
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas musada abuna
awarim maɡʼarde waχa wa balaɡʔje ditsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬe kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔaɬuqχ
ɡʔjeb biχʔun χadub munɡi dur wats ɡʔarunɡo ɡʼadin kʼudijab saparalde durɡo umumuzuqχe ine wuɡo
ʃːajɡureɬul tsin awlaqχalda rukʼaɡo χalqʼ dida dande baqχindal nuʒetsa ditsa abuqχe ɡʔabitʃʼo wa dob itsːuqχ χalqʼalda tsebe dir tʼadeɡʼanab batsʼtsʼaɬi biχʔizabitʃʼo
ɡʔjeb kːana meriwajaɬul itsːuqχ tsin aburab salul awlaqχalda kadeʃalda
musatsa betʼjerhanasda abuna
ja betʼjerhan bitʃːante ʃːibab ʒojalda ruχʼ ɬolew allaɡʔas ɡʔab ʒamaɡʼatalda tʼad tʃi teze
ɡʔjezul betʼjerɬun wukʼineɡi χalqʼ tsebe batʃineɡi ɡʔjezije nuχmaɬi ɡʔabizeɡi baʒari buɡew weχʔ ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ɡʼijal reqχen ɡʼadin betʼjerhanasul χalqʼ χutʼunɡutʼize
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
aχʼje ɡʔjeb iʃaɬe reqʼarab ɡʼamal χasijat buɡew nunil jeɡʔoʃua wa ɡʔjesda tʼad kweral ɬe
kaʃiʃ eleazaridaɡi tʼolabɡo ʒamaɡʼataldaɡi tsewe tʃʼjezawe ɡʔjew wa kinazdaɡo ɬazabe ɡʔjew dur waris wukʼin
duqχ buɡeb iχtijaraɬul butʼa kʔje ɡʔjesuqχe ɡʼizrailal ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼjenekːize rukʼine
kaʃiʃ eleazaritsa urimaldaɬun betʼjerhanasul amru ɬazabila wa jeɡʔoʃua ɡʔjeɬuqχ ɡʼjenekːila jeɡʔoʃuaɡi tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailalɡi ɡʔjesul amrujaldaɬun saparalde raqχine ruɡo wa ɡʔjesul amrujaldaɬun tʼadrusːineɡi ruɡo
musatsa kinabɡo betʼjerhanas ʒinda maɬuqχe ɡʔabuna jeɡʔoʃua aχʼana wa kaʃiʃ eleazaridaɡi ʒamaɡʼataldaɡi tsewe tʃʼjezawuna
tsinɡi musatsa ɡʔjesda tʼad kweral ɬuna wa ɡʔjew ʒindir waris wukʼin ɬazabuna betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɬazabe qʼurbanazul tadbir muχʼkanɡo tʼubazabejan ʒindi ʒindir riɡʔalda dije qʼurbanalɡi roɬul χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi ɡʔarejan ɡʔjel ruɡo tsʼadudaɬun dije kʔolel wa ʒider maχʼ dije χirijal qʼurbanal
ɡʔjezda abe ɡʔale nuʒetsa betʼjerhanase qʼojil ɡʔabize kːoleb tsʼadul qʼurban kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ʒindiɬ ɡʔjetʃʼjeb kʼiɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjer ɡʔjedinab bukʼine buɡo qʼo ɡʔorkʔob bitʃːatʃʼoɡo ɡʔabuleb tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban
tsojab kʔjeɡʼjer roɡʔalil qʼurbanaɬe tsoɡidab baqʼanil qʼurbanaɬe qχwe
ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ bukʼine kːola roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi batsʼtsʼadab zajtunaɬul naχul ɡinaɬul
ɡʔjel kidaɡosel tʼuran ruχʼulel qʼurbanazul tadbir tʃʼjezabuna sinaj maɡʼardaɡo ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase rokʔulel maχʼal raqχinarijaɬe tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb tsʼadul qʼurban
ʃːibab kʔjeɡʼjeralda tsadaqχ bukʼine kːola ɡinaɬul unqʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa tʃaʁiraɬulɡi ɡʔjeb tʃaʁir tʼjeze kːola betʼjerhanasul muqʼadasab bakʼalde
kʼiabileb kʔjeɡʼjer qʼurban ɡʔabize kːola baqʼanida radal batʃʼaralda tsadaqχɡo ɡʼadin roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡun wa tʃaʁirɡun ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase rokʔulel maχʼal raqχinarijaɬe tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb tsʼadul qʼurban
ʃamatqʼojaɬ qʼurbanaɬe qχwe kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ʒindiɬ ɡʔjetʃʼjeb kʼiɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjer ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ bukʼine kːola roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi ʁorɬe zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʒubarab jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun kʼiɡo butʼa χanʒdal wa tsadaqχɡo tʃʼjezaburab qʼadaralda tʃaʁirɡi
kidaɡo ɡʔarize tʼadal ʃːibab qʼojaɬul aslijal qʼurbanalɡi ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ bukʼine kːoleb tʃaʁirɡi maɬitʃʼoɡo ɡʔjel ruɡo ʃːibab ʃamatqʼojaɬ ɡʔarulel tʼuran ruχʼulel qʼurbanal
ʃːibab motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanase tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχwe ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb kʼiɡo basiɡi tso kujɡi ankʔɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi
ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ bukʼine kːola zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʁorɬe ʒubarab roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi basijalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun ɬabɡo butʼa χanʒdal kujalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun kʼiɡo butʼa
wa ʃːibab kʔjeɡʼjeralda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase χirijal maχʼal raqχinarijaɬe tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb tsʼadul qʼurban
ʃːibab basijalda tsadaqχ batʃʼine kːola baʃːadab ɡin tsʼurab tʃaʁir kujalda tsadaqχ ɡinaɬul ɬabɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa wa kʔjeɡʼjeralda tsadaqχ ɡinaɬul unqʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa ɡʔjeb buɡo ʃːibab motsʼrol awalalda tʼobitʼuleb tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurban ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize kːola ɬaɡʼalil ʃːibab motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ
tʼubanɡo ruχʼulel qʼurbanazda tʼade munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe betʼjerhanasda tsebe tso deɡʼjenɡi qχweze kːola
tʼotsebeseb motsʼaɬul antsʼila unqʼabileb qʼojaɬ iχdalil awal betʼjerhanase pesaχaɬul qʼurbanal tʼoritʼje
antsʼila ʃːuabileb qʼo bajramqʼoɬun bukʼina ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ buɡʔurɡo tʃed kwanaj
ɡʔjeb ankʔil tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje wa kinabɡʼaɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe
betʼjerhanase tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb tsʼadul qʼurbanaɬe ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb kʼiɡo basiɡi tso kujɡi ankʔɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi qχwe
ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi bose ʃːibab basijalda tsadaqχ zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʒubarab jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun ɬabɡo butʼa χanʒdal kujalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun kʼiɡo butʼa
ʃːibab kʔjeɡʼjeralda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa
nuʒɡo munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬe munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe tso deɡʼjenɡi qχwe
ɡʔal qʼurbanal ɡʔarize kːola kidaɡo ɡʔarize tʼadal ʃːibab qʼojaɬul roɡʔalil qʼurbanazda tʼade
ɡʔjedinal qʼurbanal ɡʔare ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanase rokʔulel maχʼazdaɬun ɡʔjesije kʔoleb niɡʼmat χʼisabalda ɡʔjel qʼurbanal ɡʔare kidaɡo ɡʔarize tʼadal tsʼadul qʼurbanazda wa χirijal sadaqʼabazda tʼade
tsinɡi ankʔabileb qʼojaɬɡi dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje wa ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬɡi kinabɡʼaɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe
χʼaluqχen bakʼarize bajbiχʔijaɬul qʼojaɬ aj tsʼijab tʼorʃːalidasa roɬul χirijab sadaqʼa betʼjerhanase kʔoleb ankʔazul bajramqʼojaɬ dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje wa ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ ʃːibɡo χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe
betʼjerhanase bokʔuleb maχʼ baqχinabize tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχwe kʼiɡo basiɡi tso kujɡi ankʔɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi
ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ roɬul sadaqʼaɡi bose ʃːibab basijalda tsadaqχ zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʒubarab jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun ɬabɡo butʼa χanʒdal kujalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun kʼiɡo butʼa
ʃːibab kʔjeɡʼjeralda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa
nuʒɡo munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬe munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe tso deɡʼjenɡi qχwe
ɡʔal qʼurbanal ɡʔarize kːola qʼojil ɡʔarulel qʼurbanazdaɡi ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ ratʃʼunel tʃadilɡun tʃaʁiraɬul χirijal sadaqʼabazdaɡi tʼade nuʒetsa qʼurbanaɬe qχweze ratʃʼaral χʼajwanal rukʼine kːola kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjel

ankʔabileb motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχwe kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjel tʼasa riʃːun tso basiɡi tso kujɡi ankʔɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi betʼjerhanase bokʔuleb maχʼ baqχinabize
ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ batʃʼine kːola zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʁorɬe ʒubarab roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi ʃːibab basijalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun ɬabɡo butʼa χanʒdal kujalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun kʼiɡo butʼa
ʃːibab kʔjeɡʼjeralda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa χanʒdal
nuʒɡo munaɡʔazdasa ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬe munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe tso deɡʼjenɡi qχwe
ɡʔal qʼurbanal ɡʔarize kːola qʼojil ɡʔarulel qʼurbanazdaɡi tsʼijab motsʼ bakːijaɬul qʼurbanazdaɡi wa ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ ratʃʼunel tʃadilɡun tʃaʁiraɬul χirijal sadaqʼabazdaɡi tʼade ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase rokʔulel maχʼal raqχinarijaɬe tʼubanɡo buχʼuleb tsʼadul qʼurban
ankʔabileb motsʼaɬul antsʼabileb qʼojaɬ dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ allaɡʔase mutʼiɡʼɬun kʼal kːwe wa kinabɡʼaɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe
tʼuban buχʼuleb qʼurbanaɬe qχwe kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjel tʼasa riʃːun tso basiɡi tso kujɡi ankʔɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi betʼjerhanase bokʔuleb maχʼ baqχinabize
ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ bose zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʁorɬe ʒubarab roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi ʃːibab basijalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun ɬabɡo butʼa χanʒdal kujalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun kʼiɡo butʼa
ʃːibab kʔjeɡʼjeralda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa χanʒdal
ɡʔjedinɡo munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe tso deɡʼjenɡi qχwe ɡʔjeb ɡʔabe munaɡʔazdasa χwasarɬijaɬul qʼurbanazdaɡi ɡʔjedinɡo qʼojil ɡʔarulel qʼurbanazdaɡi wa ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ ratʃʼunel tʃadilɡun tʃaʁiraɬul χirijal sadaqʼabazdaɡi tʼade
ankʔabileb motsʼaɬul antsʼila ʃːuabileb qʼojaɬɡi dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje wa ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ kinabɡʼaɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhan kʼodo ɡʔawun bajram tʼobitʼje
tʼuban ruχʼulel qʼurbanaze betʼjerhanase bokʔuleb ɡʔuinab maχʼ baqχinabijaɬe qχwe antsʼila ɬabɡo basiɡi kʼiɡo kujɡi antsʼila unqʼɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ʒindiɬ ɡʔjetʃʼjel tʼasa riʃːun
ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ batʃʼine kːola zajtunaɬul naχɡi ʁorɬe ʒubarab roɬul χirijab sadaqʼaɡi antsʼila ɬababɡo basijaɬul ʃːibalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun ɬabɡo butʼa χanʒdal ʃːibab kujalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun kʼiɡo butʼa
antsʼila unqʼabɡo kʔaɡʼril ʃːibalda tsadaqχ jefajaɬul antsʼɡo butʼa ɡʔabun tso butʼa χanʒdal
ɡʔjedinɡo qʼojil ɡʔarulel qʼurbanazdaɡi ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ ratʃʼunel tʃadilɡun tʃaʁiraɬul χirijal sadaqʼabazdaɡi tʼade munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe tso deɡʼjenɡi qχwe
kʼiabileb qʼojaɬ qʼurbanaɬe qχwe kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ɡʔjetʃʼjel tʼasa riʃːun antsʼila kʼiɡo basiɡi kʼiɡo kujɡi antsʼila unqʼɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi
busbuzdaɡi kujduzdaɡi kʔaɡʼrazdaɡi tsadaqχ rukʼine kːolel roɬulɡun tʃaʁiraɬul χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi ɡʔare tʃʼjezaburab rotsenalda reqʼon
ɡʔjedinɡo qʼojil ɡʔarulel qʼurbanazdaɡi ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ ratʃʼunel tʃadilɡun tʃaʁiraɬul χirijal sadaqʼabazdaɡi tʼade munaɡʔ tʃurijaɬul qʼurbanaɬe tso deɡʼjenɡi qχwe
ɬababileb qʼojaɬ kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi ʒideɬ ɡʔjetʃʼjel tʼasa riʃːun antsʼila tso basiɡi kʼiɡo kujɡi antsʼila unqʼɡo ɬaɡʼarab kʔjeɡʼjerɡi

musatsa ɡʼizrailazda ritsana kinalɡo betʼjerhanasul tʼadqʼajal
musatsa ɡʼizrailazul qʼawmazul butʼruzda abuna
ɡʔadinab amru ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas
naɡaɡʔ insanas betʼjerhanase ʃːibniɡi ʒo nazru ɡʔabuni jaɡi naps qʼezabizeɬun ʃːibɡʼaɡi ɡʔabilin ɡʔjedani ɡʔjeb ɡʔa biχːizabize beɡʔularo wa ʒintsa ɡʔabize tʼade bosarab kinabɡo tʼubazabize kːola
naɡaɡʔ rosase intʃʼjej jasaɬ ʒeɡi insul roqʼoj jikʼaɡo betʼjerhanase sundulniɡi nazru ɡʔabuni jaɡi ɡʔjedun raɡʼi kʔuni
wa ɡʔjeɬul insuda ɡʔjeb nazru ɡʔabi raɡʼani amma ɡʔjes ɡʔjelda ʃːibɡo ʒo abitʃʼoni ɡʔjeɬ kʔurab raɡʼiɡi ɡʔaburab nazruɡi tʼubazabize kːola
amma jasaɬ ɡʔaburab nazruɡi ɡʔjedun kʔurab raɡʼiɡi raɡʼaraw insutsa ɡʔjeb ɡʔuqʼani ɡʔjeɬ nazruɡi kʔurab raɡʼiɡi tʼubazabize kːolaro betʼjerhan ɡʔjelda tʼasaɬuɡʔuna ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeɬije ɡʔjeb insutsa ɡʔuqʼun bukʼun
sundulniɡi nazruɡi ɡʔabun bukʼaɡo jaɡi urʁitʃʼoɡo kʼaldisa bortʃʼarab ɡʔjediɡi bukʼaɡo jas rosase ani
wa ɡʔjeɬul rosasda ɡʔjeɬ nazru ɡʔabiɡi ɡʔjedun raɡʼi kʔjejɡi ɬan χadub rosas ɡʔjelda ʃːibniɡi abitʃʼoni ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjeb kinabɡo tʼubazabize kːola
waamma ɡʔjeɬul nazru ɡʔjedi raɡʼidal rosas ɡʔjeɬije ɡʔuqʼani ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔjediɡi kʔurab raɡʼiɡi naqχ busːinabula betʼjerhanɡi ɡʔjeldasa tʼasaɬuɡʔuna
amma qʼorolaɬ jaɡi rosasdasa jatʼaɬaraj ɡʼadanaɬ ɡʔaburab nazruɡi ɡʔjedun kʔurab raɡʼiɡi ɡʔjelda tʼadabɬun χutʼula
naɡaɡʔ rosasda tsadaqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabulej ɡʼadanaɬ ʃːibniɡi nazru ɡʔabuni jaɡi ɡʔjedun raɡʼi kʔuni
amma ɡʔjebɡi ɬalew ɡʔjeɬul rosas ɡʔjelda ʃːibniɡi abitʃʼoni wa ɡʔjeb ɡʔuqʼitʃʼoni ɡʔjeɬ tʼubazabize kːola ʒindirɡo ʃːibab nazruɡi kʔurab raɡʼiɡi
waamma ɡʔjeɬul nazru jaɡi ɡʔjedi raɡʼaraw rosas ɡʔjeb naqχtʃʼwani ɡʔjeɬul kʼaldisa qʼwatʼibe batʃʼarab kinab bataniɡi nazruɡi ɡʔjediɡi ɡʔjelda tʼasa una rosas naqχtʃʼwana ɡʔjeb ɡʔjedinɬidal betʼjerhanɡi ɡʔjelda tʼasaɬuɡʔana
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ ɡʔaburab kinab buɡoniɡi nazruɡi ʒindirɡo naps qʼinabijaɬe pulanab iʃ ɡʔabilin ɡʔjeɬ kʔurab raɡʼiɡi ɡʔjeɬul rosas tasdiqʼ ɡʔabize jaɬuni naqχtʃʼwaze kːola
amma ɡʔjeb raɡʼun χadub rosas ʃːibɡo abitʃʼoni ɡʔjeldaɬun ɡʔjes tasdiqʼ ɡʔabula ɡʔjeɬul ʃːibab nazruɡi ɡʔjedarab ɡʔaɡi ɡʔjes ɡʔjel tasdiqʼ ɡʔaruna siχʼqʼotʼun tʃʼjejaldaɬun
amma ɡʔorkʔob zaman indal ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬul nazruɡi ɡʔjedun kʔurab raɡʼiɡi naqχtʃʼwani ɡʔjeɬul ɡʼajib ɡʔjesda tʼade kːeze buɡo
ɡʔjele rosasulɡi ɬadulɡi wa insulɡi ɡʔjesul roqʼoj jiɡej rosase intʃʼjej jasaɬulɡi ɡʔorkʔorɬabazul raqχaɬ betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔarural amrabi

musatsa ɡʼizrailazda abuna
raʁuqχabi tʃabqχad raqχine qʼatʃʼaj midjanijazda dande raʁ ɡʔabize wa betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjezdasa retsʼjel bosize
ɡʼizrailazul ʃːibab qʼawmaldasa aza azar raʁuqχan tʃabqχad waqχine kːola jan
tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔosa wiʃːana   raʁuqχan ʃːibab qʼawmaldasa aza azar tʃi
musatsa ɡʔjel raʁde ritʼana ʃːibab qʼawmaldasa aza azar raʁuqχan wa muqʼadasab ruqʼaɬul tsʼaraɡʼɡun pulaɡo ɡʼartsul suralɡun ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ witʼana kaʃiʃ eleazaril was pinχasɡi
midjanijazda dande raʁɡi ɡʔabun betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon ɡʼizrailaz ɡʔjezul kinalɡo biχʔinal tʃʼwana
ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ midjanaɬul ʃːujawɡo χanɡi tʃʼwana ewiɡi rekemɡi tsurɡi χʼurɡi rewaɡi ɡʔjedinɡo beoril was bilɡʼamɡi χwaltʃatsa tʃʼwana
ɡʼizrailaz midjanaɬul rutʃːabiɡi ɬimalɡi asirɬude ratʃana wa ɡʔjezul kinabɡo botsʼiɡi ɡʼijal reqχabiɡi tʼolabɡo mulkɡi ʒideeɡo dawlaɬun bosana
ɡʔjezul ʃaɡʔaralɡun rosabijan abuni tsʼaɡi ʁun ruχʼana
kinabɡo dawlaɡun aj ɡʼadamalɡi botsʼi riqʼziɡi tsadaqχɡi bosun
ɡʔjel tʼadrusːana jeriχon ʃaɡʔaralda dandbitʼarab iordan ɡʼurul raɡʼalda moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalda χalqʼ reʃːtʼarab bakʼalde wa asiralɡi tʼolabɡo dawlaɡi ʃːwezabuna musaqχeɡi kaʃiʃ eleazariqχeɡi ɡʼizrailazul ʒamaɡʼataɬuqχeɡi
musaɡi kaʃiʃ eleazarɡi χalqʼazul butʼrulɡi ɡʔjezda dande riɬːana
tsinɡi musal kutakalda tsːin baqχana raʁdasa rusːun ratʃʼunel raʁul tsereqχabazda azaril wa nusil butʼruzda
nuʒetsa rutʃːabi tʃʼaɡojiʃː taral in kʼalɡʔiqʼana musatsa ɡʔjezda
ɡʔjel rutʃːabaz ɡuriʃː bilɡʼamil maɬa qχwajalda naqχɡi riɬːun ɡʼizrailal betʼjerhanase χilipɬize tʼamural peoralda rukʼaɡo betʼjerhanasul χalqʼalda tʼade kweʃab untiɡi ɡʔjel sababɬun ɡuriʃː bitʃːarab
tʃʼwaj ɡʔabsaɡʼatalda kinalɡo biχʔinɬimalɡi biχʔinalɡun rukʼaral kinalɡo rutʃːabiɡi
biχʔintʃi qχwatʃʼjel jasal tʃʼaɡo te nuʒeeɡo
χadub nuʒ ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ qʼaji tʃʼwarab bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼireχun tʃʼa tʃi tʃʼwaraw jaɡi ʒanazajalda qχwaraw ʃːiwaw tʃijas nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔosa wukʼaniɡi asirazda ɡʔorkʔosa wukʼaniɡi ɬababilebɡi ankʔabilebɡi qʼojaɬ ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul nizam tʼobitʼize kːola
kinabɡo retʼjelɡi batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabize kːola qʼoχʔolɡi tsʼtsʼjel kwasulɡi tsʼulalɡi ɡʔaburab ʃːibab ʒo
kaʃiʃ eleazaritsa raʁda rukʼaral raʁuqχabazda abuna
ɡʔale betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujaldaɬun tʃʼjezaburab qʼanun
mesedɡi ɡʼaratsɡi mazɡarɡi maχːɡi ʁalajɡi tʼuχʔiɡi
tsʼajaɬ buχʼularebʃːinab kinabɡo ʒoɡi tsʼaduɬan bitʃːaze kːola tsinɡi ɡʔjeb batsʼtsʼadabɬun ɬuɡʔuna amma ɡʔjel ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬetsaɡi tʃurize kːola tsʼa rekʼunebʃːinab ʒojin abuni ɡʼitsʼɡo ratsʼtsʼaɬijaɬul ɬetsa tʃurize kːola
ankʔabileb qʼojalda nuʒerɡo partal tʃure wa ɡʔjebmeχalda nuʒ ratsʼtsʼaɬila ɡʔjeldasa χadub nuʒ χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔore ratʃʼine beɡʔula
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
kaʃiʃ eleazarɡun wa tuχumazul kʼudijalɡun tsadaqχ asiralɡi botsʼiɡi rikʼkʼje
wa raʁda rukʼaral raʁuqχabazdaɡi χutʼarab χalqʼaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔjeb kinabɡo dawlaɡi baʃːad bikʔje
tʃabqχad un rukʼarazul butʼajaldasa betʼjerhanase maʁalo bakʼare ʃːiwaw ʃːunusɡo asirasdasa tso tso tʃi ɡʼi botsʼul wa χʼamuzul ʃːibab ʃːunusɡo ʒojaldasaɡi tso tso betʼjer
ɡʔjeb butʼa baqχe raʁuqχabazul butʼajaldasa wa kaʃiʃ eleazarije kʔje betʼjerhanasul butʼa χʼisabalda
χutʼaral ɡʼizrailaze kːoleb butʼajaldasa baqχe kʼiqʼojalda antsʼ antsʼ asirasdasaɡi χʼajwanaldasaɡi χʼamidasaɡi ɡʼijaɬaʒojaldasaɡi tso tso betʼjer ɡʔjeb kinabɡo kʔje betʼjerhanasul muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul tʼalab aʁazalda rukʼunel lewitaze

raʁuqχabazul dawlajaldasa batʼa ɡʔabun musatsa χutʼaral ɡʼizrailaze kʔurab butʼa

wa   asir
ɡʼizrailazul butʼajaldasa musatsa bosana kʼiqʼojalda antsʼ antsʼ asirasdasa tso tso asir ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʼi botsʼudasaɡi wa ɡʔjel kinalɡo kʔuna betʼjerhanasul muqʼadasab tʃadiraɬul tʼalab aʁazalda rukʼunel lewitaze betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon
raʁuqχabazul butʼrulɡi azaril wa nusil butʼrulɡi ratʃʼana musaqχe
wa ɡʔjez abuna
niʒetsa dur laʁzaderitsa niʒer nuχmaɬijalda ʁorkʔ ruɡel raʁuqχabi rikʼkʼana wa ɡʔjezul tsoniɡijaw tʼasa kamun watitʃʼo
ɡʔale niʒetsa niʒer ɡʼumrujaɬuqχ χʼaqʼ χʼisabalda betʼjerhanase kʔoleb buɡo niʒer ʃːiwase dawlaɬun ʃːwarab mesed ʁuʒduzda ralel ruχʔabi kurχʔabi barʁitʃal kʼilkʼal wa ʒawɡʔarazul tsʼalal
musatsaɡi kaʃiʃ eleazaritsaɡi ɡʔjezuqχa ɡʔjel kinalɡo mesedil tʼaɡʼjelal qʼabul ɡʔaruna
raʁul tsereqχabaz batʃʼarab wa musatsaɡi eleazaritsaɡi betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo sadaqʼa ɡʔaburab mesedalda kinabniɡi bukʼana   ʃekel
raʁuqχabaze ʃːwarab χutʼarab dawla ɡʔjezije tana
musatsa wa kaʃiʃ eleazaritsa raʁul butʼruzuqχaɡi azaril wa nusil butʼruzuqχaɡi qʼabul ɡʔaburab mesed dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiraɬub betʼjerhanasda tsebe ɬuna ɡʼizrailal kidaɡo ɡʔjesda tsere rukʼinaɬul ɡʼalamat χʼisabalda

ruwimilɡi ɡadilɡi naslabazul bukʼana kutakalda ɡʼjemerab botsʼi ɡʔjezda biχʔana jazeraɬulɡi ɡilɡʼadaɬulɡi rakʔal botsʼi χʔiχʔize sanaɡʼatal ruɡebɬi
ɡʔjel ratʃʼana musaqχeɡi kaʃiʃ eleazariqχeɡi χalqʼazul kʼudijazuqχeɡi wa ɡʔjez abuna
niʒer dur laʁzaderil ɡʼjemerab botsʼi buɡo betʼjerhanas ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬe mutʼiɡʼ ɡʔarural rakʔalin abuni atarotɡi diwonɡi jazerɡi nimraɡi χeʃbonɡi elealeɡi newoɡi beonɡi botsʼi χʔiχʔize sanaɡʼatal rakʔal ruɡo
dur rakʼ reqʼani kʔje ɡʔjel rakʔal niʒee dur laʁzaderije ratʃunɡe niʒ iordan baχun doreχun
musatsa ɡadilɡi ruwimilɡi naslabazda abuna
nuʒer watsal raʁde arab meχalda nuʒ ɡʔaniriʃː tʃʼjeze ruɡel
ʃːaj nuʒetsa betʼjerhanas kʔural rakʔazde ine ɡʼizrailazul ʁira tʃʼwaleb
ɡʔjebɡo ɡʔabuna nuʒer umumuz kadeʃ barneajaldasa χanaanaɬul rakʔaɬul χal ʃal ɡʔabize ditsa ɡʔjel ritʼarab meχaldaɡi
eʃkolaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalde ʃːwezeɡʼan rakʔaɬul χalɡi ɡʔabun tʼadrusːindal ɡʔjez ɡʼizrailazul ʁira tʃʼwana betʼjerhanas ɡʔjezije kʔurab rakʔalde ine
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanasul tsːin baqχana wa ɡʔjew ɡʔjedana
misrijaldasa qʼwatʼiwe waqχaraw qʼoɡo sonaldasa tʼade arab riɡʔaɬul tsoniɡi tʃijasda biχʔize ɡʔjetʃʼo ibraɡʔimijeɡi isχʼaqʼijeɡi jaqʼubijeɡi kʔjeze buɡin abun dun ɡʔjedarab rakʔ ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjel rakʼ rakʼaɬ dida χadur riɬːintʃʼo
ɡʼitsʼɡo kenizijaw jefunnil was χalewɡi nunil was jeɡʔoʃuaɡi rakʼ rakʼaɬ dir amrujalda naqχ riɬːana jan
ɡʼizrailazda baqχarab tsːidatsa betʼjerhanas kʼiqʼoɡo sonaɬ awlaqχalda swerdize tʼamuna χalqʼ betʼjerhanasda riχaralʃːinal ʒal ɡʔarurab ɡʼjel tʼubanɡo tʼaɡʼineɡʼan
ɡʔanʒe nuʒetsaɡi nuʒer umumuzɡo ɡʔaburab ɡʔabuleb buɡo munaɡʔ χʼaqʼaɬul aɡʔlu nuʒee tsʼidasan ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalde betʼjerhanasul tsːin batʃine qʼwariɡʼuniʃː buɡeb
betʼjerhanase nuʒ mutʼiɡʼɬitʃʼoni ɡʔjes ɡʔab χalqʼ naqχeɡi teze buɡo salul awlaqχalda wa nuʒ sababɬun tʼolabɡo χalqʼɡi χweze buɡo
musada askʼoreɡʼanɡi ratʃʼun ɡʔjez abuna
niʒetsa ɡʔanir niʒer botsʼuje rutʃnalɡi qχizan ɬimalaze ʃaɡʔaralɡi rala
tsinɡi niʒ bortʃun jaraʁɡun ɡʼizrailazul tʼotseresel kʔjerazdaɡi tʃʼun ɡʔjel ɡʔjezul rakʔalde ʃːwezarize riɬːina ɡʔjeb zamanalda niʒer qχizan ɬimal swerun qʼaral ʃaɡʔarazda rukʼina ɡʔab rakʔaɬul ɡʼadamazdasaɡi tsʼuna qʼan
ɡʼizrailazul ʃːiwase ʒindirɡo rakʔaɬul butʼa ʃːwezeɡʼan niʒ roqʼore tʼadrusːinaro
iordan ɡʼurul dob raqχalda rakʔaɬul butʼaɡi bosilaro niʒetsa ʃːajɡureɬul niʒer butʼa ɡʔanib iordanaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda bukʼine buɡeɬul
musatsa ɡʔjezda abuna
nuʒetsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuni betʼjerhanase ɡʼolo raʁize jaraʁɡi bortʃani
jaraʁ bortʃaraw ʃːiwaw tʃi betʼjerhanasda tsewe iordan ɡʼor tun doweχunɡi wiɬːani tuʃbabazuqχa baqχarab
ɡʔjeb rakʔ betʼjerhanase mukʼurɬun χadub ɡuroni nuʒ roqʼoreɡi tʼadrusːintʃʼoni ɡʔjebmeχalda nuʒetsa betʼjerhanasda wa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda tsebe nuʒerɡo naɬi tʼubazabila tsinɡi ɡʔab rakʔ nuʒee betʼjerhanasuqχa ʃːwarab daimab mulkɬun bukʼina
amma nuʒetsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabitʃʼoni nuʒ betʼjerhanasda tsere munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːeze ruɡo ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nuʒeda ɬan bukʼa munaɡʔaɬuqχ bukʼuneb ʒazajaldasa rortʃʼize bakʼ nuʒee ɡʔjetʃʼo
raj nuʒerɡo qχizan ɬimalaze ʃaɡʔaralɡi botsʼuje rutʃnalɡi wa nuʒetsaɡo kʔurab raɡʼiɡi kːwe
ɡadilɡi ruwimilɡi naslabaz musada abuna
niʒ ruɡo dur laʁzal dutsa maɬuqχe ɡʔabila niʒetsa
niʒer qχizan ɬimalɡi ɡʼi botsʼul reqχabiɡi ɡʔanir tela ɡilɡʼadaɬul ʃaɡʔarazda
amma niʒ dur laʁzal aj raʁuje jaraʁ bortʃaral kinalɡo betʼjerhanasul amru tʼuban ɡʼurul dob tsojab raqχalda raʁize riɬːina dutsa maɬuqχe
ɡʔjebmeχalda musatsa kaʃiʃ eleazarideɡi nunil was jeɡʔoʃuadeɡi ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬul kʼudijazdeɡi
ɡʔadinab amru ɡʔabuna
ɡadilɡi ruwimilɡi qʼawmazul jaraʁ bortʃaralʃːinal biχʔinal betʼjerhanase mutʼiɡʼɡo nuʒeda tsadaqχ raʁize iordan baχun doreχun riɬːani ɡʔjeb rakʔ nuʒetsa kwerde bosun χadub ɡʔjezije mulkɬun kʔje ɡʔab ɡilɡʼadaɬul rakʔ
naɡaɡʔ ɡʔjel bortʃun jaraʁɡun nuʒeda tsadaqχ riɬːintʃʼoni ɡʔjezul rakʔaɬul butʼabi rukʼine ruɡo nuʒerazda askʼor χanaanalda
ɡadilɡi ruwimilɡi naslabaz ʒawab kʔuna
niʒ ruɡo dur laʁzal niʒetsa betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabila kinabɡo
niʒetsa bortʃun jaraʁɡun ɡʼor baχina wa betʼjerhanasda tsere χanaanalde riɬːina amma bitʃːante niʒer mulkɬun bukʼine iordanaɬul ɡʔab raqχalda buɡeb rakʔ
ɡʔjebmeχalda ɡadilɡi ruwimilɡi naslabazeɡi jusupil was manasːil baʃːdab qʼawmaɬeɡi musatsa kʔuna amorijazul siχon patʃajasul bukʼarab ulkaɡi baʃanaɬul oɡ patʃajasul bukʼarab ulkaɡi ɡʔjezul kinalɡo rakʔal tsadaqχ tʼolalɡo ʃaɡʔaralɡun wa ʃaɡʔarazul sweruqχɬabiɡun
ɡadil naslabaz tsʼidasan rana diwon atarot aroɡʼjer
aterot ʃofan jazer jaɡboɡʔa
bet nimra wa bet ɡʔaran abural swerun qʼaral ʃaɡʔaralɡi botsʼi ʁeze rutʃnalɡi
ruwimil naslabaz tsʼidasan rana χeʃbon eleale kirjatajim
newo wa baɡʼal meon ɡʔjez ɡʔjezul tsʼaral χisizaruna wa siwma abural ʃaɡʔaral tsʼidasan raral ʃaɡʔaraze ɡʔjez batʼijal tsʼaral kʔuna
manasːil was maχiril naslabaz ɡilɡʼadalde ɡʔuʒum ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjenir rukʼaral amorijalɡi naqχe qʼotʼun ɡʔjenir tʃʼana
musatsa ɡilɡʼad kʔuna manasːil was maχiril naslabaze wa ɡʔjel ɡʔjenir reʃːtʼana
manasːilɡo qʼawmaldasa jairitsa ɡʔjenir sweruqχɬijalda rukʼaral rosabi raqχana wa ɡʔjezda jairil rosabi aburab tsʼar ɬuna
nowaχitsa kenatɡi ɡʔjelda sweruqχ rukʼaral rosabiɡi raqχana wa ɡʔjezda ʒindirɡo tsʼar ɬuna nowaχ abun

ɡʔale musalɡi ɡʔarunilɡi nuχmaɬijalda ʁorkʔ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire raqχaral ɡʼizrailaz nuχda tʃʼjel ɡʔabural bakʼazul tsʼaral
betʼjerhanasul amrujaldaɬun qχwana ɡʔab musatsa saparalda rukʼaɡo ɡʔale ɡʔjezul saparazul nuχ ɡʔjez nuχda tʃʼjel ɡʔaburabʃːinab bakʼɡi χʼisabalde bosun qχwarab
ɡʼizrailal raamsesaldasa saparalde raqχana tʼotsebeseb motsʼaɬul antsʼila ʃːuabileb qʼojaɬ ɡʔjeb bukʼana pesaχalda naqχiseb qʼo ɡʔjel χʼinqʼitʃʼoɡo misrijazdaɡi riχʔulaɡo raqχana ɡʔjenisa qʼwatʼire
misrijalin abuni betʼjerhanas tʃʼwaral ɬimal χabaɬ ɬolel rukʼana ɡʔjedin betʼjerhanas ʒaza ɡʔabuna ɡʔjezul allaɡʔzabaze
raamsesɡi naqχa tun ɡʼizrailal ɬalqχana sukːotalda
sukːotaldasa qʼwatʼire raqχun χadur ɡʔjel ɬalqχana etamalda salul awlaqχaɬul raɡʼalda
etamɡi tun ɡʔjel swerana baɡʼal tsefonaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda buɡeb pi ɡʔaχirotaldeχun wa miɡdolalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ ɬalqχana
pi ɡʔaχirotɡi tun ɡʔjez raɬad baχana wa salul awlaqχalde ʃːwana ɬabɡo qʼojaɬ ana ɡʔjel etam aburab salul awlaqχaldasan wa marajalda reʃːtʼana
marajaldasa un ɡʔjel elimalde ʃːwana elimalda bukʼana antsʼila kʼiɡo itsːɡi ɬabqʼojalda antsʼɡo tʃamasdakil ʁwetʼɡi ɡʔjel ɡʔjenir reʃːtʼana
elimaldasaɡi raqχun ɡʔjel baɡʼarab raɬdal raɡʼalda reʃːtʼana
baɡʼarab raɬdaqχa ɡʔjel ana wa sin aburab salul awlaqχalda reʃːtʼana
sin aburab salul awlaqχaldasaɡi un ɡʔjel dofkajalda ɬalqχana
dofkajaldasaɡi un ɡʔjel aluʃalda reʃːtʼana
aluʃɡi naqχa tun ɡʔjel reʃːtʼana refidimalda ɡʔjenib χalqʼaɬe ɡʔjeqʼeze ɬim bukʼintʃʼo
refidimaldasa raqχun aral ɡʔjel reʃːtʼana sinaj aburab salul awlaqχalda
sinaj salul awlaqχaldasaɡi un ɡʔjel ɬalqχana kiwrot ɡʔataawajalda
kiwrot ɡʔataawajaldasaɡi ana wa χatserotalda ɬalqχana
χatserotaldasa aral ɡʔjel ritmajalda reʃːtʼana
ritmajaldasa un χadur ɡʔjel rimmon paretsalda reʃːtʼana
rimmon paretsaldasaɡi ana wa liwnajalda ɬalqχana
liwnajaldasa aral ɡʔjel risːajalda reʃːtʼana
risːajaldasa ana keɡʔjelatalde
keɡʔjelataldasaɡi un ɡʔjel ʃefer maɡʼarda askʼor ɬalqχana
ʃefer meɡʼjerɡi tun ɡʔjel ana χaradajalde
χaradajaldasaɡi ana makɡʔjelotalde
makɡʔjelotaldasaɡi un ɡʔjel taχatalda reʃːtʼana
taχatɡi naqχa tun ɡʔjel teraχalde ʃːwana
teraχaldasaɡi un ɡʔjel mitkajalde ʃːwana
mitkajaldasaɡi ɡʔjel ana χaʃmonajalde
χaʃmonaɡi naqχa tun ɡʔjel moserotalda reʃːtʼana
moserotaldasaɡi ɡʔjel ana bene jaakanalde
bene jaakanaldasaɡi ana ɡʔjel wa χor χaɡidɡadalda reʃːtʼana
χor χaɡidɡadaldasaɡi ɡʔjel ana jotbatajalde
jotbatajaldasa ɡʔjel awronajalde ana
awronajaldasaɡi un ɡʔjel jetsion ɡeweralda reʃːtʼana
jetsion ɡeweraldasaɡi ɡʔjel ana tsin aburab salul awlaqχalda buɡeb kadeʃalde
kadeʃaldasa un χadur ɡʔjel reʃːtʼana edomaɬul ɡʼorqχoda buɡeb ɡʔor meɡʼjeralda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ
betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon kaʃiʃ ɡʔarun waχana ɡʔor maɡʼarde wa ɡʔjeniw χwana ɡʔjeb bukʼana misrijaldasa ɡʼizrailal qʼwatʼire raqχaraldasa kʼiqʼoabileb son ʃːuabileb motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼo
ɡʔor maɡʼarda χwaraw ɡʔarunitsa ban bukʼana nusijalda qʼolo ɬabɡo son
ɡʔjeb zamanaldajin χanaanaɬul neɡew ʃaɡʔaralda χanɬuda wukʼaraw patʃa aradida raɡʼarab ɡʼizrailal ratʃʼunel ruɡebɬi
ɡʔor meɡʼjerɡi naqχa tun ɡʔjel reʃːtʼana tsalmonajalda
tsalmonajaldasaɡi raqχun ɡʔjel punonalda reʃːtʼana
punonaldasa un ɡʔjel owotalde ʃːwana
owotɡi naqχa tun ɡʔjel moɡʼawaɬul rakʔazde ʃːwana wa ijje ɡʔaawarimalda reʃːtʼana
ɡʔjenisaɡi un ɡʔjel diwon ɡadalda ɬalqχana
diwon ɡadaldasaɡi un ɡʔjel almon diwlatajimalde ʃːwana
almon diwlatajimaldasaɡi un ɡʔjel newojalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ ruɡel awarim muɡʼruzda askʼor reʃːtʼana
awarim muɡʼrulɡi naqχa tun ɡʔjel reʃːtʼana iordan ɡʼurul raɡʼalda jeriχon ʃaɡʔaralda dandbitʼun buɡeb moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalda
iordan ɡʼuruqχ moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalda bet jeʃimotaldasa baqχarab awel ʃittimalde ʃːwezeɡʼan qʼaji tʃʼwana ɡʔjez
moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalda jeriχon ʃaɡʔaralda dandbitʼun iordan ɡʼuruqχ rukʼaɡo betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazda abe iordanɡi baχun χanaanalde nuʒ ʃːwarab meχalda
ɡʔjeb rakʔalda ruɡel kinalɡo ɡʼadamal ɡʔjenisa naqχe qχame ʁure ɡʔjezul ɡantʃʼilɡi tsʼulalɡi maχːulɡi ɡʔarural jasikʼo allaɡʔzabi wa ʃːuʃːaqχ riχːizare ɡʔjezul kinalɡo muqʼadasal abulel bakʼal
ɡʔjeb rakʔ mukʼur ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabe ditsa nuʒee irsaɬe kʔoleb buɡo ɡʔjeb rakʔ
ɡʼizrailazul qʼawmazda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔjeb rakʔ bikʔje moʒoroɡi baqχun kʼudijab qʼawmaɬe kʼudijab rakʔ kʔje wa ɡʔitʼinaɬe ɡʔitʼinab kʔje moʒorojaɬ biχʔizaburab rakʔ bukʼine buɡo nuʒer qʼawmazeɡi tuχumazeɡi
amma ɡʔjeb rakʔaɬul ɡʼadamal naqχe qʼotʼitʃʼoni ɡʔjenir χutʼaral ɡʼadamal nuʒee rukʼine ruɡo badib qʼarab zazɬun wa χʔolboɬ qʼarab rukʼkʼjenɬun nuʒetsa ɡʼumru ɡʔabize buɡeb ɡʔjeb rakʔalda ɡʔjez χʼalχʔi teze ɡʔjetʃʼo nuʒee
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsaɡi nuʒee ɡʔabila ɡʔjezije ɡʔabize dida rakʼalda bukʼarab ʒo jan

betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔadin ɬazabe ɡʼizrailazda χanaanaɬul rakʔalde ɬuɡʔindal nuʒee kʔurab rakʔaɬul rukʼine ruɡo ɡʔadinal ɡʼorqχabi
qʼilbajaɬul raqχalda nuʒer rakʔal bajbiχʔize ruɡo tsin aburab salul awlaqχaldasan wa edomaɬul ɡʼorqχodasan baqʼbakːul raqχalda nuʒer qʼilbajaɬulab ɡʼorqχi bajbiχʔize buɡo tsʼamɡʼalab raɬdal raɡʼaldasan
χadub ine buɡo itʃʼkʼalaɬul ʃːobil qʼilbajaɬul raqχaldasan χadub tsin salul awlaqχaldasan χadub kadeʃ barneajaɬul qʼilbajaɬul raqχaldasan wa χatsar adarɡi baχun atsmonalde
atsmonaldasa misrijaɬul ɡʼorqχoda buɡeb ɬaraqχe swerize buɡo wa ɡʔjeb ɡʼorqχidul aχir kʼudijab raɬdaqχ bukʼine buɡo
nuʒer baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχaɬul ɡʼorqχiɬun bukʼine buɡo kʼudijab raɬdal
ʃimalijab ɡʼorqχi bukʼina kʼudijab raɬdaqχa ɡʔor maɡʼarde ʃːwezeɡʼan
ɡʔor maɡʼardasa lewo χamatalde ɡʔjenisan tsedadalde ɡʼuntʼila
χadub zifronalde batʃʼina wa aχiralda χatsar enanalde ɡʼuntʼila ɡʔjeb buɡo nuʒer ʃimalijab raqχaɬul ɡʼorqχi
nuʒer baqʼbakːul raqχaɬul ɡʼorqχi ɬe χatsar enanaldasa ʃefamalde ʃːwezeɡʼan
ʃefamaldasa nuʒer ɡʼorqχi ine buɡo ajinaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda buɡeb riwlajalde ʃːwezeɡʼan wa ɡʔjenisan ɡʼodobeχunɡi un kinneret χʼoraɬul baqʼbakːul raɡʼalde ɡʼuntʼize buɡo
ɡʔjenisan ɡʼorqχi ine buɡo iordan ɡʼuruqχe balaɡʔun wa tsʼamɡʼalab raɬdaqχe ʃːweze buɡo
ɡʔjele nuʒer rakʔaɬul ɡʼorqχabi
tsinɡi musatsa ɡʼizrailazda abuna
ɡʔjele ɡʔjeb buɡo nuʒetsa moʒorojaldaɬun nuʒedaɡo ɡʔorkʔob bikʔize kːoleb rakʔ betʼjerhanas amru ɡʔabuna ɡʔjeb rakʔ itʃʼɡoɡun baʃːdab qʼawmalda ɡʔorkʔob bikʔjejan
ʃːajɡureɬul ruwimilɡi ɡadilɡi qʼawmazeɡi manasːil baʃːdab qʼawmaɬeɡi rakʔaɬul butʼabi ʃːwana
ɡʔjeb kʼiɡoɡun baʃːdab qʼawmaɬul naslabaze ʃːwana iordanaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda ruɡel jeriχonalda dandritʼaral rakʔal
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʔale nuʒee rakʔaɬul butʼabi rikʔize ruɡel ɡʼadamazul tsʼaral
kaʃiʃ eleazarɡi nunil was jeɡʔoʃuaɡi
ɡʔjedinɡo ʃːibab qʼawmaldasa tso tso kʼudijawɡi
ɡʔale ɡʔjezul tsʼaral
jaɡʔudal qʼawmaldasa jefunnil was χalew
ʃimeonil qʼawmaldasa ammiɡʔudil was ʃemuel
bunjaminil qʼawmaldasa kislonil was elidad
danil qʼawmaldasa kʼudijaw jaɡlil was bukːij
jusupil was manasːil qʼawmaldasa kʼudijaw efodil was χaniel
jusupil was jefraimil qʼawmaldasa kʼudijaw ʃiftanil was kemuel
zewulunil qʼawmaldasa kʼudijaw parnaχil was elitsafan
isːaχaril qʼawmaldasa kʼudijaw azanil was paltiel
aʃeril qʼawmaldasa ʃelomijil was aχiɡʔud
naftalil qʼawmaldasa ammiɡʔudil was pedael
ɡʔjel ruɡo ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔob χanaanaɬul rakʔ bikʔjejan betʼjerhanas amru ɡʔabural ɡʼadamal

jeriχon ʃaɡʔaralda dandbitʼun iordan ɡʼurul raɡʼalda moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalda betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailil qʼawmazda ɬazabe ʒideeɡo ʃːwaral rakʔazdasa lewitaze tʃanɡo ʃaɡʔar kʔjejan abun ɡʼi botsʼi χʔiχʔize ɡʔjel ʃaɡʔarazda sweruqχ rakʔalɡi kʔje lewitaze
tsinɡi ɡʼumru ɡʔabize ʃaɡʔaralɡi rukʼina ɡʔjezul tʼolabɡo botsʼi panz χʔiχʔize meʁ rakʔɡi bukʼina
nuʒetsa lewitaze kʔjeze kːola ʃaɡʔarazul qʼadazdasa ʃːibab raqχalde azarɡo natʼaɬul
ʃaɡʔaraɬul rakʔazul ɡʼorqχabazul χalaɬi bukʼine kːola baqʼbakːul raqχalda kʼiazarɡo natʼ
nuʒetsa lewitaze kʔural ʃaɡʔarazul anɬɡojab bitʃːante bukʼine ɬutunʃaɡʔarɬun ɡʔjenire ɬutize ruɡo ɬatʃʼoɡo tʃi tʃʼwaral ɡʼadamal ɡʔjezde tʼadeɡi lewitaze kʔje ʒeɡi kʼiqʼojalda kʼiɡo ʃaɡʔar
kinabniɡi nuʒetsa lewitaze kʔje kʼiqʼojalda mikʔɡo ʃaɡʔarɡi ɡʔjezda sweruqχ buɡeb meʁ rakʔɡi
ɡʼizrailazul mulkaldasa ʃaɡʔaral lewitaze kʔolaɡo ɡʼjemeral ʃaɡʔaral ruɡeb qʼawmaɬuqχa tsʼikʼkʼun rose daɡʔal ʃaɡʔaral ruɡeb qʼawmaɬuqχa daɡʔal rose ʃaɡʔaral
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
ɡʼizrailazda abe iordanɡi baχun nuʒ χanaanalde ʃːwarab meχaɬ
nuʒeeɡo ɬutunʃaɡʔaral tʼasa riʃːe naɡaɡʔ ɬitsaniɡi toχɬukʔjeɡo tʃi tʃʼwani ɡʔjenire ɬutize rukʼine
ɡʔjel ʃaɡʔaral rukʼina biduqχ qʼisas bosize bokʔaraw tʃijasdasa waχtʃize insanase res kʔolel bakʼalɬun tʃʼwadaruqχanɬun rikʼkʼunew tʃi diwanalda tsewe aχʼitʃʼoɡo χwezawize beɡʔularo
ɡʔjedinab bukʼine kːola anɬɡo ʃaɡʔar
ɬabɡo ʃaɡʔar iordanaɬul ɡʔab raɡʼalda wa ɬabɡo χanaanalda ɡʔjel rukʼina ɬutunʃaɡʔaralɬun
ɡʔjeb anɬabɡo ʃaɡʔaraɬul tsojalda waχtʃize res bukʼina toχɬukʔje tʃi tʃʼwaraw tʃijase ɡʼizrailaseɡi tʃijar χalqʼaɬul tʃijaseɡi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabulew bokʔaraw tsoɡi tʃijaseɡi
amma tso tʃijas tsoɡidaw tʃijasda maχːul alat kʔabuni wa ɡʔjew χwani χwarasda kʔaburaw tʃi tʃʼwadaruqχan kːola ɡʔjewɡi tʃʼwaze kːola
jaɡi tso tʃijasuqχ kodob tʃi tʃʼwaze ɡʼurab ɡamatʃʼɡi bukʼun ɡʔjes ɡʔjeb tsoɡidaw tʃijasda kʔabuni wa ɡʔjew tʃi χwani ɡamatʃʼ kʔaburaw tʃi kːola tʃʼwadaruqχan ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjewɡi tʃʼwaze kːola
jaɡi tso tʃijasuqχ kodob tʃi tʃʼwaze ɡʼurab tsʼulal alatɡi bukʼun ɡʔjes ɡʔjeb tsoɡidaw tʃijasda kʔabuni wa ɡʔjew χwani ɡʔjew kːola tʃʼwadaruqχan ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjewɡi tʃʼwaze kːola
ɡʔjedinaw tʃi kiw wataniɡi tʃʼwaze beɡʔula χwarasul biduqχ qʼisas bosulew tʃijas ɡʔjesul iχtijar buɡo watarab bakʼaldaɡo ɡʔjew tʃʼwaze
naɡaɡʔ tso tʃijas rekʼjeɬ kweʃab qʼasdɡun tsoɡidaw tʃijasda tunkani jaɡi urʁunɡo ɡʔjesda tso ʃːib buɡoniɡi retʃʼtʃʼani wa ɡʔjew χwani
jaɡi tsːidaɬ ɡʔjew χoleduqχ ɡʔjesda zar bani wa ɡʔjew χwani ɡʔjew unɡo unɡojaw tʃʼwadaruqχan kːola ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjewɡi tʃʼwaze kːola χwarasul biduqχ qʼisas bosules kiw wataniɡi watarab bakʼalda tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjew
amma tso tʃijas tsoɡidaw tʃijasda toχɬukʔjeɡo kinabɡʼaɡi rokʔuqʼɬi ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo tunkani jaɡi ɡʔjes retʃʼtʃʼarab ʒo tsoɡidasda toχɬukʔjeɡo ʃːwani
jaɬuni ɡʔjewɡi wiχʔitʃʼoɡo ɡʔjesde tʼade ɡamatʃʼ bortizabuni wa ɡʔjew tʃi χwani rekʼjeɬ kinabɡʼaɡi tsːinɡi bukʼintʃʼoɡo wa ɡʔjesdeχun tuʃmanɬiɡi bukʼintʃʼoɡo
ɡʔjebmeχalda toχɬukʔjeɡo tʃi tʃʼwaraseɡi ɡʔjesdasa qʼisas bosuleseɡi χʼukmu qʼotʼize kːola ʒamaɡʼataɬ ɡʔal qʼanunalɡi χʼisabalde rosun
ɡʔjedinaw tʃʼwadaruqχan ʒamaɡʼataɬ bidul qʼisasaldasa χwasar ɡʔawize kːola wa ɡʔjew witʼize kːola ɬutunʃaɡʔaralde ɡʔjeniw waχtʃun wukʼine ɡʔjew ɡʔjeniw tʃʼjeze kːola kʼudijaw kaʃiʃ χwezeɡʼan
amma ʒiw waχtʃarab ɬutunʃaɡʔaraldasa tʃʼwadaruqχan qʼwatʼiwe ani
wa biduqχ qʼisas bosulesda ʃaɡʔar tun qʼwatʼiweχun ɡʔjew watani ɡʔjebmeχalda qʼisas bosulesul iχtijar buɡo ɡʔjew tʃʼwaze wa ɡʔjesda ɡʔjew tʃʼwajaɬul ɡʼajibɡi bukʼunaro
ʒiw waχtʃize arab ʃaɡʔaralda tʃʼwadaruqχan wukʼine kːola kʼudijaw kaʃiʃ χwezeɡʼan ɡʼitsʼɡo kʼudijaw kaʃiʃ χun χadub ɡuroni ɡʔjesije iχtijar ɡʔjetʃʼo roqʼowe tʼadwusːine
kib ɡʼumru ɡʔabun ruɡoniɡi ɡʔal qʼanunal tʼurazare nuʒetsaɡi nuʒer naslabazɡi
tʃʼwadaruqχan tʃʼwaze kːani nuɡʼzal rukʼine kːola ɡʔjez bitsarab ʒoɡi kʔotʃʼoje bosun ɡuroni tʃʼwalaro ɡʔjew ɡʔjew tʃʼwaze χʼukmu ɡʔabijaɬe tsoχʼo tʃijasul nuɡʼɬiɡi ɡʼolaro
tʃʼwaze mustaχʼiqʼaw tʃʼwadaruqχanas ʒindirɡo ɡʼumru ɡʼartsuqχ bitʃun bosize toɡe ɡʔjesda ɡʼajib batani tʃʼwadaruqχan tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo tʃʼwaze kːola
ɬutunʃaɡʔaralda waχtʃaraw tʃiɡi kʼudijaw kaʃiʃ χwezeɡʼan ʒindirɡo rakʔalde ɡʼartsuqχ tʼadwusːine witʃːan teze beɡʔularo
nuʒetsaɡo ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb rakʔ qχubɬizabuɡe ɡʼodobe tʼurab insanasul bijaɬ qχubɬizabula rakʔ wa ɡʔjeb bijaldasa rakʔ batsʼtsʼaɬularo rakʔalde ɡʔjeb bi tʼurasul bijaɬ ɡuroni
qχubɬizabuɡe nuʒetsaɡo ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb wa dun wukʼuneb rakʔ dun wuɡeɬul ɡʼizrailil χalqʼɡun wukʼunew betʼjerhan

jusupil was manasː manasːil was maχir maχiril was ɡilɡʼad ɡʔjele ɡʔjew ɡilɡʼadil tuχumaɬul kʼudijal ratʃʼana musaqχeɡi ɡʼizrailazul qʼawmazul butʼruzuqχeɡi
ɡʔjez abuna
ja betʼjertʃʼaqχad betʼjerhanas amru ɡʔabuna moʒoroɡi reχun ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔob rakʔ bikʔjejan betʼjerhanas dude niʒer betʼjertʃʼaqχadide amru ɡʔabuna niʒer wats tselofχadil rakʔaɬul butʼa ɡʔjesul jasaze kʔjejan
amma ɡʔjel ɡʼizrailazul batʼijal qʼawmazul wasaze rosase ani ɡʔjezul rakʔaɬul butʼa niʒer qʼawmaɬul mulkaldasa naqχe ine buɡo wa ɡʔjezul rosazul qʼawmazul mulkalde tʼade ʒubaze buɡo ɡʔjebmeχalda moʒorojalda reqʼon niʒee irsɬun ʃːwarab rakʔ tʼasa qʼotʼize buɡo
tsinɡi ɡʼizrailazul jubilejaɬul son tʼade ʃːwedalɡi ɡʔjel jasaze kʔurab rakʔaɬul butʼa ʒubaze buɡo ɡʔjezulɡun riɡʔin ɡʔabural qʼawmazul rakʔazde tʼade wa ɡʔjezul rakʔaɬul butʼa niʒer umumuzul rakʔaɬul butʼajaldasa tʼubanɡo baqχize buɡo
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanasul amrujaldaɬun musatsa ɡʼizrailazda abuna
jusupil qʼawmaɬ bitʼarab abuleb buɡo
betʼjerhanas ɡʔadinab amru ɡʔabuleb buɡo tselofχadil jasazde ɡʔjezul iχtijar buɡo bokʔaraw tʃijase rosase ine amma ɡʔjew wukʼine kːola ɡʔjezul qʼawmaɬul tuχumazda ɡʔorkʔosa tʃi
ɡʼizrailil qʼawmazul rakʔal tso qʼawmaɬuqχa tsoɡidab qʼawmaɬuqχe kʔjeze beɡʔularo ʃːiwaw ɡʼizrailas tsʼunize kːola ʒindirɡo umumuzul qʼawmalda ʒanib ɡʔjesije ʃːwarab rakʔaɬul butʼa
naɡaɡʔ ɡʼizrailaɬul tsoniɡi qʼawmaɬul jasaɬe irsaɬe insul rakʔaɬul butʼa ʃːwani ɡʔjej rosase ine kːola ʒindirɡo insul tuχumaldasa tʃijase ʒide ʒider umumuzul rakʔazul betʼjerɡʔabiɬun ɡʼizrailal χutʼijaɬul muradalda
kinabɡʼaɡi mulk ine beɡʔularo tso qʼawmaɬuqχa tsoɡidab qʼawmaɬuqχe bitʃːante ɡʼizrailazul ʃːibab qʼawmaɬ ʒindiqχɡo kːweze umumuzdasan irsaɬe ʃːwarab rakʔ
tselofχadil jasaz kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhanas musade ɡʔaburab amrujalda reqʼon
tselofχadil jasal maχlaɡi tirzaɡi χoɡlaɡi milkaɡi noɡʼaɡi ʒiderɡo insul raqχaɬan watsɡʼalzabaze rosase ana
ɡʔjel rukʼana jusupil was manasːil qʼawmaldasa wasal ɡʔjedinɬidal tselofχadil jasazul rakʔalɡi χutʼana ɡʔjezul umumuzul qʼawmaɬul mulkɬun
ɡʔjedinal rukʼana jeriχon ʃaɡʔaralda dandbitʼun iordan ɡʼurul raɡʼalda moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalda rukʼaɡo betʼjerhanas musadasan ɡʼizrailazde ɡʔarural amrabiɡi qʼanunalɡi

ɡʔale iordan ɡʼurul baqʼbakːul raqχaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔalda rukʼaɡo musatsa tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailaze ɡʔaburab waɡʼza nasiχʼat ɡʔjeb zamanalda ɡʔjel rukʼana sufalda askʼor paranaldaɡi tofelaldaɡi lawanaldaɡi χatserotaldaɡi di zaɡʔawaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob buɡeb awlaqχalda
seiraɬul muɡʼruzdeχun balaɡʔun ani χoriwaldasa kadeʃ barneajalde ʃːweze antsʼila tso qʼo bala nuχda
misri tun χaduseb kʼiqʼoabileb sonaɬul antsʼila tsoabileb motsʼaɬul tʼotsebeseb qʼojaɬ musa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda kʼaɬana betʼjerhanas tʼadqʼaral tʼolalɡo amrabiɡi ɡʔjezda rakʼalde ʃːwezarun
ɡʔjeb kːana χeʃbonalda taχ ɬuraw amorijazul patʃa siχonidaɡi aʃtarotaldaɡi edreijaldaɡi taχ ɬuraw baʃanaɬul patʃa oɡidaɡi tʼad berɡʔjenɬi bosun χadub
moɡʼawaɬul rakʔalda iordan ɡʼurul baqʼbakːul raqχalda χalqʼalda kʼaɬana musa wa ɡʔjezda qʼanun maɬana
χoriwalda niɬ rukʼaɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas niɬeda abuna ɡʼjela ɡʔab meɡʼjeralda askʼor rukʼaral
rakʼare nuʒerɡo tʃadral wa nuχda raqχa nuʒ amorijazul tʼaɬijalde wa tʼolabɡo ɡʔjezul maduɡʔalɬijalde aj awlaqχazda muɡʼruzda neɡewalda wa raɬdal raɡʼalɬijalda ruɡel rakʔazde a χanaanaɬul wa liwanaɬul rakʔazdasan kʼudijab jefrat ɡʼuruqχe ʃːwezeɡʼan a
ditsa nuʒee kʔoleb buɡo tʼolabɡo ɡʔjeb rakʔ ineɡi un baqχe ɡʔjeb dun ɡʔjedun wukʼana nuʒer umumul ibraɡʔimijeɡi isχʼaqʼijeɡi jaqʼubijeɡi ɡʔjezul naslabazeɡi ɡʔjeb rakʔ kʔjelin abun
dob zamanalda ditsa abuna ɡʼitsʼɡo dida baʒarularo nuʒee nuχmaɬi ɡʔabijaɬul bakʼab ɡʔir batʃːun
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒer qʼadar tsʼikʼkʼinabuna wa ɡʔale ʒaqʼa nuʒ zodir tsʼwabiɡʼanɡi ɡʼjemeral ruɡo
bitʃːante nuʒer umumuzul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒer qʼadar ɡʔjeldasaɡi azarɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼinabize bitʃːante ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo raɡʼuda reqʼon nuʒee barakatab ɡʼumruɡi kʔjeze
amma kinχa ɡʼitsʼɡo ditsa nuʒɡi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob kːolebʃːinab daɡʼba raɡʼiɡi nuχda batʃineb
ʃːibab qʼawmalda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼasa riʃːe ɡʼaqʼilal ɬajɡi χʼalbiχʔiɡi buɡel tʃaɡʼi wa ditsa ɡʔjel tʼamila nuʒer butʼrulɬun
nuʒetsa ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjeb ɬikʼab ɡʼaqʼlu buɡo ɡʔjedin ɡʔabila jan
tsinɡi ditsa tʼasa riʃːana nuʒer qʼawmazdasa ɡʼaqʼilal wa χʼalbiχʔi buɡel tʃaɡʼi wa ɡʔjel tana nuʒer diwantʃaɡʼiɬun azarɡojazul nusɡojazul kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡojazul wa antsʼɡojazul butʼrulɬun
ditsa nuʒer diwantʃaɡʼazda ɬazabuna nuʒer watsazda ɡʔorkʔob kːarab daɡʼba raɡʼijaɬuqχ ɡʼjenekːe wa ritʼuqχab χʼukmu qʼotʼje ɡʔjeb ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔob kːarab bukʼa jaɬuni batʼijab χalqʼaɬul tʃaɡʼazulɡun kːarab bukʼa batʼaɬi ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo
χʼukmu qʼotʼuleɬul ʃːiwniɡi insan batʼa ɡʔawuɡe qʼuwataw jaɡi zaɡʼipaw batʼa waqχitʃʼoɡo qʼotʼje χʼukmu ɡʼadamazukʔa χʼinqʼuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul diwan qʼotʼi ɡʔjeb allaɡʔasul iʃ kːoleɬul nuʒeqχan baʒarulareb tsʼaqʼɡo zaχʼmatab iʃ kːani diqχe bose dun ɡʼjenekːila ɡʔjeɬuqχ
dob meχalda ditsa nuʒeda ɬazabuna kinabɡo nuʒetsa ɡʔabize kːolebʃːinab
χadubɡi betʼjerhanasul amrujaldaɬun niɬ χoriwaldasa qʼwatʼire raqχana wa kʼudijab χʼinqʼarab awlaqχ qʼotʼun nuʒeda biχʔana dob awlaqχ amorijazul muɡʼruzde riɬːana wa kadeʃ barneajalde ʃːwana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsa nuʒeda abuna nuʒ ʃːwana betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔolel ruɡel amorijazul muɡʼruzde
ɡʔale betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔuna ɡʔab rakʔ nuʒerɡo kwerʃːalikʔje bose ɡʔjeb nuʒer umumuzul betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrujalda reqʼon ja χʼinqʼuɡe ja qʼurkʔuɡe
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nuʒ kinalɡo ratʃʼana diqχe wa nuʒetsa abuna ratʃʼa tsin ɡʔjenire tʃaɡʼi ritʼize dol rakʔazul χal ʃalɡi ɡʔabun niɬ ine kːoleb nuχaɬulɡi niɬetsa kwerde rosize ruɡel ʃaɡʔarazulɡi niɬeqχe χabar bosun ratʃʼine
dir ɡʔjelda rakʼ reqʼana wa nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔosa antsʼila kʼiɡo tʃi tʼasa wiʃːana ʃːibab qʼawmaldasa tso tso tʃi
ɡʔjel nuχda ana muɡʼrul tʼaɬijaldeɡi raχun eʃkol aburab ɡʼatʼidab rasaɬijalde ʃːwezeɡʼan ana ɡʔjel wa kinabɡo rakʔaɬul χal ʃal ɡʔabuna
ɡʔjenisan piqχɡi bosun niɬeqχe tʼadrusːindal ɡʔjez abuna betʼjerhan allaɡʔas niɬee barakatab rakʔ kʔoleb buɡo jan
amma nuʒee bokʔitʃʼo ɡʔjenire ine nuʒ betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrujalda dande tʃʼana
nuʒ qʼulqʼudana nuʒerɡo tʃadrazda ʒanir betʼjerhanasda niʒ riχun ruɡo ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjes misrijaldasa qʼwatʼireɡi ratʃun amorijazul kwerʃːalikʔje kʔolel ruɡo niɬ ɡʔjez ʁurize rukʼine
kire unel tʃaɡʼi niɬ niɬer watsaz bitsaraɬɡi rakʼal tamaχɬizarun ruɡeb meχaɬ ɡʔjez abuna dob χalqʼ niɬedasa qʼuwatabɡi tʃʼaχʼijabɡi buɡilan wa dozul ʃaɡʔaral kʼudijal zodire ɡʼuntʼaral qʼadaz swerun kːural ruɡilan ɡʔjenir anakilaltsin
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsa nuʒeda abuna nuʒ ɡʔjezukʔa χʼinqʼuɡe
misrijaldaɡo ɡʼadin nuʒee ɡʼolo waʁize nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ unew wuɡo nuʒeda tsewe tsewe nuʒerɡo berazda biχʔana ɡʔjew nuʒeda tsewe tsewe unew wukʼin
salul awlaqχaldasaɡi nuʒedaɡo biχʔana ɡʔjeb insutsa kodowɡi kːun ʒindirɡo was watʃunew kiniɡin ratʃana nuʒ betʼjerhanas tʼolabɡo nuχda ɡʔanire ʃːwezeɡʼan
ɡʔjebɡi ɡʼjetʃʼoɡo nuʒ ɡʔanʒeɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda boʒulel ɡʔjetʃʼo
ɡʔjewin abuni nuʒ nuχda ruɡebɡʼan zamanalda nuʒeda tsewe tsewe wukʼana qʼasi tsʼaɬun qʼad nakʼkʼul partʃaɬun nuʒeda nuχɡi χʼuχʔbaqχize bakʼɡi biχʔizabulaɡo
dobmeχaɬ nuʒer kʼaɬaj raɡʼana betʼjerhanasda wa ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjesul kutakalda tsːin baqχana wa ɡʔjes χʼukmu qʼotʼana
ɡʔab kweʃab ɡʼjelaɬul tsoniɡi tʃijasda biχʔize ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjezul umumuze dun ɡʔjedarab ɡʔarzajab rakʔ
jefunnil was χalewida ɡuroni ɡʔjesda biχʔila ɡʔjeb wa ɡʔjesijeɡi ɡʔjesul ɬimalazeɡi kʔjela ditsa ɡʔjeb ɡʔjew rakʼ rakʼaɬ betʼjerhanase mutʼiɡʼaw wukʼindal in
nuʒ sababɬun dideɡi tsːin baqχana betʼjerhanasul wa ɡʔjes abuna munɡi ɬuɡʔine ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjeniwe
amma dur kumektʃi nunil was jeɡʔoʃua ɬuɡʔina ɡʔjeb rakʔalde ɡʔjesda qʼwakʼun tʃʼajan abe ɡʔjes batʃine buɡeɬul ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ ɡʔjeb rakʔ mukʼur ɡʔabize
nuʒer ɬimal asirɬude kːelin χʼinqʼana nuʒ amma kweʃab ɬikʼab ʒeɡi batʼa baqχize ɬalarel ɡʔjel ɬimal ine ruɡo ɡʔjeb rakʔalde ɡʔjezije kʔjeze buɡo ditsa ɡʔjeb rakʔ wa ɡʔjel rukʼine ruɡo ɡʔjeɬul irsilal
nuʒin abuni tʼadrusːa wa baɡʼarab raɬdaqχe uneb nuχda buɡeb salul awlaqχalde a
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nuʒetsa abuna niʒetsa betʼjerhanasda dandeɡi raqχun munaɡʔ ɡʔabuna amma ɡʔanʒe niʒ ina raʁ ɡʔabize betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrujalda reqʼon nuʒetsa jaraʁ bortʃana dob muɡʼruzul ulka kwerde bosi biɡʔajab ʒojilanɡi kːun
amma betʼjerhanas dida abuna ɡʔjezda abe unɡe ɡʔjeb tʼaɬijalde wa ɡʔjezulɡun raʁ ɡʔabuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul dun nuʒɡun wukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo wa tuʃbabaz nuʒ ʁurize ruɡo jan
ditsa ɡʔjeb nuʒeda bitsana amma nuʒ ɡʔjeɬuqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼo betʼjerhanasul amruɡi ɡʼadaqχ bositʃʼoɡo ɡʼamal kʼodoɡo muɡʼrul tʼaɬijalde ana nuʒ
ɡʔjenir tʃʼaral amorijazɡi nuʒeda dande raʁ ɡʔabuna najazul bo kiniɡin nuʒeda χadur ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjel wa seiraldasa χormajalde ʃːwezeɡʼan nuʒ ʁurana
tsinɡi tʼadɡi rusːun nuʒetsa betʼjerhanasda tsebe maɡʼu tʼuna amma nuʒer ɡʼodijaɬul ɡʔjes kʼwar ɡʔabitʃʼo ɡʔjew nuʒeqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼo
nuʒɡi ɡʼjemerab meχaɬ kadeʃalda χutʼana

betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon naqχɡi rusːun niɬ baɡʼarab raɬdaqχe uneb nuχda buɡeb ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχalde riɬːana ɡʼjemerab zamanaɬ seir meɡʼjeralda swerun χʔwadize kːana niɬ
χadub betʼjerhanas dida abuna
ɡʼjela ɡʔal muɡʼrul ʃːobal swerun χʔwadaral ɡʔanʒe ʃimalaɬul raqχalde rusːa
χalqʼaɬe ɡʔadinab bujuruqχɡi kʔje ɡʔanʒe nuʒ ineqχin ruɡo seiralda tʃʼaral nuʒer watsazul aj ɡʼisawil naslabazul rakʔaldasan ɡʔjel nuʒekʔa χʼinqʼize ruɡo amma tsʼodorɬi ɡʔabe
ɡʔjelɡun raʁ ɡʔabizejan ɬuɡʔunɡe ʃːajɡureɬul ditsa nuʒee ɡʔjezul rakʔazul tso tsedertsin kʔjeze ɡʔjetʃʼo
nuʒetsa ɡʔjenib kwanarab niɡʼmataɬuqχɡi ɡʔjeqʼarab ɬadaqχɡi ɡʔjezije muχʔ kʔje jan
nuʒetsa ɡʔabulebʃːinaɬuɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔas barakat reʃːtʼinabuna nuʒee ɡʔjesda ɬaleɬul raɡʼa rakʔan ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχalda nuʒetsa ɡʔaburab sapar kʼiqʼojabɡo sonaɬ nuʒɡun wukʼana nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wa ɡʔjedinɬidal nuʒee qʼwariɡʼarabʃːinabɡi ɡʼunɡi tʼokʼ bukʼana
ɡʔjedinab χʼalalda seiralda tʃʼjel ɡʔabural watsazda aj ɡʼisawil naslabazda askʼosan ana niɬ iordanaɬul rasaɬijaldasan elataldeɡi jetsion ɡeweraldeɡi uneb nuχdasaɡi swerun niɬ riɬːana moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχalde
betʼjerhanas dida abuna moɡʼawijazul raχʼat χwezabuɡe wa ɡʔjezulɡun raʁ ɡʔabuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul ditsa nuʒee ɡʔjezul rakʔ kʔjeze ɡʔjetʃʼo ditsa ar
tsebe doba ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bukʼana emejaz anakilal ɡʼadinal qʼuwatal wa loɡoɬa tʃʼaχʼijal ɡʼadamal rukʼana ɡʔjel ɡʼjemerab χalqʼɡi bukʼana ɡʔjezul
anakil naslabiɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjelɡi refaimalɬun
seiraldajin abuni tsebe χorijaz ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bukʼana amma ɡʼisawil naslabaz ɡʔjel ɡʔjenisa naqχe aχʼana wa ɡʔjezul bakʼalda ʒalɡo tʃʼana betʼjerhanas kʔurab rakʔalda ɡʼizrailaz ɡʔaburabɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔabuna ɡʔjezɡi
raqχa ɡʔanʒe wa zaredaɬul kʼkʼal baχe jan abuna betʼjerɡʔanas wa niɬetsa ɡʔjeb kʼkʼal baχana
niɬetsa kadeʃ barnea tarab zamanaldaɡi zaredaɬul kʼkʼal baχarab zamanaldaɡi ɡʔorkʔob ɬeberalda mikʔɡo son ana ɡʔjebɡoʃːinab zamanalda ʒanib betʼjerhanasul ɡʔajalda reqʼon tso tʼubarab ɡʼjelaɬul raʁuje jaraɡʔunewʃːinaw tʃi χwana
ɡʼizrailazda ʁorɬa ɡʔjel tʼuran tʼaɡʼinarizeɡʼan betʼjerhan ɡʔjezda dande tʃʼana
raʁuje jaraɡʔunel ɡʔjel kinalɡo biχʔinal χwarab meχaɬ
betʼjerhanas dida abuna
ɡʔanʒe nuʒ moɡʼawaɬul rakʔaldasan ar ʃaɡʔaralda askʼosan a
kwatʼitʃʼoɡo nuʒ ammonijazda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχe ʃːwela amma ɡʔjezul raχʼat χwezabuɡe wa ɡʔjezulɡun raʁ ɡʔabuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul ditsa nuʒee ammonijazul rakʔaɬul tso tsedertsin kʔjeze ɡʔjetʃʼo ditsa ɡʔjeb lutʼil naslabaze kʔuna
kidajaliɡo ɡʔjel refaimazul rakʔalin rikʼkʼunaan tsebe ɡʔjez tʃʼjel ɡʔabun bukʼindal ɡʔjenib amma ammonijaz ɡʔjezda zamzummejalin abulaan
ɡʔjelɡi rukʼana anakilal ɡʼadinal qʼuwatal wa loɡoɬa rorχatal ɡʼadamal ɡʼjemerab χalqʼ bukʼana ɡʔjezul amma betʼjerhanas tʼaɡʼinaruna ɡʔjel ɡʔjelɡi naqχe qχamun ammonijal raqχana ɡʔjezul bakʼalde
betʼjerɡʔanas ɡʔjebɡo ɡʔabuna seiralda tʃʼjel ɡʔabural ɡʼisawil naslabazeɡi tserekːun ɡʔjenir rukʼaral χorijalɡi tʼaɡʼinarun ɡʼisawilaz naqχe aχʼana ɡʔjel wa ɡʔjezul bakʼalda ʒalɡo tʃʼana
ɡazajalde ɡʼuntʼizeɡʼanɡi rosabaɬ ɡʼumru ɡʔabun rukʼaral awwijal ʁurana kritaldasa
saparalde raqχa arnon ɡʼor baχe jan abuna betʼjerhanas ditsa duqχe kʔolel ruɡo χeʃbonaɬul patʃa amorijaw siχonɡi ɡʔjesul ulkaɡi raʁ bajbiχʔje wa ɡʔjezul rakʔal kwerde rose
ʒaqʼa qʼojaldasa naqχe ditsa dukʔan ɡʼasijab χʼinqʼi reʃːtʼinabila ɡʔab dunjalaɬul tʼolalɡo χalqʼazde ɡʔjezda dur χʼaqʼaɬuɬ χabar raɡʼila wa χʼinqʼarab χʼinqʼijaɬ sorodizarila ɡʔjel
tsinɡi kedemotaldasa wakilzabi ritʼana ditsa χeʃbonaɬul patʃa siχoniqχe raqʼlilab χabarɡun
ritʃːante niʒ dur ulka qʼotʼun ine kʼudijab nuχkːun ina niʒ ja kwaranab ja kweɡʼab raqχalde swerilaro
ɡʼartsuqχ bitʃe niʒee kwanaze kwenɡi ɡʔjeqʼeze ɬimɡi ɡʼitsʼɡo iznu kʔje niʒee dur ulkajaɬul nuχkːun ine
seiralda tʃʼjel ɡʔabural ɡʼisawil naslabazɡi aralda tʃʼaral moɡʼawijazɡi ɡʔaburabɡo ɡʼadin niʒ iordan baχun doreχun betʼjerhan allaɡʔas niʒee kʔurab rakʔalde unel ruɡo
amma χeʃbonaɬul patʃa siχonitsa ritʃːatʃʼo niɬ ɡʔjesul ulkajaldasa ine ʃːajɡureɬul niɬer betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔjesul rekʼjeɬ rokʔuqʼɬi ɬun bukʼun siχon patʃa nuʒer kwerʃːalikʔje kʔjeze ɡʼolo ɡʔjedin kːezeɡi kːana
betʼjerhanas dida abuna ɡʔale ditsa duqχe kʔolew wuɡo siχonɡi ɡʔjesul ulkaɡi ɡʔanʒe baqχe ɡʔjesul rakʔ wa ɡʔjelda tʼad kwerʃːel ɡʔabe
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ siχon watʃʼana niɬeda dande tʼolabɡo ʒindirɡo askarɡun wa jaχatsalda askʼob raʁ kːana
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔjewɡi niɬer kwerʃːalikʔje kʔuna niɬetsa tʃʼwana ɡʔjew ɡʔjesul wasalɡun wa askarɡun tsadaqχ
dob meχaɬ niɬetsa ɡʔjesul tʼolalɡo ʃaɡʔaral kwerde rosana wa ɡʔjezul biχʔinalɡi rutʃːabiɡi ɬimalɡi tso tʃi naqχe tetʃʼoɡo χerem
amma ɡʼi botsʼiɡi ʃaɡʔarazdasa ʃːwarab dawlaɡi niɬeeɡo tana
arnon ɡʼuruqχ buɡeb aroɡʼjer ʃaɡʔaraldasa baqχarab ɡilɡʼadalde ʃːwezeɡʼan tso ʃaɡʔar χutʼitʃʼo niɬeda baqχun baʒaritʃʼjeb betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kinabɡo kʔuna niɬer kwerʃːalikʔje
amma betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrujaldaɬun ja ammonijazul rakʔazde ja jabbok ɡʼurul raɡʼalɬijalda ruɡel rakʔazde ja ʃaɡʔarazul sweruqχɬijaɬul muɡʼruzda ruɡel rakʔazde niɬetsa kwer beɡʔitʃʼo

ɡʔjenisa niɬ swerana wa baʃanalde uneb nuχkːun ana baʃanaɬul patʃa oɡ watʃʼana niɬeda dande tʼolabɡo ʒindirɡo askarɡun wa edrei ʃaɡʔaralda askʼob niɬɡun raʁ ɡʔabuna
betʼjerhanas dida abuna mun ɡʔjesukʔa χʼinqʼuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul ditsa duqχe kʔolew wuɡo ɡʔjewɡi ɡʔjesul askarɡi ɡʔjesul rakʔɡi χeʃbonaɬul patʃa siχonije ɡʔaburab ɡʔabe ɡʔjesijeɡi
ɡʔjedin betʼjerhan allaɡʔas niɬer kwerʃːalikʔje kʔuna baʃanaɬul patʃa oɡɡi ɡʔjesul tʼolabɡo askarɡi niɬetsa kinalɡo ʁurana ɡʔjezul tsoniɡi tʃi tʃʼaɡo tetʃʼo
dobmeχalda ɡʔjesul kinalɡo ʃaɡʔaralɡi kwerde rosana niɬetsa baʃanalda bukʼarab oɡil ulkajalda arɡowaɬul wilajataɬul ɬabqʼojabɡo ʃaɡʔar baqχana
ɡʔjel kinalɡo ʃaɡʔaral swerun rorχatal qʼadalɡi ran ʃːula ɡʔarun rukʼana wa ʃaɡʔarazul kawabazda ʃːulijal raχajalɡi ran rukʼana ɡʔjedinɡo qʼadaz swerun kːwetʃʼjel rosabiɡi ɡʼjemeral rukʼana
niɬetsa tʼuran tʼaɡʼinaruna ɡʔjelɡi χeʃbonaɬul patʃa siχonije ɡʔaburabɡo ɡʔabun ʃːibab ʃaɡʔarɡi χerem ɡʔabuna biχʔinal rutʃːabi ɬimalɡun tsadaqχ
amma tʼolabɡo ɡʼi botsʼiɡi ʃaɡʔarazdasa ʃːwarab dawlaɡi niɬeeɡo tana
palχʼasil dob zamanalda niɬetsa iordanaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda arnon ɡʼuruqχa baqχarab χermon maɡʼarde ʃːwezeɡʼan amorijazul kʼijawɡo patʃajasul rakʔal kwerde rosana
sidonijaz χermonalda abulaan sirionilan amorijaz senirilan
niɬetsa ɡʔjezul tʼaɬijalda rukʼaral oɡil ulkajaɬul kinalɡo ʃaɡʔaral kwerde rosana tʼolabɡo ɡilɡʼadɡi tʼolabɡo baʃanɡi aj baʃanaɬul ʃaɡʔaral salχajaldeɡi edreijaldeɡi ʃːwezeɡʼan
baʃanaɬul patʃa oɡ wukʼana refaimazul tsoχʼoɡo tso χutʼaraw tʃi ɡʔjesul kʔiʒuleb bakʼ bukʼana maχːul ɡʔaburab itʃʼɡo rukʔ χalaɬuqχeɡi unqʼɡo rukʔ ɡʼjebɬuqχeɡi buɡeb
dob meχalda raqχaral rakʔazul butʼabi ruwimilɡi ɡadilɡi naslabaze kʔuna ditsa arnon rasaɬijalda buɡeb aroɡʼjeraldasa bajbiχʔun bakʼalɡi ɡilɡʼadaɬul baʃːdab tʼaɬiɡi ɡʔjenir ruɡel ʃaɡʔaralɡi
ɡilɡʼadaɬul χutʼarab rakʔɡi oɡil bukʼarab tʼolabɡo baʃanɡi ditsa manasːil baʃːdab qʼawmaɬe kʔuna
tsebe arɡowaɬul wilajatalda abulaan refaimazul rakʔin
manasːil naslujaɬul tʃi jairitsa kwerde bosana tʼolabɡo arɡow wilajat ɡeʃurijazulɡi maɡʼaχijazulɡi ɡʼorqχabazde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo tsʼar kʔuna ɡʔjeɬije wa ʒaqʼa qʼojaɬɡi baʃanalda abula jairil rosabijan
ɡilɡʼad ditsa maχiril kʔibilaɬe kʔuna
ruwimilazeɡi ɡadilazeɡi kʔuna ɡilɡʼadaldasa arnonaɬul ɬaramuqχalde ɡʔjeb ɬaral bakʔuɬan bukʼana ɡʼorqχi wa ammonijazul ɡʼorqχiɬun kːoleb jabbok ɬaraqχe ʃːwezeɡʼan rakʔal
ɡʔjezul tsoɡidab raqχaɬul ɡʼorqχiɬun bukʼana iordan kinneret χʼoraldasa baqχarab arawa raɬdaqχe tsʼamul raɬdaqχe wa baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχalda fasɡa meɡʼjeraɬul ʁulduqχe ʃːwezeɡʼan
dobmeχalda ditsa nuʒede amru ɡʔabuna betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee ɡʔab rakʔ kʔuna nuʒetsa betʼjerɡʔanɬi ɡʔabize nuʒer kinalɡo raʁde raqχun baʒarulel biχʔinaz bortʃun jaraʁɡun nuʒer watsal ɡʼizrailazda tsere tsere riɬːun ɡʼor baχine kːola
ɡʼitsʼɡo nuʒer ɬudbiɡi ɬimalɡi ɡʼi botsʼiɡi dida ɬala nuʒer ɡʼjemerab ɡʼi botsʼi buɡebɬi ditsa nuʒee kʔural ʃaɡʔarazda tʃʼjeze beɡʔula
betʼjerhanas nuʒer watsazeɡi nuʒeeɡo ɡʼadin paraχaɬi kʔurab meχaɬ aj iordanaɬul dob tsojab raqχalda betʼjerhanas ɡʔjezije kʔural rakʔal ɡʔjez mukʼur ɡʔarurab meχaɬ nuʒɡi ditsa nuʒee kʔural rakʔazde tʼad rusːine beɡʔula
dob meχaɬ ditsa jeɡʔoʃuada abuna durɡo berazda biχʔana betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dow kʼijawɡo patʃajase ɡʔaburab ʒo ɡʔjebɡo ɡʔabize buɡo betʼjerhanas mun ʃːwaralʃːinal rakʔazeɡi ɡʔjezul patʃabazeɡi
nuʒ ɡʔjezukʔa χʼinqʼuɡe nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ waʁize wuɡo nuʒer raqχaɬan
dob meχalda ditsa betʼjerhanasda ɡʔarana
χʼalkʼolew betʼjerhan dutsa dida dur laʁasda biχʔizabuna durɡo χʼalkʼoɬiɡi kʼudijab qʼuwatɡi zobalazdaɡi rakʔaldaɡi kiw watulew dur ɡʼadinal χʼikmatal iʃal ɡʔarize baʒarulew batʼijaw allaɡʔ
unɡo beɡʔilariʃːχa ditsaɡi ɡʼor baχine wa iordanaɬul dobeχun raqχalda buɡeb ɡʔajbatab ulka didaɡi biχʔize dol bertsinal muɡʼrulɡi tʼjeɡʔarab liwanɡi
amma nuʒ sababɬun dida tsːin baqχana betʼjerhanasul wa dir ɡʔari qʼabul ɡʔabitʃʼo ɡʼjela jan abuna betʼjerhanas tʼokʼaɬ dida ɡʔjeɬul bitsunɡe
fasɡajaɬul tʼoɡʔiwe waχa wa ɡʔjenisan walaɡʔje baqʼtʼjerχʔulɡi ʃimalaɬulɡi baqʼbakːulɡi qʼilbajaɬulɡi raqχazde duda biχʔila ɡʔjeb amma iordan baχun doweχun mun ine ɡʔjetʃʼo
jeɡʔoʃuada maɬa qχwajɡi ɡʔabe ɡʔjewɡi qʼwakʼizawe ʃːajɡureɬul χalqʼaɬul betʼjerɬudaɡi wukʼun ɡʔjes baχine buɡeɬul iordan wa duda biχʔarab rakʔɡi χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔob bikʔize buɡeɬul ɡʔjes
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ niɬ bet peoralda askʼob buɡeb rasaɬijalda ɬalqχana

ɡʼjenekːe ɡʔanʒe ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ ditsa nuʒeda maɬulel ruɡel allaɡʔasul qʼanunazuqχɡi χʼukmabazuqχɡi ɡʔjel tʼurazare nuʒɡo tʃʼaɡo rukʼine wa betʼjerhanas nuʒer umumuz iman ɬuraw allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔaɬe nuʒetsa betʼjerɡʔanɬi ɡʔabize bukʼine
ditsa nuʒeda ɬazaburabʃːinalda tʼade ʃːibɡo ʒubaɡe ʃːibɡo tʼasaɡi baqχuɡe ditsa nuʒeda maɬaral betʼjerhanasul amrabi tʼurazare
nuʒerɡo berazda biχʔana betʼjerhanas baɡʼal peoralda ɡʔaburab ʒo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼaɡʼinaruna kinalɡo baɡʼal peorida naqχ riɬːanʃːinal tʃaɡʼi
amma betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda boʒun tʃʼaral tʃaɡʼi ʒaqʼa qʼojaɬɡi tʃʼaɡo ruɡo
ɡʔale ditsa nuʒeda maɬulel ruɡo allaɡʔasul qʼanunalɡi χʼukmabiɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dide amru ɡʔaburab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ nuʒ unel ruɡeb wa nuʒetsa mukʼur ɡʔabize buɡeb rakʔalda nuʒetsa ɡʔjel tʼurazarize kːola
raɡʼa rakʔande ʃːun tʼurazare ɡʔjel tsinɡi tʼolalɡo χalqʼazda biχʔila nuʒer ɡʼaqʼluɡi ɬajɡi ɡʔjel kinalɡo qʼanunal raɡʼidal ɡʔjez abila unɡo ɡʔab kʼudijab χalqʼaɬul buɡeb ɡʼaqʼilɬiɡi tsʼodorɬiɡi jan
ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul niɬede ɡʼadin ʒider allaɡʔzabi ʒidede ɡʼaɡarɬarab tsoniɡi batʼijab kʼudijab χalqʼ niɬer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ niɬede ɡʼaɡaraw wuɡo kida ʃːib niɬetsa ɡʔaraniɡi
ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒeda maɬulel ruɡel ɡʼadinal ritʼuqχal qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi ʒider ruɡeb tsoɡi batʼijab kʼudijab χalqʼ ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul
woreχa tsʼodorɡo rukʼa kidaniɡi kʼotʃonɡe nuʒer berazda biχʔarab nuʒɡo tʃʼaɡo ruɡebɡʼan meχaɬ rekʼjeɬ tsʼune wa nuʒerɡo ɬimalazdaɡi ɡʔjezul ɬimalazdaɡi maɬe ɡʔjeb
kʼotʃene toɡe χoriwalda betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsere nuʒ eχetun rukʼarab qʼoɡi wa ɡʔjes dide ɡʔaburab amruɡi χalqʼ dida tsebe bakʼare ditsa ɡʔjezda dirɡo amrabi raɡʼizarize bitʃːante ɡʔab dunjalaɬul roqʼor ruɡebɡʼan meχaɬ ɡʔjel ruɡʔunɬize dikʔa χʼinqʼizeɡi dun kʼodo ɡʔawizeɡi bitʃːante ɡʔjebɡo ʒo ɬimalazdaɡi maɬize jan
nuʒ ɡʼaɡarɬana zodobe ɡʼuntʼarab tsʼaɡi rekʼarab tʃʼjeɡʼjeral nakʼkʼazɡi laχʼtʃʼjeɡʼjerab betsʼɬijaɬɡi baχtʃarab meɡʼjeraɬul aχade wa ɡʔjenir raqχun tʃʼana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ tsʼaduɬan betʼjerhan kʼaɬana nuʒeda nuʒeda raɡʼuleb bukʼana amma sipat biχʔuleb bukʼintʃʼo ɡʼitsʼɡo ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼun ɡuroni
wa ɡʔjes nuʒeda ʒindirɡo qʼotʼijaɬul ʃartʼal ɬazaruna nuʒetsa tʼubazabize tʼadabɬun ɡʔaburab antsʼɡo amru ɡʔjes ɡantʃʼil kʼiɡo qʼonojalda qχwana ɡʔjel amrabi
betʼjerhanas dida tʼad qʼana nuʒeda ɡʔjesul qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi maɬejan nuʒ unel ruɡeb wa nuʒetsa kwerde bosize buɡeb rakʔalda nuʒetsa ɡʔjel tʼurazarize rukʼine
χoriw maɡʼarda rukʼaɡo tsʼaduɬan betʼjerhan nuʒɡun kʼaɬarab qʼojaɬ nuʒeda kinabɡʼaɡi sipat biχʔitʃʼo ɡʔjedinɬidal nuʒɡo tsʼune
kinab bukʼaniɡi sipat suratalda tsebe tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabijaldasa ɡʔjedinab qʼasdɡun ja biχʔintʃijasul jaɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬul
kinab bukʼaniɡi χʼajwanaɬul jaɡi zodil χʼintʃʼaɬul
rakʔaldasan ʃuruleb jaɡi ɬadaɬ ɬedoleb ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬijaɬul surat ɡʔabuɡe
mun zodiwe walaɡʔidal wa baqʼɡi motsʼɡi tsʼwabiɡi aj tʼolabɡo zobalazul askar biχʔidal munɡo qʼosun kːeze witʃːaɡe ɡʔjezije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabuɡe nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔun ruɡeɬul ɡʔjel ɡʔab dunjalaɬul kinalɡo χalqʼaze
nuʒin abuni misrijaɬul tsʼadul korinisa naqχe ratʃana betʼjerhanas ʒindirɡo χalqʼɬun wa irsilalɬun ɡʔarize ɡʔjedin kːezeɡi kːana
amma nuʒ sababɬun betʼjerhanasul dida tsːin baqχana wa ɡʔjew ɡʔjedana ditsa iordan ɡʼor baχinarin wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee irsɬun kʔoleb buɡeb ɡʔajbatab rakʔalde dun ɬuɡʔine ɡʔjetʃʼin abun
ɡʔjedinɬidal dun iordanɡi baχintʃʼoɡo ɡʔab rakʔaldaɡo χweze wuɡo nuʒetsa abuni ɡʼorɡi baχina wa dob ɡʔajbatab rakʔɡi mukʼur ɡʔabila
amma tsʼodorɬi ɡʔabe betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul qʼotʼi kʼotʃonɡe kinab bataniɡi sipat surataɬul ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔ ɡʔabuɡe betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔuqʼarab buɡo ɡʔjeb nuʒee
nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wuɡo ʃːibɡoɡi kʼkʼwinabuleb tsʼaɬun ɡʔjew wuɡo χilipɬi χʼjeχʔolarew allaɡʔ
nuʒ dob rakʔalde raqχaraldasa ɡʼjemerab meχ ina nuʒee ɬimalɡi ɬimalazul ɬimalɡi ɡʔarila nuʒɡi χerɬila amma χadubkːun nuʒetsa kweʃɬi ɡʔabize buɡo nuʒetsa ɡʔarize ruɡo batʼi batʼijal sipatazul ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔzabi wa nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda riχaralʃːinal ʒalɡi ɡʔarun ɡʔjesul tsːin baqχinabize buɡo
ɡʔjedinɬidal ʒaqʼa zobɡi rakʔɡi nuɡʼzalɬun rukʼa abe ditsa bitsuneb raɡʼuje ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuni nuʒ dob rakʔaldasa χeχɡo tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡo ʒaqʼa nuʒetsa iordan baχuneb buɡo dob rakʔ kwerde bosize ɡʼolo amma ɡʔjeldasa χadub nuʒetsa ɡʔjenib ɡʼjemer meχ baze ɡʔjetʃʼo nuʒ tʼuran tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡo
betʼjerhanas nuʒ batʼi batʼijal χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔore qχamila wa ɡʔjezul rakʔazda betʼjerhanas nuʒer daɡʔal tʃaɡʼi ɡuroni tʃʼaɡo telaro
ɡʔjenib nuʒetsa tsʼulɡi ɡamatʃʼɡi bosun insanasul kweraz ɡʔarural ʒideda ʃːibɡo raɡʼularel biχʔularel kwen kwanalarel jaɡi maχʼ tʃʼwalarel ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔzabaze ɡʼibadat ɡʔabila
χadub nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasde rusːine bokʔila nuʒee ɡʔjesɡi ʒiwɡo zaɡʔir ɡʔawize wuɡo tʼolabɡo ruχʼɡi ʒanɡi kʔun rakʼ rakʼaɬɡo nuʒ ɡʔjesdeχun rusːani
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɬuɡʔarab wa balaɡʔazukʔje nuʒɡi kːarab zaman batʃʼindal nuʒ tsʼidasan betʼjerhan allaɡʔasde rusːina wa ɡʔjesije mutʼiɡʼɬila
nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ raχʼmujaw wuɡeɬul ɡʔjes nuʒ reχun telaro wa rakʔaldasa tʼaɡʼinarilaro nuʒer umumulɡun ɡʔaburab ʒindirɡo qʼotʼiɡi ɡʔjedarab ɡʔaɡi ɡʔjesda kʼotʃon teze ɡʔjetʃʼo
arab zamanalda tsʼjeχe mun rakʔalda wiʒilalde tsebeɡo bukʼaraɬul χʼisab ɡʔabe ɡʔab rakʔalda allaɡʔas insan wiʒarab qʼojaldasa naqχe ɡʔadinab χʼalkʼoɬi bukʼaniʃː ɡʔab dunjalalda kibniɡi tsojab zob rakʔaɬul raɡʼaldasa tsoɡidab raɡʼalde ʃːwezeɡʼan kidaniɡi raɡʼarab ʒo buɡiʃː ɡʔab
tsoɡi batʼijab χalqʼ buɡiʃː nuʒeda ɡʼadin tsʼaduɬan kʼaɬaleb allaɡʔasul ɡʔarakʔɡi raɡʼarab ɡʔjeb raɡʼun χadub tʃʼaɡoɡi χutʼarab
tsoniɡi allaɡʔ wukʼaniʃː tso χalqʼaɬul zulmujalda ʁorkʔ buɡeb tsoɡidab χalqʼ ʒindijeɡo batʃine watʃʼaraw nuʒedaɡo biχʔana ɡʔjes ritʃːaral kʼudijal balaɡʔalɡi ɡʔjesul χʼikmatalɡun muɡʼʒizatalɡi raʁɡi ʒindirɡo kʼudijab qʼudrataldaɬun ɡʔjes ɡʔarural χʼinqʼaral χʼalkʼoɬabiɡi ɡʔjeb kinabɡo ɡʔabuna betʼjerhan allaɡʔas misrijalda nuʒee ɡʼolo
nuʒeda ɡʔjeb kinabɡo biχʔizabuna betʼjerhan allaɡʔ tsoχʼo wukʼin wa ɡʔjew tun batʼijaw tsoɡi allaɡʔ ɡʔjetʃʼjewɬi nuʒeda ɬan bukʼine
ɡʔjes zobalazdasa ʒindirɡo ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼizabuna nuʒee waɡʼzaɬun bukʼine ɡʼodob rakʔalda ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo ɡutʃab tsʼa biχʔizabuna wa ɡʔjeb tsʼaduɬan nuʒeda kʼaɬana
betʼjerhanase rokʔana nuʒer umumul ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjes nuʒɡi tʼasa riʃːana wa misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃana ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo qʼuwataldaɬun ratʃana nuʒ ɡʔjenisa qʼwatʼire
nuʒedasa ɡʼjemerɡo qʼadar tsʼikʼkʼaral wa qʼuwatal χalqʼal nuʒer nuχdasaɡi ratsʼtsʼunaɡo ɡʔjezul rakʔazde nuʒɡi ratʃun ɡʔjel rakʔal nuʒee irsɬun kʔjeze ɡʼolo ɡʔjedin ɡʔabulebɡi buɡo
nuʒeda ɬaj wa kidaɡo rekʼjeɬ tsʼune betʼjerhan wuɡo zobalazulɡi rakʔaɬulɡi allaɡʔ ɡʔjew tun batʼijaw tsoɡi allaɡʔ ɡʔjetʃʼo
ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒeda maɬaral ɡʔjesul qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi tʼurazare betʼjerhan allaɡʔas abadijaɬeɡo nuʒee nasib ɡʔaburab rakʔalda nuʒeeɡi nuʒer naslabazeɡi χalatab wa barakatab ɡʼumru bukʼine
iordanaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda ɬabɡo ʃaɡʔar batʼa ɡʔabuna musatsa
rekʼjeɬ tsːinɡi ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo toχɬukʔje tʃi tʃʼwaraw insan ɡʔjezul tsojalde ɬutize wa ɡʔjeldaɬun ɡʔjesul ɡʼumru tsʼunun χutʼize
ɡʔale ɡʔjel ʃaɡʔaral ruwimilaze muɡʼrul tʼaɬijalda buɡeb betser ɡadilaze ɡilɡʼadalda buɡeb ramot manasːilaze baʃanalda buɡeb ɡolan
ɡʔale musatsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬe tsʼalarab qʼanun
ɡʔal qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi χʼukmabiɡi kʔuna musatsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬe ɡʔjez misri naqχa tarab meχaɬ
iordanaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχalda bet peoralda askʼor χeʃbonalda taχ ɬuraw amorijazul patʃa siχonil ulkajalda rukʼaɡo
misrijaldasa un χadub musatsaɡi ɡʼizrailazɡi berɡʔjenɬi bosana siχonida tʼad
wa ɡʔjesulɡi baʃanaɬul patʃa oɡilɡi kʼijawɡo amorijazul patʃajasul rukʼaral iordanaɬul baqʼbakːul raqχaɬul rakʔal kwerde rosana
arnonaɬul ɬaramuqχalda askʼob buɡeb aroɡʼjeraldasa baqχarab sirion χermon maɡʼarde ʃːwezeɡʼan ruɡel rakʔal kːola ɡʔjel
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔjezul kːolaan arawa raɬdaqχe tsʼamul raɬdaqχe ʃːwezeɡʼan wa ɡʔjenisaɡi un fasɡa meɡʼjeraɬul ʁulduqχe ʃːwezeɡʼan buɡeb iordan ɡʼurul tʼolabɡo baqʼbakːul raqχaɬul raɡʼalɬiɡi

musatsa tʼolabɡo χalqʼ bakʼarana wa abuna
ɡʼjenekːe ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒee tsʼalulel ruɡel qʼanunazuqχɡi amrabazuqχɡi ɬazare ɡʔjel wa muχʼkanɡo tʼurazare
χoriwalda rukʼaɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas niɬerɡun qʼotʼi ɡʔabuna
betʼjerhanas ɡʔab qʼotʼi tsoχʼo niɬer umumuzulɡun ɡʔabitʃʼo amma niɬɡun kinalɡo ɡʔanir eχetun ruɡel tʃʼaɡojalʃːinazulɡun ɡʔabuna
betʼjerhan kʼaɬana nuʒeda maɡʼardasa tsʼaduɬan badisa badiwe
dun nuʒedaɡi betʼjerhanasdaɡi ɡʔorkʔow tʃʼana wa dosul amrabi nuʒeda ritsana ʃːajɡureɬul nuʒ tsʼadukʔa χʼinqʼun maɡʼarde raχintʃʼjeɬul dos abuna
dun wuɡo dur betʼjerhan laʁɬun mun wukʼarab rakʔaldasa aj misrijaldasa mun qʼwatʼiwe watʃaraw dur allaɡʔ
dun tun batʼijal allaɡʔzabi dur rukʼine beɡʔularo
dujeɡo χanɬi laʁɬijaɬe ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔ ɡʔabuɡe tʼad zobalazda buɡeɬul jaɡi ɡʼodob rakʔalda buɡeɬul raɬdaɬ jaɡi rakʔuɬ buɡeɬul kinabɡʼaɡi sipat surat ɡʔabuɡe
ɡʔjezije suʒdaɡun tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabuɡe dun dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔɬidal χilipɬi χʼjeχʔolarew
amma dun wokʔulezul wa dir amrabi tʼurazarulezul naslabaze ɡʔjezul azarabilel ɡʼjelazde ɡʼuntʼunɡi raχʼmatal rikʔulew
betʼjerhanasul durɡo allaɡʔasul tsʼar baqχuɡe ɡʼadada kʼwar ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo
ʃamatqʼojaɬul adab ɡʔabe betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjeb χirijab qʼoɬun tsʼune
anɬɡo qʼojaɬ χʼaltʼje wa tʼolalɡo durɡo iʃal tʼurazare
amma ankʔabileb qʼo ɡʔjeb kːola betʼjerhan allaɡʔase batʼa ɡʔaburab ʃamatqʼo ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ dutsa kinab buɡoniɡi χʼaltʼi ɡʔabuɡe ja dutsa ja dur wasas jaɡi jasaɬ ja dur laʁas jaɡi laʁaɬ ja dur χʼajwanaɬ ja dur ʃaɡʔaralda tʃʼjel ɡʔaburaw qʼwatʼisa watʃʼaraw tʃijas bitʃːante dutsaɡo ɡʼadin χʼalχʔi ɡʔabize dur laʁasɡi ʁarawaʃaɬɡi
kʼotʃonɡe munɡoɡi misrijaɬul rakʔalda laʁɬun wukʼarabɬi wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ʒindirɡo qʼudrataldaɬun wa χʼalkʼoɬijaldaɬun mun ɡʔjenisa naqχe watʃarabɬi ɡʔjedinɬidal betʼjerhan allaɡʔas amru ɡʔabuleb buɡo ʃamatqʼojaɬul qʼimat ɡʔabejan
durɡo insulɡi ebelaɬulɡi adab qχatir ɡʔabe betʼjerhan allaɡʔas duje kʔurab rakʔalda durɡo ɡʼumru χalatab wa barakatab bukʼine
tʃi tʃʼwaɡe
zina ɡʔabuɡe
tsʼoɡʔ ɡʔabuɡe
ɡʔjeresinuɡʼɬi ɡʔabuɡe
tʃijar ɬadude χʔul ɬoɡe tʃijar ruqʼalde χʔul ɬoɡe ɡʔjesul laʁasde jaɡi laʁalde tʃijar otsalde jaɬuni χʼamide ʃːibɡʼaɡi tʃijar ʒojalde χʔul ɬoɡe
betʼjerhanas ɡʔal amrabi kʔuna tʼolabɡo nuʒer ʒamaɡʼataɬe tsʼadukʔan nakʼkʼukʔan wa laχʼtʃʼjeɡʼjerab betsʼɬuda ɡʔorkʔosan kʼudijab ɡʔarkʔidaɬunɡi kʼaɬan ɡʔal raɡʼabazda tʼade ɡʔjes tʼokʼaɬ ʃːibɡo ʒubatʃʼo χadub ɡʔjes ɡʔjel qχwana kʼiɡo ɡantʃʼil qʼonojalda tʼad wa diqχe kʔuna
betsʼab nakʼkʼukʔan ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼidal wa tsʼaduɬ bosarab meɡʼjer biχʔidal nuʒer qʼawmazul butʼrulɡi nuʒer kʼudijalɡi ratʃʼana diqχe
ɡʔjez dida abuna betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ʒindirɡo retsːɡi kʼodoɬiɡi biχʔizabuna niʒeda tsʼaduɬan kʼaɬaleb ɡʔjesul ɡʔarakʔɡi raɡʼana ʒaqʼa niʒeda ɬana allaɡʔasul ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼaniɡi insan tʃʼaɡo χutʼize beɡʔulewɬi
ʃːajχa niʒ χweze kːolel tsodaɡʔabɡi dob ɡʔarkʔiqχ niʒ ɡʼjenekːani dob ɡʼasijab tsʼajaɬ niʒer raqχu ɬuɡʔinabila wa niʒ χwela
kidaniɡi bukʼarab ʒo buɡiʃː ɡʔab niʒeda ɡʼadin χʼaqʼaw allaɡʔasul ɡʔarakʔɡi raɡʼun χadub insan tʃʼaɡo χutʼarab
munɡo a betʼjerhan allaɡʔasuqχe ɡʔjes abulebʃːinaɬuqχ ɡʼjenekːe wa χadub ɡʔjeb niʒeda bitse niʒ duqχ ɡʼjenekːila wa kinabɡo tʼubazabila
betʼjerhanasda raɡʼana nuʒetsa dida bitsarab raɡʼi wa ɡʔjes dida abuna ɡʔjeb χalqʼaɬ bitsuneb ʒo dida raɡʼana bitʼun abuleb buɡo ɡʔjez
unɡo unɡoɬunɡi ɡʔjel kidaɡo χʼinqʼulelani dikʔan dir amrabiɡi ɡʔjez tʼurazarulelani ɡʔjezijeɡi ɡʔjezul ɬimalazeɡi mirkaɬɡo ɬikʼ bukʼinaan
wiɬːa ʒiderɡo tʃadrazuqχe rusːajan abe ɡʔjezda
munin abuni ɡʔaniw dunɡun wukʼa ditsa duda ritsina kinalɡo dutsa ɡʔjezda maɬize kːolel qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi χʼukmabiɡi bitʃːante ditsa ɡʔjezije kʔurab rakʔalda ɡʔjez ɡʔjeb kinabɡo tʼubazabize
nuʒetsa tʼadtʃʼun tʼurazare betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔural amrabi ja kwaranab ja kweɡʼab raqχalde kʔuritʃʼoɡo
nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒeda biχʔizaburab nuχkːun χʔwade ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nuʒer ɡʼumruɡi χalaɬila barakatɡi bukʼina nuʒee ʃːweze buɡeb rakʔalda

ɡʔale betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒeda maɬejan dida tʼadqʼaral nuʒerɬun bukʼine buɡeb rakʔalde ʃːwedal nuʒetsa tʼurazarize kːolel qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nuʒɡi nuʒer ɬimalɡi ɡʔjezulɡi ɬimalɡi ɡʼumrujaɬɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼila ditsa nuʒeda maɬaral ɡʔjesul qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi nuʒetsa tʼurazarila wa ɡʔjeldaɬun nuʒer ɡʼumruɡi χalaɬila
ɡʼjenekːe ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ tʼadtʃʼun tʼubazabe ɡʔab kinabɡo tsinɡi nuʒeeɡi ɬikʼ bukʼina wa nuʒer umumuz iman ɬuraw betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔurab raɡʼuda reqʼon raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb rakʔalda nuʒer χalqʼɡi kutakalda ɡʼjemerɬila
ɡʼjenekːe ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ niɬer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wuɡo tsoχʼoɡo tso wuɡew betʼjerhan
durɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔ χiraɬe rakʼ rakʼaɬ tʼolabɡo ruχʼaldaɬun wa qʼuwat ʒanaldaɬun
ʒaqʼa ditsa duje kʔural amrabi kidaɡo rekʼjeɬ tsʼune
tʼadtʃʼun durɡo ɬimalazdaɡi maɬe kidaɡo takrar ɡʔare ɡʔjel roqʼor ɡʼodor tʃʼun rukʼaɡoɡi qʼwatʼir saparalda rukʼaɡoɡi kʔiʒuleb meχaɬɡi tʼade raqχuneb meχaɬɡi
rakʼalde ʃːwejaɬul ɡʼalamat χʼisabalda kwerda ruχʔje ɡʔjel ɡʔjedinɡo nadaldaɡi ruχʔje
durɡo ruqʼaɬul nutsʼil raχazdaɡi ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabazdaɡi qχwaj ɡʔjel
dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔas mun watʃina duje kʔjelin ɡʔjedarab ulkajalde dur umumuze aj ibraɡʔimijeɡi isχʼaqʼijeɡi jaqʼubijeɡi ɡʔjes ɡʔjedinab raɡʼi kʔun bukʼindal ɡʔjenir ruɡo dutsa ɡʼutsʼitʃʼjel kʼudijal ɡʔajbatal ʃaɡʔaral
dutsa bakʼaritʃʼjeb betʃeɬijaɬul tsʼural ruqʼzal dutsa ruqχitʃʼjel ʁujal dutsa tʃʼjetʃʼjel tsʼolbol aχalɡi zajtunaɬul awlaqχalɡi ɡʔjenib duje ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwen bukʼina
amma woreχa munɡo misrijaɬul laʁɬijaldasa naqχe watʃaraw betʼjerhan kʼotʃonɡe
durɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼa tsoχʼo ɡʔjesije tʼaɡʼat ɡʔabe wa ɡʔa ɡʔjeduleɬul ɡʔjesul tsʼar ɡuroni baqχuɡe
batʼijal allaɡʔzabazda naqχ riɬːunɡe sweruqχ ruɡel χalqʼazul allaɡʔzabazdeɡi rusːunɡe
ʃːajɡureɬul nuʒɡun wuɡew betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wuɡo χilipɬi χʼjeχʔolarew allaɡʔ ɡʔjesul tsːin ɡʔalaɡɬitʃʼoɡo bukʼine nuʒɡi dunjalaldasaɡo tʼaɡʼinaritʃʼoɡo rukʼine
masːajalda ɡʼadin nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul χʼalal riχʔuɡe
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔural qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi χʼukmabiɡi tʼadtʃʼun tʼurazare
betʼjerhanasda bertsin biχʔulebʃːinab ɡʔabe ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nuʒeeɡi ɬikʼ bukʼina betʼjerhanas nuʒee kʔjelin nuʒer umumuzeɡo ɡʔa barab ɡʔajbatab ulkajalde ʃːwela nuʒ wa ɡʔjeb mukʼur ɡʔabila
ɡʔjes tuʃbabi nuʒeda tseresa naqχe ʁela betʼjerhanas ɡʔjedin abun bukʼindal
χadubkːun dur naslabazul ɬimalaz tsʼjeχani betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔural ɡʔal qʼanunazulɡi amrabazulɡi aχʼkamazulɡi maɡʼna ʃːib in
dutsa abe niʒ rukʼana misrijalda pirɡʼawnasul laʁzalɬun betʼjerhanas ʒindirɡo qʼudrataldaɬun naqχe ratʃana niʒ ɡʔjenisa
misrijaldeɡi pirɡʼawnasdeɡi ɡʔjesul tʼolabɡo ɡʼaɡarɬijaldeɡi balaɡʔ reʃːtʼinabural kʼudijal muɡʼʒizatalɡi ɡʼalamatalɡi riχʔizaruna betʼjerhanas niʒer berda tsere
niʒin abuni ɡʔjes ɡʔjenisa naqχe ratʃana niʒer umumuzeɡo raɡʼi kʔun bukʼarab ɡʔab rakʔ niʒee nasib ɡʔabize ɡʼolo
betʼjerhanas niʒede amru ɡʔabuna ɡʔal kinalɡo qʼanunal tʼurazarejan betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul adab ɡʔabejan wa ɡʔjesukʔa χʼinqʼajan niɬee ɬikʼ bukʼinaɬe wa niɬer ɡʼumru tsʼunijaɬe ɡʼolo ʒaqʼaɡi ɡʔjedin buɡo
allaɡʔ niɬeda razi wukʼina betʼjerhanas abuqχe niɬetsa ɡʔal kinalɡo amrabi tʼurazaruni

betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒ dob rakʔalde ʃːwezarila wa ɡʔjenir ruɡel ɡʼjemeral χalqʼal naqχe qʼotʼila χitijalɡi ɡirɡaʃijalɡi amorijalɡi χanaanijalɡi perizijalɡi χiwijalɡi jewusijalɡi nuʒedasa rikʼkʼjen ɡʼjemerab wa qʼuwatab ankʔɡo χalqʼ
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔjel nuʒer kwerde kʔurab meχaɬ wa nuʒetsa ɡʔjezda tʼad berɡʔjenɬi bosarab meχaɬ ɡʔjel χerem
ɡʔjezulɡun riɡʔnalɡi ɡʔaruɡe nuʒerɡo jasal ɡʔjezul wasaze rosːabaze kʔoɡe ɡʔjezul jasal nuʒerɡo wasaze ɬudbiɬunɡi ratʃunɡe
ɡuroni ɡʔjez nuʒer wasal dir nuχdasaɡi qʼosinarun batʼijal allaɡʔzabaze tʼaɡʼat ɡʔabijalde tsʼaze ruɡo wa betʼjerhanasul ɡʔalaɡab tsːinɡi reʃːtʼun nuʒɡi qʼoqʼab zamanalda ʒanir tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡo
ɡʔale nuʒetsa ɡʔabize kːoleb ʒo ɡʔjezul qʼurbanazul bakʼal riχːizare dinijal ɡantʃʼal ʁure aʃeral χʼubal qʼotʼje wa ɡʔjezul ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔzabi tsʼaduɬ ruχʼje
nuʒ betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ʒindijeɡo batʼa ɡʔaburab χalqʼɬidal betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼolɡo dunjalaɬul χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼasa riʃːun ruɡo nuʒ ɡʔjesul χirijab χalqʼɬun wa qʼimatal irsilalɬun ɡʔarize
tsoɡidab χalqʼaldasa rikʼkʼjen ɡʼjemeral rukʼinaɬ ɡuro betʼjerhanase nuʒ χiraɬaral wa tʼasa riʃːaral ɡʔjeɬul ɡʼaksalda tsoɡidal χalqʼazda dande kːun nuʒer χalqʼaɬul qʼadar buɡo biʃːun daɡʔab
amma betʼjerhanas ʒindirɡo qʼudratab kweraldaɬun misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃana nuʒ laʁɬijaldasa χwasarɡi ɡʔarun wa misrijaɬul patʃa pirɡʼawnasul kwerʃːalikʔa rortʃʼizaruna nuʒ bitʃase χirijal rukʼun wa nuʒer umumuze kʔurab raɡʼi kːweze bokʔun
kidaɡo kʼotʃon toɡe dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wukʼin χʼaqʼaw allaɡʔ ɡʔjew wuɡo ritʼuqχaw allaɡʔ ɡʔjew wokʔulezul wa ɡʔjesul amrabiɡi tʼurazarulezul naslabaze ɡʔjezul azarabileb ɡʼjelalde ɡʼuntʼunɡi raχʼmujaɬul qʼotʼi tsʼunulew
amma ɡʔjew riχaraze ɡʼaʒal qχwala ɡʔjes
naqχ baqχitʃʼoɡo ʒaza ɡʔabula ɡʔjedinaze
palχʼasil ditsa ʒaqʼa nuʒee kʔural amrabiɡi qʼanunalɡi χʼukmabiɡi tsʼunun χʔwade
nuʒ ɡʔal qʼanunazuqχ ɡʼjenekːani wa nuʒetsa ɡʔjel muχʼkanɡo tʼurazarulel ruɡoni nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔasɡi tʼubazabila ʒindirɡo raχʼmu tsʼobaɬul qʼotʼi nuʒer umumuze kʔurab raɡʼuda reqʼon
ɡʔjesije χirijal rukʼina nuʒ ɡʔjes barakat ɬela nuʒeda wa rikʼkʼjen ɡʼjemerab kʼudijab χalqʼɬun ɡʔarila nuʒ ɡʔjes nuʒee ɡʼjemeral ɬimal kʔjela ɡʔarzajab χʼaluqχen kʔjela tsʼibaqχarab tʃaʁirɡi zajtunaɬul naχɡi kʔjela botsʼuje batʃal ɡʼjemeral ɡʔarila ɡʼi tsʼanazul reqχaɬ burtʼal wa kʔaɡʼi ɡʼjemerɬila nuʒer umumuze raɡʼi kʔurab rakʔalda ɡʔjedin bukʼine buɡo nuʒee
nuʒee ɡʼadin riqʼzi bitʼarab χalqʼ tʼokʼaɬ tsoniɡi bukʼinaro ɬimal ɡʔarularew biχʔintʃi jaɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor rukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo tsoniɡi χʼorab ʒo ɡʼi botsʼuda ɡʔorkʔobɡi bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo
betʼjerhanas kinalɡo untabi tʼasa rosila nuʒedasa misrijaɬul kweʃal untabi nuʒeda ɬala ɡʔjel ritʃːalaro nuʒeda tʼade ɡʔjel ritʃːala nuʒer tuʃbabazde
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒer kwerʃːalikʔje kʔural kinalɡo χalqʼal nuʒetsa tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjezda ɡurχʼize beɡʔularo wa ɡʔjezul allaɡʔzabaze tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadatɡi ɡʔabize beɡʔularo ɡuroni ɡʔjeb nuʒeeɡo ʁurab qʼorɬun bukʼine buɡo
nuʒeda rakʼalda kːeze beɡʔula ɡʔal niʒedasaɡi qʼuwatal χalqʼal ruɡo kin niʒeqχa baʒarileb ɡʔal naqχe qʼotʼun in
nuʒ ɡʔjezukʔa χʼinqʼuɡe rakʼalde ʃːwezabe betʼjerhanas pirɡʼawnaseɡi tʼolabɡo misrijaɬeɡi ɡʔaburab
nuʒerɡo berazda biχʔana dob meχaɬ ɡʔjes ritʃːaral kʼudijal balaɡʔalɡi ɡʔjesul χʼikmatalɡi muɡʼʒizatalɡi ɡʔjenisa qʼwatʼire nuʒ ratʃaraw betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul qʼuwatab kwerɡi qʼudratɡi ɡʔjebɡo ɡʔabize buɡo ɡʔanʒe nuʒ χʼinqʼun ruɡel kinalɡo tsoɡidal χalqʼazeɡi
kʔuʒnajal ritʃːaze ruɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔjezda tʼade nuʒedasa raχtʃun tʃʼaɡo χutʼaraltsin χwezarize
χʼinqʼuɡe ɡʔjezukʔa ʃːajɡureɬul nuʒ tsʼunulew betʼjerhan allaɡʔ kːola qʼudrataw wa χʼinqʼi kʔolew allaɡʔ
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒeda tseresan tso tsokːun ɡʔjel χalqʼal naqχe qʼotʼila kinalɡo tsadaqχ ʁurize beɡʔulareɬul nuʒeda sweruqχ ɡʼalχul ʒanawaral ɡʼjemerɬize ɡurilan
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔjel χalqʼazda tʼad berɡʔjenɬi kʔjela nuʒee riχːa χotʃizarila wa ʁurila ɡʔjel
ɡʔjes ɡʔjezul patʃazabi nuʒer kwerde kʔjeze ruɡo wa nuʒetsa ɡʔjezul tsʼaraltsin dunjalaldasa naqχe qχwaɡʼaze ruɡo ɬidaniɡi baʒarize ɡʔjetʃʼo nuʒeda dande tʃʼun nuʒetsa kinalɡo tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡo
ɡʔjezul allaɡʔzabazul sipat suratal nuʒetsa tsʼa ʁun ruχʼize kːola ɡʔjezda tʼad bekʔarab ɡʼarats mesedalde kwer beɡʔuɡe ɡuroni ɡʔjeb nuʒee qʼorɬun kːeze buɡo nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔase kutakalda riχarab ʒo buɡo ɡʔjeb
qχubab riχarab ʒo nuʒerɡo roqʼobe ʒanibe bosuɡe ɡuroni nuʒɡi ɡʔjeb ʒojalda tsadaqχ χerem ɡʔarize ruɡo ɡʔjedinal ʒalazdasa tsʼune nuʒɡo ɡʔjel tʼuran tʼaɡʼinarize kːola

tʼadtʃʼun tʼubazabe ditsa ʒaqʼa nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb allaɡʔasul ʃːibab amru nuʒer ɡʼumruɡi tsʼunize χalqʼɡi tsʼikʼkʼine bukʼine tsinɡi betʼjerhanas nuʒee kʔjelin nuʒer umumuze ɡʔa barab rakʔalde ɬuɡʔina nuʒ wa ɡʔjeb mukʼur ɡʔabila
nuʒeda kʼotʃonɡe nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʼiqʼoɡo sonaɬ nuʒ ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχaldasan saparalda ratʃarab kuts nuʒer χʼalbiχʔizeɡi nuʒ mutʼiɡʼ ɡʔarizeɡi rekʼjeɬ buɡeb ɬazabizeɡi ɡʼolo ɡʔabuna ɡʔjeb nuʒetsa ɡʔjesul amrabi tʼurazaruliʃːali balaɡʔize
ɡʔjes nuʒ kweʁana raqʼijaɬ kʼwekʼun χadub nuʒeda jaɡi nuʒer umumuzda tsebe biχʔa raɡʼitʃʼjeb mannaɡi kʔun χʔiχʔana ɡʔjes nuʒeda biχʔizabuna tsoχʼo tʃed χinkʼaldaɬun ɡurew insan tʃʼaɡo wukʼunebɬi insanase tʃʼaɡoɬi betʼjerhanasul kʼaldisan batʃʼarab ʃːibab raɡʼudasan bukʼunebɬi
kʼiqʼojabɡo sonaɬ nuʒer retʼjel basraɬitʃʼo χʼatʼalɡi ɡʔorotʃʼo
bitʃʼtʃʼa nuʒeda betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒeda maɬula insanas ʒindirɡo wasasda maɬuleb ɡʼadin
betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrabi tsʼune ɡʔjesul nuχkːun χʔwade wa ɡʔjesukʔa χʼinqʼa
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒ ratʃina ɡʔajbatab ulkajalde ɡʼoralɡi tʃwaχuleb ɬadal χʼawuzalɡi ruɡeb ɡʼatʼirakʔazdaɡun muɡʼruzda itsːalɡi tʃwaχuleb
roɬɡi purtʃʼinaɡi ɡʔarzajab ulkajalde ɡʔjedinɡo tsʼibilɡi inʒirɡi sonoɡʼjetʃɡi ɡʔarzajab zajtunaɬul ʁutʼbiɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi ɡʼjemerab rakʔalde
ɡʔjenib tʃadil muqʼsanɬi bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo wa ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwen bukʼine buɡo nuʒee ɡʼolareb ʒo ɡʔjenib ʃːibɡo bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡantʃʼiɬ maχː buɡo ɡʔjenib kʔurabaɬan mazɡarɡun paχʔ baqχize beɡʔula
ɡʔjenir ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwanaleb meχaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔase retsː ɡʔabe ɡʔjes nuʒee kʔurab barakatab rakʔaɬuqχ
woreɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔ kʼotʃonɡe ditsa ʒaqʼa nuʒee kʔural ɡʔjesul qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi χʼukmabiɡi tʼurazare
nuʒee ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwanaze ʒoɡi ʃːwarab ɬikʼal minabiɡi ran nuʒ ɡʔjenireɡi raqχarab wa
ɡʼi botsʼiɡi ɡʼarats mesedɡi tsoɡidab betʃeɬiɡi ɡʼjemerɬarab meχaɬ
nuʒer ɡʼamal kʼodoɬuɡe wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔ kʼotʃon toɡe ɡʔjesɬidal nuʒ misrijaldasa nuʒer laʁɬijaldasa χwasar ɡʔarural
wa zaɡʔrujal borχʔazulɡi itʃʼkʼalazulɡi tsʼurab χʼinqʼi tsʼikʼkʼarab salul awlaqχaldasan wa baqʼwarab tʃʼoboɡojab rakʔaldasan nuʒ tsere ratʃaral nuʒee ɡʼolo ɡʔjes kʔuruɬa qʼwatʼibe ɬim batʃʼinabuna
wa baqʼwarab awlaqχalda nuʒer umumuzda biχʔa raɡʼitʃʼjeb manna kʔuna kwanaze ɡʔjes nuʒ kweʁulel rukʼana wa χʼalal riχʔulel rukʼana χadubkːun nuʒee ɬikʼɬi paraχaɬi bukʼinaɬul muradalda
nuʒeda kːoɡe ɡʔjeb kinabɡo betʃeɬi nuʒerɡo baʒarijaldaɬun ʃːwarab buɡin
betʼjerhan allaɡʔ kʼotʃonɡe ɡʔjesin nuʒee riqʼzi kʔoleb buɡeb ʒaqʼa qʼojalde ʃːwezeɡʼanɡi nuʒer umumulɡun ɡʔaburab ʒindirɡo qʼotʼi tsʼunijaɬe ɡʼolo
amma nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔɡi kʼotʃon tani tsoɡidal allaɡʔzabazda naqχɡi riɬːun ɡʔjezije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadatɡi ɡʔabuni ɡʔale ditsa nuʒeda ɬazabuleb buɡo tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo nuʒ χweze ruɡo
nuʒ nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasuqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼoni nuʒee rakʔal kʔjejaɬe ɡʼolo betʼjerhanas tʼaɡʼinarize qχwaral χalqʼal ɡʼadin nuʒɡi χwezarize ruɡo

ɡʼjenekːe ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ ɡʔanʒe dutsa
ɡʔjezul ɡʼadamal ruɡo zalimal wa qʼuwatal anakil naslu duda ɬala ɡʔjel wa duda ɡʼjemer raɡʼana anakilazda dande tʃʼun ɬiqχa baʒarulebilan ɡʔjezul raqχaɬ bitsuneb
amma duda ɬan bukʼa ʒiwɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔ unew wukʼin duda tsewe tsewe tsebe batanʃːinab kʼkʼuneb borkʔarab tsʼa ɡʼadin ɡʔjes ʁurize ruɡo ɡʔjel wa duje berɡʔjenɬi kʔjeze buɡo wa betʼjerhanasul raɡʼuda reqʼon dutsa kwerde bosize buɡo ɡʔjezul rakʔ ɡʔjelɡi arab bakʼ ɬatʃʼoɡo χeχɡo tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡo
dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔjel duda tseresa qʼotʼidal duda rakʼalde kːoɡe niʒer ritʼuqχɬijaɬuqχ ratʃana betʼjerhanas niʒ ɡʔanire ɡʔab rakʔ niʒee kʔjeze ɡʼolo jan ɡʔjel χalqʼazul kapurɬi sababɬunin betʼjerhanas ɡʔjel duda tseresa naqχe aχʼizeqχin ruɡel
dur ritʼuqχal iʃazdaɬun jaɬuni dur rekʼjeɬ kutakab iman jaχʼ bukʼun ɡureb dutsa ɡʔjezul rakʔazda χanɬi ɡʔabizeqχin buɡeb betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔoleb buɡo ɡʔjezul rakʔ duje ɡʔjezul kweʃɬi sababɬun wa dur umumuze aj ibraɡʔimijeɡi isχʼaqʼijeɡi jaqʼubijeɡi ɡʔjes kʔurab raɡʼi bukʼun
palχʼasil duda ɬan bukʼa mun ritʼuqχab bukʼinaɬ ɡureb betʼjerhan allaɡʔas duje dob ɡʔajbatab rakʔ kʔoleb buɡeb χʼaqʼiqʼatalda mun buɡo rakʼ bitsːatab χalqʼ
kidaniɡi kʼotʃonɡe ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχalda rukʼaɡo kiɡʼan nuʒetsa tsːin baqχinabuleb bukʼarabali betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul misri taraldasa naqχe ʒaqʼa qʼojalde ʃːwezeɡʼanɡi nuʒetsa betʼjerhanasuqχ ɡʼin tʼamitʃʼo
χoriwalda nuʒetsa baqχinaburab tsːidal kutakaɬ betʼjerhanas nuʒ tʼaɡʼinarizeqχin rukʼana
ɡantʃʼil qʼanal aj betʼjerhanas niɬerɡun ɡʔaburab qʼotʼijaɬul qʼanal rosize maɡʼarde tʼade waχarab meχaɬ ditsa ɡʔjenib bana kʼiqʼoɡo sordo qʼo kwenɡi kwanatʃʼoɡo ɬimɡi ɡʔjeqʼetʃʼoɡo
ɡʔjenib betʼjerhanas kʼiɡo ɡantʃʼil qʼono kʔuna diqχe ɡʔjezda tʼad allaɡʔasul kilʃːitsa qχwan bukʼana ʒamaɡʼataɬul dandeɬi aχʼarab qʼojaɬ maɡʼardasa tsʼaduda ɡʔorkʔosa betʼjerhanas nuʒeda aburabʃːinab ʒo
kʼiqʼoɡo sordo qʼojaldasan betʼjerhanas kʼiɡo ɡantʃʼil qʼono kʔuna diqχe qʼotʼijaɬul qʼanal
betʼjerhanas dida abuna χeχɬi ɡʔabun maɡʼardasa ʁorkʔje reʃːtʼa dutsa misrijaldasa qʼwatʼibe batʃarab χalqʼ pasaɬun buɡo kiɡʼan χeχɡoχa ɡʔjel ditsa maɬarab nuχdasa tararal mesedil biun tʼurab basi ɡʔabuna ɡʔjez ʒideeɡo tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadataɬe
wa betʼjerhanas dida abuna χʼaqʼiqʼataldaɡi dida biχʔuleb buɡo ɡʔjeb bukʼin rakʼ bitsːatab χalqʼ
bitʃːante ditsa ɡʔjel χwezarize wa arab bakʼ ɬatʃʼoɡo dunjalaldasaɡo tʼaɡʼinarize χadub ditsa dudasan ɬuɡʔinabila ɡʔjezdasaɡi qʼadar tsʼikʼkʼarab wa qʼuwatab χalqʼ
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ dun tsʼaduɬ bosarab maɡʼardasa ʁorkʔje wiɬːana kodob kːun qʼotʼijaɬul kʼiɡo qʼonoɡi bukʼana
wa dida biχʔana χʼaqʼiqʼataldaɡi biun tʼurab basiɡi ɡʔabun nuʒetsa betʼjerhanasda dande munaɡʔ ɡʔabun bukʼin ɡʔjediɡʼanɡi χeχɡo tarana nuʒ betʼjerhanas maɬarab nuχdasa
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsa kʼijabɡo qʼono nuʒer berazda tsebe ɡʼodobɡi retʃʼtʃʼun bekana
χaduw dun naqχeɡi betʼjerhanasda tsewe kʼalaʁorkʔje kːana wa ɡʔjedin wukʼana kʼiqʼoɡo sordo qʼojaɬ tsebeseb nuχalda ɡʼadin kwenɡi kwanatʃʼoɡo ɬimɡi ɡʔjeqʼetʃʼoɡo betʼjerhanasda riχarab ʒoɡi ɡʔabun kːarab nuʒer kweʃab munaɡʔaɬ betʼjerhanasul tsːin baqχinabun bukʼun
dun kweʃɡo χʼinqʼun wukʼana betʼjerhanasul tsːidakʔa ɡʔjeb tsːidal χʼalutsinaɬ ɡʔjes nuʒ tʼaɡʼinarizeqχin rukʼindal amma betʼjerhanas ɡʔjebmeχaɬɡi dir ɡʔari qʼabul ɡʔabuna
ɡʔarunideɡi betʼjerhanasul tsːin bukʼana ɡʔjew bitʼaqχe tʃʼwazeqχin wukʼana amma ditsa ɡʔarunijeɡi duɡʼa ɡʔabuna
nuʒer munaɡʔin abuni aj nuʒetsa ɡʔaburab basi ditsa tsʼaduɬeɡi reχun biinabuna χadub χʼur ɬuɡʔineɡʼan qχurun maɡʼardasa ʁorkʔje tʃwaχuleb ɬeɬe bana
ɡʔjedinɡo nuʒetsa tawerajaldaɡi masːajaldaɡi kiwrot ɡʔataawajaldaɡi betʼjerhanasul tsːin baqχinabuna
kadeʃ barneajaldasa nuʒ qʼwatʼire ritʼulaɡo betʼjerhanas abuna raqχa ditsa nuʒee kʔurab rakʔalda kwerʃːel ɡʔabe jan amma nuʒetsa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrujalda dandetʃʼjej ɡʔabuna nuʒ ɡʔjesda boʒitʃʼo ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼo
dida ɬaraldasa naqχe nuʒ betʼjerhanase mutʼiɡʼɬitʃʼo
betʼjerhanas nuʒ tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡin aburab meχalda kʼiqʼoɡo sordo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanasda tsewe kʼalaʁorkʔje kːana dun
