wa ɡʔarana ɡʔjesda oɡʔ χʼalkʼolew betʼjerhan tʼaɡʼinabuɡe durɡo χalqʼ durɡo irs durɡo χʼalkʼoɬijaldaɬun wa qʼudrataldaɬun dutsa χwasar ɡʔaruna wa misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃana ɡʔjel
durɡo laʁzal ibraɡʔimɡi isχʼaqʼɡi jaqʼubɡi rakʼalde ʃːwezare ɡʔazul rakʼazul soɡʼɬijaɬuqχɡi ɡʔazul munaɡʔazuqχɡi ɡʔazda kːarab ɡʼajibaɬuqχɡi walaɡʔuɡe ja allaɡʔ
ɡuroni dutsa durɡo χalqʼ naqχe batʃarab ulkajaɬul tʃaɡʼaz abize buɡo balaɡʔje betʼjerhanasda baʒarun ɡʔjetʃʼo ʒintsaɡo ratʃun ʃːwezarize raɡʼi kʔurab rakʔalde dol ratʃine ʒindaɡo ɡʼjemeral riχijaɬ ratʃun rukʼun ruɡo dos dol ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχalda χwezarize jan
amma ɡʔab χalqʼ dur irsɬidal durɡo χʼalkʼoɬijaldaɬun wa qʼudrataldaɬun dutsa erken ɡʔaburab

ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanas dida abuna kʼiɡo qʼono bekʼkʼje dol tsere rukʼaral qʼanazda reɬːarab wa diqχe maɡʼarde tʼade watʃʼa ɡʔjedinɡo tsʼulal ʁamasɡi ɡʔabe
ditsa ɡʔjel qʼanazda qχwala dol dutsa rekaral tʼotseresel qʼanazda rukʼaral raɡʼabi wa dutsa ɡʔjel qʼotʼijaɬul ʁansida ʒanir ɬela
ditsa akatsijaɬul tsʼulal ʁamasɡi ɡʔabuna tsere rukʼarazda reɬːaral qʼanalɡi rekʼkʼana wa ɡʔjelɡi rosun maɡʼarde tʼade waχana
betʼjerhanas tsebeχunɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjezda tʼadɡi qχwana nuʒer ʒamaɡʼataɬe maɡʼarda tʼad tsʼaduda ɡʔorkʔosa kʔun bukʼarab antsʼɡo amru wa betʼjerhanas ɡʔjel diqχe kʔuna
tsinɡi dun maɡʼardasa ʁorkʔje wiɬːana wa ɡʔjel ditsaɡo ɡʔaburab ʁansida ʒanir ɬuna ɡʔanʒeɡi ɡʔjenir ruɡo ɡʔjel ɡʔjedin amru ɡʔabuna dide betʼjerhanas
beerot bene jaakanaldasa ɡʼizrailal ana moserajalde ɡʔjeniw ɡʔarun χwana wa ɡʔjeniwɡo χabaɬɡi wuqʼana ɡʔarunil bakʼalda ɡʔjesul was eleazar tana kaʃiʃɬun
ɡʔjenisa ɡʔjel ana ɡudɡodalde ɡudɡodaldasa itsːal ɡʼjemerab jotbatajalde
dob zamanalda betʼjerhanas kinalɡo qʼawmazda ɡʔorkʔosa lewijil qʼawm batʼa ɡʔabuna wa ɡʔjezda tʼad qʼana betʼjerhanasul qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas batʃːize ɡʔjedinɡo betʼjerhanasda tsere tʃʼun kaʃiʃɬi ɡʔabize wa ɡʔjesul tsʼaraldaɬun χalqʼaɬe duɡʼa ɡʔabize ʒaqʼa qʼojaɬɡi ɡʔjeb ɡʔjedin buɡo
ɡʔjedinɬidalin lewitaze tsoɡidal qʼawmaze ɡʼadin rakʔazul butʼabi kʔjetʃʼjel betʼjerhan allaɡʔas aburalda reqʼon betʼjerhan ʒiwɡo wuɡo ɡʔjezul butʼaɡi ɡʔjezul irsɡi
tsebeseb nuχaɬ ɡʼadin kʼiqʼoɡo qʼoɡi kʼiqʼoɡo sordoɡi bana ditsa maɡʼarda wa betʼjerhanas dir ɡʔari qʼabul ɡʔabuna ɡʔab nuχaɬɡi betʼjerhanas nuʒ χwezaritʃʼoɡo tana
betʼjerhanas dida abuna waqχa χalqʼ tsebe batʃe bitʃːante ɡʔjezul umumuze dun ɡʔjedarab rakʔ ɡʔjez kwerde bosize
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ʃːib dudasa tʼalab ɡʔabuleb buɡeb ɡʔjes tʼalab ɡʔabuleb buɡo mun betʼjerhan allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼi ɡʔjesul nuχda bitʼun χʔwadi ɡʔjew duje χiraɬi ɡʔjesije dutsa rakʼ rakʼaɬɡo tʼolabɡo ruχʼaldaɬun wa qʼuwat ʒanaldaɬun tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabi wa
dujeɡo ɬikʼ bukʼinaɬe ɡʼolo ʒaqʼa ditsa kʔural ɡʔjesul amrabiɡi qʼanunalɡi dutsa tsʼuni
dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul kːola zobalɡi zobalazul zobalɡi ɡʔab dunjalɡi dunjalalda buɡebʃːinabɡi
amma betʼjerhanase nuʒer umumul χiraɬana wa tʼolalɡo χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔosa nuʒ ɡʔjezul naslabi tʼasa riʃːana ɡʔjedin buɡo ʒaqʼaɡi
nuʒerɡo rakʼal tʼjeren ɡʔare
ʃːajɡureɬul nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wuɡeɬul allaɡʔzabazulɡi allaɡʔ betʼjerɡʔanzabazulɡi betʼjerɡʔan χʼalkʼoɬi tsʼikʼkʼaraw qʼudrataw χʼinqʼun ruχʼ bosizabulew ɡʔurmaqχ tsʼaruqχ balaɡʔularew riʃwat bosularew
besdalazeɡi qʼorolzabazeɡi χʼalaje waqχuna ɡʔjew aparaɡzabi rokʔula ɡʔjesije wa ɡʔjezije kwenɡi retʼjelɡi kʔola
ɡʔjedinɬidal nuʒeeɡi rokʔa tʃijar rakʔaldasa ratʃʼaral tʃaɡʼi misrijalda nuʒɡoɡi rukʼindal tʃijar rakʔaldasa ratʃʼaralɬun
durɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼa ɡʔjesije tʼaɡʼat ɡʔabe ɡʔjesije ritʼuqχɬi tsʼune wa ɡʔa balaɡo ɡʔjesul tsʼaraldaɬun ɡuroni ɡʔjeduɡe
tsoχʼo ɡʔjesije ɡʔabize kːola dutsa retsː ɡʔjew wuɡo dur allaɡʔ ɡʔjes duje ɡʼolo kʼudijal wa χʼinqʼaral χʼalkʼoɬabi ɡʔaruna wa ɡʔjeb kinabɡo dur berazda biχʔana
misrijalde ɡotʃarab meχaɬ dur umumuzul wukʼana  tʃi ɡʔanʒejin abuni betʼjerhan allaɡʔas zodir tsʼwabiɡʼanɡi ɡʼjemerɬizaruna nuʒ

betʼjerhan allaɡʔ χiraɬe wa tʼadtʃʼun tʼurazare ɡʔjesul qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi aχʼkamalɡi
ʒaqʼa nuʒetsa kinabɡo rakʼalde ʃːwezabe nuʒer ɬimalaz ɡuro χʼjeχʔarab wa ɡʔjezda ɡuro biχʔarab betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul ɡʼadluɡi ɡʔjesul qʼudrataɬul kwerɡi ɡʔjesul ɡutʃɡi
misrijalda ɡʔjes ɡʔarural χʼikmatal ɡʼalamatal iʃalɡi ɡʔjes pirɡʼawnase wa dosul χalqʼɡun ulkajaɬe ɡʔaburabɡi
ɡʔjes misrijaɬul askaraɬeɡi tʃujazeɡi tʃolɡʔakazeɡi ɡʔaburabɡi ɡʼizrailazda χadur ɬuɡʔaral dol kinalɡo baɡʼarab raɬdal karatʃelazuɬɡi ʁanqʼizarun allaɡʔas tʼaɡʼinaruna dol kinalɡo dob qʼojaɬ ʒaqʼa qʼojaɬɡi ɡʔjedin buɡo ɡʔjeb
nuʒer ɬimalazda ɡuro biχʔarab saparazda ɡʼitsʼab awlaqχalda rukʼaɡo ɡʔjes nuʒee ɡʔaburabʃːinab
wa ruwimil naslujaɬul eliawil wasaze aj datanije wa awiramije ɡʔaburabɡi ɡʼizrailaz tʃʼjel ɡʔaburab bakʼaɬul bakʔuɬan rakʔɡi kʔwatʼun ɡʔjelɡi ɡʔjezul qχizan ɬimalɡi tʃadralɡi ɡʼi botsʼiɡi tʃʼaɡo rakʔuɬe kʼkʼun arab kuts
nuʒerɡo berazda riχʔana betʼjerhanas ɡʔarural kinalɡo kutakal iʃal
ɡʔjedinɬidal ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒeda maɬaral tʼolalɡo amrabi tʼurazare tsinɡi nuʒer qʼuwat bukʼine buɡo iordan baχun ineɡi nuʒee kʔurab ulkajalde ɬuɡʔineɡi wa ɡʔjeb kwerde bosizeɡi
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nuʒer umumuzeɡi ɡʔjezul naslabazeɡi kʔjelin betʼjerhan ɡʔjedarab rakʔalda χalatab ɡʼumruɡi bukʼine buɡo nuʒer raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb rakʔ buɡo ɡʔjeb
nuʒ unel ruɡeb wa nuʒetsa kwerde bosizeqχin buɡeb ulka nuʒetsa tarab misrijaɬul ulkajalda reɬːarab ɡʔjetʃʼo doba nuʒetsa χuribe χʔon χʔalaan χadub baχtʃa ɡʼadin ɬaɬaze kːolaan ɡʔjeb χʼatʼalɡi χʼaltʼizarun
nuʒ unel ruɡeb ulkajaldajin abuni muɡʼrul ʃːobalɡi ɡʼatʼirakʔɡi zodisa tʃwaχarab tsʼadatsa ɬaɬala
ɡʔjeb buɡo ʒiwɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas χʔiχʔarab ulka ɬaɡʼalil bajbiχʔudasa aχiralde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjes kidaɡo ɡʔjelda tʼasa ber bosularo
ʒaqʼa ditsa kʔural amrabazuqχ nuʒ kʼwar kʔun ɡʼjenekːani rakʼ rakʼaɬ tʼolabɡo ruχʼaldaɬun betʼjerhan allaɡʔɡi χiraɬani ɡʔjesije tʼaɡʼatɡi ɡʔabuni
ditsa ʒindir ɡʼuʒda bazabila tsʼad nuʒer rakʔalde iχdalilɡi χasaliqχɬijaɬulɡi tsʼad wa ɡʔarzaɡo bukʼina nuʒee buɡʼa roɬɡi tʃaʁirɡi zajtunaɬul naχɡi
ditsa ɡʼalaχalda nuʒer botsʼuje χer biʒizabila wa ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwanaze nuʒee kwenɡi bukʼina
woreχa tsʼodorɬi ɡʔabe nuʒer rakʼal qʼosine ɡurin wa bitʼarab nuχdasaɡi kʔurun tʃijar allaɡʔzabaze qχuluqχ ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔine ɡurin
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanasul tsːin ɡʔalaɡɬila ɡʔjes zobalazul nutsʼbi raχala rakʔaɬe tsʼadɡi bukʼinaro batʃʼinɡi ʃːwelaro nuʒɡi betʼjerhanas nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb ɡʔajbatab ulkajaldasa χeχɡo tʼaɡʼinarila
ditsa kʔural amrabi rekʼjeɬɡi urɡʔirɡi tsʼune rakʼalde ʃːwejaɬul ɡʼalamat χʼisabalda kwerda ruχʔje ɡʔjel ɡʔjedinɡo nadaldaɡi ruχʔje kʼotʃon tetʃʼoɡo rukʼine
nuʒerɡo ɬimalazdaɡi maɬe ɡʔjel roqʼor ɡʼodor tʃʼun rukʼaɡoɡi qʼwatʼir saparalda rukʼaɡoɡi kʔiʒuleb meχaɬɡi tʼade raqχuleb meχaɬɡi takrar ɡʔare ɡʔjel
durɡo ruqʼaɬul nutsʼil raχazdaɡi ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabazdaɡi qχwaj ɡʔjel
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas nuʒer umumuze kʔjelin ɡʔjedarab rakʔalda nuʒerɡi nuʒer ɬimalazulɡi ɡʼumru χalaɬila rakʔalda tʼad zob buɡebɡʼan zamanalda nuʒetsaɡi ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabila
ditsa kʔural tʼolalɡo amrabiɡi tʼurazaruni betʼjerhan allaɡʔɡi χiraɬani ɡʔjesul nuχdasaɡi kʔuritʃʼoni ɡʔjesije ritʼuqχalɬunɡi ruɡoni
betʼjerhanasɡi nuʒer nuχdasa naqχe qʼotʼila kinalɡo tsoɡidal χalqʼal wa nuʒedasaɡi rikʼkʼjen ɡʼjemeral qʼuwatal χalqʼazul rakʔal nuʒetsaɡi kwerde rosila
nuʒetsa χʼjetʼje tʃʼarabʃːinab rakʔ nuʒee bukʼine buɡo kʼudijab awlaqχaldasa liwanalde ʃːwezeɡʼan wa jefrat ɡʼuruqχa kʼudijab raɬdaqχe ʃːwezeɡʼan tʼolalɡo rakʔal nuʒer rukʼine ruɡo
ɬidaɡo kʼweze ɡʔjetʃʼo nuʒeda dande tʃʼjeze nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʼudijab χʼinqʼi kʔjeze buɡo nuʒ ʃːwaralʃːinal ulkabazul χalqʼaze ɡʔjes nuʒee kʔurab raɡʼuda reqʼon
ɡʔale ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒee res kʔoleb buɡo barakat jaɡi naɡʼana tʼasa biʃːize
ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒee kʔural betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul kinalɡo amrabazuqχ ɡʼjenekːani wa ɡʔjel tʼurazaruni nuʒee barakat bukʼina
amma betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrabazuqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼoni wa ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒeda maɬarab ɡʔjesul nuχdasaɡi kʔurun ɬazeɡo ɬalarel tsoɡidal allaɡʔzabazda χadur ani nuʒee naɡʼana bukʼine buɡo
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒ nuʒerɡo rakʔalde ʃːwezarurab meχaɬ ɡerizim maɡʼardeɡi raχun barakat kʔoleb duɡʼa ɡʔabe wa ɡewal maɡʼarde raχun naɡʼana kʔoleb duɡʼa ɡʔabe
ɡʔjel muɡʼrul ruɡo iordan baχun dob tsojab raqχalda ɡilɡalalda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ more abulel mikːil ʁutʼbuzda askʼor arawajalda tʃʼaral χanaanijazul rakʔalda baqʼtʼjerχʔul raqχalde uneb nuχlul rakʔankːun
ɡʔanʒe nuʒetsa iordan ɡʼor baχuneb buɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔurab rakʔ kwerʃːalikʔje bosize ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo nuʒer rakʔɬun wa ɡʔjenib ɡʼumruɡi ɡʔabize buɡo nuʒetsa
ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒee zaɡʔir ɡʔarural kinalɡo qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi tʼadtʃʼun tʼurazare

ɡʔale nuʒer umumuzul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔurab rakʔalde ʃːwarab meχaɬ nuʒetsa dumaɬɡo tʼurazarize kːolel allaɡʔasul qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi ɡʔjel tʼurazare nuʒetsa ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabulebʃːinab zamanalda
ʒiderɡo allaɡʔzabaze qχuluqχ ɡʔabulel rukʼaral ɡʔjel χalqʼazul muqʼadasal bakʼal riχːe muɡʼruzul tʼoɡʔazda ɡoχʼ ʃːobazda wa kinalɡo ʁutʼbuzda ʁorkʔ
ɡʔjezul qʼurban bakʼal riχːe muqʼadasal ɡantʃʼal ʁure aʃeral χʼubal ruχʼje wa allaɡʔzabazul sipat suratal rek rekun raj ʃːibɡo naqχe tetʃʼoɡo
ɡʔjezda reɬːun ɡʔabuɡe nuʒetsa nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔase ɡʔabuleb qχuluqχɡi
qʼurbanalɡi χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi rosun nuʒ ratʃʼine kːola ɡʼitsʼɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa biʃːarab wa ɡʔjesul tsʼar tʃʼwarab bakʼalde kinalɡo qʼawmazul rakʔazda ɡʔorkʔosa ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo muqʼadasab ruqʼɬun tʼasa biʃːarab bakʼalde
ɡʔjenire ratʃʼa nuʒ tʼuran ruχʼulel qʼurbanalɡi tsoɡidal qʼurbanalɡi antsʼil butʼabiɡi χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi nazrujaɬul wa sunnatal qʼurbanalɡi ɡʼi botsʼul tʼotsere ɡʔarural χʼajwanalɡi ratʃun
ɡʔjenib betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsebe awadanab kwana ɡʔjeqʼej ɡʼutsʼje qχizan ɬimalɡun tsadaqχ nuʒɡo χʼaltʼun wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul kwerbaqʼijaldaɬun ʃːwarab buɡoɬijaldasaɡi roχun
ɡʔanʒe ɡʼadin ʃːiwasda bertsin biχʔuqχe ʒindijeɡo bokʔa bokʔarabɡi ɡʔabun rukʼine beɡʔularo nuʒ
nuʒ ʒeɡi ʃːwetʃʼo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb paraχatab rakʔalde
amma iordan ɡʼor baχarabɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔalde ʃːwela nuʒ ɡʔjes nuʒee ɡʔjenib χʼalχʔiɡi kʔjela kinabɡo raqχaɬ tuʃbabazdasa tsʼunarab paraχatab ɡʼumruɡi bukʼina nuʒer
ɡʔjeb meχaɬ ditsa aburab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ tʼuran ruχʼulel qʼurbanalɡi tsoɡidal qʼurbanalɡi antsʼil butʼabiɡi χirijal sadaqʼabiɡi nazrujaɬul qʼurbanalɡi rosun nuʒ ratʃʼine kːola nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa biʃːarab wa ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo muqʼadasab ruqʼɬun ɡʔaburab bakʼalde
ɡʔjenib betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsebe iχtilat ɡʔabe nuʒerɡo wasalɡun jasalɡun laʁzalɡun wa ʁarawaʃalɡun nuʒer ʃaɡʔarazda tʃʼaral lewitalɡi kʼotʃonɡe ɡʔjezije rakʔazul butʼaɡi maɡʼiʃatɡi ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul nuʒee buɡeb ɡʼadin
woreɡi tsebe kːarab bakʼalda qʼurbanal ruχʼuɡe
ɡʼitsʼɡo nuʒer qʼawmazul rakʔazda ɡʔorkʔosa betʼjerhanas tʼasa biʃːarab bakʼalda ruχʼje qʼurbanal wa ditsa maɬarabʃːinabɡi ɡʔjenib tʼubazabe
amma dutsa ɡʼi botsʼi qχweze beɡʔula dutsaɡo ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb bokʔarab bakʼalda wa bokʔarabɡʼan ɡʔanɡi kwanaze beɡʔula durɡo resaɬuqχ balaɡʔun aj betʼjerhan allaɡʔas duje kʔurab botsʼi riqʼzijaɬuqχ balaɡʔun nuʒer bokʔaras kwanaze beɡʔula ɡʔjedinab ɡʔan qχubasɡi watsʼtsʼadasɡi ritʼutʃʼaɬul jaɡi ʒajranaɬul ɡʔan kwine beɡʔuleb ɡʼadin
ɡʼitsʼɡo bi kwanije χʼaltʼizabuɡe ɡʔjeb ɬim ɡʼadin rakʔalde ɡʼodobe tʼje
dutsa durɡo roqʼob kwanaze beɡʔularo buɡʼa roɬul wa zajtunaɬul naχul antsʼil butʼa ɡʼi botsʼul tʼotsebeseb qʼinɬijaɬul ɡʔan nazrujaɬul wa sunnatab qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔan wa χirijal sadaqʼabazul niɡʼmat
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo kwanaj betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa biʃːarab bakʼalda ɡʔjesda tsebe bitʃːante duda tsadaqχ ɡʔjeb kwanaze dur wasazɡi jasazɡi laʁzaderitsaɡi ʁarawaʃazɡi dur ʃaɡʔaraldasa lewitazɡi munɡo χʼaltʼun ʃːwarab niɡʼmataɬul lazat bose ɡʔjenib durɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsebe
woreɡi durɡo rakʔalda paraχaɬarab meχaɬ lewital kʼotʃonɡe
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ʒindirɡo raɡʼuda reqʼon dur rakʔal ɡʼatʼid ɡʔarila wa ɡʔanade χʔul ɬuni kida bokʔaniɡi ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan ɡʔan kwanaze beɡʔula dutsa
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa biʃːarab muqʼadasab bakʼ dudasa tsʼaqʼɡo rikʼkʼada buɡoni betʼjerhanas duje kʔurab ɡʼi botsʼi dutsa durɡo bakʼalda bokʔarab meχaɬ qχweze beɡʔula wa bokʔarabɡʼan ɡʔan kwanaze beɡʔula
ritʼutʃʼaɬul jaɡi ʒajranaɬul ɡʔan ɡʼadin kwanaj ɡʔjeb qχubasɡi watsʼtsʼadasɡi kwanaze beɡʔula ɡʔjeb
amma bi ɡʔjeqʼejaldasa tsʼune ʃːajɡureɬul biduɬ buɡo ɡʼumru ɡʔanɡun tsadaqχ ɡʼumru kwanaɡe
bi kwanije χʼaltʼizabize beɡʔularo ɬim ɡʼadin rakʔalde ɡʼodobe tʼje ɡʔjeb
ɡʔjeqʼoɡe bi betʼjerhanase bokʔarab ɡʔabuni dujeɡi dur naslabazeɡi ɬikʼ bukʼina
amma allaɡʔase batʼa ɡʔaburabɡi nazru ɡʔaburabɡi ʒo betʼjerhanas tʼasa biʃːarab bakʼalde bosize kːola
tʼuran ruχʼulel qʼurbanal ɡʔanɡi biɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul qʼurban bakʼalde rose raqʼlil qʼurbanazul biɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul qʼurban bakʼalde tʼjeze kːola ɡʔjezul ɡʔan kwanaze beɡʔula
tʼadtʃʼun tʼubazabe ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒeda maɬarabʃːinab dutsa betʼjerhan allaɡʔase bokʔarab ɡʔabuni dujeɡi dur naslabazeɡi ɬikʼ bukʼine buɡo
nuʒetsa tsoɡidal χalqʼazuqχ buɡeb rakʔ kwerde bosize buɡo wa ɡʔjezul rakʔazda ɡʼumru ɡʔabize buɡo betʼjerhanas nuʒeda tseresa tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡo ɡʔjel χalqʼal
ɡʔjel χalqʼal tʼaɡʼinarun χadub ɡʔjezul allaɡʔzabiɡi tsʼjeχon qʼorikʔje kːejaldasa tsʼune ɡʔal χalqʼaz kinab din ɡʔabuleb bukʼarab ditsaɡi ɡʔjebɡo ɡʔabila jan abuɡe
betʼjerhanase ɡʔjedinab ʒo ɡʔabuɡe ɡʔjez ʒiderɡo allaɡʔzabaze ɡʔjesda riχaral qχubal ʒal ɡʔarula ɡʔjez ʒiderɡo ɬimaltsin ruχʼula ɡʔjel allaɡʔzabaze ɡʼolo
muχʼkanɡo tʼubazabe ditsa maɬarab kinabɡo ʒo ɡʔjelda tʼade ʃːibɡo ʒubaɡe jaɡi tʼasa baqχuɡe

duda ɡʔorkʔow awaraɡ jaɬuni χʼikmatal makʔabi riχʔulew tʃi waqχani wa ɡʔjes tso pulanab ʒo kːeze buɡin jaɬuni tso ɡʼalamat ɬuɡʔine buɡin tsebekːunɡo bitsani
wa ɡʔjes bitsarab ʒo χʼaqʼiqʼataldaɡi kːani ɡʔjes abize beɡʔula ratʃʼa tsoɡidal nuʒeda ɬalarel allaɡʔzabazda naqχ riɬːine wa ɡʔjezije qχuluqχ ɡʔabize jan
ɡʔjew tʃijasuqχ ɡʼin tʼamize beɡʔularo ʃːajɡureɬul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔjedin χʼal biχʔize buɡo nuʒer ɡʔjew nuʒee rakʼ rakʼaɬ χirijaw wuɡiʃːali balaɡʔize
nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda naqχ riɬːa ɡʔjesukʔa χʼinqʼa wa ɡʔjesije ɡʔabe tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔjesul amrabi tʼurazare wa ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼjenekːe ɡʔjesije qχuluqχ ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjesije mutʼiɡʼɡo χʔwade
ɡʔjedinaw awaraɡɡi makʔabi riχʔulew tʃiɡi tʃʼwaze kːola misrijaldasa nuʒ naqχe ratʃaraw wa laʁɬijaldasa nuʒ erken ɡʔaruraw betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul nuχdasa nuʒ qʼosinarize ɬuɡʔaraɬuqχ ɡʔjedinab kweʃɬi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob toɡe naqχe qχame ɡʔjeb
dur wats was jas jaɡi dur jokʔulej ɬadi jaɬuni ɬikʼaw ɡʔudul baɬɡoɡo mun tsoɡidal allaɡʔzabazde tsʼaze ɬuɡʔani wa ɡʔjez abuni riɬːa tsoɡidal allaɡʔzabaze qχuluqχ ɡʔabize jan ja duda ja dur umumuzda ɬalel rukʼintʃʼjel allaɡʔzabaze
sweruqχɬijaɬul ɡʼaɡardasa jaɡi rikʼkʼadasa kinal rataniɡi dunjalaɬul χalqʼazul allaɡʔzabaze
ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasda tʼad reqʼoɡe ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼintsin tʼamuɡe ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasda baraχʃːuɡe wa ɡʔjew tʃi waχtʃuɡe
ɡʔjew tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo tʃʼwaj tʼotsebeseb ɡamatʃʼ dutsa retʃʼtʃʼize kːola duda χadub χutʼarab χalqʼaɬɡi
ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwaj ɡʔjew misrijaldasa nuʒerɡo laʁɬijaldasa nuʒ erken ɡʔaruraw betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul nuχdasa nuʒ qʼosinarize χʼal biχʔaraɬuqχ
ɡʼizrailazul tʼolabɡo χalqʼalda ɡʔjeb raɡʼidal ɡʔjel χʼinqʼila tʼokʼaɬ nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɬitsaniɡi ɡʔjedinab iʃɡi ɡʔabilaro
duda raɡʼani betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔural ʃaɡʔarazul tsojalda
χʼaliχʔatal tʃaɡʼi rakːun ruɡin wa ɡʔjez nuʒeda tserekːun riχʔa raɡʼitʃʼjel tʃijar allaɡʔzabaze tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabize tsoɡidal ɡʼadamalɡi tsʼalel ruɡin
dutsa raɡʼa rakʔande ʃːun tsʼjeχ reχ ɡʔabize kːola ɡʔjeb iʃaɬul ɡʔjeb bitʼarab ʒo batani wa χʼaqʼiqʼataldaɡi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʔjedinab maχʼtsarab iʃ ɡʔabun batani
ʃaɡʔaraɬul kinalɡo tʃaɡʼi tʃara ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo tʃʼwaze kːola tʼolabɡo ʃaɡʔarɡi ɡʔjenib buɡebʃːinabɡi ɡʼi botsʼiɡun tsadaqχ χerem ɡʔabize kːola χwaltʃatsa tʃʼwaj kinalɡo
ɡʔjenib batarabʃːinab betʃeɬiɡi ʃaɡʔaraɬul majdanalde bakʼare wa tʼolabɡo ʃaɡʔarɡun tsadaqχ buχʼje nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔase kʔoleb tsʼadul qʼurban χʼisabalda ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔar tʃʼuntelazul ɡoχʼɬun χutʼize kːola abadijaɬeɡo wa tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔjeb tsʼi ɡʔabun baze beɡʔularo
χerem ɡʔaburab ʒojalde nuʒetsa kwer beɡʔize beɡʔularo ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhanasul tsːin naqχ busːina nuʒeda ɡurχʼila wa raχʼmu tsʼob ɬela nuʒer umumuze kʔurab raɡʼuda reqʼon nuʒee ɡʼjemeral naslabiɡi kʔjela
ɡʔjedin bukʼina nuʒetsa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasuqχ ɡʼin tʼamuni ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒee zaɡʔir ɡʔarural ɡʔjesul kinalɡo amrabi tʼurazaruni wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔase bokʔuleb qʼaɡʼidajaɬ χʔwadani

nuʒ ruɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul ɬimal ɡʔjedinɬidal χwarazda χadub maɡʼu ɡʔabuleɬul tʃerχalda ruʁnalɡi ɬoɡe nadalda tʼasaχun rasɡi kʼkʼwaɡe
betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul χirijab χalqʼɬidal nuʒ dunjalaɬul kinalɡo χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔosa betʼjerhanas tʼasa riʃːana nuʒ ʒindirɡo χasab irs χʼisabalda
kinab bukʼaniɡi qχubab ʒo kwanaɡe
ɡʔale nuʒee χʼalalab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi tʃʼjeɡʼjerbotsʼi ɡʼi tsʼani
ritʼutʃʼal ʒajranal baɡʼnasal tʃanitsʼani antilopabi wa ɡʼalχul kujdul
nuʒetsa kwanaze beɡʔula ʃːinkʼilɡi kʼikʼwekʔab tʃʼamun laɡʼɡi reχuleb bokʔarab χʼajwanaɬul ɡʔan
amma waranidul ɡʼankʼil wa damanaɬul ɡʔan nuʒetsa kwanaɡe ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjez tʃʼamun laɡʼ reχaniɡi ɡʔjezul kʼikʼwekʔal ʃːankʼlal ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjel nuʒee qχubalɬun kːola
boɬonaɬul ɡʔanɡi kwanaɡe ɡʔjeɬul kʼikʼwekʔaral ʃːankʼlal ruɡo amma ɡʔjeɬ tʃʼamun laɡʼ reχularo ɡʔjeb nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔanɡi kwanaɡe ɡʔjeɬul balkanaldaɡi kwer qχwaɡe
ɬadaɬ rukʼunel ʒalazda ɡʔorkʔosa nuʒetsa kwanaze beɡʔula ʁataχarab qχalɡi ɬedoleb tʃːuɡʼil kwatʃʼɡi buɡeb ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi
amma ʁataχarab qχalɡi ɬedoleb tʃːuɡʼil kwatʃʼɡi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb raɬdal jaɡi ɡʼurul ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi kwanaɡe ɡʔjeb nuʒee χʼaramab buɡo
bokʔarab batsʼtsʼadab χʼantʃʼil ɡʔanɡi kwanaze beɡʔula nuʒetsa
amma nuʒetsa kwanaze beɡʔularo tsʼum qχwek qχerʁu
kanjuk qχartʃiʁa lutʃnuzul kinabniɡi tajpa
ʁuduzul kinabniɡi tajpa
waraniχʼintʃʼ betsːaruz raɬdaχʼintʃʼ qχartʃiʁabazul kinabniɡi tajpa
keturuz χʔutsʼiχʼintʃʼ qχaχʼab betsːaruz
pelikan sip tʃuduk
χʔutsʼitʃʼorolo χʔutsʼiqχazazul kinabɡʼaɡi tajpa ɡʔudɡʔud wa ɡʼunkʼkʼχʼintʃʼ
borʒineɡi borʒuneb ɡʔjedinɡo unqʼɡo χʼatʼida rakʔaldasanɡi ʃuruleb kinabniɡi ɡʼisi biqʼinab ruχʼtʃʼaɡoɬi nuʒee qχubabɬun kːola ɡʔjeb kwanaze beɡʔularo
amma bokʔarab batsʼtsʼadab χʼintʃʼ nuʒetsa kwanaze beɡʔula
χwarab jaɬuni ʒanawaraz tʃʼwarab χʼajwanaɬul ɡʔan kwanaɡe ɡʔjeb kʔje jaɬuni bitʃe nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor tʃʼjel ɡʔabural tʃijar χalqʼazul tʃaɡʼaze ɡʔjez kwanaze beɡʔula ɡʔjeb amma nuʒ ruɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas χira ɡʔaburab ɡʔjesul χalqʼ
burutʼ beɬinabuɡe ɡʔjeɬul ebelaɬul raχʔdaɬ
ʃːibab sonaɬ durɡo aχ χuraldasan ʃːwarab ʒojaɬul antsʼil butʼa batʼa ɡʔabe
betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsebe ɡʔjes tʼasa biʃːarab muqʼadasab bakʼalda kwanaze kːola dutsa buɡʼa roɬul tsʼibaqχarab tʃaʁiraɬul wa zajtunaɬul naχul antsʼil butʼaɡi reqχadul ʃːibab tʼotsebeseb qʼinɬijaɬul ɡʔanɡi ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize kːola betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul kidaɡoseb χʼurmat adabalde mun ruɡʔunɬun wukʼine
amma ɡʔjeb bakʼ dudasa tsʼaqʼɡo rikʼkʼada buɡoni betʼjerhan allaɡʔas duje kʔurab χʼaluqχenaɬul antsʼil butʼa ɡʔjenibe bosize resɡi batitʃʼoni betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa biʃːarab muqʼadasab bakʼ dudasa tsʼaqʼɡo rikʼkʼada bukʼinaɬ
kinabɡo antsʼil butʼa ɡʼartsuqχ χise wa ɡʔjeb ɡʼaratsɡi bosun a betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa biʃːarab bakʼalde
ɡʔjenib ɡʔjeb ɡʼartsuqχ dujeɡo bokʔarab bose qχweze ʒalɡi tʃaʁirɡi tʃʼaɡʼaɡi wa tsoɡi ʃːib bokʔaniɡi wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsebe durɡo qχizan ɬimalɡun tsadaqχ roχalil kwana ɡʔjeqʼej ɡʼutsʼje
nuʒeda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel lewitalɡi kʼotʃonɡe ɡʔjezije rakʔazul butʼaɡi maɡʼiʃatɡi ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul nuʒee buɡeb ɡʼadin
ʃːibab ɬababileb ɬaɡʼalil aχiralda ɡʔjeb sonaɬ batʃʼarab tʼolabɡo χʼaluqχenaɬul antsʼil butʼaɡi ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabaqχe naqχratel ɬoleb bakʼalde bose
ɡʔjeb bukʼina lewitazeɡi nuʒeda ɬaleɬul nuʒer ɡʼadinab irsɡi mal mulkɡi ɡʔjezul ɡʔjetʃʼjebɬi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel tʃijar χalqʼazul tʃaɡʼazeɡi besdalazeɡi qʼorolzabazeɡi ritʃːante ɡʔjelɡi ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwanaze ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dutsa ɡʔabulebʃːinalda barakat ɬela

ʃːibab ankʔɡo sonaldasan nuʒ naɬulazda tʼasaɬuɡʔine kːola
ɡʔjeb ɡʔadin ɡʔabe bitʃːante ʒindirɡo χalqʼaɬul tʃijase qʼarzaɬe ʃːib bukʼaniɡi ʒo kʔuraw tʃijas ɡʔjeb tʼasaɬuɡʔun teze betʼjerhanasul amru buɡeɬul ɡʔjedin ɡʔabejan tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔjeb naɬi naqχe tʼalab ɡʔabize beɡʔularo
tʃijar χalqʼazul tʃaɡʼazuqχa naɬi tʼalab ɡʔabize beɡʔula amma durɡo χalqʼaɬul tʃijase aj ɡʼizrailase kʔurab naɬuda tʼasa ɬuɡʔa
miskinal tʃaɡʼi rukʼine kːolaro nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor ʃːajɡureɬul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔalda betʼjerhanas ɡʔarzajab maɡʼiʃat kʔjeze buɡeɬul nuʒee
amma ɡʔjedin bukʼina betʼjerhan allaɡʔasuqχ ɡʼinɡi tʼamuni ʒaqʼa ditsa kʔural allaɡʔasul amrabiɡi muχʼkanɡo tʼurazaruni
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʼudijab barakat ɬela nuʒeda wa ɡʼjemeral χalqʼaze qʼarzaɬe kʔjezeɡi res bukʼina nuʒer nuʒetsajin abuni kidaniɡi naɬi ɡʔabize kːelaro nuʒetsa ɡʼjemeral χalqʼazda tʼad kwerʃːel ɡʔabila amma nuʒeda tʼad ɬitsaniɡi kwerʃːel ɡʔabilaro
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔurab rakʔalda nuʒer ʃaɡʔarazul tsojalda dur ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬul ʃːiwniɡi tʃi miskinɬani durɡo urʁelɡi ɡʔabun wukʼintʃʼoɡo miskinazda kwer tʃʼwalewɬun wukʼa
ɡʔjezije qʼwariɡʼarabʃːinabɡi saχawatɡo wa ʁirajalda kʔje qʼarzaɬe
kweʃab pikru rekʼjeɬe bitʃːaɡe ankʔabileb aj naɬulazda tʼasa ɬuɡʔuneb son tʼade ɡʼuntʼuleb buɡilan rokʔuqʼɡo walaɡʔun miskinɬaraw tʃi naqχ tʃʼwaɡe tsinɡi ɡʔjes betʼjerhanasde ɡʼarz baqχila munɡi munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːela
kwer ɡʼatʼidɡo rekʼjeɬ tsːinɡi kːwetʃʼoɡo kʔje ɡʔjesije qʼarzaɬe kʔoleb ʒo ɡʔjele ɡʔjedin ɡʔaburaɬuqχin betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dutsa ɡʔabulebʃːinaɬeɡi kwerbaqʼize buɡeb
miskinal tʃaɡʼi rakʔaldasa kidaɡo ɬuɡʼize ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjedinɬidal ditsa duda tʼadqʼaleb buɡo kidaɡo kwer ɡʼatʼidawɬun wukʼa durɡo ɡʼaɡaral ɡʼizrailazdeχunɡi tsoɡidaw kinaw wukʼaniɡi miskin paqʼirasdeχunɡi
dur χalqʼtsojaz aj ʒuɡʔutʼaz biχʔintʃi jaɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan batʼaɬi ɡʔjetʃʼo ʒalɡo duje laʁzalɬun ritʃani wa anɬɡo sonaɬ duje χʼaltʼani ankʔabileb sonaɬ dutsa ɡʔjel tarqχan ɡʔarize kːola
amma tarqχan ɡʔawuleɬul tʃʼowoɡo witʃːaɡe ɡʔjedinaw tʃi
saχawatɡo kʔje ɡʔjesije durɡo reqχaɬa tʼorʃːalidasa wa tʃaʁiraldasa butʼa betʼjerhan allaɡʔas duje kʔurabʃːinaldasa butʼa ɡʔjesijeɡi kʔje
duda kʼotʃonɡe munɡoɡi misrijalda laʁɬun wukʼarawɬi wa dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔas mun ɡʔjenisa χwasar ɡʔawurawɬi ɡʔjedinɬidalin ʒaqʼa ditsa dude ɡʔab amru ɡʔabuleb buɡeb
amma laʁas abuni naqχe ine bokʔun ɡʔjetʃʼin ʃːajɡureɬul munɡi dur qχizan qʼajɡi bokʔun dur bakʼalda ɬikʼ buɡin ʒindijejan
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ nutsʼida askʼowɡi tʃʼjezawun ɡʼjebujaɬ ɡʔjesul ɡʼin borɬe ɡʔjeb ɡʼjebu nutsʼida qʼaleb χʼalaɬ ɡʔjeb bukʼina ɡʔjew ɡʼumrujaɬɡo dur laʁɬun χutʼulew wukʼinaɬul ɡʼuʒɬun ɡʔjebɡo ɡʔabe ʁarawaʃaɬeɡi
amma laʁ erken ɡʔawize kːanin abun dur tsːin baqχunɡe ɡʔjew anɬɡo sonaɬ duda tsewe χʼaltʼun wuɡeɬul kːun watʃaraw χʼaltʼuqχanase kʔoleldasa kʼiɡo nuχaɬ daɡʔab χarʒaɬuqχ tsinɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔasɡi ɡʔabulebʃːinaɬuɬ kwerbaqʼila duje
durɡo ɡʼi botsʼijaldasa ʃːibab tʼotsebe ɡʔaburab biχʔinab χʼajwan betʼjerhan allaɡʔase batʼa ɡʔabe tʼotsebe ɡʔaburab basi χʼaltʼizabuɡe tʼotsebe ɡʔaburab kujdul kwasɡi qʼuntsʼuɡe
ɡʔjezul ɡʔan ʃːibab sonaɬ dutsaɡi dur qχizan ɬimalazɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsebe ɡʔjes tʼasa biʃːarab muqʼadasab bakʼalda kwanaze kːola
amma ɡʔjedinab χʼajwanaɬe kinabɡʼaɡi ʒaʁalɬi kːani reqʼɬun betsːɬun jaɬuni tsoɡi kinab bukʼaniɡi ɡʼuzru kːun ɡʔjeb betʼjerhan allaɡʔase qʼurbanaɬe qχweze beɡʔularo
durɡo ʃaɡʔaralda qχwezeɡi qχun kwanaj ɡʔjeb qχubasɡi watsʼtsʼadasɡi kwanaze beɡʔula ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔan ritʼutʃʼaɬul jaɡi ʒajranaɬul ɡʔan kwanaze beɡʔuleb ɡʼadin
amma ɡʔjeɬul bi kwanije χʼaltʼizabuɡe ɡʔjeb ɬim ɡʼadin rakʔalde ɡʼodobe tʼje

awiw motsʼ kʼotʃonɡe wa ɡʔjeb motsʼaɬ nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔase pesaχaɬul bajram tʼobitʼje ʃːajɡureɬul awiw motsʼaɬul sardiɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃana
betʼjerhan allaɡʔase pesaχaɬul qʼurban qχwe betʼjerhanas tʼasa biʃːarab muqʼadasab bakʼalda
pesaχaɬul qʼojaz retʃːeb ʒubarab kwen kwanaɡe ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʼitsʼɡo buɡʔurɡo tʃed kwanaj ɡʼazabaɬul tʃed ʃːajɡureɬul misrijaldasa qʼwatʼiwe mun ɡʼjedeɡʼun waqχine kːedal ɡʔjedin ɡʔabe nuʒɡo misrijaldasa naqχe arab qʼo kidaniɡi kʼotʃon tetʃʼoɡo bukʼineɬun
ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ nuʒer ulkajalda kibniɡi retʃːeb bukʼine beɡʔularo qʼasi qχurab qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔanɡi roɡʔineɡʼan naqχe toɡe
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔurab tsoniɡi ʃaɡʔaralda qʼurban qχoɡe
ɡʔjes ʒinditsaɡo tʼasa biʃːarab muqʼadasab bakʼalda ɡuroni ɡʼitsʼɡo ɡʔjenib qχwe pesaχaɬul qʼurban baqʼtʼjerχʔul ɡʼuʒalda munɡo misrijaldasa qʼwatʼiwe waqχarab ɡʼuʒalda
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa biʃːarab bakʼalda beɬe wa ɡʔjenib kwanaj qʼurbanaɬul ɡʔan wa radal roqʼowe tʼad wusːa
anɬɡo qʼojaɬ buɡʔurɡo tʃed kwanaj ankʔabileb qʼojaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔase ɡʼolo dinijab dandeɬi aχʼje ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ kinabɡʼaɡi χʼaltʼiɡi ɡʔabuɡe
ɬiɬari bajbiχʔaraldasa naqχe ankʔɡo ankʔ rikʼkʼje
wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔase ɡʼolo ankʔazul bajram tʼobitʼje betʼjerhan allaɡʔas duje ɡʔarzaɡo kʔurab ɡʼadin dutsaɡi ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ kwerɡʼatʼidɡo χirijal sadaqʼabi ɡʔare
durɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa biʃːarab bakʼalda awadanab kwana ɡʔjeqʼej ɡʼutsʼje wa ritʃːante duda tsadaqχ rukʼine dur wasalɡi jasalɡi laʁzalɡi ʁarawaʃalɡi duda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel lewitalɡi ɡʔjedinɡo nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel aparaɡzabiɡi besdalzabiɡi qʼorolzabiɡi
kidaniɡi kʼotʃonɡe munɡo misrijalda laʁɬun wukʼarawɬi wa ɡʔal qʼanunal tʼurazare
qχoʃazul bajram tʼobitʼje ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔotsʼib lalɡi tʼamun tʃanaɬub tsʼibilɡi tsʼtsʼun ɬuɡʼarab meχaɬ
awadanab kwana ɡʔjeqʼej ɡʼutsʼje ɡʔjeb bajramaɬul qʼojaz wa duda tsadaqχ rukʼine te dur wasalɡi jasalɡi laʁzalɡi ʁarawaʃalɡi duda ɡʼaɡarɬuqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel lewitalɡi ɡʔjedinɡo nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel aparaɡzabiɡi besdalzabiɡi qʼorolzabiɡi
betʼjerhanas tʼasa biʃːarab bakʼalda ankʔɡo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔase ɡʼolo bajram tʼobitʼje betʼjerhan allaɡʔas duje ɬikʼab batʃʼinɡi kʔun ɡʔabulebʃːinalda barakatɡi ɬun buɡeɬul rakʼ rakʼaɬ woχun awadanɡo wukʼa
ɬaɡʼalida ʒanib ɬabɡo nuχaɬ nuʒer kinalɡo biχʔinal ratʃʼine kːola betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsere ɡʔjes tʼasa biʃːarab bakʼalde buɡʔurɡo tʃadazul bajramqʼojaɬ ankʔazul bajramqʼojaɬ wa qχoʃazul bajramqʼojaɬ betʼjerhanasda tsewe tʃʼowoɡo tʃi watʃʼine beɡʔularo
bitʃːante ʃːiwaw tʃijas ʒindirɡo resalda reqʼon betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔurab botsʼi riqʼzijaldasa χirijab sadaqʼa bosun batʃʼine muqʼadasab bakʼalde
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔural kinalɡo ʃaɡʔarazda diwantʃaɡʼiɡi χʼakimzabiɡi tʼame ɡʔjedin ɡʔabe ʃːibab qʼawmalda ʒanib wa bitʃːante ɡʔjez ritʼuqχab diwan ɡʔabize
diwan rakʼbatsʼtsʼadɡo ɡʔabe tʃi watʼa ɡʔawuɡe riʃwat bosuɡe riʃwataz ɡʼaqʼilzabiɡi betsːɬizarula rakʼ batsʼtsʼadalɡi ɡʔjersiqχabiɬun kːezarula
ritʼuqχɬi tsʼune ɡʼitsʼɡo ritʼuqχɬi tsinɡi dujeɡi ɡʼumru bukʼina wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔas duje kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔaɬul χwaʒainɬunɡi waqχila
dutsa betʼjerhan allaɡʔase baze buɡeb qʼurban bakʼalda askʼob aʃeral χʼubi tʃʼoɡe kinabɡʼaɡi χʼubi tʃʼoɡe
maʒusijazul muqʼadasal ɡantʃʼalɡi ɬoɡe dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔase riχarab ʒo buɡo ɡʔjeb

ʒaʁalɬi buɡeb jaɡi kinabɡʼaɡi ɡʼuzru kːarab ɡʼi botsʼi betʼjerhan allaɡʔase qʼurban ɡʔabuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul betʼjerhan allaɡʔase kutakalda riχarab ʒo buɡo ɡʔjeb
nuʒee betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔurab tsoniɡi ʃaɡʔaralda ɡʔjesulɡun qʼotʼiɡi χwezabun betʼjerhan allaɡʔase riχarab ʒo ɡʔabulel biχʔinal jaɡi rutʃːabi ratani
jaɬuni dir amruɡi ɡʼadaqχ bositʃʼoɡo tsoniɡi tʃi tsoɡidal allaɡʔzabaze qχuluqχ ɡʔabize wa baqʼuje motsʼroje jaɡi zobalazul bojaɬe suʒda ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔani
wa ɡʔjeb duda raɡʼani ɡʔjeɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ raɡʼa rakʔande ʃːun tsʼjeχ reχ ɡʔabe ɡʔjeb bitʼarab batani wa ɡʼizrailalda χʼaqʼiqʼataldaɡi ɡʔjedinab naqχeɡʼanab iʃ ɡʔabun batani
ɡʔjeb iʃ ɡʔabural tʃaɡʼi biχʔintʃi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan batʼaɬi ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabaqχeɡi ratʃun ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwaze kːola
amma tamiχʼ ɡʔabize kːani kʼiɡo jaɬuni ɬabɡo nuɡʼ qʼwariɡʼuna tsoχʼo ɡuroni nuɡʼ ɡʔjetʃʼoni ɡʔjew tʃi tʃʼwaze beɡʔularo
nuɡʼzabaz retʃʼtʃʼize kːola tʼotsebe ɡamatʃʼ ɡʔjezda χadub χutʼarab χalqʼaɬɡi kweʃɬi naqχe ɡʔabe nuʒedaɡo ɡʔorkʔosa
tso tso iʃaze χʼukmu qʼotʼize tʃʼwaj qχwej bukʼa pulanab daɡʼba qʼets bukʼa tsotsaɬ raʁun kːarab ɡʼaʒizɬi bukʼa dur ʃaɡʔaraɬul diwantʃaɡʼaze zaχʼmaɬize beɡʔula ɡʔjebmeχaɬ mun a betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa biʃːarab muqʼadasab bakʼalde
lewijil qʼawmaldasa kaʃiʃzabazuqχe wa ɡʔjeniw wuɡew diwantʃijasuqχe ɡʔjezda tsʼjeχe ɡʔjez bitsina duda bitʼarab χʼukmu
betʼjerhanasul muqʼadasab bakʼalda qʼotʼarab χʼukmu tʼubazabize kːola ɡʔjez maɬarab qʼaɡʼidajalda ɡʔabe kinabɡo
ɡʔjez maɬarab qʼanunaldaɡi ɡʔjez qʼotʼarab χʼukmujaldaɡi reqʼon ɡʔabe kinabɡo ɡʔjeldasa dowe ʁowe kʔuruɡe
ɡʔjeniw betʼjerhan allaɡʔase qχuluqχaɬe tʃʼaraw kaʃiʃasuqχ jaɬuni diwantʃijasuqχ ɡʼjenekːilarilan ɬuɡʔaraw tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola kweʃɬijaldasa batsʼtsʼje ɡʼizrail
tsinɡi tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazda raɡʼila ɡʔjeb wa ɡʔjel χʼinqʼila ɡʔjedinab tʼasankːarab ʒoɡi tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔabilaro
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔaldeɡi ʃːun ɡʔjebɡi kwerde bosun ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb meχaɬ nuʒetsa abila ratʃʼa niɬetsa niɬeeɡo patʃa wiʃːize niɬeda sweruqχ ruɡel tsoɡidal χalqʼazɡo ɡʼadin an
nuʒetsa patʃaɬun wiʃːize kːola betʼjerhan allaɡʔas wiχʔizawuraw tʃi ɡʔjew wukʼine kːola nuʒerɡo χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔosa tʃi dur χalqʼaɬul ɡurew qʼwatʼisa rakʔaɬul tʃi dudaɡo tʼad patʃaɬun toɡe
patʃajas ʒindijeɡo tʃujal ɡʼjemerɬizarize beɡʔularo wa ʒeɡi tsʼikʼkʼun tʃujal rosize ɡʼolo misrijalde tʃaɡʼi ritʼize beɡʔularo betʼjerhanas nuʒeda abun buɡeɬul nuʒ tʼokʼaɬ dore naqχ rusːunɡe jan
patʃajas ɡʼjemeral ɬudbi ratʃine beɡʔularo ɡuroni ɡʔjew bitʼarab nuχdasa qʼosine wuɡo ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʼjemerab ɡʼarats mesedɡi bukʼine beɡʔularo patʃajasul
patʃaɬijaɬul taχide waχarab meχaɬ dob kaʃiʃzabazuqχɡi lewitazuqχɡi buɡeb qʼanun qχwaze kːola ɡʔjes ʒindijeɡo
bitʃːante ɡʔjeb kidaɡo ɡʔjesuqχ bukʼine wa ɡʔjes tsʼalize tsinɡi ɡʔjew betʼjerhan allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼize ruɡʔunɬila qʼanunalda qχwaraɬe mutʼiɡʼɬila wa kinalɡo allaɡʔasul tʼadqʼajalɡi tʼurazarila
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ patʃajas ʒiwɡo χalqʼaldasa tʼadeɡʼan ɡʔawilaro ɡʔal amrabazdasaɡi kiweɡo kʔurilaro tsinɡi ɡʔjew patʃaɡi ɡʔjesul nasluɡi ɡʼizrailaɬul patʃaɬijaɬul taχida ɡʼjemerab meχaɬ χutʼila

ɡʼizrailalda lewijil naslujaɬe aj kaʃiʃzabazeɡun lewitaze rakʔazul butʼaɡi irsɡi bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjezul butʼa buɡo betʼjerhanase kʔolel χirijal sadaqʼabiɡun qʼurbanazdasa ɡʔjezdasan bukʼina ɡʔjezije kwen tʼjeχ
lewijil qʼawmaɬe watsazda ɡʔorkʔob butʼa ɡʔjetʃʼo ʃːajɡureɬul ʒiwɡo betʼjerhan wuɡo ɡʔjezije irsaɬul bakʼalda ɡʔjesul amrujalda reqʼon
ɡʔale kaʃiʃzabaze kʔjeze kːoleb butʼa χalqʼaɬ qʼurbanaɬe qχurabʃːinab botsʼudasaɡi ɡʼijadasaɡi ɡʔjezul ratʼaɡi betʼjer kʼalɡi kwaniruqʼɡi
ɡʔjedinɡo χʼaluqχenaɬul buɡʼa roɬul tʃaʁiraɬul zajtunaɬul naχul tʼotseresel butʼabiɡi ɡʼijal tʼotsebe qʼuntsʼarab kwasɡi
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kinalɡo qʼawmazda ɡʔorkʔosa tsoχʼo ɡʔjelɬidal tʼasa riʃːaral ɡʔjelɡi ɡʔjezul naslabiɡi kidaɡo betʼjerhanasda tsere tʃʼun ɡʔjesije qχuluqχaɬe rukʼine
ɡʼizrailazul kinab bukʼaniɡi ʃaɡʔaralda ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼaraw lewit ʒindijeɡo bokʔarab meχalda betʼjerhanas tʼasa biʃːarab muqʼadasab bakʼalde ɡotʃine beɡʔula
ɡʔjesul iχtijar buɡo betʼjerhanase qχuluqχaɬe tʃʼaral ʒindirɡo watsal lewitalɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjenib betʼjerhan allaɡʔase qχuluqχ ɡʔabun wukʼine
ɡʔjew lewitase ɡʔjesul watsazda baʃːadab sursat kʔjeze kːola ʒindirɡo umumuzul irs bitʃun ʃːwarab buɡoɬi ɡʔjesul bataniɡi
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔoleb rakʔalde ʃːwarab meχalda nuʒetsa ɡʔjenir ruɡel χalqʼazul qʼabiχʼal ɡʼadatal rosize beɡʔularo
qʼurban bakʼalda nuʒer wasal jaɡi jasal tsʼadul qʼurbanɬun ɡʔaruɡe wa siχʼrutʃaɡʼiɡi paliqχabiɡi baɬɡoɬi bitsunel wa tsoɡi ɡʔjelda reɬːarab ʒo ɡʔabulel tʃaɡʼiɡi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor rukʼine ritʃːaɡe
nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor rukʼine beɡʔularo insanasul ɡʼaqʼlu χisizabulel siχʼrutʃaɡʼi jaɡi χwarazul ruχʼal ratʃʼinarulel wa batʼi batʼijal ruχʼazda kʼaɬalel tʃaɡʼi
ɡʔjedinal iʃal ɡʔarulew ʃːiwaw tʃi betʼjerhanase riχaraw wuɡo ɡʔjel qχubal iʃal sababɬunin betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dol χalqʼal nuʒer berzukʔan naqχe qʼotʼulel ruɡel
betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsere ratsʼtsʼadɡo rukʼa
nuʒetsa naqχe ʁeze ruɡel χalqʼaz paliqχabazuqχɡi baɬɡoɬi bitsunel tʃaɡʼazuqχɡi ɡʼin tʼamula amma nuʒede betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amru ɡʔjedinab ɡʔjetʃʼo
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dunɡo ɡʼadin nuʒedaɡo ɡʔorkʔosa awaraɡ waqχinawize wuɡo nuʒee ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼjenekːe
χoriwalda ʒamaɡʼataɬul dandeɬijalda nuʒetsa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda ɡʔarun bukʼindal betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼizeɡi ɡʔab kutakab tsʼa biχʔizeɡi bitʃːaɡe niʒeda ɡuroni niʒ χwezeqχin ruɡo jan
wa betʼjerhanas dida abuna ɡʔjez ɡʔjedin ɡʔaruleb bukʼin ɬikʼ buɡo
ditsa ɡʔjezije munɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔosa awaraɡ kʔjela wa ɡʔjesul kʼaldib ɬela ɡʔjezda abize kːoleb ʒo ɡʔjes bitsina ɡʔjezda ditsa amru ɡʔabunʃːinab
ɡʔjew awaraɡɡi ɡʔorkʔow kːun ditsa zaɡʔir ɡʔarural raɡʼabazuqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼjew tʃi ditsaɡo tamiχʼalde tsʼala
amma dir tsʼaraldasan ditsa amru ɡʔabitʃʼjeb ʒo bitsaraw jaɬuni batʼijaw allaɡʔasul tsʼaraldasan kʼaɬalew awaraɡ tʃʼwaze kːola
duda rakʼalda kːeze beɡʔula kin dida ɬaleb betʼjerhanasul raɡʼi ɡʔjeb ɡurebɬi jan
betʼjerhanasul tsʼaraldasan aburab ʒo ɬuɡʔintʃʼoni wa ɡʔjes abuqχe kːetʃʼoni ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasul raɡʼi ɡuro ʒindijeɡo bokʔarab bitsunew awaraɡ wuɡo ɡʔjew ɡʔjesukʔa χʼinqʼuɡe

betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔaldasa χalqʼalɡi naqχe qʼotʼarab nuʒetsa ɡʔjeb rakʔɡi kwerde bosarab wa ɡʔjezul ʃaɡʔarazdeɡi minabazdeɡi nuʒ raqχarab meχaɬ
ɡʔjeb betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔurab rakʔ ɬabide bikʔje wa ʃːibab butʼajalda tso tso ʃaɡʔar tʼasa biʃːe kinabniɡi ɬabɡo ʃaɡʔar tsinɡi ɡʔjel ʃaɡʔarazuqχe nuχ ɡʔabe wa bitʃːante betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔurab rakʔalda toχɬukʔje tʃi tʃʼwaraw insan ɡʔjeniwe ɬutize
ɬideɡo rokʔuqʼɬi tsːin ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo toχɬukʔje tʃi tʃʼwan wuɡoni ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasul iχtijar buɡo ʒindirɡo ɡʼumru χwasar ɡʔabizeɬun ɡʔjel ʃaɡʔarazde ɬutize
masala pulanaw tʃi ɡʔalmaʁɡun tsadaqχ roχʔowe tsʼul ɡʔabize un wuɡoni wa ɡʔjes tsʼulade χʔwaɡʼarab ɡʼoʃːtʼodasa toχɬukʔjeɡo bortarab beɡʼjerab maχːɡi ʃːun ɡʔjesul ɡʔalmaʁ χwani ɡʔjew tʃi ɡʔjeb ɬababɡo ʃaɡʔaraɬul tsojaɬuwe ɬutize beɡʔula ʒindirɡo ɡʼumru tsʼunizeɬun
amma ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔar tsʼaqʼɡo rikʼkʼada buɡoni qʼisas bosules ɡʔjesda χaduwɡi ɡʼuntʼun tsːidakʔje ɡʔjew tʃʼwaze res buɡo ɡʔjedinaw tʃijin abuni tʃʼwaze mustaχʼiqʼaw ɡʔjetʃʼo tʃʼwarasdeχun ɡʔjesul tsːin bukʼintʃʼjeɬul
ɡʔjedinɬidalin ditsa duda ɬazaburab ɬabɡo ʃaɡʔar batʼa ɡʔabejan
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒer umumuze raɡʼi kʔuna nuʒer rakʔal ɡʼatʼid ɡʔarilin nuʒer umumuze kʔjelin ɡʔjedaral rakʔal ɡʔjes nuʒee kʔjeze ruɡo
ʒaqʼa ditsa zaɡʔir ɡʔarural ɡʔjesul amrabi muχʼkanɡo tʼurazaruni betʼjerhan allaɡʔ nuʒee χiraɬani wa ɡʔjesul qʼanunazda reqʼarab ɡʼumruɡi ɡʔabuni ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjeb ɬababɡo ʃaɡʔaralde tʼade ʒeɡi ɬabɡo ʃaɡʔar tʼasa biʃːe
ɡʔjedin ɡʔabe betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee irsaɬe kʔurab rakʔalda ɡʼajibɡo ɡʔjetʃʼjeb bi ɡʼodobe tʼjetʃʼoɡo bukʼine wa ɡʔjeb bidul ɡʼajibijalɬun nuʒɡo kːetʃʼoɡo rukʼine ɡʼolo
amma ɬitsaniɡi ɡʔalmaʁasdeχun tsːinɡi rekʼjeɬ χʔiχʔun ɡʔjesije ʁorkʔtʃʼjel ɡʔabuni wa tʼadɡi retʃʼtʃʼun ɡʔjewɡi tʃʼwan ʒiwɡo ɡʔjel ʃaɡʔarazul tsojalde ɬutani
ɡʔjew tʃʼwadaruqχanas ɡʼumru ɡʔabuleb ʃaɡʔaraɬul kʼudijaz ɡʔjesda χadur tʃaɡʼi ritʼize kːola ɡʔjew ɡʔjenisa naqχe watʃine tsinɡi ɡʔjew kʔjeze kːola bidul qʼisas bosulesul kwerde ɡʔjes tʃʼwaze wukʼine
ɡʔjesda ɡurχʼuɡe ɡʼajib ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo ɡʼodobe tʼurab bidul munaɡʔaldasa ɡʼizrail tsʼune nuʒeeɡo ɬikʼ bukʼine
maduɡʔalasulɡun buɡeb ɡʼorqχi kidaniɡi dobeɡʼan tsʼaɡe ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb buɡo nuʒer umumuz ɬurab betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔural rakʔazul ɡʼorqχi
pulanaw tʃijas ɡʔaburab kweʃɬi taqʼsiraɬe diwanχanajalda χʼukmu qʼotʼize kːani tsoχʼo tʃijasul nuɡʼɬi ɡʼolaro kinab ɡʼajib tʃijasde ɡʼuntʼizabuleb buɡoniɡi ɡʔjeb tasdiqʼ ɡʔabula kʼiɡo jaɡi ɬabɡo tʃijasul nuɡʼɬijaldaɬun
naɡaɡʔ tsoniɡi tʃijas ɡʔjeresijab nuɡʼɬiɡi ɡʔabun tsoɡidaw ɡʼajibijawɬun kːezawulew wuɡoni
ɡʔjew kʼijawɡo tʃi betʼjerhanasda tsewe watʃine kːola ɡʔjenir ruɡel kaʃiʃzabazɡun diwantʃaɡʼaz χʼukmu qʼotʼize
diwantʃaɡʼaz ɡʔjeb iʃaɬul muχʼkanɡo tsʼjeχ reχ ɡʔabize kːola wa ɡʔjew tʃijas ɡʔjeresijab nuɡʼɬiɡi ɡʔabun ʒindirɡo χalqʼtsojasda buɡʔtan ɬun bukʼin tʼatani
ɡʔjes tsoɡidase ɡʔabizeqχin bukʼarab ʒo ɡʔjesije ʒindijeɡo ɡʔabize kːola ɡʔjedinab kweʃɬi nuʒedaɡo ɡʔorkʔob bitʃːaɡe
ɡʔjeb raɡʼidal kinalɡo χʼinqʼila wa tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔjedinab χʼaliχʔaɬi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɬitsaniɡi ɡʔabilaro
ɡurχʼjel ɡʔabuɡe ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasda ɡʼumrujaɬuqχ ɡʼumru beraɬuqχ ber ɡʼusaɬuqχ ɡʼus kweraɬuqχ kwer boχaɬuqχ boχ

tuʃbabiɡun raʁ kːani wa nuʒeda biχʔani ɡʔjezul nuʒedasa ɡʼjemer tsʼikʼkʼaral tʃujalɡi tʃolɡʔakalɡi raʁuqχabiɡi rukʼin nuʒ ɡʔjezukʔa χʼinqʼuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul nuʒ misrijaldasa qʼwatʼire ratʃaraw betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wukʼine wuɡeɬul nuʒeda tsadaqχ
bitʃːante raʁ bajbiχʔilalde raʁuqχabazda tseweɡi waqχun kaʃiʃ kʼaɬaze
ɡʔjes abize bitʃːaj ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ ɡʼjenekːe nuʒ ʒaqʼa tuʃbabiɡun raʁize ruɡo nuʒ qʼwakʼun tʃʼa ɡʔjezukʔa χʼinqʼuɡe naqχe qʼaɡe wa ɡʔjezda tsebe rakʼ tʼurkʼize bitʃːaɡe
betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wukʼine wuɡo nuʒeda tsadaqχ nuʒer tuʃbabazda dande waʁize wa nuʒee berɡʔjenɬi kʔjeze muradalda
χadub bitʃːante tsereqχabaz raʁuqχabazda abize nuʒer ɬitsaniɡi tsʼijab mina ban batani amma ʒeɡi ɡʔjeniwe waqχun watitʃʼoni witʃːante ɡʔjew roqʼowe tʼadwusːine ɡuroni ɡʔjew raʁda tʃʼwaze beɡʔula tsinɡi ɡʔjesul minajaɬuwe tsoɡidaw waqχina wa tsoɡidas tʼobitʼila tsʼijab minajalde raqχinaɬul suχʼmatɡi
ɬitsaniɡi tsʼolbol aχ ɡʼjezabun batani amma ʒeɡi ɡʔjenisa piqχaɬul pajda bosun batitʃʼoni witʃːante ɡʔjew roqʼowe tʼadwusːine ɡuroni ɡʔjew raʁda tʃʼwaze beɡʔula tsinɡi ɡʔjesul aχil piqχaldasa tsoɡidas pajda bosila
nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔosa ɬijeniɡi jas abun jatani amma ʒeɡi bertin ɡʔabun batitʃʼoni witʃːante ɡʔjew roqʼowe tʼadwusːine ɡuroni ɡʔjew raʁda tʃʼwaze beɡʔula wa ɡʔjesul aburajɡi tʃijatsa jatʃina
χadub χalqʼaɬul tsereqχabaz abize kːola nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔow watani rakʼ χʼinqʼaraw jaɡi tamaχaw tʃi witʃːante ɡʔjedinaw tʃi roqʼowe tʼadwusːine tsoɡidazulɡi rakʼal tamaχɬitʃʼoɡo rukʼine jan
ɡʔjeldasa χadub bitʃːante ɡʔjez askarazda tʼad raʁul tsereqχabi teze
ʃaɡʔaralde tʼade ɡʔuʒum ɡʔabilalde tsebe tsin nuʒerɡun raqʼlil qʼotʼi qʼaj ɡʔabize res kʔje ɡʔjezije
ʃaɡʔaraɬul ʒamaɡʼat ɡʔjelda raziɬani wa ɡʔjez nuʒee kawabi raɡʔani ritʃːante ɡʔjel nuʒeda tsere χʼaltʼize
amma ɡʔjez nuʒerɡun raqʼlil qʼotʼi qʼaj ɡʔabitʃʼoni ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔar swerun kːwe
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔar nuʒer kwerde kʔun χadub ɡʔjenir rataral tʼolalɡo biχʔinal tʃʼwaj
rutʃːabiɡi ɬimalɡi ɡʼi botsʼiɡi nuʒeeɡo dawlaɬun bose ɡʔjeb kinabɡo tuʃbabazul buɡoɬijaldasa pajda bose betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔun buɡeɬul ɡʔjeb
ɡʔjedin ɡʔabe nuʒedasa rikʼkʼada ruɡel batʼijal rakʔazul χalqʼazul ʃaɡʔaraze
amma betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee irsaɬe kʔurab rakʔaɬul ʃaɡʔarazda tsoniɡi insan tʃʼaɡo toɡe
tʼuran tʼaɡʼinare ɡʔjel χitijalɡi amorijalɡi χanaanijalɡi perizijalɡi χiwijalɡi jewusijalɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul raɡʼuda reqʼon
ɡuroni ɡʔjez nuʒɡi kutsaze ruɡo ʒiderɡo allaɡʔzabaze ɡʔjez ɡʔarulel qχubal iʃazde wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsere nuʒ munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːeze ruɡo
ʃaɡʔar ɡʼjemerab meχaɬ swerun kːun buɡoni ɡʔjenir ruɡel ʁutʼbuze zaral ɡʔabuɡe ɡʔjezda ɡʼaʃːtʼi qχwaɡe ɡʔjezdasan piqχ kwanaj amma ʁutʼbi qʼotʼuɡe awlaqχalda ruɡel ʁutʼbi ɡʼadamal ɡureɬul ɡʔjezda dande raʁ ɡʔabize kːani
piqχ biʒularel ʁutʼbi qʼotʼize beɡʔula wa ʃaɡʔar swerun kːweze ʃːulaɬabi raze χʼaltʼizarize beɡʔula duda dande tʃʼarab ʃaɡʔar kwerde bosizeɡʼan

duje betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔalda kibɡʼaɡi ɡʼalaχalda insanasul ʒanaza batani wa ɡʔjew tʃi ɬitsa tʃʼwarawali ɬaze res ɡʔjetʃʼoni
bitʃːante nuʒer kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazɡi diwantʃaɡʼazɡi ɡʔjeb bakʼaldasa sweruqχ ruɡel ʃaɡʔarazde buɡeb manzil bortsine
wa biʃːun ɡʼaɡardeɡʼanaseb ʃaɡʔar tʼasa biʃːize bitʃːante ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔaraɬul kʼudijal tʃaɡʼaz batʃine ʒeɡi ɡarbida rukʔɡi batʃʼjeb χʼaltʼizabitʃʼjeb ɡʼatʃʼar
χadub ɡʔjez ɡʔjeb ɬaral raɡʼalda buɡeb awlaqχalde ʒeɡi kidaɡo χʔonɡi χʔatʃʼjeb χurɡi bekʔitʃʼjeb bakʼalde batʃina wa ɡʔjenib ɡʔjeb ɡʼatʃʼaraɬul ɡabur bekila
lewijil naslujaɬul kaʃiʃzabiɡi rukʼine kːola ɡʔjenir ɡʔjelɬidal betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa riʃːaral ɡʔjesije qχuluqχaɬe tʃʼjeze wa nuʒee duɡʼaɡi ɡʔabize ɡʔjezul raɡʼudaɬun ɬuɡʼize kːola bokʔarab daɡʼba qʼets wa kʔal
χadub ɡʔjeb ʒanaza batarab bakʼaldasa biʃːun ɡʼaɡarda buɡeb ʃaɡʔaraɬul kʼudijal tʃaɡʼaz ɬaraqχ ɡabur bekarab dob ɡʼatʃʼaralda tʼadɡi kːun kweral tʃurize kːola
bitʃːante ɡʔjez abize niʒer kweraz ɡʔjew tʃijasul bi ɡʼodobe tʼjetʃʼo niʒer berazda ɡʔjebɡi biχʔitʃʼo
ja betʼjerɡʔan tʼasaɬuɡʔa dutsaɡo χwasar ɡʔaburab durɡo χalqʼ ɡʼizrailil aɡʔlujaldasa ɡʼajib ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo ɡʼodobe tʼurab bijaɬuqχ durɡo χalqʼ ɡʼizrailal ʒawabalde aχʼuɡe ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjeb bijaɬul ɡʼajib nuʒede kːelaro
ɡʔjedin betʼjerhanasul amru tʼubazabijaldaɬun nuʒ tʃijar bijaɬul ɡʼajibaldasa ratsʼtsʼadalɬun rukʼina
raʁ kːarab meχaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tuʃbabi nuʒer kwerde kʔjedal wa dutsa ɡʔjel asirɬude ratʃindal
naɡaɡʔ asirazda ɡʔorkʔoj bertsinaj tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan jiχʔani ɡʔjeɬuqχ rokʔi kːani wa ɡʔjej dujeɡo jatʃine bokʔani
ɡʔjej durɡo roqʼoje jatʃe bitʃːante ɡʔjeɬ betʼjerɡi kʼkʼwaze maɬalɡi qʼuntsʼize
asirɬijaɬul retʼjelɡi χisize
naɡaɡʔ ɡʔjej duje rekʼjee ɡʼolej ɡʔjetʃʼoni dutsa ɡʔjej ʒindijeɡo bokʔaraɬuje ine jitʃːante dur iχtijar ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjej jitʃize jaɬuni laʁɬun ɡʔajize ʃːajɡureɬul dutsa ɡʔjeɬulɡun busen ɡʼaχʔal ɡʔabidal
pulanaw tʃijasul kʼiɡo ɬadi jiɡoni tso jokʔulej tsoɡidaj jokʔularej kʼijazulɡo wasalɡi ruɡoni amma biʃːun kʼudijaw was jokʔularej ɬadutsa ɡʔawuraw wuɡoni
ɬimalazda ɡʔorkʔob irs bikʔuleɬul biʃːun kʼudijaw wasase bukʼine kːoleb butʼa jokʔularej ɬadul wasɡi maχʼrum ɡʔawun jokʔulej ɬadul wasase kʔjeze beɡʔularo
jokʔularej ɬadul was tʼotsewe ɡʔawuraw wukʼinalda raziɬize kːola ɡʔjew wa ɡʔjesije kʔjeze kːola kinabɡo ʒindirɡo mal mulkaldasa kʼiɡo nuχaɬ tsʼikʼkʼarab butʼa ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjew wuɡo ɡʔjesul biχʔinab qʼuwataɬul tʼotsebeseb tʃʼil tʼotsewesew wasasul iχtijaralɡi ɡʔjesuqχ rukʼuna
ɬilniɡi wuɡoni qʼosarab ɡʼamalɡi buɡew maɬarabɡi ɡʔabularew kiɡʼan tamiχʼ ɡʔabuniɡi ebel insuqχɡi ɡʼjenekːularew was
bitʃːante insutsaɡi ebelaɬɡi ɡʔjew watʃine ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabaqχe
ɡʔjez kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazda abize kːola niʒer wasasul meqʼab ɡʼamal buɡo maɬarabɡi ɡʔabuleb ɡʔjetʃʼo niʒeqχ ɡʼjenekːulewɡi ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʼitsʼɡo kwanazeɡi ɡʔjeqʼoldizeɡi ɬala ɡʔjesda jan
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ʃaɡʔaraɬul tʼolalɡo biχʔinaz ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjew ɡʔjedinab χʼaliχʔaɬi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob toɡe kːarab ʒo kinalɡo ɡʼizrailazda raɡʼidal ɡʔjel χʼinqʼila ɡʔjedinab ʒojaldasa
tʃʼwaze mustaχʼiqʼab taqʼsiraɬuqχ tamiχʼɡi ɡʔabun ɬil bukʼaniɡi ʒanaza ʁotʼoda dalizabun buɡoni
sordo ban ɡʔjeb ɡʔjenib teze beɡʔularo ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ ɡʔjew wuqʼize kːola ʃːajɡureɬul ʁotʼoda waraw tʃi allaɡʔasul naɡʼana ʃːwaraw tʃi kːola betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee irsaɬe kʔurab rakʔ qχubɬizabuɡe

duda biχʔani tʃijar ɡʼaka jaɬuni tʃaqχu reqχadasaɡi batʼaɬun nuχ qʼosun kːun bukʼin ɡʔjeb biχʔitʃʼjeb χwel ɡʔabuɡe χwaʒainasuqχe ʃːwezabe
ɡʔjew tʃi dudasa rikʼkʼada watani jaɡi χʼajwanaɬul χwaʒain ʃːiw kːolewali duda ɬaleb batitʃʼoni ɡʔjeb duqχeɡo batʃe ɡʔjelda χaduw χwaʒain watʃʼineɡʼan durɡo roqʼobɡi χʔiχʔun tsinɡi naqχe kʔje
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔabe tʃijar χʼama retʼjel jaɡi bokʔarab ɬiqχaniɡi bilarab ʒo batani kumek ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo askʼosa unɡe
duda biχʔani ɬilniɡi χʼama jaɡi ots ɡʼodob kːun bukʼin biχʔitʃʼjeb χwelɡi ɡʔabun naqχe unɡe ɡʔjeɬul χwaʒainase kumek ɡʔabe ɡʔjel tʼade raqχinarize
tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬ biχʔintʃijasul partal retʼine beɡʔularo biχʔintʃijas tʃʼuʒuɡʼadanaɬul partalɡi retʼine beɡʔularo ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjedinab iʃ ɡʔabulew tʃi betʼjerhan allaɡʔase kutakalda riχaraw wuɡo
nuχda uneɬul ʁotʼoda tʼad jaɬuni ɡʼodob nuχda χʼantʃʼil busen batani wa ɡʔjenib ʒindirɡo tʼantʃʼiɡun jaɡi χanalɡun ebelab χʼintʃʼ batani χʼintʃʼɡi ɡʔjeɬul tʼantʃʼiɡi tsadaqχ rosuɡe dujeɡo
dutsa tʼantʃʼi rosize beɡʔula amma ɡʔjezul ebel bitʃːante ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuni duje ɬikʼ bukʼina wa χalatab ɡʼumruɡi kʔjela
tsʼijab mina balaɡo ɡʔjeɬul tʼoχaɬul raɡʼalɬabazda swerun ʒo kːwe
tsʼolbol aχikʔ tsoɡi batʼijab χʔon tʃʼoɡe tʃʼani ɡʔjeb kinabɡo duje χʼaramab bukʼine buɡo dutsa tʃʼarab χʔonaɬul batʃʼinɡi tsʼolbol ʁabujaɬul piqχɡi
otsɡi χʼamaɡi tsadaqχ tso puruts rukʔalda baɡe
kwasul wa ɬoɬol kunɡi tsadaqχ χʼaltʼizabun ɡʔaburab χːamil buqʼarab partal retʼunɡe
dutsaɡo retʼuneb partalaɬul aχada unqʼabɡo bokʼnida ɡʼjertelal
pulanaw tʃijas pulanaj jas ʒindijeɡo ɬadiɬun jatʃani amma ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡun χadub ɡʔjesije ɡʔjej jokʔitʃʼoni
wa ɡʔjeɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ matsʼal ɡʔarize ʒuwani ditsa doj ɡʼadan jatʃana amma ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡidal ɡʔjej jasɡʼadan jatitʃʼo janɡi abun
bitʃːante jasaɬul ebel insutsa ɡʔjej jasɡʼadan jikʼarajɬi tasdiqʼ ɡʔabuleb χʼuʒa bosize ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabaqχe kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazuqχe
wa bitʃːante insutsa kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazda abize ditsa dirɡo jas kʔuna ɡʔaw tʃijase rosase ɡʔanʒejin abuni ɡʔjesije ɡʔjej riχun jiɡo
dur jas jasɡʼadan jiɡin abize bakʼ dida batitʃʼo janɡi abun ɡʔaw tʃijas buɡʔtanal ɬolel ruɡo dir jasalda ɡʔale ɡʔjej jasɡʼadan jikʼarajɬi biχʔizabuleb χʼuʒa
tsinɡi ʃarʃaw biχʔizabe kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazda
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ kʼudijal tʃaɡʼaz ɡʔjew tʃijase tamiχʼ ɡʔabize kːola
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔjesuqχa ɡʼakʼa baqχize kːola nusɡo ʃekel batsʼtsʼadab ɡʼartsul
amma ɡʔjesul raɡʼi bitʼarab batani ɡʔjej jasɡʼadanɡi jikʼun jatitʃʼoni
bitʃːante ɡʔjej ɡʼadan ɡʔjeɬul insul minajaɬul kawuduqχe jatʃine ɡʔjenij ʃaɡʔaraɬul biχʔinaz ɡʔjej ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔob surarab iʃ ɡʔaburaɬuqχ ʒindirɡo insul roqʼoj jikʼaɡo sajaqχɡo χʔwadaraɬuqχ ɡʔjedinab kweʃɬi nuʒedaɡo ɡʔorkʔosa tʼaɡʼinabe
tʃijar ɬadiɡun tsoniɡi tʃi weɡun wukʼarawɬi tʼatani ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjedinab kweʃɬi ɡʼizrailaldasa tʼaɡʼinabe
ʃaɡʔaralda ʒanib pulanaw biχʔintʃijasda tʃijae aburaj jas dandtʃʼwani wa ɡʔjew ɡʔjejɡun weɡani
ɡʔjel kʼijalɡo ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabaqχeɡi ratʃun ɡʔjenir ɡantʃʼitsa tʃʼwaze kːola jas kumekaɬe tʃaɡʼi aχʼitʃʼjeɬuqχ biχʔintʃijan abuni ʒindirɡo rakʔtsojase aburaj jasɡʼadan basra ɡʔajuraɬuqχ ɡʔjedinab kweʃɬi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼaɡʼinabe
pulanaw biχʔintʃijas awlaqχalda dandtʃʼwaraj wa tʃijae aburaj jasalda tʼadeɡi ɬuɡʔun ɡʔjej basra ɡʔajuni ɡʼitsʼɡo biχʔintʃi tʃʼwaze kːola
jasaɬe kinabɡʼaɡi tamiχʼ ɡʔabuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeɬ ʃːibɡo χwalije mustaχʼiqʼab ʒo ɡʔabitʃʼjeɬul ɡʔjeb buɡo ɬitsa bukʼaniɡi toχɬukʔjeɡo tʼadɡi retʃʼtʃʼun tʃi tʃʼwaj ɡʼadab ʒo
awlaqχalda jiχʔaraj tʃijae aburaj jasalda tʼade ɬuɡʔidal ɡʔjew biχʔintʃi wa ɡʔjej aχʼdaniɡi aχʼdetʃʼoniɡi kumek ɡʔarun ɡʔjeɬije kumekaɬe tʃi wukʼintʃʼjeɬul
kinaw wukʼaniɡi biχʔintʃijasda jiχʔani ʒeɡi ɬijeɡo abitʃʼjej jasɡʼadan wa ɡʔjew ɡʔjejɡun weɡani wa ɡʔjel tʼad kːuni
ɡʔjes jasaɬul insuje kʼiqʼojalda antsʼɡo ʃekel
tsoniɡi biχʔintʃi ʒindirɡo insul ɬadiɡun weɡize beɡʔularo ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb iʃ emen inʒit ɡʔawi kːola

betʼjerhanasul dinijab dandeɬijalde watʃʼine beɡʔularo χʼanaze ʒaʁalɬi kːaraw jaɬuni biχʔinɬi naqχe qʼotʼaraw tsoniɡi tʃi
qʼwatʼuɬa ɡʔawuraw tʃiɡi betʼjerhanasul dinijab dandeɬijalde witʃːaze beɡʔularo ɡʔjedinɡo antsʼabileb kʔjeralde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjesul tsoniɡi nasluɡi betʼjerhanasul dinijab dandeɬijalde witʃːaze beɡʔularo
ɡʔjedinɡo ammonijawɡi moɡʼawijawɡi antsʼabileb kʔjeralde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjezul tsoniɡi nasluɡi betʼjerhanasul dandeɬijalde ratʃʼine beɡʔularo ɡʔjeb buɡo abadijab qʼanun
ʃːajɡureɬul nuʒ misrijaldasa ratʃʼuneb meχaɬ ɡʔjez tʃed tsʼamɡun
amma betʼjerhan allaɡʔas qʼabul ɡʔabitʃʼo ɡʔjeb wa ɡʔjesul naɡʼana barakatalde swerizabuna ʃːajɡureɬul betʼjerhan allaɡʔase nuʒ χirijal rukʼun
ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʼumrujalda ʒanib kidaniɡi ɡʔjezulɡun ɡʔudulɬi kːoɡe wa ʃːibniɡi ɬikʼɬi ɡʔjezije ɡʔabuɡe
edomijawɡun rokʔuqʼɡo wukʼunɡe ɡʔjew dur watsɬidal ɡʔjedinɡo misrijawɡunɡi ʃːajɡureɬul munɡi ɡʔjesul ulkajalda aparaɡɬun wukʼindal
nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼaral ɡʔjezul ɬimalazul ɬimal betʼjerhanasul dinijab dandeɬijalde qʼabul ɡʔarize beɡʔula
tuʃbabazda dande raʁizeɬun qʼaji tʃʼwarab bakʼalda kinab bataniɡi qχubɬi bitʃːaɡe
naɡaɡʔ qʼasi sardiɬ nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɬilniɡi mani batʃʼani wa ɡʔjeldaɬun pulanaw tʃi qχubɬani ɡʔjew tʃi χalqʼaldasa doweɡʼanɡi un ɡʔjeniw tʃʼjeze kːola
baqʼanida ɡʔjes tʃerχ tʃurize kːola wa baqʼ tʼjerχʔarabɡo χalqʼ tʃʼarab bakʼalde tʼad wusːine beɡʔula
nuʒ tʃʼarab bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼibeχun tso bakʼ tʼasa biʃːe χʼaʒat tʼubajaɬe
jaraʁalda tsadaqχ duqχ bukʼine kːola rakʔ buqχize sanaɡʼatab alat χʼaʒat tʼubaleb meχaɬ ɡwend buqχize wa χadub ɡʔjelda tʼade rakʔ qχwaze bukʼine
betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wukʼine wuɡeɬul nuʒɡun nuʒ tsʼunize wa tuʃbabi nuʒer kwerde kʔjeze ɡʼolo ɡʔjedinɬidal nuʒ tʃʼarab bakʼ batsʼtsʼadɡo bukʼine kːola ɡʔjesda ʃːibɡo qχubɬi ɡʔjenib biχʔunɡutʼize wa ɡʔjes nuʒede muʁ reχitʃʼoɡo bukʼine
ɬutun duqχe waχtʃize watʃʼaraw laʁ ɡʔjesul χwaʒainasuqχe kʔoɡe
witʃːante ɡʔjew nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔow ʒindijeɡo bokʔarab ʃaɡʔaralda ɡʼumru ɡʔabun wukʼine ɡʔjesije zulmu ɡʔabuɡe
ɡʼizrailazul tsoniɡi tʃi ja biχʔinal ja rutʃːabi maʒusijaz ɡʔabuleb ɡʼadab dinijab qχaχʼbaɬijalde
qχaχʼbajaɬuqχ ʃːwarab jaɬuni ɡʔoj bitʃun
durɡo rakʔtsojase qʼarzaɬe ɡʼarats jaɡi kinab bataniɡi niɡʼmat jaɡi tsoɡi ʃːib bukʼaniɡi kʔoleb buɡoni ɡʔjelda tʼade dujeɡo χajir bosuɡe
dutsa batʼijab millataɬul tʃaɡʼazuqχa bosize beɡʔula tʼokʼbortʃʼarab pajda χajir amma durɡo watsasuqχa bosuɡe ɡʔjebmeχaɬ mun unew wuɡeb wa dutsa kwerde bosize buɡeb rakʔalda betʼjerhan allaɡʔasɡi sunduɬɡoɡi duje kwerbaqʼila
betʼjerhan allaɡʔase dutsa kinabɡʼaɡi nazru ɡʔabun buɡoni ɡʔjeb χeχɡo tʼubazabe ɡuroni betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dudasa ɡʔjeb tʼalab ɡʔabila wa mun munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːela
nazru ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo wukʼani duje munaɡʔ bukʼinaro
amma ʃːibniɡi ɡʔabilin raɡʼi kʔun buɡoni ɡʔjeb tʼubazabe munɡo raziɬun betʼjerhan allaɡʔase nazru ɡʔabun buɡeɬul durɡo kʼalaɬ
durɡo rakʔtsojasul tsʼolbol aχikʔa ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan piqχ kwanaze beɡʔula amma ɡʔjenisa qʼwatʼibe ʃːibɡo bosuɡe
tsoɡidasul χurib ɬiɬari ɡʔabuleb meχaɬ kweraz dujeɡo tʼoral rakʼarize beɡʔula amma χaritselɡi χʔwaɡʼun tʃijar batʃʼin dujeɡo bakʼaruɡe

pulanaw tʃijas ɬadi jatʃani wa tsadaqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔindal ɡʔjeɬuɬ tso reqʼetʃʼjeb ʒoɡi batun ɡʔjej ɡʔjesije riχani ɡʔjes jatʼa ɡʔajijaɬul kaʁat qχwaze beɡʔula wa ɡʔjebɡi ɡʔjeɬuqχe kʔun ɡʔjej ʒindirɡo roqʼosa naqχe jitʼize beɡʔula
ɡʔjesdasa jatʼaɬun χaduj ɡʔjej tsoɡi tʃijase rosase ine beɡʔula
amma kʼiabilew rosaseɡi ɡʔjej riχani wa jatʼa ɡʔajijaɬul kaʁatɡi kʔun ɡʔjesɡi ʒindirɡo roqʼosa naqχe jitʼani jaɡi ɡʔjeɬul kʼiabilew ros χwani
tʼotsewesew rosasul iχtijar ɡʔjetʃʼo tsʼidasan ɡʔjej jatʃine ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjesije ɡʔjej χʼaramaj jikʼuna ɡʔjedinab iʃ betʼjerhanase kutakalda riχarab buɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔurab rakʔ ɡʔjedinal munaɡʔazdaɬun qχubɬizabuɡe
ɡʔanʒeɡo ɡʔanʒe ɬadi jatʃaraw tʃi raʁde witʼize beɡʔularo jaɬuni tsoɡi batʼijab bortʃ ɡʔjesda tʼad ɬeze beɡʔularo witʃːante ɡʔjew tso ɬaɡʼjel ineɡʼan ʒindirɡo jatʃaraj ɬadiɡi razi ɡʔajun paraχat roqʼow wukʼine
ʁorkʔɬalije kwerzul ɡʔobo wa ɡʔjeɬul tʼasijab raqχtsin bosuɡe ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeb baʃːaɬula insanasuqχa ɡʔjesul tʃed χinkʼ baqχijalda
ɬitsaniɡi ʒindirɡo wats ɡʼizrailaw wiqʼani wa laʁ χʼisabalda χʼaltʼizawuni jaɡi ɡʼartsuqχ witʃani ɡʔjew tʼadɡi kːuni ɡʔjew tʃi tʃʼwaze kːola ɡʔjedinab kweʃɬi nuʒedaɡo ɡʔorkʔosa naqχe tʼaɡʼinabe
barasaɬul untuda χurχun kinabɡo tʼubazabe lewijil qʼawmaɬul kaʃiʃzabaz maɬuqχe nuʒetsa muχʼkanɡo tʼubazabize kːola ditsa ɡʔjezije amru ɡʔabunʃːinab ʒo
nuʒ misrijaldasa ratʃʼuneɬul dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔas marjamije ɡʔaburab kʼotʃonɡe
dutsa ɬijeniɡi qʼarzaɬe ɡʼarats kʔoleb buɡoni ɡʔjeɬuqχ ʁorkʔɬalije ʒo bosize ɡʼolo ɡʔjesul roqʼowe ʒaniwe ɬuɡʔunɡe
qʼwatʼiweχunɡo tʃʼa wa dutsa qʼarzaɬe ɡʼarats kʔoles ʒintsaɡo qʼwatʼibe bosun batʃʼine te ʁorkʔɬel
ɡʔjew miskinaw tʃi watani ʁorkʔɬalije ɡʔjes kʔurab ɡʼaba qʼasi kʔiʒilalde naqχe ʃːwezabe
baqʼ tʼjerχʔinalde ɡʔjeb naqχe kʔje tsinɡi ɡʔjesije res bukʼina ʒindirɡo ɡʼabaɡi tʼad ban kʔiʒize wa ɡʔjesul rakʼɡi dudasa boχila ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔɡi duda raziɬila
kːun watʃaraw miskinaw paqʼiraw χʼaltʼuqχan qʼwarid ɡʔawuɡe ɡʔjew dur rakʔtsojaw wataniɡi jaɡi tʃijar rakʔaldasa watʃʼaraw dur ulkajaɬul ʃaɡʔarazul tsojalda tʃʼaraw tʃi wataniɡi
ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ baqʼ tʼjerχʔinalde ɡʔjesije χʼaltʼuqχ χarʒ kʔje ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjew miskintʃi wuɡeɬul wa ɡʔjeb χarʒalda barab ɡʼumru buɡeɬul ɡʔjesul ɡuroni ɡʔjew ɡʼarz baqχun betʼjerhanasde qʼwariɬaqχdila munɡi munaɡʔaɬukʔje kːela
ɬimalazul taqʼsir sababɬun umumul tʃʼwaze beɡʔularo umumuzul taqʼsir sababɬun ɬimalɡi tʃʼwaze beɡʔularo ʃːiwaw tʃi ʒindirɡo taqʼsir sababɬun χwela
aparaɡasulɡi besdalasulɡi iχtijaral χwezaruɡe qʼorolaɬuqχa ʁorkʔɬalije partal bosuɡe
duda kʼotʃonɡe munɡoɡi misrijalda laʁɬun wukʼarawɬi wa dur betʼjerhan allaɡʔas mun ɡʔjenisa tarqχan ɡʔawurawɬi ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔal dir amrabi tʼurazare
ɬiɬaruleb meχaɬ duda χurib ɡul kʼotʃon tani ɡʔjelda χaduw tʼad wusːunɡe bitʃːante ɡʔjeb aparaɡzabazeɡi besdalazeɡi qʼorolzabazeɡi bukʼine ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dutsa ɡʔabulebʃːinalda barakat ɬela
ʁutʼbuzdasa tʼilitsa buχun zajtun ʁenezabuleb meχaɬ kʼiabileb nuχaɬɡi tʼad wusːun χutʼa kʼutʃarab zajtun ʁenezabuɡe ʁutʼbuzda tʼad χutʼarab ʒo aparaɡzabazeɡi besdalazeɡi qʼorolzabazeɡi te
tsʼibil bakʼaruleb meχaɬ ʁabujalda ʒeɡi ʃːibniɡi χutʼun buɡiʃːali χal ɡʔabuɡe ɡʔjenib χutʼarab ʒo aparaɡzabazeɡi besdalazeɡi qʼorolzabazeɡi te
duda kʼotʃonɡe munɡoɡi misrijalda laʁɬun wukʼarawɬi ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔal dir amrabi tʼurazare

kʼiɡo tʃijasda ɡʔorkʔob daɡʼba qʼets kːani ɡʔjel diwanχanajalde ine kːola wa diwantʃaɡʼaz χʼukmuɡi qʼotʼila witʼaraw ritʼuqχ ɡʔawila ɡʼajibijase tamiχʼ ɡʔabila
ɡʼajibijaw kʔabize mustaχʼiqʼaw watani bitʃːante diwantʃijas ɡʔjeb bakʼaldaɡo ʒindirɡo berazda tsebe ɡʼodowɡi weɡizawun tʃan nuχaɬ kʔabize kːoleb bataniɡi ɡʔjediɡʼanab qʼadaralda ɡʔjesda kʔabize
amma kʼiqʼoɡojaldasa tsʼikʼkʼun kʔabize beɡʔularo tsʼaqʼɡo ɡʼjemerɡi kʔabun durɡo wats kinazdaɡo tsewe inʒitɬizawitʃʼoɡo wukʼine
χʼaltʼuleb buɡeb otsol kʼal buχʔunɡe
kʼiɡo wats tsadaqχ ɡʼumru ɡʔabun wuɡoni wa wasɡi naqχa tetʃʼoɡo tsojaw χwani χwarasul ɬadi tʃijae rosase ine beɡʔularo bitʃːante ɡʔjej ɡʔjesul watsas jatʃine wa watsasul bakʼalda ɡʔjeɬulɡun ros ɬadulab ɡʼumru ɡʔabize
ɡʔjeldasan ɡʔawuraw tʼotsewesew was χwarasul wasɬun rikʼkʼine kːola ɡʼizrailalda ɡʔjesul tsʼar tʼaɡʼintʃʼoɡo bukʼine
amma ɡʔjesije bokʔitʃʼoni χwaraw watsasul jikʼaraj ɬadi jatʃine ɡʔjej jatʃʼine kːola ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabaqχe kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazuqχe wa ɡʔjeɬ abize kːola dir χwaraw rosasul watsase bokʔun ɡʔjetʃʼo ʒindirɡo watsasul tsʼar ɡʼizrailalda tsʼunize wa watsasul bakʼalde ɬuɡʔine inkar ɡʔabuleb buɡo jan
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ʃaɡʔaraɬul kʼudijal tʃaɡʼaz ɡʔjew aχʼila wa ɡʔjewɡun kʼaɬala amma ɡʔjes tʼirun tʃʼun ɡʔjej jatʃine inkar ɡʔabuni
watsasul qʼorolaj jatʃʼine te ɡʔjesda askʼoje kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazul berazda jiχʔun bitʃːante ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjesul tso sandala tʼasa baqχize wa ɡʔjesul ɡʔurmadeɡi tun abize ɡʔadin ɡʔabula ʒindirɡo watsasul ruqʼ ɡʼutsʼularew tʃijase jan
ɡʔjew tʃijasul naslujalda ɡʼizrailaz tʼokʼtsʼar ɬeze buɡo χʔit baqχarasul aɡʔlu abun
kʼiɡojaw tsotsaɬ waʁulaɡo tsojasul ɬadi jatʃʼani rosase kumekaɬe wa ros wuχulesul ɡʼawrat qʼan kːuni
ɡʔjeɬul kwer qʼotʼje ɡurχʼuɡe ɡʔjelda
dur bukʼunɡe kʼiɡo batʼijab ɡira tso bakʼab bitʃun ʒo bosize tso tʼadaɡʔab witʃarize
dur roqʼob bukʼunɡe kʼiɡo batʼijab rotsen tso kʼudijab tso ɡʔitʼinab
dur ɡirabiɡi dur rotsenalɡi rukʼine te durusal wa ritʼaral betʼjerhan allaɡʔas duje kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔalda durɡo ɡʼumru χalaɬize
χʼaram ɡʔabulew tʃi ʃːiw tʃi ɡʔjew wataniɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔase kutakalda riχaraw wuɡo
misrijaldasa nuʒ ratʃʼuneɬul amalekijaz ɡʔaburabɡi kʼotʃonɡe
nuχda swakan tatu χun nuʒ rukʼaɡo ɡʔjel nuʒeda tʼade kʼantsʼana wa allaɡʔasukʔaɡi χʼinqʼitʃʼoɡo naqχa χutʼaralʃːinal χʼal daɡʔɬaral tʃʼwana ɡʔjez
ɡʔjedinɬidal nuʒee kʔurab rakʔalda betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒ paraχaɬizarurab wa kinalɡo tuʃbabazda tʼad nuʒee berɡʔjenɬi kʔurab meχaɬ amalekijazul tsʼar tʼaɡʼinabe dunjalaldasa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabize kʼotʃonɡe

kwatʼitʃʼoɡo nuʒ ʃːwela betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔalde wa ɡʔjebɡi kwerʃːalikʔje bosun ɡʔjenib nuʒetsa ɡʼumru ɡʔabize bajbiχʔila
duje betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔurab rakʔaldasa ʃːwarab batʃʼinaɬul tʼotseresel niɡʼmatal ɡʔaɡʔida ʒanirɡi ɬun betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼasa biʃːarab muqʼadasab bakʼalde ʃːwezare
ɡʔjenib kaʃiʃasda abe betʼjerhan allaɡʔ niʒer umumuze ɡʔjedun wukʼana ɡʔab rakʔ niʒee kʔjelilan ɡʔjedinɬidal dun watʃʼun wuɡo ɡʔab rakʔalda wuɡin dunilan abize
tsinɡi kaʃiʃas duqχa ɡʔjeɡʔ bosila wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul qʼurban bakʼalda tsebe ɬela
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsebe dutsa abe dir nekʼsijaw emen wukʼana aramejaw ɡʔjew misrijalde waqχana daɡʔal tʃaɡʼiɡun wa ɡʔjeniw ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼana aparaɡ χʼisabalda ɡʔjenib ɡʔjesdasan ɬuɡʔana kʼudijab qʼuwatab wa rikʼkʼjen ɡʼjemerab χalqʼ
amma misrijaz kweʃab berbalaɡʔi ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔana niʒedeχun zulmu χʼal ɡʔabun zaχʼmatɡo χʼaltʼizarulel rukʼana niʒ
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ niʒerɡo umumuzul betʼjerhan allaɡʔasde aχʼi bana niʒetsa wa betʼjerhanas ɡʔjeb qʼabul ɡʔabuna ɡʔjesda biχʔana niʒer qʼwariɬiɡi zaχʼmatab χʼaltʼiɡi zulmu χʼalɡi
wa betʼjerhanas niʒ misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃana ʒindirɡo qʼuwatab kweraldaɬun ɡutʃal iʃazdaɬun kʼudi kʼudijal muɡʼʒizatazdaɬun wa χʼikmaɬabazdaɬun
ɡʔjes ɡʔab bakʼalde ratʃana niʒ wa niʒee raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb ɡʔab rakʔ kʔuna
ɡʔale ɡʔanʒe betʼjerhan allaɡʔ ditsa rosun ratʃʼana dutsa kʔurab rakʔaldasa ʃːwarab tʼotsebeseb batʃʼinaɬul niɡʼmatal tsinɡi ɡʔjeɡʔ betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsebe ɬe wa ɡʔjesije suʒda ɡʔabe
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dujeɡi dur qχizan ɬimalazeɡi kʔurabʃːinaldasa woχun awadanɬi ɡʔabe bitʃːante dur awadanɬi ɡʼaχʔal ɡʔabize lewitazɡi nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔor tʃʼjel ɡʔabural batʼijal χalqʼazul tʃaɡʼazɡi
ʃːibab ɬababileb sonaɬ aj antsʼil butʼabazul sonaɬ kinabɡo ʒojaldasa antsʼil butʼa batʼa ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjeb kʔje lewitazeɡi tʃijar rakʔaldasa ratʃʼaral tʃaɡʼazeɡi besdalazeɡi qʼorolzabazeɡi nuʒer ʃaɡʔarazda ɡʔjelɡi ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwanaze rukʼine
wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda abe ditsa dirɡo roqʼosa χiraɬijaɬul butʼa bosana wa dur amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔjeb lewitazeɡi qʼwatʼisa ratʃʼaral tʃaɡʼazeɡi besdalazeɡi qʼorolzabazeɡi kʔuna dida dur tsoniɡi amru kʼotʃon tetʃʼo wa ɡʔjeb tʼubazabitʃʼoɡo tetʃʼo
χirijab antsʼil butʼajalda tʼasa bosun tʃi χwarab bakʼalda ditsa ʃːibɡo kwanatʃʼo qχubɬun wukʼaɡo ɡʔjelda tʼasa ʃːibɡo bositʃʼo wa χwarazul ruχʼaze ɡʔjelda tʼasa ʃːibɡo kʔjetʃʼo
χirijaw allaɡʔ zobalazdasa durɡo tʼadeɡʼanab roqʼosa walaɡʔje niʒeqχ durɡo χalqʼ ɡʼizrailazdeɡi wa dutsa niʒer umumuze kʔurab raɡʼuda reqʼon niʒee nasib ɡʔaburab raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb ulkajaldeɡi barakat reʃːtʼinabe
ʒaqʼa betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒ aχʼulel ruɡo ɡʔal qʼanunalɡi χʼukmabiɡi tʼurazarijalde tʼolabɡo ruχʼɡi ʒanɡi kʔun rakʼ rakʼaɬɡo tʼurazare ɡʔjel
ʒaqʼa nuʒetsa abuna betʼjerhan wuɡin nuʒer allaɡʔ ɡʔjesul nuχda χʔwadize wa ɡʔjesul qʼanunalɡi amrabiɡi χʼukmabiɡi tʼurazarize ruɡin wa ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼin tʼamize buɡin
ʒaqʼa betʼjerhanasɡi abuna ɡʔjes tsebekːunɡo abun bukʼaralda reqʼon nuʒ ɡʔjesul qʼimat tʼadeɡʼanab irs kːolin wa nuʒetsa ɡʔjesul amrabi tsʼunize kːolin
ɡʔjes abuna ʒintsa dunjalalda riʒaralʃːinal χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼadeɡʼan ɡʔarilin nuʒ nuʒee retsːɡi kʼodoɬiɡi qʼadruɡi kʔjelin wa ɡʔjes tsebekːun aburalda reqʼon nuʒ rukʼine ruɡin ɡʔjesul tʼasa biʃːarab χirijab χalqʼɬun

ɡʼizrailaɬul kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazda tsebe musatsa χalqʼalda abuna
ditsa ʒaqʼa nuʒee zaɡʔir ɡʔarural tʼolalɡo amrabi tʼurazare
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔ kwerde bosizeɬun iordan ɡʼurul dob raqχalde ʃːwedal ɡʔjenib kʼiɡo kʼudijab ɡamatʃʼ ɬe ɡʔjezda qχaχʼab ɡatʃɡi baχe
ɡʔjel ɡantʃʼazda qʼanunaɬul kinalɡo raɡʼabi qχwaj ɡʔjedin ɡʔabe iordan ɡʼurul dob raqχalde ʃːwedal nuʒer umumuzul betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔurab raɡʼuda reqʼon betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒee kʔoleb buɡeb raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb rakʔalde nuʒ ɬuɡʔinalda tsebe
ditsa maɬarab qʼaɡʼidajaɬ qχaχʼab ɡatʃɡi baχun ɡʔjel ɡantʃʼal ɬe ɡewal maɡʼarda iordanaɬul dob tsojab raqχalde ʃːwedal
ɡʔjenib betʼjerhan allaɡʔase ɡantʃʼil ɡʔabun qʼurban bakʼ baj ɡantʃʼida kwartʼaɡi kʼutʼitʃʼoɡo
betʼjerhan allaɡʔase qʼurban bakʼ baj bekʼkʼitʃʼjeb ɡantʃʼil wa ɡʔjelda tʼad betʼjerhan allaɡʔase tsʼadul qʼurbanal ɡʔare
ɡʔjedinɡo raqʼlil qʼurbanalɡi qχwe wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsebe kwanaj qʼurbanazul ɡʔan roχel awadanɬijalda
ɡʔab qʼanunaɬul tʼolalɡo raɡʼabi muχʼkanɡo wa jaqʼinɡo qχwaj nuʒetsa ɡʔjeb kʼijabɡo ɡantʃʼida tʼad
χadub musatsaɡi lewitazɡi kaʃiʃzabazɡi tʼolabɡo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abuna
ɡʼizrail kʼwar kʔun ɡʼjenekːe ɡʔanʒe nuʒ raqχana betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul χalqʼɬun
nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasuqχ ɡʼin tʼame wa ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒee zaɡʔir ɡʔarural ɡʔjesul amrabiɡi qʼanunalɡi tʼurazare
ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ musatsa χalqʼalde ɡʔadinab amru ɡʔabuna
iordanaɬul dob tsojab raqχalde ʃːwarab meχaɬ ɡerizim maɡʼarde tʼadeɡi raχun χalqʼaɬe barakataɬul duɡʼa ɡʔabize kːolel qʼawmal ɡʔale ʃimeonilɡi lewijilɡi jaɡʔudalɡi isːaχarilɡi jusupilɡi bunjaminilɡi qʼawmal
wa ɡewal maɡʼarda tʼadeɡi raχun naɡʼana kʔjejaɬul duɡʼa ɡʔabize kːolel qʼawmal ɡʔale ruwimilɡi ɡadilɡi aʃerilɡi zewulunilɡi danilɡi naftalilɡi qʼawmal
bitʃːante lewitaz kinazdaɡo raɡʼuleb χʼalaɬ ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda abize
bekʼkʼun jaɡi biun tʼun ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔ ɡʔaburaw wa baɬɡoɡo ɡʔjeb ɬuraw tʃijase naɡʼana buɡo ɡʔjeb buɡo betʼjerhanase riχarab ʒo ustarasul kwerzul χʼaltʼi
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
insul jaɡi ebelaɬul adab reχarab ʒo ɡʔaburaw tʃijase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
maduɡʔalasul ɡʼorqχi ʒanibe batʃaraw tʃijase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
betsːaw tʃi nuχdasa qʼosinawuraw tʃijase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
aparaɡzabazulɡi besdalazulɡi qʼorolzabazulɡi iχtijaral tsʼunularew tʃijase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
insul ɬaduda askʼow weɡaraw wa ɡʔjeldaɬun emen inʒit ɡʔawuraw tʃijase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
kinab bukʼaniɡi χʼajwanɡun qχubal ɡʔorkʔorɬabi ɡʔaruraw tʃijase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
ʒindirɡo jatsalda aj insul jaɬuni ebelaɬul jasalda askʼow weɡaraw tʃijase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
jakʔadalda askʼow weɡaraw tʃijase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
baɬɡo tʃi tʃʼwarase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
ɡʼartsuqχ ɡʼajibɡo ɡʔjetʃʼjew tʃi tʃʼwarase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin
ɡʔab qʼanunaɬuqχ ɡʼjenekːularew wa ɡʔjeb tʼubazabularew tʃijase naɡʼana buɡo
wa bitʃːante tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ abize amin

rakʼ rakʼaɬɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔase mutʼiɡʼɬani wa ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒee zaɡʔir ɡʔarural tʼolalɡo ɡʔjesul amrabazda reqʼon χʔwadani betʼjerhan allaɡʔas dunjalaɬulɡo χalqʼazdasa tʼadeɡʼan ɡʔarize ruɡo nuʒ
betʼjerhan allaɡʔase mutʼiɡʼɬani ɡʔale nuʒee bukʼine buɡeb barakat
ʃaɡʔaraldaɡi barakat bukʼina nuʒee awlaqχaldaɡi barakat bukʼina
nuʒer naslu bukʼina barakatab aχ χuraɬul batʃʼinɡi ɡʔarzaɬila nuʒer ɡʼi botsʼiɡi tsʼikʼkʼina ɡʼi botsʼul qʼinɬiɡi ɡʼjemerɬila
nuʒer ɡʔjeɡʔɡi qχabaɡi χʼjertʃɡi tʼasa tʃwaχila
qʼwatʼire uneɬulɡi nuʒee barakat roqʼore tʼadrusːuneɬulɡi barakat
nuʒeda dande raʁize tuʃbabi raqχani ɡʔjel ʁurize betʼjerhanas kumek ɡʔabila nuʒee nuʒeda dande ɡʔjel tso nuχkːun ratʃʼina amma ankʔɡo nuχkːun nuʒeqχa ɬutila
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas barakat reʃːtʼinabila nuʒer ɡʔor bokʔalde wa kinabɡo ɡʔabulebʃːinalde betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔurab rakʔalda ɡʔjes barakatalɬun ɡʔarila nuʒ
betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrabi tsʼunani wa ɡʔjesul nuχda χʔwadani ɡʔjes kʔurab raɡʼuda reqʼon betʼjerhanas ʒindirɡo χirijab χalqʼɬun ɡʔarila nuʒ
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ dunjalaɬulɡo χalqʼazda biχʔila nuʒ betʼjerhanasul χalqʼɬun rukʼin wa ɡʔjel nuʒekʔa χʼinqʼila
nuʒee kʔjelin nuʒer umumuze ɡʔjedun wukʼarab rakʔalda betʼjerhanas kinabɡo ɡʔarzaɡo kʔjela nuʒee ɬimalɡi ɡʼi botsʼiɡi aχ χuraɬul batʃʼinɡi
betʼjerhanas zobalazdasa ʒindirɡo betʃeɬijaɬul ʁamas raɡʔila nuʒee wa riɡʔ riɡʔalda tsʼadɡi tʃwaχizabila ɡʔabulebʃːinalda barakatɡi ɬela nuʒetsa ɡʼjemerab χalqʼaɬe ɡʼarats qʼarzaɬe kʔjela amma nuʒetsa ɬiqχaɡo bosize kːelaro
ʒaqʼa ditsa zaɡʔir ɡʔarural betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrabi muχʼkanɡo tʼurazarulel ruɡoni betʼjerhanas nuʒ ratʃʼɬun ɡurel betʼjerɬun ɡʔarila wa kidaɡo tʼaɬuda rukʼina ʁorkʔje kːelaro
ditsa nuʒeda maɬaral amrabazul tsoniɡijaldasa dore ɡʔanire kʔuruɡe batʼijal allaɡʔzabazda naqχ riɬːunɡe wa ɡʔjezije qχuluqχ ɡʔabuɡe
amma nuʒ betʼjerhan allaɡʔase mutʼiɡʼɬitʃʼoni wa ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒee zaɡʔir ɡʔarural betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul amrabiɡi qʼanunalɡi muχʼkanɡo tʼurazarulel ɡʔjetʃʼoni ɡʔal kinalɡo naɡʼanabi ratʃʼine ruɡo nuʒeda tʼade
ʃaɡʔaraldaɡi nuʒee naɡʼana awlaqχaldaɡi naɡʼana
nuʒer ɡʔjeɡʔɡi qχabaɡi χʼjertʃɡi naɡʼanadukʔje kːela
nuʒer ɬimalazeɡi naɡʼana aχ χuraɬul batʃʼinaɬeɡi naɡʼana wa nuʒer batʃazeɡi burtʼazeɡi kʔaɡʼazeɡi naɡʼana
qʼwatʼire uneɬulɡi nuʒee naɡʼana roqʼore tʼadrusːuneɬulɡi naɡʼana
betʼjerhanas nuʒeda tʼade bitʃːala naɡʼana taliχʼqʼosinɡi ɡʔabulebʃːinaɬuɬ bitʼɡʔjetʃʼoɬiɡi dunɡi reχun tun ɡʔarural kweʃɬabi sababɬun nuʒ tʼaɡʼinarila wa χeχab aχirɡi kːela nuʒee
betʼjerhanas kweʃal untabi ritʃːalelɡo ritʃːalel rukʼina nuʒeda tʼade nuʒetsa kwerde bosizeqχin buɡeb rakʔaldasa nuʒ tʼuran tʼaɡʼineɡʼan
betʼjerhanas nuʒeda tʼade bitʃːala ɡʔuʔruzul untiɡi tsʼadul untiɡi baqʼul buχʼiɡi raqʼdalɬiɡi buχʼarab ɡʔuriɡi kːal tʃʼwajɡi tʼuran tʼaɡʼineɡʼan ɡʔjel balaɡʔaz teze ɡʔjetʃʼo nuʒ
zobal nuʒee paχʔude swerila rakʔ maχːude swerila
betʼjerhanas χʼurul tsʼad bazabila nuʒer rakʔalde wa ɡʔjeb balebɡo baleb bukʼina nuʒ tʼuran χwezeɡʼan
betʼjerhanas nuʒer tuʃbabaze nuʒeda tʼad berɡʔjenɬi kʔjela tso nuχkːun ɡʔjezda dande raʁize ina nuʒ ankʔɡo nuχkːun ɡʔjezuqχa ɬutila ɡʔjeb qʼismat biχʔarabɡo tʼolalɡo χalqʼalɡi χʼinqʼila
nuʒer ʒanazabi zodil χʼantʃʼazeɡun ɡʼalχul ʒanawaraze dawlaɬun rukʼina wa ɡʔjel naqχe ʁeze tʃi wukʼinaro
betʼjerhanas nuʒeda tʼade ritʃːala misrijaɬul saχɬizarize kʼolarel retsʼtsʼutsa kwanalel tʼiχʔalɡi
betʼjersweriɡi betsːɬiɡi ɡʼaqʼlu bosiɡi bitʃːala betʼjerhanas nuʒeda tʼade
betsʼab dunjalalda betsːal tʃaɡʼi ɡʼadin qʼad qʼojaɬɡi kwer kwaʃːun nuχ balaɡʔulel χutʼila nuʒ ɡʔabulebʃːinaɬuɬ bitʼ ɡʔjetʃʼjelɬun ɬuɡʔina qʼojidasa qʼojide nuʒee ɡʔabuleb zaral wa tsʼoɡʔ tsʼikʼkʼina nuʒee kumekaɬeɡi ʃːiwɡo wukʼinaro
wasase jas abila amma batʼijaw weɡila ɡʔjejɡun mina bala amma ɡʔjenib ʒanib ɡʼumru ɡʔabilaro tsʼolbol aχ tʃʼjela amma ɡʔjenisa tʼotsebeseb piqχ bakʼarizetsin ʃːwelaro
berazda tsebe ʒindirɡo ots qχuniɡi χʼalbiχʔizetsin ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔan ʃːwelaro nuʒer χʼama batʃun ina wa tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔjeb tʼad busːinabilaro nuʒer ɡʼi tsʼani tuʃbabaze ʃːwela wa nuʒee kumekaɬe ʃːiwɡo wukʼinaro
nuʒer wasalɡi jasalɡi tʃijar χalqʼaɬuqχe kʔjela beral swakazeɡʼan ɡʔjel ralaɡʔulel nuʒɡi χutʼila ʃːibɡo ɡʔabun baʒarunɡutʼijaɬ maɬqʼosijalde kːela
nuʒ tʼad χʼaltʼun nuʒerɡo rakʔalda ɡʼjezaburabʃːinab ʒo nuʒeda biχʔa raɡʼitʃʼjeb χalqʼaɬ kwanala nuʒeejan abuni tsʼob tarab zulmu χʼal bukʼina ɡʼumrujaɬɡo
wa nuʒetsa χʼjeχʔjeze kːarabʃːinaɬ nuʒ ɡʼadalɬila
kweʃal saχɬizarize kʼolarel ruʁnal ritʃːala betʼjerhanas nuʒer nakabazdeɡun boχduzde wa χʼatʼil kilʃːidasa tʼonotsʼalde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjel nuʒer tʃerχaldaɡo tʼiritʼila
betʼjerhanas nuʒɡi nuʒedaɡo tʼad ɬuraw patʃaɡi nuʒedaɡi nuʒer umumuzdaɡi biχʔa raɡʼitʃʼjeb χalqʼaɬul kwerʃːalikʔje kʔjela wa ɡʔjenir nuʒ ɬuɡʔina tsʼulalɡi ɡantʃʼilɡi ɡʔarural jasikʼo allaɡʔzabaze qχuluqχ ɡʔabize
betʼjerhanas nuʒ raqχinarural rakʔazul χalqʼaz nuʒ χʼaqʼir ɡʔarila ɡʔjel nuʒeda tʼad reɬanqχila wa ɡʔjenir inʒitɬijalda rukʼina
nuʒetsa χuribe ɡʼjemerab χʔon χʔala amma batʃʼin muqʼsanab ɡuroni ʃːwelaro ʃːajɡureɬul raqʼul ɡartsʼaɬ kwanan bukʼun ɡʔjeb
nuʒetsa tsʼolbol ʁabu tʃʼjela wa ɡʔjeɬul aχ ɡʼjezabila amma ɡʔjenisa tsʼibil tsʼtsʼun tʃaʁir ɡʔjeqʼelaro ʃːajɡureɬul nuʒer tsʼolboda χʼapara ban bukʼun
kisa kireɡo ulkajalda zajtunaɬul ʁutʼbi riʒila amma zajtunaɬul naχ nuʒeda biχʔilaro ʃːajɡureɬul zajtun tsebeɡo ʁenon bukʼun
nuʒee wasalɡi jasalɡi ɡʔarila amma ɡʔjel nuʒɡun χutʼilaro ʃːajɡureɬul asirɬude ratʃun un rukʼun
nuʒer tʼolalɡo ʁutʼbiɡi χurul batʃʼinɡi χʼutʼ qχumuraɬul dawlaɬun kːela
nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabulel batʼijal χalqʼazul ɡʼadamal qʼojidasa qʼojide tʼadeɡʼanɬila nuʒin abuni qʼojidasa qʼojide ɡʼodoreɡʼanɬila
ɡʔjezda tsere naɬukʔje kːela nuʒ nuʒerin abuni ɡʔjezije kʔjeze ʃːibɡo bukʼinaro ɡʔjel rukʼina betʼjerɬun nuʒ ratʃʼɬun
ɡʔal kinalɡo balaɡʔal reʃːtʼina nuʒede tʼade nuʒeda χadur ɬuɡʔina ɡʔjel nuʒ telaro ɡʔjez betʼjerhan allaɡʔasuqχ ɡʼjenekːitʃʼoɬi wa ɡʔjes tʼad qʼaral amrabiɡi qʼanunalɡi tʼurazaritʃʼoɬi sababɬun nuʒ tʼaɡʼinarila
ɡʔjel balaɡʔal rukʼina nuʒeeɡi nuʒer naslabazeɡi abadijal nuɡʼzalɬun wa ɡʼalamatɬun
ɡʼortsʼarab ɡʼumru buɡeb meχalda nuʒetsa betʼjerhan allaɡʔase raziɡo wa awadanɡo qχuluqχ ɡʔabitʃʼjeɬul
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒeda tʼade ritʃːaral tuʃbabazda tsere χʼaltʼila nuʒ raqʼiɡi qʼetʃɡi ɡʼitsʼɬiɡi miskinɬiɡi χʼjeχʔolaɡo tuʃmanas nuʒer ɡorboda maχːul rukʔ bala ɡʔjeb ɡʼazab ɡʼaqʼubajalda nuʒɡi χwezarila
rikʼkʼadasa dunjalaɬul raɡʼaldasa nuʒeda bitʃʼtʃʼulareb matsʼaɬul χalqʼ tʼamila betʼjerhanas nuʒeda tʼade tsʼum kiniɡin nuʒeda tʼad retʃʼtʃʼila ɡʔjel
ɡʔjeb buɡo waχʼʃijab χalqʼ χarabazul adab ɡʔabulareb ɬimalazda ɡurχʼulareb
nuʒer ɡʼi botsʼiɡi aχ χuraɬul batʃʼinɡi ɡʔjez kwanan ɬuɡʼizabila nuʒɡi χwela
tuʃmanas nuʒer ulkajaɬul kinalɡo ʃaɡʔaral swerun kːwela nuʒer ʃaɡʔarazul rorχatal ʃːulijal qʼadazɡi nuʒ tsʼunilaro wa ɡʔjezde χʔulɡi ɬun nuʒ rukʼaniɡi ɡʔjel ʃːuʃːaqχ razarila betʼjerhanas nuʒee kʔurab ulkajaɬul kinalɡo ʃaɡʔaral swerun kːwela
ʃaɡʔaral swerun kːuraw tuʃmanas nuʒee kʔurab ɡʼazabaɬul kutakɬijaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔas kʔural nuʒerɡo ɬimalazul wasazulɡi jasazulɡi ɡʔan kwanaze buɡo nuʒetsa
nuʒer biʃːun χʼjerenawɡi χʼalimawɡi ɡurχʼize ɡʔjetʃʼo ʒindirɡo watsasdaɡi ɬadudaɡi χutʼaral ɬimalazdaɡi
wa ɡʔjezijeɡi kʔjetʃʼoɡo ʒintsaɡo kwanaze buɡo ʒindirɡo ɬimadul ɡʔan tuʃmanas nuʒer ʃaɡʔaralɡi swerun kːun nuʒ kʼudijab balaɡʔaɬukʔje kːarab meχaɬ nuʒee tʼokʼaɬ kwanaze ʒo bukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul
biʃːun χʼjerenajɡi χʼalimajɡi tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan raɡʼizabun ʒintsa ɡʼodob χʼjetʼje tʃʼolarej tsːidaɬ jalaɡʔize jiɡo ʒindirɡo rosasuqχɡi wasasuqχɡi jasaɬuqχɡi
wa baɬɡo ɬimerɡi ɡʔabun ʒintsaɡo kwanaze buɡo ɡʔjebɡi ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ qʼwatʼibe batʃʼarabʃːinab ʒoɡi tuʃmanas nuʒer ʃaɡʔaral swerun kːurab meχaɬ ɡʔjedinab ɡʼazab bukʼine buɡo nuʒee
ɡʔab tʼjeχʔalda qχwarab qʼanunaɬul ʃːibab raɡʼi muχʼkanɡo tʼubazabitʃʼoni wa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul tʼadeɡʼanab tsʼar kʼodo ɡʔabuleb ɡʔjetʃʼoni
betʼjerhanas nuʒedeɡi nuʒer naslabazdeɡi kidaɡo rukʼintʃʼjel waχʼʃijal balaɡʔalɡi ɡʼasijal tʼasaɡo unarel untabiɡi ritʃːaze ruɡo
ɡʔjes nuʒeda tʼade ritʃːaze ruɡo misrijaɬul kinalɡo waχʼʃijal untabi wa ɡʔjel nuʒeda tʼasa ine ɡʔjetʃʼo
betʼjerhanas nuʒeda tʼade ritʃːaze ruɡo ɡʔab qʼanunalda reχsetʃʼjelɡi untabiɡun balaɡʔal nuʒ tʼaɡʼinaritʃʼoɡo teze ɡʔjetʃʼo
zodir tsʼwabiɡʼan nuʒ ɡʼjemerɬun rukʼaniɡi nuʒer daɡʔal tʃaɡʼi ɡuroni χutʼize ɡʔjetʃʼo nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔase nuʒ mutʼiɡʼɬitʃʼoɬi sababɬun
nuʒee ɬikʼɬiɡi ɡʔabuleb nuʒer qʼadarɡi tsʼikʼkʼinabuleb meχaɬ ɡʔjew woχun wukʼarawɡo ɡʼadin ɡʔjedinɡo nuʒ ʁurijaldasaɡi ʃːuʃːaqχ razarijaldasaɡi woχize wuɡo ɡʔjew wa nuʒetsa kwerde bosizeqχin buɡeb rakʔaldasa nuʒ naqχe qχamize ruɡo
tsinɡi betʼjerhanas nuʒ dunjalaɬul tsojab raɡʼaldasa tsoɡijab raɡʼalde ʃːwezeɡʼan χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔor rikʔ rikʔizarila ɡʔjenir batʼijal allaɡʔzabaze qχuluqχ ɡʔabulel rukʼina nuʒ ja nuʒeda ja nuʒer umumuzda ɬalel rukʼintʃʼjel tsʼulalɡi ɡantʃʼilɡi ɡʔarural allaɡʔzabaze
ɡʔjel χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔob nuʒee paraχaɬi bukʼinaro nuʒer χʼatʼaze χʼalχʔi ʃːwelaro ɡʔjenib betʼjerhanas nuʒer ɡʼaqʼlu urʁalabazul tsʼjezabila berazul kanɬi swinabila wa ruχʼaɬul tʃara qʼosinabila
nuʒer ɡʼumrujaɬe kidaɡoseb χʼinqʼi bukʼina rekʼjeɬ paraχaɬi buɡeb meχɡo ʃːwelaro qʼasiɡi qʼadɡi χʼinqʼun sorodulel rukʼina tʃʼaɡo χutʼiliʃː χutʼilariʃː ɬalaroɡo
radal dutsa abila waj χeχɡo sordo ʃːolebani qʼasi waj χeχɡo roɡʔunebani jan biχʔa tarabʃːinaɬ rekʼjeɬ reʃːtʼarab χʼinqʼi sababɬun
ɡumuzdaɡi rekʼun betʼjerhanas misrijalde tʼad rusːinarila nuʒ nuʒ tʼokʼaɬ ɡʔjenire tʼad rusːine ɡʔjetʃʼin abun bukʼaniɡi betʼjerhanas ɡʔjenire ritʼila nuʒ wa ɡʔjenir tuʃbabaze nuʒɡo laʁɬijalde ritʃize ɬuɡʔina amma nuʒ ritʃun rosulew tʃiɡi wukʼinaro

betʼjerhanasul amrujaldaɬun χoriwalda musatsa ɡʼizrailazulɡun qʼotʼi ɡʔabuna ɡʔjedinɡo moɡʼawalda rukʼaɡo betʼjerhanas musade amru ɡʔabuna ɡʼizrailazulɡun tsoɡi nuχaɬ qʼotʼi ɡʔabejan ɡʔale ɡʔjeb qʼotʼi
kinalɡo ɡʼizrailalɡi aχʼun musatsa ɡʔjezda abuna
nuʒerɡo berazda biχʔana betʼjerhanas misrijalda pirɡʼawnaseɡi kinalɡo ɡʔjesul tʃaɡʼazeɡi ɡʔjesul tʼolabɡo ulkajaɬeɡi ɡʔaburab
nuʒerɡo berazda biχʔana ɡʔjezije ɡʔaburab qʼwakʼarab tamiχʼɡi ɡʔjedinɡo kʼudijal ɡʼalamatalɡi χʼikmatal iʃalɡi
amma ʒaqʼa qʼojalde ʃːwezeɡʼanɡi [nuʒer ritsːatal rakʼal sababɬun] kʔjetʃʼo betʼjerhanas nuʒee bitʃʼtʃʼi buɡeb ɡʼaqʼluɡi biχʔarab bosulel beralɡi raɡʼaraɬul maɡʼna ɡʔabulel ɡʼundulɡi
ditsa kʼiqʼoɡo sonaɬ awlaqχalda nuʒee nuχmaɬi ɡʔabuna nuʒer retʼjelɡi basraɬitʃʼo χʔitɡi biqχitʃʼo
ɡʔjenib nuʒetsa tʃed ɡuro kwanarab tʃʼaɡʼa jaɡi tʃaʁir ɡuro ɡʔjeqʼarab ɡʔjedin ɡʔabuna dun nuʒer betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wukʼin nuʒeda bitʃʼtʃʼize ɡʼolo
aχir qʼadɡi ɡʔanire ʃːwana niɬ tsinɡi χeʃbonaɬul patʃa siχonɡi baʃanaɬul patʃa oɡɡi ratʃʼana niɬɡun raʁize amma niɬetsa ʁurana ɡʔjel
ɡʔjezul rakʔalɡi kwerde rosana wa ɡʔjel rakʔal ruwimilazeɡi ɡadilazeɡi manasːilazul baʃːdab qʼawmaɬeɡi kʔuna
ɡʔab qʼotʼijaɬul kinalɡo ʃartʼal tʼurazaruni ɡʔabulebʃːinaɬuɬ nuʒee iqʼbal bukʼine buɡo
ʒaqʼa nuʒ kinalɡo ɡʔab bakʼalda betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsere tʃʼun ruɡo qʼawmazul butʼrulɡi tuχumazul kʼudijalɡi tsereqχabiɡi kinalɡo ɡʼizrailalɡi
ɡʔjedinɡo ɡʔanir ruɡo nuʒer ɬudbiɡi ɬimalɡi kinalɡo nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔob ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼaral batʼijal χalqʼazul ɡʼadamalɡi nuʒee tsʼul bitʃʼulel tʃaɡʼazdasa baqχarab ɬim batʃːulel tʃaɡʼazde ɡʼuntʼizeɡʼan
nuʒ ɡʔanire rakʼarun ruɡo nuʒetsa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul qʼotʼi qʼabul ɡʔabijaɬe ɡʼolo betʼjerhanas nuʒɡun ɡʔjeb qʼotʼi ɡʔabuleb buɡo ɡʔaɡi ɡʔjedun
ɡʔjes nuʒer umumuze aj ibraɡʔimijeɡi isχʼaqʼijeɡi jaqʼubijeɡi kʔurab raɡʼuda reqʼon nuʒ ʒindirɡo χalqʼɬun ɡʔarijaɬe wa nuʒer allaɡʔɬun ʒiwɡo wukʼinaɬe ɡʼolo
ɡʼitsʼɡo nuʒerɡun ɡuro ditsa ɡʔab ɡʔa ɡʔjedarab qʼotʼi ɡʔabuleb buɡeb
ɡʔab qʼotʼi ɡʔabuleb buɡo ɡʔanir betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsere rakʼarun ruɡezulɡunɡi ʒeɡi ʒaqʼa niɬeda ɡʔorkʔor ɡʔjetʃʼjezulɡunɡi
nuʒedaɡo ɬala misrijalda niɬer bukʼarab ɡʼumruɡi tʃijar χalqʼazul rakʔazdasan niɬetsa ɡʔaburab saparɡi
nuʒeda riχʔana ɡʔjezul tsʼulalɡi ɡantʃʼilɡi ɡʼartsulɡi mesedilɡi ɡʔarural rokʔuqʼal ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔzabi
nuʒeda ɡʔorkʔow kidaniɡi wukʼine witʃːaɡe betʼjerhan allaɡʔasde muʁɡi reχun dol χalqʼazul allaɡʔzabaze tʼaɡʼat ɡʔabulew tʃi ja biχʔintʃi ja tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan ja tʼubarab qʼawm jaɡi tuχum woreɡi kʔoɡʼab jaɡi zaɡʔrujab ɡʼarkʔjel tʼad biʒuleb kʔibil nuʒedaɡo ɡʔorkʔob bitʃːaɡe
qʼotʼijaɬul naɡʼanabiɡi ɬalew tsoniɡi tʃijas ɡʔjezul kʼwarɡi ɡʔabitʃʼoɡo ʒindirɡo duɡʼajaldaɬun rakʼ ɡʼodobe bitʃːazabuleb buɡoni dijeɡo bokʔarabɡi ɡʔabun wukʼina ɡʔabulebʃːinaɬuɬ dije bitʼɡi kːela jan pikruɡi abun ɡʔjeb ɡʼamal sababɬun χweze wuɡo ɡʔjew ɬadatsa ɡʼortsʼarabɡi baqʼwarabɡi rakʔ tsadaqχ tʼaɡʼinabila
ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasdasa betʼjerhan kidaɡo tʼasaɬuɡʔunaro χilipɬi χʼjeχʔolarew betʼjerhanasul ɡʔalaɡab tsːin reʃːtʼine buɡo ɡʔjedinaw tʃijasde wa ɡʔab tʼjeχʔalda qχwaral kinalɡo naɡʼanabi ɡʼuntʼize ruɡo ɡʔjesde ɡʔjesul tsʼarɡi betʼjerhanas dunjalaldasaɡo naqχe qχwaɡʼaze buɡo
ɡʼizrailazul tʼolalɡo qʼawmazda ɡʔorkʔosa watʼaɡi ɡʔawun ɡʔjew tʃijase betʼjerhanas ʒaza ɡʔabila ɡʔab qʼanunaɬul tʼjeχʔalda qχwaral qʼotʼijaɬul kinalɡo naɡʼanabazda reqʼon
nuʒer rukʼinesel ɡʼjelazdaɡi nuʒer naslabazdaɡi rikʼkʼadal rakʔazdasa ratʃʼaral batʼijal χalqʼazul tʃaɡʼazdaɡi biχʔila ɡʔab rakʔalde ratʃʼine ruɡel balaɡʔalɡi betʼjerhanas ritʃːaze ruɡel untabiɡi
ɡʔjezda biχʔila tʃʼabtʼitsaɡi tsʼamutsaɡi buχʼarab tʼolabɡo rakʔ ʃːibɡo bekʔizeɡi biʒizeɡi res ɡʔjetʃʼjeb kinabɡʼaɡi ɡʼurtʃːinɬitsin ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ɡʔjeb bukʼina ɡʔjeleɡʔarab tsːidaɬ betʼjerhanas tʼaɡʼinarural ʃaɡʔaral sodomɡi ɡomorraɡi admaɡi tsewoimɡi ɡʼadin
tʼolalɡo χalqʼaz abize buɡo ʃːib sababɬun betʼjerhanas ɡʔab rakʔalda ɡʔab qʼo tʃʼjezaburab suntsa allaɡʔasul tsːin ɡʔadiɡʼan ɡʔalaɡ ɡʔaburab in
ɡʔjezda abila ɡʔjedin kːana ɡʔjeb χalqʼaɬ ʒindirɡo umumuzul betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul qʼotʼi reχun tejaɬ ɡʔjel misrijaldasa naqχe ratʃun χadub ɡʔjes ɡʔjezulɡun ɡʔabun bukʼarab qʼotʼijaɬe ɡʔjel χilipɬijaɬ
tsere ʒideda kidaniɡi ɬalel rukʼintʃʼjel wa allaɡʔas ɡʔuqʼaral batʼijal allaɡʔzabazda χadur ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjel wa ɡʔjezije tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadat ɡʔabuna
ɡʔjeb sababɬun betʼjerhanasul tsːin ɡʔalaɡɬana ɡʔjeb ulkajalde wa tʼjeχʔalda qχwaral kinalɡo naɡʼanabiɡi ʃːwana ɡʔjeɬul χalqʼaɬe
ɡʔalaɡab tsːidaɬ betʼjerhanas ʒindirɡo rakʔaldasa naqχeɡi qʼotʼun tʃijar rakʔalde reχana ɡʔjel ɡʔanʒeɡi ɡʔjel ɡʔjenir ruɡo jan
betʼjerhan allaɡʔasul niɬeda ɬalarel baɬɡoɬabi ruɡo amma ɡʼadamaze zaɡʔir ɡʔaburabʃːinab ɡʔjes abadijaɬeɡo niɬeeɡi niɬer naslabazeɡi kʔun buɡo niɬ ɡʔjesul qʼanunalda reqʼon χʔwadize rukʼine ɡʼolo

ditsa nuʒee zaɡʔir ɡʔarural ɡʔal kinalɡo ɬikʼɬabiɡi balaɡʔalɡi nuʒeda tʼade ratʃʼine ruɡo ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʃijar χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔor rikʔ rikʔizarural nuʒ rekʼjede ratʃʼina
ɬimalɡun tsadaqχ nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasde rusːina ɡʔjesije mutʼiɡʼɬila wa ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒee zaɡʔir ɡʔaburabʃːinab rakʼ rakʼaɬ wa tʼolabɡo ruχʼ ʒanaldaɬun tʼubazabila
tsinɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒ asirɬudasa tʼad rusːinarila ɡʔjew nuʒeda ɡurχʼila wa ʒintsaɡo kinalɡo χalqʼazda ɡʔorkʔor rikʔ rikʔizarural nuʒ tsʼidasan dande rakʼarila
dunjalaɬul raɡʼalde ʃːwezarun rukʼun rataniɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒ ɡʔjenisaɡi rakʼarila wa tʼadrusːinarila
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒerɡo umumuzul rakʔalde ratʃina nuʒ wa tsʼidasan ɡʔjeb rakʔ kwerde bosila nuʒetsa umumuzul bukʼaraldasaɡi tsʼikʼkʼun betʃeɬiɡi kʔjela nuʒee wa ɡʔjezdasaɡi tsʼikʼkʼina nuʒer qʼadarɡi
betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒerɡi nuʒer naslabazulɡi rakʼaze ɡʔabila sunnat rakʼ rakʼaɬɡo tʼolabɡo ruχʼ ʒanaldaɬun nuʒee betʼjerhan allaɡʔ χiraɬize wa nuʒ tʃʼaɡo χutʼize ɡʼolo
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan allaɡʔas tʼolalɡo balaɡʔal reʃːtʼinarila nuʒɡi riχaral nuʒee ɡʼazab ɡʼaqʼubaɡi kʔjeze bokʔaral nuʒer tuʃbabazde tʼade
nuʒɡi tsʼidasan betʼjerhan allaɡʔase mutʼiɡʼɬila wa ʒaqʼa ditsa maɬaral ɡʔjesul kinalɡo amrabiɡi tʼurazarila
tsinɡi betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒetsa ɡʔabulebʃːinalda kʼudijab barakat ɬela nuʒee ɬimal ɡʼjemer ɡʔarila ɡʼi botsʼul qʼinɬi ɡʼjemerɬila wa aχ χuraɬul batʃʼinɡi ɡʔarzaɬila betʼjerhan naqχeɡi nuʒedasa raziɬila nuʒer umumuzdasa raziɬaraw ɡʼadin wa nuʒee ɬikʼabʃːinab kʔjela
ɡʔjedin bukʼina nuʒ betʼjerhan allaɡʔasuqχ ɡʼjenekːulel ruɡoni wa ɡʔab qʼanunaɬul tʼjeχʔalda qχwaral ɡʔjesul amrabiɡi tʼadqʼajalɡi tʼurazarun χʔwadani rakʼ rakʼaɬɡo tʼolabɡo ruχʼ ʒanaldaɬun nuʒerɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔasde rusːani
ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒee kʔolel ruɡel amrabi tʼurazarize tsʼaqʼɡo zaχʼmatal jaɡi naqχ ɡʼuntʼun baʒarularel ɡʔjetʃʼo
ɡʔjel zobalazda ɡuro ruɡel zobalazde ʃːiw waχinew ɡʔjel rosize wa niʒee zaɡʔir ɡʔarize niʒetsa ɡʔjel tʼurazarize rukʼine jan nuʒetsa abize kːani
raɬad tun doreχunɡi ɡuro ɡʔjel ruɡel raɬad baχun doweχun ʃːiw inew ɡʔjel rosize wa niʒeqχe kʔjeze niʒetsa ɡʔjel tʼurazarize rukʼine janɡi abize kːolaro
ɡuro ɡʔjel amrabi nuʒɡun ruɡo ɡʔjel nuʒer matsʼalda ruɡo wa nuʒer rekʼjeɬ ruɡo ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjel tʼurazare
balaɡʔje ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒeda tsebe ɬoleb buɡo ɡʼumruɡi barakatɡi χwelɡi balaɡʔɡi
ɡʔale dir amru betʼjerhan allaɡʔ χiraɬe ɡʔjesul nuχkːun χʔwade ɡʔjesul amrabiɡi tʼadqʼajalɡi qʼanunalɡi tʼurazare tsinɡi nuʒ tʃʼaɡo χutʼila nuʒer qʼadarɡi tʼadejaldasa tʼade tsʼikʼkʼina wa nuʒ ʒanire ɬuɡʔineqχin ruɡeb rakʔalda betʼjerhan allaɡʔas nuʒede barakatɡi reʃːtʼinabila
amma nuʒetsa betʼjerhan allaɡʔasde muʁ reχani nuʒ ɡʔjesije mutʼiɡʼɬitʃʼoni wa ɡʔjesul nuχdasaɡi kʔurun batʼijal allaɡʔzabaze qχuluqχ ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔani
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ rakʼtʃʼun nuʒ tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡo nuʒ uneb wa nuʒetsa kwerde bosize buɡeb iordanaɬul dob tsojab raqχaɬul rakʔalda nuʒer ɡʼumruɡi χalat baqχize ɡʔjetʃʼo
ʒaqʼa ditsa zobɡi rakʔɡi nuʒeda dande nuɡʼzalɬun aχʼulel ruɡo ditsa nuʒeda tsebe ɬuna ɡʼumru jaɡi χwel barakat jaɡi naɡʼana ɡʼumru tʼasa biʃːe nuʒɡoɡi nuʒer naslabiɡi tʃʼaɡo rukʼine
betʼjerhan allaɡʔ nuʒee χiraɬize ɡʔjesuqχ ɡʼjenekːize wa ɡʔjesulɡun ʃːulijab buχʔjen ɡʔabize ɡʔjesdasan buɡeɬul nuʒee ɡʼumru nuʒee kʔjelin abun nuʒer umumuze aj ibraɡʔimijeɡi isχʼaqʼijeɡi jaqʼubijeɡi ɡʔjedun wukʼarab rakʔalda ɡʔjes kʔjela nuʒee χalatab ɡʼumru

aχiraldaɡi musatsa tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazde ɡʔadinab χitʼab ɡʔabuna
musatsa abuna ditsa nusijalda qʼoɡo son bana wa tʼokʼaɬ baʒarularo diqχa nuʒeda tsadaqχ χʔwadun betʼjerhanasɡi abuna dun iordan baχun doweχun ine ɡʔjetʃʼilan
ʒiwɡo betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wukʼine wuɡo nuʒeda tsadaqχ dora ruɡel χalqʼalɡi ɡʔjes nuʒeda tseresa tʼaɡʼinarize ruɡo wa nuʒetsa dob rakʔɡi kwerde bosize buɡo jeɡʔoʃuatsa tsere ratʃine ruɡo nuʒ betʼjerhanasul raɡʼuda reqʼon
betʼjerhanas ɡʔjel χalqʼazeɡi ɡʔabila amorijazul patʃazabi siχonijeɡi oɡijeɡi ɡʔjezul rakʔazeɡi ɡʔaburab ɡʔjel χalqʼalɡi ɡʔjedinɡo ʁurila
betʼjerhanas nuʒer kwerde kʔjeze ruɡo ɡʔjel wa nuʒetsa ɡʔjezije ditsa nuʒeda tʼadqʼarabʃːinab ɡʔabize kːola
nuʒ ʃːulaɡo tʃʼa qʼwakʼun rukʼa ɡʔjezukʔa χʼinqʼuɡe ja naqχe qʼaɡe betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wuɡeɬul nuʒɡun ɡʔjes nuʒ kidaniɡi reχun teze ɡʔjetʃʼo
χadub musatsa jeɡʔoʃua aχʼana wa tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazda tsebe ɡʔjesda abuna
