mun qʼwakʼun wa kʔwarun tʃʼa ʃːajɡureɬul mun ine kːola betʼjerhanas niɬer umumuze raɡʼi kʔun bukʼarab rakʔalde ɡʔab χalqʼɡi batʃun wa ɡʔjezul irs χʼisabalda dutsa ɡʔjezda ɡʔorkʔob bikʔize kːola ɡʔjeb rakʔɡi
ʒiwɡo betʼjerhan ine wuɡo duda tsewe tsewe wa ɡʔjew munɡun wukʼine wuɡo ɡʔjes mun kidaɡo reχun teze ɡʔjetʃʼo mun sunkʔaniɡi χʼinqʼuɡe wa rakʼ tʼurkʼize bitʃːaɡe
musatsa ɡʔab qʼanun qχwana wa betʼjerhanasul qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas batʃːulel lewijil qʼawmaɬul kaʃiʃzabazuqχe wa ɡʼizrailaɬul kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazuqχe kʔuna
χadub musatsa abuna
ankʔɡo sonalda ʒanib tso nuχaɬ tʼasaɬuɡʔinaɬul sonaɬ qχoʃazul bajramqʼojaz
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ betʼjerhan allaɡʔasda tsebe tʃʼjeze ɡʔjes tʼasa biʃːarab muqʼadasab bakʼalde bakʼararab meχaɬ kinalɡo ɡʼizrailazda raɡʼun ɡʔab qʼanun tsʼale
tʼolabɡo χalqʼ bakʼare biχʔinalɡi rutʃːabiɡi ɬimalɡi nuʒer ʃaɡʔarazda tʃʼaral tsoɡidal χalqʼazul ɡʼadamalɡi bitʃːante ɡʔjezda raɡʼize wa ɬan bukʼine ɡʔjel ruɡʔunɬize kːola betʼjerhan allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼize ɡʔjesije suʒda ɡʔabize wa ɡʔjesul qʼanunɡi muχʼkanɡo tʼubazabize
bitʃːante ʒeɡi ɡʔab qʼanun ɬalarel ɬimalɡi ɡʼjenekːize wa ɡʔjezdaɡi ɬan bukʼine ɡʔjel ruɡʔunɬize kːola betʼjerhan allaɡʔasukʔa χʼinqʼize wa ɡʔjesije suʒda ɡʔabize ɡʔjedin bukʼine kːola kidaɡo iordanaɬul dob tsojab raqχalda nuʒetsa kwerde bosizeqχin buɡeb rakʔalda nuʒetsa ɡʼumru ɡʔabulebʃːinab meχaɬ
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
duje χweze zaman ʃːoleb buɡo jeɡʔoʃua aχʼje wa dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsere tʃʼa ditsa ɡʔjesije amru ɡʔabize bukʼine
musaɡi jeɡʔoʃuaɡi dandtʃʼwajaɬul tʃadiralda tsere tʃʼana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ betʼjerhan zaɡʔirɬana nakʼkʼul partʃadul χʼubijaɬuɬ wa tʃadiraɬul kʼaltʼa tʃʼana
betʼjerhanas musada abuna
mun kwatʼitʃʼoɡo durɡo umumulɡun paraχaɬize wuɡo ɡʔab χalqʼin abuni ʒib uneb buɡeb rakʔaɬul ɡʔjeresiallaɡʔzabazda χadubɡi un pasaɬize buɡo ɡʔjez dun reχun teze wuɡo wa ʒiderɡun ɡʔaburab dir qʼotʼiɡi χwezabize buɡo
ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ dir ɡʔjezda ɡʔalaɡab tsːin baqχila wa ditsa ɡʔjelɡi reχun tela ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ditsa ɡʔjezdasa dirɡo ɡʔumer baχtʃila ɡʔjelɡi tʃijar dawlaɬun kːela ɡʼjemeral waχʼʃijal balaɡʔal ratʃʼina ɡʔjezda tʼade ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ɡʔjez abila ɡʔalɡoʃːinal balaɡʔal niɬeda tʼade ratʃʼun ruɡo niɬɡun niɬer allaɡʔ ɡʔjetʃʼoɬijaɬ in
ditsajin abuni ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ rakʼtʃʼun dirɡo ɡʔumer baχtʃize buɡo batʼijal allaɡʔzabazdeɡi rusːun ɡʔjez ɡʔaburabʃːinab kweʃɬi sababɬun
ɡʔanʒe ɡʔab turki qχwaj wa ɡʼizrailazda maɬe bitʃːante ɡʔjez ɡʔjeb aχʼize ɡʔjeb bukʼine buɡo ɡʔjezda dande tʃʼarab dir nuɡʼɬun
ditsa ɡʔjel ratʃina raχʔɡi ɡʔotsʼoɡi tʃwaχuleb rakʔalde ɡʔjezije kʔjelin ɡʔjezul umumuze dun ɡʔjedarab rakʔalde ɡʔjenib ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwanaze kwenɡi ʃːun kʔaraɬarab meχaɬ dunɡi reχun tun wa dir qʼotʼiɡi χwezabun ɡʔjel batʼijal allaɡʔzabazde rusːina wa ɡʔjezije qχuluqχ ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔina
χadub ɡʼjemeral balaɡʔalɡi ɡʼazab ɡʼaqʼubaɡi χʼjeχʔjeze kːarab meχaɬ ɡʔab turki ɡʔjezda dande nuɡʼɬun tʃʼjela ratʃʼunel ɡʼjelazdaɡi kʼotʃene ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul ɡʔab turki dida ɡʔanʒeɡo ɬala ɡʔjezul rakʼazul qʼasdal ɡʔjezije kʔjelin dun ɡʔjedarab rakʔalde ɡʔjel ʃːwelaldeɡo
dob qʼojaɬ musatsa turki qχwana wa ɡʼizrailazda maɬana
nunil was jeɡʔoʃuade betʼjerhanas ɡʔadinab amru ɡʔabuna
mun qʼwakʼun wa kʔwarun tʃʼa ʃːajɡureɬul dutsa ratʃine kːoleɬul ɡʼizrailal ɡʔjezije kʔjelin dun ɡʔjedarab rakʔalde dunɡi wukʼine wuɡo munɡun
bajbiχʔudasa aχiralde ʃːwezeɡʼan tʼolabɡo qʼanun qχwan ɬuɡʼarabɡo
musatsa betʼjerhanasul qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas batʃːulel lewitazde ɡʔadinab amru ɡʔabuna
ɡʔab qʼanunaɬul tʼjeχʔ bose wa qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamasalda askʼob ɬe ɡʔjeb ɡʔjenib bukʼina nuʒeda dande tʃʼarab nuɡʼ χʼisabalda
dida ɬaleɬul nuʒeeɡo bokʔarabɡi ɡʔabun tʃʼolel tʃaɡʼi nuʒ rukʼin ʒaqʼa dun ʒeɡi nuʒɡun wuɡeb meχaɬtsin ɡʔjediɡʼan betʼjerhanase mutʼiɡʼɬularel nuʒer dun χun χadub ʃːibdaj bukʼina
nuʒer qʼawmazul kʼudijalɡi tsereqχabiɡi diqχe aχʼje ɡʔjezije ditsa ɡʔal raɡʼabi tsʼalize wa ɡʔjezda dande nuɡʼzalɬun zobɡi rakʔɡi aχʼize
dida ɬaleɬul dun χun χadub nuʒ rakʼtʃʼun pasaɬize rukʼin wa ditsa maɬarab nuχɡi tun qʼosun kːeze rukʼin zamanaldasan nuʒeda tʼade balaɡʔal reʃːtʼine ruɡo betʼjerhanasda tsere nuʒetsa ɡʔarural kweʃɬabi wa ɡʔjesul tsːin baqχinabulel nuʒer iʃal sababɬun
musatsa tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazda raɡʼun bajbiχʔudasa aχiralde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔab turki tsʼalana

kobrajaɬul χwalil zaɡʔru
ditsa baχtʃun ɡurebiʃː ɡʔjeb buɡeb
dir naqχaroqʼob muɡʔruɡi tʃʼwan tun ɡurebiʃː ɡʔjeb buɡeb
retsʼjel bosulew dun wuɡo qʼisas ditsa bosila
ɡʔjezul χʼjetʼje qχuʃːtʼarab qʼo batʃʼindal
ɡʔjezde tʃʼjeɡʼjerab qʼo batʃʼuneb buɡo
ɡʔjezije qʼatʃʼarab qʼadar ɡʼjedeɡʼun ʃːoleb buɡo
betʼjerhanas diwan ɡʔabila ʒindirɡo χalqʼaɬe
wa ʒindirɡo laʁzaderida ɡurχʼila
ɡʔjezul paqʼirɬiɡi biχʔun
ja asiral ja erkenal naqχe tʃaɡʼiɡo χutʼun ɡʔjetʃʼoɬiɡi biχʔun
wa ɡʔjes abila kireχa aral ɡʔjezul allaɡʔzabi
kib buɡeb ɡʔjez muʁtʃʼwaleb bukʼarab kʔuru
nuʒerɡo qʼurbanazul tʼatʼi ɡʔjezije kʔuna nuʒetsa
ɡʔjezije tʃaʁirɡi tʼuna
bitʃːante ɡʔanʒe ɡʔjez kumek ɡʔabize nuʒee
bitʃːante ɡʔjez tsʼunize nuʒ
ɡʔanʒeɡʼaɡi bitʃʼtʃʼa nuʒeda tsoχʼo dun wukʼin allaɡʔ
dun ɡurew batʼijaw allaɡʔ ɡʔjetʃʼjewɬi
ɡʼaʒalɡi qχwala ditsa ɡʼumruɡi kʔola ditsa
ditsa ruʁun ɬola ditsaɡo saχɡi ɡʔarula
didasa χwasar ɡʔarize ɬidaɡo kʼolaro
eχede kwerɡi borχun ɡʔjedulew wuɡo dun
dirɡo abadijab tsʼaralχʼa
dirɡo χwaltʃenaɬul piri beɡʼjer ɡʔaburabɡo wa
ʒaza ɡʔabize ɡʔjeb kodobe bosarabɡo
ditsa retsʼjel bosila tuʃbabazdasa
dun riχaraze ʒaza ɡʔabila
ditsa bidutsa meχtizarila dirɡo tʃʼoral
dir χwaltʃatsaɡi ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan ɡʔan kwanala
tʃʼwarazulɡi asirazulɡi bi
tuʃbabazul tsereqχabazul butʼrul
dunjalaɬul χalqʼal nuʒ ɡʔjesul χalqʼaldasa roχa
ʒindirɡo laʁzaderil biduqχ betʼjerhanas qʼisas bosize buɡo
ɡʔjes tuʃbabaze ʒaza ɡʔabila
ʒindirɡo χalqʼaɬul rakʔɡi batsʼtsʼad ɡʔabila
ɡʔjedin χalqʼalda tseweɡi waqχun musatsa kinazdaɡo raɡʼun ɡʔjeb turkijaɬul raɡʼabi tsʼalana ɡʔjesda tsadaqχ nunil was ɡʔoʃeaɡi
tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailaze kinabɡo waɡʼza nasiχʼatɡi χitʼabɡi ɡʔabun ɬuɡʼarabɡo
musatsa abuna
ʒaqʼa ditsa nuʒeda maɬarabʃːinab ʒo rekʼjeɬ tsʼune nuʒerɡo ɬimalazdaɡi maɬe ɡʔab qʼanunalda qχwaral amrabi muχʼkanɡo tʼurazarize
ɡʔjel tʃʼoroɡojal raɡʼabi ɡuro ɡʔjel raɡʼabazuɬ buɡo nuʒer ɡʼumrujaɬul maɡʼna iordan ɡʼoraɬul dob tsojab raqχalda nuʒetsa kwerde bosizeqχin buɡeb rakʔalda ɡʔjezdaɬun bukʼine buɡo nuʒee χalatab ɡʼumruɡi
ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanas musada abuna
awarim muɡʼruzde a jeriχonalda dandbitʼun moɡʼawaɬul rakʔalda buɡeb newo maɡʼarde waχa wa ditsa ɡʼizrailaze kʔoleb buɡeb χanaanaɬul rakʔaɬuqχ walaɡʔje
ɡʔjeb maɡʼarde tʼade waχine wuɡo mun wa ɡʔjeniw χweze wuɡo tsinɡi durɡo umumulɡun tsoɬize wuɡo ɡʔor maɡʼarda dur wats ɡʔarunɡi ɡʔjedinɡo χwana wa ʒindirɡo umumuzuqχe ana
ɡʔjedin kːana tsin aburab salul awlaqχalda rukʼaɡo kadeʃalda buɡeb meriwa aburab itsːuqχ ɡʼizrailazda tsebe dir adab ɡʔjetʃʼjeb ʒoɡi ɡʔabun nuʒetsa ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda dir tʼadeɡʼanab χiraɬi biχʔizabitʃʼoɬi sababɬun
ɡʔjedinɬidal ditsa ɡʼizrailaze kʔoleb buɡeb rakʔ biχʔila duda rikʼkʼadasan amma ɡʔjeniwe mun ɬuɡʔinaro

ɡʔale musatsa ʒiwɡo χwelalde tsebe ɡʼizrailil naslabaze ɡʔaburab barakataɬul duɡʼa
ɡʔjes abuna
betʼjerhan sinajaldasa zaɡʔirɬana
seiralda tʼad ɡʔjesul nur ɡwanʁana
paranalda ɡʔjesul kanɬi qʼaɬana
zobalazul antsʼ antsʼ azarilal bojalɡun ɡʔjew watʃʼindal
ɡʔjesul kwaranab raqχaldasan ruruduleb tsʼaɡi
χʼaqʼiqʼataldaɡi duje durɡo χalqʼ ɡʼizrail χirijab buɡo
boʒi imanaɬul aɡʔlu dur qχatikʔ buɡo
ɡʔjel kinalɡo duda tsere nakabazda tʃʼola
dur nasiχʼatazuqχɡi ɡʼjenekːulaɡo
musatsa ɡʔjezuqχe kʔurab qʼanun
jaqʼubil χalqʼaɬul irsɬun kːola
ɡʼizrailaɬul tʼolabɡo χalqʼɡi ɡʔjezul qʼawmazul butʼrulɡi
maʒlisalde rakʼararab meχalda
jeʃurunaɬul partʃːaχʼɬun ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjew
ruwimil naslabi ɬuɡʼuɡeɡi ɡʔjezije ɡʼumru kʔjeɡi
ɡʔjesul qʼawmaɬul tʃaɡʼi daɡʔal rukʼaniɡi
jaɡʔudal qʼawmaɬul raqχaɬ ɡʔjes ɡʔadin abuna
ja betʼjerhan jaɡʔudal naslabazul aχʼi duda raɡʼaɡi
ɡʔjel ɡʔjezul χalqʼɡun tsoɬizare
ɡʔjel ʒiderɡo qʼuwataldaɬun tuʃmanasda dande raʁula
amma dudasan buɡo ɡʔjezije kumek
lewijil qʼawmaɬul raqχaɬ ɡʔjes ɡʔadin abuna
lewijil naslabi dur boʒaral laʁzal
ɡʔjez tsʼunula tummimɡi urimɡi
masːajalda dutsa χʼalbiχʔana ɡʔjezul
meriwajaɬul itsːuqχ ɡʔjelɡun waʁana
ɡʔjez ebel insul raqχaɬ abula
niʒee kʼwar ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjel ebel emen rukʼinaɬul in
watsazul ɡʔurmaqχ ɡʔjel ralaɡʔularo
ɬimalazuqχ ɡʼin tʼamularo
ʃːajin abuni biʃːun kʼwar buɡebɬun ɡʔjezije buɡo dur amru tʼubazabi
wa dur qʼotʼi tsʼuni
ɡʔjez jaqʼubil naslabazda dur nuχalɡi
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda dur qʼanunɡi maɬula
ɡʔjez duda tsere ɡʔuinmaχʼal ruχʼula
dur qʼurban bakʼalda tʼad tsʼadul qʼurbanal ɬola
ja betʼjerhan barakat ɬe ɡʔjezda wa ɡʔjezul maχʃːel ɡʔunar tsʼikʼkʼinabe
ɡʔjez ɡʔabulebʃːinaldasa mun raziɬaɡi
ɡʔjezul tuʃbabazul muʁ bekizabe
wa ɡʔjel riχaral ɡʼodor kːezare
tʼokʼaɬ tʼade raqχunareb χʼalaɬ
bunjaminil qʼawmaɬul raqχaɬ ɡʔjes ɡʔadin abuna
bitʃːante betʼjerhanase χirijaw
ɡʔjesda askʼow χʼinqʼi ɡʔjetʃʼjeb raχʼatalda wukʼine
betʼjerhanas kidaɡo tsʼunula ɡʔjew
ʒindirɡo kʼiʁuʒduzda tʼadeɡi watʃun χʼalχʔi kʔola ɡʔjesije
jusupil qʼawmaɬul raqχaɬ ɡʔjes abuna
ja betʼjerhan jusupil naslabazul rakʔalde barakat reʃːtʼinabe
tʼad zobalazdasa ʃːub bazabe
rakʔuɬa ʒanisan itsːal tʃwaχizare
baqʼ ɡʼun barʃːarab ɡʔuinab piqχ kʔje
motsʼaldasa motsʼalde buɡʼa roɬ ɡʔarzaɬizabe
ɡʔjezul nekʼsijal muɡʼruzdaɡi batʼi batʼijab χirijab niɡʼmat biʒaɡi
ɡoχʼal ʃːobazdaɡi piqχ ɡʔarzaɬaɡi
rakʔaldasa χʼaluqχen ɡʔarzaɡo ʃːwaɡi
zazil qχarqχida ɡʔorkʔosa kʼaɬaraw betʼjerhanasul tsʼobaldaɬun
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo kʔjeɡi jusupil naslabaze
watsazda ɡʔorkʔow ʒiw tʼasa wiʃːarase
ɡutʃab otsoda reɬːuna jusupil qʼuwat
ɡʼalχul buʁil ɬːurdulin kːola ɡʔjesul wasal
ɡʔjez χalqʼazda χʼunkula
dunjalaɬul raɡʼalda ruɡezdeɡi ɡʼuntʼula
jefraimil naslu antsʼ antsʼ azarɡo
manasːil aza azarɡo
zewulunil qʼawmaɬul raqχaɬ ɡʔjes abuna
zewulunil naslabi saparalde raqχuneɬul nuʒ raziɬaɡi
isːaχaril naslabi nuʒerɡo tʃadrazuqχ nuʒɡi roχaɡi
ɡʔjez maɡʼarde ʒideqχeɡo qʼawmal aχʼula
wa ɡʔjenir ratsʼtsʼadal qʼurbanal ɡʔarula
raɬdal betʃeɬijaɬ χʔiχʔula ɡʔjel
raɬdal saludasa χajir bosula
ɡadil qʼawmaɬul raqχaɬ ɡʔjes ɡʔadin abuna
ɡadil naslabazul rakʔ ɡʼatʼid ɡʔaburase barakat ʃːwaɡi
ɡʔjel reɬːuna paraχatɡo ɡʼodob beɡarab ʁalbatsʼalda
toχɬukʔje tʼadɡi retʃʼtʃʼun betʼjerɡi kwerɡi tʼjeze qʼatʃʼarab
ɡʔjez biʃːun ɬikʼab rakʔ tʼasa biʃːana
χalqʼaɬul betʼjerase mustaχʼiqʼab rakʔ
χalqʼaɬul butʼrul dande rakʼararab meχaɬ
ɡʔjez betʼjerhanasul amrujalda reqʼon ɡʔabuna
ɡʼizrailaɬe betʼjerhanas qʼotʼarab χʼukmu tʼubazabuna
danil qʼawmaɬul raqχaɬ ɡʔjes abuna
baʃanaɬul muɡʼruzdasa ʒib kʼantsʼuleb
ʁalbatsʼaɬul tʼintʃʼalda reɬːuna danil naslabi
naftalil raqχaɬ ɡʔjes abuna
barakatal ruɡo naftalil naslabi
betʼjerhanasdasa barakat ʃːwaral ruɡo ɡʔjel
ɡʔjezul irsɬun kːola [ɡalilejaɬul] χʼorɡi qʼilbajaɬul raqχɡi
aʃeril qʼawmaɬul raqχaɬ ɡʔjes abuna
aʃeril naslabi kinalɡo watsazda ɡʔorkʔor biʃːun barakatal
zajtunaɬul naχul ɡʼoral tʃwaχaɡi ɡʔjezije
kinalɡo qʼawmaze χiraɬaɡi ɡʔjel
nuʒer kawabazul raχajal maχːulɡi mazɡaraɬulɡi ɡʔarural rukʼina
nuʒer ɡʼumrujaɬul qʼojal ɡʼadin nuʒer betʃeɬiɡi tsʼikʼkʼina
jeʃurunaɬul allaɡʔasda baʃːadaw ʃːiwɡo ɡʔjetʃʼo
ɡʔjew zobalazdasan duje kumekaɬe worʒuna
ʒindirɡo kʼudijab qʼudratɡun nakʼkʼul partʃabazdaɡi rekʼun
abadijaw allaɡʔ ɡʔjew wuɡo mun waχtʃuleb qχala
abadijasul kwer duj muʁtʃʼwajaɬe
ɡʔjes dur tuʃbabi naqχe aχʼana
wa ɡʔjel tʼaɡʼinarejan bujuruqχ kʔuna
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ paraχatɡo bukʼina
ɡʼitsʼɡo jaqʼubil aɡʔlujaɬ ɡʼumru ɡʔabila
tʃedɡi tʃaʁirɡi ɡʔarzajab ulkajalda
zobalaz kidaɡo tʼade ʃːub betsʼtsʼuleb rakʔalda
barakatab buɡo mun ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ
ʃːal duda reɬːunel
betʼjerhanas erken ɡʔaburab χalqʼ
dur qχalqχanɡi kumektʃiɡi ɡʔjew wuɡo
dur retsːaɬul χwaltʃenɡi ɡʔjew wuɡo
tuʃbabi duje χʼjelχʼjedila
dutsajin abuni ɡʔjel χʼatʼikʔ merχʔina

tsinɡi moɡʼawaɬul ɡʼatʼirakʔaldasa musa newo maɡʼarde wiɬːana wa jeriχonalda dandbitʼun buɡeb fasɡa meɡʼjeraɬul tʼoɡʔiwe waχana ɡʔjenisan betʼjerhanas musada biχʔizabuna ɡilɡʼadaldasa danalde ʃːwezeɡʼan tʼolabɡo rakʔ
ɡʔjedinɡo naftalil tʼolabɡo rakʔɡi jefraimil wa manasːil rakʔalɡi kʼudijab raɬdaqχe ɡʼuntʼarab jaɡʔudal tʼolabɡo rakʔɡi
neɡewɡi tʃamasdakaɬul ʁutʼbuzul ʃaɡʔaraldasa baqχarab tsoɡʼaralde ʃːwezeɡʼan tʼibitʼarab jeriχonaɬul tʼolabɡo rakʔɡi
betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesda abuna
ɡʔale ibraɡʔimijeɡi isχʼaqʼijeɡi jaqʼubijeɡi dun ɡʔjedarab ɡʔjezul naslabaze kʔjelin ditsa amru ɡʔarurab rakʔ ditsa duda ɡʔjeb biχʔize res kʔoleb buɡo amma mun ɡʔjeniwe ine ɡʔjetʃʼo
tsinɡi betʼjerhanasul laʁ musa χwana betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesda abuqχe moɡʼawaɬul rakʔalda
wa ɡʔjew moɡʼawalda bet peoralda askʼob buɡeb rasaɬijalda wuqʼana amma ʒaqʼa qʼojaɬɡi ɬidaɡo ɬalaro ɡʔjesul χob buɡeb bakʼ
musatsa nusijalda qʼoɡo son ban bukʼana amma χwezeɡʼan ɡʔjesul berazul kanɬiɡi swintʃʼo tʃorχol ruχʼ ʒanɡi daɡʔɬitʃʼo
ɡʼizrailil χalqʼaɬ ɬeberɡo qʼojaɬ maɡʼu baqχana musada χadub moɡʼawaɬul rasaɬijalda musada χadur ɡʼodijaɬul qʼojal ɡʔjedin tʼurazaruna
nunil was jeɡʔoʃuade ɡʼaqʼilɬijaɬul ruχʼ reʃːtʼana musatsa kweral ɬun rukʼun ɡʔjesda wa ɡʼizrailal ɡʔjesda naqχ riɬːana musatsa maɬarabʃːinabɡi tʼubazabuleb bukʼana
ɡʔjeldasa naqχe musa ɡʼadinaw betʼjerhanasul ɡʔumer ɬalew awaraɡ ɡʼizrailalda tʼokʼaɬ waqχintʃʼo
ɡʔjes betʼjerhanasul amrujaldaɬun misrijalda pirɡʼawnasdaɡi ɡʔjesul tʼolalɡo tʃaɡʼazdaɡi riχʔizarural wa pirɡʼawnasul rakʔalda ɡʔarural ɡʼadinal kʼudijal χʼikmaɬabiɡi ɡʼalamatalɡi tʼokʼaɬ ɬitsaɡo ɡʔaritʃʼo
musatsa tʼolabɡo ɡʼizrailil χalqʼalda tsebe biχʔizaburab kʼudijab qʼudratɡi kutakal wa χʼinqʼaral muɡʼʒizatalɡi tʼokʼaɬ ɬitsaɡo riχʔizaritʃʼo

dob qʼadizabazul
ɡʔjew tʃijasda tsʼar bukʼana eli malik ɡʔjesul ɬaduda tsʼar bukʼana noɡʼomi wa ɡʔjesul wasazda tsʼar bukʼana maχʼlon wa kileon ɡʔjel rukʼana jaɡʔudijalda buɡeb betleɡʔjemaldasa epratil qʼawmaɬul tʃaɡʼi
ɡʔjel ratʃʼana moɡʼawaɬul rakʔalde wa ɡʔjenib ɡʼumru ɡʔabun tʃʼana
kwatʼitʃʼoɡo χwana eli malik wa χutʼana noɡʼomi ʒindirɡo kʼijawɡo wasɡun
moɡʼawaɬul rutʃːabazda ɡʔorkʔosa ɬudbi ratʃana ɡʔjez ʒideeɡo tsojalda tsʼar orpat tsoɡijalda tsʼar rut bukʼana antsʼɡo sonɡʼanaseb zaman bana ɡʔjez ɡʔjeb bakʼalda
amma χadur ɡʔjeɬul kʼijawɡo was χwana maχʼlonɡi kileonɡi wa χutʼana ɡʔjej ɡʼadan ʒijɡo rosɡi χun ɬimalɡi χun
betʼjerɡʔanasul raχʼmu reʃːtʼun buɡin ɡʔjesul χalqʼalde wa kʼudijab riqʼzi kʔun buɡin raɡʼun noɡʼomil qʼasd kːana moɡʼawaɬul awlaqχazdasa ʒindirɡo rakʔalde tʼad jusːine kʼijajɡo nusɡi jaqχana ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ
raqχana noɡʼomiɡi kʼijajɡo nusɡi tsadaqχ ɡʔjeb bakʼaldasa qʼwatʼire wa jaɡʔudijalde nuχ bosana
noɡʼomitsa nusazdeχun jusːun ɡʔadinab kalam ɡʔabuna nuʒ tʼadrusːa nuʒerɡo ebel insul roqʼore betʼjerɡʔanas lʔikʼabʃːinab ɡʔabeɡi nuʒee nuʒetsa nuʒer χwaral rosaze wa dije ɡʔaburab ɡʼadin
betʼjerɡʔanas kumek ɡʔabeɡi nuʒee wa taliχʼɡi kʔjeɡi tsʼijal rosabazul roqʼob
ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjezda ubatʃalɡi ɡʔarun qʼo meχ ɬikʼ ɡʔabulaɡo ɡʔjel bitʃːan ɡʔarakʔɡun ɡʼodana
wa ɡʔjez abuna niʒ duda tsadaqχ riɬːina dur χalqʼalda ɡʔorkʔor rukʼine
noɡʼomitsa abuna tʼadrusːa dir jasal ʃːaj nuʒee dida tsadaqχ riɬːun nuʒee rosalɬun raqχine ʒeɡi wasal ɡʔarize dir χʼalkʼweliʃː
tʼadrusːa dir jasal nuʒ a rosase ine dunɡi ɡʔanʒe χerɬun jiɡeɬul ʒeɡi χʔul kwatʼun ɡʔjetʃʼinɡi abun ʒaqʼaɡo rosaseɡi un qʼasiɡo dir urɡʔire wasal kːeze res bukʼarabaniɡitsin
beɡʔilaaniʃː ɡʔjel kʼudijal ɡʼjezeɡʼan nuʒ ralaɡʔun tʃʼjeze
tsʼidasan ritʃːan ɡʔarkʔalɡun ɡʼodize ɬuɡʔana ɡʔjel orpatitsa ubatʃɡi ɡʔabun ʒindirɡo jakʔadaɬulɡun qʼo ɬikʼ ɡʔabuna amma rut ɡʔjelda askʼosa jaʁaritʃʼo
noɡʼomitsa abuna balaɡʔje dur dandijaj unej jiɡo tʼadjusːun ʒindirɡo χalqʼaɬuqχe wa ʒindirɡo allaɡʔzabazuqχe munɡi a dolda tsadaqχ
amma rutitsa ʒawab kʔuna munɡi reχun tun dun χʼalitsaɡo naqχe ʁoɡe mun araɬuje dunɡi ina mun tʃʼaraɬuj dunɡi tʃʼjela dur χalqʼ bukʼina dir χalqʼɬun dur allaɡʔ wukʼina dir allaɡʔɬun
mun χwaraɬuj dunɡi χwela mun juqʼaraɬuj dunɡi juqʼila betʼjerɡʔanasul tsːin reʃːtʼaɡi dida tʼade dida tʼad qʼono tʃʼwarab qʼojaɬ ɡuroni ditsa mun reχun tani
noɡʼomida bitʃʼtʃʼana ɡʔjelda tsadaqχ jiɬːine ɡʔaburab rutil χʼukmu ʃːulijab bukʼin wa tokʼab ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjelda tʼadjusːinaɬul tsʼar baqχitʃʼo
ɡʔjej kʼijajɡo ɡʼadan ana betleɡʔjemalde ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjel ʃaɡʔaralde ʒanire ʃːwarabɡo ɡʔjenib kʼudijab baʁa batʃari ɬuɡʔana ɡʔaj ɡʼadan unɡoɡi noɡʼomijiʃː ʁarin an χʼikmaɬun kʼaɬalel rukʼana rutʃːabi
noɡʼomitsa ɡʔjezije ʒawab kʔun abuna dida tʼokʼab noɡʼomijan ɡʔuinajin abuɡe marajin kʔoɡʼajin abe ʃːajɡureɬul dide qʼudrataw allaɡʔasul kʼudijab balaɡʔ reʃːtʼun buɡeɬul
dun ɡʔanisa ana betʃedaj ɡʼadanɬun amma ɡʔale betʼjerɡʔanas tʃʼoɡo tʼad jusːinajuna ʃːaj nuʒetsa dida noɡʼomijan abuleb betʼjerɡʔanas dije tamiχʼ ɡʔabuna qʼudrataw allaɡʔas dida tʼade balaɡʔ reʃːtʼinabuna
ɡʔjedin jusːana noɡʼomi tsadaqχ ʒindirɡo nus rut moɡʼawijajɡun moɡʼawaɬul rakʔaldasa betleɡʔjemalde ɡʔjeb bukʼana purtʃʼina ɬiɬize bajbiχʔuleb zaman

noɡʼomil wukʼana rosasul raqχaɬan ɡʼaɡaraw ɡʼjezeɡʼan qʼadru qʼimat buɡew eli malikilɡun tso qʼawmaɬul tʃi ɡʔjesda tsʼar bukʼana boɡʼaz
rut ana wa ɬiɬaruqχabazda χadu χaduj jiɬːun ɡʔjezuqχa ʁorkʔa χutʼarab tʼor biʃːize ʒujana ɡʔjeb χuraɬul betʼjerɡʔan watana boɡʼaz eli malikil aɡʔlujaɬul tʃi
ɡʔjelde tʼadeɡi ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ ʒiwɡo boɡʼazɡi watʃʼana ɡʔjeniwe betleɡʔjemaldasan
betʼjerɡʔanas kumek ɡʔabeɡi jan kʼaɬana ɡʔjew ɬiɬaruqχabazda
betʼjerɡʔanasul barkat dudeɡi reʃːtʼaɡi jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjez ɡʔjesije
ʒindirɡo ɬiɬaruqχabaze betʼjerɬi ɡʔabize taraw tso tsewetelasda boɡʼazitsa tsʼjeχana doj ɡʼoloqχanaj jas ɬil kːolej jan
noɡʼomida tsadaqχ moɡʼawijazul rakʔaldasan jatʃʼaraj moɡʼawijaj jiɡin abun ʒawab kʔuna tsewetelas
doɬ dida tsʼjeχana beɡʔiliʃː ditsa ɬiɬaruqχabazda χadu χaduj jiɬːun ɡʔjezuqχa ʁorkʔ χutʼarab tʼor biʃːun ɡʔjeɬul dijeɡo ɡulal qʼaze jan radalɡo jatʃʼana doj wa ɡʔanʒeɬizeɡʼan tsodaɡʔabɡo meχaɬ ɡuroni ɬalqχitʃʼoɡo χʼaltʼulej jiɡo
ɡʔjebmeχalda boɡʼaz kʼaɬana rutida dir jas ɡʼjenekːe diqχ mun tʼokʼaj tsoɡidal χurzabaqχe unɡe tʼor biʃːize ɡʔanisa kijeɡo unɡe mun dir ɡʔanir χʼaltʼulel ruɡel rutʃːabazda tsadaqχ jikʼa
ɬiɬaruqχabi χʼaltʼuleb bakʼ biχʔun ɡʔjezda χaduj χʔwade ditsa dir kinalɡo χʼaltʼuqχabazda ɬazabun buɡo mun qʼwarid ɡʔajuɡejan qʼetʃon ɬim ɡʔjeqʼeze bokʔani dir tseretelaz tsʼun ɬun ruɡel ɡʼjertʼazuqχa ɡʔjeqʼe jan
ɡʼodor nakabiɡi tʃʼwan qʼulana ɡʔjej ɡʔjesije wa abuna ʃːaj dutsa ɡʔjediɡʼan dida tsʼob ɬun dir tʼalab aʁaz ɡʔabuleb dun qʼwatʼisejɬidal
boɡʼazitsa ʒawab ɡʔabun abuna dida raɡʼana dur ros χun χadub dutsa durɡo jakʔadaɬe ɡʔaburabʃːinab ɬikʼɬijaɬul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ ebel emenɡi durɡo watʼanɡi reχun tun mun tʃijar rakʔalde ɡotʃarajɬi
razi ɡʔajeɡi mun betʼjerɡʔanas ɡʼizrailil allaɡʔas dutsa ɡʔaburab ɬikʼabʃːinaɬuqχ dutsa ɡʔjesul tsʼobalda muʁtʃʼwan buɡeɬul
ɡʔjeɬ abuna betʼjertʃʼaqχad χadu χadubɡi dur ɡurχʼjel raχʼmujalde χʔul buɡo dir dutsa dun raziɬizajuna rekʼjee χʼalχʔi ɡʔabuna dur laʁtsin dun ɡureb meχaɬ
qʼade kwanije zaman ʃːwarabɡo boɡʼazitsa abuna rutida ɡʔanije jatʃʼa kʼaldib ʒo ɬe ɡʔanib qʼantsʼaduɬɡi tʃːun kwanaj durɡo tʃadil motʃʼu rut jatʃʼun ɬiɬaruqχabazda askʼoj ɡʼodoj tʃʼjedal ɡʔjes ɡʔjeɬije basːarab roɬul tʃʼjer kʔuna ɡʔjeɬ ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwana ʒeɡi naqχeɡi χutʼana
χaduj tʼadeɡi jaqχun ʒeɡi tʼor bakʼarize ɬuɡʔana boɡʼazitsa ʒindirɡo χʼaltʼuqχabazda ɬazabuna bitʃːante doɬ ɡulazda ɡʔorkʔosaɡi tʼor biʃːize woreɡi nuʒetsa doɬul rakʼ baqʼwazabuɡe
ɡulal qʼaleɬul nuʒetsaɡoɡi tso tso kwatsʼi ʁorkʔ te doɬije wa ʃːibɡo ɡʼajibɡi tʃʼwaɡe dolda
ɡʔjedinab χʼalalda markʼatʃʼumeχ ʃːwezeɡʼan bakʼarana rutitsa purtʃʼina lal tʼamun χadub ɡʔjeɬul baqχana ɡʼaɡa ʃaɡarɡo tso qʼali tsʼurab ʒo
ɡʔjebɡi bosun ʃaɡʔaralde ʃːwana wa ɡʔaɬul jakʔadalda biχʔana ɡʔaɬ ɡʼjezeɡʼan ʒo bakʼarun buɡebɬi ɡʔjelda tʼadeɡi rutitsa qʼwatʼibe baqχun batʃʼana wa jakʔadaɬe kʔuna qʼade kwanil tʼokɬun χutʼarab butʼa
jakʔadaɬ ɡʔalda tsʼjeχana kisa ʒaqʼa dutsa tʼor bakʼararab mun kij jikʼaraj χʼaltʼulej barkat ɬeɡi ʒaqʼa ɡʔadin dur tʼalab ɡʔaburaw tʃijasda
rutitsa ʒindirɡo jakʔadalda bitsana ɬil bakʼalda jikʼarajali ʒij χʼaltʼulej jikʼarab χurul betʼjerɡʔanasda tsʼar boɡʼaz buɡilan bitsana rutitsa
betʼjerɡʔanas barkat ɬeɡijin dosda tʃʼaɡojazeɡi χwarazeɡi ritʼuqχaw wuɡeɬul in abuna noɡʼomitsa nusalda noɡʼomitsa tʼadeɡi ʒubana dow tʃi niɬer ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi kːola dosda kʼola niɬee kumek ɡʔabize
moɡʼawijaj rutitsa abuna ʒindir χurzal rakʼarun ɬuɡʼizeɡʼan ʒindir χurzabaqχ wa ʒindir χʼaltʼuqχabazda askʼoj jikʼajilantsin abuna dos dida
noɡʼomitsa abuna ʒindirɡo nus rutida dosda tsere χʼaltʼulel rutʃːabazda tsadaqχ mun jikʼine jiɡebɬi ɬikʼ buɡo dir jas wa ɡʔjedin buɡoni ɬitsaɡo mun inʒit χʼaqʼir ɡʔajizeɡi ɡʔjetʃʼo
χurzabazuqχa purtʃʼina wa roɬ bakʼarun ɬuɡʼizeɡʼan

jakʔad noɡʼomitsa ɡʔjelda abuna munɡo jusːine tso ruqʼ qʼaj balaɡʔun ɬikʼ ɡuriʃː dir jas dujeɡo sanaɡʼat bukʼine
dole munɡun tsadaqχ χʼaltʼulel rukʼaral ɬiɬaruqχabazul betʼjerɡʔanɬun kːolew dow boɡʼaz ɡurewiʃː niɬer ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi qʼasi dos ɡʔotsʼib purtʃʼinadul lal reχuleb buɡo
ɡʔanʒe dutsa ɡʔumer kʼal wa tʃerχ tʃure ɡʔuinab maχʼaɬul naχɡi baχe wa biʃːun bertsinab retʼjelɡi retʼje mun ɡʔotsʼije a amma dow kwana ɡʔjeqʼon ɬuɡʼizeɡʼan dosda jiχʔize tʃʼoɡe
dow kʔiʒize weɡuleb bakʼ ɬazabe χaduj ineɡi un dosul χʼatʼazdasa jurʁan naqχe ɡʔabe wa ɡʔjesul χʼatʼaaχada jeɡa χadub ɡʔabize kːoleb dos bitsina duda jan
dutsa aburab ɡʔabila ditsa jan ʒawab kʔuna rutitsa
ɡʔjej ɡʔotsʼije ana wa kinabɡo jakʔadaɬ maɬuqχe ɡʔabuna
boɡʼaz ɡʼortsʼizeɡʼan kwanana wa ɡʔjeqʼana wa rakʼ raziɡo tʼorʃːalil ɡʼarijalda naqχa kʔiʒize weɡana ɡʔawuɡʔinɡo askʼojeɡi un jurʁanɡi tʼade borχun rut ɡʔjesul χʼatʼaaχada jeɡana
sordo baʃːaɬarab meχalda ɡʔjew tʼurkʼun wortʃʼana χʔibil swerize ɬuɡʔindal ʒinda askʼoj tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan jikʼin biχʔana
mun ʃːij kːolej jan ɡʔiqʼana ɡʔjes dun jiɡo dur laʁ rut jan ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjeɬ mun ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi wuɡeɬul dida tʼadeɡi durɡo kwarkʔi batʃe dutsa
betʼjerɡʔanas barkat ɬeɡi duda dir jas an ʒawab kʔuna ɡʔjes dutsa tsebe ɡʔaburaldasaɡi ɡʔab iʃ ʒeɡi qʼimatab buɡo mun ɡʼoloqχanal wasal ralaɡʔize ɬuɡʔintʃʼjeɬul ja betʃedal ja miskinal
ɡʔanʒe dir jas mun sunkʔaɡo χʼinqʼuɡe ditsa kinabɡo ɡʔabila dur ɡʔarijalda reqʼon ɡʔab ʃaɡʔaralda kinazdaɡo ɬaleɬul mun namus batsʼtsʼadaj ɡʼadan jikʼin
dun χʼaqʼiqʼataldaɡi dur ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi kːola amma didasa ɡʼaɡarawɡijin wuɡew
mun roɡʔineɡʼan ɡʔanij tʃʼa radal dosije bokʔani ʒindirɡo iχtijaraldasa pajda bosize ɡʔjedin bukʼine te amma dos inkar ɡʔabuni ɡʔale ʒiw χʼaqʼaw betʼjerɡʔanasul tsʼar baqχun ɡʔjedula dun duje ditsa ɡʔabila ɡʔjebmeχalda dur tʼalab kʔiʒa roɡʔine ʒeɡi ɡʼjezeɡʼan meχ buɡin
roɡʔineɡʼan ɡʔjej ɡʔjesul χʼatʼaaχada kʔiʒana wa qχaχʼɬi balelde tʼade jaqχana tʃʼuʒuɡʼadan ɡʔotsʼije jatʃʼun jikʼin ɬidaɡo ɬatʃʼoɡo ɬikʼ bukʼinilan pikru ɡʔabuna boɡʼazitsa
ɡʔjes abuna duda tʼad retʼun buɡeb ɡʼaba bose ɡʔanibe wa dida tsebe kːwe ɡʔjeb rutitsa ɡʔjedin ɡʔabidal anɬɡo rotsen
rut ʒindirɡo jakʔadaɬuqχe tʼad jusːindal noɡʼomitsa tsʼjeχana ʃːib kːarab dir jas in
rutitsa bitsana kinabɡo boɡʼazitsa ɡʔaburab ɬikʼɬi
wa tʼade ʒubana tʃʼoɡo jakʔadaɬuqχe tʼadjusːunɡejanɡi abun ɡʔale ɡʔab anɬɡo rotsen purtʃʼinadul kʔuna dos dije
noɡʼomitsa abuna ɡʔanʒe dir jas mun balaɡʔun tʃʼa kwatʼitʃʼoɡo ɬala duda ɡʔab iʃaɬul aχir ʒaqʼaɡo ɡʔaɬul tso χʼasil kːetʃʼoɡo dosul rakʼ sasine ɡʔjetʃʼo jan

boɡʼazitsa aχʼana ʃaɡʔaraɬul antsʼɡo kʼudijaw tʃi wa ɡʔjezda abuna ɡʼodor tʃʼa ɡʔanir ɡʔjel ɡʼodor tʃʼana
χaduw ɡʔaw kʼaɬana dow ɡʼaɡaraw tʃijasda moɡʼawijaldasa tʼadjusːaraj noɡʼomitsa rakʔ bitʃuleb buɡo ɡʔjeb kːola niɬer ɡʼaɡaraw tʃi eli malikil baɬ
ditsa χʼisab ɡʔabuna ɡʔjeb iʃ duda ɬazabize kːelin bitʃun bose ɡʔjeb ɡʔal kinalɡo ɡʔanir ɡʼodor tʃʼun ruɡezda wa ʒamaɡʼataɬul kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazda tsebe bosuleb batani bose bosulareb batani bosularebɬi ɬazabe dida tʼotsebeseb iχtijar dur buɡeɬul dun duda χadusew kːola jan
ditsa bitʃun bosila ɡʔjeb in abuna dos
tsinɡi boɡʼazitsa abuna dutsa ɡʔjeb rakʔ bitʃun bosarab qʼojaɬ dutsa jatʃine kːola χwarasul jikʼaraj ɬadi qʼorolaj moɡʼawijaj rutɡi ɡʔjeɬije ɡʔawuraw wasɡi ɡʼjezawize kːola ɡʔjeb rakʔ χwarasul naslujaɬe χutʼize
ɡʔjelda dande dow ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬul tʃijas ʒawab kʔun abuna ɡʔjedin batani dida kʼolaro ɡʔjeb rakʔ bitʃun bosize ʃːajɡureɬul dirɡo buɡebɡi maɡʼiʃat biχːula dir ɡʔjebmeχalda dur bukʼa abe iχtijar dida kʼolaro ɡʔjeb bosize
tsebe zamanajalda ɡʼizrailalda bukʼana ɡʔadinab ɡʼadat tsojas tsojasuqχe tso ʒo betsʼun bosize jaɬuni mulkaɬul betʼjerɡʔanɬi ɡʔabize ʒindirɡo buɡeb iχtijar kʔoleb buɡoni ɡʔaburab qʼotʼi ʃːula ɡʔabizeɬun ɡʔjew tʃijas tʼasa baqχulaan ʒindirɡo χʔit wa ɡʔjeb kʔolaan dow ʒinditsa iχtijar tʼade bosulew tʃijasuqχe ɡʼizrailaɬul χalqʼaɬul ɡʼadatalda reqʼon ɡʔjedin tasdiqʼ ɡʔabulaan qʼotʼi
ɡʼaɡarɬijaɬul tʃijas abuna boɡʼazida dutsaɡo bose jan wa ɡʔjes ʒindirɡo χʔit baqχun kʔuna ɡʔjesuqχe
ɡʔjebmeχalda boɡʼazitsa kʼudijal tʃaɡʼazda wa kinabɡo ʒamaɡʼatalda raɡʼizabun abuna ɡʔale nuʒ ruɡo ʒaqʼa nuɡʼzalɬun ditsa noɡʼomiqχa bosuleb buɡo kinabɡo eli malikil kileonil wa maχʼlonil bukʼarab milk
ɡʔjedinɡo maχʼlonida jikʼaraj moɡʼawijaj rutɡi jatʃunej jiɡo ditsa ɬadiɬun maχʼlonil bukʼarab maɡʼiʃat ɡʔjeɬul ɬimalaze irsaɬe ʃːweze wa ɡʔjesul aɡʔlu tʼaɡʼintʃʼoɡo bukʼine niɬer ʃaɡʔaralda nuʒ kinalɡo ruɡo ɡʔjeɬije nuɡʼzalɬun
tsinɡi kinalɡo ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabaqχ rukʼaraz wa kʼudijal tʃaɡʼaz abuna u niʒ ruɡo nuɡʼzalɬun betʼjerɡʔanas ʒindidasan ɡʼizrailil χalqʼ biʒaral rakelɡi leaɡi ɡʼadin ɡʔajeɡi dur minajaɬuje ʒanije ɬuɡʔunej jiɡej dur ɬadi wa ɡʼjemeral ɬimal ɡʔareɡi ɡʔjeɬ duje efratalda qʼudrat tsʼikʼkʼaɡi dur betleɡʔjemalda maʃɡʔurɬaɡi mun
bitʃːante ɡʔjeldaɬun betʼjerɡʔanas kʔurab naslujaɬ dur tuχum tamaritsa jaɡʔudaje ɡʔawuraw paretsil ɡʼadinab bukʼine
boɡʼazitsa rut ɬadiɬun jatʃana ɡʔjew ɡʔjelda askʼow weɡana wa betʼjerɡʔanas ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer kʔuna wa ɡʔjeɬije was ɡʔawuna
rutʃːabaz noɡʼomida abuleb bukʼana retsː betʼjerɡʔanase ɡʔjes mun irsilaw kamun tetʃʼo ɡʼizrailaldaɡo tsʼar raɡʼaraw waqχaɡi ɡʔjew was
ɡʔjes tsʼiɡʔabila dur ɡʼumru wa χerɬarab meχaɬ dur tʼalabɡi ɡʔabila mun jokʔulej wa ankʔɡo wasasdasaɡi duje ɬikʼaj dur nusaɬːidal ɡʔjew ɡʔawuraw
noɡʼomitsa kodowe watʃun χʔiχʔana ɡʔjew was
maduɡʔaliqχa rutʃːabaz abuleb bukʼana noɡʼomije was ɡʔawuna jan ɡʔjez ɡʔjesda owid abun tsʼar ɬuna ɡʔjew waqχana dawudil emen jiʃawil emenɬun
ɡʔale paretsil naslujaɬul raχas
paretsije ɡʔawuna χʼjetsron
χʼjetsronije ɡʔawuna ram
ramije ɡʔawuna ɡʼaminadaw
ɡʼaminadawije ɡʔawuna naχʼʃon
naχʼʃonije ɡʔawuna ʃalmon
ʃalmonije ɡʔawuna boɡʼaz
boɡʼazije ɡʔawuna owid
owidije ɡʔawuna jiʃaw
jiʃawije ɡʔawuna dawud

jefraimil tʼaɬijalda buɡeb tsufimazul ramataimaldasa
elkanaɡʔil kʼiɡo ɬadi jikʼana tsojalda tsʼar χanna tsoɡidalda tsʼar fenanna bukʼana fenannaje ɬimal ɡʔaruna χannaje ɡʔaritʃʼo
ʃːibab sonaɬ ʒindirɡo ʃaɡʔaraldasa waqχun unaan ɡʔjew tʃi ʃilojalde ɡutʃal askarazul betʼjerhanase
qʼurban qχunʃːinaqχe elkanaɡʔitsa fenannajeɡi ɡʔjeɬul wasal jasazeɡi butʼa kʔolaan
amma χannaje ɡʔjes kʼi kʼi butʼa kʔolaan ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjeɬije betʼjerhanas ɬimal kʔolel rukʼintʃʼoniɡi ɡʔjesije ɡʔjej χirijaj jikʼindal
betʼjerhanas ɡʔjeɬije ɬimal kʔolel rukʼintʃʼjeɬul fenannatsa kweʃɡo inʒit χʼaqʼir ɡʔajulaan ɡʔjej
ɬaɡʼalidasa ɬaɡʼalide ɡʔjedin kːolaan ʃːibab nuχaɬ betʼjerhanasul roqʼoje
elkanaɡʔitsa ɡʔjelda abulaan χanna ʃːaj mun ɡʼodulej ʃːaj dutsa kwen kwanalareb mun rakʼ baqʼwan ʃːaj jikʼunej antsʼɡo wasasdasaɡi ɬikʼaw ɡʔjetʃʼiʃː dun duje jan
tso qʼojaɬ ʃilojalda ɡʔjel kwana ɡʔjeqʼon χadub χanna tʼade jaqχana kaʃiʃ eliɡi wukʼana betʼjerhanasul ruqʼaɬul kʼaltʼa ɡʼodow tʃʼun
rakʼ baqʼwan ɡʼjek ɡʼjekijalda ɡʼodilaɡo betʼjerhanase duɡʼa ɡʔabize ɬuɡʔana χanna
betʼjerhanase nazru ɡʔabun χannatsa abuna
waj ɡutʃal askarazul betʼjerhan ɡʔaj dur laʁaɬul buɡeb dir qʼwariɬiɡi biχʔun ɡʔjelde dutsa ber balaɡʔani wa dur laʁ ɡʔaj dunɡi kʼotʃon tetʃʼoɡo dutsa ɡʔjeɬije ɬimerɬun was kʔuni ditsa ɡʔjew ɡʼumrujaɬeɡo betʼjerhanase qχuluqχaɬe wukʼine kʔjela wa ɡʔjesul botʼroda kidaɡo nusɡi qχwalaro
ɡʔjedin ɡʔorkʔosa qʼotʼitʃʼoɡo betʼjerhanasda tsee duɡʼa ɡʔabulej ɡʔjej jikʼaɡo eli wukʼana ɡʔjeɬul kʼutʼbuzda χadub χal kːun tʃʼun
χannatsa rekʼjeɬ ʒanib ʃːuruleb bukʼana duɡʼa ɡʔjeɬul kʼutʼbi raʁa ratʃarulel rukʼana amma qʼwatʼibe raɡʼi raɡʼuleb bukʼintʃʼo ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjej meχtaraj ɡʼadan jiɡin kːana elida
elitsa ɡʔjelda abuna mun kije ʃːwezeɡʼan ɡʔjedin meχtaliɬ jikʼine jiɡej ɡʔjeb meχtel te dutsa
ɡʔjelda dande ʒawab ɡʔabun χannatsa abuna ɡuro dir χʼaltʃʼaqχajaw emen tʃara buχʼun betʼjerhanasda tsebe dirɡo rekʼjel unti ɡʔurʃːulej ɡʼadan jiɡo dun tʃaʁiralda jaɡi tsoɡi ɡʔjeqʼoleb ʒojallda ditsa kʼal qχwatʃʼo
dun dur laʁ pasiqʼaj ɡʼadanɬun rikʼkʼunɡe dutsa kʼudijab paʃmanɬijaɬ rakʼ untun duɡʼa ɡʔabulej jikʼaraj ɡʼadan jiɡo dun ɡʔabɡoʃːinab meχaɬ
tsinɡi elitsa abuna paraχatɡo roqʼoje a durɡo ɡʼizrailaɬul allaɡʔas dur ɡʔari qʼabul ɡʔabeɡi
mun dida dur laʁalda ɡurχʼana janɡi abun ɡʔjej ɡʼadan ʒindirɡo nuχda ana kwanana ɡʔjeqʼana wa tʼokʼab ɡʔjeɬul ɡʔurmada paʃmanɬi zaɡʔirɬitʃʼo
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ radalɡo raqχun betʼjerhanase tʼaɡʼat ɡʼibadatɡi ɡʔabun ɡʔjel qʼwatʼire raqχana wa ramajalde
elkanaɡʔ ʒindirɡo ɬadi χannada askʼow weɡana betʼjerhanas ɡʔjelda tsʼob ɬuna wa
χannal urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana χaduseb sonaɬ ɡʔjeɬije was ɡʔawuna betʼjerhanasdasa ɡʔarun ʃːwana dije ɡʔaw ilanɡi abun ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjesda ʃamuil betʼjerhanasda raɡʼaraw aburab tsʼar ɬuna
elkanaɡʔ wa kinabɡo ɡʔjesul qχizan qʼaj betʼjerhanase qʼurban qχweze wa ʒindirɡo nazrabi tʼurazarize χaduseb sonaɬɡi qʼwatʼire raqχuneɬul
χanna ɡʔjezda tsadaqχ jiɬːintʃʼo
ɡʔjeɬ rosasda abuna betʼjerhanasda tsewe waqχun tʃʼjeze wa mirkaɬɡo dowa wukʼineɬun karandasa tʼjezawurawɡo ʃamuil ditsa ʃilojalde ʃːwezawila
tsinɡi elkanaɡʔitsa abuna duda bertsin biχʔarab ɡʔabe ɡʔjedin batani ɡʔjew karandasa tʼjezawizeɡʼan roqʼoj tʃʼa betʼjerhanas ʒindirɡo
ɡʔjedin roqʼoj tʃʼun χʔiχʔana ɡʔjeɬ was karandasa tʼjezawizeɡʼan
ʒeɡi ɡʔitʼinaw ɬimer wukʼaniɡi karandasa tʼjezawurawɡo betʼjerhanasul roqʼowe ʃilojalde ɡʔjew ʃːwezawize jatʃʼana χanna tsadaqχ qʼurbanaɬe qχweze ɬabɡo son barab basiɡi tso jefa
basi qʼurbanaɬe qχun χadub ɡʔjez was eliqχe watʃana
χannatsa elida abuna ja dir χʼaltʃʼaqχajaw emen duda rakʼalda jiɡiʃː dun dur berazda tsee ɡʔab bakʼalda betʼjerhanase duɡʼa ɡʔabulej jikʼaraj ɡʼadan jiɡo dun
ɡʔale ɡʔaw wasase ɡʼolo ɡʔardana dun dob qʼojaɬ betʼjerhanas qʼabul ɡʔabuna dir ɡʔari wa dir rekʼjel murad tʼubazabuna
ɡʔanʒe ditsaɡi betʼjerhanase wukʼine tʼokʼ ɡʔawun kʔolew wuɡo ɡʔaw mirkaɬɡo
tsinɡi ɡʔjez betʼjerhanase suʒda ɡʔabuna

χadub χannatsa ɡʔadinab duɡʼa ɡʔabuna
ja dir betʼjerhan dutsa dir rakʼ boχizabuna
dutsa dije qʼuwatɡi kʔuna
tuʃbabazda tsee kʼodo ɡʔajuna
dutsa tarqχan ɡʔajun awadanɬana
betʼjerhan ɡʼadin watsʼtsʼadaw ʃːiwɡo ɡʔjetʃʼo
ɡʔjetʃʼo tʼokʼaw mun ɡʼadaw
niʒer allaɡʔ borχatab kʔuru duda baʃːadab ʒo ʃːibniɡi ɡʔjetʃʼo
nuʒ tʼokʼaɬ tʃʼuχʼadɡo kʼaɬaɡe
qχatʃʼab kalam kʼaldisa qʼwatʼibe ine bitʃːaɡe
betʼjerhan allaɡʔ wuɡo kinabɡo ɬalew
ɡʼadamazul iʃal tsʼadirabazda tʼad ɬunin ruɡel
ɡutʃal raʁuqχabi ɡʼodor retʃʼtʃʼula
ɡutʃdaqʼal abuni qʼuwataɬ tsʼola
ɡʼortsʼun rukʼaral kwaniqχ χʼaltʼula
raqʼutsa χolel rukʼarazda raqʼi kʼotʃona
ɬimal ɡʔarulej jikʼintʃʼjeɬe ankʔɡo ɬimer ɡʔabula
amma ɡʼjemeral wasazul ebel janʁizɬula
betʼjerhanas ruχʼ baqχula wa ɡʔjesɡo ɡʼumruɡi kʔola
ɡʔjes ʒaɡʔandamanaɬul kʼkʼalaqχe reχula wa ɡʔjenisa rortʃʼizeɡi ɡʔarula
betʼjerhanas miskinɬizeɡi ɡʔarula wa ɡʔjesɡo betʃedɡi ɡʔarula
ɡʼodoreɡʼan kːezarula wa tʼadeɡʼanɬizeɡi ɡʔarula
χʼuruɬa raqχun rorχize ɡʔarula miskinal
wa raqχuɬa paqʼiral
χʼurmatijal taχbakʼazde raχinarula wa qʼadru qʼimatɡi nasibɬizabula ɡʔjezije
ɡʔab rakʔaɬe kʔutʃʼɡi betʼjerhanas ɬedal
wa ɡʔjeb kʔutʃʼalda tʼad ɡʔab dunjalɡi ɡʔjes reqʼezabidal
ʒindije ritʼuqχazul nuχal ɡʔjes tsʼunula
amma kweʃal tʃaɡʼi betsʼɬijaɬul tʼinda kʼalal ruqʼun kːezarula
ʃːajɡureɬul insan ʒindirɡo qʼuwataldaɬun berɡʔunareɬul
betʼjerhanasda dande tʃʼaral ʃːuʃːaqχ razarila
ɡʔjew zobalazdasa ʁuʁadila ɡʔjezde
tsojab raɡʼaldasa tsoɡidab raɡʼalde ʃːwezeɡʼan tʼolabɡo dunjal diwanalde aχʼize buɡo betʼjerhanas
ʒindirɡo patʃajase qʼuwat ɡʔjes kʔola
ʒindirɡo tʼasa wiʃːarase ɡutʃɡi ɡʔjesɡo kʔola
tsinɡi elkanaɡʔ ramatalde roqʼowe tʼadwusːana wasɡi kaʃiʃ elida askʼow betʼjerhanase qχuluqχaɬe tana
elil wasal χʼaliχʔatal ʒal rukʼana ɡʔjez ja betʼjerhanasul milat ɡʔabularoan
ja χalqʼalda χurχun kaʃiʃzabazda tʼadal iʃal tʼurazarularoan tso pulanaw tʃijas qʼurban qχoleb meχaɬ ɡʔan beɬine barabɡo kaʃiʃzabazul tsewetel watʃʼunaan ɬabɡʼusilab kʼudijab ɡʼutʃʼɡi kodob kːun
wa beɡʔulaan ɡʔjeb χʔaɡinibe jaɬuni qʼonojalde jaɬuni bolχʔaɡinibe jaɬuni qχabinibe ʒanibe wa ɡʼotʃʼoda qʼaze ʃːwarab ʒo ʒindijeɡo bosulaan ɡʔjedin ɡʔabulaan ɡʔjez kinalɡo ʃilojalde ratʃʼaral ɡʼizrailaze
ɡʔjebɡi ɡʼjetʃʼoɡo ʒeɡi tʼatʼi buχʼilalda tsebe kaʃiʃasul tsewetel watʃʼunaan wa qʼurbanaɬul χwaʒainasda abulaan kaʃiʃase beʒize ɡʔan kʔje beɬarab ɡʔan bosize ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔjes ɡʼatʼɡojab ɡuroni jan
ɡʔjew tʃijas tsin tʼatʼi buχʼizeɡʼan tʃʼa χadub bose dujeɡo bokʔarab ʒojan abuni tʃʼjelarin ɡʔabsaɡʼatɡo kʔje kʔjetʃʼoni χʼal ɡʔabun baqχililan abulaan
ɡʔjedin betʼjerhanasul qʼurbanal χʼaqʼir ɡʔaruraɬuqχ kʼudijab χʼaqʼ bukʼana ɡʔjel ɡʼoloqχanal kaʃiʃzabaze
ʃamuil abuni betʼjerhanase qχuluqχaɬe eχetun wukʼana ɡʔjew wukʼana muqʼadasab efod retʼunew was
ʃːibab sonaɬ ebelaɬ ɡʔitʼinab ɡʼaba buqʼulaan ɡʔjesije wa rosɡun tsadaqχ ɬaɡʼalil qʼurban qχweze jatʃʼarajɡo tsadaqχ ɡʔjebɡi bosun batʃʼunaan
elitsa elkanaɡʔil wa ɡʔjesul ɬadul raqχaldasan duɡʼa ɡʔabulaan
betʼjerhanas barakat ɬeɡi wa duje ɡʔaj ɡʼadanaldasa ɬimal kʔjeɡi ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔarun ʃːwaraw wa betʼjerhanase tʼokʼ ɡʔawun kʔuraw wasasul bakʼalda jan
χadur ɡʔjel roqʼore tʼadrusːunaan
betʼjerhanasul raχʼmu reʃːtʼana χannade wa ɡʔjeɬul urɡʔibe ɬimer kːana ʒeɡi ɬabɡo wasɡi kʼiɡo jasɡi ɡʔaruna ɡʔjeɬije ʃamuilin abuni betʼjerhanase qχuluqχɡi ɡʔabulaɡo kʼudijaw ɡʼolew wukʼana
eli tʼuwan χerɬana ɡʔjesda raɡʼuleb bukʼana ɡʔjesul wasaz ɡʼizrailaze ɡʔarulelʃːinal tʼjeqʼɬabazul χʼaqʼaɬuɬ wa maʒlisaɬul tʃodroda tsere qχuluqχ ɡʔabulel rutʃːabazda askʼor ɡʔjel reɡulebɬiɡi
ɡʔjew wasazda kʼaɬana ʃːaj nuʒetsa ɡʔjedinal ʒal ɡʔarulel tʼolabɡo χalqʼaɬ bitsuneb buɡo nuʒer qʼabiχʼal iʃazul
joqχ dir ɬimal ɬikʼab χabar ɡʔjetʃʼo ɡʔab dida raɡʼuleb wa betʼjerhanasul χalqʼaldaɡo ɡʔorkʔob tʼobitʼuleb buɡeb χabar
tso tʃijas tsoɡi tʃijase kweʃɬi ɡʔabuni ɡʔjesije duɡʼa ɡʔabila wa allaɡʔ tʼasa ɬuɡʔina amma insanas betʼjerhanasda dande tʃʼarab kweʃɬi ɡʔabuleb buɡoni ɬitsa ɡʔjesul raqχ kːweze buɡeb
amma ɡʔjesul wasaz insul raɡʼuqχ ɡʼin batʃʼo betʼjerhanas χwalil χʼukmu qʼotʼun bukʼindal ɡʔjezije
ʃamuilin abuni kʼudijaw ɡʼolew wukʼana wa betʼjerhanaseɡi ɡʼadamazeɡi χirijaw wukʼana ɡʔjew
tso qʼojaɬ allaɡʔasul awaraɡ watʃʼana kaʃiʃ eliqχe ɡʔadinab kalimaɡun
ɡʔadin abuleb buɡo betʼjerhanas dun watʃʼintʃʼiʃː dur ankʔumumuzuqχe ɡʔjel ʒeɡi misrijalda pirɡʼawnasul laʁzalɬun ruɡeb meχaldaɡo
kinalɡo ɡʼizrailaɬul qʼawmazda ɡʔorkʔosa tʼasa riʃːana ditsa ɡʔjel dijeɡo kaʃiʃzabiɬun rukʼine qʼurban qχoleb bakʼalde tʼade raχine kʔjekːenal ruχʼize wa dida tsebe efod bosize dur umumuzul iχtijaralde kʔuna ditsa tʼolalɡo ɡʼizrailazul ruχʼulel qʼurbanalɡi
ab ʃːaj dir roqʼor tʼurazarejan ditsa tʼad ɬural qʼurbanalɡi sajʁatalɡi χʼatʼikʔ merχʔulel dutsa dir ɡʼizrail χalqʼaɬ bosun batʃʼarabʃːinab sajʁataɬul biʃːun ɬikʼab butʼaɡi kwanan ɡarbalɡi ritsːat ɡʔarun didasaɡi tsere durɡo wasal ʃːaj ɡʔarulel
ɡʔjedinɬidal betʼjerhanas abuleb buɡo dur qχizan aɡʔlu wa dur insul tʼolabɡo ɡʼaɡarɬi abadijaɬeɡo dije qχuluqχaɬe rukʼine ruɡilan ɡʔjedun wukʼana dun amma betʼjerhanas ɡʔanʒe ɡʔadin ɬazabuleb buɡo ɡʔjedin bukʼinaro dun kʼodo ɡʔarural ditsaɡi kʼodo ɡʔarila amma dir tsʼar inʒit ɡʔabural ditsaɡi basra ɡʔarila
ditsa dur naslu wa dur ɡʼaɡarɬi ruχʼdaqʼɬizaburab zaman batʃʼuneb buɡo dur naslujaɬul tsoniɡi tʃi χerɬizeɡʼan χutʼize ɡʔjetʃʼo
duda tʼade balaɡʔ batʃʼina wa tsoɡidal ɡʼizrailazul riqʼzi ɡʔarzaɬi biχʔarabɡo baχilɬun χutʼila mun dur naslujalda ʒaniw tʼokʼaɬ kidaniɡi wukʼine ɡʔjetʃʼjeɬul ɡʼumru χalataw tʃi
naɡaɡʔɬun dir qʼurban qχoleb bakʼaldasa naqχe qʼotʼitʃʼoɡo dur naslujaɬul tʃi χutʼani ɡʔjewɡi dur beral maɡʼil tsʼjezarize wa rakʼ untizabize tarawɬun wukʼina wa dur naslujaɬul ʃːiwaw tʃi bitʼun ɡʼumru tʼjeɡʔarab zawalalda χolewɬun wukʼina
dur kʼijawɡo was χofniɡi pinχasɡi tso qʼojalda ʒanir χweze ruɡo ɡʔjele ɡʔjeb duje ɡʼalamatɬun bukʼina
tsinɡi ditsa dijeɡo waqχinawila dije bokʔuqχe χʔwadulew kaʃiʃ ditsa ɡʔjesul aɡʔlu ʃːulaɬizabila wa ditsa tʼasa wiʃːaraw patʃajasda tsadaqχ kidaɡo ɡʔjesul naslu bukʼina
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ dur aɡʔlu qχizamaɬul tʃʼaɡo χutʼarawʃːinaw tʃi ɡʼartsul ɡeraɬe

elil nuχmaɬijalda ʁorkʔ ʃamuil betʼjerhanase qχuluqχaɬe tʃʼun wukʼana betʼjerhanasul kalima wa ɡʔjesul ilɡʔam qʼanaɡʼatɬun bukʼana ɡʔjel qʼojaz
tso sordojaɬ eli ʒindirɡo busada weɡun wukʼana ɡʔjesul berazda kanɬi χutʼun bukʼintʃʼo ʃːibɡo biχʔularoan ɡʔjesda
ʒeɡi allaɡʔasul tʃiraqχ swintʃʼjeb ɡʼuʒ bukʼana wa ʃamuil allaɡʔasul ʁamas ʒanib ɬurab betʼjerhanasul roqʼow weɡun wukʼana
betʼjerhanas ʃamuilin abun aχʼana wa ɡʔjes ɡʔale watʃʼunew wuɡin ʒawab kʔuna
tsinɡi eliqχe wekerana ʃamuil dutsa aχʼun watʃʼana dun inɡi abun
amma ɡʔjes abuna ditsa aχʼitʃʼo mun tʼadwusːun weɡize a jan ʃamuil tʼadwusːun weɡize ana
betʼjerhanas tsoɡi nuχaɬ aχʼana ʃamuil ʃamuil in naqχeɡi eliqχe wekerana ɡʔjew dutsa aχʼun watʃʼana dun in abuna ɡʔjes amma elitsa abuna ditsa aχʼitʃʼo mun dir was tʼadwusːun weɡize a jan
ʃamuilida ʒeɡi betʼjerhanasul ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼun bukʼintʃʼo wa ʒeɡi betʼjerhanasul kalima ɡʔjesuqχe reʃːtʼun bukʼintʃʼo
betʼjerhanas ɬababileb nuχaɬɡi aχʼana ʃamuilide tʼade waqχun naqχeɡi eliqχe wiɬːana ɡʔjew dutsa aχʼun watʃʼana dun in abuna ɡʔjes
ɡʔjeb meχaɬ bitʃʼtʃʼana elida betʼjerhanas aχʼuleb bukʼin wasasde
tsinɡi elitsa ʃamuilida abuna mun tʼadwusːun weɡa naqχeɡi dude dob ɡʔarakʔaɬ aχʼani dutsa abe kʼaɬaj betʼjerhan dur laʁ ɡʼjenekːun wuɡo jan tsinɡi ʃamuil tʼadwusːun ʒindirɡo bakʼalda weɡana
betʼjerhan ilɡʔam ɡʔabun watʃʼun eχetana wa tsebeɡo ɡʼadin naqχeɡi aχʼana ʃamuil ʃamuil in ʃamuilitsa ʒawab kʔuna kʼaɬaj betʼjerɡʔan dur laʁ duqχ ɡʼjenekːun wuɡo jan
tsinɡi betʼjerhan ʃamuilida kʼaɬana ditsa ɡʼizrailalda ɡʔabize buɡo bitsun ʒib raɡʼarabʃːinasul ɡʼunduzuɬ baʁuleb iʃ
ditsa elil qχizan qʼajalda tʼade bitʼun bukʼarab kalima raɡʼa rakʔande ʃːun tʼubazabila ɡʔjeb qʼojaɬ
ditsa ɡʔjesda ɬazabun bukʼana ʒindir wasazul pasatab χʔwada tʃʼwadi bukʼin ɬaniɡi ɡʔjezije ɡʼadlu ɡʔabitʃʼjeɬuqχ ditsa tamiχʼ ɡʔabize buɡin ɡʔjesul qχizan aɡʔlujaɬeɡojan
ɡʔjedinɬidal dun ɡʔjedulew wuɡo elil qχizan qʼajaɬul χʼaqʼ ja qʼurbanaz ja tsoɡidal roɬul sajʁataz abadijaɬɡo tʃurize ɡʔjetʃʼjeb
roɡʔineɡʼan paraχatɡo kʔiʒana tsinɡi ʃamuil wa radalɡo tʼadeɡi waqχun betʼjerhanasul ruqʼaɬul nutsʼbi ritʃʼana ʃamuil χʼinqʼun wukʼana qʼasi ɬuɡʔarab ʒo elida bitsine
ʃamuil dir was in aχʼana elitsa ʃamuilide ɡʔale dun in dande ʒawab ɡʔabuna ɡʔjes
ʃːib duda betʼjerɡʔanas aburab ʃːibɡo baχtʃuɡe didasa duda bitsaraɬul tso raɡʼiɡitsin dutsa didasa baχtʃani betʼjerɡʔanas balaɡʔaɬukʔje kːezawila mun
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ʃamuilitsa kinabɡo zaɡʔir ɡʔabuna ɡʔjesije tso raɡʼi ɡʔorkʔob bitʃːatʃʼoɡo tsinɡi elitsa abuna ɡʔjew betʼjerhan wuɡeɬul ɡʔjes ʒindaɡo ɬikʼ biχʔarab ɡʔabeɡi jan
ʃamuil sanade waχana wa betʼjerhanas ɡʔjesije sunduɬɡo kumek ɡʔabuleb bukʼana ɡʔjes bitsuqχe kːoleb bukʼana kinabɡoɡi
ɡʔjedin danaldasa baqχarab beer ʃewalde ʃːwezeɡʼan tʼolabɡo ɡʼizrailalda ɬana ʃamuil betʼjerhanasul awaraɡ wukʼin
naqχe naqχeɡi ilɡʔam ɡʔabun ʃamuiliqχe watʃʼunaan betʼjerhan ʃilojalda wa ɡʔjeniw ʒindirɡo kalimajaldaɬun ɡʔjesije ʒiwɡo zaɡʔirɡi ɡʔawulaan

ʃamuilil raɡʼuqχ ɡʼjenekːulaan tʼolabɡo ɡʼizrail
pilistimalɡun raʁize qʼwatʼire raqχana ɡʼizrailal wa ewen ezeralda askʼob qʼaji tʃʼwan tʃʼana pilistimal apekalda rukʼana
pilistimal ɡʼizrailazda dande raʁize raqχana wa ɡʔjeb raʁuɬ ɡʔjez ɡʼizrailal ʁurana ɡʼizrailazul unqʼazarɡo tʃi tʃʼwana ɡʔjeniw
raʁuqχabi qʼaji tʃʼwarab bakʼalde tʼadrusːindal ɡʼizrailaɬul tsereqχabaz abuna
kinan betʼjerhanas niɬ ʒaqʼa pilistimazul kwerde kʔural ratʃʼa niɬetsa betʼjerhanasul qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas ʃilojaldasa ɡʔanibe bosize ɡʔjeb niɬeda tsadaqχ buɡoni niɬ tuʃbabazdasa χwasarɬize ruɡo
χalqʼaɬ ʃilojalde tʃaɡʼi ritʼana wa qχeruwimazul
ɡʔjeb betʼjerhanasul qʼotʼijaɬul ʁamas ɡʔjenibe ʃːwarabɡo ɡʼizrailaz ritʃːaral kʼudijal ɡʔarkʔaz rakʔ sorodizabuna
ɡʔjeb ɡʔarakʔ raɡʼun pilistimaz abuna
ɡʼizrailazda ɡʔorkʔob baqχarab dob kʼudijab aχʼi χʼuraɬul maɡʼna ʃːib
tsinɡi ɡʔjezda ɬana betʼjerhanasul ʁamas ɡʔjenibe batʃʼun bukʼin
wa ɡʔjel kutakalda χʼinqʼana
dozuqχe allaɡʔ watʃʼun wuɡo jan kʼaɬana ɡʔjel tsotsada waj balaɡʔ batʃʼana ɡʔanʒe niɬede ɡʔjeb ʒeɡi kːarab ʒo bukʼintʃʼo
waj ʃːibdaj ɡʔanʒe niɬetsa ɡʔabileb dozul ɡutʃal allaɡʔzabazdasa niɬ ɬitsa χwasar ɡʔarilel tʼade kʼudijal balaɡʔalɡi ritʃːan awlaqχalda dol misrijal ʁuraral allaɡʔzabiɬidal dol
jaχʼ ɡʔabe pilistimal qʼwakʼun tʃʼa dol nuʒer laʁzalɬun rukʼaral ɡʼadin nuʒɡo kːeze ɡurin ɡʔanʒe dozul laʁzalɬun
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ pilistimaz ɡʔjezda tʼade ɡʔalaɡab ɡʔuʒum ɡʔabuna wa ɡʼizrailal qʼezaruna ɡʼizrailal ʒiderɡo tʃadrazuqχe ɬutana tsʼaqʼ ɡʼasijab raʁ kːana ɡʔjenib wa ɡʼizrailazul ɬeberazarɡo tʃi tʃʼwana
betʼjerɡʔanasul ʁamasɡi baqχana pilistimaz wa elil kʼijawɡo was χofniɡi pinχasɡi tʃʼwana
ɡʔjebɡo qʼojaɬ raʁ kːarab bakʼaldasa wekerun ʃilojalde watʃʼana tso bunjaminijaw botʼrode χʼatʼɡi ban retʼjelɡi biqχun
ɡʔjew ɡʔjeniwe ʃːwarawɡo eli ʒindirɡo bakʼida nuχlul rakʔanda ɡʼodow tʃʼun wukʼana allaɡʔasul ʁansil urʁalida nuχde walaɡʔun tʃʼun wukʼana ɡʔjew watʃʼun ɡʔjew tʃijas kːarab ʒo bitsindal tʼolabɡo ʃaɡʔaralda kʼudijab maɡʼil ɡʔarakʔ baqχana
ɡʔjeb raɡʼun elitsa tsʼjeχana ɡʔab ʃːib aχʼi χʼur in
bunjaminijaw χeχɡo elida askʼowe wiɬːana
elitsa unqʼojalda antsʼila mikʔɡo son ban bukʼana wa ɡʔjesul beral tʼuran betsːɬun rukʼana
bunjaminijas elida abuna dun wuɡo raʁ kːarab bakʼaldasa ɡʔabsaɡʼat ʃːwaraw tʃi ʒaqʼa waqχana dun dowasa tsinɡi elitsa tsʼjeχana ʃːib doba kːarab dir was in
ɡʔjew χabar bosun watʃʼaraw tʃijas abuna ɡʼizrailal pilistimazuqχa qʼuna wa ɡʔjezul bojaɬe kʼudijab kami kːana dur kʼijawɡo was χofniɡi pinχasɡi tʃʼwana allaɡʔasul ʁamasɡi baqχun ana
ɡʔjes allaɡʔasul ʁansil tsʼar baqχarabɡo ʃaɡʔaraɬul kawabaqχ ʒindirɡo taχida ɡʼodow tʃʼun wukʼaraw eli naqχeχun reχun ɡʼodow retʃʼtʃʼana ɡʔjew wukʼana ʒanib tsʼurab qʼarqʼalajaɬul χeraw tʃi ɡʔjedinɬidal ɡʔjeb bakʼaldaɡo ɡaburɡi bekun ɡʔjew χwana kʼiqʼoɡo sonaɬ ɡʼizrailaɬe nuχmaɬi
ɡʔjesul nus pinχasil ɬadi ɬimade jikʼana ɡʔjebmeχalda wa ɬimer ɡʔabize meχ ɡʼaɡarɬuleb bukʼana allaɡʔasul ʁamas baqχun un buɡin wa wakʔadɡi rosɡi χun ruɡin raɡʼidal ɡʔjej untijaɬ ɡʼodoj ɬuna ɡʔjeb bakʼaldaɡo χʼaraɡi tʃʼwan ɬimerɡi ɡʔabuna
χwaliɬ jiɡej ɡʔjelda askʼor ruɡel rutʃːabaz abuleb bukʼana urʁel kːoɡe duje was ɡʔawuna jan
amma ɡʔjeɬ ɡʔjeb raɡʼuda dande ʃːibɡo ʒawab ɡʔabitʃʼo
wasasda iχawod qʼadru qʼuwataɬ taraw abun tsʼarɡi ɬun qʼadru qʼuwataɬ tana ɡʼizrail in abuna ɡʔjeɬ ʃːajɡureɬul betʼjerɡʔanasul ʁamas baqχun un bukʼindal wa ɡʔjeɬul wakʔadɡi rosɡi χun rukʼindal
ɡʔjeɬ abuna allaɡʔasul ʁamas baqχun un buɡeɬul ɡʼizrail qʼadru qʼuwataɬ tana jan

pilistimaz allaɡʔasul ʁamas ewen ezeraldasa bosun aʃdodalde ʃːwezabuna
tsinɡi ɡʔjez ɡʔjeb daɡonil
naqχiseb qʼojaɬ radalɡo tʼade raqχaral aʃdodaɬul ɡʼadamazda betʼjerhanasul ʁansida tsebe kʼalaʁorkʔje ɡʼodob retʃʼtʃʼun batana daɡonil statuja ɡʔjez ɡʔjeb daɡonil statuja tʼadbusːun ʒindirɡo bakʼalda eχetizabuna
χaduseb qʼojaɬ radalɡo tʼade raqχun ralaɡʔidal daɡonil statuja dodinɡo kʼalaʁorkʔje kːun betʼjerhanasul ʁansida tsebe ɡʼodob retʃʼtʃʼun batana ɡʔjeɬul betʼjerɡi kweralɡi rek rekun raɡʔumaχʼujalde reχun ratana daɡonil naqχe χutʼarab ʒo tsoχʼo qʼarqʼala buɡoan
ɡʔjedinɬidal ʒaqʼa qʼojalde ʃːwezeɡʼanɡi daɡonil kaʃiʃzabaz wa aʃdodalda buɡeb ɡʔjesul roqʼore ratʃʼunel ɡʼadamaz ɡʔjeb raɡʔumaχʼujalda tʼad χʼjetʼje tʃʼolaro
betʼjerhanasul tsːin reʃːtʼana aʃdodaɬul ʒamaɡʼatalde wa ɡʔjezul sweruqχɬijaldeɡo aʃdodɡi tʼolabɡo sweruqχɬiɡi tʃʼuntizabuna ɡʔjes wa retsʼtsʼ kːaral ruʁnal raqχana ɡʼadamazul tʃerχalda
ɡʔjeb kinabɡo biχʔidal aʃdodaɬul ɡʼadamaz abuna
ɡʼizrailaɬul allaɡʔasul ʁamas niɬer ɡʔanib teze beɡʔularo ʃːajɡureɬul ɡʔjesul ɡʼasijab tsːin buɡo niɬedaɡi niɬer allaɡʔ daɡonidaɡi
tsinɡi tʼolalɡo pilistimazul tsereqχabi dande aχʼana ɡʔjez wa ɡʔjezda tsʼjeχana ɡʼizrailaɬul allaɡʔasul ʁansida ʃːibdaj ɡʔabun ɬikʼ in ɡʔjez ʒawab kʔuna ɡʼizrailaɬul allaɡʔasul ʁamas ɡatalde ʃːwezabe jan
tsinɡi ɡʔjez ɡʼizrailaɬul allaɡʔasul ʁamas ɡatalde ʃːwezabuna
amma ɡʔjeb ɡʔjenibe ʃːwarabɡo ɡʔjeb ʃaɡʔaralda tʼadeɡi betʼjerhanasul tsːin reʃːtʼana wa tʼolabɡo ʃaɡʔar χʼinqʼun biχːa χotʃana kʼudijal ɡʔitʼinal batʼaɬi ɡʔjetʃʼoɡo kinazdaɡo retsʼtsʼulel ruʁnal raqχana
tsinɡi ɡʔjez ɡʔjeb allaɡʔasul ʁamas ekronalde bitʼana
ɡʔjebmeχaɬ ekronaɬul ʒamaɡʼat tʃʼtʃʼi tʃʼtʃʼidana niɬ kinalɡo χwezarize ɡʼizrailaɬul allaɡʔasul ʁamas batʃʼun buɡo niɬeqχe janɡi abun
tsinɡi pilistimazul tsereqχabi dandeɬana wa ɡʔjez ɬazabuna ɡʼizrailaɬul allaɡʔasul ʁamas naqχe bitʼje ʒindirɡo bakʼalde tʼadbusːinabe ɡʔjeb niɬ kinalɡo χwezaritʃʼoɡo rukʼine
χʼinqʼarab χʼinqʼijaɬ tʼolabɡo ʃaɡʔaraɬul ruχʼ tʼun bukʼana allaɡʔasul ɡʔalaɡab tsːin reʃːtʼun bukʼindal ɡʔjezda tʼade
tʃʼaɡo χutʼaral ɡʼadamalɡi retsʼtsʼulel ruʁnal tʼad raqχun ɡʼazab ɡʼaqʼubajalda rukʼana wa kʼudi kʼudijal ɡʔarkʔazdaɬun zobalazdasa kumek ɡʔarulel ɡʔuja ɡʔarajalda ɡʼoda tʃʼwadijalda rukʼana
